Matthew1:1 Enkitabu eiunoto e Yesus Kristos-- enkerai e David-- enkerai e Abraham."
Matthew1:2 Etoiwuo Abraham Isaak. Neiu Isaak Yakoob. Neiu Yakoob Yuda o lalashera lenyena;
Matthew1:3 neiu Yuda Peres o Seraa te Tamar; neiu Peres Esrom; neiu Esrom Raam;
Matthew1:4 neiu Raam Aminadab; neiu Aminadab Naashon; neiu Naashon Salmon;
Matthew1:5 neiu Salmon Boas te Rahab; neiu Boas Obed te Rut; neiu Obed Yese;
Matthew1:6 neiu Yese olkarsis David. Neiu David Salomo tʼengʼoroyoni e Uria:
Matthew1:7 neiu Salomo Rehabeam; neiu Rehabeam Abia; neiu Abia Asa;
Matthew1:8 neiu Asa Yosafat; neiu Yosafat Yoram; neiu Yoram Usiya;
Matthew1:9 neiu Usiya Yotam; neiu Yotam Ahas; neiu Ahas Hiskiya;
Matthew1:10 neiu Hiskiya Manase; neiu Manase Amon neiu Amon Yosiya;
Matthew1:11 neiu Yosiya Yekonya o lalashera lenyena tʼenkata enkibooroto te Babel.
Matthew1:12 Ore peishunye enkibooroto te Babel-- neiu Yekonya Sealtiel; neiu Sealtiel Serubabel;"
Matthew1:13 neiu Serubabel Abihud; neiu Abihud Eliakim; neiu Eliakim Asor;
Matthew1:14 neiu Asor Sadok; neiu Sadok Akim; neiu Akim Eliud;
Matthew1:15 neiu Eliud Eleasar; neiu Eleasar Matan; neiu Matan Yakoob;
Matthew1:16 neiu Yakoob Yosef-- olmoruo le Maria natoiwuo Yesus-- oji Kristos."
Matthew1:17 Akae-- ore lajijik pookin eiter te Abraham metabaiki David-- naa lajijik tomon o ong'wan; ore eiter te David metabaiki enkibooroto te Babel-- lajijik tomon o ongʼwan; ore eiter tʼenkibooroto te Babel metabaiki Kristos-- lajijik tomon o ong'wan."
Matthew1:18 Neaku eiunoto e Yesus Kristos nji: Ore Maria ng'otonye enye-- esanjanita Yosef neton eitu enyikakino-- nelioi emena tʼenkidimata Olmumua Sinyati."
Matthew1:19 Tiaraki nara Yosef oltung'ani supat-- neitu eyeu neitukurru neyeu neing'ua ninye tʼemikio."
Matthew1:20 Ore eibirribirrita kuna-- ng'orai-- nelioi olmalaika lʼOlaitoriani te ninye tʼenkidetidetata ejo: Yosef-- nakerai e David-- miurei iamaa eng'oroyoni ino Maria-- amu etaa emenai enye tʼenkidimata Olmumua Sinyati."
Matthew1:21 Nelaiu ninye enkerai olee nimpot engarna enye Yesus-- amu ninye olaitopok olorere lenye tiatua nkitarruot enye."
Matthew1:22 Etaa kuna pookin-- pebaia enairoro Olaitoriani tʼolayolounoni ejo:"
Matthew1:23 Ng'orai-- elamenai entito neiu enkerai olee-- nepuo aaipot ninje engarna enye: Imanuel-- ore enkitaalata enye: Eboitare yook Engai."
Matthew1:24 Ore peinyototo Yosef too njok-- neitobir anaa peitanapa ninye olmalaika lʼOlaitoriani-- neamaa eng'oroyoni enye."
Matthew1:25 Neitu eyolou ninye tukul-- metabana nelaiu olkikau lenye; neipot engarna enye Yesus."
Matthew2:1 Ore peiuni Yesus te Betlehem e Yudaya-- tʼenkata olkarsis Herodes-- ng'orai-- nepuonu lang'eni ooing'ua enkilepunoto engolong'-- nebau Yerusalem--"
Matthew2:2 ejo: Kaji etii olotoiwuoki olkarsis loo Yudayoi? Amu kitadua olakira lenye tʼenkilepunoto engolong-- nikietuo si yook aaserem ninye."
Matthew2:3 Ore pening' olkarsis Herodes kuna-- neng'ayung'ayu ninye te nebo o Yerusalem pookin."
Matthew2:4 Ore peiturrur laidasak kituak pookin o layolok lʼesirata tiatua olorere-- nesipunye ninje eneiunyeki Kristos."
Matthew2:5 Nejoki si ninje: Te Betlehem e Yudaya-- amu neijia etisiraki tʼolayolounoni:"
Matthew2:6 Ore iye-- Betlehem-- olosho le Yuda-- mira kiti tukul too laigwenak le Yuda; amu epuku te iye olaiturukoni olairrita olorere lai Israel."
Matthew2:7 Ore peidipai-- neipot Herodes lang'eni tʼenkilepata netum too ninje esiparoto enkata natalie olakira--"
Matthew2:8 neutaki Betlehem-- nejo: Embung'a engoitoi-- entisiputu naleng' mbaak enkerai; ore pindipidipi aatadol-- nikintayololo-- peiye alotu si nanu aserem ninye."
Matthew2:9 Ore peidip aatoning' olkarsis-- neibung' engoitoi-- naa ng'orai-- neiturukie ninje ilo akira lotadua tʼenkilepunoto engolong'-- metabana nelotu aitashe te shumata ene wueji netii enkerai."
Matthew2:10 Ore pedol ninje ilo akira-- neng'ida tʼeng'ida kitok naleng'."
Matthew2:11 Nejing' aji nedol enkerai te nebo o Maria ng'otonye enye-- nebatata aaserem ninye; nebolu masaa enye neisho ninye esahabu o emanoo narropil o eilata enkinyang'a nagol."
Matthew2:12 Neitanap Engai ninje tiatua enkidetidetata-- pemerrinyokino Herodes; neim engai oitoi aapuo enkop enye."
Matthew2:13 Ore peidip aashom lelo-- ng'orai-- nelioi olmalaika lʼOlaitoriani te Yosef tiatua enkidetidetata-- ejo: Tudumunye-- toriko enkerai o ng'otonye-- sikaki Misri-- pibik te ina alo metabana naaliki iye; amu eyeu Herodes neing'oru ina kerai-- peiminye."
Matthew2:14 Nedumunye ninye neibung' enkerai o ng'otonye kiarie nelo metabaiki Misri.
Matthew2:15 Nebik te ina alo-- metabana nee Herodes-- pebaia enairoro Olaitoriani tʼolayolounoni ejo: Aipoto enkerai ai aitung'ua Misri."
Matthew2:16 Ore pedol Herodes-- ajo eteleja lang'eni ninye-- negoro naleng'-- neirriwaa-- peari nkera oo leak pookin naatii Betlehem o nkutot enyena pookin-- eiter too noo larin aare o neitu eishu-- tʼenkata natisipua too lang'eni."
Matthew2:17 Nebaia enairoro olayolounoni Yeremiya ejo:
Matthew2:18 Etoning'oki oltoilo te Rama-- enkishirata kitok o olkiyoi; Rahel naishiraki nkera enyena-- nemeitigirai-- amu mekure etii."
Matthew2:19 Ore pee Herodes-- ng'orai-- nelioi olmalaika lʼOlaitoriani te Yosef tiatua enkidetidetata te Misri"
Matthew2:20 ejo: Tudumunye-- mbung'a enkerai o ng'otonye-- mbung'a engoitoi alo olosho le Israel-- amu etuata looing'orutua oltau lʼenkerai."
Matthew2:21 Nedumunye neibung' enkerai o ng'otonye nelotu olosho le Israel.
Matthew2:22 Kake ore pening'-- ajo eitorisho Arkelaos te Yudaya tʼewueji e Herodes lora menye-- neurei elo ina alo; neroji tʼenkidetidetata-- pelo metabaiki mbat e Galilaya."
Matthew2:23 Nelotu nebik tʼengang' naji Nasaret-- pebaia enairoro layolounok aajo: Eipoti ninye Olnasarayos."
Matthew3:1 Nedumunye too nona olong'i Yohanes Olaibatisani neinosu lomon lʼEngai ti ang'ata e Yudaya
Matthew3:2 nejo: Entaalata! amu etinyikua enkarsishu e shumata.
Matthew3:3 Nera ninye ake ilo loiroro olayolounoni Yesaya otejo: Etii oltoilo lʼoloipotisho ti ang'ata: Entobira engoitoi Olaitoriani-- entorioi nkiimat enyena!"
Matthew3:4 Neishopito Yohanes openy olkila loo lpapit lʼendames o enkimeita enjoni tʼempolos enye; nera endaa enye ilmaat o naishi oo mulugi.
Matthew3:5 Nepuo enetii ninve lootii Yerusalem o Yudaya pookin o loshon pookin lʼembata e Yordan
Matthew3:6 neisho eibatis ninye ninje tiatua engare Yordan-- neibalu nkitarruot enye."
Matthew3:7 Ore pedol ninye Ilfarisayoi o Sadukayoi kumok epuonu enetii enkibatisa enye-- nejoki ninje: Ndai embeu oo lasuria-- kang'ai otiaka ndai-- ajo ilanyaanya engoro e akenya?"
Matthew3:8 Akae-- entoiu ilmomo sidan lʼenkitaalata!"
Matthew3:9 Emijo too ltauja linyi aajo: Kiata papa lora Abraham. Amu aliki ndai-- ajo eidim Engai ainyeyeki Abraham nkera tiatua kulo soito."
Matthew3:10 Eidipaki aatipik entolu entonata oljani; akae-- ore oljani pookin lemeiu ilmomo sidan-- nedung'i nenang'akini atua enkima."
Matthew3:11 Aibatis nanu ndai tʼengare-- pitumutumu aataalata; ore ninye olotu tekurum ai egol naalang' nanu-- namaiteu atanapa namuka enyena; elaibatis ninye ndai tʼOlmumua Sinyati o tʼenkima."
Matthew3:12 Neata enkutet enye tiatua engaina enye nelaor ninye naleng' eneisalaashishore-- neiturrur entapa enye tʼembeje; kake ore suut nepej tʼenkima nememuta."
Matthew3:13 Nelotu Yesus eing'ua Galilaya metabaiki Yordan enetii Yohanes-- peiye eibatisi ninye."
Matthew3:14 Kake etomitikio ilo ninye nejo: Eaku pikimbatis iye nanu-- nilotu si iye enatii?"
Matthew3:15 Nealiki ake Yesus nejoki: Tapala nena taata! amu meata kata nimikintabaia erioto pookin. Akae-- neiruk ninye."
Matthew3:16 Ore peidipi aaibatisa Yesus-- neilepu nabokata tʼengare; naa ng'orai-- nebolo shumata-- nedol ninye Olmumua lʼEngai edou anaa olmaitai nelotu shumata enye."
Matthew3:17 Naa ng'orai-- neing'ua oltoilo shumata nejo: Nyele Oinoti lai lanyor oshipakino oltau lai."
Matthew4:1 Nerik Olmumua Yesus te ina kata ang'ata-- peiye etem satan ninye."
Matthew4:2 Neitupukoo kion ngolong'i artam-- dama o kiarie-- netum tekurum olamei."
Matthew4:3 Nelotu olaitasuroni enetii ninye nejo: Teni ira Oinoti lʼEngai-- ntanapa kulo soito-- peaku endaa."
Matthew4:4 Nealiki nejo: Etisiraki: Meishiu oltung'ani tʼendaa ake-- kake tʼororei pookin opuku tʼenkutuk Engai."
Matthew4:5 Neitoki arik satan ninye atua engang' sinyati neitasheye ninye tʼoldidio lʼengaji sinyati
Matthew4:6 nejoki ninye: Teni ira Oinoti lʼEngai-- tusulakinoi enkop-- amu etisiraki: Kintanapaki ilmalaikan lenyena-- pekinap te shumata oo ngaik-- pemikinkob osoit enkeju ino."
Matthew4:7 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Eitoki si asira: Mitem Olaitoriani-- Engai ino!"
Matthew4:8 Neitoki arik satan ninye shumata oldonyo oado naleng' neitadol ninye nkarsishuni pookin olmaa o enkitook enye
Matthew4:9 nejoki ninye: Aaisho iye kuna pookin-- teni kibatatakino nikiserem."
Matthew4:10 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Nno-- satan! amu etisiraki: Teserema Olaitoriani-- Engai ino-- syayaki ninye openy ake!"
Matthew4:11 Neing'ua satan ninye-- ng'orai-- nepuonu ilmalaikan aaisyayaki ninye."
Matthew4:12 Ore pening' Yesus-- ajo eteenaki Yohanes-- nedumunye alo Galilaya."
Matthew4:13 Neing'ua engang' Nasaret nelotu aton te Kapernaum natii embata olbalbal-- erishata e Sebulon o Naftali--"
Matthew4:14 peiye ebaia enairoro olayolounoni Yesaya ojo:
Matthew4:15 Olosho le Sebulon o olosho le Naftali tʼembata engoitoi olbalbal-- lido kekun le Yordan-- o Galilaya oo loreren--"
Matthew4:16 olorere otii atua enaimin-- etadua ninye enkilang'et kitok; o kulo oototonitio tʼolosho o tʼoloip lʼenkea-- eilepaka ninje enkilang'et."
Matthew4:17 Neiter Yesus te ina kata ainosu lomon lʼEngai ejo: Entaalata-- amu etinyikua enkarsishu e shumata."
Matthew4:18 Nelimana Yesus tʼembata olbalbal le Galilaya nedol lalashera aare-- Simon oji Petros-- o Andreas-- olalashe lenye-- enang'aki rresheta enye atua olbalbal-- amu era larreshok loo singir."
Matthew4:19 Nejoki ninje: Entusujaki-- aitaa ndai larreshok loo ltung'anak!"
Matthew4:20 Neing'ua nabokata rresheta enye nesuj ninye.
Matthew4:21 Ore peigut peno-- nedol kulekai alashera aare-- Yakobos le Sebedayos o Yohanes-- olalashe lenye-- te nebo o Sebedayos-- menye lenye-- tiatua engalawa-- eripita rresheta enye; neipot ninje."
Matthew4:22 Neing'ua ninje nabokata engalawa o menye lenye-- nesuj ninye."
Matthew4:23 Nemanaa Yesus te Galilaya pookin-- eiteng'enisho too ngajijik Engai enye neinosu lomon lʼeng'ida lʼenkarsishu neishiunye moiyaitin pookin o menatishuitin pookin tiatua olorere."
Matthew4:24 Neibulu mbaak enyena atua Siria pookin. Neaki ninye loomoiyaa pookin-- looibung'a nkeaitin o mioitin kumok-- looata ilmeneng'a-- looata olkiterriata-- looata supeta-- neishiunye ninje pookin."
Matthew4:25 Nesuj isiamin kumok ninye eing'ua Galilaya o Manyat tomon o Yerusalem o Yudaya o lido kekun le Yordan.
Matthew5:1 Ore pedol ninye siamin-- neilepaki oldonyo neton; nepuonu laiteng'enuok enetii ninye."
Matthew5:2 Nebol enkutuk enye neiteng'en ninje ejo:
Matthew5:3 Teshi loora laisinak lʼolmumua-- amu era enkarsishu Engai enenye."
Matthew5:4 Teshi looata enkilishoto-- amu epuoi aaitigir lelo."
Matthew5:5 Teshi loobor-- amu epuo aajung'u lelo enkop."
Matthew5:6 Teshi looata olamei o enkure esupato-- amu epuo aaraposho lelo."
Matthew5:7 Teshi loonana oshuak-- amu epuoi aaibung'aki engoshoke nanana."
Matthew5:8 Teshi looibor iltauja-- amu epuo aadol lelo Engai."
Matthew5:9 Teshi loonyor eseriani-- amu epuoi aaipot lelo nkera Engai."
Matthew5:10 Teshi looinyali tʼolbae lʼesupato-- amu enenye enkarsishu e shumata."
Matthew5:11 Irara ndai teshi-- teni emor neinyal iltung'anak ndai neiro ntorrok too ndai tʼolbae lai-- elejisho."
Matthew5:12 Enting'idata-- entagoluoto-- amu kitok olkwaje linyi te shumata. Amu neijia einyala ninje layolounok looiturukie ndai."
Matthew5:13 Irara ndai emakat olmaa. Kake teni etarruoiye emakat — kainyo epiki-- pejing'aa? Meitoki aaku tukul-- kake eiturrakini boo-- neroro olorere ninye."
Matthew5:14 Irara ndai enkilang'et olmaa. Meidim engang' aisudori natii enetala.
Matthew5:15 Nemeinok iltung'anak enkilang'et nepik kop olkisembe-- kake epik shumata enkibung'et-- peilang'aki pookin lootii atua aji."
Matthew5:16 Neijia njeilang'isho enkilang'et inyi tʼengomom oo ltung'anak-- petum aatadol nkitobirat inyi sidan-- peitadaraa Minyi linyi otii shumata."
Matthew5:17 Emijo-- aajo aewuo nanu-- paar nkitanapat o layolounok; me-- eitu alotu-- paar ninje-- kake aewuo-- paitabaia."
Matthew5:18 Amu japa aliki ndai: Metabana nemuta shumata o enkop-- memuta oltipoto arashu oltili obo loo nkitanapat oo metaa pookin."
Matthew5:19 Akae-- ore oltung'ani omen enkitanapata nabo too kuna kutiti neiteng'en iltung'anak nji-- neipoti olkiti tukul tiatua enkarsishu e shumata: ore oltung'ani loitobir neiteng'enu ninje-- neipoti ilo olkitok tiatua enkarsishu e shumata."
Matthew5:20 Amu aliki ndai: Teni melang' esupato inyi esupato oo layolok lʼesirata o noo Lfarisayoi-- nimijing'ijing'i enkarsishu e shumata tukul."
Matthew5:21 Itoning'o-- aajo etiakaki iltung'anak le opa: Miar metua; oloar metua-- meata kata nemeigwenakini."
Matthew5:22 Kake aliki nanu ndai: Ologoroki olalashe lenye-- meata kata nemeigwenakini; olojoki olalashe lenye: Mira toki! meata kata nemeigwenakini tiatua esiamu; olojo ake: Kimba Engai! meata kata nemear ninye enkima nememuta."
Matthew5:23 Akae-- teni iau enkishooroto ino olperere lʼenkidasare nidamu te ina alo-- ajo kiataiye olalashe lino ororei--"
Matthew5:24 tung'ai enkishooroto ino tʼengomom olperere lʼenkidasare-- nno-- tang'asa ntobirakinore olalashe lino-- pitum atorrinyoi-- pintarasaa enkishooroto ino."
Matthew5:25 Ntobirakinore olaitang'oroni lino asioki-- epon iriamunyenye t'engoitoi-- pimikirik ele aitang'oroni lino enetii olaigwenani-- nikintarasaki olaigwenani ngaik olaisyayani-- pikieni."
Matthew5:26 Japa-- aaliki iye: Mipuku tiatua tukul-- metabana nindip atalaa empesai enkiting'oto."
Matthew5:27 Itoning'o-- aajo etiakaki iltung'anak le opa: Miar enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni!"
Matthew5:28 Kake aliki nanu ndai: Oloing'oraa eng'oroyoni neng'war ninye-- eidipa ilo ataara enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni tiatua oltau lenye."
Matthew5:29 Teni kintapong'oo engong'u ino e tatene-- tukurtu ninye-- nturraki enelakwa; amu eikash te iye-- teni eimin embata ino nabo-- nemenang'akini osesen lino olulung'a atua enkima e gehena."
Matthew5:30 Teni kintapong'oo engaina ino e tatene-- tudung'o ninye-- nturraki enelakwa-- amu eikash te iye-- teni eimin embata ino nabo-- pemelo osesen lino olulung'a atua gehena."
Matthew5:31 Etejoki si: Teni eing'ua oltung'ani eng'oroyoni enye-- njeisho ninye empalai erishata."
Matthew5:32 Kake aliki nanu ndai: Oloing'ua eng'oroyoni enye neme too mbaak entalare-- eitaa ninye-- peaku engaarani enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni; ore oloamu enatung'aiyoki-- near ninye enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni. Mindimidimi aaisyayakiti Engai o mamon (masaa)."
Matthew5:33 Ninyaakitia si aaning'-- aajo etiakaki iltung'anak le opa: Minturuj ilejisho-- kake ntabaiki Olaitoriani nkiturujat inono."
Matthew5:34 Kake aliki nanu ndai: Minturujishore tukul-- neme shumata-- amu ninye olorika lʼEngai;"
Matthew5:35 neme baiki enkop-- amu ninye eiteleiki Engai nkejek enyena; neme baiki Yerusalem-- amu ninye engang' olkarsis kitok."
Matthew5:36 Minturujishore baiki elukunya ino-- amu mindim aitaala olpapita o obo-- peiborru arashu eroku."
Matthew5:37 Njeaku rorei linyi: Ee-- ee; me-- me! Enalang' kulo-- nepukunye oltorrono."
Matthew5:38 Itoning'o-- aajo etejoki: Engong'u tʼengongʼu-- olalai tʼolalai!"
Matthew5:39 Kake aliki nanu ndai: Emigilunore entorroni! kake olikiosh eseder e tatene-- mbelekenyaki ninye en e are!"
Matthew5:40 Ore olikintang'or nikioru emekiti-- tung'aiki ninye baiki oliopore!"
Matthew5:41 Ore olikintanapaki pintare emaili nabo-- turubare too are!"
Matthew5:42 Olikiomonu-- njoo ninye! olikisilen-- minjo empiding'!"
Matthew5:43 Itoning'o-- aajo etejoki: Tonyorra ol elatia ino nimbai olmang'atinda lino!"
Matthew5:44 Kake aliki nanu ndai: Entonyor ilmang'ati linyi; entamayan loodek ndai; entobirakiti sidan looiba ndai; entasayakiti looitarriki neinyal ndai--"
Matthew5:45 peiye iakuku nkera e Minyi linyi otii shumata; amu eisho ninye-- peilepaki engolong' enye iltorrok o sidan-- neshaiki enjan enye loora supati o lemera supati."
Matthew5:46 Amu teni inyorrurru loonyor ndai — kalo kwaje itumutumu? Meiko neijia baiki laoshok le kodi?
Matthew5:47 Ore piborrurru too lalashera linyi ake — kaa ponata inkoko? Meiko neijia baiki lemeata Engai?
Matthew5:48 Onaa meata kata nimintabaiaia aten anaa peata Minyi linyi le shumata enkitabaiaroto.
Matthew6:1 Eng'orai-- piminjoioio nkishoorot inyi t'engomom oo ltung'anak-- peiye edol ninje ndai; amu teni inkoko neijia-- mitumutumu olkwaje te Minyi linyi otii shumata."
Matthew6:2 Akae-- teni injooio enkishooroto ino-- miosh esekegwa tʼengomom ino anaa peiko laitusupatuok tiatua ngajijik Engai o too ngoitoi-- peiye eitadaraa iltung'anak ninje. Japa-- aliki ndai: Eidipa aainoto ninje olkwaje lenye."
Matthew6:3 Kake teni injooio iye enkishooroto-- njoo meyolo engaina ino e kedyanye enaitobirita engaina ino e tatene--"
Matthew6:4 peshuma enkishooroto ino; nikirrinyoki Minyi lino lodolita nashuma-- tʼewuas."
Matthew6:5 Teni isaishosho-- eminyanyukie laitusupatuok-- amu enyor aatasaishoto eitashe tiatua ngajijik Engai o too rishat oo ngoitoi-- peiye eitadaraa iltung'anak ninje. Japa-- aliki ndai: Eidipa aainoto olkwaje lenye."
Matthew6:6 Kake teni isaisho iye-- tijing'a olgilata lino-- ngeno kutukaji ino-- pisai Minyi lino ishuma; nikirrinyoki Minyi lino lodolita nashuma-- tʼewuas."
Matthew6:7 Teni isaishosho-- emiyang'iyang' anaa iltungʼanak lemeata Engai; amu ejo ninje-- eningʼi-- tiaraki naa kumok rorei lenye."
Matthew6:8 Akae-- eminyanyukiei lelo! Eyolo Minyi linyi-- enimindimidimi aatalaita-- eton eitu iomonunu ninye."
Matthew6:9 Akae-- entasaishoto ndai nji: Papa lang' litii shumata-- njesinyari engarna ino!"
Matthew6:10 Njelotu enkarsishu ino! Njeaku eyeunoto ino tʼenkop anaa peaku te shumata!
Matthew6:11 Njoo yook taata endaa ang' nabaiki yook!
Matthew6:12 Tung'aiki yook silen inono-- anaa piking'uaiki si yook loo silen ang'!"
Matthew6:13 Mirik yook atua enkitasuroto-- kake ntopua yook tʼentorroni! Amu era enino enkarsishu o engolon o enkitook nkatan pookin. Amen."
Matthew6:14 Amu teni ing'uaikiki iltung'anak nkitarruot enye-- neing'uaiki baiki ndai Minyi linyi le shumata."
Matthew6:15 Kake teni ming'uaikiki iltung'anak nkitarruot enye-- nemeingʼuaiki baiki Minyi linyi ndai nkitarruot inyi."
Matthew6:16 Teni ipukooko-- eminyanyukiei laitusupatuok ooata nkirribon naasoto-- amu eitaal nkirribon enye-- pelioi too ltung'anak-- aajo etupukoitie. Japa-- aliki ndai: Eidipa aainoto ninje olkwaje lenye."
Matthew6:17 Kake teni ipukoo iye-- ielie eilata elukunya misuj engomom ino--"
Matthew6:18 pimilioi too ltung'anak itupukoiye-- kake te Minyi lino oshuma; nikirrinyoki Minyi lino odolita nashuma-- tʼewuas."
Matthew6:19 Eminturrurroki aten masaa tʼenkop-- peitarruo lai-ng'ur o endoran-- nejing'aki lapurrok nepurroo;"
Matthew6:20 kake enturrurroki aten masaa te shumata nemeitarruo laing'ur-- baiki endoran-- nemejing'aki lapurrok aapuroo."
Matthew6:21 Amu enetii masaa inono-- naa ine etii oltau lino."
Matthew6:22 Nera engongʼu enkilang'et osesen. Akae-- ten aa sidai engong'u ino-- neata osesen lino pookin enkilang'et;"
Matthew6:23 kake ten aa torrono engong'u ino-- neaku osesen lino pookin enaimin. Akae-- teni era enkilang'et natii atua iye enaimin — kaa aimin ina!"
Matthew6:24 Metii oltung'ani oidim aisyayaki laitoriak aare; amu elaibai obo nenyorru oliare-- arashu eibung' obo nemenu oliare."
Matthew6:25 Onaa aliki ndai: Emiekenyakino empuan inyi eninyanya o eniokioko-- baiki seseni linyi eninjopishopo. Melang' empuan endaa? nemelang' osesen olkila?"
Matthew6:26 Eng'orai ntaritik e shumata-- aajo meun nemeisambu nemeiturrur ninje too mbejen-- kake eitoti Minyi linyi le shumata ninje. Miororere ndai aalang' ninje?"
Matthew6:27 Kang'ai too ndai loidim ateekenyai-- pepon engadoro enye engaina nabo?"
Matthew6:28 Ainyo piekenyakinono ilkilani? Eng'orai ntapuka enkuruma eneiko teni ebulu: meitobir ninje enkyas nemeshetisho.
Matthew6:29 Aliki ndai-- ajo eitu eishopi baiki Salomo tʼenkitook enye pookin anaa nabo too nena."
Matthew6:30 Teni eishop Engai olkujita lʼenkuruma nji-- lotii taata nenang'akini taisere enkima — me naleng' eishop ndai-- ndai lʼenkirukoto kinyi?"
Matthew6:31 Akae-- emiekenya aajo: Ainyo kinya arashu ainyo kiok arashu ainyo kinjop?"
Matthew6:32 Eing'oru loreren lemeata Engai kuna pookin; amu eyolo Minyi linyi le shumata-- ajo mindimidimi aatalaita kuna pookin."
Matthew6:33 Entang'as eng'orutu enkarsishu Engai o esupato enye-- neponikini ndai kuna pookin."
Matthew6:34 Akae-- emiekenyakino entaisere-- amu eshilaa entaisere mbaak enyena. Ebaiki neata engolong' pookin entorroni enye."
Matthew7:1 Emingwenaki-- pemeigwenakini ndai."
Matthew7:2 Amu ore enkigwena ningwenunu-- ninye epuoi aaigwenakinye ndai; ore entemet nitemishorere-- ninye epuoi aatemakinye ndai."
Matthew7:3 Ainyo ping'oraa iye embajuai natii engong'u olalashe lino nimidol olmuambai otii engong'u ino?
Matthew7:4 Arashu kaji inko teni ijoki olalashe lino: Ntasho-- ayeu naaitaiki iye embajuai tʼengong'u ino-- — naa ng'orai-- etii olmuambai tʼengong'u ino?"
Matthew7:5 Iye laitusupatuoni-- tang'asa ntai olmuambai otii engong'u ino-- pitum atadua naleng' aitai embajuai tʼengong'u olalashe lino."
Matthew7:6 Eminjo ildiain naara sinyat-- niminang'akiki ilpusi linyi engomom oo lbitiro-- pemeroruaki enkop too nkejek enye-- nemeibelekenya aapolos ndai."
Matthew7:7 Entoomonutu-- neishori ndai; eng'orutu-- nitumutumu; entooshiosh-- nebolokini ndai."
Matthew7:8 Amu oloomonu-- neng'amu; oloing'oru-- netum; olooshiosh-- nebolokini."
Matthew7:9 Kalo tung'ani too ndai loata enkerai-- teni eomonu olmkate — keisho osoit?"
Matthew7:10 Arashu teni eomonu osingirri — keisho olasurai?
Matthew7:11 Akae-- teni iyololo ndai lirara torrok aaishoo nkera inyi nkishoorot sidan-- me naleng' eisho minyi linyi le shumata sidan loomonu ninye!"
Matthew7:12 Akae-- ore pookin niyeuu neitobiraki iltung'anak ndai-- nji entobirakiti si ndai ninje. Nera ina nkitanapat o layolounok."
Matthew7:13 Eima kishomi napirik-- amu elala kishomi naa dapash engoitoi naitahaia enkiminata-- naa kumok kulo looim ina."
Matthew7:14 Nepirik ake kishomi-- naa rongai engoitoi naitahaia empuan-- naa kuti kulo lootum ninye."
Matthew7:15 Entaduai aten too layolounok lʼelejare loopuonu enitiiti-- ooishopito ndapan oo nkerra-- kake ore tiatua naa suiyan malmalin."
Matthew7:16 Iyolouu ninje too lmomo lenye. Keisambuni lama too lbibia-- arashu ilng'abolo too ntulele?"
Matthew7:17 Neijia eiu oljani sidai ilmomo sidan-- neiu oljani torrono ilmomo torrok."
Matthew7:18 Meidim oljani sidai atoiu ilmomo torrok-- nemeidim atoiu oljani torrono ilmomo sidan."
Matthew7:19 Ore oljani lemeiu ilmomo sidan-- nedung'i nenang akini enkima."
Matthew7:20 Akae-- ipuopuo aayolou ninje too lmomo lenye."
Matthew7:21 Mejing' oltung'ani pookin laajoki: Laitoriani-- Laitoriani! enkarsishu e shumata-- kake ele ake loitobir enayeu Papa lai le shumata."
Matthew7:22 Kumok laapuo aajoki te ina olong': Laitoriani-- Laitoriani! eitu kintayolou mbaak e akenya tʼengarna ino? Eitu kimir ilmeneng'a Tengarna ino? Eitu kintobir nkitobirat engolon kumok tʼengarna ino?"
Matthew7:23 Te ine alaibalaki ninje: Eitu ayolou ndai tukul; entung'aiyoki-- ndai looitobir ntorrok."
Matthew7:24 Akae-- ore oltung'ani pookin loning' kulo rorei neitobir ninje-- naitanyanyukie ninye olee ng'en lotesheta engaji enye te shumata osoit."
Matthew7:25 Esha enjan nelotu engare kitok nekutishoi olkutati neipony ena aji nemeurori-- amu etii entonata enye atua osoit."
Matthew7:26 Ore oltung'ani pookin loning' kulo rorei nemeitobir-- naitanyanyukie ninye olee modai lotesheta engaji enye tiatua osunyai."
Matthew7:27 Nesha enjan nelotu engare kitok nekutishoi olkutati neipony ena aji-- neurori neaku kitok erratanyata enye."
Matthew7:28 Neaku ore peidip Yesus kulo rorei-- neiputukuny siamin tʼenkiteng'enare enye--"
Matthew7:29 amu eiteng'ena ninye anaa oloata engolon-- neme neijia anaa layolok lʼesirata."
Matthew8:1 Ore pedou tʼoldonyo-- nesuj isiamin kumok ninye."
Matthew8:2 Naa ng'orai-- nelotu oltung'ani obo loata enkea oo lbolot neserem ninye-- ejo: Laitoriani-- teni iyeu-- nikindim aisuja."
Matthew8:3 Neitorioo Yesus engaina enye neing'unye ninye nejo: Ayeu-- sujai! Neisujunye nabokata enkea enye oo lbolot."
Matthew8:4 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Ng'orai-- pimiliki oltung'ani-- kake nno-- pintadol kion olaidasani-- pinjooio enkishooroto naitanapua Mose-- peaku enjakenishu too ninje."
Matthew8:5 Ore pejing' Yesus Kapernaum-- nelotu olkigeluni obo loo lmurran enetii ninye nesai ninye:"
Matthew8:6 nejo: Laitoriani-- eirrag olaisyayani lai tiatua aji-- emoi osupetai nemeikini torrono naleng'."
Matthew8:7 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Alotu paishiunye ninye.
Matthew8:8 Nealiki olkigeluni loo lmurran ninye nejo: Laitoriani-- mara toki-- pijing' iye abori e keperaji ai-- kake tolimu ororei obo ake-- neishiu olaisyayani lai."
Matthew8:9 Amu ara si nanu oltung'ani otii abori enkitoria-- naata ilmurran tiabori ai. Teni ajoki obo: Nno! nelo; o olekai: Wou! nelotu; o olaisyayani lai: Ntobira ena! neitobir."
Matthew8:10 Ore pening' Yesus ena-- neiputukuny nejoki kulo lootusuja ninye: Japa-- aliki ndai-- eitu aikata adol tiatua Israel enkirukoto kitok anaa ena."
Matthew8:11 Kake aliki ndai: Kumok loopuonu eing'ua enkilepunoto o endoiyoroto engolong' netoni te nebo o Abraham o Isaak o Yakoob tʼenkarsishu e shumata--"
Matthew8:12 kake eiturrakini nkera enkarsishu atua enaimin e aulo; netii ina alo enkishirata o eonyoto oo lala.
Matthew8:13 Nejoki Yesus olkigeluni loo lmurran: Nno-- njeaku neijia anaa piruko! Neishiu olaisyayani lenye te ina kata ake."
Matthew8:14 Ore pelotu Yesus engaji e Petros-- nedol engaputani enye eirrag-- emoi oltikana."
Matthew8:15 Neibung' engaina enye neingʼuaiki oltikana ninye. Neinyototo neisyayaki ninye.
Matthew8:16 Ore peaku teipa-- nerikoki ninje ninye ilkumok looata ilmenengʼa-- nemir ilmeneng'a too rorei neishiunye loomoiyaa--"
Matthew8:17 peiye ebaia enairoro olayolounoni Yesaya-- ejo: Nedumaki ninye kion menatishuitin ang'-- nenap nkeaitin ang."
Matthew8:18 Ore pedol Yesus siamin kumok emanita ninye-- neitanapu-- pelangʼaa aabaiki lido kekun."
Matthew8:19 Nelotu olayoloni obo lʼesirata nejoki ninye: Laiteng'enani-- ayeu naasuj iye tʼewueji pookin nilo."
Matthew8:20 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Eata ntirrashin ngumot neata ntaritik singin-- kake meata Enkerai oltung'ani eneiteleiki elukunya enye."
Matthew8:21 Nejoki olekai tiatua laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye: Laitoriani-- njooki-- pang'as alanuk papa lai."
Matthew8:22 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Tusujaki iye-- tapala lootuata metunuka lootuata lenye."
Matthew8:23 Neilepaki ninye engalawa nesuj laitengʼenuok lenyena ninye.
Matthew8:24 Naa ng'orai-- nejing' enkiposhiposhata kitok atua olbalbal neopoo lopir lʼengare engalawa; neirura ninye."
Matthew8:25 Nepuonu laitengʼenuok lenyena enetii ninye neinyeye ninye nejo: Laitoriani-- ntopua yook-- kimin!"
Matthew8:26 Nejoki ninje: Ainyo pirara kureti-- ndai lʼenkirukoto kinyi? Neinyototo nebuaki olkutati o olbalbal; neaku olgira kitok."
Matthew8:27 Neiputukuny ake iltung'anak nejo: Kalo tung'ani ele loning' olkutati o olbalbal ninye?
Matthew8:28 Ore pebaiki ninye lido kekun atua olosho loo Lgadarenoi-- netumore ninye iltung'anak aare looata ilmeneng'a eing'ua nkuraren-- malmalin naleng'-- neitu eiteu oltung'ani aima baiki ena oitoi."
Matthew8:29 Naa ng'orai-- nedar tʼoltoilo nejo: Ainyo kiataiye yook iye-- Yesus-- Oinoti lʼEngai? Amaa-- iewuo ene-- pintame yook-- eitu ebau enkata?"
Matthew8:30 Netii enelakwaniki ninje emboo oo lbitiro looirrititai.
Matthew8:31 Nesai ilmeneng'a ninye nejo: Teni imir yook-- njoo yook-- pikijing' atua emboo oo lbitiro."
Matthew8:32 Nejoki ninje: Enjom! Nepuku nejing' atua ilbitiro. Naa ng'orai-- nesulakino emboo pookin aasioki tʼemarti atua olbalbal nee tʼengare."
Matthew8:33 Nekwet lairritak nepuo engang' neinosu mbaak pookin naataa o mbaak oo kulo looata ilmeneng'a.
Matthew8:34 Naa ng'orai-- nepuku engang' pookin alanang'are Yesus. Ore pedol ninye-- nesai-- pepuku too mbatai enye."
Matthew9:1 Neilepaki ninye engalawa nelang' nebaia engang' enye.
Matthew9:2 Naa ng'orai-- nerikoki ninje oltamoiyai lʼosupetai oirragieki tʼerruat. Ore pedol Yesus enkirukoto enye-- nejoki ele tamoiyai lʼosupetai: Ntagoluoi tʼoltau-- nakerai ai-- kintaikiaki nkitarruot inono."
Matthew9:3 Naa ng'orai-- nejo ematua oo layolok lʼesirata tiatua aten: Emor ele Engai."
Matthew9:4 Ore peyolou Yesus nkibirribirrat enye-- nejo: Kaji etiu-- pimbirribirrirri ntorrok too ltauja linyi?"
Matthew9:5 Kaa nalelek; teni ajo: Kintaikiaki nkitarruot inono-- arashu: Nyototoi-- tilimanai?"
Matthew9:6 Kake piyolouu-- aajo eata Enkerai oltung'ani engolon naitaunye nkitarruot tʼenkop-- nejoki ele tamoiyai lʼosupetai: Nyototoi-- tudumu erruat ino-- nno ang'!"
Matthew9:7 Neinyototo nelo ang'.
Matthew9:8 Ore pedol isiamin ena-- neiputukuny neitadaraa Engai naishoo iltung'anak engolon naba nji."
Matthew9:9 Ore peing'ua Yesus ina alo-- nedol oltung'ani eton tʼeneitainyeki kodi-- oji engarna enye Matayos-- nejoki ninye; Tusujaki! Neinyototo nesuj ninye."
Matthew9:10 Neaku-- ore peton ninye tʼengaji-- pedaa-- naa ng'orai-- nepuonu laoshok le kodi kumok o laitarruok-- netoni te nebo o Yesus o laiteng'enuok lenyena."
Matthew9:11 Ore pedol Ilfarisayoi ina-- nejoki ninje laiteng'enuok lenyena: Ainyo pedaa olaiteng'enani linyi te nebo o laoshok le kodi o laitarruok?"
Matthew9:12 Ore pening' Yesus ina-- nejoki ninje: Meyeu loora biot olaishiunoni-- kake loomoiyaa."
Matthew9:13 Embung'a engoitoi ake-- enteng'enuoto enkitaalata oo kulo rorei: Anyor eng'adunoto neme enkidasare. Eitu alotu nanu-- paipot supati-- kake laitarruok-- petum aataalata."
Matthew9:14 Nepuonu te ina kata laiteng'enuok le Yohanes enetii ninye nejo: Ainyo pikipukoo yook o Ilfarisayoi aigil kumok nemepukoo laiteng'enuok linono?
Matthew9:15 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Keidim iltung'anak lʼengiama aaishira-- epon eboitare ninje osanja? Kake epuonu ngolong'i neoruni ninje osanja-- nepukoo te ina kata."
Matthew9:16 Metii oltung'ani opik erashet olkila ng'ejuk atua olkila musana; amu epolos ena rashet olkila neaku empolosata torrono naleng'.
Matthew9:17 Nemepiki olmarua ng'ejuk atua ilbenia musan; teni epiki-- nepolosa ilbenia neibukori olmarua-- nerruoio ilbenia. Kake epiki olmarua ng'ejuk atua ilbenia ng'ejuko-- nepoku pokira are."
Matthew9:18 Ore epon eliki ninje kuna-- ng'orai-- nelotu olkitok obo negilaki ninye kung' nejo: Etua entito ai taata nji-- kake wou-- pinteleiki engaina ino-- pepiu."
Matthew9:19 Nedumunye Yesus nesuj ninye te nebo o laiteng'enuok lenyena.
Matthew9:20 Naa ng'orai-- nelotu tekurum enye eng'oroyoni nabo naata empukunoto osarge enkata oo larin tomon o are-- neporoo enaipukoi olkila lenye;"
Matthew9:21 amu etejo tʼoltau lenye: Teni aporoo ake enaipukoi olkila lenye-- naishiu."
Matthew9:22 Neibelekenya Yesus nedol ninye nejoki: Ntagoluoi tʼoltau-- entito ai-- enkirukoto ino nikintopua. Neishiu ena ng'oroyoni eiter te ina kata."
Matthew9:23 Ore pebaia Yesus engaji olkitok nedol lakutak loo nkisuleta o enkiposhiposharoto olorere--"
Matthew9:24 nejoki ninje: Ewuang'a! amu eitu ee entito-- eirura. Nekweniye ninye."
Matthew9:25 Ore peitupukuni olorere-- nejing'aki neibung' engaina enye-- neinyototo entito."
Matthew9:26 Neibulaa kuna baak atua ilo osho pookin.
Matthew9:27 Ore peing'ua Yesus te ina alo-- nesuj ninye ilmodook aare-- edarita nejo: Tokordu yook-- nakerai e David!"
Matthew9:28 Ore pebaia ang' nepuonu ilmodook enetii ninye. Nejoki Yesus ninje: Irukuruku-- aajo aidim aitobira kuna? Nejoki ninje: Ee-- Laitoriani!"
Matthew9:29 Neporoo ninye ngonyek enye nejo: Njeaku neijia anaa piruko.
Matthew9:30 Nebolo ngonyek enye. Neiture Yesus ninje nejo: Eng'orai-- pemeyolou oltung'ani o obo."
Matthew9:31 Kake nepuku neibulunye ninye atua ilo osho pookin.
Matthew9:32 Ore pepuku lelo-- nerikokini ninye oltung'ani lemeidim airoro neata ilmeneng'a."
Matthew9:33 Ore pemiri olmeneng'ani-- neiro leitu eidim airoro. Neiputukuny isiamin nejo: Eitu edoli tʼewueji o nabo tiatua Israel nji."
Matthew9:34 Nejo ake Ilfarisayoi: Emir ninye ilmeneng'a tʼolkitok loo lmeneng'a.
Matthew9:35 Nemanaa Yesus tiatua ngang'itie kituak o kutiti neiteng'enisho tiatua ngajijik Engai enye neinosu lomon lʼeng'ida lʼenkarsishu neishiunye nkeaitin pookin o menatishuitin pookin tʼempolos olorere.
Matthew9:36 Ore pedol ninye siamin-- neibung'aki ninje engoshoke nanana-- amu etanaurate neisardaka anaa ntare nemeata oljokut."
Matthew9:37 Nejoki ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena: Kitok enkisambuare naa kuti laitobirak;
Matthew9:38 akae-- entasai Olaitoriani lʼenkisambuare-- peirriwaa laitobirak atua enkisambuare enye."
Matthew10:1 Neipot ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena tomon o are neisho ninje engolon too lmumuan ooiduruk-- pemir ninje neishiunye nkeaitin pookin o menatishuitin pookin."
Matthew10:2 Ore ngam oo lairriwak tomon o are ninje kuna: ol elukunya Simon oipotoki Petros-- o Andreas-- olalashe lenye; Yakobos le Sebedayos o Yohanes-- olalashe lenye;"
Matthew10:3 Filipos o Bartolomayos; Tomas o Matayos-- olaoshoni le kodi; Yakobos le Alfayos; Lebayos oipotoki Tadayos:"
Matthew10:4 Simon Olkananayos o Yudas Iskariotes oitarasaiye ninye.
Matthew10:5 Neirriwaa Yesus kulo tomon o are neitanap ninje nejo: Emiim ngoitoi oo loreren lemeata Engai-- emijing' atua ngang'itie oo Samareites--"
Matthew10:6 kake enaikash enjom enetii nkerra naaimina engaji Israel.
Matthew10:7 Enjom ake-- enosai-- entejo: Etinyikua enkarsishu e shumata!"
Matthew10:8 Enjiunye loomoiyaa-- esuja looata enkea oo lbolot-- entopiu lootuata entimir ilmeneng'a. Inoto pesho-- enjooi pesho!"
Matthew10:9 Eminap esahabu-- baiki ngoshola-- baiki mpesai tiatua nkimeitan inyi--"
Matthew10:10 arashu olbene lʼolototo arashu ilkilani aare arashu namuka arashu olartat; amu eaku-- petum olaitobirani loo nkyasin endaa enye."
Matthew10:11 Ore engang' pookin-- kitok arashu enkiti-- nijing'ijing'i-- eng'orutu oltung'ani Ioaku; entobik te nebo o ninye metabana nipukuku."
Matthew10:12 Teni ijing'ijing'i engaji-- erorokiti ninye;"
Matthew10:13 teni eaku ena aji-- nejing'aki eseriani inyi atua ninye; teni meaku-- nerrinyokino ndai eseriani inyi."
Matthew10:14 Teni meitoomon oltung'ani ndai nemening' rorei linyi-- entupukutu te ina aji o te ina ang'-- empiripiroi enterit oo nkejek inyi."
Matthew10:15 Japa-- aliki ndai; Eikashieki Sodom o Gomora tʼengolong' enkigwena e akenya nelang' ina ang'."
Matthew10:16 Eng'orai-- airriwaa nanu ndai anaa nkerra atua suiyan; onaa enteng'enuoto anaa lasuria nimiatata olosek anaa ilmaita."
Matthew10:17 Entaduai aten tiatua iltung'anak! Amu epuo aaitarasaki ndai atua nkigwenaitin enye nepuo aar ndai tiatua ngajijik Engai enye;
Matthew10:18 neriki ndai ngomomi oo laiturukok o noo lkarsisi tʼolbae lai-- peaku enjakenishu too ninje o too loreren lemeata Engai."
Matthew10:19 Kake teni eitarasaa ninje ndai-- eming'ayung'ayu aajo kainyo kilimu-- amu eishori ndai te ina kata ake enilimumu;"
Matthew10:20 amu me ndai ooiro-- kake Olmumua le Minyi linyi oiro tiatua ndai."
Matthew10:21 Neitarasaa olalashe olalashe lenye-- petum atua-- o menye enkerai enye-- nedumakino nkera lootoiutuo ninje-- neisho metaari metuata."
Matthew10:22 Neibai ndai iltung'anak pookin tʼolbae Tengarna ai; kake olong'iri metabaiki enkiting'oto-- ninye olapok."
Matthew10:23 Teni einyal ninje ndai tiatua engang' nabo-- enkwetikiti engai. Japa-- aliki ndai: Mipuopuo aaidip ngang'itie pookin e Israel-- metabana nelotu Enkerai oltung'ani."
Matthew10:24 Melang' olaiteng'enuoni olaiteng'enani lenye o olaisyayani olaitoriani lenye.
Matthew10:25 Ebaiki olaiteng'enuoni peaku anaa olaiteng'enani-- o olaisyayani anaa olaitoriani. Teni eipoto ninje olopeny engaji Beelsebul-- me naleng' eipot neijia kulo loora lʼengaji enye!"
Matthew10:26 Akae-- emiurei ninje! Metii embae naisudori nemelo abolunye tekurum-- nemetii entoki emikio nemeyolouni."
Matthew10:27 Enaliki ndai tʼenaimin-- entolimutu tiatua enkilang'et; ore enining'ining'i tʼenking'oming'om-- enosutu too nkeperi oo ngajijik."
Matthew10:28 Emiurei looar osesen metua nemeidim aataar olmumua metua; sidai-- teni iureii ele loata engolon naiminye osesen o olmumua te gehena enkima."
Matthew10:29 Meinyang'uni nkipaikut are tʼempesai nabo? Kake medoiki o nabo too ninje enkop nemeyolo Minyi linyi.
Matthew10:30 Eikenaki baiki ilpapit linyi pookin lʼelukunya.
Matthew10:31 Akae-- emiurei! Irara ndai sidan nilang'ilang'a nkipaikut kumok."
Matthew10:32 Olaaibalu nanu tʼengomom oo ltung'anak-- naibalu si nanu ninye tʼengomom e Papa lai le shumata;"
Matthew10:33 olaamiki nanu tʼengomom oo ltung'anak-- nayeu namiki si nanu ninye tʼengomom e Papa lai le shumata."
Matthew10:34 Emijo-- aajo aewuo nanu-- paau eseriani; me-- eitu alotu-- paau eseriani-- kake olalem."
Matthew10:35 Amu aewuo nanu-- pairriki oltung'ani o menye lenye-- entito o ng'otonye enye-- esyayunoti o engaputani enye;"
Matthew10:36 neaku ilmang'ati lʼoltung'ani kulo lootii engaji enye.
Matthew10:37 Olonyor menye arashu ng'otonye naalang' nanu-- nemeaku olalai; olonyor olaiyoni lenye arashu entito enye naalang' nanu-- nemeaku olalai."
Matthew10:38 Olemedumu esalaba enye-- paasuj tekurum ai-- nemeaku olalai."
Matthew10:39 Oloyeu netum empuan enye-- nelaiminye ninye; ore oloiminye empuan enye tʼolbae lai-- nelatum ninye."
Matthew10:40 Oloitoomon ndai-- naaitoomon nanu; olaaitoomon nanu-- neitoomon olaairriua."
Matthew10:41 Oloitoomon olayolounoni tʼengarna olayolounoni-- nelang'amu olkwaje l'olayolounoni; oloitoomon osupat tʼengarna osupat-- nelang'amu olkwaje lʼosupat."
Matthew10:42 Oloitook obo too kulo kunyinyi tʼeoket engare nairobi ake tʼengarna olaiteng'enuoni-- japa-- aliki ndai-- melau ninye tukul olkwaje lenye."
Matthew11:1 Ore peidip Yesus aitanapa laiteng'enuok lenyena tomon o are-- nepuku te ina alo neiteng'enisho neinosu lomon lʼEngai tiatua ngang'itie enye."
Matthew11:2 Ore pening' Yohanes tiatua engaji eenata nkitobirat e Kristos-- neirriwaa laiteng'enuok lenyena aare--"
Matthew11:3 pejoki ninye: Ira iye ololotu arashu kianyu olekai?
Matthew11:4 Nealiki Yesus nejoki ninje: Embung'a engoitoi-- enosakiti Yohanes nining'itoto o nidolitata:"
Matthew11:5 edolisho ilmodook-- nelimana lemeidim aashom-- neisuja looata enkea oo lbolot-- nening'isho ilming'an-- neitopiuni lootuata-- neinosakini laisinak lomon lʼeng'ida;"
Matthew11:6 naa tesh oltung'ani lamaarikare nanu.
Matthew11:7 Ore peing'ua ninje ninye-- neiter Yesus aliki siamin mbaak e Yohanes: Kainyo ishomo ndai aaing'oraa ti ang'ata? Itayeutuo nidolidolo olperesi ong'uyanita olkutati?"
Matthew11:8 Arashu ainyo ishomo aadol? Itayeutuo nidolidolo oltung'ani oishopito ilkilani oopuyapui? Eng'orai-- etii iltung'anak ooishopito ilkilani oopuyapui atua ngajijik oo lkarsisi."
Matthew11:9 Arashu ainyo ishomo aadol? Itayeutuo nidolidolo olayolounoni? Ee-- aliki ndai ololang' olayolounoni."
Matthew11:10 Amu ilo ninye etisiraki: Ng'orai-- airriwaa olmalaika lai lukunya engomom ino-- olikintobiraki engoitoi tʼengomom ino."
Matthew11:11 Japa-- aliki ndai: Metii tukul atua kulo ootoiwuoki too ng'oroyok olkitok lolang' Yohanes Olaibatisani; kake olora kiti tukul tiatua enkarsishu e shumata-- naa kitok nelang' ninye."
Matthew11:12 Ore eiter too ngolong'i e Yohanes Olaibatisani metabaiki taata etumi enkarsishu e shumata t'engolon-- nearu kulo looibung' ninye tʼengolon."
Matthew11:13 Amu eitayoloutuo layolounok pookin o nkitanapat metabaiki Yohanes mbaak naaku.
Matthew11:14 Naa teni iyeuu nirukuruku-- ninye lora Eliya olalotu."
Matthew11:15 Ore oloata nkiyaa naaning'ie-- njening'!"
Matthew11:16 Kainyo aitanyanyukie ena kishon? Enyanyukie ninye nkera naatoni tʼosingira neipot nʼemboitei enye
Matthew11:17 nejo: Kitooshokitio ndai nkisuleta-- neitu iyeuu ninguranana; kinjirakitia ndai-- neitu iyeuu nintong'ung'u ilkiyo."
Matthew11:18 Eewuo Yohanes-- neitu enya-- neitu eok; nejo ninje: eata olmeneng'ani."
Matthew11:19 Eewuo Enkerai oltung'ani-- nenya-- neok; nejo ninje: Eng'orai-- era ele tung'ani olainosani o olaokoni lʼolmarua-- oljore loo laoshok le kodi o loo laitarruok! Meata kata nemeitaai supat eng'eno too nkera enyena."
Matthew11:20 Neiter ailepilepaki ngang'itie enetaa nkitobirat enyena kumok-- tiaraki neitu eala:"
Matthew11:21 Ee kake aiya-- Korasin! Ee kake aiya-- Betsaida! Ten emutu etaa nena kitobirat te Tiros o te Sidon naataa too ndai-- anaata etaalate opa tiatua ilguniani o nkuruon."
Matthew11:22 Kake aliki ndai: Eikashieki Tiros o Sidon tʼengolong' enkigwena nelang' ndai.
Matthew11:23 Ore iye-- Kapernaum-- nikintadaraiyoki metabaiki shumata-- kipuo aaitadou metabaiki abori enkop: amu ten emutu etaa nkitobirat engolon naataa te iye-- te Sodom-- anaata etii metabaiki taata."
Matthew11:24 Kake aliki nanu ndai: Eikashieki olosho le Sodom tʼengolong' enkigwena e akenya nikilang' iye.
Matthew11:25 Nealu te ina kata Yesus nejo: Aaitoning'oo iye-- Papa o Olaitoriani le shumata o enkop-- tiaraki nitushumaka kuna lang'eni o iljartani-- nintayolo ilkutiti."
Matthew11:26 Ee-- Papa-- amu neijia itonyorrua tʼengomom ino."
Matthew11:27 Aaitarasaka Papa lai ntokitin pookin-- nemetii oloyolo Oinoti neme Menye-- nemetii oloyolo Menye neme Oinoti o oloyeu neitayolo Oinoti ninye."
Matthew11:28 Ewotu enatii nanu pookin lootanaurate neiroshiki rridat-- nayeu naeng'ieng'ie nanu ndai."
Matthew11:29 Entudumakiti aten enkiroshi ai-- enteng'enuoto te nanu; amu abor nanu naitadou kion tʼoltau-- nipuopuo aatum eng'ieng'are oo lmumuan linyi;"
Matthew11:30 amu eneneng' enkiroshi ai nelelek orridati lai.
Matthew12:1 Neim Yesus te ina kata tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki atua nkuruman; neata laiteng'enuok lenyena olamei neiter aadung' lukuny entapa nenya.
Matthew12:2 Ore pedol Ilfarisayoi nona-- nejoki ninye: Ng'orai-- eitobirita laiteng'enuok linono nemeaku tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki."
Matthew12:3 Nejoki ninye ninje: Eitu isomama enaitobira David-- eata olamei o lʼemboitei enye?"
Matthew12:4 Eneikuna nejing' engaji Engai nenya ilmkaten lʼenkitaduaroto-- nemeaku te ninye-- penya o lʼemboitei enye-- neme laidasak oopeny ake."
Matthew12:5 Arashu eitu isomama tiatua nkitanapat-- ajo eitaa laidasak engolong' naeng'ieng'areki torrono tʼengaji sinyati tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki-- neitu eitarruo?"
Matthew12:6 Kake aliki nanu ndai-- ajo etii ene olora kitok nelang' engaji sinyati."
Matthew12:7 Ten emutu iyololo enkitaalata oo kulo rorei: Anyor enkordunoto neme enkidasare-- — anaata eitu idekideke kulo leitu eitarruo."
Matthew12:8 Amu era Enkerai oltung'ani baiki Olaitoriani lʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki.
Matthew12:9 Nepuku te ina alo nejing' atua engaji Engai enye.
Matthew12:10 Naa ng'orai-- etii oltung'ani oikang'a engaina. Neikilikwan ninje ninye nejo: Keaku-- teni eishiunyeki tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki? Petum enaitang'orie."
Matthew12:11 Nejoki ninje: Kalo obo too ndai loata enker nabo nadoiki atua engumoto tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki nemeibung' ninye ailepunye?
Matthew12:12 Amaa-- melang' naleng' oltung'ani enker? Onaa-- eaku-- teni eitobiri sidan tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki."
Matthew12:13 Nejoki ninye ele tung'ani: Ntorioi engaina ino! Neitorioo ninye neishiu-- neaku bioto anaa engai aina."
Matthew12:14 Neipung' Ilfarisayoi neigwenare ninye-- petum aaiminye."
Matthew12:15 Ore peyolou Yesus kuna-- neing'ua ina alo. Nesuj isiamin kumok ninye-- neishiunye ninje pookin--"
Matthew12:16 neitanap ninje naleng'-- pemelimu ninye--"
Matthew12:17 pebaia enairoro aloyolounoni Yesaya nejo:
Matthew12:18 Ng'orai-- era ele olaisyayani lai lategelua-- olanyor lai-- oshipakino oltau lai; ayeu naisho ninye Olmumua lai-- neinosaki ninye loreren enkigwena."
Matthew12:19 Meitarrikisho ninye nemedar nemening'i oltoilo lenye too ngoitoi;
Matthew12:20 nemegil ninye olperesi otororoki-- nemear enkishinga nailiilaa-- pee-- metabana neitupuku enkigwena enye-- peaku engilunoto;"
Matthew12:21 neng'idare loreren engarna enye.
Matthew12:22 Nerikoki ninye oloata ilmeneng'a-- ora olmodooni nemeidim airoro; neishiunye ninye-- neidim ele leitu eiro-- airoro nedolishoi."
Matthew12:23 Neing'asia pookin nejo: Mera ele enkerai e David?
Matthew12:24 Kake ore pening' Ilfarisayoi kuna-- nejo: Memir ele ilmeneng'a neme tʼengolon e Beelsebul-- ora olkitok loo lmeneng'a."
Matthew12:25 Ore peyolou Yesus ndamunot enye-- nejoki ninje: Teni eitarrikino enkarsishu tiatua kion-- neimin; Teni eitarrikino engang' arashu engaji tiatua kion-- nemebik."
Matthew12:26 Teni emir satan obo olekai-- neitarrikinore tiatua kion; kaji eiko teni elabik enkarsishu enye?"
Matthew12:27 Teni amir si nanu ilmeneng'a tʼengolon e Beelsebul — ke tʼengolon e ng'ai emir nkera inyi ninje. Onaa eaku ninje laigwenak linyi.
Matthew12:28 Kake teni amir nanu ilmeneng'a tʼengolon Olmumua lʼEngai-- eewuo enkarsishu Engai enitiiti."
Matthew12:29 Arashu kaji eiko teni eidim atijing'a oltung'ani engaji oloata engolon nearaa masaa engaji enye-- nemeng'as aen oloata engolon-- petum ataarai engaji enye?"
Matthew12:30 Ore oltung'ani lemera lʼematua ai-- nera olmang'atinda lai; olemeiturrur te nebo o nanu-- neisardakie."
Matthew12:31 Onaa aliki ndai: Eing'uaikini iltung'anak nkitarruot o emoroto pookin-- kake meing'uaikini iltung'anak loomor Olmumua."
Matthew12:32 Ore oloimakinye ororei Enkerai oltung'ani-- neinguaikini ninye; kake oloimakinye Olmumua Sinyati-- meing'uaikini ninye; tiatua ele maa le taata-- baiki tiatua lido olotu akenya."
Matthew12:33 Arashu entuun oljani sidai-- neaku ilmomo sidan; arashu entuun oljani torrono-- neaku ilmomo torrok. Amu too lmomo eyolouni oljani."
Matthew12:34 Ndai eishoi oo lasuria-- kaji inkoko teni iroro sidan-- irara torrok? Ore enatii atua oltau-- neiro enkutuk."
Matthew12:35 Eiu oltung'ani sidai sidan too masaa sidan oltau lenye; neiu oltung'ani torrono ntorrok too masaa torrok enyena.
Matthew12:36 Aliki nanu ndai ake-- ajo meata kata nemeisho iltung'anak alat enye tiatua enkigwena e akenya tʼolbae lʼororei pookin le pesho looiroro ninje."
Matthew12:37 Kinjori esupato too rorei linono-- nikipuoi aadek too rorei linono."
Matthew12:38 Nealiki ematua oo layolok lʼesirata o en oo Lfarisoyoi ninye nejo: Laiteng'enani-- kitayeutuo nikidol olponoto te iye."
Matthew12:39 Nealiki nejoki ninje: Eing'oru ena kishon torrono naar osotua l'enkiama olponoto-- nemeishori ninye olponoto neme olponoto lʼolayolounoni Yona."
Matthew12:40 Amu neijia anaa petobiko Yona ngolong'i uni-- dama o kiarie-- tiatua engoshoke osingirri-- neijia elabik Enkerai oltung'ani ngolong'i uni-- dama o kiarie-- tiatua oltau lʼenkop."
Matthew12:41 Nepuo aaitashe iltung'anak le Ninive tʼenkigwena e akenya te nebo o iltung'anak lʼena kishon-- nepuo aadek ninye; amu etaalate tʼenkinosunoto e Yona; eng'orai-- etii ene ololang' Yona."
Matthew12:42 Nelaitashe enkarsis eunore engolong' tʼenkigwena e akenya te nebo o iltung'anak lʼena kishon-- neladek ninye; amu eewuo ninye eing'ua nkiting'ot enkop-- peinining' eng'eno e Salomo; engorai-- etii ene ololang' Salomo."
Matthew12:43 Teni eidip atupuku olmeneng'ani duruki tiatua oltung'ani-- neim atua wuejitin engaroni-- neing'oru eneeng'ieng'are-- nelau."
Matthew12:44 Nejo tekurum: Arrinyokino engaji ai natung'aiye; ore pelotu-- neinepu erok neoro nekaji."
Matthew12:45 Nelo nabokata ninye neriku te nebo o ninye kulekai meneng'a oopishana-- torrok nelang' ninye; ore pejing'-- nebik tiatua; neaku tʼenkiting'oto mbaak ele tung'ani torrok nelang' nʼenkata elukunya. Neijia elaaku tʼena kishon torrono."
Matthew12:46 Ore epon eirorita o siamin-- ng'orai-- neitashe te boo ng'otonye o lalashera lenyena neyeu neirorie ninye."
Matthew12:47 Nejoki oltung'ani obo ninye: Ng'orai-- eitashe ng'utunyi o lalashera linono te boo neyeu nikirorie."
Matthew12:48 Nealiki nejoki olojoki ninye: Kang'ai yeiyo ai o kang'ai lalashera lainei?
Matthew12:49 Neitorioki engaina shumata oo laiteng'enuok lenyena nejo: Eng'orai yeiyo ai o lalashera lainei!
Matthew12:50 Amu oloitobir enayeu Papa lai le shumata-- nera ninye olalashe lai o enganashe o yeiyo."
Matthew13:1 Nepuku Yesus te ina olong' neing'ua ang' nelo aton tʼembata olbalbal.
Matthew13:2 Neiturrurrokino ninye siamin kumok neilepaki engalawa neton-- neitashe siamin pookin tʼembata olbalbal."
Matthew13:3 Neirorie ninje too nkitanyanyukieta kumok nejo: Eng'orai-- etupukuo olaisuaroni-- pelaisuaisho."
Matthew13:4 Ore peisuaia-- nedoiki ematua embeu engoitoi; nepuonu ntaritik nenya ina."
Matthew13:5 Nedoiki engai matua enetii soito nemetum nkulupuok kumok; nebulu nabokata-- tiaraki neitu etum nkulupuok naasur."
Matthew13:6 Ore peilepu engolong'-- neinaaia-- netoi-- tiaraki nemeata ntonat."
Matthew13:7 Neitoki adoiki engai matua atua ilkikarreta; nebulu ilkikarreta-- negor ina."
Matthew13:8 Neitoki adoiki engai matua enetii nkulupuok sidan-- neiu ilmomo-- ematua iip-- ematua ntomoni ile-- ematua osom."
Matthew13:9 Oloata nkiyaa naaning'ie-- njening'."
Matthew13:10 Nepuonu laiteng'enuok nejoki ninye: Ainyo pirorie ninje too nkitanyanyukieta?
Matthew13:11 Nealiki nejoki ninje: Eitumunyanaki ndai-- piyolouu njumat enkarsishu e shumata-- kake meitumunyani lelo."
Matthew13:12 Amu ore oloata-- neishori ninye aaiganyaki; ore olemeata-- neoruni baiki ena naata."
Matthew13:13 Onaa airorie ninje too nkitanyanyukieta; amu eing'orisho — nemedol; neinining'isho — nemening'-- nemeyolou kuna."
Matthew13:14 Nebaia too lelo enkitayolounoto e Yesaya najo: „Ore ening'oto ipuopuo aaning'-- nimiyolouu; ore enking'oraroto ipuopuo aaing'oraa-- nimidolidolo."
Matthew13:15 Amu epising'a iltauja lʼele orere-- neiroshieki nkiyaa enye tʼening'oto-- neiturukuny ngonyek enye-- pemedol too ngonyek-- nemening' too nkiyaa-- nemeyolou too ltauja-- nemeibelekenya-- paitopok ninje.“"
Matthew13:16 Kake teshi ngonyek inyi-- amu edolita-- o nkiyaa inyi-- amu ening'ito."
Matthew13:17 Amu-- japa-- aliki ndai: Etayeutuo layolounok kumok o loora supati nedol nidolitata ndai-- neitu edol-- neyeu nening' nining'itoto-- neitu ening'."
Matthew13:18 Akae-- entoning' ndai enkitanyanyukiet olaisuaroni."
Matthew13:19 Ore oltung'ani pookin loning' ororei lʼenkarsishu nemeyolou-- nelotu oltorrono neoru enaisuakaki atua oltau lenye; ninye enaisuakaki engoitoi."
Matthew13:20 Ore enaisuakaki enetii soito-- nera ninye oloning' ororei neng'amu nabokata tʼeng'ida."
Matthew13:21 Kake meata ntonat tiatua ninye-- nebik enkiti kata; ore pebau enkilishoto o enkinyala tʼolbae le ilo rorei-- nerikai nabokata."
Matthew13:22 Ore enaisuakaki atua ilkikarreta-- nera ninye oloning' ororei-- negor enkishilaroto ele maa o elejata oo masaa ororei-- neaku meiu ilmomo."
Matthew13:23 Ore enaisuakaki atua enkulupuoni sidai-- nera ninye oloning' ororei neyolou ninye neiu baiki ilmomo-- ematua iip-- ematua ntomoni ile-- ematua osom."
Matthew13:24 Neitoki aliki ninje engai kitanyanyukiet nejo: Enyanyukie enkarsishu e shumata oltung'ani oisuaka embeu sidai atua enkuruma enye.
Matthew13:25 Ore peirura iltung'anak-- nelotu olmang'atinda lenye neisuaki olmasinde empolos engano nelo ninye."
Matthew13:26 Ore pebulu engano neisho-- nelioi olmasinde."
Matthew13:27 Nepuonu laisyayak lʼolopeny enkuruma nejoki: Laitoriani-- eitu isuaki embeu sidai atua enkuruma ino? Akae-- kaji einotie olmasinde?"
Matthew13:28 Nejoki ninye ninje: Olmang'atinda lai oikuna nji. Nejoki laisyayak ninye: Akae-- iyeu nikipuo aadotoki enkop?"
Matthew13:29 Nejoki: Me! pemidotutu engano te nebo o olmasinde.
Matthew13:30 Enjoo pebulu pokira are metabaiki endung'ore; ore tʼenkata endung'ore naliki ladung'ok: Enturrurro aang'as olmasinde nieniene rridat-- pepeji ninye; kake enturrurrokiti engano atua embeje ai."
Matthew13:31 Neitoki aliki ninje engai kitanyanyukiet nejo: Enyanyukie enkarsishu e shumata embeu e karadali naibun'ga oltung'ani obo neisuaki atua enkuruma enye--"
Matthew13:32 nera kinyi nelang' mbeun pookin; kake ore pebulu-- neaku kitok nelang' mbenek pookin-- neaku enjani-- nepuonu ntaritik e shumata neshet singin tiatua ilng'osil lenyena."
Matthew13:33 Neliki ninje engai kitanyanyukiet: Enyanyukie en-karsishu e shumata enkisiijoi naibung'a eng'oroyoni nabo neitushulie ntemeta uni entapa-- metabana neisiijoi pookin."
Matthew13:34 Etiaka Yesus kuna pookin isiamin too nkitanyanyukieta-- neitu eliki ninje ororei neme too nkitanyanyukieta ake--"
Matthew13:35 pebaia enairoro olayolounoni ejo: Abol enkutuk ai too nkitanyanyukieta nayeu nalimu njumat tʼenkiterata enkop.
Matthew13:36 Ore peidip Yesus aitanapare siamin-- nelo aji. Nepuonu laiteng'enuok enetii ninye nejo: Ntaaliki yook enkitanyanyukiet olmasinde lʼenkuruma."
Matthew13:37 Nealu nejo: Era Enkerai oltung'ani oloisuaia embeu sidai.
Matthew13:38 Nera olmaa enkuruma. Nera olmasinde nkera oltorrono.
Matthew13:39 Nera olmang'atinda oisuaia ninye satan. Nera en-dung'ore enkiting'oto olmaa. Nera ladung'ok ilmalaikan.
Matthew13:40 Akae-- neijia anaa pedotuni olmasinde nepeji tʼenkima neijia eaku tʼenkiting'oto ele maa:"
Matthew13:41 Elairriu Enkerai oltung'ani ilmalaikan lenyena-- nepuo aaiturrur ninje tiatua enkarsishu enye nkitarrikinot pookin o kulo looitobir ntorrok--"
Matthew13:42 nenang'aki ninje atua engaji enkima; atua eakunye enkishirata o eonyoto oo lala.
Matthew13:43 Nepuo aailang'isho supati anaa engolong' tiatua enkarsishu e Menye lenye. Oloata nkiyaa naaning'ie-- njening'!"
Matthew13:44 Neitoki anyanyukie enkarsishu e shumata masaa naashuma tiatua enkuruma-- naatadua oltung'ani obo neisudoo ninje-- nelo tʼeng'ida enye nemir pookin naata ninye-- neinyang'u ena kuruma."
Matthew13:45 Neitoki anyanyukie enkarsishu e shumata olamirani obo loing'orua ilpusi sidan.
Matthew13:46 Ore petum olpusi obo lʼenkinyang'a kitok-- nelo nemir pookin naata ninye-- neinyang'u ilo."
Matthew13:47 Neitoki anyanyukie enkarsishu e shumata erreshet nabo natanang'akaki atua olbalbal-- perreshieki noo muain pookin."
Matthew13:48 Ore peigany-- neilepunye embata-- netoni ninje neiturrurroki naara sidan atua enaret enye-- neiturraa ntorrok."
Matthew13:49 Neijia elaaku tʼenkiting'oto olmaa: nepuo aapuku ilmalaikan nerishu iltorrok tiatua supati--"
Matthew13:50 nepuo aanang'aki ninje atua engaji enkima; atua eakunye enkishirata o eonyoto oo lala.
Matthew13:51 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Ketijing'aitie ndai kuna pookin? Nejoki ninje ninye: Ee-- Laitoriani!"
Matthew13:52 Nejoki ninje: Onaa enyanyukie olayoloni pookin lʼesirata oata eng'eno en-karsishu e shumata olopeny engaji oitupuku tiatua masaa enyena ntokitin ng'ejuko o musan.
Matthew13:53 Neaku ore peidip Yesus kuna kitanyanyukieta-- neing'ua ina alo--"
Matthew13:54 nelotu engang' e menye neiteng'en ninje tiatua engaji Engai enye-- neing'asia ninje baiki nejo: Kaji einotie ele ena ng'eno o kuna kitobirat engolon?"
Matthew13:55 Mera ele enkeiai olagwetani? Me ninye eji ng'otonye Maria? o lalashera lenyena Yakoob o Yoses o Simon o Yudas?
Matthew13:56 Metii nganashera enyena pookin enikitii yook? Akae-- kaji einotie ele kuna pookin?"
Matthew13:57 Nerikare ninje ninye. Nejoki Yesus ninje: Melau olayolounoni enganyit enye neme tiatua olosho lenye o tʼengaji enye.
Matthew13:58 Neitu eitobir te ina alo nkitobirat engolon kumok-- tiaraki natanyaita eiruk ninye."
Matthew14:1 Nening' te ina kata Herodes-- Olaitoriani lʼematua e ong'wan olosho-- mbaak e Yesus."
Matthew14:2 Nejoki ninye laisyayak lenyena: Era ele Yohanes Olaibatisani; etopiwuo ninye too lootuata-- onaa epuku te ninye kuna kitobirat engolon."
Matthew14:3 Amu eibung'a Herodes Yohanes-- neen ninye nepik engaji eenata tʼolbae le Herodias-- eng'oroyoni e Filipos-- olalashe lenye."
Matthew14:4 Amu etiaka Yohanes ninye: torrono te iye-- teni iata ninye."
Matthew14:5 Ore peyeu near ninye metua-- neurei olorere-- amu etejo-- aajo era ninye olayolounoni."
Matthew14:6 Ore tʼengolong' eiunoto e Herodes neiguran entito e Herodias tʼengomom enye. Neiting'id Herodes.
Matthew14:7 Onaa eisiliga ninye tʼenkiturujata-- ajo eisho ninye pookin nayeu ninye."
Matthew14:8 Ore peiteng'en ng'otonye ninye-- nejo: Njooki tene tʼengirra elukunya e Yohanes Olaibatisani!"
Matthew14:9 Neilish olkarsis; kake tʼolbae lʼenkiturujata enye o tʼolbae loo kulo oototonitio te nebo tʼendaata-- neitanapisho-- peishori ninye."
Matthew14:10 Neirriwaa oltung'ani nedung' ninye Yohanes elukunya tiatua engaji eenata.
Matthew14:11 Neauni elukunya enye tʼengirra neishori entito; neaki ng'otonye.
Matthew14:12 Nepuonu laiteng'enuok lenyena neibung' osesen lenye nepuo aanuk; nepuonu neinosaki Yesus ina.
Matthew14:13 Ore pening' Yesus ina-- neing'ua ina alo tʼengalawa nelo ewueji nemetii olorere. Ore pening' isiamin ina-- nesuj ninye too nkejek-- eing'ua ngang'itie."
Matthew14:14 Nepuku si ninye Yesus nedol isiamin kumok; neibung'aki ninje engoshoke nanana neishiunye iltamoiya lenye.
Matthew14:15 Ore peaku teipa-- nepuonu laiteng'enuok lenyena enetii ninye nejo: Etii ene ang'ata nebau enkiarie; ntanapare siamin-- pepuo ngang'itie-- peinyang'aki aten ndaikin."
Matthew14:16 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Meaku-- pepuo; enjoo ndai ninje endaa!"
Matthew14:17 Nejoki si ninje ninye: Mikiata toki tene-- neme ilmkaten imiet o singir aare."
Matthew14:18 Nejo: Eakaki nena tene!
Matthew14:19 Neitanapu-- petoni siamin tʼolkujita-- neibung' kulo mkaten imiet o singir aare-- neimariri shumata nejo ashe negiligil neisho laiteng'enuok kulo mkaten-- neitarasaki laiteng'enuok ninje siamin."
Matthew14:20 Nenya pookin neraposho-- nedumu mbelat naatelekutua ilbenia tomon o are oolulung'a."
Matthew14:21 Ore looinosa era leak iip onom-- metii ng'oroyok o nkera."
Matthew14:22 Neitanap Yesus te ina kata laiteng'enuok lenyena-- peilepaki engalawa-- peiturukie ninye aapuo lido kekun-- metabana neitanapare siamin."
Matthew14:23 Ore peidip aitanapare siamin-- neilepaki oldonyo openy alasaisho. Neaku teipa-- etii ewueji enye openy."
Matthew14:24 Eidipa atabai engalawa empolos olbalbal-- etumito osina too lopir lʼengare-- amu etii olkutati orrinyito."
Matthew14:25 Ore tʼerripore e ong'wan e kiarie nelotu Yesus enetii ninje-- elimana ti oriong' olbalbal."
Matthew14:26 Ore pedol laiteng'enuok ninye elimana ti oriong' olbalbal-- neng'ayung'ayu ejo: Oloip ele! neyetaki t'enkuretishu."
Matthew14:27 Neirorie Yesus ninje nabokata nejo: Entagolo iltauja-- nanu ele; emiureisho!"
Matthew14:28 Nealiki Petros ninye nejo: Laitoriani-- teni ira iye-- ntanapuaki-- palotu enitii ti oriong' engare."
Matthew14:29 Nejo ninye: Wou! Nepuku Petros tʼengalawa nelimana ti oriong' engare alo enetii Yesus.
Matthew14:30 Kake ore pedol olkutati lʼengolon-- neureishoi neiter aasurori-- neyetaki ajo: Laitoriani-- ntopuaki!"
Matthew14:31 Neitorioo Yesus nabokata engaina enye neibung' ninye nejoki: Iye loata enkirukoto kinyi-- ainyo ping'arrirre?"
Matthew14:32 Neilepaki ninje engalawa negira olkutati.
Matthew14:33 Nepuonu si ninje lootii engalawa aaserem ninye nejo: Esipa-- ira iye Oinoti lʼEngai."
Matthew14:34 Ore peidip ninje aatalang'-- nebaia olosho Genesaret."
Matthew14:35 Ore peyolou iltung'anak le ine wueji ninye-- neirriwaki mbat pookin naamanita-- neaki ninye iltamoiya pookin"
Matthew14:36 nesai ninye-- peporoo ake tʼenaipukoi olkila lenye. Ore pookin lootaporoitie-- eishiutuo tukul."
Matthew15:1 Nepuonu te ina kata enetii ninye layolok lʼesirata o Ilfarisayoi-- eing'ua Yerusalem nejo:"
Matthew15:2 Ainyo pelang' laiteng'enuok linono ng'amunot oo lpaiyani? Amu meisuj ngaik-- teni enya endaa."
Matthew15:3 Nealiki Yesus nejoki ninje: Ainyo pilang'ilang'a ndai enkitanapata Engai t'olbae loo ng'amunot inyi?
Matthew15:4 Amu eitanapua Engai: Ntaa kituak minyi o ng'utunyi; ore olodek menye arashu ng'otonye-- njee tʼenkea."
Matthew15:5 Ilimumu ndai ake: Olojoki menye arashu ng'otonye: Era ena toki enkidasare Engai natayeuo naaisho nanu iye-- — neitobir sidai."
Matthew15:6 Neaku te ina kata-- ajo metii oloitaa menye o ng'otonye kitok-- niariara neijia enkitanapata Engai too ng'amunot inyi."
Matthew15:7 Ndai laitusupatuok-- sidai enaitayolouo Yesaya too ndai nejo:"
Matthew15:8 Aanyikaki ele orere too nkutukie enye naaitaa kitok too njonito oo nkutukie enye-- kake aalakwaniki iltauja lenye;"
Matthew15:9 naaisyayaki ninje pesho-- tiaraki naiteng'enu nkiteng'enareitin naara nkitanapat oo ltung'anak."
Matthew15:10 Neipot isiamin nejoki ninje: Entoning'-- piyolouu!"
Matthew15:11 Me enajing' atua enkutuk naitaa oltung'ani torrono-- kake enapuku tʼenkutuk-- ninye naitaa oltung'ani torrono."
Matthew15:12 Nepuonu laiteng'enuok lenyena enetii ninye nejoki: Iyolo-- ajo etirikate Ilfarisayoi te ilo rorei lotoning'o?"
Matthew15:13 Nealu ninye nejo: Ore unot pookin neitu eun Papa lai le shumata-- nedotuni."
Matthew15:14 Entung'ai lelo! Era ninje ilmodook o larikok loo lmodook; teni erik olmodooni obo olekai-- nesulakino atua engumoto pokira are."
Matthew15:15 Nealu Petros nejoki ninye: Ntaaliki yook ena kitanyanyukiet.
Matthew15:16 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Epon si ndai miatata eng'eno?
Matthew15:17 Midamumu-- aajo ore pookin najing' atua enkutuk-- nelo engoshoke nenang'akini tʼosiadi?"
Matthew15:18 Kake napuku tʼenkutuk-- nepuku tʼoltau-- naa nena naaitaa oltung'ani torrono."
Matthew15:19 Amu epuku tʼoltau ndamunot torrok: earata metua-- earata enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni-- entalare-- empurrore-- enjakenishu elejare-- emoroto."
Matthew15:20 Nena tokitin naaitaa oltung'ani torrono; kake enkinosata endaa meisuja ngaik-- meitaa ninye oltung'ani torrono."
Matthew15:21 Nepuku Yesus te ina alo nelo mbat e Tiros o Sidon.
Matthew15:22 Naa ng'orai-- nepuku eng'oroyoni nara Enkananaya oo nona rishat-- neapaa oltoilo nejo: Laitoriani-- nakerai e David-- tokorduaki! Eitameito naleng' ilmeneng'a entito ai."
Matthew15:23 Neitu ealiki ninye ororei. Nepuonu laiteng'enuok lenyena nesai ninye nejo: Njoo elo ang'-- amu eapaa oltoilo tekurum ang'."
Matthew15:24 Nealu ninye nejo: Eitu aairriwari nanu neme enetii nkerra naaimina engaji Israel.
Matthew15:25 Nelotu ninye ake negilaki kung' nejo: Laitoriani-- taretokoki!"
Matthew15:26 Nealu ninye nejo: Me sidai-- teni eoruni nkera endaa enye nenang'akini ildiain."
Matthew15:27 Nejo ninye: Ee-- Laitoriani-- kake enya si ildiain mbelat kunyinyi naadoiyo tʼenaraa oo laitoriak lenye."
Matthew15:28 Nealu Yesus te ina nejoki ninye: Iye-- nang'oroyoni-- kitok enkirukoto ino! Njeaku anaa piyeu! Neishiu entito enye te ina kata ake."
Matthew15:29 Neing'ua Yesus ina alo nelotu embata olbalbal le Galilaya neilepaki oldonyo neton te ina alo.
Matthew15:30 Nepuonu siamin kumok enetii ninye-- eata te nebo o ninje lemeidim aashom o ilmodook o lemeidim aairoro o looata rrugi o ilkulekai kumok-- neitaperoki nkejek e Yesus neishiunye ninje."
Matthew15:31 Neing'asia siamin edolita eiro lemeidim aairoro naa biot looata rrugi-- nepuo lemeidim aashom-- nedolisho ilmodook; neitadaraa ninje Engai e Israel."
Matthew15:32 Neipot Yesus laiteng'enuok lenyena nejo: Aibung'aki siamin engoshoke nanana-- amu etaa ngolong'i uni ebik enatii nanu nemeata endaa; namayeu naitanapaa etupukoitie-- pemeiterre tʼengoitoi."
Matthew15:33 Nejoki laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye: Ke ti aji kitum tene ti ang'ata ilmkaten kumok-- peraposho esiamu kitok naba nji?"
Matthew15:34 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Iatata ndai ilmkaten aja? Nejo ninje: Oopishana o singir kuti.
Matthew15:35 Neitanap isiamin-- petoni tʼenkop--"
Matthew15:36 neibung' kulo mkaten oopishana o kulo singir-- nejo ashe nebelibel neisho laiteng'enuok lenyena; neitarasaki si ninje-- laiteng'enuok lenyena-- siamin."
Matthew15:37 Nenya pookin neraposho; nesotu lekunot oo mbelat ilbenia oopishana oolulung'a.
Matthew15:38 Ore looinosa nera leak iip artam-- metii ng'oroyok o nkera."
Matthew15:39 Ore peidip aitanapare siamin-- neilepaki engalawa nelotu embata e Magdala."
Matthew16:1 Nepuonu Ilfarisayoi o Sadukayoi netem ninye-- peitadol ninje olponoto oing'ua shumata."
Matthew16:2 Nealuninyenejoki: Ijojo ndai teipa: Elakiny-- amu edo shumata;"
Matthew16:3 ore enasirie ijojo ndai: Eirujuruj taata-- amu edo shumata neopoko. Ndai laitusupatuok-- indimidimi aatayolo emua e shumata-- kake mindimidimi aatayolo ntokitin kituak ena kata?"
Matthew16:4 Eing'oru ena kishon torrono nanyor mbaak eloloito olponoto-- nemeishori olponoto neme olponoto lʼolayolounoni Yona. Neing'ua ninje alo."
Matthew16:5 Ore peidip aatalang' laiteng'enuok lenyena aabaiki lido kekun-- nerikino enap ilmkaten."
Matthew16:6 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Eng'orai-- piduaiaia aten tʼenkisiijoi oo Lfarisayoi o noo Sadukayoi."
Matthew16:7 Neishangarrakino ninje oopeny nejo: Tiaraki mikinapita ilmkaten.
Matthew16:8 Ore peyolou Yesus ina-- nejoki ninje: Ainyo pinjangarrakinono ndai maten-- ndai lʼenkirukoto kinyi-- tiaraki neitu iauu ilmkaten?"
Matthew16:9 Epon eitu iyolouu ndai o nyoo? Midamumu ndai kulo mkaten imiet too kulo iip onom o ilbenia aja litudumutua ndai?
Matthew16:10 Baiki kulo mkaten oopishana too kulo iip artam o ilbenia aja litudumutua?
Matthew16:11 Kaji inkoko teni miyololo-- aajo maliki ndai embae oo lmkaten-- teni ajo: Entaduai aten tʼenkisiijoi oo Lfarisayoi o noo Sadukayoi!"
Matthew16:12 Neyolou ninje te ina kata-- aajo eitu ejo-- peduaia aten tʼenkisiijoi olmkate-- kake tʼenkiteng'enare oo Lfarisayoi o noo Sadukayoi."
Matthew16:13 Ore pelotu Yesus engalo engang' Kaisarea-Filipi-- neikilikwan ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena nejo: Kejo iltung'anak era Enkerai oltung'ani ng'ai?"
Matthew16:14 Nejo ninje: Ejo ilkulekai-- aajo ira Yohanes Olaibatisani-- nejo ilkulekai: Eliya-- nejo ilkulekai: Yeremiya-- arashu obo too layolounok."
Matthew16:15 Nejoki ninye ninje: Kake ijojo ndai ara nanu ng'ai?
Matthew16:16 Nealu Simon Petros nejo: Ira iye Kristos-- Oinoti lʼEngai naishiu!"
Matthew16:17 Nealiki Yesus nejoki ninye: Ira tesh-- Simon le Yona-- amu eitu kintayolo nkiri o osarge-- kake Papa lai le shumata."
Matthew16:18 Naaliki si nanu iye: Ira iye Petros-- nayeu nashet te shumata ele soit esirit ai nemegilu kishomini engang' e satan ninye."
Matthew16:19 Nayeu naaisho iye mboleta enkarsishu e shumata. Ore pookin nien iye tʼenkop-- neaku eteenaki te shumata; o pookin nilalak iye tʼenkop-- neaku etalaaki te shumata."
Matthew16:20 Neitanap te ina alo naleng' laiteng'enuok lenyena-- pemeliki ninje oltung ani-- ajo era ninye Kristos."
Matthew16:21 Ore te ina kata neiter Yesus aitayolo laiteng'enuok lenyena-- ajo meata kata nemelo ninye Yerusalem-- neitame naleng' laigwenak o laidasak kituak o layolok lʼesirata ninye-- neari metua-- nepiu tʼengolong' e uni."
Matthew16:22 Neibung' Petros ninye nerik enkilepata neiter aikok ninye nejo: Laitoriani-- taduai kion-- njoo mikitum kuna!"
Matthew16:23 Neibelekenya ninye nejoki Petros: Nyaai kurum ai-- satan-- ira erikata ai-- amu mimbirribir nara nʼEngai neme nʼentung'anishu."
Matthew16:24 Nejoki Yesus te ina kata laiteng'enuok lenyena: Ore oltung'ani loyeu naasuj-- njeisim kion-- njedumakino esalaba enye-- paasuj."
Matthew16:25 Amu teni eyeu oltung'ani neitopok empuan enye-- neiminye ninye; ore oltung'ani oiminye empuan enye tʼolbae lai-- netum ninye."
Matthew16:26 Kaa dupoto etum oltung'ani-- teni eng'eru olmaa pookin-- netum elaunoto olmumua lenye? Arashu kainyo elakunye oltung'ani olmumua lenye?"
Matthew16:27 Amu eaku elotu Enkerai oltung'ani tʼenkitook e Menye lenye te nebo o ilmalaikan lenyena; te ina kata elalaaki oltung'ani pookin anaa peitobira ninye.
Matthew16:28 Japa-- aliki ndai: Etii iltung'anak atua kulo ooitashe tene-- lemeinyorrinyor ninje enkea tukul-- metabana nedol Enkerai oltung'ani elotu tiatua enkarsishu enye."
Matthew17:1 Ore peishunye ngolong'i ile-- negelu Yesus Petros o Yakobos o Yohanes-- olalashe lenye-- nerik ninje shumata oldonyo oado oopeny."
Matthew17:2 Neala emua enye neilang'isho engomom enye anaa engolong' neiborru ilkilani lenyena anaa enkilang'et.
Matthew17:3 Naa ng'orai nelioi too ninje Mose o Eliya; neirorie ninje ninye.
Matthew17:4 Nealu Petros nejoki Yesus: Laitoriani-- sidai-- kitii yook ene! Teni iyeu-- nashet tene iltomboitie okuni: obo lino-- obo le Mose-- obo le Eliya."
Matthew17:5 Ore epon eirorita-- neopoo ninje erukenya naibor; naa ng'orai-- neing'ua oltoilo erukenya ejo: Nyele Oinoti lai lanyor oshipakino oltau lai; entoning' ninye!"
Matthew17:6 Ore pening' laiteng'enuok kuna-- nebatata aaijululo neureishoi naleng'."
Matthew17:7 Nelotu Yesus enetii ninje neiseiye ninje nejo: Enyoito-- emiureisho!"
Matthew17:8 Ore peapu ngonyek enye-- neitu edol oltung'ani neme Yesus ake."
Matthew17:9 Ore pedou ninje tʼoldonyo-- neitanap Yesus ninje ejo: Emiliki oltung'ani ina duaroto-- metabana nepiu Enkerai oltung'ani tiatua lootuata."
Matthew17:10 Neikilikwan laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye ejo: Ainyo naa pejo layolok lʼesirata-- aajo meata kata nemeng'as alotu Eliya?"
Matthew17:11 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninje: Esipa-- eng'as alotu Eliya neibelekeny pookin metaa ng'ejuko;"
Matthew17:12 kake aliki nanu ndai: Eidipa aeu Eliya-- neitu eyolou ninje ninye-- kake eitobirakitia ninye enatayeutuo ninje. Neijia meata kata nemeitame ninje Enkerai oltung'ani."
Matthew17:13 Neyolou te ina kata laiteng'enuok lenyena-- aajo einosaki ninje mbaak e Yohanes Olaibatisani."
Matthew17:14 Ore pepuonu ninje enetii esiamu-- nelotu oltung'ani obo enetii ninye negilaki kung'"
Matthew17:15 ejo: Laitoriani-- to-kordu enkerai ai-- amu eibung' olkiterriata ninye neata emion torrono: Eurokino aigil kumok enkima-- aigil kumok engare;"
Matthew17:16 nariku ninye enetii laiteng'enuok linono-- neru aaishiunye ninye."
Matthew17:17 Nealu Yesus nejo: Ndai enkishon nemeiruk neriwuo-- ke metabaiki anu atii e nebo o ndai? Ke metabaiki anu ang'iriaki ndai? Eakaki ilo!"
Matthew17:18 Nebuaki Yesus ninye-- nepuku olmeneng'ani te ninye neishiu ena kerai eiter te ina kata."
Matthew17:19 Nepuonu ina kata laiteng'enuok enetii Yesus tʼewueji enye oopeny nejo: Ainyo peitu kindim yook aatimir ninye?
Matthew17:20 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Tiaraki nimirukuruku ndai; amu japa-- aliki ndai: Teni iatata enkirukoto anaa embeu e karadali-- nijokiki ele donyo: Tadotunye tene abaiki idya alo! nedotunye si ninye; nemetii entoki nemeaku too ndai."
Matthew17:21 Kake mepuku ena mua neme tʼesayata o tʼempukoroto.
Matthew17:22 Ore etii ninje Galilaya-- nejoki Yesus ninje: Eaku eitarasakini Enkerai oltung'ani ngaik oo ltung'anak--"
Matthew17:23 near ninje ninye metua-- nepiu tʼengolong' e uni. Neilish ninje naleng'."
Matthew17:24 Ore pepuonu ninje Kapernaum-- nepuonu kulo loobosu kodi engaji Engai enetii Petros nejo: Melak olaiteng'enani linyi kodi engaji Engai?"
Matthew17:25 Nejo: Elak. Ore pelotu engaji-- neiter Yesus aikilikwan ninye nejo: Ijo aa-- Simon? Ke too akua tung'anak eaiye ilkarsisi kodi? Too nkera enye arashu too lomon?"
Matthew17:26 Nejoki Petros: Too lomon. Nejoki Yesus ninye: Akae-- elakuno nkera."
Matthew17:27 Kake pimikintirik yook ninje-- nno embata olbalbal-- ntadoiki erreshet-- mbung'a osingirri lʼelukunya opuku; ore pibol enkutuk enye-- nilatum engosholai: mbung'a ina-- njooi tʼolbae lai o lino."
Matthew18:1 Nepuonu te ina kata laiteng'enuok enetii Yesus nejo: Ang'ai naa ora kitok tʼenkarsishu e shumata?
Matthew18:2 Neipot Yesus enkerai nabo neitasheye tʼempolos enye
Matthew18:3 nejo: Japa-- aliki ndai-- teni mimbelekenyanya aaku anaa nkera-- mijing'ijing'i tukul atua enkarsishu e shumata."
Matthew18:4 Akae-- ore oltung'ani pookin loitadou kion anaa ena kerai-- ele lora kitok tʼenkarsishu e shumata."
Matthew18:5 Ore oltung'ani pookin loitoomon enkerai nabo nanyanyukie ena tʼengarna ai-- naaitoomon nanu."
Matthew18:6 Ore oloitapong'oo nabo too kuna kunyinyi naairuk nanu-- eikash-- teni eenikini emurt enye osoit oituutishoreki neitadoikini ninye eneasur olbalbal."
Matthew18:7 Ee-- kake aiya olmaa tʼolbae loo nkitarrikinot! Amu meata kata nemepuonu nkitarrikinot; kake ee-- kake aiya oltung'ani oau nkitarrikinot!"
Matthew18:8 Teni kintadiak engaina ino arashu enkeju ino-- tudung'o ninye-- pinang'aki enelakwa. Eikash te iye-- pijing' atua empuan-- miata engaina arashu enkeju-- nelang' iata ngaik are arashu nkejek are-- nikinang'akini atua enkima nememuta."
Matthew18:9 Ore pikintadiak engong'u ino-- tukurtu ninye-- pinang'aki enelakwa. Eikash te iye-- pijing' atua empuan-- niata engong'u nabo-- nelang' iata ngonyek are-- nikinang'akini atua enkima nememuta."
Matthew18:10 Eng'orai-- pemimenimene nabo too kuna kutiti. Amu aliki ndai: Edol ilmalaikan lenye le shumata ngolong'i pookin engomom e Papa lai le shumata."
Matthew18:11 Amu eewuo Enkerai oltung'ani-- peitopok enaimina."
Matthew18:12 Ijojo aa? Teni eata oltung'ani nkerra iip neimin nabo too ninje-- aa meing'ua ninye kuna ntomoni enturuj o enturuj tʼoldonyo neibung' engoitoi-- pelaing'oru ina naimina?"
Matthew18:13 Ore pelatum-- japa-- aliki ndai: Eng'idakino ena naleng' nelang' kuna ntomoni enturuj o enturuj neitu eimin."
Matthew18:14 Neijia meiting'idisho tʼengomom e Minyi linyi le shumata-- teni eimin nabo too kuna kutiti."
Matthew18:15 Teni kintarruoki olalashe lino-- nno-- toroja ninye iboitata o ninye openy. Teni kining'-- inoto olalashe lino;"
Matthew18:16 teni mikining'-- mbung'a obo arashu aare te nebo o iye-- peiye eaku nkutukie oo ljaken aare arashu okuni-- peitagoli ororei pookin."
Matthew18:17 Ore pemening' kulo-- tiaki esirit; ore pemening' baiki esirit-- njeaku te iye anaa oltung'ani lemeata Engai o olaoshoni le kodi."
Matthew18:18 Japa-- aliki ndai: Ore pookin nieniene tʼenkop-- neeni te shumata; o pookin nilakilaka tʼenkop-- nelaki te shumata."
Matthew18:19 Naitoki ajoki ndai: Teni eibung'are ilkulinyi aare tʼenkop tʼembae pookin naomonu-- neitobiraki ninje Papa lai le shumata."
Matthew18:20 Amu teni etumo aare arashu okuni tʼengarna ai-- natii nanu empolos enye."
Matthew18:21 Nelotu Petros enetii ninye nejoki ninye: Laitoriani-- kaigil aja aing'uaiki olalashe lai laaitarruoki? Mebaiki aigil naapishana?"
Matthew18:22 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Aaliki nanu iye: me aigil naapishana-- kake aigil ntomoni naapishana kat naapishana."
Matthew18:23 Onaa-- enyanyukie enkarsishu e shumata olkarsis obo oikenakinore laisyayak lenyena."
Matthew18:24 Ore peiter aikenakinore-- nerikokini obo oata esile enye talanta iip kat iip."
Matthew18:25 Ore pemeata entoki nalakie-- neitanapisho Olaitoriani lenye-- pemiri ninye o eng'oroyoni enye o nkera enyena o pookin naata ninye-- pelaki ena sile."
Matthew18:26 Akae-- nebatata olaisyayani nesai ninye nejo: Laitoriani-- ntirring'akaki-- paalaaki iye tukul."
Matthew18:27 Neibung'aki olaitoriani ilo aisyayani engoshoke nanana-- nelaku ninye neing'uaiki ena sile."
Matthew18:28 Nepuku ilo aisyayani nedol obo too lalashera lenyena oata esile enye denaria iip; newuap ninye neibung' olgos lenye nejo: Talaakaki esile ai!
Matthew18:29 Akae-- nebatatakino olalashe lenye nkejek enyena nesai ninye nejo: Ntirring'akaki-- paalaaki iye tukul."
Matthew18:30 Neitu eyeu ninye-- nelo nenang'aki ninye engaji eenata-- metabana nelak ena sile."
Matthew18:31 Ore pedol lalashera lenyena kuna naataa-- neilish naleng'-- nepuonu neitayolo olaitoriani lenye pookin naataa."
Matthew18:32 Akae-- neipot olaitoriani lenye ninye nejoki: Iye-- laisyayani torrono-- aatung'aikia nanu iye ena sile pookin-- kitasaiya."
Matthew18:33 Ainyo peitu imbung'aki iye olalashe lino engoshoke nanana anaa paaibung'aka nanu iye engoshoke nanana?
Matthew18:34 Negoro olaitoriani lenye neitarasaki ninye laitamiok-- metabana nelak ena sile pookin."
Matthew18:35 Neijia elaikunaki ndai Papa lai le shumata-- teni ming'uaikiki too ltauja linyi oltung'ani pookin olalashe lenye nkitarruot enyena."
Matthew19:1 Neaku ore peidip Yesus kulo rorei-- nedumunye te Galilaya nelotu rishat e Yudaya-- tʼolkekun le Yordan."
Matthew19:2 Nesuj isiamin kumok ninye neishiunye ninje te ina alo.
Matthew19:3 Nepuonu Ilfarisayoi enetii ninye-- netem ninye nejoki ninye: Ke sidai-- teni erishare olmoruo eng'oroyoni enye tʼolbae lʼentoki naje?"
Matthew19:4 Nealiki nejoki ninje: Eitu isomama-- ajo oloitobira tʼenkiterata oltung'ani-- eitobira-- peaku olmoruo obo o eng'oroyoni nabo--"
Matthew19:5 nejo: Onaa elaing'ua oltung'ani menye o ng'otonye neibung'are eng'oroyoni enye-- neaku pokira are osesen obo?"
Matthew19:6 Akae-- nemeitoki aaku are-- kake osesen obo. Ore enaidikidiko Engai-- njoo merish oltung'ani."
Matthew19:7 Nejoki ninje ninye: Ainyo peitanapua Mose-- peishori empalai erishata-- peing'uari eng'oroyoni?"
Matthew19:8 Nejoki ninye ninje: Tiaraki natagolito iltauja linyi-- neisho Mose ndai-- irisharere ng'oroyok inyi; eitu eaku neijia neba tʼenkiterata."
Matthew19:9 Kake aliki nanu ndai: Olonshare eng'oroyoni enye neme tʼolbae loo mbaak eloloito neamaa engai-- near ninye enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni; ore oloamaa enatirishareki-- near enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni."
Matthew19:10 Nejoki laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye: Teni eaku mbaak oltung'ani nji-- sidai-- teni meamisho."
Matthew19:11 Nejoki ninje: me pookin ooidim aatayolo ele rorei neme kulo ake ooitumunyanaki.
Matthew19:12 Amu etii loogelema looing'ua ngoshuak oo noong'otonye etiu nji; netii loogelema ootegelema iltung'anak; netii loogelema looitaa aten loogelema tʼolbae lʼenkarsishu e shumata. Oloidim atayolou-- njeyolou."
Matthew19:13 Nerikuni nkera enetii ninye-- peiteleiki ngaik ninje nesaisho; nebuaki ake laiteng'enuok ninje."
Matthew19:14 Kake etejo Yesus: Enjoo nkera epuonu enatii-- emimitiki ninje-- amu era enkarsishu e shumata noo loonyanyukie kuna."
Matthew19:15 Neiteleiki ninje ngaik; neing'ua ina alo.
Matthew19:16 Naa ng'orai-- nelotu oltung'ani obo enetii ninye nejoki ninye: Laiteng'enani sidai-- kaa toki sidai aitobir-- peiye atum empuan nemeiting'?"
Matthew19:17 Nejoki ninye: Ainyo pikijo sidai? Metii osidai neme obo lora Engai; kake teni iyeu nijing' atua empuan-- mbung'a nkitanapat."
Matthew19:18 Nejoki ninye: Akua? Nejo Yesus: Miar metua! Miar enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni! Mipurrisho! Minjakenu elejare!
Matthew19:19 Ntaa kituak minyi o ng'utunyi o: Meata kata niminyor olʼelatia ino anaa pinyor kion!
Matthew19:20 Nejoki ele barnoti ninye: Aibung'a kuna pookin neba tʼenkitishu ai — ainyo naainyaaka ang'oriki?
Matthew19:21 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Teni iyeu niaku olbaiaroti-- nno-- timira pookin niata-- pinjo laisinak-- piata iye masaa te shumata; ore pindip-- nikilotu asuj."
Matthew19:22 Ore pening' ele barnoti ena bae-- nelo ang' eilish; amu eata masaa kumok."
Matthew19:23 Nejoki Yesus laiteng'enuok lenyena: Japa-- aliki ndai: Egol-- pejing' oladupani atua enkarsishu e shumata."
Matthew19:24 Naitoki aliki ndai: Elelek eim endames eudoto esindano nelang' oladupani ejing' atua enkarsishu Engai.
Matthew19:25 Ore pening' laiteng'enuok lenyena kuna-- neing'asia naleng' nejo: Ang'ai naa loidim atopua?"
Matthew19:26 Neing'oraa Yesus ninje nejoki ninje: Meidimai ena too ltung'anak-- kake eidimai ntokitin pookin tʼEngai."
Matthew19:27 Nealiki Petros nejoki ninye: Ng'orai-- kitung'aitie yook pookin nikisuj iye. Kainyo naa kitum?"
Matthew19:28 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Japa-- aliki ndai: Ore ndai likitusuja-- tʼeiunoto e are nipuopuo aatonie lorikaishi tomon o are-- ingwenakiki njomito tomon o are e Israel-- teni elatonie Enkerai oltung'ani olorika lʼenkitook enye."
Matthew19:29 Ore pookin looing'ua ngajijik arashu lalashera arashu nganashera arashu menye arashu ng'otonye arashu eng'oroyoni arashu nkera arashu nkuruman tʼolbae lʼengarna ai-- nelang'amu ninye aigil iip nejung'u empuan nemeiting'."
Matthew19:30 Kake ore lkumok loora lʼelukunya-- neaku lʼenkiting'oto-- neaku lʼenkiting'oto lʼelukunya."
Matthew20:1 Amu enyanyukie enkarsishu e shumata olopeny engaji otupukuo enasirie alaing'oru laisyayak-- perik atua enkuruma enye oo nkeek olmarua."
Matthew20:2 Ore peitobirakinore laisyayak te denarion nabo endama-- neirriwaa ninje atua enkuruma enye oo nkeek olmarua."
Matthew20:3 Nepuku te saa uni-- nedol kulekai looitashe tʼosingira-- meata enkyas."
Matthew20:4 Neitoki ajoki ninje: Enjom si ndai atua enkuruma ai oo nkeek olmarua; ayeu naisho ndai enairirikinore.
Matthew20:5 Nepuo. Neitoki apuku te saa ile o te saa enturuj-- neiko neijia ake."
Matthew20:6 Ore te saa tomon o nabo nepuku neinepu ilkulekai looitashe-- meata enkyas-- nejoki ninje: Ainyo pintasheshe tene endama pookin-- miatata enkyas?"
Matthew20:7 Nejoki si ninje: Ai-- metii oltung'ani oewuo aing'oru yook. Nejoki ninye ninje: Enjom si ndai atua enkuruma ai oo nkeek olmarua-- nipuopuo aatum enairirikinore."
