Matthew20:8 Ore pemutu-- nejoki olaitoriani lʼenkuruma oo nkeek olmarua olaing'orani lenye: Mpoto laisyayak-- pinjo ninje olkwaje-- ninter too lʼenkiting'oto metabaiki lʼelukunya."
Matthew20:9 Nepuonu looipotoki te saa tomon o nabo-- neng'amu oltung'ani pookin denarion enye."
Matthew20:10 Ore pepuonu kulo lʼelukunya-- nejo ninje-- aajo eng'amu enalang'; neng'amu si ninje oltung'ani pookin denarion enye."
Matthew20:11 Ore peidip aatang'amutu ina-- neing'unyung'unyaki olopeny engaji--"
Matthew20:12 nejo: Ore kulo lʼenkiting'oto eitobira enkyas esaa nabo ake-- nintorisioki ninje yook likiting'iriakitia osina o enkirowuaj endama."
Matthew20:13 Nealiki ninye nejoki obo too ninje: Oljore lai-- eitu aaisil iye. Eitu kidung'okino nanu o iye te denarion nabo?"
Matthew20:14 Eao enara enino-- nno ang'! Anyor aishoo ele lʼenkiting'oto enarisiore enino."
Matthew20:15 Arashu maata engolon-- paitobir tʼentoki ai enayeu? Ke torrono engong'u ino-- tiaraki nara arip?"
Matthew20:16 Neijia eaku lʼenkiting'oto lʼenkiterata-- neaku lʼenkiterata lʼenkiting'oto. Amu eipotoki ilkumok-- kake etegeluaki ilkuti."
Matthew20:17 Ore peyeu neilep Yesus alo Yerusalem-- nerik laiteng'enuok tomon o are enkilepata nejoki ninje tʼengoitoi:"
Matthew20:18 Eng'orai-- kishumari metabaiki Yerusalem-- neitarasakini Enkerai oltung'ani ngaik oo laidasak kituak o layolok lʼesirata-- neigwenaki ninye-- peari metua--"
Matthew20:19 neitarasaki ninje ninye atua ngaik oo loreren-- petum aatamor-- near ninye too nkeenda nesheiki esalaba; nelapiu tʼengolong' e uni."
Matthew20:20 Nelotu enetii ninye ng'otonye oo nkera e Sebedayos te nebo o nkera enyena-- negilaki ninye kung' neomonu ororei te ninye."
Matthew20:21 Nejoki ninye: Kainyo iyeu? Nejoki ninye: Njoo etoni kulo inot lainei aare tʼenkarsishu ino-- obo te tatene ino-- olekai te kedyanye ino."
Matthew20:22 Nealu Yesus nejo: Miyololo ndai eniomonunu. Indimidimi aatook ndai enkwaru naok nanu-- neibatisi ndai tʼenkibatisa naaibatisieki nanu? Nejoki ninje ninye: Ee-- kindim."
Matthew20:23 Nejoki ninye ninje: Esipa-- iokioko enkwaru ai-- neibatisi ndai tʼenkibatisa naaibatisieki nanu-- kake ore entonata te tatene o te kedyanye ai maata enkitanapata naishorie ndai-- kake noo kulo looitobiraka Papa lai."
Matthew20:24 Ore pening' kulo tomon kuna-- nelisaki kulo alashera pokira are."
Matthew20:25 Kake neipot Yesus ninje nejo: Iyololo ndai-- aajo eitorisho ilkarsisi loo loreren neata ilkituak lenye engolon too ninje."
Matthew20:26 Meaku nji too ndai! Kake oloyeu neaku kitok too ndai-- njeaku olaisyayani linyi."
Matthew20:27 Ore oltung'ani pookin loyeu neaku olaiturukoni too ndai-- njeaku olaisyayani linyi--"
Matthew20:28 neijia anaa peitu elotu Enkerai oltung'ani-- peisho eisyayakini ninye-- kake peisyaisho neishooio empuan enye-- peaku elakunoto oo lkumok."
Matthew20:29 Ore pepuku te Yeriko-- nesuj esiamu kitok ninye."
Matthew20:30 Naa ng'orai-- netoni ilmodook aare tʼembata engoitoi; ore pening'-- aajo Yesu oimita-- neapaa iltoiloi nejo: Laitoriani-- nakerai e David-- tokordu yook!"
Matthew20:31 Nebuaki esiamu ninje-- peiye egira. Kake nepon aapaa iltoiloi lenye nejo: Laitoriani-- nakerai e David-- tokordu yook!"
Matthew20:32 Neitashe Yesus neipot ninje nejo: Ainyo iyeuu naasaki ndai?
Matthew20:33 Nejoki ninje ninye: Laitoriani-- pebolo ngonyek ang'."
Matthew20:34 Neibung'aki Yesus ninje engoshoke nanana neporoo ninje ngonyek; nedolishoi ngonyek enye nabokata nesuj ninje ninye.
Matthew21:1 Ore petaaniki ninje Yerusalem-- nebaia Betfage tʼOldonyo loo loirienito-- neirriwa te ine Yesus laiteng'enuok aare nejoki ninje:"
Matthew21:2 Embung'a engoitoi metabaiki engang' naitoriokinore ndai-- ninepupu nabokata esikiria lipong' naena te nebo o enkurrarru enye; entalakutu-- pikireakiki!"
Matthew21:3 Naa teni eliki ndai oltung'ani ororei-- entejo: Olaitoriani oyeu ninje; neisho ndai nabokata."
Matthew21:4 Etaa kuna pookin-- pebaia enairoro olayolounoni ejo:"
Matthew21:5 Entiakiti entito Sion: Ng'orai-- elotu olkarsis lino enitii-- obor-- neilepaka esikiria o enkurrarru elipong' nanapita orridati."
Matthew21:6 Neibung' kulo aiteng'enuok engoitoi neiko anaa peitanapa Yesus ninje--"
Matthew21:7 nereu esikiria lipong' o enkurrarru-- neisalaashaki ilkarashi lenye shumata enye-- neitoton ninye te shumata enye."
Matthew21:8 Neisalaash ilkumok tʼesiamu ilkarashi lenye t'engoitoi; nedung'u ilkulekai ilng'osil loo ljanito neisalaash tʼengoitoi.
Matthew21:9 Ore esiamu naituruk o nasujita neapaa iltoiloi ejo: Hosiana-- enkerai e David! Njeitadarari ololotu tʼengarna Olaitoriani! Hosiana te shumata!"
Matthew21:10 Ore pejing' ninye Yerusalem-- neing'oling'ola engang' pookin nejo: Kang'ai ele?"
Matthew21:11 Nejo siamin ake: Era ele Yesus-- olayolounoni le Nasaret e Galilaya."
Matthew21:12 Nejing' Yesus engaji sinyati nemir lamirak o lainyang'ak pookin tʼengaji sinyati neibelekeny naraan oo kulo ooitaalita ngoshola o lorikaishi loo lamirak loo lmaita--"
Matthew21:13 nejoki ninje: Etisiraki: „Meata kata nemeipoti engaji ai engaji esayata“-- kake intaa ndai ninye engapunet oo laisimak."
Matthew21:14 Nejing'aki ninye tiatua engaji sinyati ilmodook o lemeidim aashom-- neishiunye ninje."
Matthew21:15 Ore pedol laidasak kituak o layolok lʼesirata mbaak naaiputukunyisho naaitobira ninye-- o nkera tiatua engaji sinyati naapaa iltoiloi-- nejo: Hosiana-- enkerai e David! nelis ninje"
Matthew21:16 nejoki ninye: Ining'ito enajoito kuna? Nejoki Yesus ninje: Ee! Eitu isomama ndai tukul: „Intabaiye enkitadararoto too nkutukie oo nkunyinyi o nganaak?“
Matthew21:17 Neing'ua ninje alo aulo engang' metabaiki Betania neirrag te ina alo.
Matthew21:18 Ore enasirie errinyokino engang'-- neibung' olamei ninye."
Matthew21:19 Nedol ninye olng'aboli obo tʼembata engoitoi-- nenyikaki neitu edol toki te shumata enye neme mbenek ake-- nejoki ninye: Mintoki aiu ilmomo nkatan pookin! Neinaaia olng'aboli nabokata."
Matthew21:20 Ore pedol laiteng'enuok kuna-- neing'asia nejo: Kaji eikuna teni einaaia olng'aboli nabokata?"
Matthew21:21 Nealiki Yesus nejoki ninje: Japa-- aliki ndai: Teni iatata enkirukoto niming'arrirrorro-- nintobiribiri neme ina nʼolng'aboli ake-- kake teni ijokiki baiki ele donyo: Tadotunye-- tanang'akinoi atua olbalbal! neaku."
Matthew21:22 Ore pookin eniomonunu tʼesayata-- teni irukuruku-- nipuopuo aang'amu."
Matthew21:23 Ore pejing' ninye atua engaji sinyati-- nepuonu enetii ninye laidasak kituak o laigwenak lʼolorere-- eiteng'enisho ninye-- nejo; Ke ti aa golon intobirita kuna? Kang'ai likinjoo ena golon?"
Matthew21:24 Nealiki Yesus nejoki ninje: Ayeu naikilikwan nanu si ndai ororei obo; teni kialikiki-- naliki si nanu ndai-- ajo ke ti aa golon aitobirita kuna."
Matthew21:25 Kaji eing'ua enkibatisa e Yohanes? Keing'ua shumata arashu atua iltung'anak? Neirorioro ninje oopeny nejo: Teni kijo: Eing'ua shumata! ejoki yook: Ainyo naa peitu irukuruku ninye?
Matthew21:26 Teni kijo: Atua iltung'anak! nikiure esiamu; amu edolita pookin Yohanes-- ajo era olayolounoni."
Matthew21:27 Nealiki ninje Yesus nejo: Mikiyolo. Nejoki si ninye ninje: Onaa maliki si nanu ndai-- ajo ke ti aa golon aitobirita kuna."
Matthew21:28 Ijojo aa? Etii oltung'ani obo oata nkera are-- nelo ninye enetii olbotor nejo: Nakerai ai-- nno taata-- ntobira nkyasin tiatua enkuruma ai oo nkeek olmarua."
Matthew21:29 Nealu ninye nejo: Mayeu naitobir. Tekurum neala nelo.
Matthew21:30 Nelo enetii oliare nejoki neijia. Nealu si ninye nejo: Laitoriani-- alo-- — neitu elo."
Matthew21:31 Kalo obo too kulo pokira are oitobira enanyor menye lenye? Nejoki ninje: ilo botor. Nejoki Yesus ninje: Japa-- aliki ndai: Eiturukie ndai laoshok le kodi o iltung'anak lʼentalare aajing' enkarsishu e shumata nelang' ndai."
Matthew21:32 Amu eewuo Yohanes enitiiti neiteng'en ndai engoitoi naitoriori-- neitu irukuruku ndai ninye; kake eiruko ninye laoshok le kodi o iltung'anak lʼentalare. Ore itadua ndai-- neitu ialala-- pitumutumu aairuko ninye."
Matthew21:33 Entoning' engai kitanyanyukiet: Etii olopeny engaji otuuno enkuruma oo nkeek olmarua-- neitaman osariko netur engumoto naironyishoreki neshet olmnara neitamany laturok nelo enelakwa."
Matthew21:34 Ore petaanu eng'erunoto oo lmomo-- neirriwaa laisyayak lenyena enetii laturok-- peng'amu ilmomo lenyena."
Matthew21:35 Neibung' kulo aturok laisyayak lenyena; near obo-- near olekai metua-- near oli okuni too soito."
Matthew21:36 Neitoki airriwaa ilkulekai aisyayak-- kumok loolang' kulo lʼelukunya; neikunaki ninje ake neijia."
Matthew21:37 Tekurum neirriwaki oinoti lenye nejo: Epuo aaanyit oinoti lai.
Matthew21:38 Ore pedol laturok oinoti-- neirorioro oopeny: Nyelido lora olajung'oni; ewotu-- mataar ninye metua-- pikiea enjung'o enye!"
Matthew21:39 Neibung' ninje ninye nenang'aki oriong' enkuruma oo nkeek olmarua near ninye metua.
Matthew21:40 Ore pelalotu ele aitoriani lʼenkuruma oo nkeek olmarua-- kainyo easaki kulo aturok?"
Matthew21:41 Nejoki ninje ninye: Ear torrono kulo torrok-- neitamany ilkulekai aturok atua enkuruma oo nkeek olmarua loopuo aaisho ilmomo tʼenkata enye."
Matthew21:42 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Eitu isomama tukul tiatua esirata: Ore osoit lotanyaita lashetak-- etaa ele osoit kitok lʼolpijata. Etaa ina tʼOlaitoriani-- neiputukunyisho ninye too ngonyek ang'?"
Matthew21:43 Onaa-- aliki nanu ndai: Eitauni enkarsishu Engai too ndai neishori olorere oiu ilmomo lenyena."
Matthew21:44 Ore loobatatakino shumata ele soit-- negiligila: olourokino ninye-- nepurdupurd."
Matthew21:45 Ore pening' laidasak kituak o Ilfarisayoi kuna kitanyanyukieta enyena-- neyolou-- aajo eimaki ninje."
Matthew21:46 Neing'oru eneiko-- peibung' ninye; neurei ake siamin-- amu etadua ninye-- aajo era olayolounoni."
Matthew22:1 Nealu Yesus neitoki ajoki ninje too nkitanyanyukieta ejo:
Matthew22:2 Enyanyukie enkarsishu e shumata olkarsis obo oamaka olaiyoni lenye.
Matthew22:3 Neirriwaa laisyayak lenyena-- peipot looyeuni-- pepuonu enkiama; neitu eyeu nepuonu."
Matthew22:4 Neitoki airriwaa ilkulekai aisyayak nejo: Entiakiti looyeuni: Eng'orai-- aitobiraka ndai endaa ai-- ateyeng'a ilmong'i o ilkerra oopir-- eidipate pookin; ewotu enkiama!"
Matthew22:5 Neitu eshilu ninje ina nepuo wuejitin enye: obo enkuruma enye-- olekai enkinyang'a enye."
Matthew22:6 Ore lootelekutua neibung' laisyayak lenyena-- nesul near ninje metuata."
Matthew22:7 Ore pening' olkarsis ina-- negoro neirriwaa iltimito lenyena near kulo arak metuata-- nepej engang' enye."
Matthew22:8 Tekurum nejoki laisyayak lenyena: Eitobirakine enkiama-- kake eitu eaku too kulo looitobirakaki."
Matthew22:9 Onaa enjom rishat oo ngoitoi-- entorikutu pookin lidolidolo meetu enkiama."
Matthew22:10 Nepuku laisyayak aapuo ngoitoi neiturrur pookin lootadua-- iltorrok o sidan-- neborei enkiama too lomon."
Matthew22:11 Nejing' olkarsis-- peing'oraa lomon-- nedol oltung'ani obo tiatua lemeishopito olkarash lʼenkiama;"
Matthew22:12 nejoki ninye: Oljore-- kaji inkuna teni ijing'u iye ene-- miata olkarash lʼenkiama? Negira ninye."
Matthew22:13 Nejoki olkarsis laisyayak lenyena: Enteen nkejek o ngaik enyena-- entanang'akiti ninye atua enaimin e aulo; neaku ine enkishirata o eonyoto oo lala."
Matthew22:14 Amu eipotoki ilkumok-- negeluni ilkuti."
Matthew22:15 Nepuo ina kata Ilfarisayoi aanya enkigwena eneiko-- perresh ninye too rorei."
Matthew22:16 Neirriwaki ninye laiteng'enuok lenye te nebo o laisyayak le Herodes. Nejo ninje: Laiteng'enani-- kiyolo iye-- aajo ira oltung'ani lʼesipata nintorioo aiteng'enu engoitoi Engai tʼesipata nimishilu oltung'ani o obo niming'oraa entemet oltung'ani."
Matthew22:17 Akae-- tiaki yook-- ijo aa? Ke sidai-- teni eishori kaisar kodi arashu me?"
Matthew22:18 Ore peyolou Yesus olosek lenye nejo: Ndai laitusupatuok-- ainyo pikitemiteme?"
Matthew22:19 Entaduaki engosholai e kodi! Neaki ninye endenarion nabo.
Matthew22:20 Nejoki ninye ninje: Ken e ng'ai ena mua o ena sirata?
Matthew22:21 Nejoki ninje ninye: Ne kaisar. Nejoki ninye ninje: Akae-- enjoo kaisar en e kaisar-- o Engai en Engai!"
Matthew22:22 Ore pening' ninje kuna-- neiputukuny neing'ua ninye nepuo."
Matthew22:23 Nepuonu te ina olong' Sadukayoi enetii ninye-- oojo: metii empiunoto oo lootuata-- neikilikwan ninye--"
Matthew22:24 nejo: Laiteng'enani-- etejo opa Mose: Teni ee oltung'ani nemeata ninye nkera-- njeea olalashe lenye eng'oroyoni enye-- peiye etumoki ainyeyeki olalashe olmuate."
Matthew22:25 Etii opa atua yook lalashera oopishana. Neamisho ol elukunya nee; ore meata olmuate-- neing'uaiki olalashe eng'oroyoni enye;"
Matthew22:26 neijia si ninye oliare o oliokuni metabaiki pokira oopishana.
Matthew22:27 Ore tʼenkiting'oto oo pookin nee si ninye-- ina ng'oroyoni."
Matthew22:28 Akae-- keaku eng'oroyoni en e alo too kulo oopishana tʼengolong' empiunoto? Amu eama pookin ninye."
Matthew22:29 Nealiki Yesus nejoki ninje: Imanimanaana ndai-- amu miyololo sirat o engolon Engai."
Matthew22:30 Amu metii atua empiunoto looamisho o naayamari-- kake enyanyukie ninje ilmalaikan lʼEngai te shumata."
Matthew22:31 Eitu isomama ndai tiatua mbaak empiunoto oo lootuata enatiaka Engai ndai ejo:
Matthew22:32 Ara nanu Engai e Abraham o Engai e Isaak o Engai e Yakoob? Mera Engai Engai oo lootuata-- kake noo looishiu."
Matthew22:33 Ore pening' siamin nena-- neing'asia tʼeng'eno enye."
Matthew22:34 Ore pening' Ilfarisayoi-- aajo eitigira ninye Sadukayoi-- neiturrurro te nebo."
Matthew22:35 Ore obo too ninje lora olayoloni lʼesirata neikilikwan etem ninye nejo:
Matthew22:36 Laiteng'enani-- kaa kitanapata nara kitok tiatua nkitanapat?"
Matthew22:37 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Meata kata niminyor Olaitoriani-- Engai ino-- tʼoltau lino pookin o tʼolmumua lino pookin o tʼeng'eno ino pookin."
Matthew22:38 Ena enkitanapata elukunya nara kitok.
Matthew22:39 Ore eniare narisiore ninye ena: Meata kata niminyor oltung'ani lʼelatia ino anaa pinyor kion.
Matthew22:40 Kuna kitanapat are naaum nkitanapat pookin o layolounok.
Matthew22:41 Ore peiturrurro Ilfarisayoi-- neikilikwan Yesus ninje"
Matthew22:42 ejo: Ijojo aa tiatua mbaak e Kristos? Kera enkerai e ng'ai? Nejoki ninje ninye: Ne David.
Matthew22:43 Nejoki ninje: Kaji eiko teni eipot David ninye tʼolmumua Olaitoriani ejo:
Matthew22:44 Etiaka Olaitoriani Olaitoriani lai; Totona te tatene ai-- metabana napik ilmang'ati linono abori oo nkejek inono?"
Matthew22:45 Akae-- teni eipot David ninye Olaitoriani-- kaji eiko teni eaku enkerai enye?"
Matthew22:46 Nemetii oltung'ani oitewuo aikilikwana ninye ororei eiter te ina olong'.
Matthew23:1 Neirorie Yesus te ina kata siamin o laiteng'enuok lenyena
Matthew23:2 ejo: Etoni layolok lʼesirata o Ilfarisayoi tʼolorika le Mose.
Matthew23:3 Akae-- ore pookin naliki ninje ndai-- embung'a nintobiribiri nena-- kake emisuj nkitobirat enye. Amu eiro ake-- nemeitobir."
Matthew23:4 Amu een irridat ooiroshi lemenapai-- nedumaki ninje ronyi loo ltung'anak-- kake meyeu oopeny neing'unye ninje tʼolkimojino lenye."
Matthew23:5 Eitobir ake nkitobirat-- enye pookin-- peiye eing'oraa iltung'anak. Neitaa dapashi nkeenda enye esirata nepon too naipuko oo lkilani lenye."
Matthew23:6 Nenyor aatotoni too wuejitin elukunya tʼenedaareki o tiatua ngajijik Engai--"
Matthew23:7 o nkirorokinot tiatua singiraitin neipot iltung'anak ninje ilkituak.
Matthew23:8 Eminjo eipoti ndai ilkituak; amu etii olaiteng'enani obo ake too ndai-- nera Kristos-- nirara ndai pookin lalashera."
Matthew23:9 Nimimpotipoto oltung'ani o obo tʼenkop minyi linyi-- amu obo ake lora Minyi linyi-- olotii shumata."
Matthew23:10 Eminjo eipoti ndai laiteng'enak-- amu obo ake lora olaiteng'enani linyi-- nera Kristos."
Matthew23:11 Olora kitok too ndai-- njeaku olaisyayani linyi."
Matthew23:12 Ore pookin loitaa kion kitok-- neitadouni; ore oloitadou kion-- neitaai kitok."
Matthew23:13 Ee-- kake aiya-- ndai layolok lʼesirata o Ilfarisayoi-- ndai laitusupatuok-- lingenigene enkarsishu e shumata too ngomomi oo ltung'anak!"
Matthew23:14 Ee-- kake aiya-- ndai layolok lʼesirata o Ilfarisayoi-- ndai laitusupatuok-- lidaarere ngajijik oo ngolia niyetiyete sayat tʼenkitusupatuo! Onaa ipuopuo aang'amu enkigwena kitok nalang'."
Matthew23:15 Ee-- kake aiya-- ndai layolok lʼesirata o Ilfarisayoi-- ndai laitusupatuok-- limanimana olbalbal o olosho otoiyo-- peiye intaata oltung'ani obo olkalotuij ore peidip ataa-- nintaata-- peaku enkerai eweji enkima aigil are nelang' ndai oopeny."
Matthew23:16 Ee-- kake aiya-- ndai larikok modook-- ndai lijojo: Me o nyoo-- teni eiturujishore oltung'ani engaji sinyati; kake ore oltung'ani oiturujishore esahabu engaji sinyati-- eteena kion."
Matthew23:17 Ndai ilmoda naa modook! Amu kaa kitok: esahabu arashu ina aji sinyati nasinyaa esahabu?
Matthew23:18 o: Oloiturujishore olperere lʼenkidasare-- mera o nyoo; kake oloiturujishore enkidasare natii shumata enye-- eteena kion."
Matthew23:19 Ndai ilmoda naa modook! Amu kaa kitok: enkidasare arashu olperere lʼenkidasare losinyaa enkidasare?
Matthew23:20 Akae-- ore oloiturujishore olperere lʼenkidasare-- neiturujishore ninye o pookin natii shumata enye."
Matthew23:21 Ore oloiturujishore engaji sinyati-- neiturujishore ninye o olomanya atua."
Matthew23:22 Ore oloiturujishore shumata-- neiturujishore olorika lʼEngai o olotonie shumata enye."
Matthew23:23 Ee-- kake aiya-- ndai layolok lʼesirata o Ilfarisayoi-- ndai laitusupatuok-- linjoioio ematua e tomon olkujitai orropil o embeu naitorropil ndaikin-- nipalipala mbaak kituak tiatua nkitanapat-- eji enkigwena o eng'adunoto o enkirukoto! Meata kata nemeitobiri nena-- nemepali nkulie."
Matthew23:24 Ndai larikok modook-- lijiaiaia engojong'ani-- niijoojo endames."
Matthew23:25 Ee-- kake aiya-- ndai layolok lʼesirata o Ilfarisayoi-- ndai laitusupatuok-- lisujusuju oriong' oo nkwarun o motiok-- nebore atua enkisima o entootiki!"
Matthew23:26 Iye Olfarisayos modooni-- tang'asa suja atua enkwaru o emoti-- petum ataa sidai oriong' enye."
Matthew23:27 Ee-- kake aiya-- ndai layolok lʼesirata o Ilfarisayoi-- ndai laitusupatuok-- linyanyukiekie nkuraren naaelaki tʼenturoto-- nelioi te boo ekaja-- kake ore tiatua ebore loik loo lootuata o olduruki pookin!"
Matthew23:28 Neijia baiki ndai: iliolio te boo too ltung'anak anaa looata esupato-- kake ore tiatua eiganya ndai enkitusupatuo o ntorrok."
Matthew23:29 Ee-- kake aiya-- ndai layolok lʼesirata o Ilfarisayoi-- ndai laitusupatuok-- lishetishete nkuraren oo layolounok-- nikajikaja oo looata esupato--"
Matthew23:30 ijojo: Ten emutu kitii yook tʼenkata oo loopapa lang'-- anaata eitu king'arie ninje osarge loo layolounok!"
Matthew23:31 Nji injakenunu tiatua ndai oopeny-- ajo irara nkera oo kulo lootara layolounok."
Matthew23:32 Aiya-- enganya naa si ndai entemet oo loominyi linyi."
Matthew23:33 Ndai lasuria o embeu oo lasuria! Kaji inkoko teni ikwetikwete enkiminata enkima e gehena?
Matthew23:34 Onaa-- eng'orai-- airriwaki nanu ndai layolounok o lang'eni o layolok lʼesirata; niariara ilkulekai lenye metuata nisheshe-- niariara ilkulekai lenye too nkeenda tiatua ngajijik Engai inyi-- ninyalinyala ninje too ngang'itie--"
Matthew23:35 pebaiki ndai sargeta pookin supati ooibukokinote enkop-- eiter tʼosarge le Abel supat metabaiki osarge le Sakarias-- enkerai e Barakias-- litaara metua tʼempolos ewueji sinyati o olperere lʼenkidasare."
Matthew23:36 Japa-- aliki ndai-- ajo ebaiki kuna pookin ena kishon."
Matthew23:37 Oi Yerusalem-- Yerusalem-- niar layolounok metuata ninang' too soito likirriwakaki! Kaigil aja atayeuo naiturrur nkera inono anaa peiturrur enkikusieki te nebo nkera enyena tiabori oo naipuko-- neitu iyeuu ndai!"
Matthew23:38 Eng'orai-- eing'uaikini ndai engaji inyi-- metii toki."
Matthew23:39 Amu aliki ndai: Mikintokiki aadol nanu tukul eiter taata-- metabana nipuopuo aajo: Njeitadarari ololotu tʼengarna Olaitoriani."
Matthew24:1 Nepuku Yesus tʼengaji sinyati nelo-- nepuonu laiteng'enuok lenyena aaitadol ninye enjetunoto engaji sinyati."
Matthew24:2 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninje: Midolidolo kuna pookin? Japa-- aliki ndai: Meleku tene osoit te shumata olekai soit lemerratanyuni."
Matthew24:3 Ore peton tʼOldonyo loo loirienito-- nepuonu laiteng'enuok enetii ninye tʼenkilepata nejo: Tiaki yook-- kanu eaku kuna? Ainyo olponoto lilotunye o lʼenkiting'oto olmaa?"
Matthew24:4 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninje: Eng'orai-- pemeitapong'oo ndai oltung'ani."
Matthew24:5 Amu epuo aapuonu ilkumok tʼengarna ai nejo: Ara nanu Kristos-- nepuo aalej ilkumok."
Matthew24:6 Nipuopuo aaning' njorin o ririn loo njorin; eng'orai-- pemiruturutu. Amu meata kata nemeaku nona pookin-- kake eton eitu ebau enkiting'oto."
Matthew24:7 Amu edumunye olorere aarare olekai orere o enkarsishu nabo engai arsishu-- nepuo aaku lameitin o nkeaitin o nkikirikirat enkop too wuejitin o wuejitin."
Matthew24:8 Nera nona pookin enkiterata oo sinaitin.
Matthew24:9 Ore te ina kata nepuo aaitarasaki ndai atua enkisiloto-- nepuo aar ndai entuata. Nipuopuo aaku looibaini tiatua loreren pookin t'olbae lʼengarna ai."
Matthew24:10 Nepuo aarika ilkumok neikitalaro oopeny neibaro oopeny.
Matthew24:11 Nepuo aainyototo layolounok kumok lʼelejare nepuo aaiminye ilkumok.
Matthew24:12 Tiaraki napona ntorrok-- nelairobiju enyorrata oo lkumok."
Matthew24:13 Kake olong'iri metabaiki enkiting'oto-- ninye lolapok."
Matthew24:14 Neinosuni kulo omon lʼeng'ida o lʼenkarsishu tiatua olmaa pookin-- peaku enjakenishu too loreren pookin-- tekurum nelotu enkiting'oto."
Matthew24:15 Teni ipuopuo aadol entorroni erruoroto nairoro olayolounoni Daniel-- eitashe tʼewueji sinyati-- oloisoma-- njeyolou!"
Matthew24:16 Ore lootii Yudaya-- njekwetiki te ina kata ildonyo;"
Matthew24:17 oloti keper aji-- njoo meitoki adou-- peau natii atua engaji enye;"
Matthew24:18 ore olotii atua enkuruma-- njoo merrinyo-- peau ilkilani lenyena."
Matthew24:19 Ee-- kake aiya-- naamena o naaitanakisho too nona olong'i!"
Matthew24:20 Entasaishoto-- pemeaku enkwetata inyi tʼenkata oloirujuruj arashu tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki."
Matthew24:21 Amu elaaku te ina kata osina kitok leitu eaku neba tʼenkiterata olmaa metabaiki taata-- nemeitoki aaku tukul."
Matthew24:22 Naa ten emutu meitadorropi nona olong'i-- anaata mepoku oltung'ani o obo; kake epuoi aaitadorropu nona olong'i tʼolbae loo lootegeluaki."
Matthew24:23 Teni elajoki ndai te ina kata oltung'ani: Eng'orai-- etii Kristos ene! arashu: idye! — emiruk."
Matthew24:24 Amu epuo aainyototo ilkristoi lʼelejare o layolounok lʼelejare kumok-- neitobir ilponot kituak o nkiputukunyot-- pepuoi aaitapong'oo baiki lootegeluaki-- teni eidimu."
Matthew24:25 Eng'orai-- aitera aliki ndai."
Matthew24:26 Akae-- teni ejoki ninje ndai: Eng'orai-- etii ang'ata! emipuku; — eng'orai-- etii aji! emiruk."
Matthew24:27 Amu neijia anaa enkiwang'ata naing'ua enkilepunoto nelioi tʼendoiyoroto-- neijia elaaku elotunoto Enkerai oltung'ani;"
Matthew24:28 amu ewueji pookin netii empopong'-- neiturrurrokino ilmotonyi."
Matthew24:29 Ore pesioki aaidipai sinaitin lo nona olong'i-- neopokino engolong' enaimin nemeitoki ailang'isho olapa-- nesulunye lakir te shumata-- neing'unung'un ngoloni e shumata."
Matthew24:30 Nelalioi te ina kata olponoto lʼEngerai oltung'ani te shumata. Nepuo aaishir tʼolbae lʼosina njomito pookin olmaa-- nepuo aadol Enkerai oltung'ani elotu te shumata erukenya e shumata tʼengolon o tʼenkitook kitok."
Matthew24:31 Nelairriwaa ninye ilmalaikan lenyena tʼoltoilo kitok lʼesekegwa-- nepuo aaiturrur ninje lootegeluaki lenyena aaitung'ua ilkutat ong'wan-- eiter tematua nabo metabaiki engai matua e shumata."
Matthew24:32 Enteng'enuoto enkitanyanyukiet tʼolng'aboli: teni enanau olng'osilai lenye nedanyu mbenek-- niyolouu-- aajo etaana enkata olodalu."
Matthew24:33 Neija si ndai-- teni idolidolo kuna pookin-- entayolou-- aajo etii enetaana metabaiki kutukaji."
Matthew24:34 Japa-- aliki ndai: Memuta ena kishon-- metabana neaku kuna pookin."
Matthew24:35 Epuo aamuta shumata o enkop-- kake mepuo aamuta rorei lainei tukul."
Matthew24:36 Nemetii oloyolo ina olong' o ina saa-- baiki ilmalaikan le shumata o Oinoti-- neme Papa lai ake openy."
Matthew24:37 Kake neijia anaa petaa too ngolong'i e Noa-- neijia elaaku elotunoto Enkerai oltung'ani."
Matthew24:38 Amu neijia anaa petaa ninje too nona olong'i-- eton eitu eaku engare kitok: edaa-- neokisho-- neamisho-- neamari-- metabaiki ena olong' natijing'ie Noa engalawa;"
Matthew24:39 neitu eshilu ninje-- metabana nelotu engare nea pookin-- — neijia eaku baiki elotunoto Enkerai oltung'ani."
Matthew24:40 Nelaaku etii aare enkuruma-- nepuoi aang'amu obo-- neing'uari olekai;"
Matthew24:41 neituutisho are eneituutishoreki-- nepuoi aang'amu nabo-- neing'uari engai."
Matthew24:42 Akae-- enjololoto-- amu miyololo-- kaa kata elalotu Olaitoriani linyi."
Matthew24:43 Kake entayolou ena: Ten emutu eyolo olopeny engaji enkata nalotunye olapurroni-- anaata eishololo nemeisho engaji enye metuudi."
Matthew24:44 Onaa entobirakinoto si ndai-- amu elalotu Enkerai oltung'ani tʼenkata nimijojo."
Matthew24:45 Akae-- kang'ai lora olaisyayani airukoni naa ng'en-- otipika olaitoriani lenye shumata enkisyayare enye-- peisho kulekai aisyayak endaa tʼenkata enye?"
Matthew24:46 Tesh ele aisyayani loinepu olaitoriani lenye eiko nji-- teni elotu."
Matthew24:47 Japa-- aliki ndai-- Elapik ninye shumata oo masaa enyena pookin."
Matthew24:48 Kake ore olaisyayani torrono olojo tʼoltau lenye: Mesioku olaitoriani lai!
Matthew24:49 neiter aar lalashera lenyena-- nenya neokisho te nebo o lamerak:"
Matthew24:50 nelotu olaitoriani lʼele aisyayani tʼengolong' nemeanyunye o tʼesaa nemeyolo--"
Matthew24:51 ne-dung'udung' too nkeenda osesen lenye neisho earata enye te nebo o laitusupatuok; neaku ina alo enkishirata o eonyoto oo lala.
Matthew25:1 Nelanyanyukiei enkarsishu e shumata ntoiye tomon naatudumutua taai enye-- nepuku aapuo aanang'are osanja."
Matthew25:2 Kake imiet moda too ninje-- naa ng'eni imiet."
Matthew25:3 Nedumu kuna moda taai enye neitu eshoroo eilata te nebo o ninje.
Matthew25:4 Kake ore kuna ng'eni neshoroo eilata too ltuleta lenye te nebo o taai enye.
Matthew25:5 Ore peimutie osanja-- neimug pookin neirura."
Matthew25:6 Ore tʼempolos enkiarie neaku olodoo: Eng'orai-- elotu osanja-- entupukutu aapuo aanang'are ninye!"
Matthew25:7 Neinyototo nabokata kuna toiye pookin neitobir taai enye.
Matthew25:8 Nejoki kuna moda nena ng'eni: Enjoo yook ematua eilata inyi-- amu ee taai ang'."
Matthew25:9 Kake nealiki kuna ng'eni ninje nejo: Me neijia-- pemekilau yook o ndai; enaikash-- embung'a engoitoi aapuo enetii lamirak-- pinyang'ung'u oopeny."
Matthew25:10 Ore peidip aashom ninje-- peinyang'u-- nelotu osanja; ore naaitobirakinote nejing' te nebo o ninye enkiama-- neigeni kutukaji."
Matthew25:11 Ore tekurum nepuonu si ninje kuna kulie toiye nejo: Laitoriani-- laitoriani-- tabolu yook!"
Matthew25:12 Kake nealiki ninye nejo: Japa-- aliki ndai: Mayolo nanu ndai."
Matthew25:13 Onaa enjololoto! amu miyololo engolong' arashu esaa nalotu Enkerai oltung'ani.
Matthew25:14 Amu neijia anaa peipot oltung'ani oyeu nelo olekai osho loo nkwapi laisyayak lenyena-- neshum too ninje masaa enyena--"
Matthew25:15 neisho obo talanta imiet-- olekai talanta are-- oliokuni entalanton nabo-- oltung'ani pookin anaa peidim ninye-- nelo olekai osho."
Matthew25:16 Ore olotang'amua talanta imiet-- neibung' engoitoi neitobirishore ninje netumie nkulie talanta imiet."
Matthew25:17 Neiko neijia ake si ninye oloata are-- netumie nkulie are endupoto."
Matthew25:18 Ore ele otang'amua nabo-- nelo ninye-- neturoki enkop neshum ngoshola olaitoriani lenye."
Matthew25:19 Ore peishunye enkata kitok-- nelotu olaitoriani loo kulo aisyayak neikenishore ninje."
Matthew25:20 Nelotu ele lotang'amua talanta imiet-- neaunye nkulie talanta imiet-- nejo: Laitoriani-- itushuma te nanu talanta imiet-- ng'orai-- ainoto too ninje endupoto oo nkulie talanta imiet."
Matthew25:21 Nejoki olaitoriani lenye ninye: Ee-- laisyayani sidai naa airukoni-- itaa supat to nkuti-- ayeu naapik iye-- pintore nkumok; tijing'a atua eng'ida Olaitoriani lino!"
Matthew25:22 Nelotu si ninye ele lotang'amua talanta are nejo: Laitoriani-- itushuma te nanu talanta are; ng'orai-- ainoto too ninje endupoto oo nkulie talanta are."
Matthew25:23 Nejoki olaitoriani lenye ninye: Ee-- laisyayani sidai naa airukoni-- itaa supat too nkuti-- ayeu naapik iye-- pintore nkumok; tijing'a atua eng'ida olaitoriani lino!"
Matthew25:24 Nelotu si ninye-- ele otang'amua entalanton nabo-- nejo: Laitoriani-- aatayolo iye-- ajo ira oltung'ani ogol oshoke-- nisambu neitu iun-- ninturrur neitu isuaia;"
Matthew25:25 naureishoi-- nalo nashum entalanton ino tʼenkop. Ng'orai-- nko enino."
Matthew25:26 Nealiki olaitoriani lenye nejoki: Iye laisyayani torrono nishal! itayolo-- ajo aisambu-- eitu aun-- naiturrur-- eitu aisuaia;"
Matthew25:27 akae-- anaata itushuma ngoshola ainei too laitaalak loo ngoshola-- ore palotu nanu-- anaata ainoto nanu enara enai o endupoto enye."
Matthew25:28 Onaa entoorutu ninye entalanton enye-- enjoo oloata talanta tomon."
Matthew25:29 Amu ore pookin looata-- neishori ninye-- petum nkumok; ore pookin lemeata-- neoruni baiki ina naata."
Matthew25:30 Entanang'akiti olaisyayani lemeaku atua enaimin e aulo; neaku inalo enkishirata o eonyoto oo lala.
Matthew25:31 Teni elalotu Enkerai oltung'ani tʼenkitook enye o ilmalaikan sinyat pookin te nebo o ninye-- nelaton te ina kata tʼolorika lʼenkitook enye--"
Matthew25:32 neiturrurro loreren pookin tʼengomom enye; nerish ninye ninje tʼempolos anaa olairritani orish nkerra o ilkerra.
Matthew25:33 Nearaki nkerra ematua e tatene enye o ilkerra kedyanye.
Matthew25:34 Ore peidipai-- nejoki olkarsis kulo lootii tatene enye: Ewotu ndai-- lootamayana Papa lai-- entujung'u enkarsishu naitobirakaki ndai tʼenkiterata olmaa!"
Matthew25:35 Amu aainosa olamei-- nikinjosho endaa; ainoto enkure-- nikintookioko; ataa olomoni-- nikintoomonimono;"
Matthew25:36 ashomo neijia-- nikinjopishopo; atamoiya-- nikibaikiki; aateenaki-- nipuonunu enatii."
Matthew25:37 Nealiki te ina kata kulo supati ninye nejo: Laitoriani-- kanu kitadua iye iata olamei-- nikintoti iye? arashu iata enkure-- nikintook iye?"
Matthew25:38 Kanu kitadua iye ira olomoni-- nikintoomon iye? arashu ishomo neijia-- nikinjop iye?"
Matthew25:39 Kanu kitadua iye itamoiya arashu kiteenaki-- nikipuonu enitii iye?"
Matthew25:40 Nealiki olkarsis nejoki ninje: Japa-- aliki ndai: Ore enitaasakitia obo tiatua kulo alashera lainei kutiti-- kitaasakitia nanu."
Matthew25:41 Ore peidip-- nejoki si ninje lootii kedyanye: Entung'aiyoki nanu-- ndai lootediaki-- enjom atua enkima nememuta-- naitobirakaki satan o ilmalaikan lenyena!"
Matthew25:42 Amu aainosa olamei-- neitu kinjosho endaa; natum enkure-- neitu kintookioko;"
Matthew25:43 ataa olomoni-- neitu kintoomonimono; ashomo neijia-- neitu kinjopishopo; atamoiya naaeni-- neitu kibaikiki."
Matthew25:44 Nepuo aalu ake si ninje nejo: Laitoriani-- kanu kitadua iye iata olamei arashu enkure arashu ira olomoni arashu ishomo neijia arashu itamoiya arashu kiteenaki-- neitu kisyayaki iye?"
Matthew25:45 Nealiki si ninye ninje nejo: Japa-- aliki ndai: Ore eneitu iasakiki obo tiatua kulo loora kutiti-- neitu kiasakiki si nanu."
Matthew25:46 Nepuo kulo atua emion nemeiting'-- kake supati atua empuan nemeiting'."
Matthew26:1 Neaku ore peidip Yesus kulo rorei pookin-- nejoki ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena:"
Matthew26:2 Iyololo-- aajo ore peishunye ngolong'i are-- neaku pasaka; nepuoi aaitarasaa Enkerai oltung'ani-- peoshokini esalaba."
Matthew26:3 Nepuo aaiturrurro te ina kata laidasak kituak o layolok lʼesirata o laigwenak lʼolorere tʼengaji olaidasani kitok oji Kayafas--"
Matthew26:4 neigwena te nebo-- peiye eibung' Yesus tʼolosek near ninye metua."
Matthew26:5 Etejo ninje ake: Me tʼenkata oo ngolong'i kituak-- pemeaku enkiposhai tiatua olorere!"
Matthew26:6 Ore etii Yesus te Betania-- atua engaji e Simon loata enkea oo lbolot--"
Matthew26:7 nenyikaki ninye eng'oroyoni nabo-- naata oltulet lʼeilata narropil nagol enkinyang'a-- nejiaki ninye elukunya-- eton edaa."
Matthew26:8 Ore pedol laiteng'enuok lenyena ina-- neibai nejo: Ken e nyoo ena kiminata?"
Matthew26:9 Amu anaata etimiraki ena ilata too ngoshola kumok neishori laisinak.
Matthew26:10 Ore peyolou Yesus ina-- nejoki ninje: Ainyo pinosiesie osina eng'oroyoni?"
Matthew26:11 Etii laisinak atua ndai ngolong'i pookin-- kake mikiatata nanu ngolong'i pookin."
Matthew26:12 Ore paatubukoko ninye ena ilata osesen lai-- naaitobiraki enukare ai."
Matthew26:13 Japa-- aliki ndai-- ore tʼewueji pookin neinosuni kulo omon lʼeng'ida-- neinosuni baiki nedamuni enaitobira ninye."
Matthew26:14 Nelo te ina kata obo too lelo tomon o are-- oji Yudas Iskariotes-- enetii laidasak kituak--"
Matthew26:15 nejo: Kainyo iyeuu nikinjosho-- paitarasaki ndai ilo? Ayeu naitarasaki ninye ndai. Nedung'oki ninye ngoshola osom."
Matthew26:16 Neiter aing'oru te ina kata erishata naitarasarie ninye.
Matthew26:17 Ore tʼengolong' elukunya oo lmkaten lemeisiijo nepuonu laiteng'enuok enetii Yesus nejoki ninye: Kaji iyeu nikintobirakinye endaata e pasaka?
Matthew26:18 Nejo ninye: Enjom engang' enetii ng'ania-- entiakiti ninye: Ejo Olaiteng'enani: Etaana enkata ai; ayeu naitaa pasaka tʼengaji ino te nebo o laiteng'enuok lainei."
Matthew26:19 Neiko laiteng'enuok neijia anaa peitanapa Yesus ninje-- neitobir pasaka."
Matthew26:20 Ore peaku teipa-- neton te nebo o kulo aiteng'enuok tomono are."
Matthew26:21 Ore edaa ninje-- nejo: Aalikioo obo too ndai."
Matthew26:22 Neilish ninje naleng'-- neiter oltung'ani pookin ajoki ninye: Ke nanu-- Laitoriani?"
Matthew26:23 Nealu ninye nejo: Ore ele likiriamaki endaa tʼengirra-- ninye laalo alikioo."
Matthew26:24 Elo Enkerai oltung'ani anaa petisirakaki ninye; ee-- kake aiya ele tung'ani lolaitarasaa Engerai oltung'ani! Eikash-- ten emutu eitu eiuni ele tung'ani."
Matthew26:25 Nealu Yudas otolikioiye ninye nejo: Ke nanu-- Laiteng'enani? Nejoki ninye: Itejo iye."
Matthew26:26 Ore einosita endaa-- neibung' Yesus olmkate-- nemayan nebelibel neisho laiteng'enuok lenyena nejo: Enkoito-- entaam; nera ele osesen lai."
Matthew26:27 Neibung' enkwaru nejo ashe-- neisho ninje nejo: Entookie pookin ena;"
Matthew26:28 amu era ele osarge lai lʼosotua ng'ejuk-- oibukorieki ilkumok-- peaku enkitaunoto oo nkitarruot."
Matthew26:29 Kake aliki ndai: Maitoki aok tukul eiter taata te ina ishoi oo nkeek olmarua metabaiki ina olong' naok eng'ejuk te nebo o ndai tiatua enkarsishu e Papa lai.
Matthew26:30 Ore peidip aaitadarai-- nepuku boo-- nepuo Oldonyo loo loirienito."
Matthew26:31 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Kipuopuo aarikare ndai pookin tʼena kiarie; amu etisiraki: Alaar olairritani-- neisardak enjoo oo ntare."
Matthew26:32 Kake ore paidip atopiu-- naaiturukie ndai alo Galilaya."
Matthew26:33 Nealiki Petros nejoki ninye: Teni kirikare ilkulekai pookin-- namaarikare nanu tukul."
Matthew26:34 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Japa-- aaliki iye: Ore tʼena kiarie-- eton eitu eorito olkikusieki-- nikimiki iye kat uni."
Matthew26:35 Nejoki Petros ninye: Baiki teni ae te nebo o iye-- maamiki iye. Nejo laiteng'enuok pookin neijia."
Matthew26:36 Nelotu Yesus te nebo o ninje metabaiki enkuruma naji Getsemane nejoki laiteng'enuok lenyena: Entotoni tene-- palo idyalo asaisho."
Matthew26:37 Nerik ninye Petros o nkera are e Sebedayos neiter atum enkilishoto neisuuto.
Matthew26:38 Nejoki Yesus ninje te ina kata: Eata olmumua lai enkilishoto metabaiki enkea; entotoni tene-- enjololoto te nebo o nanu!"
Matthew26:39 Nenyikaa peno-- nebatata aijululo nesaisho ejo: Papa lai-- teni eaku-- njaalusoo ena kwaru; kake me neijia anaa payeu nanu-- njeaku anaa piyeu iye!"
Matthew26:40 Nelotu enetii laiteng'enuok neinepu-- eirurate-- nejoki Petros: Ke nji miatata engolon ninjololorere te nebo o nanu esaa nabo?"
Matthew26:41 Enjololoto-- entasaishoto-- pemijing'ijing'i atua enkitasuroto! Eidipakine Olmumua-- kake eshal osesen."
Matthew26:42 Neitoki alo engaigil e are nesaisho nejo: Papa lai-- teni meaku-- paalusoo ena kwaru-- pamaok ninye-- njeaku eyeunoto ino!"
Matthew26:43 Nelotu neinepu ninje-- einyaakitia aairura-- amu eiroshiutuo ngonyek enye."
Matthew26:44 Neitoki aing'ua ninje nelo nesaisho en e uni nelimu kulo rorei ake.
Matthew26:45 Tekurum nelotu enetii laiteng'enuok lenyena nejoki ninje: Erraga tekurum-- eeng'ieng'ata! Eng'orai-- etabaua enkata-- peitarasakini Enkerai oltung'ani atua ngaik oo laitarruok."
Matthew26:46 Enyoito-- maapeti! Eng'orai-- etinyikua olaaitarasaa."
Matthew26:47 Ore epon eirorita-- ng'orai-- nelotu Yudas-- obo too kulo tomon o are-- te nebo o esiamu kitok-- neata lalema o siaren-- eing'ua enetii laidasak kituak o laigwenak lʼolorere."
Matthew26:48 Eidipa aishoo olaitarasaroni lenye ninje olponoto nejo: Ore olang'utut-- ninye ilo; embung'a ninye!"
Matthew26:49 Nelotu nabokata enetii Yesus nejo: Supai-- Laiteng'enani! neng'utut ninye."
Matthew26:50 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Oljore-- kainyo ieunye? Nepuonu neaki Yesus ngaik neibung' ninye."
Matthew26:51 Naa ng'orai-- obo too kulo lootaboitare Yesus-- neitorioo engaina enye neshitu olalem lenye neosh olaisyayani lʼolaidasani kitok adung'u ninye enkiyok."
Matthew26:52 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Torrinyoki olalem lino ewueji enye! amu ore oltung'ani pookin loibung' olalem-- neimin tʼolalem."
Matthew26:53 Arashu ijo iye-- ajo maidim atasaya Papa lai-- paairriwaki ninye iltimito tomon o are loo lmalaikan?"
Matthew26:54 Kaji eiko peidipai naa esirata-- ajo neijia meata kata nemeaku?"
Matthew26:55 Ore te ina kata nejoki Yesus nena siamin: Itupukutuo ndai too lalema o siaren ninyanyukiekie anaa iltung'anak loomirita olaisimani-- pikimbung'ubung'u. O patotona too ngolong'i pookin tiatua engaji sinyati neiteng'enisho-- neitu kimbung'ubung'u."
Matthew26:56 Kake etaa kuna pookin-- peiye ebaia sirat o layolounok. Neing'ua te ina kata laiteng'enuok pookin ninye aailanyisho."
Matthew26:57 Ore kulo looibung'a Yesus-- nerik enetii olaidasani kitok-- Kayafas-- enetutumore layolok lʼesirata o laigwenak."
Matthew26:58 Nesujita Petros ninye tʼenelakwa metabaiki engang' olaidasani kitok-- nejing' atua neton te nebo o laisyayak pedol enkiting'oto."
Matthew26:59 Neing'oraki laidasak kituak o enkigwena pookin Yesus enjakenishu elejare-- peiye ear ninye metua--"
Matthew26:60 neitu etum o nyoo. Tekurum nepuonu iljaken aare lʼelejare
Matthew26:61 nejo: Etejo ele: Aidim atigila ena aji sinyati-- naitoki ashet ninye too ngolong'i uni--"
Matthew26:62 Neinyototo olaidasani kitok nejoki ninye: Mialu ororei kainyo kinjakenoki kulo?
Matthew26:63 Negira Yesus. Nealiki olaidasani kitok ninye nejoki: Aaiturujaki iye tʼEngai naishiu-- piliki yook-- ten ake ira iye Kristos-- Oinoti lʼEngai."
Matthew26:64 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Itejo iye. Kake aaliki iye: Ore eiter taata nipuopuo aadol Enkerai oltung'ani eton te tatene Engolon-- elotu tʼerukenya e shumata."
Matthew26:65 Nepolos te ina kata olaidasani kitok ilkilani lenyena nejo: Etamoro Engai! Kainyo pikintoki aayeu niking'oru iljaken? Eng'orai-- itoning'o taata nji emoroto enye."
Matthew26:66 Ijojo aa? Nealu ninje nejo: Meata kata nemee!
Matthew26:67 Nenotaki ninje ngamulak engomom enye-- near ninye too ntinan-- near kulekai ninye too ndapi"
Matthew26:68 nejo: Tiaki yook-- iye Kristos-- kang'ai likitaara?"
Matthew26:69 Neton Petros ake te boo engaji: nelotu enetii ninye engaisyayani nabo nejo: Itii si iye e nebo o Yesus le Galilaya.
Matthew26:70 Kake nemiki ninye too ngomomi pookin nejo: Mayolo enijoito.
Matthew26:71 Ore pepuku nebaiki kishomi-- nedol engai aisyayani ninye nejoki kulo ootii: Etii opa ele e nebo o Yesus le Nasaret."
Matthew26:72 Neitoki amiki tʼenkiturujata: Mayolo nanu ele tung'ani.
Matthew26:73 Ore tʼenkiti kata nepuonu looitashe te ine nejoki Petros: Esipa-- ira si iye obo lenye-- amu kilimu enkiroroto ino."
Matthew26:74 Neiter ninye adek kion neituruj-- ajo: Mayolo nanu ele tung'ani. Neorito nabokata olkikusieki."
Matthew26:75 Nedamu Petros ilo rorei le Yesus lotiaka ninye: Ore eton eitu eorito olkikusieki-- nikilamiki aigil uni-- nelo aulo neishir tʼemion."
Matthew27:1 Ore pekenyu-- neigwena laidasak kituak o laigwenak lʼolorere tʼolbae le Yesus-- petum aataar metua."
Matthew27:2 Neen ninje ninye nerik neitarasaki olkitok lʼolosho Pontios Pilatos.
Matthew27:3 Ore pedol Yudas oitarasaiye ninye-- ajo eidipaki aaigwenaki-- neirridu ninye entorroni enye-- nerrinyoki laidasak kituak o laigwenak kuna dung'ot oo ngoshola"
Matthew27:4 nejo: Aitarruoiye-- tiaraki natolikioiye osarge lemeata eleyata. Nejo ninje: Akae-- naa ainyo naatii ninje yook? Ng'orai-- eninko openy!"
Matthew27:5 Nenang'aki ninye kuna dung'ot oo ngoshola atua engaji sinyati nedumunye nelo negor kion.
Matthew27:6 Nedumu laidasak kituak kuna dung'ot oo ngoshola nejo: Menare-- teni kipik nena atua osanduku lʼEngai; amu era enkinyang'a osarge."
Matthew27:7 Neigwena neinyang'u too ninje enkuruma olaitobirani loo motiok-- penukieki lomon."
Matthew27:8 Onaa eipoti ena kuruma enkuruma osarge oo taata.
Matthew27:9 Nebaia enairoro olayolounoni Yeremiya ejo: Eibung'a ninje ndung'ot osom oo ngoshola nara enkinyang'a olotimiraki loinvang'utua ninje too nkera Israel--"
Matthew27:10 neishooio tʼenkuruma olaitobirani loo motiok anaa paaitanapa Olaitoriani.
Matthew27:11 Neitashe Yesus tʼengomom olkitok lʼolosho neikilikwan olkitok lʼolosho ninye nejo: Ira iye olkarsis loo Yudayoi? Nejoki Yesus ninye: Itejo iye.
Matthew27:12 Ore peitang'or laidasak kituak o laigwenak ninye-- neitu ealu ororei."
Matthew27:13 Nejoki Pilatos ninye: mining'ito-- ke mbaak aja kintang'orie ninje?"
Matthew27:14 Neitu ealiki ninye ororei o obo neiputukuny baiki olkitok lʼolosho naleng'.
Matthew27:15 Ore tʼenkata oo ngolong'i kituak neata olkitok lʼolosho orregie-- pelaaki olorere obo loena lotayeutuo ninje."
Matthew27:16 Neata ake te ina kata oloena oyoloi oji Barabas.
Matthew27:17 Akae-- ore peiturrurro ninje-- nejoki Pilatos ninje: Kalo iyeuu nalaaki ndai? Barabas arashu Yesus oipoti Kristos?"
Matthew27:18 Amu etayolo-- ajo eitarasutua ninye tʼengilata e tau."
Matthew27:19 Ore peton ninye tʼolorika lʼenkigwena-- neirriwaki eng'oroyoni enye embae nejo: Miasaki toki ilo loata esupato; amu aaitamioki too nkumok taata tiatua enkidetidetata tʼolbae lenye."
Matthew27:20 Neisis laidasak kituak o laigwenak olorere-- peyeu ninje Barabas neiminye Yesus"
Matthew27:21 Nealu olkitok lʼolosho nejoki ninje: Kalo iyeuu-- palaaki ndai too kulo pokira are? Nejo ninje: Barabas!"
Matthew27:22 Nejoki Pilatos ninje: Akae-- kaji aikunaki Yesus loipoti Kristos? Nejo ninje pookin: Njoo eoshokini esalaba!"
Matthew27:23 Nejo olkitok lʼolosho: Kaa torroni eitobira ninye? Nepon ninje naleng' aapaa iltoiloi ejo: Njoo eoshokini esalaba!
Matthew27:24 Ore pedol Pilatos-- ajo meidim o nyoo-- epona ake oloilepilep-- neibung' engare neisuj ngaik tʼengomom olorere nejo: Maata nanu eng'oki tʼosarge lʼele tung'ani lora supat; eng'orai ndai oopeny!"
Matthew27:25 Nealu olorere pookin nejo: Njelotu osarge lenye shumata ang' o shumata oo nkera ang'!
Matthew27:26 Nelaaki te ina kata ninje Barabas; ore peidip ataara Yesus too nkeenda-- neitarasaa ninye-- petumi aatooshoki esalaba."
Matthew27:27 Nerik isikerin lʼolkitok Yesus atua engaji enkigwena-- neitasheiki ninye oltim olulung'a--"
Matthew27:28 neitai ninye ilkilani neishopoki olkila odo--"
Matthew27:29 neoi olmarisian loo lkikarreta neishopoki elukunya enye neitarasaki ninye eng'udi olmoloi engaina enye e tatene negil kung' tʼengomom enye nekweniye ninye nejo: Supai-- lekarsis loo Yudayoi!"
Matthew27:30 Nenotaki ninye ngamulak neoru eng'udi olmoloi nearie ninye elukunya.
Matthew27:31 Ore peidip ninje aatakweniye ninye-- neitai ilo kila neishopoki ninye ilkilani lenyena nerik-- peoshoki esalaba."
Matthew27:32 Ore peidip aatupukutu-- netumore ninje oltung'ani obo le Kirene oji engarna enye Simon; neitanap ilo tʼengolon-- penap esalaba enye."
Matthew27:33 Ore pebaia ewueji naji Golgota-- nera enkitaalata enye: Emborbor--"
Matthew27:34 neisho ninje ninye engare naitiming'anisho neshulare olodua; ore peinyorrinyor-- neitu eyeu neok."
Matthew27:35 Ore peidip ninje aatooshokiti ninye esalaba-- neor ninje ilkilani lenyena neosh olenkukuo-- peiye ebaia enairoro olayolounoni: Etoorikinote ilkilani lainei tʼempolos enye neosh olenkukuo tʼolbae lʼolkarash lai."
Matthew27:36 Netoni aarrip ninye te ina alo.
Matthew27:37 Nepik shumata elukunya enye enkitang'oroto enye natisiraki: Era ele Yesus-- olkarsis loo Yudayoi."
Matthew27:38 Neoshokini te ine laisimak aare esalaba te nebo o ninye-- obo te tatene o olekai te kedyanye."
Matthew27:39 Ore kulo looimita engoitoi nemor ninye eipiripir lukuny enye--"
Matthew27:40 nejo: Iye logil engaji Engai nintoki ashet ninye too ngolong'i uni-- ntopua kion! Teni ira Oinoti lʼEngai-- tadou tʼesalaba!"
Matthew27:41 Neiko si ninje neijia-- laidasak kituak-- nekweniye ninye te nebo o layolok lʼesirata o laigwenak nejo:"
Matthew27:42 Eitopua kulekai nemeidim aitopua kion. Teni era ninye olkarsis le Israel-- njedou taata tʼesalaba-- pikiruk si yook ninye."
Matthew27:43 Eting'idare ninye Engai; njeitopok taata-- teni enyor ninye; amu etejo ninye: Ara nanu Oinoti lʼEngai."
Matthew27:44 Etamoro si ninje laisimak ootooshokoki esalaba te nebo o ninye.
Matthew27:45 Ore eiter te saa ile nejing' enaimin shumata enkop pookin metabaiki saa enturuj.
Matthew27:46 Ore te saa enturuj nedar Yesus tʼoltoilo lʼengolon nejo: Eli-- Eli-- lamaa asabtani? eji: Engai ai-- Engai ai-- ainyo pikitung'aiye?"
Matthew27:47 Ore kulekai looitashe te ine nening' nejo: Eipot Eliya.
Matthew27:48 Nekwet nabokata obo lenye neibung' enjutet neigany ninye engare naitiming'anisho nepik shumata eng'udi olmoloi neitook ninye.
Matthew27:49 Nejo ake kulekai: Tapala-- maing'orai-- ten ake elotu Eliya aitopok ninye."
Matthew27:50 Ore peidip Yesus ataapai kat are oltoilo tʼengolon-- nedung'o tau."
Matthew27:51 Naa ng'orai-- nepolosa olkarash lʼengaji sinyati matuan are-- eiter te shumata metabaiki enkop."
Matthew27:52 Neikirikira enkop nedanya soito kituak-- nebolo nkuraren nepuku seseni kumok loo sinyat ooirura;"
Matthew27:53 ore peidip aatupukutu-- eidipe empiunoto enye-- nejing' engang' sinyati nelioi too lkumok."
Matthew27:54 Ore pedol olkitok loo sikerin te nebo o lootaboitare ninye-- erripito Yesus-- enkikirikirata enkop o mbaak naataa-- neureishoi naleng' nejo: Esipa-- era ele tung'ani Oinoti lʼEngai!"
Matthew27:55 Netii ng'oroyok kumok naaing'oraitie t'enelakwa-- naa nena naatusuja Yesus-- eing'ua Galilaya neisyayaki ninye;"
Matthew27:56 netii empolos enye Maria Magdalena o Maria-- ng'otonye e Yakobos o Yosef-- o ng'otonye oo nkera e Sebedayos."
Matthew27:57 Ore peaku teipa-- nelotu oltung'ani obo adupani le Arimatia-- oji engarna enye Yosef-- nera si ninye olaiteng'enuoni le Yesus."
Matthew27:58 Nelo ninye enetii Pilatos neomonu osesen le Yesus. Neitanapu Pilatos-- peishori ninye."
Matthew27:59 Neibung' Yosef osesen neirin ninye tʼolkarash opukenya sidai
Matthew27:60 nepik ninye atua enkurare natabatua tiatua osoit neibeleleng'oki osoit kitok kutukaji enkurare-- nelo."
Matthew27:61 Netii ina alo Maria Magdalena o engai Maria-- netoni tʼeneitoriokinore enkurare."
Matthew27:62 Ore tʼengai olong' nasuj engolong' enkitobirakinore-- neiturrurrokino laidasak kituak o Ilfarisayoi Pilatos"
Matthew27:63 nejo: Laitoriani-- kitadamutua-- aajo etejo ilo alejani te ina kata eishiu: Ayeu napiu-- eishunye ngolong'i uni."
Matthew27:64 Akae-- ntanapu-- perripi enkurare metabaiki engolong' e uni-- pemepuonu laiteng'enuok lenyena kiarie aapurroo ninye-- nejoki olorere: Etopiwuo ninye aing'ua lootuata-- — nelang' elejare enkiting'oto en elukunya."
Matthew27:65 Nejoki Pilatos ninje: Iatata larripok-- enjom-- entorrip naleng' anaa piyololo."
Matthew27:66 Nepuo ninje nerrip naleng' enkurare te nebo o larripok neen osoit tʼolmishire.
Matthew28:1 Ore peishunye engolong' naeng'ieng'areki nekenyu engolong' elukunya enjuma-- nelotu Maria Magdalena o engai Maria aaing'oraa enkurare."
Matthew28:2 Naa ng'orai-- neaku enkikirikirata kitok enkop. Amu etadouo olmalaika lʼOlaitoriani te shumata nelotu neibeleleng'oo osoit te kutukaji neton te shumata enye."
Matthew28:3 Nenyanyukie emua enye enkiwang'ata neibor ilkilani lenyena anaa esiret.
Matthew28:4 Neikirikira larripok tʼenkuretishu neaku anaa lootuata.
Matthew28:5 Nealiki olmalaika nejoki ng'oroyok: Emiureisho ndai! Amu ayolo nanu-- ajo ing'oruru Yesus otooshokoki esalaba."
Matthew28:6 Metii ene; amu etopiwuo anaa petejo. Ewotu-- eng'orai ewueji neirragie Olaitoriani."
Matthew28:7 Embung'a engoitoi aasioki-- entiakiti laiteng'enuok lenyena-- aajo etopiwuo ninye aing'ua lootuata. Eng'orai-- elaiturukie ninye ndai alo Galilaya-- nipuopuo aadol ninye te ina alo. Eng'orai-- atiaka ndai."
Matthew28:8 Nedumunye ninje aasioki t:enkurare-- eata enkuretishu o eng'ida kitok-- nekwet aainosaki laiteng'enuok lenyena. Ore epuoito ninje aainosaki laiteng'enuok lenyena--"
Matthew28:9 naa ng'orai-- netumore Yesus ninje-- nejo: Entakwenia! Nepuonu neibung' nkejek enyena neserem ninye."
Matthew28:10 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Emiureisho! Enjom-- enosakiti lalashera lainei-- pepuo Galilaya-- ina alo aapuo aadolie."
Matthew28:11 Ore epuoito tʼengoitoi-- nepuonu kulekai too larripok atua engang'-- neinosaki laidasak kituak mbaak pookin naataa."
Matthew28:12 Neiturrurro ninje te nebo o laigwenak neigwena-- neisho sikerin ngoshola kumok"
Matthew28:13 nejo: Entejo: Laiteng'enuok lenyena ooetuo kiarie nepurroo ninye-- kirura yook."
Matthew28:14 Ore pening' olkitok lʼolosho ena bae-- nikiropirop yook ninye nikimitoo ndai."
Matthew28:15 Neng'amu ninje ngoshola neiko neijia anaa peiteng'enaki. Neibulu ele rorei atua Yudayoi metabaiki taata.
Matthew28:16 Neibung' kulo aiteng'enuok tomon o obo engoitoi aapuo Galilaya metabaiki oldonyo oitanapa Yesus ninje.
Matthew28:17 Ore pedol ninje ninye-- neserem ninye; neing'arrirro kulekai."
Matthew28:18 Nelotu Yesus enetii ninje neirorie ninje nejo: Aaishooki engolon pookin te shumata o tʼenkop.
Matthew28:19 Akae-- embung'a engoitoi-- entaa laiteng'enuok loreren pookin-- imbatisisi ninje atua engarna e Papa o Oinoti o Olmumua Sinyati--"
Matthew28:20 inteng'ening'ene ninje-- peibung' pookin naitanapa nanu ndai. Naa ng'orai-- aboitare nanu ndai ngolong'i pookin metabaiki enkiting'oto olmaa."
Mark1:1 Nyena enkiterata oo lomon Peng'ida le Yesus Kristos-- Oinoti lʼEngai."
Mark1:2 Anaa petisiraki tiatua sirat oo layolounok: Ng'orai-- airriwaa nanu olmalaika lai lukunya engomom ino-- oitobir engoitoi ino;"
Mark1:3 etii ang'ata oltoilo lʼoloipotisho: Entobira engoitoi Olaitoriani-- entorioi nkiimat enyena!"
Mark1:4 Neaku eibatis Yohanes ti angʼata neinosu enkibatisa enkitaalata nʼenkitaunoto oo nkitarruot.
Mark1:5 Neipungʼoki ninye olosho pookin le Yudaya o pookin le Yerusalem neibatis ninye ninje tiatua engare Yordan-- neibalu ninje nkitarruot enye."
Mark1:6 Neaku eishopito Yohanes ilpapit lʼendames neata enkimeita enjoni tʼempolos enye nenya ilmaat o naishi oo mulugi;
Mark1:7 neinosu ejo: Elotu tekurum ai ologol naalang' nanu namaiteu airrugoi-- palaku nkeenda oo namuka enyena."
Mark1:8 Aibatis nanu ndai tʼengare-- kake elaibatis ninye ndai tʼOlmumua Sinyati."
Mark1:9 Neaku too nona olong'i eewuo Yesus aing'ua Nasaret e Galilaya-- neibatis Yohanes ninye te Yordan."
Mark1:10 Ore peilepu nabokata eingʼua engare-- nedol ebolo shumata nedoiki Olmumua ninye anaa olmaitai."
Mark1:11 Neaku oltoilo eing'ua shumata ajo: Ira iye Oinoti lai lanyor oshipakino oltau lai.
Mark1:12 Nearaa Olmumua ninye nabokata atua ang'ata.
Mark1:13 Netii ninye ang'ata ngolong'i artam-- etemita satan ninye-- netii e nebo o iljangʼit-- neisyayaki ilmalaikan ninye."
Mark1:14 Ore peidip aaitarasai Yohanes-- nelotu Yesus Galilaya-- neinosu lomon lʼeng'ida lʼenkarsishu Engai ejo:"
Mark1:15 Etabaua enkata nenyiku enkarsishu Engai. Entaalata-- eruko lomon lʼeng'ida!"
Mark1:16 Ore peim ninye embata olbalbal le Galilaya-- nedol Simon o Andreas-- olalashe le Simon-- enang'aki rresheta enye atua olbalbal; amu era ninje larreshok loo singir."
Mark1:17 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Ewotu-- entusujaki tekurum ai-- paitaa ndai larreshok loo ltung'anak."
Mark1:18 Neing'ua ninje nabokata rresheta enye-- nesuj ninye."
Mark1:19 Nenyikaa ninye peno nedol Yakobos le Sebedayos o Yohanes-- olalashe lenye-- ootii atua engalawa-- eitobirita rresheta; neipot ninje nabokata."
Mark1:20 Neing'ua ninje menye lenye Sebedayos tiatua engalawa te nebo o laisyayak-- nepuo nesuj ninye."
Mark1:21 Neibung' ninje engoitoi nepuo Kapernaum; nejing' ninye nabokata tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki atua engaji Engai neiteng'enisho.
Mark1:22 Neing'asia ninje tʼenkiteng'enare enye-- amu eiteng'ena ninye ninje anaa olopeny engolon-- neme neijia anaa layolok lʼesirata."
Mark1:23 Netii atua engaji Engai enye oltung'ani oata Olmumua duruki-- neapaa ninye oltoilo"
Mark1:24 ejo: Kainyo kiataiye iye-- Yesus le Nasaret? Iewuo iye-- piminye yook. Ayolo olira iye-- Osinyati lʼEngai."
Mark1:25 Nebuaki Yesus ninye ejo: Tumuka enkutuk-- tupuku te ninye!"
Mark1:26 Neipushunye Olmumua duruki te ninye-- neishir tʼoltoilo kitok-- nepuku te ninye."
Mark1:27 Neing'asia pookin neikilikwanaro baiki aajo: Kainyo ena? Kaa kiteng'enare ng'ejuk engolon ena? Neitanap ninye ilmumuan duruk nening' ninje ninye.
Mark1:28 Neibulu mbaak enyena nabokata ewueji pookin nemanita Galilaya.
Mark1:29 Nepuku ninje nabokata tʼengaji Engai nepuo atua engaji e Simon o Andreas te nebo o Yakobos o Yohanes.
Mark1:30 Neirrag engaputani e Simon-- eata oltikana-- neliki ninje ninye mbaak enyena."
Mark1:31 Nelotu neapaa aibung' engaina enye-- neing'ua oltikana ninye-- neisyayaki ninye ninje."
Mark1:32 Ore peaku teipa-- eidipa atadoi engolong'-- neaki ninje ninye loomoiyaa pookin o looata ilmeneng'a."
Mark1:33 Neiturrurro engang' pookin tʼendaloishi.
Mark1:34 Neishiunye ninye loomoiyaa kumok-- neitupuku ilmeneng'a kumok neitu eisho ilmeneng'a meiroro-- amu etayoloutuo ninje ninye."
Mark1:35 Ore pepej ewuas-- eitu ekenyu abaraki-- neinyototo ninye nepuku nelo ewueji nemetii iltung'anak-- nesaisho te ina alo."
Mark1:36 Nesuj ninye Simon o lʼemboitei enye.
Mark1:37 Ore petum ninye-- nejoki ninye: King'oru pookin."
Mark1:38 Nejoki ninye ninje: Maapeti engai wueji tiatua ngang'itie naataana-- patum ainosu lomon lʼEngai te ina alo; amu te ina atupukuo."
Mark1:39 Nelo einosaa lomon lʼEngai tiatua ngajijik Engai enye te Galilaya pookin nemir ilmeneng'a.
Mark1:40 Nelotu enetii ninye oltung'ani loata enkea oo lbolot nesai ninye negilaki kung' nejoki ninye: Teni iyeu-- nikindim aisuja."
Mark1:41 Neibung'aki Yesus ninye engoshoke nanana neitorioo engaina enye neporoo ninye nejoki: Ayeu-- sujai!"
Mark1:42 Ore ake eirorita-- neing'ua enkea oo lbolot ninye nabokata neisujai."
Mark1:43 Neitanap ninye tʼengolon nearaa ninye nabokata
Mark1:44 nejoki ninye: Ng'orai-- pimiliki oltung'ani ororei-- kake nno-- pintadol kion olaidasani-- pintarasaa nʼenkisujata ino naitanapua Mose-- peaku enjakenishu too ninje."
Mark1:45 Ore peidip atupuku ninye-- neiter ainosu nkumok neibulunye ororei neijia-- ajo eitu eidim ninye atijing'a atua engang' tʼewuas-- kake etii aulo-- ewueji nemetii iltung'anak; nepuonu enetii ninye-- eing'ua wuejitin pookin."
Mark2:1 Neitoki ajing' Kapernaum-- eishunye ngolong'i naaje; nening'i-- ajo etii aji."
Mark2:2 Neiturrurro nabokata ilkumok metaa mekure etii enkigutata te kutuk aji-- neliki ninje lomon."
Mark2:3 Nepuonu neaki ninye oltung'ani onunukito osupetai-- enapita iltung'anak ong'wan ninye."
Mark2:4 Ore peitu eidim ninje aatinyikaki ninye tʼolbae lʼolorere-- nebol keper aji ene wueji netii ninye; ore peidip aatuud-- neitadou erruat nairragie ele tung'ani lonunukito osupetai."
Mark2:5 Ore pedol Yesus enkirukoto enye-- nejoki ele loata osupetai: Nakerai ai-- kintaikiaki nkitarruot inono."
Mark2:6 Netii ina alo ematua oo layolok lʼesirata oototonitio neibirribir too ltauja lenye:
Mark2:7 Kainyo pemor ele Engai nji? Kang'ai loidim aitau nkitarruot neme obo-- nera Engai?"
Mark2:8 Neyolou Yesus nabokata tʼolmumua lenye-- ajo eibirribirrita nji tiatua ninje-- nejoki ninje: Kainyo pimbirribirrirri kuna too ltauja linyi?"
Mark2:9 Kaa nalelek-- teni ajoki Oloata osupetai: Kintaikiaki nkitarruot inono-- arashu: Tudumunye-- tudumakinoi erruat ino-- tilimanai!?"
Mark2:10 Kake piyolouu-- aajo eata Engerai oltung'ani engolon naitaunye nkitarruot tʼenkop-- nejoki ele loata osupetai:"
Mark2:11 Aajoki iye-- nyototoi-- tudumakinoi erruat ino-- nno ang'!"
Mark2:12 Nedumunye nedumakino nabokata erruat enye nepuku tʼengomom oo pookin-- neiputukuny baiki pookin neitadaraa Engai ejo: Eitu ai kata kidol nji tukul."
Mark2:13 Neitoki apuku nelo embata olbalbal; nelotu olorere pookin enetii ninye neiteng'en ninje.
Mark2:14 Ore eimita-- nedol Levi le Alfayos-- eton tʼewueji e kodi-- nejoki ninye: Tusujuaki! Nedumunye nesuj ninye."
Mark2:15 Neaku ore einosaa endaa tʼengaji enye-- netoni laoshok le kodi kumok o laitarruok te nebo o Yesus o laiteng'enuok lenyena; amu etii ilkumok lootusuja ninye."
Mark2:16 Ore pedol layolok lʼesirata o Ilfarisayoi-- aajo edaa te nebo o laitarruok o laoshok le kodi-- nejoki ninje laiteng'enuok lenyena: Kainyo pedaa neokisho ninye te nebo o laoshok le kodi o laitarruok?"
Mark2:17 Ore pening' Yesus ina-- nejoki ninje: Meyeu loora biot olaishiunoni-- neme kulo oomoiyaa. Eitu alotu aipot looata esupato-- kake laitarruok-- petum aataalata."
Mark2:18 Neaku epukoo laiteng'enuok le Yohanes o loo Lfarisayoi. Nepuonu looje nejoki ninye: Kainyo pepukoo laiteng'enuok le Yohanes o laiteng'enuok loo Lfarisayoi-- kake mepukoo laiteng'enuok linono?"
Mark2:19 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Kaji eiko teni epukoo nkera enkiama tʼenkata napon etii osanja te nebo o ninje? Meidim aatupukoi ninje te ina kata natii e nebo o osanja.
Mark2:20 Kake epuonu ngolong'i naaoruni ninje osanja-- nepuo aapukoo te ina olong'."
Mark2:21 Metii oltung'ani oripaki erashet olkila ng'ejuk atua olkila musana; teni eripaki-- neitarruo ena rashet ng'ejuk ilo musana-- nepona empolosata."
Mark2:22 Nemetii olopik olmarua ng'ejuk atua ilbenia musan; teni epik-- nepolos ilo marua ng'ejuk ilbenia-- neibukori olmarua nerruoio ilbenia. Kake epik olmarua ng'ejuk atua ilbenia ng'ejuko."
Mark2:23 Neaku ore peim ninye tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki atua nkuruman endaa-- neiter laiteng'enuok lenyena aagilu lukuny entapa."
Mark2:24 Nejoki Lfarisayoi ninye: Ng'orai kainyo peitobir ninje nemeaku tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki?
Mark2:25 Nejoki ninye ninje: Eitu isomama ndai tukul eneikuna David-- eata osina neibung' olamei ninye o lʼemboitoi?"
Mark2:26 Eneikuna nejing' atua engaji Engai tʼenkata olaidasani kitok Abyatar nenya ilmkaten lʼenkitaduaroto nemeaku-- peinosi neme too laidasak-- neisho si ninye lʼemboitoi enye?"
Mark2:27 Nejoki ninye ninje: Etaa engolong' naeng'ieng'areki tʼolbae lʼoltung'ani-- me oltung'ani tʼolbae lʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki."
Mark2:28 Nji era Enkerai oltung'ani baiki Olaitoriani lʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki.
Mark3:1 Neitoki ajing' ninye atua engaji Engai; netii ina alo oltung'ani loata engaina tasat.
Mark3:2 Neing oraa ninje-- ten ake eishiunye ninye tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki-- petum aaitang'oro ninye."
Mark3:3 Nejoki ninye ele tung ani tasat aina: Wou empolos!
Mark3:4 Nejoki ninye ninje: Keaku-- peitobiri sidan arashu ntorrok tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki? peitopoki oltau arashu peari? Negira ninje."
Mark3:5 Neing'oraa ninje aman too mbat pookin tʼengoro neilish tʼolbae loo ltauja lenye oogol nejoki ninye oltung'ani: Ntorioi engaina ino! Neitorioo neishiu engaina enye neaku bioto anaa en e are.
Mark3:6 Nepuku nabokata lelo Farisayoi-- neigwena te nebo o iltung'anak le Herodes eneiko teni eiminye ninye."
Mark3:7 Neing'ua Yesus o laiteng'enuok lenyena ine-- nelo metabaiki olbalbal. Nesuj olorere kitok ninye-- eing'ua Galilaya o Yudaya"
Mark3:8 o Yerusalem o Idumaya o olkekun le Yordan o mbat e Tiros o Sidon; esiamu kitok natoning'o mbaak naaitobir-- nelotu enetii ninye."
Mark3:9 Nejoki ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena-- njetaaniki ninye engalawa kinyi tʼolbae lʼesiamu-- pemeroosh ninye."
Mark3:10 Amu eishiunye ninye ilkumok-- neurokino ninje pookin ninye-- petum aataporoi ninye kulo looata moiyaitin."
Mark3:11 Ore pedol ilmumuan duruk ninye-- neurori tʼengomom enye neishir ejo: Ira iye Oinoti lʼEngai."
Mark3:12 Neitanap ninje naleng'-- pemeitalioio ninye."
Mark3:13 Neilepaki ninye oldonyo neipot lekua lootayeuo ninye openy-- nepuo ninje enetii ninye."
Mark3:14 Negelu ninye tomon o are-- petum aataboitare ninye-- petum si ninye airriwai ninje-- peinosaa lomon lʼEngai--"
Mark3:15 peata engolon naishiunye nkeaitin o namirie ilmeneng'a.
Mark3:16 Negelu ninye kulo tomon o are-- neisho Simon engarna Petros;"
Mark3:17 o Yakobos le Sebedayos o Yohanes-- olalashe le Yakobos-- neisho ninje engarna Boanerges-- neji: nkera enkikurrukurroto;"
Mark3:18 o Andreas o Filipos o Bartolomayos o Matayos o Tomas o Yakobos le Alfayos o Tadayos o Simon Olkananayos
Mark3:19 o Yudas Iskariotes-- ilo loitarasaiye ninye."
Mark3:20 Nejing' ninye aji; neitoki aiturrurro esiamu-- neitu eidim ninje baiki aainosa endaa."
Mark3:21 Ore pening' kulo lʼengang' enye mbaak-- nepuku aapuo aaibung' ninye-- amu etejo: Etooshe elukunya."
Mark3:22 Nejo layolok lʼesirata lootadoutuo aaing'ua Yerusalem: Eata ninye Beelsebul nemir ilmeneng'a tʼenkidimata olkitok loo lmeneng'a.
Mark3:23 Neipot ninye ninje enetii nejoki ninje too nkitanyanyukieta: Kaji eiko teni eidim satan ataarai satan?
Mark3:24 Teni ekesho enkarsishu tiatua kion-- meidim aitasho ena arsishu."
Mark3:25 Teni ekesho engaji tiatua kion-- meidim aitasho ena aji."
Mark3:26 Teni etudumakine satan kion nekesho-- meidim aitasho-- kake emuta ninye."
Mark3:27 Meidim atijing'a oltung'ani engaji ologol-- peoru masaa enyena-- eitu eng'as aen ele ogol-- petum atooru engaji enye."
Mark3:28 Japa-- aliki ndai: Eitaikini nkera oo ltung'anak nkitarruot pookin-- baiki morot Engai naamorie ninje Engai;"
Mark3:29 kake olomor Olmumua Sinyati-- meata ninye enkitaunoto nkatan pookin-- kake etaa te ninye enkitarruoto oo nkatan pookin."
Mark3:30 Amu etejo ninje: Eata ninye Olmumua duruki.
Mark3:31 Nepuonu ng'otonye enye o lalashera lenyena neitashe te boo-- neirriwaki oltung'ani-- peipot ninye."
Mark3:32 Etotona esiamu aman ninye. Nejoki ninje ninye: Ng'orai-- etii ng'utunyi o lalashera linono boo niking'oru iye."
Mark3:33 Nealiki ninje ejo: Ang'ai nara yeiyo ai o lalashera lainei?
Mark3:34 Neing'oraa lootoni emanita ninye too ngaloli pookin nejo: Eng'orai-- yeiyo ai o lalashera lainei!"
Mark3:35 Amu oltung'ani pookin oitobir eyeunoto Engai-- nera ninye olalashe lai o enganashe ai o yeiyo."
Mark4:1 Neitoki aiter aiteng'enishe tʼembata olbalbal-- neiturrurro esiamu kitok tʼenetii ninye metijing'a atua engalawa neton tʼolbalbal; netii esiamu olosho otoiyo tʼembata olbalbal."
Mark4:2 Neiteng'en ninje nkumok too nkitanyanyukieta-- neliki ninje tiatua enkiteng'enare enye:"
Mark4:3 Entoning'! Eng'orai-- etupukuo olaisuaroni alo aisuaisho."
Mark4:4 Neaku ore eisuaisho-- nedoiki ematua engoitoi-- nepuonu ntaritik e shumata nenya ina."
Mark4:5 Nedoiki engai matua atua soito neitu eata nkulupuok kumok nebulu asioki-- tiaraki neitu eata nkulupuok naasur."
Mark4:6 Ore peilepu engolong'-- neinaaia netoi-- tiaraki neitu eata ntonat."
Mark4:7 Nedoiki engai matua ilkikarreta-- nebulu lelo kikarreta negor ninye nemeiu ilmomo."
Mark4:8 Nedoiki engai matua atua enkulupuoni sidai-- neiu ilmomo nebulu nepona-- neisho nabo osom-- nabo ntomoni ile-- nabo iip."
Mark4:9 Nejoki ninye ninje: Oloata nkiyaa naaning'ie njening'.
Mark4:10 Ore etii ewueji enye openy-- neikilikwan kulo lootamana ninye te nebo o kulo tomon o are mbaak oo nkitanyanyukieta."
Mark4:11 Nejoki ninje: Eitumunyanaki ndai piyolouu njumat enkarsishu Engai; ore lekua ootii boo-- eaku too nkitanyanyukieta--"
Mark4:12 peiye eing'oraa eing'orita nemedol-- peiye ening' ening'ito nemeyolou-- pemeibelekenya o akenya neitaikini ninje nkitarruot."
Mark4:13 Nejoki ninye ninje: Miyololo ndai ena kitanyanyukiet? Kaji inkoko teni iyeuu niyolouu nkulie kitanyanyukieta pookin?
Mark4:14 Eisuaia olaisuaroni ororei.
Mark4:15 Nera kulo lootii engoitoi: enaisuakini ororei-- ore peidip aatoning'-- nelotu nabokata satan neitau ele rorei oisuakaki atua ninje."
Mark4:16 Enyanyukie si ninje looisuakaki atua soito kulo looning' ororei-- nabokata neng'amu ninye tʼeng'ida--"
Mark4:17 nemeata ntonat tiatua ninje-- kake ebik enkata kiti; ore peaku osina arashu enkinyala tʼolbae lʼororei-- nerikai nabokata."
Mark4:18 Nera looisuakaki atua ilkikarreta kulo lootoning'o ororei--"
Mark4:19 nejing' nkishilarot olmaa o elejata endupai o olng'warra loo nkulie baak negor ilo rorei-- neaku meisho."
Mark4:20 Nera kulo looisuakaki atua enkulupuoni sidai iltung'anak looning' ororei-- neng'amu neiu ilmomo-- obo osom-- obo ntomoni ile-- obo iip."
Mark4:21 Nejoki ninye ninje: Ketii Oloata enkilang'et-- pepik kop olkisembe arashu kop erruat? Mepiki ninye shumata enkibung'et?"
Mark4:22 Amu metii enaisudori-- nemelalioi-- nemetii enashuma-- nemelotu ewuas."
Mark4:23 Oloata nkiyaa naaning'ie-- njening'."
Mark4:24 Nejoki ninye ninje: Eng'orai enining'itoto! Ore entemet nitemishorere-- ninye epuoi aatemakinye ndai-- neponikini ndai lining'ining'i."
Mark4:25 Amu Oloata-- neishori ninye; ore olemeata-- neoruni ninye baiki enaata."
Mark4:26 Nejo ninye: Nji etiu enkarsishu Engai anaa oltung'ani oisuaki embeu enkop--"
Mark4:27 neirura neinyototo-- dama o kiarie-- nepuku embeu-- nebulu-- meyolo ninye."
Mark4:28 Neisho enkop openy-- neng'as olkujita-- tekurum elukunya-- tekurum engano nao tiatua elukunya."
Mark4:29 Ore peidip aaoto ilmomo-- neirriwaa nabokata emundo-- amu etabaua endung'ore."
Mark4:30 Nejo ninye: Kainyo kintanyanyukie enkarsishu Engai? Arashu ke ti aa kitanyanyukiet kintanyanyukie ninye?
Mark4:31 Anaa embeu e karadali-- teni eisuakini enkop-- nera kinyi nelang' nkulie beun pookin naatii enkop;"
Mark4:32 kake ore peidipi aisuai-- nebulu neaku kitok nelang' mbenek pookin-- netum ilng'osil kituak neidim baiki ntaritik e shumata aatamany abori oloip lenye."
Mark4:33 Neinosaki ninje lomon too nkitanyanyukieta kumok anaa nena-- neijia anaa peidima aatoning'."
Mark4:34 Neitu eirorie ninye ninje neme tʼenkitanyanyukiet-- neitaaliki laiteng'enuok lenyena pookin tʼewueji enye oopeny."
Mark4:35 Ore peaku teipa te ina olong'-- nejoki ninye ninje: Matalang' aabaiki lido kekun!"
Mark4:36 Ore peidip ninje aaitanapare olorere-- neng'amu ninje ninye anaa petiu atua engalawa; netii nkulie alawani e nebo o ninye."
Mark4:37 Neaku enkutishoto olkutati kitok nenang'aki lopir lʼengare atua engalawa-- neaku eiganya engalawa."
Mark4:38 Netii ninye openy kurum engalawa-- epetita enkirishet elukunya. Neinyeye ninje ninye nejoki ninye: Laiteng'enani-- me toki te iye-- teni kimin yook?"
Mark4:39 Neinyototo ninye nebuaki olkutati nejoki olbalbal: Tigirai-- tirria! Negira olkutati neaku olgira kitok."
Mark4:40 Nejoki ninye ninje: Ainyo pirara kureti nji? Kainyo-- miatata enkirukoto?"
Mark4:41 Neureishoi ninje tʼenkuretishu kitok nejokino: Kang'ai ele? Ajo ening' ninye olkutati o olbalbal.
Mark5:1 Nebaiki lido kekun lʼolbalbal-- atua olosho loo Lgerasenoi."
Mark5:2 Ore pedou ninye tʼengalawa-- nenang'are ninye nabokata oltung'ani otupukuo too nkuraren neata Olmumua duruki--"
Mark5:3 loata ntonat tiatua nkuraren-- neitu etumi oltung'ani loidim ateena ninye-- baiki too lpisia;"
Mark5:4 amu eteenaki ninye aigil kumok too ngoteta o too lpisia-- negiligil ninye lelo pisia nepurdupurd ngoteta-- neitu eidim o obo atigilu ninye."
Mark5:5 Ore tʼenkiarie o dama pookin netii atua nkuraren o ildonyo-- eishir near kion too soito."
Mark5:6 Ore pedol ninye Yesus tʼenelakua-- nekwetiki negilaki kung' ninye neishir tʼoltoilo kitok ejo:"
Mark5:7 Kainyo aataiye iye-- Yesus-- Oinoti lʼEngai natii shumata naleng'? Aaiturujie iye Engai-- pimikintame!"
Mark5:8 Amu etiaka ninye: Tupuku iye-- lemumua duruki-- tiatua ele tung'ani!"
Mark5:9 Neikilikwan ninye: Keji aa engarna ino? Nejoki ninye: Eji engarna ai empuoto-- amu kira kumok."
Mark5:10 Nesai ninye naleng'-- pememiraki atua ele osho."
Mark5:11 Netii ina alo oldonyo emboo oo lbitiro looirrititai.
Mark5:12 Nesai ilmeneng'a pookin ninye nejo: Rriwaki yook atua ilbitiro-- pikijing' atua ninje."
Mark5:13 Neisho epuo. Nepuku kulo mumuan duruk nejing' atua lelo bitiro-- nesulakino emboo asioki tʼemarti atua olbalbal-- loobaia iip tikitam-- nee tiatua olbalbal."
Mark5:14 Nekwet lairritak lenye neibulunye mbaak atua engang' o atua nkuruman. Nepuonu iltung'anak-- peing'oraa enataa."
Mark5:15 Nepuonu enetii Yesus neing'oraa Oloata opa ilmeneng'a-- eton neishopo neata eng'eno naa ninye duo oata empuoto-- neureishoi ninje."
Mark5:16 Neinosaki ninje kulo lootadua enataa tʼoltung'ani loo lmeneng'a o mbaak oo lbitiro.
Mark5:17 Neiter aasai ninye-- pepuku tiatua mbatai enye."
Mark5:18 Ore peilepaki ninye engalawa-- nesai Oloata ilmeneng'a ninye-- peruba te nebo."
Mark5:19 Neitu eiruk ninye-- kake nejoki ninye: Nno engaji ino enetii iltung'anak linono-- pinosaki ninje enikinkunaka Olaitoriani nikimbung'aki engoshoke nanana."
Mark5:20 Nelo ninye aiter ainosu tiatua Manyat tomon eneikunaka Yesus ninye; neing'asia ninje pookin.
Mark5:21 Ore peitoki aidip Yesus atalang'a tʼengalawa-- neiturrurrokino ninye esiamu kitok-- netii ninye embata olbalbal."
Mark5:22 Nelotu obo too lkituak lʼengaji Engai-- oji Yairos; ore pedol ninye-- nebatatakino nkejek enyena"
Mark5:23 nesai ninye naleng' ejo: Eng'or peno ee entito ai kiti; teni iyeu nilotu ninteleiki ngaik-- petum atopua neishiu."
Mark5:24 Nelo te nebo o ninye. Nesuj ninye esiamu kitok neroosh ninye.
Mark5:25 Netii eng'oroyoni nabo naata empukunoto osarge enkata oo larin tomon o are--"
Mark5:26 nening' emion naleng' too laishiunok kumok neishooio naata pookin te ina-- neitu eretoki hoo nyoo-- kake nepona ake eneikununo aaku torrono."
Mark5:27 Ore pening' ninye mbaak e Yesus-- nelotu tekurum tiatua olorere neing'unye olkila lenye;"
Mark5:28 amu etejo ninye: Teni aing'unye ilkilani lenyena ake-- napok."
Mark5:29 Netoi nabokata engong'u osarge lenye nening' tʼosesen lenye-- ajo eishiunyeki tʼele sina."
Mark5:30 Nening' Yesus nabokata tiatua kion-- ajo etupukuo engolon te ninye-- neibelekenyakino olorere nejo: Ang'ai loing'unye ilkilani lainei?"
Mark5:31 Nejoki laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye: Idolita-- kirooshita olorere-- nijo: Ang'ai liking'unye?"
Mark5:32 Neing'oraa mbat pookin-- pedol enataasa ena."
Mark5:33 Neureisho ake ena ng'oroyoni neikirikira-- eyolo enataa te ninye-- nelotu nebatatakino ninye neliki esipata pookin."
Mark5:34 Nejoki ninye: Naito-- kintopua enkirukoto ino-- nno ang' tʼeseriani-- taa bioto tʼosina lino!"
Mark5:35 Ore epon eirorita-- nepuonu iltung'anak-- eing'ua engang' olkitok lʼengaji Engai-- ejo: Eidipa atua entito ino. Ainyo pintoki aitirik Olaiteng'enani?"
Mark5:36 Nening' Yesus nabokata ilo rorei oiroritai-- nejoki ninye olkitok lʼengaji Engai: Miureisho-- ruko ake!"
Mark5:37 Neitu eisho oltung'ani o obo losuj ninye neme Petros o Yakobos o Yohanes-- olalashe le Yakobos."
Mark5:38 Nelotu atua aji olkitok lʼengaji Engai neing'oraa enkipushoi oo looishirita o looilishito naleng'.
Mark5:39 Ore peidip atijing'a atua nejoki ninje: Ainyo pimpushosho ninjirishiri? Eitu ee enkerai-- kake eirura. Nekweniye ninye."
Mark5:40 Ore peitupuku iltung'anak pookin-- nerik menye lʼenkerai o ng'otonye o lʼemboitei enye-- nejing' atua enetii enkerai."
Mark5:41 Neibung' enkerai engaina-- nejoki ninye: Talita kumi! nera enkitaalata enye: Nairo-- aaliki iye-- nyototoi!"
Mark5:42 Neitashe ina ito nabokata nelimana; nera ninye ake noo larin tomon o are. Neing'asia ninje tʼenking'asiata kitok.
Mark5:43 Neitanap ninje naleng'-- pemeyolou oltung'ani o obo ena; neitanapu-- peishori ninye endaa."
Mark6:1 Nepuku te ina alo nebaia engang' e menye lenye-- nesuj laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye."
Mark6:2 Ore peaku engolong' naeng'ieng'areki-- neiter aiteng'enisho tiatua engaji Engai. Ore ilkumok looning' ena-- neing'asia nejo: Kaji einotie ele kuna? Kaa ng'eno ena naishooki ele? O kuna kitobirat engolon naaku too ngaik enyena?"
Mark6:3 Mera ninye olagwetani-- Oinoti le Maria o olalashe le Yakobos o le Yoses o le Yudas o le Simon? Metii baiki nganashera enyena ene atua yook? Nerikareki ninje ninye."
Mark6:4 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Melau olayolounoni enkitook neme tiatua olosho le menye o tiatua iltung'anak lʼenkishomi enye o tiatua engaji enye.
Mark6:5 Neitu eidim ninye aitobira enkitobirata engolon o nabo te ina alo neme ake eiteleikio ngaik loomoiyaa kuti neishiunye ninje.
Mark6:6 Neiputukuny ninye-- tiaraki neitu eiruk ninje. Nemanaa tiatua ngang'itie too mbat pookin-- eiteng'enisho."
Mark6:7 Neipot ninye kulo tomon o are neiter airriwaa ninje are are-- neisho ninje engolon too lmumuan duruk--"
Mark6:8 neitanap ninje-- pemenap toki tʼengoitoi neme eng'udi ake-- me olmkate-- me olbene-- me mpesai tiatua enyorret;"
Mark6:9 kake njeenikino namuka-- pemeishop ilkilani are."
Mark6:10 Nejoki ninje: Ore engaji pookin nijing'ijing'i-- entobik tiatua metabana nipukuku te ine wueji."
Mark6:11 Ore lemeng'amu ndai-- entupukutu te ina alo-- nimpiripirooro enterit tiabori oo nkejek inyi-- peaku enjakenishu too ninje. Japa-- aliki ndai: Eiteleleki Sodom o Gomora tʼengolong' enkigwena nelang' ina ang'."
Mark6:12 Ore peidip ninje aatupukutu-- neinosu ninje-- peala iltung'anak"
Mark6:13 nemir ninje ilmumuan duruk kumok neel loomoiyaa kumok tʼeilata neishiunye ninje.
Mark6:14 Nening' olkarsis Herodes mbaak enyena-- amu eibale engarna enye-- nejo: Etopiwuo Yohanes Olaibatisani too lootuata-- onaa eitobirisho nkyasin enkidimata tiatua ninye."
Mark6:15 Nejo ilkulekai: Era ninye Eliya; nejo ilkulekai: Era ninye olayolounoni arashu obo too layolounok.
Mark6:16 Ore pening' Herodes kuna-- nejo: Etopiwuo Yohanes latudung'o elukunya-- too lootuata."
Mark6:17 Amu eirriwaiye Herodes openy neibung' Yohanes neen ninye tʼengaji eenata tʼolbae le Herodias-- eng'oroyoni olalashe lenye Filipos; amu eamaiye ninye."
Mark6:18 Amu etiaka Yohanes Herodes: Me sidai te iye-- teni iata eng'oroyoni olalashe lino."
Mark6:19 Akae-- eibaiye Herodias ninye neyeu near ninye metua-- neitu eidim."
Mark6:20 Amu eturia Herodes Yohanes-- tiaraki natayolo-- ajo era ninye oltung'ani supat naa sinyati; negolie ninye; ore pening' ninye-- neitobir nkumok too nona-- neinining' ninye tʼeng'ida."
Mark6:21 Ore peaku engolong' sidai-- neitobiraki Herodes tʼengolong' eiunoto enye ilkituak lenyena o ilkigeluni o laigwenak le Galilaya endaa kitok."
Mark6:22 Nejing'aki entito e ina Herodias neiguran neiting'id Herodes o kulo oototonitio o ninye. Nejoki olkarsis entito: Toomonuoki eniyeu ake-- naalaisho iye;"
Mark6:23 neiturujaki ninye: Ore enikiomonu ake-- naalaisho iye-- baiki ematua enkarsishu ai."
Mark6:24 Nepuku entito nejoki ng'otonye enye: Kainyo aomonu? Nejoki ninye: Elukunya e Yohanes Olaibatisani.
Mark6:25 Nejing' asioki enetii olkarsis neomonu ninye ejo: Ayeu nikinjo taata nji tʼengirra elukunya e Yohanes Olaibatisani.
Mark6:26 Neilish olkarsis naleng'-- kake tʼolbae lʼenkiturujata o tʼolbae loo kulo oototonitio tʼendaa-- neitu eyeu neany ninye."
Mark6:27 Neirriwaa nabokata olkarsis olarani neitanapu-- peauni elukunya enye tiatua engaji eenata."
Mark6:28 Neau elukunya enye tʼengirra neisho entito-- neisho entito ninye ng'otonye enye."
Mark6:29 Ore peidip aatoning' laiteng'enuok lenyena nena-- nepuonu nenap empopong' enye-- nenuk ninye tʼenkurare."
Mark6:30 Neiturrurrokino lairriwak Yesus neinosaki ninye mbaak pookin naaitobira ninje o naaiteng'enutua.
Mark6:31 Nejoki ninye ninje: Ewotu ndai oopeny ewueji ang' nemetii oltung'ani-- pieng'ieng'ang'a peno. Amu etii kumok loopuonu o loopuo; neitu eata ninje baiki erishata nadaare."
Mark6:32 Nepuo ninje tʼengalawa ewueji enye openy nemetii iltung'anak.
Mark6:33 Neduaia ilkumok ninje epuoito neyolou ninye-- nepuo aasioio ina alo too nkejek-- eing'ua ngang'itie pookin-- neituruk ninje aabaia neiturrurro."
Mark6:34 Ore pepuku Yesus nedol olorere-- neibung'aki ninye engoshoke nanana ninje-- amu etanyanyukie ninje ntare nemeata olairritani-- neiter aiteng'en ninje too nkumok."
Mark6:35 Ore peaku namutu-- nepuonu laiteng'enuok lenyena enetii ninye nejo: Era ene wueji ang'ata narok netaa namutu;"
Mark6:36 ntanapare kulo-- pepuo nkuruman o mbat pookin oo ngang'itie-- peinyang'aki aten endaa."
Mark6:37 Nealiki nejoki Yesus ninje: Enjoo ndai ninje endaa. Nejoki ninje ninye: Ke kipuo ainyang'aki ninje ilmkaten loo ndenaria iip are-- pikinjo ninje enya?"
Mark6:38 Nejoki ninje: Ke ilmkaten aja iatata? Enjom-- eng'orai! Ore peidip aatayolo ninje-- nejo: Imiet o singir are."
Mark6:39 Neitanap ninje-- peitoton ninje pookin tʼenkop too nkisotin-- tʼolkujita onyori."
Mark6:40 Netoni too lkererin-- aa ip ip o aa onom onom."
Mark6:41 Neibung' ninye kulo mkaten imiet o kulo singir aare neimariri shumata-- nemayan negiligil ilmkaten neisho ninje laiteng'enuok-- peitarasaki olorere; neoriki baiki kulo singir aare ninje pookin."
Mark6:42 Nenya pookin neraposho.
Mark6:43 Nesotu ninje mbelat ilbenia tomon o are oobore o ndung'ot oo singir.
Mark6:44 Ore looinosa endaa-- nera leak iip onom."
Mark6:45 Nearaki nabokata laiteng'enuok lenyena meilepakiii engalawa-- peituruk aapuo lido kekun metabaiki Betsaida-- metabana neitanapare ninye olorere."
Mark6:46 Ore peidip aitanapare ninje-- nelo ninye oldonyo asaisho."
Mark6:47 Ore pemutu neaku etii engalawa empolos olbalbal netii ninye openy atua olosho otoiyo.
Mark6:48 Nedol ninye eata ninje osina tʼeyetunoto-- amu etii olkutati lorrinyu ninje. Ore tʼerripore e ong'wan e kiarie nelotu enetii ninje-- elimana te shumata olbalbal. Neyeu negiroo."
Mark6:49 Ore pedol ninje ninye elimana te shumata olbalbal-- nejo ninje era oloip-- neyetaki aaishir;"
Mark6:50 amu etadua pookin ninye neng'ayung'ayu. Neirorie si ninye ninje nabokata nejoki ninje: Entagoluoto too ltauja-- amu nanu-- emiureisho!"
Mark6:51 Neilepaki ninje tiatua engalawa-- negira olkutati. Neing'asia ninje naleng' tiatua aten."
Mark6:52 Amu eitu edamu ninje mbaak oo lmkaten-- kake etagolito iltauja lenye."
Mark6:53 Ore peidip aatalang'-- nebaia olosho le Genesaret neitadoiyo eenet tʼembata."
Mark6:54 Ore pedou ninje tʼengalawa-- neyolou ninje ninye nabokata"
Mark6:55 nekwetikwet aasioio atua ilo osho pookin neiter aanapu loomoiyaa too rruatin-- nepuo wuejitin neetoning'ie-- aajo etii ninye."
Mark6:56 Ore ewueji pookin-- teni etijing'a ninye ngang'itie kutiti arashu kituak arashu nkuruman-- neitaper loomoiyaa too singiran nesai ninye-- peporoo ninje tʼenaipukoi olkila lenye; ore pookin lootaporoitie ninye nepok."
Mark7:1 Neiturrurrokino ninye Ilfarisayoi o ematua o layolok lʼesirata ooing'ua Yerusalem.
Mark7:2 Ore pedol ninje ematua oo laiteng'enuok lenyena einosita endaa too ngaik torrok-- eji nemeisuja-- neisurdany."
Mark7:3 Amu menya Ilfarisayoi o Yudayoi pookin endaa eitu eisuj ngaik enye naleng'-- neibung' ng'amunot oo lpaiyani."
Mark7:4 Naa teni epuonu t'osingira-- nemedaa eitu eisuja. Netii nkulie ng'amunot kumok naatang'amutua aaibung'-- anaa enkisujata oo nkwarun o noo lkoboi o noo nareta osuiai o noo lkitareta."
Mark7:5 Akae-- neikilikwan Ilfarisayoi o layolok lʼesirata ninye: Ainyo pemesuj laiteng'enuok linono ng'amunot oo lpaiyani-- kake enya endaa too ngaik torrok?"
Mark7:6 Nejoki ninye ninje: Sidai enaitayolouo Yesaya too ndai laitusupatuok anaa pesira: Aaitaa kitok ele orere too njonito oo nkutukie-- kake aalakwaniki iltauja lenye;"
Mark7:7 naaisyayaki ninje pesho-- neiteng'enu nkiteng'enareitin aa nkitanapat oo ltung'anak."
Mark7:8 Ipalipala ndai enkitanapata Engai nimbung'ubung'u ng'amunot oo ltung'anak-- enkisujata oo lkoboi o noo nkwarun o nkulie kumok naanyanyukie nena nintobiribiri."
Mark7:9 Nejoki ninye ninje: Sidai ianyianya enkitanapata Engai-- pitumutumu aatorrip ng'amunot inyi."
Mark7:10 Amu etejo Mose: Ntaa kituak minyi o ng'utunyi! o: oloimaki menye arashu ng'otonye torrono-- njeari tʼenkea."
Mark7:11 Nijojo ndai: Ore pejoki oltung'ani menye arashu ng'otonye „Korban“-- eji: „eishooki Engai“-- naaku endupoto ino te nanu-- nebaiki--"
Mark7:12 nimintokiki aaisho ndai meitobiraki ninye menye o ng'otonye toki--"
Mark7:13 niariara ororei lʼEngai too ng'amunot inyi nitang'amutua; nintobiribiri nkumok naanyanyukie kuna.
Mark7:14 Neitoki aipot ninye esiamu nejoki ninje: Enining'oki pookin-- piyolouu!"
Mark7:15 Metii entoki e oriong' oltung'ani najing' atua ninye naidim aitaa ninye torrono; kake enapuku tiatua ninye-- ninye naitaa oltung'ani torrono."
Mark7:16 Oloata nkiyaa naaning'ie-- njening'!"
Mark7:17 Ore pejing' ninye atua aji-- eing'ua olorere-- neikilikwan laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye ina kitanyanyukiet."
