Mark7:18 Nejoki ninye ninje: Ke nji miatata si ndai eng'eno? Epon eitu iyolouu si ndai-- ajo entoki pookin e oriong' oltung'ani najing' atua ninye-- meidim aitaa ninye torrono?"
Mark7:19 Amu mejing' ninye atua oltau-- kake atua engoshoke ake-- nepuku tʼosiadi oitai ndaikin pookin."
Mark7:20 Nejo ninye: Ore enapuku tʼoltung'ani-- ninye naitaa oltung'ani torrono;"
Mark7:21 amu epuku tiatua oltau lʼoltung'ani ndamunot torrok-- entalare-- empurrore-- earata metua--"
Mark7:22 earata osotua lʼenkiama-- olng'warra-- ntorrok-- olosek-- enkiborra oo ngonyek-- engong'u torrono-- morot Engai-- olwuasa-- emodaishu."
Mark7:23 Amu tiatua epuku kuna torrok pookin neitaa oltung'ani torrono.
Mark7:24 Nedumunye ninye te ina alo nelo metabaiki rishat e Tiros o Sidon. Ore peidip atijing'a aji-- neyeu-- pemeyolou oltung'ani-- neitu eidim aisudori."
Mark7:25 Amu etoning'o nabokata eng'oroyoni nabo mbaak enyena-- neata entito enye Olmumua duruki-- nelotu nebatatakino ninye nkejek"
Mark7:26 (nera ena ng'oroyoni Engriki entipat e Siro-Foinike) nesai ninye-- pemir olmeneng'ani tiatua entito enye."
Mark7:27 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Tang'asa njoo eraposho nkera; amu me sidai-- teni eitauni endaa oo nkera-- penang'akini ildiain."
Mark7:28 Nealu si ninye nejoki ninye: Ee-- Laitoriani-- kake enya si ildiain mbelat oo nkera te kop enaraa."
Mark7:29 Nejoki ninye: Tʼolbae le ilo rorei nno! Etupukuo olmeneng'ani tʼentito ino.
Mark7:30 Nelo ang' neinepu entito-- eirrag tʼerruat-- etupukuo olmeneng'ani."
Mark7:31 Neitoki apuku tʼerishata e Tiros neim Sidon nelotu metabaiki olbalbal le Galilaya-- erishata oo Manyat tomon."
Mark7:32 Nerikoki ninje ninye oltung'ani ming'ani lemeiro sidai nesai ninye-- peiteleiki ninye engaina."
Mark7:33 Nerishu ninye lʼesiamu nerik ewueji enye openy nepik ilkimojik lenyena atua nkiyaa enyena nenotu nkamulak neing'unye olng'ejep lenye
Mark7:34 neimariri shumata neang' nejoki ninye: Efata! eji: Taboloi!
Mark7:35 Nebolo nabokata nkiyaa enyena nelaa eenet olng'ejep lenye neiro sidai.
Mark7:36 Neitanap ninye ninje-- pemeliki oltung'ani. Kake neijia anaa peitanapa ninje-- nepon naleng' aainosaa."
Mark7:37 Neing'asia naleng' nelang' ejo: Eitobira ninye pookin sidai; neisho ilming'an-- pening'ishoi-- peiro lemeidim aairoro."
Mark8:1 Ore too nona olong'i neitoki aaku esiamu kitok naleng'-- nemeata ninje endaa-- neipot Yesus laiteng'enuok lenyena nejoki ninje:"
Mark8:2 Aibung'aki olorere engoshoke nanana-- amu etaa taata ngolong'i uni-- etobiko tʼenatii-- meata enanya--"
Mark8:3 ore paitanapaa ninje-- pepuo ngang'itie enye epukoo-- nepuo aaiterre tʼengoitoi; amu eing'ua ematua enye tʼenelakwa."
Mark8:4 Nealiki laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye: Kaji etumie oltung'ani ilmkaten tʼena alo e ang'ata looraposh kulo?
Mark8:5 Neikilikwan ninje: Ke ilmkaten aja iatata? Nejo ninje: Oopishana.
Mark8:6 Neitanap esiamu-- petoni tʼenkop. Neibung' ninye kulo mkaten oopishana nejo ashe nebelibel neisho laiteng'enuok lenyena-- peitarasaa. Neitarasaki ninje olorere."
Mark8:7 Neata si looti singir kuti; ore peidip atamayana ninje-- nejo meitarasai si ninje kulo."
Mark8:8 Nenya ninje neraposho-- nedumu ilmong'oitie loo mbelat oo lmkaten ilbenia oopishana."
Mark8:9 Nebaia iltung'anak looinosa endaa-- iip artam. Neitanapaa ninje."
Mark8:10 Neilepaki ninye nabokata engalawa te nebo o laiteng'enuok lenyena nelo mbatai e Dalmanuta.
Mark8:11 Nepuku Ilfarisayoi neiter aaikilikwanaro o ninye neing'oru te ninye olponoto oing'ua shumata aatem ninye.
Mark8:12 Neang' ninye tʼolmumua lenye nejo: Ainyo peing'oru ena kishon olponoto? Japa-- aliki ndai: Meishori ena kishon olponoto."
Mark8:13 Neing'ua ninje neitoki ailepaki engalawa nelo metabaiki lido kekun.
Mark8:14 Nerikino ninje enap ilmkaten-- neitu eata tiatua engalawa neme olmkate obo ake."
Mark8:15 Neitanap ninje ejo: Eng'orai-- piduaiaia aten tʼenkisiijoi oo Lfarisayoi o tʼenkisiijoi e Herodes."
Mark8:16 Neibirribir ninje tʼempolos enye ejo: Tiaraki nimikiata ilmkaten.
Mark8:17 Neyolou Yesus ena nejoki ninje: Ainyo pimbirribirrirri-- aajo tiaraki nimikiata ilmkaten? Epon miyolouu nimidamishosho? Epon iatata iltauja oogol?"
Mark8:18 Iatata ngonyek-- nimidolishosho; niatata nkiyaa-- nimining'ishosho-- nimidamishosho."
Mark8:19 Ore patigiligilaka le naarri mkaten imiet atua iip onom-- ke ilbenia aja eiganya ndung'ot nitudumutua? Nejoki ninje ninye: Tomon o are."
Mark8:20 Ore patigiligilaka kulo oopishana atua iip artam-- ke-- ilbenia aja eiganya mbelat nitudumutua? Nejo ninje: Oopishana."
Mark8:21 Nejoki ninye ninje: Kaji etiu-- pepon eitu iyolouu?"
Mark8:22 Nepuonu ninje Betsaida. Nerikoki ninje olmodooni nesai ninye-- peporoo ninye."
Mark8:23 Neibung' ninye olmodooni engaina nerik aulo engang' nenotaki ngamulak ngonyek enyena neiteleiki ninye ngaik neikilikwan ninye: Idolita toki?
Mark8:24 Neimariri ninye shumata nejo: Adolita iltung'anak elimana anaa iljanito.
Mark8:25 Neitoki aiteleiki ninye ngaik ngonyek enyena-- neing'oraa naleng'-- netum ataa bioto nedol ntokitin pookin abaraki."
Mark8:26 Neirriwaa ninye-- pelo engaji enye-- ejo: Mijing' atua engang' nimiliki oltung'ani tiatua engang'."
Mark8:27 Nepuku Yesus o laiteng'enuok lenyena-- pepuo ngang'itie e Kaisarea-Filipi. Neikilikwan ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena tʼengoitoi nejoki ninje: Kejo iltung'anak-- ara nanu ng'ai?"
Mark8:28 Nejoki ninje ninye-- ejo: Yohanes Olaibatisani; nejo ilkulekai: Eliya; o ilkulekai: obo too layolounok."
Mark8:29 Neikilikwan ninye ninje: Ijojo ndai-- ara nanu ng'ai? Nealu Petros nejoki ninye: Ira iye Kristos!"
Mark8:30 Neitanap-- pemeliki ninje oltung'ani mbaak enyena."
Mark8:31 Neiter aiteng'en ninje-- ajo meata kata nemeisilisili Enkerai oltung'ani too nkumok-- neany laigwenak o laidasak kituak o layolok lʼesirata ninye-- near ninye metua-- nelapiu ninye-- eishunyete ngolong'i uni."
Mark8:32 Neiro ninye ele rorei abaraki. Neibung' Petros ninye nerik ewueji enye openy neiter aisikong' ninye.
Mark8:33 Neibelekenya ninye neing'oraa laiteng'enuok lenyena nebuaki Petros-- ejo: Nyaai kurum ai-- satan-- amu mimbirribir nara nʼEngai-- kake nara noo ltung'anak."
Mark8:34 Neipot esiamu enetii ninye te nebo o laiteng'enuok lenyena nejoki ninje: Oloyeu naasuj tekurum ai-- njemiki kion-- njedumakino esalaba enye-- paasuj."
Mark8:35 Amu oloyeu neitopok oltau lenye-- nelaiminye ninye; oloiminye oltau lenye tʼolbae lai o tʼolbae loo lomon lʼeng'ida-- neitopok ninye."
Mark8:36 Kaa dupoto etum oltung'ani-- teni eng'eru ninye olmaa pookin-- netum elaunoto Olmumua lenye?"
Mark8:37 Arashu kainyo elakunye oltung'ani oltau lenye?
Mark8:38 Amu oloibung' enkurruna te nanu o too rorei lainei tiatua ena kishon eloloito naitarruo-- nelaibung'aki Enkerai oltung'ani ilo enkurruna-- teni elotu tʼenkitook e Menye lenye te nebo o ilmalaikan sinyat."
Mark9:1 Nejoki ninye ninje: Japa-- aliki ndai: Etii iltung'anak atua kulo ooitashe tene lemeinyorrinyor enkea-- metabana nedol enkarsishu Engai eewuo tʼengolon."
Mark9:2 Ore peishunye ngolong'i ile-- negelu Yesus Petros o Yakobos o Yohanes nerik ninje keper oldonyo oado-- ewueji enye oopeny-- neitaali emua enye too ngomomi enye."
Mark9:3 Neaku eitintilu ilkilani lenyena neiborru naleng' anaa esiret lemeidim aiborrie olaria lʼenkop neijia.
Mark9:4 Nelioi too ninje Eliya te nebo o Mose-- neaku eder ninje o Yesus."
Mark9:5 Nealu Petros nejoki Yesus: Laiteng'enani-- sidai kitii yook ene! Mateshet tene iltomboitie okuni: obo lino-- obo le Mose-- obo le Eliya."
Mark9:6 Amu eitu eyolou ninye enataalua; amu etaa kureti.
Mark9:7 Neaku erukenya naiopoiye ninje nepuku oltoilo tʼerukenya ojo: Nyele Oinoti lai lanyor: entoning' ninye!
Mark9:8 Ore te ina kata peing'oraa ngaloli pookin neitu eitoki aadol oltung'ani neme Yesus ake openy te nebo o ninje.
Mark9:9 Ore edou ninje tʼoldonyo-- neitanap ninje-- pemeinosaki oltung'ani naatadua ninje metabaiki ina kata-- eidipa atopiu Enkerai oltung'ani tiatua lootuata."
Mark9:10 Neibung' ninje ilo rorei neikilikwanaro oopeny tʼempolos enye: Kainyo empiunoto too lootuata?
Mark9:11 Neikilikwan ninje ninye ejo: Mejo layolok lʼesirata-- aajo meata kata nemeng'as alotu Eliya?"
Mark9:12 Nejoki ninye ninje: Esipa-- eng'as alotu Eliya-- peitobiraki pookin; kake te nebo o nena etisirakinyeki Enkerai oltung'ani-- ajo eisilisili naleng' nemeni."
Mark9:13 Kake aliki ndai: Eidipa aeu Eliya-- neitobiraki ninje ninye anaa petayeutuo-- anaa petisirakaki ninye."
Mark9:14 Ore pelotu ninye enetii laiteng'enuok lenyena-- nedol esiamu kitok emanita ninje o layolok lʼesirata ooikilikwanare ninje."
Mark9:15 Ore nabokata pedol esiamu ninye-- neing'asia nekwetiki aairo roki ninye."
Mark9:16 Neikilikwan ninye layolok lʼesirata: Kainyo inkilikwanarere ninje?
Mark9:17 Nealiki oltung'ani obo tiatua esiamu ninye: Laiteng'enani-- aaua enkerai ai enitii-- neata ninye Olmumua lemeiro;"
Mark9:18 ore teni edumaki ninye-- neiponyipony ninye; nepuku olaburra nenya lala netoi; nairorie laiteng'enuok linono-- petum aatimir; neitu eidim ninje."
Mark9:19 Nealiki ninje ejo: Ndai-- enkishon nemeiruk-- ke metabaiki anu aboitare nanu ndai? Ke-- metabaiki anu ang'iriaki ndai? Eakaki!"
Mark9:20 Neaki ninye. Ore pedol Olmumua ninye-- neiponyipony nabokata ninye-- neurokino enkop neibeleleng'ori nepuku olaburra."
Mark9:21 Neikilikwan ninye menye lenye: Ke ti aa kata eitera aibung' kuna? Nejo ninye: Tʼenkitishu.
Mark9:22 Etanang'aka ninye aigil kumok atua enkima o atua engare-- peiminye ninye. Kake teni indim toki-- mbung'aki yook engoshoke nanana-- piretoki yook!"
Mark9:23 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Teni indim airuko! Eidimai pookin tʼoloiruk.
Mark9:24 Neapaa nabo kata menye lʼenkerai oltoilo-- nepuku ilkiyo-- nejo: Airuk-- Laitoriani-- taretokoki mairuk!"
Mark9:25 Ore pedol Yesus-- ajo ekwetu olorere amurutokino-- nebuaki Olmumua duruki nejoki ninye: Lemumua lemeiro naa ming'ani-- aaitanap nanu iye: Tupuku te ninye nimintoki ajing' atua ninye!"
Mark9:26 Neapaa Olmumua oltoilo neiponyipony ninye naleng' nepuku; neaku enyanyukie lemeishiu-- nejo baiki ilkumok: Etua ninye."
Mark9:27 Kake eibung'a Yesus ninye engaina neapaa; neitashe ninye.
Mark9:28 Ore peidip atijing'a aji-- neikilikwan laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye tʼewueji enye oopeny; Ainyo peitu kindim yook aatimir ninye?"
Mark9:29 Nejoki ninye ninje; Meidim ena mua atupuku neme tʼesayata o tʼempukoroto.
Mark9:30 Nepuku ninje te ina alo neibung' engoitoi neim Galilaya; neitu eyeu ninye-- peyolo oltung'ani."
Mark9:31 Amu eiteng'ena ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena nejoki ninje: Eitarasakini Enkerai oltung'ani atua ngaik oo ltung'anak near ninje ninye metua. Ore peidip aataar-- nepiu ninye-- eishunyete ngolong'i uni."
Mark9:32 Neitu eyolou ninje ilo rorei neurei eikilikwan ninye.
Mark9:33 Nepuonu ninje Kapernaum. Ore etii ninje atua aji-- neikiliwan ninye ninje: Kainyo imbirribirrutua tʼengoitoi?"
Mark9:34 Negira ninje-- amu eibirribirrutua tʼempolos enye: Kalo lora kitok."
Mark9:35 Neton ninye neipot kulo tomon o are nejoki ninje: Oloyeu neaku lʼelukunya-- njeaku lʼenkiting'oto too pookin o olaisyayani loo pookin."
Mark9:36 Neibung' ninye enkerai nabo neitasheye ninye tʼempolos enye nejap ninye nejoki ninje:
Mark9:37 Oloitoomon nabo too kuna kera tʼengarna ai-- nanu eitoomon; ore olaaitoomon nanu-- me nanu eitoomon-- kake olaairriua."
Mark9:38 Nejoki Yohanes ninye: Laiteng'enani-- kitadua oltung'ani lomirita ilmeneng'a tʼengarna ino leitu esujare yook-- nikimitiki yook ninye-- tiaraki neitu esuj yook."
Mark9:39 Nejo Yesus: Emimitiki ninye-- amu metii oltung'ani loitobir entoki engolon tʼengarna ai neiriamare aaimaki nanu tʼentorroni."
Mark9:40 Amu olemeiba yook-- nera lʼematua ang'."
Mark9:41 Amu oloitook ndai tʼeoket engare tʼengarna ai-- tiaraki nirara le Kristos-- japa-- aliki ndai: Meiminaki ninye tukul olkwaje lenye."
Mark9:42 Oloitapong'oo nabo too kuna kutiti naairuk nanu-- eikash-- teni eenikini emurt enye osoit oituutishoreki-- nenang'akini ninye atua olbalbal."
Mark9:43 Teni kintapong'oo engaina ino-- tudung'o ninye; eikash-- ijing' atua empuan-- iata enkumur-- nelang' iata ngaik pokira are-- nilo atua ewueji e satan-- atua enkima nememuta--"
Mark9:44 enemee olkurto lenye nemee enkima enye.
Mark9:45 Teni kintapong'oo enkeju ino-- tudung'o ninye; eikash-- ijing' atua empuan-- ira ng'ojine-- nelang' iata nkejek pokira are-- nikinang'akini atua ewueji e satan-- atua enkima nememuta--"
Mark9:46 enemee olkurto lenye nemee enkima enve.
Mark9:47 Teni kintapong'oo engong'u ino-- nturrai ninye; eikash-- ijing' atua enkarsishu Engai-- ira mulug ong'u-- nelang' iata ngonyek pokira are nikinang'akini atua enkima e satan--"
Mark9:48 enemee olkurto lenye nemee enkima enye.
Mark9:49 Amu eitijing'ari oltung'ani pookin emakat tʼenkima-- neitijing'ari enkidasare pookin emakat."
Mark9:50 Sidai emakat-- kake teni etarruoiye emakat-- te nyoo eitaai ninye sidai? Njoo iatata emakat tiatua ndai o eseriani tʼempolos inyi."
Mark10:1 Nedumunye te ina alo nelotu rishat e Yudaya tʼolkekun le Yordan. Neitoki aaiturrurrokino ninye siamin-- neitoki aiteng'en ninje anaa petamoo."
Mark10:2 Nepuonu enetii ninye Ilfarisayoi neikilikwan ninye: Ke sidai-- teni eing'ua olmoruo eng'oroyoni enye? etemita ninje ninye."
Mark10:3 Nealiki si ninye nejoki ninje: Ainyo eitanapa Mose ndai?
Mark10:4 Nejo si ninje: Eiruko Mose-- pesiri empalai erishata-- neing'ua ninye."
Mark10:5 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Tiaraki natagolito iltauja linyi-- onaa etisiraka ndai ena kitanapata."
Mark10:6 Kake neba tʼenkiterata enkitobirata eitobira Engai olee o eng'oroyoni;
Mark10:7 onaa-- eing'ua oltung'ani menye o ng'otonye neibung'are eng'oroyoni enye--"
Mark10:8 neaku pokira are osesen obo; nemeitoki aaku aare-- kake osesen obo."
Mark10:9 Akae-- ore enaidikidiko Engai-- njoo merish oltung'ani."
Mark10:10 Neitoki aaikilikwan laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye tiatua aji mbaak e ilo rorei.
Mark10:11 Nejoki ninje: Oloing'ua eng'oroyoni enye neamu engai-- near osotua lʼenkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni te ninye;"
Mark10:12 naa teni eing'ua eng'oroyoni olmoruo lenye neamaa olekai-- near osotua lʼenkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni."
Mark10:13 Nerikoki ninje nkera kunyinyi-- peiye eporoo ninje. Nebuaki laiteng'enuok lenyena kulo lootorikutuo."
Mark10:14 Ore pedol Yesus ena-- neisikong' ninye nejoki ninje: Enjoo nkera epuonu enatii-- emimitiki ninje-- amu era enkarsishu Engai noo loonyanyukie nena."
Mark10:15 Japa-- aliki ndai: Olemeng'amu enkarsishu Engai anaa enkerai-- nemejing' ninye atua tukul."
Mark10:16 Nejap ninje nemayan neiteleiki ninje ngaik.
Mark10:17 Ore pepuku ninye aim engoitoi-- nekwetu oltung'ani obo negilaki ninye kung' neikilikwan ninye: Laiteng'enani sidai-- kainyo aitobir-- paidim atujung'u empuan nemeiting'?"
Mark10:18 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Ainyo pikijo sidai? Metii osidai neme obo lora Engai.
Mark10:19 Itayolo nkitanapat: Miar metua; miar enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni; mipurrisho; minjakenoki oltung'ani elejare; misimaa; ntaa kituak minyi o ng'utunyi!
Mark10:20 Nejoki ninye: Laiteng'enani-- aibung'a nena pookin neba tʼenkitishu ai."
Mark10:21 Neing'oraa Yesus ninye nenyorru ninye nejoki ninye: Nabo nikitong'orikia. Nno-- timira pookin niata-- pinjo laisinak-- nilaata masaa te shumata; ore pindip-- wou-- tusujaki nidumakino esalaba ino!"
Mark10:22 Neilish ninye tʼolbae lʼele rorei-- nelo eing'irisa; amu eata masaa kumok."
Mark10:23 Neing'orong'oraa Yesus mbat pookin nejoki laiteng'enuok lenyena: Oi egol-- pejing' looata masaa atua enkarsishu Engai."
Mark10:24 Neing'asia laiteng'enuok lenyena too kulo rorei lenyena. Neitoki aliki Yesus nejoki ninje: Nakera-- oi egol looirishakino masaa ejing' atua enkarsishu Engai!"
Mark10:25 Elelek eim endames eudoto esindano nelang' oladupani ejing' atua enkarsishu Engai.
Mark10:26 Neing'asia ninje naleng' nejokino: Ang'ai naa loidim atopua?
Mark10:27 Neing'oraa Yesus ninje ejo: Meidimai ena too ltung'anak-- kake eidimai tʼEngai; amu eidimai ntokitin pookin tʼEngai."
Mark10:28 Neiter Petros ajoki ninye: Ng'orai-- kitung'aitie yook pookin nikisuj iye."
Mark10:29 Nejo Yesus: Japa-- aliki ndai: Metii oltung'ani otung'aiye engaji arashu lalashera arashu nganashera arashu ng'otonye arashu menye arashu nkera arashu nkuruman tʼolbae lai o tʼolbae loo lomon lʼeng'ida--"
Mark10:30 nemeng'amu aigil iip taata tʼena kata ngajijik o lalashera o nganashera o noong'otonye o nkera o nkuruman eshula o sinaitin-- o tiatua olmaa olotu empuan nemeiting'."
Mark10:31 Neaku ilkumok lʼelukunya lʼenkiting'oto o lʼenkiting'oto lʼelukunya.
Mark10:32 Netii ninje engoitoi eilep aapuo Yerusalem; neiturukie Yesus ninje-- neing'asia ninje neureishoi esujita. Neitoki aibung' Yesus kulo tomon o are neiter aliki ninje mbaak naapuo aaku te ninye-- ejo:"
Mark10:33 Eng'orai-- kishumari metabaiki Yerusalem-- neitarasakini Enkerai oltung'ani laidasak kituak o layolok lʼesirata-- nepuo aaigwenaki ninye-- pee-- neitarasaki ninye loreren lemeata Engai;"
Mark10:34 nemor ninje ninye nenotaki ngamulak near too nkeenda near ninye metua-- nelapiu ninye-- eishunyete ngolong'i uni."
Mark10:35 Nepuonu Yakobos o Yohanes-- nkera e Sebedayos-- enetii ninye nejoki ninye: Laiteng'enani-- kiyeu nintobiraki yook enikionionu iye."
Mark10:36 Nejoki ninye ninje: Kainyo iyeuu naitobiraki ndai?
Mark10:37 Nejoki ninje ninye: Njoo yook kitoni obo te tatene ino o obo te kedyanye ino tiatua enkitook ino.
Mark10:38 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Miyololo ndai eniomonunu. Indimidimi ndai aatook enkwaru naok nanu-- neibatisi ndai tʼenkibatisa naaibatisieki nanu?"
Mark10:39 Nejoki ninje ninye: Ee-- kindim. Nejoki Yesus ninje: Ore enkwaru naok nanu nipuopuo aaok-- neibatisi ndai tʼenkibatisa naaibatisieki nanu;"
Mark10:40 kake entonata te tatene o te kedyanye ai me enai-- paisho ndai-- kake eishori looitobirakaki."
Mark10:41 Ore pening' ena kulo tomon-- neiter aagorokino Yakobos o Yohanes."
Mark10:42 Neipotu Yesus ninje enetii ninye nejoki ninje: Iyololo-- aajo eitorisho kulo ooikenari aaku ilkarsisi loo loreren neata ilkituak lenye engolon too ninje."
Mark10:43 Meaku nji too ndai! Kake oloyeu neaku kitok too ndai-- njeaku olaisyayani linyi;"
Mark10:44 oloyeu tiatua ndai neaku lʼelukunya-- njeaku olaisyayani loo pookin."
Mark10:45 Amu eitu elotu si ninye-- Enkerai oltung'ani-- peisyayakini ninye-- kake peisyaisho ninye neishooio empuan enye-- peaku elakunoto oo lkumok."
Mark10:46 Nepuonu ninje Yeriko. Ore peibung' ninye engoitoi aing'ua Yeriko te nebo o laiteng'enuok lenyena o esiamu kitok-- neton Bartimayos-- enkerai e Timayos-- ora olmodooni-- tʼembata engoitoi eomonisho."
Mark10:47 Ore pening' ninye-- ajo ore Yesus le Nasaret ilo-- neiter aapaa oltoilo ejo: Yesus-- nakerai e David-- tokorduaki!"
Mark10:48 Nebuaki iltung'anak kumok ninye-- pegira. Nepon ninye naleng' aapaa oltoilo: Nakerai e David-- tokorduaki!"
Mark10:49 Neitashe Yesus nejo: Empoto ninye. Neipot ninje ilo modooni nejoki ninye: Ntagolo oltau-- nyototoi-- kimpot ninye!"
Mark10:50 Neiturraa ninye olkila lenye neipirri nelo enetii Yesus.
Mark10:51 Nealiki Yesus ninye nejo: Kainyo iyeu naaitobiraki? Nejoki olmodooni ninye: Laiteng'enani-- padolishoi."
Mark10:52 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Nno-- kitaretoko enkirukoto ino. Nedolishoi ninye nabokata nesuj ninye tʼengoitoi."
Mark11:1 Ore penyikaki ninje Yerusalem nebaia Betfage o Betania metabaiki Oldonyo loo loirienito-- neirriwaa ninye aare too laiteng'enuok lenyena--"
Mark11:2 nejoki ninje: Enjom enkiti ang' naitoriokinore ndai; ore nabokata-- teni ijing'ijing'i-- inepupu enkurrarru osikiria naena nepon eitu eilepaki oltung'ani o obo ninye; entalakutu ninye-- entereakaki!"
Mark11:3 Ore pejoki oltung'ani ndai: Ainyo pinkoko nji? entejo: Olaitoriani oyeu ninye; neirriu nabokata ene.
Mark11:4 Nepuo neinepu enkurrarru osikiria naena te kishomi-- ti aulo tʼerishata engoitoi-- nelaku ninye."
Mark11:5 Nejoki ematua oo kulo ooitashe te ine ninje: Kainyo intobiribiri-- ilakuku enkurrarru osikiria?"
Mark11:6 Nejoki ninje anaa peitanapua Yesus-- neing'uaiki ninje."
Mark11:7 Nereu ninje enkurrarru osikiria enetii Yesus neisalaashaki ninye ilkilani lenye-- neton ninye te shumata enye."
Mark11:8 Neisalaash ilkumok ilkilani lenye tʼengoitoi; nedung'u kulekai ilng'osil too ljanito neisalaash tʼengoitoi.
Mark11:9 Ore looiturukie o loosujita neapaa iltoiloi ejo: Hosiana! Njeitadarari ololotu lʼengarna Olaitoriani!
Mark11:10 Njeitadarari enkarsishu nalotu e papa lang' David. Hosiana te shumata!
Mark11:11 Nejing' Yesus Yerusalem atua engaji sinyati; neing'orong'oraa ngaloli pookin; ore pemutu-- nepuku nelo Betania te nebo o kulo tomon o are."
Mark11:12 Ore enasirie-- pepuku ninje te Betania-- neibung' olamei ninye."
Mark11:13 Nedol tʼenelakwa olng'aboli oata mbenek nelotu-- peiye etum toki te shumata enye. Ore pelotu enetii-- neitu etum toki neme mbenek-- amu me enkata oo lng'abolo."
Mark11:14 Nealu nejoki ninye: Njoo meitoki anya nkatan pookin oltung'ani ilmomo te iye! Nening' laiteng'enuok lenyena ina.
Mark11:15 Nepuonu Yerusalem. Nejing' Yesus atua engaji sinyati neiter amir lamirak o lainyang'ak tiatua engaji sinyati neibelekeny naraan oo laitaalak loo ngoshola o lorikaishi loo lamirak loo lmaita--"
Mark11:16 neitu eisho oltung'ani enap enaret eim engaji sinyati.
Mark11:17 Neiteng'enisho nejoki ninje: Keitu esiri: Eipoti engaji ai engaji esayata oo loreren pookin? Kake intaa ndai ninye engapunet oo laisimak.
Mark11:18 Nening' laidasak kituak o layolok lʼesirata nona neing'oru eneiko petum aaiminye ninye. Neurei ake ninye amu eing'asiaiye esiamu pookin enkiteng'enare enye.
Mark11:19 Ore peaku emutu-- nepuku nelo aulo engang'."
Mark11:20 Ore enasirie egiroo ine-- nedol ele ng'aboli etoiyo-- eiter too ntonat."
Mark11:21 Nedamu Petros nejoki ninye: Laiteng'enani-- ng'orai olng'aboli litedia etoiyo."
Mark11:22 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninje: Embung'a enkirukoto atua Engai.
Mark11:23 Japa-- aliki ndai: Ore oltung'ani pookin ojoki ele donyo: Tadotunye-- pinang'akino atua olbalbal! nemeing'arrirro tʼoltau lenye-- kake eiruk-- ajo eaku enajo — neaku te ninye anaa petejo."
Mark11:24 Onaa aliki ndai: Ore pookin niomonunu tʼesayata inyi-- eruko-- aajo ing'amumu-- neaku eninyi."
Mark11:25 Ore pintasheshe isaishosho-- entung'aikiti-- teni iataiyeye oltung'ani entoki-- peiye eing'uaiki si ninye-- Minyi linyi otii shumata-- ndai nkitarruot inyi."
Mark11:26 Teni ming'uaikiki ndai-- nemeing'uaiki baiki ndai Minyi linyi otii shumata nkitarruot inyi."
Mark11:27 Neitoki aabaia ninje Yerusalem. Ore elimana ninye tiatua engaji sinyati-- nepuonu laidasak kituak o layolok lʼesirata o laigwenak enetii ninye--"
Mark11:28 nejoki ninye: Ke ti aa golon intobirita kuna? Kang'ai likinjoo ena golon-- pitum aitobira kuna?"
Mark11:29 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Aikilikwan si nanu ndai ororei obo-- pikialikiki-- tekurum naliki si nanu ndai-- ke ti aa golon aitobirita kuna."
Mark11:30 Kera enkibatisa e Yohanes ne shumata anai noo ltung'anak? Entaalikiaki!
Mark11:31 Neibirribir ninje tʼempolos enye ejo: Teni kijo: Eing'ua shumata! nejo ninye: Ainyo naa peitu irukuruku ninye?
Mark11:32 Kake teni kijo: Eing'ua atua iltung'anak! — neturia ninje olorere. Amu etejo pookin-- ajo era Yohanes olayolounoni tʼesipata."
Mark11:33 Nealiki ninje Yesus nejo: Mikiyolo. Nejoki si Yesus ninje: Majoki si nanu ndai-- ke ti aa golon aitobirita kuna."
Mark12:1 Neiter airorie ninje too nkitanyanyukieta ajo: Etuuno oltung'ani enkuruma oo nkeek olmarua neitaman osariko netur engumoto naironyishoreki neshet olmnara neitamany laturok nelo olototo.
Mark12:2 Neirriwaki laturok tʼenkata enye olaisyayani obo-- peng'amu too laturok ilmomo lʼenkuruma oo nkeek olmarua."
Mark12:3 Neibung' ninje ninye near neitupuku-- meata toki."
Mark12:4 Neitoki airriwaki ninje olekai aisyayani; nebor ilo elukunya-- nemor ninye neitupuku."
Mark12:5 Neitoki airriwaa olekai; near ilo metua; o kulekai kumok; near ilkulekai o ilkulekai near metuata.
Mark12:6 Akae-- epon eata obo-- Oinoti lenye onyor; neitoki airriwaki ninje tʼenkiting'oto ninye ejo: Eanyitu Oinoti lai."
Mark12:7 Kake nejokino kulo aturok tʼempolos enye: Era ele olajung'oni; maapeti mataar ninye metua-- peaku enjung'o enang'."
Mark12:8 Neibung' ninje ninye near metua nenang'aki oriong' enkuruma oo nkeek olmarua.
Mark12:9 Kainyo elaitobir Olaitoriani lʼenkuruma oo nkeek olmarua? Elotu ninye neiminye kulo aturok neisho ena kuruma oo nkeek olmarua ilkulekai.
Mark12:10 Epon eitu isomama ndai ena sirata: Ore osoit lotanyaita lashetak-- etaa ele osoit kitok lʼolpijata."
Mark12:11 Etaa ina tʼOlaitoriani-- naiputukunyisho ninye too ngonyek ang'?"
Mark12:12 Neing'oru ninje eneiko-- peibung'-- neurei esiamu-- amu etayoloutuo-- aajo eirorie ninje te ina kitanyanyukiet. Neing'ua ninye nepuo."
Mark12:13 Neirriwaki ninye ematua oo Lfarisayoi o noo laisyayak le Herodes-- perresh ninye too rorei."
Mark12:14 Ore pepuonu-- nejoki ninye: Laiteng'enani-- kiyolo-- aajo ira oltung'ani lʼesipata-- nimishilaa entemet oltung'ani; amu naing'oraa emua oltung'ani-- kake inteng'enu tʼesipata engoitoi Engai. Ke sidai-- teni eishori kaisar kodi arashu me? Ke kinjooio arashu me?"
Mark12:15 Neyolou ninye enkitusupatuo enye nejoki ninje: Ainyo pikitemiteme? Eakaki endenarion nabo-- padol ninye!"
Mark12:16 Neau. Nejoki ninje: Ken e ng'ai ena mua o ena sirata? Nejoki ninje ninye: Ne kaisar.
Mark12:17 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Akae-- enjoo kaisar en e kaisar-- o Engai en Engai! Neiputukunyoki ninye naleng'."
Mark12:18 Nepuonu Sadukayoi enetii ninye oojo: metii empiunoto-- neikilikwan ninye nejo:"
Mark12:19 Laiteng'enani-- etisiraka yook Mose: Teni ee olalashe lʼoltung'ani neing'ua eng'oroyoni nemeata enkerai-- njeamaa olalashe lenye aitaa eng'oroyoni enye-- netumoki olalashe lenye olmuate."
Mark12:20 Netii lalashera oopishana: Neamu ol elukunya eng'oroyoni nee ninye-- neitu eing'ua eishoi;"
Mark12:21 neamu ole are ninye nee-- neitu eing'ua eishoi; neijia baiki oli okuni."
Mark12:22 Neamu neijia kulo oopishana ninye-- neitu eing'ua eishoi. Ore tʼenkiting'oto oo pookin nee si ninye-- ina ng'oroyoni."
Mark12:23 Akae-- ore tʼempiunoto-- teni epuo aapiu ninje-- eaku eng'oroyoni en e alo too ninje? Amu eamutua ninye kulo oopishana."
Mark12:24 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Me neijia? Imanimanaana-- amu miyololo sirat o engolon Engai."
Mark12:25 Amu teni epuo aapiu tiatua lootuata ninje-- nemepuo aamisho nemepuoi aamaa-- kake eaku ninje anaa ilmalaikan ootii shumata."
Mark12:26 Ore too mbaak oo lootuata-- aajo epuo aapiu-- eitu isomama ndai tiatua enkitabu e Mose tʼolodung'oro eneikuna teni ejoki Engai ninye-- ejo: Ara nanu Engai e Abraham o Engai e Isaak o Engai e Yakoob?"
Mark12:27 Mera Engai Engai oo lootuata-- kake noo looishiu. Onaa imanimanaana ndai naleng'."
Mark12:28 Nelotu obo loo layolok lʼesirata-- etoning'o eikilikwanaro ninje-- neyolou-- ajo etaalikia ninje sidai-- neikilikwan ninye: Kaa kitanapata nara en elukunya oo pookin?"
Mark12:29 Nealu Yesus nejo: Ena nara kitok alang' pookin: Toning'o-- Israel-- era Olaitoriani-- Engai ino-- Olaitoriani obo!"
Mark12:30 Tonyorra Olaitoriani-- Engai ino-- tʼoltau lino pookin o tʼolmumua lino pookin o tʼeng'eno ino pookin o tʼengolon ino pookin. Ena enkitanapata elukunya."
Mark12:31 Ore en e are narisiore ninye: Tonyora ol elatia ino anaa pinyor kion! Metii engai kitanapata nara kitok nelang' kuna.
Mark12:32 Nejoki olayoloni lʼesirata ninye: Sidai-- Laiteng'enani-- itolimuo esipata-- ajo etii Engai nabo ake-- nemetii engai neme ninye;"
Mark12:33 teni inyorru ninye tʼoltau pookin o tʼeyolounoto pookin o tʼolmumua pookin o tʼengolon pookin-- ninyorru ol elatia anaa kion — etalang'a ena naleng' nkidasareitin naapejori o nkulie kidasareitin."
Mark12:34 Ore pedol Yesus-- ajo etaalua ninye tʼeng'eno-- nejoki ninye: Milakwaniki enkarsishu Engai. Neitu eitoki aiteu oltung'ani o obo aikilikwana ninye ororei."
Mark12:35 Nealu Yesus nejo-- eiteng'enisho tiatua engaji sinyati: Kejaa layolok lʼesirata-- ajo era Kristos enkerai e David?"
Mark12:36 Netejo David openy tʼenkidimata Olmumua Sinyati: Etiaka Olaitoriani Olaitoriani lai: Totona te tatene ai-- metabana napik ilmang'ati linono abori oo nkejek inono."
Mark12:37 Neipot David ninye Olaitoriani lenye — kaji eiko naa teni era enkerai enye? Nenyorru olorere kitok aatoning' ninye.
Mark12:38 Nejo ninye tiatua enkiteng'enare enye: Entaduai aten too layolok lʼesirata loonyorru aalimanare tiatua ilkilani adoru nenyor nkirorokinot too singiraitin
Mark12:39 o ntoneta elukunya tiatua ngajijik Engai o nkirragat elukunya tʼengalo oo ndaikin;
Mark12:40 loonya ngajijik oo ngolia neitador sayat tʼenkitusupatuo. Nepuo aang'amu ninje enkigwena kitok nalang'.
Mark12:41 Neton Yesus aishiaakinore eneitadoikini mpesai engaji Engai neing'oraa olorere lopikita mpesai atua eneitadoikini; nepik ladupak kumok nkumok.
Mark12:42 Nelotu engoliai nabo aisinani-- nepik naabebek are-- nera esenti nabo."
Mark12:43 Neipot ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena nejoki ninje: Japa-- aliki ndai: Ore ena oliai nara aisinani etipika nelang' kulekai pookin lootipika mpesai atua eneitadoikini;"
Mark12:44 amu etipika ninje pookin tʼenkumoi enye-- ore ena etipika tʼesinaishu enye pookin naata-- baiki erripet enye."
Mark13:1 Ore pepuku ninye tʼengaji sinyati-- nejoki obo too laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye: Laiteng'enani-- ng'orai-- kakua soito kulo o kaa shetata ena!"
Mark13:2 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Idolita kuna shetat sapuki? Meleku tene osoit te shumata olekai soit lemerratanyuni.
Mark13:3 Ore peton ninye tʼOldonyo loo loirienito aitoriokino engaji sinyati-- neikilikwan Petros o Yakobos o Yohanes o Andreas ninye tʼewueji enye oopeny:"
Mark13:4 Tiaki yook-- kanu eaku nena? Kainyo olponoto obaiarie nena pookin?"
Mark13:5 Neiter Yesus ajoki ninje: Entaduai aten-- pemeitamanimanaa ndai oltung'ani!"
Mark13:6 Amu epuo aapuonu ilkumok lʼengarna ai-- ejo: Ara nanu Kristos! nepuo aaitamanimanaa ilkumok."
Mark13:7 Teni ipuopuo aaning' njorin o oriri loo njorin-- eming'aing'ai! Meata kata nemeaku kuna; kake epon eitu elotu enkiting'oto."
Mark13:8 Amu eladumunye olorere aarare olekai orere o enkarsishu nabo aarare engai arsishu. Nepuo aaku nkikirikirat enkop too wuejitin o wuejitin; nepuo aaku lameitin o nking'asiat. Nera nena enkiterata osina.
Mark13:9 Entaduai ake aten! amu eitarasakini ndai atua ngajijik enkigwena o atua ngajijik Engai; neari ndai neriki ndai ngomomi oo larikok o noo lkarsisi tʼolbae lai-- peaku enjakenishu too ninje."
Mark13:10 Meata kata nemeng'asi aainosaa lomon Peng'ida tiatua loreren pookin.
Mark13:11 Ore teni epuoi aarik neitarasari ndai-- eming'as aaekenyu eniroro-- emimbirribir baiki-- kake enaishori ndai te ina kata-- ina eroro! amu mirara ndai looirorita-- kake Olmumua Sinyati."
Mark13:12 Neitarasaki olalashe olalashe lenye atua enkea o menye enkerai enye-- nedumakino nkera lootoiutuo nepuo aar ninje metuata."
Mark13:13 Niakuku looiba pookin tʼolbae lʼengarna ai; kake olong'iriaki metabaiki enkiting'oto-- ninye olapok."
Mark13:14 Naa teni idolidolo entorroni erruoroto eitashe tʼewueji nemeaku-- (oloisoma ena-- njeyolou)-- ore lootii Yudaya-- njekwetiki ildonyo--"
Mark13:15 ore Olotii keper aji-- njoo medou ajing' atu aji-- pedumu entoki tʼengaji enye;"
Mark13:16 ore Olotii atua enkuruma-- njoo meibelekenyakino kurum adumu olkarash lenye."
Mark13:17 Ee-- kake aiya-- naamena o naaitanakisho too nona olong'i!"
Mark13:18 Entasaishoto-- pemeaku kuna tʼenkata oloirujuruj."
Mark13:19 Nepuo aaku nona olong'i sinaitin leitu eaku neba tʼenkiterata enkishirata naitobirua Engai-- metabaiki taata-- nemeitoki aaku tukul."
Mark13:20 Ten emutu eitu eitadorrop Olaitoriani nona olong'i-- anaata mepoku oltung'ani o obo; kake tʼolbae loo lootegeluaki ootegelua ninye-- eitadorropa nona olong'i."
Mark13:21 Ore pejoki baiki ndai oltung'ani te ina kata: Eng'orai-- etii Kristos ene! arashu: idye! — emiruk!"
Mark13:22 Amu epuo aainyototo ilkristoi lʼelejare o layolounok lʼelejare-- nepuo aaitobir ilponot kituak o nkiputukunyot-- petum aaitamanimanai-- ten ake eidimu-- baiki lootegeluaki."
Mark13:23 Kake entaduai aten! Aidipa atiaki ndai pookin.
Mark13:24 Kake ore too nona olong'i-- eidipe ilo sina-- neopokini engolong' enaimin neiminye olapa enkibor enye"
Mark13:25 neaku esulunye lakir te shumata neing'unung'un ngoloni naatii shumata.
Mark13:26 Nepuo aadol ninje te ina kata Enkerai oltung'ani elotu t'erukenya tʼengolon kitok o tʼenkitook.
Mark13:27 Nelairriu te ina kata ilmalaikan nelaiturrur lootegeluaki lenyena-- eing'ua nkutat ong'wan-- eiter tʼenkiting'oto enkop metabaiki enkiting'oto e shumata."
Mark13:28 Enteng'enuoto tʼenkitanyanyukiet olng'aboli: Teni enanau engaitubului enye neitupuku mbenek-- niyolouu-- aajo etataana enkata olodalu."
Mark13:29 Neijia baiki si ndai-- teni idolidolo kuna eaku-- entayolo-- aajo etataana kutukaji."
Mark13:30 Japa-- aliki ndai-- memuta ena kishon tukul-- metabana neaku kuna pookin."
Mark13:31 Nepuo aamuta shumata o enkop-- kake mepuo aamuta rorei lainei tukul."
Mark13:32 Ore mbaak e ina olong' arashu e ina saa metii oloyolo-- me ilmalaikan le shumata neme Oinoti-- kake Papa ake."
Mark13:33 Eng'orai-- enjololoto-- entasaishoto! amu miyololo enkata naaku."
Mark13:34 Neijia anaa oltung'ani tiatua olototo otung'aiye engaji enye-- neisho laisyayak lenyena engolon-- peata oltung'ani pookin enkyas enye-- neitanap olarriponi le kutukaji-- peishololo."
Mark13:35 Akae-- enjololoto-- amu miyololo enkata nalotu Olaitoriani lʼengaji-- ten aa teipa-- arashu empolos enkiarie-- arashu eorito olkikusieki-- arashu enasirie;"
Mark13:36 pemebau nabokata neinepu ndai irurate.
Mark13:37 Ore enaliki ndai-- naliki pookin: Enjololoto!"
Mark14:1 Ore peishunye ngolong'i are-- neaku pasaka o ngolong'i oo lmkaten lemeisiijo. Neing'oru laidasak kituak o layolok lʼesirata eneiko-- peibung' ninye tʼolosek-- pear metua."
Mark14:2 Nejo ake: me too ngolong'i kituak-- pemeaku enkiposhai olorere."
Mark14:3 Ore etii ninye Betania-- engaji e Simon loata enkea oo lbolot-- eton tʼendaata-- nelotu eng'oroyoni nabo naata oltulet lʼeilata narropil nara sidai tukul negol enkinyang'a-- negil oltulet-- nebukoki elukunya enye."
Mark14:4 Netii iltung'anak looibaitie ina tiatua aten nejo: Kainyo peisardakieki ena ilata narropil?
Mark14:5 Amu anaata eidimi aatimir ina ilata narropil too denaria iip uni neishori laisinak. Negoroki ninje ninye naleng'.
Mark14:6 Nejo Yesus: Entapal ninye! Ainyo pinosiesie ninye osina? Enkyas sidai eitobira ninye te nanu.
Mark14:7 Amu iatata laisinak oshi tʼempolos inyi-- ore piyeuu-- nindimidimi aaitobirakiti ninje sidan; kake mikiatata nanu oshi."
Mark14:8 Eitobira ninye anaa peidima; eitera ninye ael osesen lai tʼeilata narropil tʼenukare.
Mark14:9 Japa-- aliki ndai: Ore ewueji pookin neinosarieki lomon lʼeng'ida tʼenkop-- neinosuni baiki enaitobira ninye nedamuni ninye."
Mark14:10 Nelo Yudas Iskariotes-- obo too kulo tomon o are-- enetii laidasak kituak-- peitarasaki ninye ninje."
Mark14:11 Ore pening' ninje-- neng'ida-- neisilig ninye aaisho ngoshola. Neing'oru ninye eneiko-- peitarasaa ninye tʼenkata naaku."
Mark14:12 Ore tʼengolong' elukunya oo lmkaten lemeisiijo-- tʼenkata naidasieki pasaka-- nejoki laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye: Kaji iyeu nikipuo aaitobir-- pinosie pasaka?"
Mark14:13 Neirriwaa ninye aare loo laiteng'enuok lenyena nejoki ninje: Enjom engang'-- nelatumore ndai oltung'ani-- enapita emoti engare; entusuj ninye!"
Mark14:14 ore ewueji nelajing'-- entiakiti olopeny engaji: Ejo Olaitoriani: Kodee engaji oo lomon-- panya te ina alo pasaka te nebo o laiteng'enuok lainei?"
Mark14:15 Nelaitadol ninye ndai olgilata kitok oitobirakaki ntoneta; entobirakiti yook te ina alo!
Mark14:16 Nepuku laiteng'enuok nepuo engang' nedol anaa petiaka ninje-- neitobir pasaka te ine."
Mark14:17 Ore peaku teipa-- nelotu te nebo o kulo tomon o are."
Mark14:18 Ore petoni ninje-- einosita endaa-- nejo Yesus: Japa-- aliki ndai: Aalaitarasaa obo linyi olonya endaa te nebo o nanu."
Mark14:19 Neiter aailish ninje nejoki ninye obo obo: Ke nanu? o olekai: Ke nanu?
Mark14:20 Nejoki ninye ninje: Obo too kulo tomon o are likiriamaki aaoku endaa tʼengirra.
Mark14:21 Akae-- elo Enkerai oltung'ani anaa petisirakaki ninye-- kake aiya ele tung'ani loitarasarieki Enkerai oltung'ani! Anaata enaikash-- ten emutu eitu eiuni ilo tung'ani."
Mark14:22 Ore einosita ninje endaa-- neibung' ninye olmkate-- nemayan negiligil neisho ninje nejo: Enkoito-- entaam! nera ele osesen lai."
Mark14:23 Neibung enkwaru nejo ashe neisho ninje neok pookin te ninye.
Mark14:24 Nejoki ninje: Era ele osarge lai lʼosotua ng'ejuk oibukori tʼolbae loo lkumok.
Mark14:25 Japa-- aliki ndai: Maitoki aok tukul tiatua eishoi enjani olmarua-- metabaiki ina olong' nalaok eng'ejuk tiatua enkarsishu Engai."
Mark14:26 Ore peidip aatarany Osingolio-- nepuku aapuo Oldonyo loo loirienito."
Mark14:27 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Kipuopuo aarikare ndai pookin-- amu esira: Alaar olairritani-- nepuo aaisardak ntare."
Mark14:28 Ore eidipe empiunoto ai-- nalaiturukie ndai alo Galilaya."
Mark14:29 Nejoki Petros ninye: Teni kirikare pookin-- namaarikare nanu."
Mark14:30 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Japa-- aaliki iye: Ore taata tʼena kiarie-- eton eitu eorito olkikusieki aigil are-- nikimiki aigil uni."
Mark14:31 Nepon ninye naleng' airo: Baiki teni ae te nebo o iye-- maalamiki iye tukul. Neijia etejo ninje pookin."
Mark14:32 Nepuonu ninje enkuruma naji Getsemane-- nejoki laiteng'enuok lenyena: Entotoni tene metabana nasaisho."
Mark14:33 Nerik Petros o Yakobos o Yohanes te nebo o ninye neiter airuturut neisuuto
Mark14:34 nejoki ninje: Eata Olmumua lai enkilishoto kitok metabaiki enkea; entotoni tene-- enjololoto!"
Mark14:35 Nenyikaa peno nebatatakino enkop nesai-- peiye teni eidimai-- njelusoo ena kata ninye--"
Mark14:36 nejo: Aba-- Papa-- eidimai ntokitin pookin te iye; ntulusoiyoki ena kwaru; kake njoo meaku enayeu nanu-- njeaku eniyeu iye!"
Mark14:37 Nelotu ninye neinepu ninje eirura te-- nejoki ninye Petros: Simon-- irura? Eitu indim aishololoi esaa nabo?"
Mark14:38 Enjololoto-- entasaishoto-- pemijing'ijing'i atua enkitasuroto! Eidipakine Olmumua-- kake eshal osesen."
Mark14:39 Neitoki alo nesaisho nelimu kulo rorei ake.
Mark14:40 Neitoki arrinyo neinepu ninje eirurate-- amu eiroshiutuo ngonyek enye neitu eyolo enaliki ninye."
Mark14:41 Nelotu en e uni nejoki ninje: Erraga ade-- eeng'ieng'ata! Ebaiki. Etabaua enkata. Eng'orai-- eitarasakini Enkerai oltung'ani atua ngaik oo laitarruok."
Mark14:42 Enyoito-- maapeti! Eng'orai-- etinyikua olaaitarasaa."
Mark14:43 Ore nabokata epon eirorita ninye-- nebau Yudas-- obo loo kulo tomon o are-- o te nebo o ninye esiamu naata lalema o siaren-- eing'ua enetii laidasak kituak o layolok lʼesirata o laigwenak."
Mark14:44 Eidipa aishoo olaitarasaroni lenye ninje olponoto nejo: Ore olang'utut-- ninye ilo; embung'a ninye-- entorik-- entagolo!"
Mark14:45 Ore pebau-- nelotu nabokata enetii ninye nejo: Laiteng'enani! neng'utut ninye."
Mark14:46 Neaki ninje ninye ngaik neibung' ninye.
Mark14:47 Ore obo too kulo ootaboitare ninye-- neshitu olalem neosh olaisyayani lʼolaidasani kitok nedung'u ninye enkiyok."
Mark14:48 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninje: Itupukutuo ndai-- pikimbung'ubung'u too lalema o too siaren anaa iltung'anak loomirita olaisimani;"
Mark14:49 atii ngolong'i pookin atua ndai tiatua engaji sinyati-- aiteng'enishe-- neitu kimbung'ubung'u; kake etaa kuna-- peiye ebaia sirat."
Mark14:50 Neing'ua pookin ninye nekwet.
Mark14:51 Nesuj olbarnoti obo ninye oiopokine olkarash oibor nemeata olekai; neibung' ninje ninye.
Mark14:52 Neitiak olkarash nekwet meishopo.
Mark14:53 Nerik ninje Yesus enetii olaidasani kitok-- neiturrurrokino ninye laidasak kituak o laigwenak o layolok lʼesirata pookin"
Mark14:54 Nesuj Petros ninye tʼenelakwa metabaiki engang' olaidasani kitok nejing' atua neton te nebo o laisyayak aij enkima.
Mark14:55 Neing'oru laidasak kituak o enkigwena pookin enjakenishu te Yesus-- petum aataar ninye metua-- neitu eidim."
Mark14:56 Amu eijakenokitio ilkumok elejare-- nemenyanyukoro njakenishuni enye."
Mark14:57 Neinyototo kulekai neijakenoki ninye elejare-- ejo:"
Mark14:58 Kitoning'o yook ninye ejo: Agil nanu ena aji sinyati naitobiruaki too ngaik-- ore too ngolong'i uni nalashet engai neitu eitobiri too ngaik."
Mark14:59 Neitu eitoriori baiki ena jakenishu enye.
Mark14:60 Neinyototo olaidasani kitok nelo empolos enye neikilikwan ninye Yesus nejo: Mialu ororei too kuna nikinjakenoki kulo?
Mark14:61 Negira ninye neitu ealiki ororei. Neitoki aikilikwan olaidasani kitok ninye nejoki ninye: Ira iye Kristos-- Oinoti le Loitadarari?"
Mark14:62 Nejo Yesus: Ara nanu. Nipuopuo aadol Enkerai oltung'ani-- eton te tatene Engolon-- elotu tʼerukenya e shumata."
Mark14:63 Nepolos olaidasani kitok ilkilani lenyena-- ejo: Ainyo kintoki aayeunye iljaken?"
Mark14:64 Itoning'o emoroto Engai. Ijojo aa? Neigwenaki pookin ninye-- ajo era lʼenkea."
Mark14:65 Neiter kulekai aanotaki ninye ngamulak neop engomom enye near ninye too ntinan nejoki ninye: Ntayolou yook! Neng'amu laisyayak ninye aar engomom enye too ndapi.
Mark14:66 Ore etii Petros boo-- nelotu nabo too ngaisyayak olaidasani kitok--"
Mark14:67 nedol Petros eijita enkima neing'oraa ninye nejo: Itaboitare si iye ele Yesus le Nasaret.
Mark14:68 Nemiki ninye nejo: Mayolo nanu namaning'ito enijoito. Nepuku aulo-- neorito olkikusieki."
Mark14:69 Nedol engaisyayani ninye neitoki aiter aliki lʼemboitei-- ajo era ele obo too ninje."
Mark14:70 Neitoki amiki. Neitoki tʼenkiti kata aajoki Petros kulo ooitashe o ninye: Esipa-- ira obo too ninje-- amu ira le Galilaya-- nikilimu enkiroroto ino."
Mark14:71 Neiter adekisho-- neiturujisho-- ajo: Mayolo nanu ilo tung'ani liimakiki."
Mark14:72 Neorito nabokata olkikusieki en e are. Nedamu Petros ilo rorei otiaka Yesus ninye: Ore eton eitu eorito olkikusieki aigil are-- nikimiki aigil uni. Ore pedamu-- neishir."
Mark15:1 Ore tʼentadekeny neosh enkigwena laidasak kituak te nebo o laigwenak o layolok lʼesirata o enkigwena nalulung'a-- neen Yesus nerik neitarasaki Pilatos."
Mark15:2 Neikilikwan Pilatos ninye: Ira iye olkarsis loo Yudayoi? Nealiki ninye nejo: Ijo iye.
Mark15:3 Neitang'or laidasak kituak ninye too nkumok.
Mark15:4 Neitoki aikilikwan Pilatos ninye ejo: Mialu ororei? Ng'orai-- kaja kintang'orie ninje."
Mark15:5 Neitu ealu Yesus toki-- neiputukuny baiki Pilatos."
Mark15:6 Neata ninye orregie loo ngolong'i kituak-- pelaaki ninje obo loena otayeutuo ninje."
Mark15:7 Netii obo oji Barabas-- oteenaki te nebo o laisisak ootara oltung'ani metua tiatua enkitashoto."
Mark15:8 Neilep olorere neiter aasai-- peitobiraki ninje anaa oshi ake."
Mark15:9 Nealiki Pilatos ninje ejo: Iyeuu nalaaki ndai ele karsis loo Yudayoi?
Mark15:10 Amu etayolouo-- ajo eitarasutua laidasak kituak ninye tʼengilata e tau."
Mark15:11 Neisis laidasak kituak esiamu-- peiye eaku enaikash-- teni elaaki ninje Barabas."
Mark15:12 Neitoki aaiu Pilatos nejoki ninje: Akae-- kaa naa aikunaki ele lijojo-- era olkarsis loo Yudayoi?"
Mark15:13 Neitoki aadar ninje: Tooshoki ninye esalaba!
Mark15:14 Nejoki Pilatos ninje: Kaa torroni etaasa ninye? Nepon ninje naleng' aadar: Tooshoki ninye esalaba!
Mark15:15 Akae-- neyeu Pilatos neitobiraki olorere enanyor nelaaki ninje Barabas neitarasaa Yesus-- eidipa ataara too nkeenda-- petumi aatooshokiti ninye esalaba."
Mark15:16 Nerik isikerin ninye atua engaji enkigwena neipot ninje-- peiturrurro oltim olulung'a."
Mark15:17 Neishopoki ninje ninye olkila odo neshet olmarisian loo lkikarreta neishopoki ninye elukunya;
Mark15:18 neiter aairoroki ninye: Supai-- lekarsis loo Yudayoi!"
Mark15:19 Neosh ninye elukunya tʼolmoloi nenotaki ninye ngamulak negil kung' aaitaa ninye kitok.
Mark15:20 Ore peidip aatusul ninye-- neoru ninye olkila odo neishopoki ninye ilkilani lenyena. Nerik aulo-- peoshoki esalaba."
Mark15:21 Neitanap ninje tʼengolon oltung'ani oimita-- Simon le Kirene-- eing'ua enkuruma-- nera menye le Aleksandros o le Rufos-- penap esalaba enye."
Mark15:22 Nerik ninje ninye metabaiki ewueji Golgota-- ore enkitaalata enye: ewueji emborbor--"
Mark15:23 Neisho ninye olmarua oshulare engare naitiming'anisho; neany ninye.
Mark15:24 Ore peidip ninje aatooshokiti ninye esalaba-- neorikino ilkilani lenyena-- neoshoki olenkukuo t'olbae lenye-- peyolou ang'ai lotum toki."
Mark15:25 Etaa saa uni-- etooshokoki ninye esalaba."
Mark15:26 Netii shumata enye esirata enkitang'oroto enye: Olkarsis loo Yudayoi.
Mark15:27 Neoshoki te nebo o ninye laisimak aare esalaba-- obo te tatene o obo te kedyanye enye."
Mark15:28 Nebaia esirata najo: Eikenaiyoki ninye te nebo o laitarruok.
Mark15:29 Ore kulo ooimita nemor ninye eipiripirito lukuny enye nejo: Kiiti-- ologil engaji sinyati neshet ninye too ngolong'i uni!"
Mark15:30 Ntopua kion-- tadou tʼesalaba!"
Mark15:31 Nesul neijia baiki si ninje laidasak kituak tʼempolos enye te nebo o layolok lʼesirata nejo: Eitopua ilkulekai nemeidim aitopua kion.
Mark15:32 Njedou taata Kristos-- olkarsis le Israel-- tʼesalaba-- pekitum aatadol-- nikiruk. Etamoro si ninje lootooshokoki esalaba te nebo o ninye."
Mark15:33 Ore peaku saa ile-- neaku enaimin te shumata enkop pookin metabaiki saa enturuj."
Mark15:34 Nedar Yesus te saa enturuj tʼoltoilo kitok nejo: Eli-- Eli lamaa asabtani? neji enkitaalata enye: Engai ai-- Engai ai-- ainyo pikitung'aiye?"
Mark15:35 Ore pening' ematua oo kulo looitashe tʼenetaana-- nejo: Ng'orai-- eipotito Eliya."
Mark15:36 Nekwet oltung'ani obo neigany enjutet engare naitiming'anisho nepik shumata olmoloi neitook ninye-- ejo: Entapal-- maing'orai-- ten ake elotu Eliya-- peitadou ninye."
Mark15:37 Neitupuku Yesus oltoilo kitok-- nedung'o tau."
Mark15:38 Nepolosa olkarash lʼerishata engaji sinyati matuan are-- eiter te shumata metabaiki enkop."
Mark15:39 Ore pedol olkigeluni loitashe tʼeneitoriokinore ninye-- ajo nji etudung'e tau-- nejo: Esipa-- era ele tung'ani Oinoti lʼEngai!"
Mark15:40 Netii baiki ng'oroyok ine naaing'orita tʼenelakwa; netii atua ninje Maria Magdalena o Maria-- ng'otonye e Yakobos olkiti o ne Yoses-- o Salome--"
Mark15:41 ninje naatusuja ninye-- etii Galilaya-- neisyayaki ninye-- o nkulie kumok naaileputua te nebo o ninye metabaiki Yerusalem."
Mark15:42 Ore peaku teipa-- etii engolong' enkitobirakinore nara enaiturukie engolong' naeng'ieng'areki--"
Mark15:43 nelotu Yosef le Arimatia-- olaigwenani loataiyeki oloip-- nera ninye loanyu enkarsishu Engai-- neiteu ninye atijing'aki Pilatos neomonu osesen le Yesus."
Mark15:44 Neiputukuny Pilatos-- ajo eidipa atua; neipot olkigeluni neikilikwan ninye-- ten ake elakwa etua."
Mark15:45 Ore peyolou tʼolkigeluni esipata-- neisho Yosef empopong'."
Mark15:46 Neinyang'u olkarash oibor neitadou ninve neirinaki atua olkarash oibor nepik ninye atua enkurare natabataki tiatua osoit kitok neibeleleng'oki osoit kitok kutukaji enkurare.
Mark15:47 Neing'oraa Maria Magdalena o Maria e Yoses enetipikaki.
Mark16:1 Ore peishunye engolong' naeng'ieng'areki-- neinyang'u Maria Magdalena o Maria-- ng'otonye e Yakobos-- o Salome ilat naarropil-- pepuonu aael ninye."
Mark16:2 Ore enasirie naleng'-- tʼengolong' elukunya enjuma-- nepuonu ninje enetii enkurare-- eilepu engolong'."
Mark16:3 Nejokino ninje tʼempolos enye: Ang'ai oibelekenyaki yook osoit te kutukaji enkurare?
Mark16:4 Ore peing'oraa ninje-- nedol-- aajo eidipaki aibelekenyai osoit; amu era kitok naleng'."
Mark16:5 Ore pejing' ninje atua enkurare-- nedol olbarnoti otonita te tatene neishopito olkila oibor; neing'asia ninje."
Mark16:6 Nejoki si ninye ninje: Eming'asia! Ing'oruru ndai Yesus le Nasaret otooshokoki esalaba; etopiwuo ninye; metii ene. Eng'orai ewueji neitaperieki ninye!
Mark16:7 Kake enjom-- entiakiti laiteng'enuok lenyena o Petros-- ajo elaiturukie ndai alo Galilaya; nipuopuo aadol ninye te ina alo anaa petiaka ndai."
Mark16:8 Nepuku ninje aasioio nekwet aaing'ua enkurare-- amu eibung'a ninje enkikirikirata o enking'asiata; neitu eliki ninje oltung'ani ororei-- amu etureishote."
Mark16:9 Ore peinyototo Yesus enasirie tʼengolong' elukunya enjuma-- neng'as aitadol kion Maria Magdalena natimirie ninye ilmumuan torrok oopishana."
Mark16:10 Neibung' ninye engoitoi neinosaki mbaak kulo lootaboitare ninye-- eilishito neishir."
Mark16:11 Ore pening' si kulo-- aajo eishiu ninye netadua ninye ninye-- neitu eiruk ninje."
Mark16:12 Ore tekurum oo kuna nelioi ninye tʼengai mua too aare lenye ootilimanate aapuo enkuruma.
Mark16:13 Nepuo kulo neinosaki mbaak lootelekutua; neitu eiruk baiki lelo.
Mark16:14 Neitadol kion tʼenkiting'oto kulo tomon o obo-- etonita tʼendaata-- neilepilepaki ninje-- tiaraki neitu eiruk-- negol iltauja lenye-- aajo eitu eiruk kulo lootadua ninye etopiwuo."
Mark16:15 Nejoki ninje: Embung'a engoitoi aapuo atua olmaa pookin-- enosakiti lomon lʼeng'ida enkitobirata pookin."
Mark16:16 Oloiruk neibatisi-- nepok; olemeiruk-- nepuoi aadek."
Mark16:17 Nepuo aarubare looiruk kulo ponot: nepuo aamir ninje lʼengarna ai ilmeneng'a-- nepuo aairo too nkutukie ng'ejuko--"
Mark16:18 nepuo aadumu lasuria; naa teni eok entoki naarisho-- nemear ninje tukul; nepuo aaiteleiki ngaik loomoiyaa-- neaku ninje biot."
Mark16:19 Akae-- ore peidip Olaitoriani airorie ninje-- nedumari shumata neton te tatene Engai."
Mark16:20 Nepuku kulo neinosu lomon lʼEngai too wuejitin pookin; neretoki Olaitoriani ninje too nkyasin enye neitagol ororei too lponot looturubare. Amen.
Luke1:1 Tiaraki natii ilkumok ootipika ngaik enye aasir aabaraki lomon loo mbaak naataa tiatua yook--"
Luke1:2 anaa peakitia yook kulo loora neba tʼenkiterata lootadua too ngonyek enye oopeny nera laisyayak lʼororei--"
Luke1:3 atadua si nanu-- ajo era sidai-- teni aasiraki iye-- Teofilos lanyor naleng'-- abaraki mbaak pookin nataleeno neba tʼenkion enye osupatei--"
Luke1:4 piyolou esipata oo mbaak oo lomon likinteng'enaki.
Luke1:5 Etii tʼenkata e Herodes lora olkarsis tiatua Yudaya olaidasani obo-- oji Sakarias-- nera lʼolkamba le Abia-- o eng'oroyoni enye too ntoiye e Aron-- naji engarna enye Elisabet."
Luke1:6 Nera ninje pokira are supati tʼengomom Engai-- neibung' nkitanapat pookin o supaton Olaitoriani-- meata eleyata."
Luke1:7 Neitu eata ninje enkerai; amu eitasho Elisabet-- etaa pokira are moruak too ngolong'i enye."
Luke1:8 Akae-- eitobir ninye enkyas enkidasare abaraki tʼolkamba lenye tʼengomom Engai--"
Luke1:9 anaa pera orregie lʼenkidasare-- netum enkukuo ninye-- pejing' engaji sinyati Olaitoriani airisho."
Luke1:10 Netii enkumoi pookin olorere boo-- esaisho-- tʼenkata nairishore."
Luke1:11 Nelioi te ninye olmalaika lʼOlaitoriani-- eitashe tʼematua e tatene olperere oirishoreki."
Luke1:12 Ore pedol Sakarias ninye-- neng'ayung'ayu-- nejing' enkuretishu atua ninye."
Luke1:13 Nejoki olmalaika ninye: miureishoi-- Sakarias! amu etoning'oki esayata ino-- kilaiki eng'oroyoni Elisabet enkerai-- nimpot engarna enye Yohanes;"
Luke1:14 nilaata eng'ida o engalali-- neitoki aang'ida ilkumok tʼeiunoto enye."
Luke1:15 Amu eaku ninye kitok tʼengomom Olaitoriani-- nemeok olmarua o eokore naitemerisho-- neiganyi ninye Olmumua Sinyati-- epon etii engoshoke e ng'otonye enye;"
Luke1:16 nelarrinyoki ninye ilkumok tiatua nkera Israel Olaitoriani-- Engai enye;"
Luke1:17 nelaiturukie ninye tʼengomom enye tʼolmumua o tʼengolon Eliya arrinyoki iltauja loo loomenye nkera-- o lemeiruk eng'eno oo supati-- peiye eitobiraki Olaitoriani olorere."
Luke1:18 Nejoki Sakarias olmalaika: Kainyo ayolounye ina? Anlu ara nanu moruo naa moruo eng'oroyoni ai too ngolong'i enyena.
Luke1:19 Nealiki olmalaika nejoki ninye: Ara nanu Gabriel oitashe tʼengomom Engai naairriuaki-- paairorie iye-- paainosaki iye nena."
Luke1:20 Ng'orai-- ilagira nimindim airoro metabaiki ena olong' napuo aaku kuna-- tiaraki neitu iruk rorei lainei loopuoi aaitabaia tʼenkata enye."
Luke1:21 Netii olorere boo neanyu Sakarias-- neiputukuny tʼenkimutioto enye tiatua engaji sinyati."
Luke1:22 Ore pepuku ninye-- neitu eidim airorie ninje-- neyolou ninje-- aajo etadua ninye enkitaduaroto tiatua engaji sinyati. Neaku erojaa ninje nebik meiro."
Luke1:23 Neaku ore peidipai ngolong'i enkisyayare enye-- nelo engaji enye."
Luke1:24 Ore peishunye nona olong'i-- nemenai eng'oroyoni enye Elisabet-- neisudori lapaitin imiet-- ejo:"
Luke1:25 Nji aaitobiraka Olaitoriani too nona olong'i naaing'oraiye-- paaitaiki enkurruna ai tiatua iltung'anak."
Luke1:26 Ore tʼolapa le ile neirriwaa Engai olmalaika Gabriel atua engang' nabo e Galilaya-- naji engarna enye Nasaret--"
Luke1:27 enetii entito natisira olee obo oji Yosef-- lʼengaji e David-- neji engarna e ina ito Maria."
Luke1:28 Ore peidip atijing'a olmalaika enetii ninye-- nejo: Takwenia-- naishooki eng'adunoto! Kirubare Olaitoriani! Kitamayanaki tiatua ng'oroyok!"
Luke1:29 Ore pedol ninye-- neng'ayung'ayu naleng' too rorei lenyena neibirribir: Kaa kirorokinoto ena?"
Luke1:30 Nejoki olmalaika ninye: Miureisho-- Maria! amu inoto eng'adunoto tʼEngai."
Luke1:31 Naa ng'orai-- ilamenai nilaiu Oinoti-- nilaipot engarna enye Yesus."
Luke1:32 Neaku ele kitok-- nepuoi aaipot Oinoti lʼOlotii shumata naleng' nelaisho Olaitoriani Engai ninye olorika lʼenkitoria le menye lenye David--"
Luke1:33 nelaitore ninye engaji e Yakoob nkatan pookin-- nemeata enkarsishu enye enkiting'oto."
Luke1:34 Nejoki Maria olmalaika: Kaji eiko teni eaku ena-- amu mayolo olee?"
Luke1:35 Nealiki olmalaika nejoki ninye: Kiladoiki Olmumua Sinyati nikiopoki engolon Olotii shumata naleng'; onaa epuoi aaipot ele Sinyati loiuni Oinoti lʼEngai.
Luke1:36 Naa ng'orai-- Elisabet-- enjoruet ino-- emena si ninye tʼenkerai olee tiatua emoruao enye-- nera ele olapa le ile te ninye naipoti naitasho;"
Luke1:37 amu metii entoki o nabo nemeidimai tʼEngai.
Luke1:38 Nejo Maria: Ng'orai-- ara nanu engaisyayani Olaitoriani; njeaku te nanu anaa pitejo. Nelo olmalaika aing'ua ninye."
Luke1:39 Nedumunye Maria to nona olong'i nelo oldonyo tʼesioroto atua engang' e Yuda--"
Luke1:40 nejing' atua engaji e Sakarias neiro roki Elisabet.
Luke1:41 Neaku ore pening Elisabet enkirorokinoto e Maria-- neipid enkerai tiatua engoshoke enye-- neiganyi Elisabet Olmumua Sinyati--"
Luke1:42 nedar ninye tʼendarata kitok nejo: Kitamayanaki iye tiatua ng'oroyok nemayana eishoi engoshoke ino.
Luke1:43 Kaji eiko teni eaku ena te nanu-- ajo elotu ng'otonye Olaitoriani lai enatii nanu?"
Luke1:44 Amu ng'orai-- ore etijing'a oltoilo lʼenkirorokinoto ino atua nkiyaa ainei-- neipid tʼengalali enkerai tiatua engoshoke ai."
Luke1:45 Ira iye tesh eniruko-- amu eidipai enikitiakaki tʼOlaitoriani."
Luke1:46 Nejo Maria: Eitaa oltau lai Olaitoriani kitok
Luke1:47 neng'idakino Olmumua lai Engai-- Olaitopuani lai;"
Luke1:48 amu etadua ninye enkitadounoto engaisyayani enye. Amu ngʼorai-- eiter taata aapuo aaipot nkishomini pookin entesh;"
Luke1:49 amu aaitobiraka Oloata engolon ntokitin kituak-- naa sinyati engarna enye;"
Luke1:50 nebik eng'adunoto enye tiatua nkishomini pookin-- too kulo looure ninye."
Luke1:51 Neitaa engolon tʼengaina enye neisardakie looata olwuasa too ndamunot oo ltauja lenye;
Luke1:52 nebatat looata engolon too lorikaishi-- neitaa kituak looitadou aten;"
Luke1:53 neitaraposh too ntokitin sidan looata olamei; neing'ua ladupak neijia.
Luke1:54 Neretoki Israel lora olaisyayani lenye-- nedamu enkordunoto enye--"
Luke1:55 neijia anaa petiaka loopapa lang'-- Abraham o eishoi enye-- nkatan pookin."
Luke1:56 Nebik Maria te nebo o ninye enkata oo lapaitin okuni-- nerrinyo engaji enye."
Luke1:57 Nebaia enkata Elisabet naishore-- neiu enkerai olee."
Luke1:58 Nening' lʼelatia o lʼenkishomi enye-- ajo eitaa kitok Olaitoriani enkordunoto enye-- neng'ida te nebo o ninye."
Luke1:59 Neaku engolong' e isiet-- nepuonu aamurat enkerai nedung'oki ninye engarna e menye lenye Sakarias."
Luke1:60 Nealu ng'otonye enye nejo: Me neija-- kake eipoti ninye Yohanes."
Luke1:61 Nejoki ninje ninye: Metii o obo lʼenkishomi ino loipotieki ina arna.
Luke1:62 Neroj ninje menye lenye-- pelimu enayeu neipotieki ninye."
Luke1:63 Neyeu ninye osoit nesir nejo: Yohanes engarna enye. Neiputukuny ninje pookin.
Luke1:64 Nelaki nabokata enkutuk enye o olng'ejep lenye-- neiro neitadaraa Engai."
Luke1:65 Neaku enkuretishu too pookin lʼelatia enye-- neibulu kulo rorei pookin atua ildonyo pookin le Yudaya."
Luke1:66 Neibung' ninje pookin lootoning'o too ltauja lenye nejo: Amaa-- keaku ena kerai ng'ai? Amu eturubare engaina Olaitoriani ninye."
Luke1:67 Neigany Sakarias-- menye lenye-- Olmumua Sinyati neitayolo mbaak e akenya nejo:"
Luke1:68 Njeitadarari Olaitoriani-- Engai e Israel-- tiaraki natijing'aka neitobiraki enkitopuata olorere lenye--"
Luke1:69 neunoki yook emowuo enkitopuata tiatua engaji e David-- olaisyayani lenye--"
Luke1:70 neijia anaa petejo ninye-- eiter opa-- tʼenkutuk oo layolounok sinyat lenyena:"
Luke1:71 peitopok yook too lmang'ati lang' o too ngaik oo pookin looiba yook--"
Luke1:72 neitobiraki enkordunoto loopapa lang' nedamu osotua lenye sinyati
Luke1:73 o enkiturujata naiturujaka papa lang' Abraham ajo eisho yook
Luke1:74 kipok too ngaik oo lmang'ati lang'-- mikiata enkuretishu-- pikisyayaki ninye too ngolong'i ang' pookin"
Luke1:75 t'esinyatishu o tʼesupato tʼengomom enye.
Luke1:76 O iye-- nakerai-- kipuoi aaipot olayolounoni lʼOlotii shumata naleng'-- amu ilaiturukie engomom Olaitoriani-- pintobir ngoitoi enyena--"
Luke1:77 pinjo olorere lenye eyoloupoto enkitopuata tiatua enkitaunoto oo nkitarruot enye--"
Luke1:78 tʼoltau lʼenkordunoto Engai ang' naitijing'ua atua yook enkilepunoto naing'ua shumata--"
Luke1:79 peilang'aki lootoni tiatua enaimin o tiatua oloip lʼenkea-- nerik nkejek ang' atua engoitoi eseriani."
Luke1:80 Nebulu ena kerai negolu tʼolmumua-- netii atua ang'at metabaiki kuna olong'i naaibalakino ninye atua Israel."
Luke2:1 Neaku nepuku too nona olong'i enkitanapata e kaisar Augustos-- pesiri olmaa pookin."
Luke2:2 Nera ena sirata en elukunya nataa-- eitore Kirenios olosho Siria."
Luke2:3 Neibung' iltung'anak pookin engoitoi nepuo-- pesiri oltung'ani pookin tʼengang' enye."
Luke2:4 Nedumunye baiki si ninye Yosef-- eing'ua Galilaya-- engang' Nasaret-- neilep alo Yudaya-- metabaiki engang' e David-- naji Betlehem-- tiaraki nara ninye l'engaji o lʼenkishomi e David--"
Luke2:5 pesiri ninye te nebo o Maria-- eng'oroyoni enye-- natasanjana-- nemena ninye."
Luke2:6 Neaku ore etii ninje ina alo-- nebaia ngolong'i naaishore ninye--"
Luke2:7 neiu ninye olkikau lenye neirin ninye too rasheta oo nkera neirragie ninye tiatua embout-- tiaraki neitu etum ninje engai wueji tiatua engaji oo lomon."
Luke2:8 Netii lairritak atua ilo osho ooirritita enjoo enye te boo tʼolkamba le kiarie.
Luke2:9 Nepukoki ninje olmalaika lʼOlaitoriani neman enkitook Olaitoriani ailang'aki ninje-- neureishoi ninje tʼenkuretishu kitok."
Luke2:10 Nejoki olmalaika ninje: Emiureisho! Amu eng'orai-- ainosaki ndai eng'ida kitok naaku noo loreren pookin;"
Luke2:11 amu etoikioki ndai taata Olaitopuani-- oji Kristos-- Olaitoriani-- tʼengang' e David."
Luke2:12 Naa ele olponoto too ndai: ipuopuo aatum enkerai nairinaki too rasheta oo nkera-- eirragieki tiatua embout."
Luke2:13 Nelioi nabokata te nebo o olmalaika oltim kitok le shumata loitadaraa Engai nejo:
Luke2:14 Njeata Engai enkitook te shumata-- njeaku eseriani tʼenkop-- too ltung'anak lʼenyorrata."
Luke2:15 Neaku ore peing'ua ilmalaikan ninje-- pepuo shumata-- nejokino lairritak: Maapeti metabaiki Betlehem-- piking'oraa ena bae nataa-- naitayolo yook Olaitoriani."
Luke2:16 Nesioio ninje aapuo neinepu Maria o Yosef o enkerai-- eirrag tiatua embout."
Luke2:17 Ore peidip aatadol-- neinosaa embae natiakaki ninje tʼolbae lʼena kerai."
Luke2:18 Ore pookin lootoning'o-- neiputukuny too kuna naatiakitia lairritak ninje."
Luke2:19 Neshum Maria kuna baak pookin neibirribir tiatua oltau lenye.
Luke2:20 Nerrinyo lairritak neitaa kitok neitadaraa Engai too mbaak pookin naatoning'o nedol-- neijia anaa petiakaki ninje."
Luke2:21 Ore peishunye ngolong'i isiet-- pemurati enkerai-- neipoti engarna enye Yesus-- anaa peipoto olmalaika eton eitu eng'amuni tiatua engoshoke e ng'otonye."
Luke2:22 Ore pebau ngolong'i enkisujata enye-- anaa ejo nkitanapat e Mose-- nenap ninje ninye Yerusalem-- peitarasaki Olaitoriani--"
Luke2:23 neijia anaa petisiraki tiatua nkitanapat Olaitoriani: Ore olee pookin obol enkuset e ng'otonye-- njeipoti osinyati lʼOlaitoriani--"
Luke2:24 petum aaishoi enkidasare-- neija anaa petejoki tiatua enkitanapata Olaitoriani: ilmaita aare arashu nkera are oo lmaita."
Luke2:25 Naa ng'orai-- etii oltung'ani atua Yerusalem-- oji engarna enye Simeon; nera ele tung'ani supat neure Engai neanyu enkilejilejata e Israel-- netii Olmumua Sinyati atua ninye;"
Luke2:26 neitayolo Olmumua Sinyati ninye-- ajo medol enkea-- eitu edol Kristos lʼOlaitoriani."
Luke2:27 Nelotu ninye tʼerikunoto Olmumua atua engaji sinyati. Ore pepuonu lootoiutuo enkerai Yesus-- peitobir anaa petiu orregie loo nkitanapat tʼolbae lenye--"
Luke2:28 neng'amu ninye too ngaik enyena neitadaraa Engai-- ejo:"
Luke2:29 Laitoriani-- njoo taata olaisyayani lino-- pelo tʼeseriani anaa pitejo--"
Luke2:30 amu etadua ngonyek ainei enkitopuata ino--"
Luke2:31 nintobira tʼengomom oo loreren pookin--"
Luke2:32 enkilang'et nailang'aki loreren o enkitook olorere lino Israel.
Luke2:33 Neiputukuny menye lenye o ng'otonye too rorei looimakaki te ninye.
Luke2:34 Nemayan Simeon ninje nejoki Maria-- ng'otonye enye: Ng'orai-- epiki ninye-- peaku embatatata o enkitasheito oo lkumok tiatua Israel o olponoto oitemenetari —"
Luke2:35 nikilaim si iye olalem atua oltau —-- pebolunye ndamunot oo ltauja kumok."
Luke2:36 Netii engayolounoni nabo naji Ana-- entito e Fanuel-- lenkishomi e Aser; naa moruo ninye naleng'-- etobiko eata olmoruo larin oopishana-- eiter entitoishu enye--"
Luke2:37 nera ninye engoliai oo larin ntomoni isiet o ong'wan-- neitu eing'ua engaji sinyati neisyayaki Engai dama o kiarie too mpukorot o too sayat."
Luke2:38 Nelotu si ninye te ina kata neliki Engai ashe neinosaki mbaak enyena kulo pookin ootaanyutua enkitopuata te Yerusalem.
Luke2:39 Ore peidip ninje aaitabai pookin natii atua nkitanapat Olaitoriani-- nerrinyo aapuo Galilaya metabaiki engang' enye Nasaret."
Luke2:40 Nebulu ina kerai negolu tʼolmumua-- nebore eng'eno neboitare eng'adunoto Engai ninye."
Luke2:41 Nepuo lootoiutuo ninye Yerusalem tʼolari pookin too ngolong'i e pasaka.
Luke2:42 Ore peaku ninye noo larin tomon o are-- neilep aapuo ninje Yerusalem tʼorregie loo ngolong'i kituak."
Luke2:43 Ore peidip aaitabai nona olong i-- nerrinyo ninje ang'-- nebik enkerai Yesus te Yerusalem-- neitu eyolou ena lootoiutuo ninye."
Luke2:44 Nejo ninje-- aajo etii ninye atua iltung'anak lʼolototo-- nepuonu olototo lʼengolong' nabo neing'oru ninye tiatua iltung'anak lʼenkishomi o lʼemboitei;"
Luke2:45 ore pelau ninye-- nerrinyo metabaiki Yerusalem-- eing'oru ninye."
Luke2:46 Neaku ore peishunye ngolong'i uni-- netum ninye tiatua engaji sinyati-- eton tʼempolos oo laiteng'enak-- einining' ninje neikilikwan ninje."
Luke2:47 Neirut naleng' pookin lootoning'o ninye tʼolbae lʼeng'eno enye o tʼolbae loo aleta enyena.
Luke2:48 Ore pedol ninje ninye-- neing'asia naleng'-- nejoki ng'otonye enye ninye: Nakerai-- ainyo pinkunaka yook nji? Ng'orai-- king'orutua-- minyi lino o nanu-- tʼosina."
Luke2:49 Nejoki ninye ninje: Ainyo piking'orutua? Miyololo ndai-- aajo meata kata namatii atua ne Papa lai?"
Luke2:50 Neitu eyolou ninje ele rorei lotiaka ninje.
Luke2:51 Nedou ninye te nebo o ninje ne-lotu Nasaret neaku ening' ninje. Neshum ng'otonye enye kulo rorei pookin tiatua oltau lenye.
Luke2:52 Nenyikaa Yesus tiatua eng'eno o tiatua embulunoto o tiatua eng'adunoto tʼEngai o too ltung'anak.
Luke3:1 Ore tʼolari le tomon o imiet lʼenkitoria e kaisar Tiberias-- era Pontios Pilatos Olaitoriani le Yudaya nera Herodes Olaitoriani lʼematua e ong'wan le Galilaya nera Filipos-- olalashe lenye-- Olaitoriani lʼematua e ong'wan le Ituraya o olosho Trakonitis nera Lisanias Olaitoriani lʼematua e ong'wan le Abilene--"
Luke3:2 tʼenkata olaidasani kitok Anas o Kayafas-- nebaiki ororei lʼEngai Yohanes-- enkerai e Sakarias-- ti ang'ata."
Luke3:3 Nelotu ninye atua loshon pookin oomanita Yordan-- einosu enkibatisa enkitaalata nʼenkitaunoto oo nkitarruot--"
Luke3:4 anaa petisiraki tʼenkitabu oo rorei le Yesaya-- olayolounoni-- ojo: Etii ang'ata oltoilo lʼoloipotisho: Entobira engoitoi Olaitoriani-- entorioi nkiimat enyena!"
Luke3:5 Njeiganyi nong'ot pookin-- njeitadouni ildonyo o ndonyo pookin-- njeitoriori nariwuo-- njeari ilgurumen metorisioto ngoitoi."
Luke3:6 Nepuo aadol iseseni pookin enkitopuata Engai.
Luke3:7 Akae-- nejoki ninye siamin naaetuo-- peibatis ninye ninje: Ndai eishoi oo lasuria-- kang'ai otoroja ndai-- pikwetikwete engoro Engai nalotu?"
Luke3:8 Akae-- entoiu ilmomo sidan lʼenkitaalata! niminteritere aajo tiatua ndai: Kiata papa lora Abraham. Amu aliki nanu ndai-- ajo eidim Engai ainyeye Abraham nkera tiatua kulo soito."
Luke3:9 Akae-- eidipaki aatipik baiki entoiu ntonat oo ljanito; ore oljani pookin lemeiu ilmomo sidan-- nedung'i nenang'akini atua enkima."
Luke3:10 Neikilikwan kuna siamin ninye nejo: Kaji naa kinko?
Luke3:11 Nealiki ninye nejoki: Oloata ilkilani aare-- njoo eoriki olemeata; oloata ndaikin-- njeiko neijia ake."
Luke3:12 Nepuonu si ninje-- laoshok le kodi-- peibatisi-- nejoki ninje ninye: Laiteng'enani-- kaji kinko?"
Luke3:13 Nejoki si ninye ninje: Emiaru enalang' naitanapaki ndai.
Luke3:14 Neikilikwan si sikerin ninye ejo: Kaji kinko si yook? Nejoki ninje: Emisil oltung'ani nimisimisimi-- njoo ebaiki ndai olkwaje linyi."
Luke3:15 Akae-- ore pemusu olorere neibirribir ninje pookin too ltauja lenye mbaak e Yohanes-- ten ak era ninye Kristos arashu me--"
Luke3:16 nealiki Yohanes nejoki ninje pookin: Aibatis nanu ndai tʼengare-- kake elotu ologol laalang' nanu-- nemeaku-- palaaki enkeene oo namuka enyena; nelaibatis ninye ndai tʼOlmumua Sinyati o tʼenkima;"
Luke3:17 neata ninye enkutet enye tiatua engaina enye nelaor ninye naleng' eneisalaashishore enye-- neiturrurroki engano atua embeje enye-- kake elapej suut tʼenkima nememuta."
Luke3:18 Akae-- neitoki adiding'ie nkulie kumok neinosaki olorere lomon lʼeng'ida."
Luke3:19 Ore peitukurru ninye Herodes-- Olaitoriani lʼematua e ong'wan-- tʼolbae le Herodias-- engoroyoni olalashe lenye-- o tʼolbae loo ntorrok pookin naataasa Herodes--"
Luke3:20 neponaa ele kuna pookin neen Yohanes tʼengaji eenata.
Luke3:21 Neaku ore peibatisi olorere pookin neibatisi baiki Yesus-- esaisho-- nebolo shumata"
Luke3:22 nedoiki Olmumua Sinyati tʼemua anaa olmaitai shumata enye neaku eing'ua oltoilo shumata nejo: Ira iye Oinoti lai lanyor oshipakino oltau lai.
Luke3:23 Nera ninye Yesus te ina kata naitera anaa loo larin osom-- anaa enkerai e Yosef le Eliya--"
Luke3:24 le Matat-- le Levi-- le Melki-- le Yanai-- le Yosef--"
Luke3:25 le Matatias-- le Amos-- le Nahum-- le Esli-- le Nangai--"
Luke3:26 le Maat-- le Matatias-- le Semei-- le Yosek-- le Yoda--"
Luke3:27 le Yohanas-- le Resa-- le Serubabel-- le Salaltiel-- le Neri--"
Luke3:28 le Melki-- le Adi-- le Kosam-- le Elmadam-- le Er--"
Luke3:29 le Yesus-- le Elieser-- le Yorim-- le Matat-- le Levi--"
Luke3:30 le Simeon-- le Yuda-- le Yosef-- le Yonam-- le Eliakim--"
Luke3:31 le Melea-- le Mena-- le Matata-- le Natam-- le David--"
Luke3:32 le Yese-- le Obed-- le Boas-- le Sala-- le Naashon--"
Luke3:33 le Aminadab-- le Admin-- le Arnei-- le Esrom-- le Peres-- le Yuda--"
Luke3:34 le Yakoob-- le Isaak-- le Abraham-- le Tara-- le Nahor--"
Luke3:35 le Seruk-- le Ragau-- le Pereg-- le Eber-- le Sala--"
Luke3:36 le Kenan-- le Arpaksad-- le Shem-- le Noa-- le Lamek--"
Luke3:37 le Metusala-- le Henok-- le Yered-- le Malalel-- le Kenan--"
Luke3:38 le Enos-- le Shet-- le Adam-- lʼEngai."
Luke4:1 Nerrinyo Yesus-- eiganya Olmumua Sinyati-- eing'ua Yordan-- neriki tʼolmumua ang'ata"
Luke4:2 netem satan ninye ngolong'i artam. Neitu enya ninye toki too nona olong'i; ore peishunye ninje nening'olamei.
Luke4:3 Nejoki satan ninye: Teni ira iye Oinoti lʼEngai-- tiaki ele soit-- peaku olmkate."
Luke4:4 Nealiki Yesus ninye: Etisiraki-- ajo: Meishiu oltung'ani tʼolmkate ake-- kake tʼororei pookin lʼEngai."
Luke4:5 Nerik satan ninye shumata oldonyo oado neitadol ninye nkarsishuni pookin olmaa nabo kata.
Luke4:6 Nejoki satan ninye: Aalaisho iye ina golon pookin o enkitook enye-- amu aaitarasakaki si nanu nalaisho si nanu ninye olayeu;"
Luke4:7 akae-- teni kiserem tʼengomom ai-- neaku pookin nkunonono."
Luke4:8 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninye: Etisiraki: Teserema Olaitoriani-- Engai ino-- nisyayaki ninye openy ake!"
Luke4:9 Nerik ninye Yerusalem neitasheye ninye tʼoldidio lʼengaji sinyati nejoki ninye: Teni ira Oinoti lʼEngai-- tusulakinoi enkop--"
Luke4:10 amu etisiraki: Kintanapaki ilmalaikan lenyena-- pikirrip iye--"
Luke4:11 nikinap te shumata oo ngaik-- pemikinkob osoit enkeju ino."
Luke4:12 Nealiki Yesus nejoki ninye: Etejoki: Mitem Olaitoriani-- Engai ino!"
Luke4:13 Ore peidip satan enkitasuroto pookin-- neng'as aing'ua ninye."
Luke4:14 Neitoki alotu Yesus tʼengolon Olmumua Galilaya neibulaa mbaak enyena atua loshon pookin oomanita.
Luke4:15 Neiteng'enisho ninye tiatua ngajijik Engai enye neitaa iltung'anak pookin ninye kitok.
Luke4:16 Nelotu ninye Nasaret naitubulunyeki ninye-- nejing' tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki atua engaji Engai-- anaa petii orregie lenye-- neinyototo-- peisoma."
Luke4:17 Neishori ninye enkitabu olayolounoni Yesaya. Ore pebol ina kitabu-- netum ewueji netisiraki:"
Luke4:18 Etii Olmumua lʼOlaitoriani shumata ai-- onaa aaela-- painosaki laisinak lomon lʼeng'ida; aairriwaiye-- painosaki looteenaki elakunoto o ilmodook endolishoto; palaku naing'uaiki lootorogonyaki--"
Luke4:19 painosaki olari lotonyorraki lʼOlaitoriani.
Luke4:20 Neigen ninye enkitabu neisho olaisyayani neton. Neing'oraa ngonyek pookin tiatua engaji Engai ninye.
Luke4:21 Neiter ninye ajoki ninje: Eitabaiyoki taata ena sirata atua nkiyaa inyi.
Luke4:22 Neijakenoki pookin ninye neiputukuny tʼolbae loo rorei lʼengaripo ootupukutuo tʼenkutuk enye-- nejo: Mera ninye enkerai e Yosef?"
Luke4:23 Nejoki ninye ninje: Esipa-- kipuopuo aaliki ena kitanyanyukiet: Laishiunoni-- njiunye kion! Ai kitoning'o ntokitin kituak naataa te Kapernaum! Ntobira baiki nji tene-- tiatua olosho le minyi lino!"
Luke4:24 Nejo ninye ake: Japa-- aliki ndai: Metii olayolounoni oanyiti tiatua olosho lenye."
Luke4:25 Naliki ndai tʼesipata: Etii ngolia kumok naatii atua Israel too ngolong'i e Eliya-- eigenoki shumata larin okuni o lapaitin ile neaku olamei kitok tiatua olosho pookin--"
Luke4:26 neitu eirriwakini Eliya o nabo too ninje neme atua Sarepta oo Sidonia-- enetii eng'oroyoni oliai."
Luke4:27 Netii ilkumok lʼenkea oo lbolot atua Israel tʼenkata olayolounoni Elisa-- neitu eisuji o obo too ninje-- neme Naeman-- oltung'ani le Siria."
Luke4:28 Neigany ninje pookin engoro tiatua engaji Engai-- etoning'o kuna--"
Luke4:29 neinyototo nerrumoki aulo engang' nerik ninye metabaiki oldidio lʼoldonyo oshetakino engang' enye-- pesulaa ninye;"
Luke4:30 kake neim ninye empolos enye-- nelo."
Luke4:31 Nedou ninye metabaiki Kapernaum-- engang' e Galilaya-- neaku eiteng'en ninje too ngolong'i naaeng'ieng'areki."
Luke4:32 Neiputukuny ninje naleng' tʼenkiteng'enare enye-- amu etii rorei lenyena atua engolon."
Luke4:33 Netii atua engaji Engai oltung'ani oata Olmumua menengʼani duruki-- nedar ninye tʼoltoilo kitok:"
Luke4:34 Oi-- kainyo kiataiye iye-- Yesus le Nasaret? Iewuo iye-- piminye yook-- ayolo olira iye-- Osinyati lʼEngai."
Luke4:35 Nebuaki Yesus ninye-- ejo: Tumuka enkutuk-- tupuku tiatua ninye. Nenang'aki olmeneng'ani ninye polos nepuku te ninye neitu easaki toki."
Luke4:36 Neaku enkingʼasia too pookin neirorioro tʼempolos enye nejo: Kalo rorei ele? Amu eitanap tʼengolon o tʼenkidimata ilmumuan duruk-- nepuku."
Luke4:37 Neibulu mbaak enyena too wuejitin pookin olosho lomanita.
Luke4:38 Neinyototo ninye aing'ua engaji Engai nejing' atua engaji e Simon. Neaku eibung'ita oltikana kitok engaputani e Simon-- nesai ninje ninye tʼolbae lenye."
Luke4:39 Neitasheiki ninye nebuaki oltikana-- neing'ua ninye-- neinyototo nabokata neisyayaki ninje."
Luke4:40 Ore pedoiyo engolong'-- neaki ninje pookin ninye iltamoiya looata nkeaitin oo muain kumok. Neiteleiki ninye ninje-- oltung'ani pookin-- ngaik neishiunye ninje."
Luke4:41 Nepuku baiki ilmeneng'a too lkumok-- edar nejo: Ira iye Oinoti lʼEngai! Nebuaki neitu eisho ninje eiro; amu etayoloutuo ninje-- aajo era ninye Kristos."
Luke4:42 Ore peaku dama-- nepuku ninye nelo enemetii iltung'anak; neing'oru siamin ninye nepuonu enetii ninye neibok ninye-- pemelo aing'ua ninje."
Luke4:43 Nejoki ninye ninje: Meata kata namainosaki baiki nkulie ang'itie lomon lʼeng'ida lʼenkarsishu Engai-- amu te ina bae aairriuaki."
Luke4:44 Neaku einosaa lomon lʼEngai tiatua ngajijik Engai e Yudaya.
Luke5:1 Neaku eroosh esiamu ninye-- pening' lomon lʼEngai-- neitashe ninye tʼembata olbalbal Genesaret--"
Luke5:2 nedol ngalawani are naaitashe tʼembata olbalbal; netadoutuo larreshok too ninje-- eisujita rresheta enye."
Luke5:3 Nejing' ninye engalawa nabo nara ne Simon nesai ninye-- pelam peno enetoiyo. Ore peidip atotona-- neiteng'en isiamin tiatua engalawa."
Luke5:4 Ore peidip airoro-- nejoki ninye Simon: Tinyikai metabaiki eneasur-- entadoikiti rresheta inyi-- pirreshishosho."
Luke5:5 Nealu Simon nejo: Laiturukoni-- kiteekenyate enkiarie pookin-- neitu kitum toki; kake tʼolbae lʼororei lino alaitadoiki rresheta."
Luke5:6 Ore peidip aaikuna nji-- neiturrur enkumoi kitok oo singir-- nedung'udung'o rresheta enye."
Luke5:7 Neyuku ninje lʼemboitei enye lootii atua engai alawa-- pepuonu aaretoki ninje."
Luke5:8 Ore pedol Simon Petros ena-- nebatatakino nkung' e Yesus nejo: Tung'aiyoki-- Laitoriani-- amu ara nanu oltung'ani aitarruoni!"
Luke5:9 Amu eibung'a enking'asiata ninye o pookin ootaboitare ninye tʼolbae lʼerreshore oo singir looinoto ninje--"
Luke5:10 neijia baiki Yakobos o Yohanes-- nkera e Sebedayos-- loora lʼemboitei e Simon. Nejoki Yesus Simon: Miureisho! amu inter aaku taata olarreshoni loo ltung'anak."
Luke5:11 Ore peidip aatereu ngalawani enetoiyo-- neing'ua ninje pookin nesuj ninye."
Luke5:12 Neaku ore etii ninye atua engang' nabo-- naa ng'orai-- etii oltung'ani obo oiganya enkea oo lbolot; ore pedol ninye Yesus-- nebatata aijululori nesai ninye ejo: Laitoriani-- teni iyeu-- nikindim aisuja."
Luke5:13 Neitorioo ninye engaina enye neporoo ninye ejo: Ayeu-- sujai! Neing'uaiki enkea oo lbolot nabokata."
Luke5:14 Neitanap ninye-- pemeliki oltung'ani-- kake „nno-- pintadol kion olaidasani-- pinjooio nʼenkisujata ino anaa peitanapua Mose-- peaku enjakenishu too ninje“."
Luke5:15 Kake nepona aaibulaa mbaak enyena-- neiturrurro siamin kumok-- pening' ninye neishiunye leyat enye:"
Luke5:16 kake nerishunye nelo ewueji nemetii iltung'anak asaisho.
Luke5:17 Neaku tʼengolong' nabo-- eiteng'enisho ninye; etotonitio Ilfarisayoi o layolok lʼesirata ooetuo eing'ua ngang'itie pookin e Galilaya o Yudaya o Yerusalem; ne-tii engolon Olaitoriani e nebo o ninye-- neishiunye ninye oltung'ani pookin."
Luke5:18 Naa ng'orai-- enapita leak ooje te shumata erruat oltung'ani loata osupetai onunukisho-- neyeu nenap ninye atua-- peitaper tʼengomom enye."
Luke5:19 Ore peitu etum eneimie ninye tʼolbae lʼolorere-- neilepaki keperaji-- neimie atua ilmatofarini neitadoiyo ninye te nebo o erruat enye metabaiki tʼempolos enye-- tʼengomom e Yesus."
Luke5:20 Ore pedol ninye enkirukoto enye-- nejo: Letung'ani-- kintaikiaki nkitarruot inono!"
Luke5:21 Neiter aaibirribir layolok lʼesirata o Ilfarisayoi nejo: Kang'ai lora ele olimu morot Engai? Kang'ai loidim aitau nkitarruot neme Engai openy ake?
Luke5:22 Ore peyolou Yesus nkibirribirrat enye-- nealu nejoki ninje: Kainyo imbirribirrirri too ltauja linyi?"
Luke5:23 Kaa nalelek ajo: Kintaikiaki nkitarruot inono-- arashu: Nyototoi-- tilimanai?"
Luke5:24 Kake piyolouu-- aajo eata Enkerai oltung'ani engolon tʼenkop-- peitau nkitarruot — nejoki ele loata osupetai: Aaliki iye-- nyototoi-- tudumakinoi erruat ino-- nno engaji ino!"
Luke5:25 Neitashe ninye nabokata tʼengomom enye-- nedumu enatepetaiye nelo engaji enye-- eitadaraa Engai."
Luke5:26 Neibung' enking'asiata ninje pookin neitadaraa Engai-- neigany enkuretishu ninje nejo: Kitadua nkiputukunyot taata."
Luke5:27 Ore tekurum oo kuna baak nepuku nedol olaoshoni obo le kodi-- oji engarna enye Levi-- eton tʼeneoshieki kodi-- nejoki ninye: Tusujaki!"
Luke5:28 Neing'ua ninye pookin-- neinyototo nesuj ninye."
Luke5:29 Neitobiraki Levi ninye endaa kitok tʼengaji enye-- neaku enkiturrurroto kitok oo laoshok le kodi o lkulekai oototonitio te nebo o ninje."
Luke5:30 Neing'unyung'unyaki Ilfarisayoi o layolok lʼesirata laiteng'enuok lenyena nejo: Ainyo pidaada niokishosho ndai te nebo o laoshok le kodi o laitarruok?
Luke5:31 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninje: Meyeu loora biot olaishiunoni-- kake loomoi;"
Luke5:32 eitu alotu nanu-- paipot supati-- kake laitarruok-- petum aataalata."
Luke5:33 Nejoki si ninje ninye: Epukoo laiteng'enuok le Yohanes naleng' neitaa sayat-- neijia anaa loo Lfarisayoi-- kake nenya neokisho ilkulonono."
Luke5:34 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Mindimidimi aaitupukoi nkera enkiama-- epon etii osanja e nebo o ninje."
Luke5:35 Kake epuo aapuonu ngolong'i naapuoi aaoru ninje osanja-- nepuo aapukoo too nona olong'i--"
Luke5:36 Neliki ninje enkitanyanyukiet: Metii o obo lopolosu erashet olkila ng'ejuk nepik atua olkila musana; teni eiko nji-- nepolos baiki ele ng'ejuk-- nemenyorra erashet olkila ng'ejuk o ilo musana."
Luke5:37 Nemetii olopik olmarua ng'ejuk atua ilbenia musan; teni eiko nji-- nepolos olmarua ng'ejuk ilbenia neibukori ninye-- neimin ilbenia."
Luke5:38 Kake epiki olmarua ng'ejuk atua ilbenia ng'ejuko-- nepoku pokira are."
Luke5:39 Nemetii o obo lotooko olmarua musana neyeu olng'ejuk-- amu ejo: Eikash olmusana."
Luke6:1 Eaku eimita ninye tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki nkuruman endaa-- nedung'u laiteng'enuok lenyena lukuny engano nenya nenot too ngaik."
Luke6:2 Nejo ilkulekai too Lfarisayoi: Ainyo pintobiribiri nemeaku tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki?
Luke6:3 Nealiki Yesus nejoki ninje: Eitu isomama ndai enaikuna David-- einoto olamei ninye o lʼemboitei enye?"
Luke6:4 Eneikuna nejing' atua engaji Engai neibung' ilmkaten lʼenkitaduaroto nenya neisho baiki lʼemboitei enye-- lemeaku-- penya oltung'ani-- neme laidasak oopeny ake?"
Luke6:5 Nejoki ninje: Era Enkerai oltung'ani baiki Olaitoriani lʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki.
Luke6:6 Neaku tʼengai olong' naeng'ieng'areki ejing' ninye atua engaji Engai neiteng'enisho; netii ina alo oltung'ani otoiyo engaina enye e tatene.
Luke6:7 Neing'oraa layolok lʼesirata o Ilfarisayoi ninye-- ten ak eishiunye ninye tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki-- petum aaitang'oro ninye."
Luke6:8 Kake neyolou ninye nkibirribirrat enye nejoki ele tung'ani otoiyo engaina: Nyototoi-- ntasho tʼempolos! Neinyototo neitashe."
Luke6:9 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Aikilikwan nanu ndai: Keaku-- peitobiri tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki sidan arashu ntorrok-- peitopoki oltau arashu peari?"
Luke6:10 Neing'orong'oraa ninje aman too mbat pookin nejoki oltung'ani: Ntorioi engaina ino! Neiko neijia-- neitobiri engaina enye neaku bioto anaa en e are."
Luke6:11 Neigany ninje enkurruna neirorioro oopeny eneikunaki Yesus.
Luke6:12 Neaku elo ninye too nona olong'i shumata oldonyo-- pesaisho-- nebik enkiarie pookin-- esaita Engai."
Luke6:13 Ore peaku dama-- neipot laiteng'enuok lenyena-- negelu tomon o are tiatua ninje neisho lelo engarna lairriwak:"
Luke6:14 Simon oishoo engarna Petros-- o Andreas-- olalashe lenye-- o Yakobos o Yohanes-- o Filipos o Bartolomayos--"
Luke6:15 o Matayos o Tomas-- o Yakobos le Alfayos o Simon loipotoki Selotes (Oirowua)--"
Luke6:16 o Yudas le Yakobos o Yudas Iskariotes otaa olaitarasaroni.
Luke6:17 Ore pedou te nebo o ninje-- neitashe tʼewuas o esiamu kitok oo laiteng'enuok lenyena o olorere kumok oing'ua Yudaya pookin o Yerusalem o Tiros o Sidon tʼembata olbalbal--"
Luke6:18 nepuonu lelo-- pening' ninye-- peishiunyeki too nkeaitin enye o kulo ooitirika ilmumuan duruk-- neishiunyeki ninje."
Luke6:19 Neing'oru esiamu pookin ninye-- peporoo; amu etupukuo te ninye engolon-- neishiunye pookin."
Luke6:20 Nedumaki ninye ngonyek enyena laiteng'enuok lenyena nejo: Teshi ndai-- laisinak-- amu eninyi enkarsishu Engai."
Luke6:21 Teshi ndai-- looata olamei taata-- amu ipuopuo aaraposho. Teshi ndai-- looishirita taata-- amu ipuopuo aakweni."
Luke6:22 Teshi ndai-- teni epuo aaibai iltung'anak ndai-- teni egelaa nesul ndai-- neiturraa engarna inyi anaa entorrono tʼolbae lʼEnkerai oltung'ani."
Luke6:23 Enting'idata te ina olong'-- endumuduma; amu eng'orai-- kitok olkwaje linyi te shumata. Neijia baiki eikunakitia loomenye lenye layolounok."
Luke6:24 Ee-- kake aiya-- ndai ladupak; amu indipa aata enkilejilejata inyi."
