Luke6:25 Ee-- kake aiya-- ndai lootaraposhote taata; amu ipuopuo aatum olamei. Ee-- kake aiya-- lookweni taata; amu ipuopuo aailish-- nipuopuo aaishir."
Luke6:26 Ee-- kake aiya-- looimaki iltung'anak pookin too sidan! amu neijia baiki eikunakitia loomenye lenye layolounok lʼelejare."
Luke6:27 Kake aliki ndai lining'itoto: Entonyor ilmang'ati linyi-- entobirakiti sidan looiba ndai--"
Luke6:28 entamayan loodek ndai-- entasayakiti loosukeny ndai."
Luke6:29 Olikiosh eseder nabo-- mbelekenyaki ninye baiki engai; olikioru enkila ino-- mimitiki ninye baiki emekiti."
Luke6:30 Olikiomonu iye-- njoo ninye; olikioru masaa inono-- mintoki aikilikwanu."
Luke6:31 Ore neijia anaa piyeuu neitobiraki iltung'anak ndai-- neijia entobirakiti si ndai ninje."
Luke6:32 Ore pinyorrinyorro loonyor ndai-- — kaa aripo itumutumu? Amu enyor baiki laitarruok loonyor ninje."
Luke6:33 Ore pintobirakiki sidan looitobiraki ndai sidan-- kaa aripo itumutumu? Amu eiko baiki laitarruok neijia."
Luke6:34 Teni isilenokiki iltung'anak lianyunyu-- aajo ipuopuo aaitoki aang'amu — kaa aripo itumutumu? Eisilenoki baiki laitarruok laitarruok-- pepuo aang'amu ebaia."
Luke6:35 Kake entonyor ilmang'ati linyi; entobira sidan-- esilenokiti-- nimianyunyu toki; neaku olkwaje linyi kitok nipuopuo aaku nkera Olotii shumata naleng'-- amu ebor ninye too lemejo ashe o too ltorrok."
Luke6:36 Entaa loonana oshuak anaa peata Minyi linyi engoshoke nanana.
Luke6:37 Emingwenaki-- pemeigwenakini si ndai; emiar tʼenkigwena-- pemeari si ndai. Entung'aikiti-- neing'uaikini si ndai."
Luke6:38 Enjooi-- neishori si ndai; entemet sidai-- naitunyokino-- neiposhiposhakino-- neibukubukori-- ninye epiki atua olkila tʼolgoo linyi-- amu entemet nitemiemie ndai-- ninye etemakinyeki si ndai."
Luke6:39 Nejoki ninje enkitanyanyukiet: Keidim olmodooni atoriko olekai modooni? Medoiki ninje pokira are atua engumoto?
Luke6:40 Melang' olaiteng'enuoni olaiteng'enani lenye; ore olaiteng'enuoni pookin loidipakine-- neaku ninye anaa olaiteng'enani lenye."
Luke6:41 Akae-- ainvo pidol embajuai natii atua engong'u olalashe lino-- nimiyolou olmuambai otii atua engong'u ino?"
Luke6:42 Kaji inko teni indim atiaki olalashe lino: Lalashe-- njooki-- paitau embajuai natii engong'u ino-- nimidol openy olmuambai lotii atua engong'u ino? Iye-- laitusupatuoni-- tang'asa ntau olmuambai tʼengong'u ino-- pitum aing'orai abaraki embajuai natii atua engong'u olalashe lino-- pintau ninye."
Luke6:43 Metii oljani sidai oiu ilmomo torrok-- nemeitoki atii oljani torrono oiu ilmomo sidan."
Luke6:44 Amu eyolounye pookin too lmomo lenyena oopeny. Amu meng'eru oltung'ani ilng'abolo too lbibia-- nemeng'eru lama too ntulele."
Luke6:45 Neitupuku oltung'ani sidai too masaa sidan oltau lenye sidan; neitupuku oltorrono tʼentorroni ntorrok; amu enkiganyata oltau eiro enkutuk enye.
Luke6:46 Ainyo pikimpotipoto: Laitoriani-- Laitoriani! nimintobiribiri enajo?"
Luke6:47 Ore oltung'ani pookin olotu enatii neitobir ninje-- nalaitadol ndai-- ang'ai enyanyukie ninye."
Luke6:48 Enyanyukie ninye oltung'ani otesheta engaji enye netur naleng' nepik entonata enye shumata osoit. Ore peaku engare kitok neipony engare ina aji tʼengolon-- neitu eidim aing'unung'unye ninye-- tiaraki natipikaki entonata enye shumata osoit."
Luke6:49 Oloning' nemeitobir-- nenyanyukie ninye oltung'ani otesheta engaji enye shumata enkop-- nemeata entonata; neipony engare ninye tʼengolon-- nerratanya nabokata neaku engiligilata e ina aji kitok."
Luke7:1 Ore tekurum-- eidipaka ninye rorei lenyena pookin atua nkiyaa olorere-- nejing' Kapernaum."
Luke7:2 Netii olkigeluni loata olaisyayani lenye omoi otaa nae-- nenyor ninye."
Luke7:3 Ore pening' ninye mbaak e Yesus-- neirriwaki ninye laigwenak loo Yudayoi nesai ninye-- pelotu aitopok olaisyayani lenye."
Luke7:4 Ore pebaiki ninje Yesus-- nesai ninye osupatei nejo: Era ninye supat-- pintaasaki ninye ina;"
Luke7:5 amu enyor ninye olorere lang' neteshetaka yook engaji Engai.
Luke7:6 Akae-- nelo Yesus te nebo o ninje. Ore peaku mekure elakwaniki ninye engaji-- neirriwaki olkigeluni ninye iljorueta-- pejoki ninye: Laitoriani-- mintanyamal kion; mara nanu toki-- pijing' iye abori e keperaji ai;"
Luke7:7 onaa atejo si nanu-- mara toki-- palotu eniti iye; kake tolimu ororei obo-- neishiu olaisyayani lai."
Luke7:8 Amu ara si nanu oltung'ani otii abori enkitoria-- naata sikerin tiabori ai-- teni ajoki ele: Nno-- nelo; o olekai: Wou! nelotu; o olaisyayani lai: Ntobira ena! neitobir."
Luke7:9 Ore pening' Yesus kuna-- neiputukunyoki ninye-- neibelekenyakino esiamu natusuja ninye nejo: Aliki ndai: Eitu adol baiki tiatua Israel enkirukoto kitok anaa ena."
Luke7:10 Ore peidip aatorrinyoto looirriwaiyoki aji-- neinepu olaisyayani otamoiya aa bioto."
Luke7:11 Neaku engai olong' nelotu engang' naji Nain-- nerubare laiteng'enuok lenyena o esiamu kitok ninye."
Luke7:12 Ore penvikaki ninye kishomi engang'-- ng'orai-- enapitai olotua aaitupuku-- nera Oinoti obo te ng'otonye nara engoliai-- nerubare olorere kumok lʼengang' ninye."
Luke7:13 Ore pedol Olaitoriani ninye-- neibung'aki ninye engoshoke nanana nejoki ninye: Minjir!"
Luke7:14 Nelotu neing'unye osanduku lʼempopong'-- neitashe lanapak-- nejo: Lebarnoti-- aaliki iye-- nyototoi!"
Luke7:15 Neinyototo olotua aton neiter airo; neisho ninye ng'otonye enye.
Luke7:16 Neibung' enkuretishu iltung'anak pookin neitadaraa ninje Engai nejo: Einyotote olayolounoni kitok tiatua yook-- neiroroki Engai olorere lenye."
Luke7:17 Neibulu mbaak enyena atua Yudaya pookin o atua loshon pookin loomanita.
Luke7:18 Akae-- neinosaki laiteng'enuok le Yohanes ninye kuna baak pookin. Neipot Yohanes laiteng'enuok lenyena are"
Luke7:19 neirriwaki ninje Yesus nejo: Ira iye ololotu arashu kianyu olekai?
Luke7:20 Ore pepuonu kulo leak enetii ninye-- nejo ninje: Yohanes Olaibatisani loirriua yook ejo: Ira iye ololotu arashu kianyu olekai?"
Luke7:21 Neishiunye ninye te ina kata ilkumok too nkeaitin o too sinaitin o too lmumuan duruk neisho edolisho ilmodook kumok.
Luke7:22 Nealiki nejoki Yesus ninje: Embung'a engoitoi-- enosakiti Yohanes enidolitata o enining'itoto: Edolisho ilmodook-- nelimana lemeidim aashom-- neisuji looata enkea oo lbolot-- nening'isho ilming'an-- nepiu lootuata-- neinosakini laisinak lomon lʼeng'ida;"
Luke7:23 naa tesh oltung'ani lamaarikare nanu.
Luke7:24 Ore peidip aashom kulo kiliku le Yohanes-- neiter aliki ninye siamin mbaak e Yohanes: Itupukutuo aapuo ang'ata aaing'oraanyoo? Olperesiong'uyanita olkutati?"
Luke7:25 Arashu itupukutuo aapuo aadol nyoo? Oltung'ani oishopokoki ilkilani oopuyapui? Eng'orai-- etii iltung'anak looata ilkilani lʼendenyata o enkinosata atua ngajijik oo lkarsisi."
Luke7:26 Arashu itupukutuo aapuo aadol nyoo? Olavolounoni? Ee-- aliki ndai baiki ololang' olayolounoni."
Luke7:27 Era ninye olotisirakaki: Ng'orai-- airriwaa nanu olmalaika lai lukunya engomom ino olikintobiraki engoitoi tʼengomom ino."
Luke7:28 Aliki ndai: Metii o obo lotoiwuoki too ng'oroyok olkitok lolang' Yohanes; kake olora kiti tiatua enkarsishu Engai-- naa kitok nelang' ninye."
Luke7:29 Ore olorere pookin lotoning'o ninye o laoshok le kodi-- neitaa ninje Engai supat neisho eibatisi ninje tʼenkibatisa e Yohanes."
Luke7:30 Neany Ilfarisayoi o laiteng'enak loo nkitanapat enkigwena Engai tiatua ninje-- neitu eisho eibatis ninye ninje."
Luke7:31 Nejo Olaitoriani: Kainyo aitanyanyukie iltung'anak lʼena kishon-- kainyo enyanyukie ninje?"
Luke7:32 Enyanyukie nkera naatoni tʼosingira naaipot nkulie-- ejo: Kisulakitia ndai-- neitu intyamityamama; kinjirakitia ndai-- neitu intong'ung'u ilkiyo."
Luke7:33 Amu eewuo Yohanes Olaibatisani-- menya endaa nemeok olmarua-- nijojo: Eata olmeneng'ani."
Luke7:34 Eewuo Enkerai oltung'ani nenya neok-- nijojo: Eng'orai-- oltung'ani ainosani naa aokoni lʼolmarua-- oljore loo laoshok le kodi o loo laitarruok."
Luke7:35 Neitaai supat eng'eno too nkera enyena pookin.
Luke7:36 Nesai obo too Lfarisayoi ninye-- penya endaa te nebo o ninye; nejing' engaji e ilo Farisayos neton tʼenedaareki."
Luke7:37 Naa ng'orai-- netii eng'oroyoni nabo atua ena ang' nera engaitarruoni; ore peyolou ninye-- ajo etotona ninye tiatua engaji Olfarisayos-- neau oltulet lʼeilata narropil--"
Luke7:38 neitashe tekurum-- engalo oo nkejek enyena-- eishirita-- neiter aitong'aki ilkiyo nkejek enyena nejut ninje too lpapit lʼelukunya enye-- neng'utut naleng' nkejek enyena neel ninje tʼeilata narropil."
Luke7:39 Ore pedol Olfarisayos loipoto ninye kuna-- neiro tiatua kion nejo: Ten emutu era ele olayolounoni-- anaata eyolou enara o kaa ng'oroyoni ena naporoo ninye; amu era ninye engaitarruoni."
Luke7:40 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninye: Simon-- aata entoki naaliki iye. Nejo si ninye: Laiteng'enani-- tolimu ake."
Luke7:41 Etii iltung'anak aare looata esile oltung'ani obo: neata obo esile denaria iip imiet-- neata olekai onom."
Luke7:42 Ore peitu eata ninje enalakie-- neing'uaiki pokira are. Akae-- tolimu-- kang'ai too ninje onyor ninye nelang'?"
Luke7:43 Nealu Simon nejo: Ajo nanu ilo lotung'aikiaki nalang'. Nejoki ninye: Itaalua sidai.
Luke7:44 Neibelekenyakino ina ng'oroyoni-- nejoki Simon: Idolita ena ng'oroyoni? Atijing'ua nanu atua engaji ino-- neitu kinjo engare oo nkejek; kake aaitong'aka ilkiyo nkejek ainei nejut ninje too lpapit lenyena."
Luke7:45 Neitu kinjo eng'ututata; ore ninye neba nejing'u eitu epal ang'utut naleng' nkejek ainei.
Luke7:46 Neitu kiel tʼeilata elukunya ai; aaela ninye tʼeilata narropil nkejek ainei.
Luke7:47 Onaa aajoki iye: Etung'aikiaki ninye nkitarruot enyena naara kumok-- tiaraki natonyorra naleng'; oloing'uaikini nkuti-- nenyorru enkiti."
Luke7:48 Nejoki ninye: Kitung'aikiaki nkitarruot inono!
Luke7:49 Neiter kulo loototonitio te nebo o ninye aajo tiatua aten: Ang'ai ele oing'uaiki nkitarruot?
Luke7:50 Nejoki ninye ina ng'oroyoni: Enkirukoto ino nikintopua; nno tʼeseriani!
Luke8:1 Neaku engai olong' neim ninye ngang'itie kituak o nkutiti-- eiroru neinosu lomon lʼeng'ida lʼenkarsishu Engai-- ninye o lelo tomon o are--"
Luke8:2 netii si ematua oo ng'oroyok naaishiunye ninye too lmumuan torrok o too moiyaitin-- etii Maria naipoti Magdalena-- natupukunye ilmeneng'a oopishana--"
Luke8:3 o Yohana-- eng'oroyoni e Kusas lora olaitubulunoni le Herodes-- o Susana o nkulie kumok naaisyayakitia ninye too masaa enye."
Luke8:4 Ore petumo esiamu kitok nepuonu ninje enetii ninye-- eing'ua ngang'itie-- nelimu ninye tʼenkitanyanyukiet:"
Luke8:5 Etupukuo olaisuaroni obo-- peiye eisuaia embeu enye. Ore peisuaia ninye-- nedoiki ematua engoitoi-- neroroi nenya ntaritik e shumata ina."
Luke8:6 Nedoiki engai matua shumata osoit-- nebulu netoi-- tiaraki nemeata ntonat."
Luke8:7 Nedoiki engai matua empolos oo lkikarreta-- nebulu ina te nebo oo lkikarreta-- negor ina."
Luke8:8 Nedoiki engai matua atua enkop sidai-- nebulu-- neiu ilmomo iip. Ore ejoito nona-- nelimu tʼoltoilo: Oloata nkiyaa naaning'ie-- njening'!"
Luke8:9 Neikilikwan laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye: Kaa kitanyanyukiet ena?
Luke8:10 Nejo ninye: Eitumunyanaki ndai-- piyolouu njumat enkarsishu Engai-- o ilkulekai too nkitanyanyukieta-- pemedolisho edolita-- nememus ening'ito."
Luke8:11 Naa ena enkitanyanyukiet: Era embeu lomon lʼEngai.
Luke8:12 Ore kulo lʼengoitoi nera looning'; nelotu tekurum satan neitai ele rorei too ltauja lenye-- pemeiruk nepok."
Luke8:13 Ore kulo le shumata osoit-- nera looning' tʼeng'ida-- neng'amu ororei-- kake meata ninje ntonat; neiruk ninje tʼenkiti kata-- ore tʼenkata enkitasuroto nerishunye."
Luke8:14 Ore enatadoikio atua ilkikarreta-- nera ninje lootoning'o nepuo ninje-- negori too nkishilarot o too masaa o too naʼidaitin empuan-- nemeiu ilmomo."
Luke8:15 Ore natii enkop sidai-- nera ninje lootoning'o ororei tʼoltau sidai naa bioto neshum neiu ilmomo tʼolng'iria."
Luke8:16 Meinok o obo enkilang'et neopoo ninye tʼentutua arashu epik abori erruat; kake epik shumata enkibung'et-- pedol loojing'u enkilang'et."
Luke8:17 Amu metii enaisudori-- nemelo alioi; nemetii enashuma-- nemeyolouni-- nelotu ewuas."
Luke8:18 Eng'orai-- eninkoko-- pining'ining'i; amu oloata-- neishori ninye; ore olemeata-- neoruni ninye baiki enaata."
Luke8:19 Nepuonu enetii ninye ng'otonye o lalashera lenyena neitu eidim aatinyikakiti ninye tʼolbaelʼesiamu.
Luke8:20 Nejokini ninye: Eitashe ng'utunyi ino o lalashera linono te boo neyeu nikidol.
Luke8:21 Nealu ninye nejoki ninje: Era yeiyo ai o lalashera lainei kulo looning' lomon lʼEngai neitobir.
Luke8:22 Neaku tʼengolong' nabo neilepaki ninye engalawa te nebo o laiteng'enuok lenyena; nejoki ninye ninje: Matalang' aabaiki lido kekun lʼolbalbal! Nenyikaa.
Luke8:23 Ore epuoito ninje tʼengalawa neirrag ninye aitai njok. Nedumunye olimwa lʼenkutishoto tʼolbalbal-- neigany engalawa engare neaku atua osina etii."
Luke8:24 Nepuonu ninje neinyeye ninye nejo: Laiturukoni-- Laiturukoni-- kiminita! Neinyototo ninye nebuaki olkutati o enkiposhata engare; neagaa neaku olgira."
Luke8:25 Nejoki ninje: Kaji etii enkirukoto inyi? Neureishoi ninje neiputukuny nejokino: Kera ang'ai ele oitanap ilkutat o engare-- nening' ninye?"
Luke8:26 Nepuonu tʼengalawa metabaiki olosho loo Lgerasenoi eneishiaakinore Galilaya.
Luke8:27 Ore pepuku ninye nelotu enetoiyo-- nenang'are olee obo ninye-- eing'ua engang' neata ilmeneng'a-- neitu eishop olkila enkata naado neitu ebik tiatua aji-- kake tiatua nkuraren."
Luke8:28 Ore pedol ninye Yesus-- nedar nebatatakino ninye nejo tʼoltoilo kitok: Kainyo aataiye iye-- Yesus-- Oinoti lʼEngai natii shumata naleng'? Aasai iye-- pimikintame."
Luke8:29 Amu eitanapa ninye Olmumua duruki-- pepuku tʼoltung'ani. Amu etung'uyana ninye enkata naado-- neeni too lpisia o too ngameta oo nkejek-- nerripi-- nedung' eeneta-- nearaa olmeneng ani atua ang'ata."
Luke8:30 Neikilikwan Yesus ninye: Ke kiji aa engarna ino? Nejo si ninye: Empuoto; amu etijing'a ilmeneng'a kumok atua ninye.
Luke8:31 Nesai ninje ninye-- pemeitanap ninje-- pejing' atua easuroto."
Luke8:32 Netii ina alo emboo oo lbitiro kumok ooirrititai tʼoldonyo. Nesai ninje ninye-- peisho ejing' atua lelo. Neisho ninje."
Luke8:33 Akae-- nepuku ilmeneng'a te ilo tung'ani nejing' atua ilbitiro-- nesulakino emboo tʼemarti atua olbalbal-- nedoiki."
Luke8:34 Ore pedol lairritak enataa-- nekwet aainosu tiatua engang' o tiatua nkuruman."
Luke8:35 Nepuku ninje-- pedol enataa-- nepuonu enetii Yesus-- neinepu oltung'ani otupukunye ilmeneng'a-- etonita tʼengalo oo nkejek e Yesus eishopo-- neata eng'eno enye-- neureishoi ninje."
Luke8:36 Neinosaki ninje kulo lootadua eneikunaki eishiunyeki oloata ilmeneng'a.
Luke8:37 Nesai esiamu pookin oo mbat olosho loo Lgerasenoi ninye-- peing'ua ninje-- amu eibung'a enkuretishu kitok ninje. Akae-- nejing' ninye atua engalawa nerrinyo."
Luke8:38 Nesai ninye ele loitupukunye ninye ilmeneng'a-- pebik te nebo o ninye. Kake eitanapare ninye nejo:"
Luke8:39 Torrinyoi engaji ino-- pinosaa ntokitin kituak nikintobiraka Engai. Nelo ninye neim engang' pookin neinosu ntokitin kituak naaitobiraka Yesus ninye."
Luke8:40 Ore perrinyo Yesus-- neng'amu esiamu ninye; amu etaanyutua pookin ninye."
Luke8:41 Naa ng'orai-- nelotu olee obo oji Yairos-- nera ninye olkitok lʼengaji Engai; nebatatakino ninye nkejek e Yesus nesai ninye-- pejing' engaji enye;"
Luke8:42 amu eata entito enye nabo-- nera ninye noo larin tomon o are-- etaa nae ninye. Akae-- ore eloito ninye-- neroosh isiamin ninye."
Luke8:43 Netii eng'oroyoni nabo naata empukunoto osarge larin tomon o are-- neishaka pookin naata ninye laishiunok-- neitu eidim oltung'ani o obo aishiunye ninye;"
Luke8:44 nenyiku ninye tekurum neporoo enaipukoi olkila lenye-- neitir nabokata empukunoto osarge lenye."
Luke8:45 Nejo Yesus: Kang'ai laataporoiye nanu? Ore emiki pookin-- nejo Petros o lʼemboitei enye: Laiturukoni-- kimanita siamin nikiroosh-- nijo iye: Kang'ai laataporoiye nanu?"
Luke8:46 Nejo ake Yesus: Aataporoiye oltung'ani; amu atoning'o engolon natupukuo te nanu.
Luke8:47 Ore pedol eng'oroyoni ajo meisudori-- nelotu eikirikira-- nebatatakino ninye neinosaki ninye tʼengomom olorere pookin-- ajo ainyo petaporoiye ninye o eneikuna neishiu nabokata."
Luke8:48 Nejoki ninye: Naito-- ntagoluoi tʼoltau! enkirukoto ino nikintopua. Nno tʼeseriani!"
Luke8:49 Ore epon eirorita ninye-- nelotu oltung'ani obo oing'ua engang' olkitok lʼengaji Engai nejo: Eidipa atua entito ino; mintoki aitanyamal olaiteng'enani."
Luke8:50 Ore pening' Yesus ena-- nealiki ninye nejo: Miureisho; ruko ake-- nelapok!"
Luke8:51 Ore pelotu aji-- neitu eisho oltung'ani o obo ejing' o ninye neme Petros o Yohanes o Yakobos o menye lʼenkerai o ng'otonye."
Luke8:52 Neishir pookin aaishiraki ninye. Nejo ninye: Eminjir! eitu ee-- kake eirura."
Luke8:53 Nekweniye ninje ninye-- eyolo-- aajo eidipa atua ninye."
Luke8:54 Neitupuku ninye ninje pookin neibung' enkerai engaina neipot-- ejo: Nakerai-- nyototoi!"
Luke8:55 Nerrinyo Olmumua lenye-- neitashe nabokata-- neitanapisho-- peishori ninye endaa."
Luke8:56 Neing'asia lootoiutuo ninye. Neitanap ninje-- pemeliki oltung'ani enataa."
Luke9:1 Neipot ninye kulo tomon o are te nebo neisho ninje enkidimata naitoreye ilmeneng'a neidim aaishiunye nkeaitin;
Luke9:2 neirriwaa ninje-- peinosaa enkarsishu Engai-- peishiunye loomoiyaa--"
Luke9:3 nejoki ninje: Eminap entoki engoitoi-- olartat arashu olbene arashu endaa arashu ngoshola; emiata baiki ilkilani aare."
Luke9:4 Ore engaji pookin nitijing'a-- entobik tiatua-- metabana nipukuku te ina alo."
Luke9:5 Ore iltung'anak pookin lemeng'amu ndai-- teni ipukuku te ina ang'-- empiripiroi enterit too nkejek inyi-- peaku enjakenishu too ninje."
Luke9:6 Nepuo ninje neim ngang'itie neinosu lomon lʼeng'ida-- neishiunye too wuejitin pookin."
Luke9:7 Ore pening' Olaitoriani lʼematua e ong'wan-- Herodes-- pookin nataa-- neing'arrirro-- tiaraki natejo iltung'anak: Etopiwuo Yohanes too lootuata;"
Luke9:8 nejo ilkulekai: Etalie Eliya; naa kulekai: Etopiwuo obo too layolounok le opa.
Luke9:9 Nejo Herodes: Atudung'o Yohanes elukunya. Ang'ai ele laning'oki nji mbaak enyena? Neyeu nedol ninye.
Luke9:10 Nerrinyo lairriwak neinosaki ninye naitobira ninje. Nerik ninye ninje nerishaki ewueji enye openy tʼenetii engang' Betsaida.
Luke9:11 Ore peyolou siamin-- nesuj ninye; neng'amu ninye ninje neliki ninje mbaak enkarsishu Engai-- neishiunye kulo looaku-- peishiunyeki."
Luke9:12 Neiter anyikaa endama. Nepuonu kulo tomon o are nejoki ninye: Ntanapare olorere-- pepuo ngang'itie o nkuruman naamanita-- petum nkirragat o ndaikin-- amu kitii ene ewueji nemetii iltung'anak."
Luke9:13 Nejoki ninye ninje: Enjoo ndai ninje endaa! Nejo ninje: Mikiata enalang' ilmkaten imiet o singir aare-- arashu pikimbung' engoitoi aapuo aainyang'aki ndaikin ele orere pookin."
Luke9:14 Amu etii leak anaa iip onom. Nejoki ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena: Entotona ninje too lkererin anaa onom-- onom."
Luke9:15 Neiko neijia neitoton pookin.
Luke9:16 Neibung' ninye kulo mkaten imiet o kulo singir aare neimariri shumata nemayan ninje-- nebelibel neisho laiteng'enuok-- peoriki esiamu."
Luke9:17 Nenya neraposho pookin; nedumuni lekunot oo mbelat enye ilbenia tomon o are.
Luke9:18 Neaku ore pesaisho ninye tʼewueji enye openy netii laiteng'enuok lenyena te nebo o ninye-- neikilikwan ninje-- ejo: Kejo siamin ara nanu ng'ai?"
Luke9:19 Nealu ninje nejo: Yohanes Olaibatisani; nejo ilkulekai: Eliya; o ilkulekai: Obo too layolounok le opa otopiwuo.
Luke9:20 Nejoki ninye ninje: Kake ijojo ndai ara nanu ng'ai? Nealu Petros nejo: Kristos lʼEngai!
Luke9:21 Neitanap ninye ninje-- pemeliki oltung'ani o obo ena--"
Luke9:22 nejo: Meata kata nemeitamei Enkerai oltung'ani too nkumok-- nemeni too laigwenak o too laidasak kituak o too layolok lʼesirata-- neari metua-- nepiu tʼengolong' e uni."
Luke9:23 Nejoki ninje pookin: Oloyeu naasuj-- njemiki kion-- njedumakino esalaba enye ngolong'i pookin-- paasuj."
Luke9:24 Amu oloyeu neitopok empuan enye-- neiminye ninye; ore oloiminye empuan enye tʼolbae lai-- neitopok ele ninye."
Luke9:25 Amu kaa dupoto etum oltung'ani-- teni esot olmaa pookin neiminye kion arashu neinosie kion osina?"
Luke9:26 Amu olaaibung'aki sura nanu o rorei lainei-- nelaibung'aki Enkerai oltung'ani ninye sura-- teni elotu tʼenkitook enye o en e Menye o en oo lmalaikan sinyat."
Luke9:27 Aliki ndai tʼesipata: Etii iltung'anak tiatua kulo looitashe tene lemeinyorrinyor enkea-- metabana nepuo aadol enkarsishu Engai."
Luke9:28 Neaku anaa enkata nijo ngolong'i isiet-- eishunyete kulo rorei-- nerik ninye Petros o Yohanes o Yakobos nei lepaki oldonyo asaisho."
Luke9:29 Neaku ore esaisho ninye-- neala emua engomom enye-- neiborru ilkilani lenyena neilang'ishoi."
Luke9:30 Naa ng'orai-- netii leak aare ooderrita o ninye-- nera lelo Mose o Eliya;"
Luke9:31 etaliote ninje tiatua enkitook neimaki enkiting'oto enye nalaitabaia te Yerusalem.
Luke9:32 Ore Petros o lʼemboitei enye neiroshiki njok ninje. Ore peinyototo ninje-- nedol enkitook enye o kulo tung'anak aare ooitashe o ninye."
Luke9:33 Neaku ore perishare ninje aaing'ua ninye-- nejoki Petros Yesus: Laiturukoni-- sidai-- kitii yook ene! Mateshet iltomboitie okuni: obo lino-- obo le Mose-- obo le Eliya. Nemeyolo ninye enajoito."
Luke9:34 Ore epon eirorita ninye kuna-- nepukoki erukenya neopoo ninje; neurei ninje ejing' atua erukenya."
Luke9:35 Neaku oltoilo-- eing'ua erukenya-- ejo: Nyele Oinoti lai lategelua; entoning' ninye!"
Luke9:36 Ore peaku ele toilo-- neinepuni etii Yesus openy. Negira ninje neitu eliki too nona olong'i oltung'ani o obo toki too kuna naatadua."
Luke9:37 Neaku engai olong'-- etadoutuo ninje tʼoldonyo-- netumore esiamu kitok ninye."
Luke9:38 Naa ng'orai-- neipot olee obo tiatua esiamu nejo: Laiteng'enani-- aasai iye-- ping'oraa enkerai ai-- amu era ninye enkerai ai nabo--"
Luke9:39 naa ng'orai-- eibung' Olmumua ninye-- nedar nabokata-- neiponyipony ninye-- epuku olaburra-- neitoki aing'uaiki tʼosina-- eitalepoiye ninye."
Luke9:40 Nasai laiteng'enuok linono-- pemir ninye-- neitu eidim."
Luke9:41 Nealu Yesus nejo: Ndai enkishon nemeiruk naa aibeloni-- ke metabaiki anu aboitare nanu ndai nang'iriaki ndai? Toriku enkerai ino ene!"
Luke9:42 Ore elotu ninye-- neiponyipony olmeneng'ani ninye neisugum. Nebuaki Yesus Olmumua duruki neishiunye enkerai nerrinyoki menye lenye."
Luke9:43 Neiputukuny ninje pookin naleng' tʼolbae lʼenkitook Engai. Ore eiputukunyito ninje pookin tʼolbae loo mbaak pookin naaitobira ninye-- nejoki ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena:"
Luke9:44 Entipik kulo rorei atua nkiyaa inyi: Amu epuoi aaitarasaki Enkerai oltung'ani atua ngaik oo ltung'anak.
Luke9:45 Kake eitu eyolou ninje kulo rorei-- neaku etushumaki too ninje-- pemeyolou. Neurei ninje eikilikwan ninye mbaak oo kulo rorei."
Luke9:46 Nejing' atua ninje nkibirribirrat: Kang'ai lora kitok too ninje?
Luke9:47 Ore pedol nkibirribirrat oo ltauja lenye-- neibung' ninye enkerai nabo neitasheye ninye te bata enye"
Luke9:48 nejoki ninje: Olong'amu ena kerai tʼengarna ai-- naang'amu nanu; naa olaang'amu nanu-- neng'amu olaairriua: amu olora kinyi tiatua ndai pookin-- nera kitok."
Luke9:49 Nealu Yohanes nejo: Laiturukoni-- kitadua oltung'ani lomirita ilmeneng'a tʼengarna ino-- nikimitiki ninye-- amu eitu esujare yook."
Luke9:50 Nejoki Yesus ninye; Emimitiki! amu ore olemeiba ndai-- nera lʼematua inyi."
Luke9:51 Akae-- ore pebaia ngolong'i enkilepata enye-- neitorioo ninye engomom enye alo Yerusalem--"
Luke9:52 neirriwaa ilkiliku lukunya engomom enye; neibung' ninje engoitoi nejing' atua engang' nabo oo Samareites-- peiye eitobiraki ninye ewueji neirragieki."
Luke9:53 Neitu eng'amu ninje ninye-- tiaraki naitorioiye engomom enye alo Yerusalem."
Luke9:54 Ore pedol ena laiteng'enuok Yakobos o Yohanes-- nejo: Laitoriani-- iyeu nikintanapu enkima pedou te shumata-- peiminye ninje-- anaa peikuna Eliya?"
Luke9:55 Neibelekenya nebuaki ninje nejo: Miyololo-- aajo irara le alo mumua?"
Luke9:56 Amu eitu elotu Enkerai oltung'ani-- peiminye iltauja loo ltung'anak-- kake peitopok."
Luke9:57 Ore peibung' ninje engoitoi aapuo engai ang'-- nejoki oltung'ani obo ninye: Aasuj iye tʼewueji pookin nilo."
Luke9:58 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Eata ntirrashin ngumot neata ntaritik e shumata singin-- kake meata Enkerai oltung'ani eneiteleiki elukunya enye."
Luke9:59 Nejoki ninye olekai: Tusujaki! Nejo si ninye: Laitoriani-- njooki ang'as alo anuk papa lai."
Luke9:60 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Njoo enuk lootuata lootuata lenye-- kake nno iye-- pinosaa enkarsishu Engai!"
Luke9:61 Nejo si olekai: Laitoriani-- aalasuj iye-- kake njooki ang'as alo aitanapare kulo loora lʼengaji ai."
Luke9:62 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Metii oltung'ani opik engaina olkembe neitoki anang' silig-- peaku lʼenkarsishu Engai."
Luke10:1 Ore tekurum oo kuna negelu Olaitoriani kulekai ntomoni naapishana neirriwaki ninje aare-- aare lukunya engomom enye atua ngang'itie pookin o wuejitin pookin naatayeuo nelo ninye."
Luke10:2 Nejoki ninje: Kitok enkisambuare naa kuti laitobirak; akae-- entasai Olaitoriani lʼenkisambuare-- petum airriwaki laitobirak atua enkisambuare enye."
Luke10:3 Enjom! eng'orai-- airriwaa nanu ndai anaa mbalelon atua empolos oo suiyan."
Luke10:4 Eminap entutua arashu olbene arashu namuka; emiroroki oltung'ani o obo tʼengoitoi.
Luke10:5 Ore pijing'ijing'i engaji nabo-- entang'as entejo: Njeaku tʼena aji eseriani!"
Luke10:6 Ore petii ina alo enkerai eseriani-- nelabik eseriani inyi te shumata enye; teni metii-- neitoki arrinyokino ndai."
Luke10:7 Entobik ake tiatua ena aji-- nidaarere niokishorere naata ninje; amu eaku-- petum olaitobirani olkwaje lenye. Emindur tʼengaji aidurraki engai aji."
Luke10:8 Ore engang' pookin nijing'ijing'i neng'amuni ndai-- enosa enaitarasakaki ndai;"
Luke10:9 enjiunye loomoiyaa ootii atua ninje-- entiakiti ninje: Etinyikaka ndai enkarsishu Engai."
Luke10:10 Ore engang' pookin nijing'ijing'i nemeng'amu ninje ndai-- entupukutu-- enjom atua ngoitoi enyena-- entejo:"
Luke10:11 Kipioki ndai baiki enterit engang' inyi natijing'a nkejek ang'; entopon-- entayolo ena-- ajo etinyikaka ndai enkarsishu Engai."
Luke10:12 Aliki ndai: Eikashieki Sodom te ina olong' nelang' ena ang'.
Luke10:13 Ee-- kake aiya-- Korasin! Ee-- kake aiya-- Betsaida! Ten emutu etaa kuna kitobirat kituak tiatua Tiros o Sidon naataasaki too ndai-- anaata etotona ninje tiatua ilguniani o atua nkuruon neala."
Luke10:14 Kake eikashieki Tiros o Sidon tiatua enkigwena nelang' ndai.
Luke10:15 O iye-- Kapernaum-- nikilepieki metabaiki shumata-- kintadouni metabaiki emanyata e satan."
Luke10:16 Oloning' ndai-- naaning' nanu; olomen ndai-- naamen nanu; olaamen nanu-- nemen olaairriua."
Luke10:17 Nerrinyo kulo ntomoni naapishana tʼeng'ida nejo: Laitoriani-- etoning'o yook baiki ilmeneng'a tʼengarna ino."
Luke10:18 Nejoki ninye ninje: Atadua nanu satan anaa enkiwang'ata natusulunye te shumata.
Luke10:19 Eng'orai-- aidipa aishoo ndai engolon niroruarierie lasuria o nkulupan o enkidimata pookin olmang'atinda-- nemear ndai entoki o nabo."
Luke10:20 Epon ming'idada te ina-- ajo eisyayaki ndai ilmumuan-- kake enting'idata-- aajo etisiraki ngam inyi te shumata."
Luke10:21 Negalalu Yesus te ina kata tʼOlmumua Sinyati nejo: Aaitoning'oo iye-- Papa o Olaitoriani le shumata o enkop-- tiaraki nitushumaka kuna lang'eni o iljartani-- nintayolo ninje ilkutiti. Ee-- Papa-- amu neijia itonyorrua tʼengomom ino."
Luke10:22 Neibelekenyakino ninye laiteng'enuok tʼenkilepata nejo: Aaitarasaka Papa lai ntokitin pookin-- nemetii o obo oloyolo Oinoti neme Menye-- nemetii oloyolo Menye neme Oinoti o ele loyeu neitayolo Oinoti ninye."
Luke10:23 Neibelekenyakino ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena nejoki ninje tʼenkilepata: Teshi kuna onyek naadol enidolidolo ndai.
Luke10:24 Amu aliki nanu ndai: Etayeutuo nedol layolounok kumok o ilkarsisi enidolitata ndai-- neitu edol; neyeu nening' enining'itoto-- neitu ening'."
Luke10:25 Naa ng'orai-- neitashe olaiteng'enani obo loo nkitanapat-- petem ninye-- nejo: Laiteng'enani-- kaji aiko-- pajung'u empuan nemeiting'?"
Luke10:26 Nejoki ninye: Ainyo naa nasira tiatua nkitanapat? Ainyo isoma?
Luke10:27 Nealu ninye nejo: Tonyorra Olaitoriani-- Engai ino-- tʼoltau lino pookin o tʼolmumua lino pookin o tʼengolon ino pookin o tʼeng'eno ino pookin-- o lʼelatia ino anaa kion!"
Luke10:28 Nejoki ninye: Itaalua sidai-- nkuna ina-- nilaishiu."
Luke10:29 Kake neyeu neitaa kion supat nejoki Yesus: Ang'ai naa ol elatia ai?
Luke10:30 Nealu Yesus nejo: Etadoiye oltung'ani obo-- eing'ua Yerusalem-- pelo Yeriko-- netumore sing'ouni-- neoru ninye ilkilani nepik ilbaak nepuo neing'ua-- eirasa ee."
Luke10:31 Nedou olaidasani obo aimu ina oitoi-- meyolo o nyoo-- ore pedol ninye-- neiwang'."
Luke10:32 Neijia baiki olevites oewuo ine wueji-- nedol neiwang'."
Luke10:33 Kake eewuo tʼolototo Osamareites obo neinepu ninye; ore pedol ninye-- neibung'aki engoshoke nanana--"
Luke10:34 nerishaki ninye neen ilbaak lenyena nebukoki eilata o olmarua neilepakinye ninye shumata osikiria lenye nerik ninye engaji oo lomon neitolonyilony ninye.
Luke10:35 Ore tʼenasirie neitai denaria are neisho olopeny engaji nejo: Ntolonyilonya ninye-- teni eaku enalang'-- ore parrinyunye-- naalaisho iye."
Luke10:36 Ijo aa-- ang'ai too kulo pokira okuni lotaa ol elatia ele otijing'a atua sing'ouni?"
Luke10:37 Nejo si ninye: Ele loibung'aka ninye engoshoke nanana. Nejoki Yesus ninye: Nno-- nkuna si iye neijia!"
Luke10:38 Ore epuoito ninje-- nejing' engang' nabo. Neng'amu ninye eng'oroyoni nabo naji Marta tʼengaji enye."
Luke10:39 Neata ninye enganashe naji Maria-- neitoton ninye kion tʼengalo oo nkejek Olaitoriani ainining' lomon lenyena."
Luke10:40 Nenyamalu Marta tʼenkisyayare kitok; nelotu ninye nejo: Laitoriani-- ai mishilaa iye-- ajo aapalaki enganashe ai-- paisyaisho nanu openy ake? Akae-- tiaki ninye-- njaaretu."
Luke10:41 Nealu nejoki Olaitoriani ninye: Marta-- Marta-- intanyamaluo ning'uyana too mbaak kumok;"
Luke10:42 kake melaunoi nabo; etegelua Maria ematua sidai-- nemeoruni ninye ena."
Luke11:1 Neaku etii ninye ewueji nebo-- esaisho. Ore peidip-- nejoki obo too laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye: Laitoriani-- nteng'ena yook esayata-- anaa peiteng'ena Yohanes laiteng'enuok lenyena."
Luke11:2 Nejoki ninje: Ore pisaishosho-- entejo: Papa lang'-- litii shumata-- njesinyari engarna ino! Njelotu engarsishu ino! Njeaku eyeunoto ino tʼenkop anaa peaku te shumata!"
Luke11:3 Njoo yook endaa ang' nabaiki yook tʼengolong' pookin!
Luke11:4 Tung'aiki yook nkitarruot ang'-- amu king'uaiki si yook iltung'anak looata silen ang'! Mirik yook atua enkitasuroto-- kake ntopua yook tʼentorroni!"
Luke11:5 Nejoki ninye ninje: Kangai too ndai loata oljore lenye nelotu ninye-- eipolose enkiarie-- nejoki ninye: Oljore-- silenokoki ilmkaten okuni--"
Luke11:6 amu aatabaikia oljore lai-- eing'ua olototo-- namaata enaisho ninye--"
Luke11:7 nealu ilo otii aji-- nejo: Mikintirik-- amu eidipaki aaigeno kutukaji-- netii nkera ainei atua erruat te nebo o nanu; maidim ainyo-- paaisho iye."
Luke11:8 Aliki ndai: Ten emutu meinyototo ninye-- peisho ninye-- tiaraki nara oljore lenye-- anaata einyototo neisho ninye enayeu-- tiaraki nasaisho ninye naleng' meata sura."
Luke11:9 Naliki si nanu ndai: Entoomonutu-- neishori ndai; eng'orutu-- nitumutumu; entooshiosh-- nebolokini ndai."
Luke11:10 Amu pookin loomonu-- neng'amu; o oloing'oru-- netum; o olooshiosh-- nebolokini."
Luke11:11 Ketii atua ndai enkerai nabo naomonu menye olmkate-- neisho ninye osoit? arashu teni eomonu osingirri-- neisho ninye tʼewueji osingirri olasurai?"
Luke11:12 arashu teni eomonu olmosori-- neisho ninye enkulupa?"
Luke11:13 Akae-- teni iyololo ndai lirara torrok aaishoo nkera inyi nkishoorot sidan-- me naleng' elaisho Papa le shumata Olmumua Sinyati kulo loomonu ninye!"
Luke11:14 Neitupuku ninye olmeneng'ani leitu eidimairoro; neaku ore pepuku olmeneng'ani-- neiro oladuo lemeiro. Neiputukuny siamin."
Luke11:15 Nejo ilkulekai too ninje: Eitupuku ninye ilmeneng'a tʼenkidimata e Beelsebul-- olkitok loo lmeneng'a."
Luke11:16 Netem ilkulekai ninye neyeu olponoto oing'ua shumata.
Luke11:17 Ore peyolou ninye ndamunot enye-- nejoki ninje: Ore enkarsishu pookin naitarrikino tiatua kion-- neaku ang'ata-- neurokino engaji o engaji."
Luke11:18 Teni eitarrikino si ninye satan tiatua kion-- kaji eiko teni eitashe enkarsishu enye? Amu ijojo ndai-- aajo aitupuku nanu ilmeneng'a tʼenkidimata e Beelsebul."
Luke11:19 Kake ore pamir nanu ilmeneng'a tʼenkidimata e Beelsebul-- akae-- tʼenkidimata e ng'ai eitupuku ninje nkera inyi? Eaku ninje te ina laigwenak linyi."
Luke11:20 Kake ore pamir nanu ilmeneng'a tʼolkimojino lʼEngai-- neinepu enkarsishu Engai nabokata ndai."
Luke11:21 Teni errip oloata engolon neata remeta engaji enye-- nebik masaa enyena tʼeseriani."
Luke11:22 Ore pelotu ololang' ninye tʼengolon-- negilu ninye neoru remeta enyena pookin naating'idare ninye-- neor nkyarunot enyena."
Luke11:23 Olemera lʼematua ai-- nera olmang'atinda lai-- olemeiturrur te nebo o nanu-- neisardakie."
Luke11:24 Teni eidip atupuku Olmumua duruki tiatua oltung'ani-- neim atua wuejitin engaroni neing'oru eneeng'ieng'are nelau-- nejo: Alarrinyokino atua engaji ai natupukunye;"
Luke11:25 ore pelotu-- neinepu-- etooroki nekaji."
Luke11:26 Nelo ninye nabokata neriku te nebo o ninye kulekai mumuan oopishana loora torrok nelang' ninye; ore peidip aatijing'-- nemany ina alo-- neaku enkiting'oto e ilo tung'ani torrono nelang' enkiterata."
Luke11:27 Neaku ore eiro ninye kuna-- neapaa eng'oroyoni nabo tiatua esiamu oltoilo nejoki ninye: Tesh engoshoke nikitanapa naa teshi ilkinai litanaa."
Luke11:28 Nejo si ninye: Eikash-- teshi kulo looning' ororei lʼEngai neibung' ninye."
Luke11:29 Ore peiturrurrokino siamin-- neiter ajo: Era ena kishon enkishon torrono; eing'oru ninye olponoto-- nemeishori ninye olponoto neme olponoto le Yona."
Luke11:30 Amu neijia anaa petaa Yona olponoto too ltung'anak le Nineve-- neijia eaku Enkerai oltung'ani tʼena kishon."
Luke11:31 Nelaitashe enkarsis eunore engolong' tʼenkigwena te nebo o leak lʼena kishon nelaar ninje; amu eewuo ninye eing'ua nkiting'ot enkop-- peinining' eng'eno e Salomo; naa eng'orai-- etii ene ololang' Salomo."
Luke11:32 Nepuo aaitashe leak le Nineve tiatua enkigwena te nebo o ena kisbon nepuo aar ninje-- amu etaalate ninje tʼolbae lʼenkinosaroto e Yona; naa eng'orai-- etii ene ololang' Yona."
Luke11:33 Metii oloinok enkilang'et nepik ninye eneshuma arashu abori olkisembe-- kake shumata enkibung'et-- pedol loojing'u enkilang'et."
Luke11:34 Nera engong'u ino enkilang'et osesen; akae-- teni era engong'u ino bioto-- nera osesen lino pookin enkilang'et; kake teni era ninye torrono-- nera si osesen lino enaimin."
Luke11:35 Akae-- ng'orai-- pemeaku enkilang'et natii atua iye enaimin."
Luke11:36 Akae-- teni era osesen lino pookin enkilang'et nemeata ninye enaimin o enkinyi-- neaku ninye enkilang'et tukul-- neijia anaa pikilang'aki enkilang'et enkiwang'ata."
Luke11:37 Ore eirorita ninye-- nesai Olfarisayos obo ninye-- penya endaa te nebo o ninye. Nejing' ninye neton tʼendaata."
Luke11:38 Ore pedol Olfarisayos ina-- neiputukuny-- tiaraki neitu eng'as aisuja-- eitu edaa."
Luke11:39 Nejoki Olaitoriani ninye: Ore ndai-- Ilfarisayoi-- isujusuju oriong' enkwaru o engirra-- kake ebore atua ndai enkisimaroto o entorroni."
Luke11:40 Lemoda-- eitu eitobir oloitobira oriong' baiki atua?"
Luke11:41 Entopon aaisho entoki empuris natii-- naa eng'orai-- neaku eisuja pookin too ndai."
Luke11:42 Kake-- ee-- kake aiya-- ndai Ilfarisayoi-- tiaraki ninjoioio ematua e tomon olkujitai orropil o olkujitai oitorropil ndaikin o noo mbenek pookin-- nilusooso enkigwena o enyorrata Engai! Meata kata nemeitobiri kuna-- nemepali nena."
Luke11:43 Ee-- kake aiya-- ndai Ilfarisayoi-- tiaraki ninyorrinyorro aatotoni too wuejitin elukunya oo ngajijik Engai o nkirorokinot too singiran!"
Luke11:44 Ee-- kake aiya-- ndai layolok lʼesirata o Ilfarisayoi-- amu inyanyukiekie nkuraren nemeyolouni neroro iltung'anak shumata-- meyolo."
Luke11:45 Nealu obo too laiteng'enak loo nkitanapat nejoki ninye: Laiteng'enani-- isul yook-- teni ijo kulo rorei."
Luke11:46 Nejo si ninye: Ee-- kake aiya si ndai-- laiteng'enak loo nkitanapat-- amu intanapinapa iltung'anak irridat lemenapai-- niming'unyenye ndai oopeny kulo rridat tʼolkimojino o obo."
Luke11:47 Ee-- kake aiya ndai! amu ishetishete nkuraren oo layolounok; kake etaara loominyi linyi ninje metuata."
Luke11:48 Onaa injakenunu ning'aring'ara nkyasin oo loominyi-- amu etaara ninje lelo metuata-- nishetakiki ndai ninje nkuraren."
Luke11:49 Onaa ejo eng'eno Engai te ina: Alairriwaki atua ninje layolounok o lairriwak-- near too ninje ilkulekai metuata nemir--"
Luke11:50 petumi aaing'oru tʼena kishon osarge loo layolounok pookin oibukoiyoki-- neba tʼenkitobirata olmaa--"
Luke11:51 eiter tʼosarge le Abel metabaiki osarge le Sakarias otaraki tʼempolos olperere lʼenkidasare o engaji Engai. Ee-- aliki ndai: Epuoi aaing'oru tʼena kishon."
Luke11:52 Ee-- kake aiya-- ndai laiteng'enak loo nkitanapat-- amu iaoita embolet eyolounoto. Nimijing'ijing'i ndai oopeny-- nimitikiki kulo looyeu nejing'."
Luke11:53 Ore peidip atiaki ninje kuna-- neiter layolok lʼesirata o Ilfarisayoi aakeshore ninye naleng' neikilikwan ninye too mbaak kumok--"
Luke11:54 petum aatarresh ninye tʼolosek tʼenkutuk enye.
Luke12:1 Ore peiturrurro olorere iip nkujit neaku eroruaro-- neng'as aiter ajoki laiteng'enuok lenyena tʼenkiterata: Entaduai aten tʼenkisiijoi oo Lfarisayoi nara enkitusupatuo."
Luke12:2 Metii enaiopoiyoki-- nemelo abolunye tekurum-- nemetii enaisudori-- nemeyolouni tekurum."
Luke12:3 Akae-- ore pookin niroro tʼenaimin-- nepuoi aaning' tiatua enkilang'et; ore ening'oming'omakitia nkiyaa tiatua ilkutot-- neinosuni too nkeperi oo ngajijik."
Luke12:4 Kake aliki nanu ndai-- iljorueta lainei: Emiurei looar osesen metua nemeidim aaitobira tekurum entoki nalang'."
Luke12:5 Kake aitadol ndai oliureii: Enturia oloata engolon-- eidipa ataara metua-- nenang'aki atua ewueji enkima. Ee-- aliki ndai: enturia ele!"
Luke12:6 Memirai nkipaikut imiet too mpesai are? Merikinoi baiki nabo too ninje tʼengomom Engai.
Luke12:7 Kake eikenaki baiki ilpapit loo lukuny inyi pookin. Onaa emiureisho! Irara ndai kituak nilang'ilang'a nkipaikut kumok.
Luke12:8 Aliki ndai: Ore oltung'ani pookin laaibalu nanu tʼengomom oo ltung'anak-- nelaibalu baiki Enkerai oltung'ani ilo tʼengomom oo lmalaikan lʼEngai;"
Luke12:9 kake olaamiki nanu tʼengomom oo ltung'anak-- nemikini ninye tʼengomom oo lmalaikan lʼEngai."
Luke12:10 Eing'uaikini ele pookin oimakinye ororei Enkerai oltung'ani; kake olomor Olmumua Sinyati-- meing'uaikini ninye."
Luke12:11 Ore perik ninje ndai atua ngajijik Engai enye o engomom oo lkituak o looata engolon-- emiekenya aaibirribir eninkoko-- teni imitutu aten-- arashu enilimumu;"
Luke12:12 amu elaiteng'en Olmumua Sinyati ndai te ina kata ake enaaku nilimumu.
Luke12:13 Nejoki obo tiatua esiamu ninye: Laiteng'enani-- tiaki olalashe lai-- paaoriki enjung'o."
Luke12:14 Nejoki ninye: Letung'ani-- kang'ai laatipika-- paaku olaigwenani arashu olaoroni tiatua ndai?"
Luke12:15 Nejoki ninye ninje: Eng'orai-- piduaiaia aten tʼengong'u oo masaa; amu meishiu oltung'ani o obo-- tiaraki naata ninye masaa kumok."
Luke12:16 Neliki ninje enkitanyanyukiet nejo: Etii oltung'ani obo adupani-- neisho enkuruma enye naleng'."
Luke12:17 Neibirribir ninye tiatua kion nejo: Kaji aiko-- amu maata enaiturrurroki ng'erunot ainei?"
Luke12:18 Nejo ninye: Alaiko nji: ajar mbejen ainei-- pashet nkituak naalang' naiturrurroki ina alo enkisambuare pookin o masaa ainei"
Luke12:19 najoki Olmumua lai: Lemumua-- iata masaa kumok naashuma noo lann kumok; eng'ieng'ai-- nosa-- tooko-- ting'idai!"
Luke12:20 Nejoki Engai ninye: Lemodai-- eyeuni tʼena kiarie te iye Olmumua lino; ore kuna nintobiraiye-- keaku nkun e ng'ai?"
Luke12:21 Neijia etiu oloshumaki kion masaa nemera oladupani tʼEngai.
Luke12:22 Nejoki ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena: Onaa ajoki ndai: Emiekenvakino empuan inyi eninyanya-- arashu osesen linyi eninjopishopo."
Luke12:23 Amu kitok empuan nelang' endaa naa kitok osesen nelang' olkila.
Luke12:24 Eng'orai ilkurruki; amu meisuaisho nemeisambisho-- meata ninje eneshumishore arashu embeje-- kake eitoti Engai ninje; nirara ndai kituak naleng' nilang'ilang'a ntaritik."
Luke12:25 Kang'ai too ndai oidim ateekenyai-- pepon engadoro enye engaina nabo?"
Luke12:26 Akae-- teni mindimidimi ena nara kinyi tukul-- ainyo piekenyakinono si ninje nkulie?"
Luke12:27 Eng'orai ntapuka eneiko teni ebulu; meipilisho ninje nemeshetisho; kake aliki nanu ndai-- ajo eitu eishopi baiki Salomo tʼenkitook enye pookin anaa nabo too ninje."
Luke12:28 Akae-- teni eishop Engai nji olkujitai otii taata enkuruma nenang'akini taisere enkima-- me naleng' epon aishop ndai-- liatata enkirukoto kinyi?"
Luke12:29 Onaa eming'oru ndai eninyanya o eniokioko-- emiliman aten too nkishilarot."
Luke12:30 Amu eing'oru kuna pookin loreren lemeata Engai; eyolo Minyi linyi-- ajo mindimimdimi aatalaita kuna."
Luke12:31 Entopon aaing'oru enkarsishu enye-- neponikini ndai kuna."
Luke12:32 Miureisho-- enjoo kinyi! amu etonyorra Minyi linyi aishoo ndai enkarsishu."
Luke12:33 Entimir masaa inyi-- enjoo kulo looata osina. Entobirakiti aten ilbenia lememusanu-- masaa nemeng'oru te shumata nemenyikaki olapurroni nemeitarruo laing'ur;"
Luke12:34 amu enetii masaa inyi-- netii ine iltauja linyi."
Luke12:35 Entaa looena mpolosi neiwuwu nkilang'eta inyi--"
Luke12:36 pinyanyukiekie ndai iltung'anak looanyu Olaitoriani lenye-- teni edumunye tʼenkiama-- peiye ore pelotu neoshioshisho-- nebolu ninye nabokata."
Luke12:37 Teshi lelo aisyayak looinepu Olaitoriani lenye-- teni elotu-- eishololo. Japa-- aliki ndai: Erretena neitoton ninje tʼenedaare-- nelotu aisyayaki ninje."
Luke12:38 Ore pelotu ninye tʼerripore e are arashu e uni neinepu ninje nji-- nera teshi lelo."
Luke12:39 Kake entayolo kuna-- ten emutu eyolo olopeny engaji enkata nalotunye olapurroni-- anaata eishololo nemeisho engaji metuudi."
Luke12:40 Onaa entobirakinoto si ndai-- amu elalotu Enkerai oltung'ani tʼenkata nimijojo."
Luke12:41 Nejo Petros: Laitoriani-- ke yook iliki ena kitanyanyukiet arashu pookin?"
Luke12:42 Nejo Olaitoriani: Kang'ai lora olaing'orani supat naa ng'en-- opik Olaitoriani lenye-- peitore laisyayak lenyena-- peoriki ninje endaa tʼenkata enye?"
Luke12:43 Tesh ilo aisyayani olotu Olaitoriani lenye neinepu ninye eiko nji.
Luke12:44 Esipa-- aliki ndai: Ak eitaa ninye-- peitore masaa enyena pookin."
Luke12:45 Kake ten ejo ilo aisyayani tiatua oltau lenye: Elaimutie Olaitoriani lai elotu-- — neiter aar laisyayak o ngaisyayak nenya neok nemera--"
Luke12:46 elotu Olaitoriani le ilo aisyayani tʼengolong' nemejo-- o tʼenkata nemeyolo-- ne-dung'udung' ninye nelaisho olkwaje lenye te nebo o kulo lemeiruk."
Luke12:47 Ore ilo aisyayani lotayolo eyeunoto Olaitoriani lenye nemeitobiraki kion nemeitobir eyeunoto enye-- neari ninye naleng';"
Luke12:48 kake olemeyolo neitobir naaku-- pearieki-- eari ninye enkiti. Ore oltung'ani pookin loishooki nkumok-- neing'oruni te ninye nkumok; ore oloitarasakaki nkumok-- neyeuni te ninye nalang'."
Luke12:49 Aewuo nanu-- panang'aki enkima enkop; kaa toki aitoki ayeu teni eiwuwu!"
Luke12:50 Kake aata enkibatisa naaibatisieki-- naa kaji aiko teni aarooshi metabana nebaia!"
Luke12:51 Ijojo ndai-- aajo aewuo nanu-- peiye aau eseriani enkop? Aliki ndai: Me neijia-- kake enkitarrikino."
Luke12:52 Amu eiter taata epuo aatii imiet atua engaji nabo-- neitarrikino okuni o are-- o are o okuni--"
Luke12:53 neitarrikino menye o enkerai-- o engerai o menye; ng'otonye o entito o entito o ng'otonye; engaputani o esyayunoti-- o esyayunoti o engaputani."
Luke12:54 Nejoki ninye siamin: Teni idolidolo erukenya-- eilepu tʼendoiyoroto engolong'-- nijojo nabokata: Elotu enjan! neaku neijia."
Luke12:55 Teni ekutishoi olkutati lʼeunore engolong'-- nijojo: Eirowuaju! neaku neijia."
Luke12:56 Ndai laitusupatuok-- indimidimi aaitooro emua enkop o en e shumata-- ainyo pimintoorioro si ninye-- ena kata?"
Luke12:57 Ainyo pimingwenunu too ndai oopeny enara esupato?
Luke12:58 Akae-- teni irubare olaitang'oroni lino-- pilo enetii olkitok-- tonyua tʼengoitoi-- piking'uaiki ninye-- pemikinkurtutaki engomom olaigwenani-- nikintarasaki olaigwenani olaisyayani-- nikinang:aki olaisyayani engaji eenata."
Luke12:59 Aaliki iye: Mipuku te ina alo tukul-- metanana nilak empesai enkiting'oto."
Luke13:1 Netii te ina kata ilkulekai ooinosakitia ninye mbaak oo Lgalilayoi looitushulie Pilatos osarge o nkidasareitin enye.
Luke13:2 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninje: Ijojo ndai-- aajo etaa kulo Galilayoi laitarruok nelang' kulekai Galilayoi pookin-- tiaraki naisilote too kuna?"
Luke13:3 Aliki ndai: Me neijia-- kake teni mialala ndai-- nipuopuo aaimin pookin neijia."
Luke13:4 Arashu lelo tomon o isiet lootuurokine olmnara le Siloa near ninje metuata-- ijojo ndai-- aajo etaa ninje laitarruok nelang' kulekai tung'anak pookin oomanya Yerusalem?"
Luke13:5 Aliki ndai: Me neijia-- kake teni mialala ndai-- nipuopuo aaimin pookin neijia."
Luke13:6 Nelimu ninye ena kitanyanyukiet: Eata oltung'ani obo olng'aboli tiatua enkuruma enye oo nkeek olmarua; nelotu-- peing'oru ilmomo te shumata enye-- neitu etum."
Luke13:7 Nejoki olaturoni lʼenkuruma: Ng'orai-- aewuo larin okuni-- eiter taata-- aing'oru ilmomo te shumata ele ng'aboli-- namatum; tudung'o ninye-- amu ainyo peiding'ie ninye enkop pesho?"
Luke13:8 Nealu nejoki ninye: Laitoriani-- tapala ninye tʼele ari-- metabana naturoki ninye napik emodioi--"
Luke13:9 peiye elaiu ilmomo akenya; teni meiu-- tudung'o ninye."
Luke13:10 Neaku eiteng'enisho ninye tʼengaji Engai nabo tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki.
Luke13:11 Naa ng'orai-- netii eng'oroyoni naata Olmumua lʼembebekishu larin tomon o isiet-- netununuke ninye neitu eidim ataapunye tukul."
Luke13:12 Akae-- ore pedol Yesus ninye-- neipot nejoki ninye: Nang'oroyoni-- njoo kilakuni tʼembebekishu ino!"
Luke13:13 Neiteleiki ninye ngaik; neitoriori ninye nabokata neitadaraa Engai.
Luke13:14 Nealu olkitok lʼengaji Engai tʼerikai-- tiaraki naishiunye Yesus tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki-- nejoki olorere: Etii ngolong'i ile-- peitobiri enkyas tiatua ninje; akae-- ewotu tiatua nena-- peishiunyeki ndai-- neme tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki."
Luke13:15 Kake nealiki Olaitoriani ninye nejo: Iye laitusupatuoni-- melaku oltung'ani pookin too ndai olkiteng' lenye arashu osikiria lenye t'embout tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki-- pelo aitook?"
Luke13:16 Meaku-- pelakuni ena ito e Abraham nateena satan larin tomon o isiet tʼena keene-- tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki?"
Luke13:17 Ore ejoito ninye nena-- neibung' ninje pookin enkurruna lootiakinore ninye; neng'ida esiamu pookin too ntokitin kituak pookin naataa te ninye."
Luke13:18 Akae-- nejo: Kang'ai enyanyukie enkarsishu Engai naa ng'ai aitanyanyukie ninye?"
Luke13:19 Enyanyukie ninye embeu e karadali naibung oltung'ani nenang'aki atua enkuruma enye-- nebulu neaku oljani-- nepuo aashet ntaritik e shumata singin tiatua ilng'osil lenyena."
Luke13:20 Neitoki ajo: Kainyo aitanyanyukie enkarsishu Engai?
Luke13:21 Enyanyukie ninye enkisiijoi naibung'a eng'oroyoni nabo neitushulie ntemeta uni entapa-- metabana neisiijoi pookin."
Luke13:22 Neim ninye ngang'itie kituak o nkutiti-- eiteng'enisho-- eloito Yerusalem."
Luke13:23 Nejoki oltung'ani obo ninye: Laitoriani-- kepok ilkuti ake? Nejoki ninye ninje:"
Luke13:24 Entaapare-- pijing'ijing'i kutukaji napirik; amu aliki ndai-- ajo ilkumok ooing'oru ninye-- pejing'-- nemeidim."
Luke13:25 Neba te ina kata-- einyotote olopeny engaji neigen kutukaji-- ninteritere ndai aaitashe te boo nioshioshosho kutukaji-- ijojo: Laitoriani-- Laitoriani-- tabolu yook! Nealu ninye nejoki ndai: Mayolo ening'ua ndai."
Luke13:26 Ninteritere te ina kata aajo: Kitaama nikiokisho tʼengomom ino-- inteng'enita yook too ngoitoi ang'."
Luke13:27 Nelajoki ninye ndai: Mayolo ening'ua ndai; entung'aiyoki nanu pookin-- ndai laitobirak loo ntorrok!"
Luke13:28 Netii ina alo enkishirata o eonyoto oo lala-- teni ipuopuo aadol Abraham o Isaak o Yakoob o layolounok pookin tiatua enkarsishu Engai-- ndai ake eiturrakaki boo."
Luke13:29 Akae-- epuonu ltung'anak-- eing'ua enkilepunoto o endoiyoroto engolong'-- empolos e kiarie o eunore engolong'-- netonie enedaare tiatua enkarsishu Engai."
Luke13:30 Naa ng'orai-- netii lʼenkiting'oto looaku lʼelukunya-- netii lʼelukunya looaku lʼenkiting'oto."
Luke13:31 Nepuonu te ina kata ematua oo Lfarisayoi nejoki ninye: Tupuku-- nno te ine-- amu eyeu Herodes nikiar tua!"
Luke13:32 Nejoki ninye ninje: Embung'a engoitoi-- entiakiti ena tirrash: Ng'orai-- aitupuku ilmeneng'a naishiunye iltung'anak taata o taisere-- nalaitabaia tʼengolong' e uni."
Luke13:33 Kake meata kata namalo taata o taisere o ngailong'-- amu meaku-- peimin olayolounoni ti oriong' e Yerusalem."
Luke13:34 Oi Yerusalem-- Yerusalem naar layolounok metuata niartoosoito likirriwakini iye! Kaigil aja atayeuo naiturrur nkera inono anaa enkikusieki naiturrur eishoi enye tiabori oo naipuko enyena-- neitu iyeuu ndai!"
Luke13:35 Eng'orai-- etung'aikiaki ndai engaji inyi erok. Amu aliki ndai: Mikintokiki aadol nanu-- metabana nelotu enkata nijojo: Njeitadarari ololotu tʼengarna Olaitoriani!"
Luke14:1 Neaku nelotu ninye engaji olkitok obo loo Lfarisayoi tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki-- penya endaa; neing'oraa ninje ninye tʼerreshoto."
Luke14:2 Naa ng'orai-- etii oltung'ani obo tʼengomom enye oata emoiyan engare."
Luke14:3 Nealu Yesus nejoki laiteng'enuok loo nkitanapat o Ilfarisayoi: Keaku-- peishiunyeki tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki arashu me?"
Luke14:4 Negira ninje. Neibung' neishiunye ninye neing'uaiki meshomo.
Luke14:5 Nealu ninye nejoki ninje: Kang'ai olinyi oata osikiria arashu olkiteng' otusulakine engumoto nemeilepunye ninye nabokata tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki?
Luke14:6 Neitu eidim ninje aataalutu nena.
Luke14:7 Neinosaki ninye looipotoki enkitanyanyukiet-- etadua eneiko teni egelu ltoneta lʼelukunya tʼenedaare-- nejoki ninje:"
Luke14:8 Teni kimpot oltung'ani-- pilo enkiama-- miton tʼentonata elukunya; amu teni eipoto ninye oltung'ani kitok likilang' iye--"
Luke14:9 nelotu olikimpoto iye o ninye nikijoki: Njoo ninye ewueji! ore te ina kata ninter atum enkurruna-- piton tʼewueji e abori."
Luke14:10 Kake teni kimpotoki-- nno-- totona tʼewueji e abori; ore pelotu olikimpoto iye nikijoki: Oljore-- tinyikaki lukunya! Nilaata te ina kata enkitook t'engomom oo pookin lootoni te nebo o iye."
Luke14:11 Amu oltung'ani pookin loitaa kion kitok-- neitadouni; o oloitadou kion-- neitaai kitok."
Luke14:12 Nejoki ninye ele oipoto ninye: Teni intobir endaa enkipirata engolong' arashu enteipa-- mimpot iljorueta linono arashu lalashera linono arashu l'enkishomi ino arashu lʼelatia ino oodupa-- pemikimpot si ninje iye-- nikilaakini."
Luke14:13 Kake teni intobir enkinosata-- mpoto laisinak o loo rrugi o lemeidim aashom o ilmodook;"
Luke14:14 Niaku iye tesh-- amu meata ninje enikintoki aalaakinye; amu kilaakini tiatua empiunoto oo looata esupato."
Luke14:15 Ore pening' obo too kulo loototonitio te nebo o ninye kuna nejoki ninye: Era tesh olonya endaa tiatua enkarsishu Engai.
Luke14:16 Nejoki ninye: Eitobira oltung'ani obo endaata kitok neipot ilkumok.
Luke14:17 Neirriwaa tʼenkata endaata olaisyayani lenye-- peliki looipotoki: Ewotu-- amu eidipate pookin!"
Luke14:18 Neiter pookin aasai tʼenkidanyata nabo-- pepali. Nejoki ol elukunya ninye: Ainyang'ua enkuruma-- meata kata namapuku-- paing'oraa ninye; aasai iye-- tapalaki."
Luke14:19 Nejo olekai: Ainyang'ua nanu mboi imiet oo lmong'i nalo-- paleen ninje; aasai iye-- tapalaki!"
Luke14:20 Nejo olekai: Aamua eng'oroyoni-- onaa maidim aeu."
Luke14:21 Nelotu olaisyayani neinosaki Olaitoriani lenye nena. Negoro olopeny engaji nejoki olaisyayani lenye: Tupuku asioki-- pilo ngoitoi kituak o kutiti engang'-- ntijing'u ene laisinak o looata rrugi o ilmodook o lemeidim aashom!"
Luke14:22 Nejo olaisyayani: Laitoriani-- etaa enintanapua-- kake eng'or ewueji."
Luke14:23 Nejoki Olaitoriani olaisyayani: Tupuku-- pilo atua ngoitoi o sarikon-- ntanapu pejing'u-- peiye eigany engaji ai!"
Luke14:24 Amu aliki ndai-- ajo meinyorrinyor o obo too kulo leak looipotoki-- endaata ai."
Luke14:25 Akae-- nepuo siamin kumok te nebo o ninye; neibelekenya ninye nejoki ninje:"
Luke14:26 Teni elotu oltung'ani enatii nemeiba menye lenye o ng'otonye o eng'oroyoni o nkera o lalashera o nganashera-- metabaiki oltau lenye-- meidim ninye ataa olaiteng'enuoni lai."
Luke14:27 Olemenap esalaba enye nelotu tekurum ai-- meidim ataa olaiteng'enuoni lai."
Luke14:28 Amu kang'ai too ndai oyeu neshet olmnara nemeng'as aton neiken enkinyang'a-- anake eata nabaiki?"
Luke14:29 pemeiter aasul kulo pookin loodol ninye-- eidipa atipika entonata-- kake nemeidim aidipa--"
Luke14:30 nejo: Eitera ele tung'ani ashet-- neitu eidim aidipa."
Luke14:31 Arashu kalo karsis olagilunore olekai karsis tʼenjore nemeng'as aton neigwena-- anake eidim atanang'are too elfun tomon ele olotu too elfun tikitam-- pear ninye?"
Luke14:32 Teni me neijia-- neirriwaa olkilikwai epon elakwa olekai-- neomon ninye osotua."
Luke14:33 Akae-- neijia oltung'ani pookin too ndai lemelam pookin naata ninye-- meidim ataa ninye olaiteng'enuoni lai."
Luke14:34 Sidai emakat; kake teni erruoio emakat — ke te nyoo eitameloni?
Luke14:35 Meitoki adupa tʼenkop arashu tʼemodioi-- nemeaku tukul; neiturrakini ninye boo. Oloata nkiyaa naaning'ie-- njening'!"
Luke15:1 Neaku enyikaki ninye laoshok pookin le kodi o laitarruok-- peinining' ninye."
Luke15:2 Neing'unyung'uny Ilfarisayoi o layolok lʼesirata nejo: Eng'amu ele laitarruok nedaare ninje.
Luke15:3 Nejoki ninye ninje ena kitanyanyukiet nejo:
Luke15:4 Kalo tung'ani too ndai-- oata nkerra iip-- neiminaki nabo too ninje-- nemeing'ua kuna ntomoni enturuj o enturuj ti ang'ata-- pelaing'oru enaimina-- metabana netum ninye?"
Luke15:5 Ore petum ninye-- neiteleiki shumata oo ronyi lenyena-- eng'ida."
Luke15:6 Ore pelotu engaji enye-- neipot iljorueta o lʼelatia nejoki ninje: Enting'idata te nebo o nanu-- amu ainoto ena duo ker ai naimina."
Luke15:7 Aliki ndai: Neijia eaku eng'ida te shumata tʼolbae lʼolaitarruoni obo otaale nelang' isupati ntomoni enturuj o enturuj lemeyeu enkitaalata.
Luke15:8 Arashu kaa ng'oroyoni naata ngoshola tomon-- teni eiminaki engosholai nabo-- nemeinok enkima neor engaji nenyok aing'oru metabana netum ninye?"
Luke15:9 Ore petum ninye-- neipot njorueta enyena o nʼelatia nejo: Enting'idata te nebo o nanu-- amu ainoto ena duo osholai naimina."
Luke15:10 Neijia-- aliki ndai-- eaku eng'ida tʼengomom oo lmalaikan lʼEngai tʼolbae lʼolaitarruoni obo otaale."
Luke15:11 Nejo ninye: Eata oltung'ani obo laiyok aare.
Luke15:12 Nejoki oloti too ninje menye: Papa-- njoki ematua oo masaa naaku nkun ainei. Neoriki ninje masaa."
Luke15:13 Ore eitu eishunye ngolong'i kumok-- neiturrur ena duo kerai kiti pookin nelo olosho olakwa; neisardakie te ina alo masaa enyena too ntokitin eng'ida osesen."
Luke15:14 Ore peidip aisardakie masaa enyena pookin-- neaku olamei kitok tiatua ilo osho-- neiter aning' si ninye osina."
Luke15:15 Nelo aisyai obo loo loopeny ilo osho-- neirriwaki ilo ninye atua nkuruman enyena-- peirrita ilbitiro;"
Luke15:16 Neng'war ninye aitaraposh engoshoke enye too ngabobok naainosa ilbitiro-- neitu eisho oltung'ani o obo ninye toki."
Luke15:17 Nerrinyokino kion nejo: Kaja laisyayak le papa lai ooata endaa kitok neiteleku-- ore nanu nae tene tʼolamei!"
Luke15:18 Adumunye alo enetii papa lai-- pajoki ninye: Papa-- aitarruoko shumata o engomom ino--"
Luke15:19 mekure eaku-- paaipoti enkerai ino; nkunakaki anaa obo too laisyayak linono!"
Luke15:20 Nedumunye nelo enetii menye lenye. Ore epon etii enelakwa-- nedolu menye lenye neibung'aki ninye engoshoke nanana nekwet asioio neurokino emurt enye neng'utut ninye naleng'."
Luke15:21 Nejoki ena duo kerai ninye: Papa-- aitarruoko shumata o engomom ino-- mekure eaku-- paaipoti enkerai ino."
Luke15:22 Kake nejoki menye laisyayak lenyena: Eautu asioki olkila lora sidai-- enjopokiti ninye-- entipik olgisoi olkimojino lenye o namuka nkejek enyena--"
Luke15:23 nireuu si olashe opir-- enteyeng'-- mainosa-- mating'idata!"
Luke15:24 amu etua ena kerai ai-- neitoki apiu; eimina ninye-- neinotoki. Neiter aaitaa eng'ida."
Luke15:25 Akae-- netii olbotor lenye enkuruma; ore pelotu anyikaki engaji-- nening' isingolioitin o enkiguran--"
Luke15:26 neipot obo too laisyayak neikilikwan ninye: Ainyo ina?
Luke15:27 Nejoki si ninye: olalashe lino oewuo-- neyeng' minyi lino olashe opir-- tiaraki nainoto ninye aa bioto."
Luke15:28 Negoro ninye neitu eyeu baiki nejing'. Akae-- nepuku menye lenye ailejilej ninye."
Luke15:29 Nealunejoki menye: Ng'orai-- ke larin aja aaisyayaka iye neitu alang' enkitanapata ino tukul-- neitu kinjo iye olker-- pang'ida te nebo o iljorueta lainei."
Luke15:30 Kake ore pelotu ena kerai ino nainosa masaa inono too sindan-- niyeng'aki ninye olashe opir."
Luke15:31 Nejoki si ninye: Nakerai-- itii iye oshi e nebo o nanu; ore pookin naara nkun ainei-- naa nkunonono."
Luke15:32 Kake meata kata nimishipai ning'ida-- amu etua ele alashe lino-- neitoki apiu; eimina ninye-- neinotoki."
Luke16:1 Nejoki si ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena: Etii oltung'ani adupani loata olaing'orani lʼengaji; neitang'ori ele te ninye-- aajo eisardakie masaa enyena."
Luke16:2 Neipot ninye nejoki ninye: Kaa bae ena naning' te iye? Njooki esiana enking'orare ino e atua aji! amu mintoki aidim ataa olaing'orani.
Luke16:3 Nejo oladuo aing'orani tiatua kion; Kaji aiko? Amu aaitau Olaitoriani lai tʼenking'orare engaji; namaidim atuturisho-- natum enkurruna-- teni aomonisho."
Luke16:4 Atayolo enaiko-- teni aaitauni tʼenking'orare engaji-- paapuo aang'amu ninje nanu tiatua ngajijik enye."
Luke16:5 Akae-- neipot ninye iltung'anak pookin looata esile Olaitoriani lenye-- nejoki ol elukunya: Kainyo esile Olaitoriani lai niata?"
Luke16:6 Nejo ninye: Iltuleta iip lʼeilata. Nejoki ninye: Mbung'a sirat inono-- totona asioki-- tisira onom."
Luke16:7 Ore peidip-- nejoki olekai: o iye-- kainyo esile niata? Nejo si ninye: Ntemeta iip engano. Nejoki ninye: Mbung'a sirat inono-- tisira ntomoni isiet."
Luke16:8 Neitadaraa Olaitoriani oladuo aing'orani torrono-- tiaraki naikuna tʼeng'eno; amu era nkera ele maa ng'eni nelang' nkera enkilang'et tiatua enkishon enye openy."
Luke16:9 Naliki si nanu ndai: Entobirakiti aten iljorueta too masaa torrok-- peiye teni iatata osina-- neng'amu ninje ndai tiatua ntoneta oo nkatan pookin."
Luke16:10 Olora supat tʼentoki kinyi-- nera baiki supat tʼentoki kitok; olora torrono tʼentoki kinyi-- nera baiki torrono tʼentoki kitok."
Luke16:11 Teni miakuku supati too masaa torrok-- kang'ai loirukoki ndai enara esipata?"
Luke16:12 Ore pemiakuku supati tiatua masaa olekai-- kang'ai olaislio ndai enara eninyi?"
Luke16:13 Metii olaisyayani loidim aisyayaki laitoriak aare: amu elaibai obo nelanyorru oliare-- arashu elaibung' obo-- nelamenu oliare. Mindimidimi aaisyayakiti Engai o mamon (masaa)."
Luke16:14 Nening' Ilfarisayoi kuna pookin nera ninje loonyor masaa nekweniye ninye.
Luke16:15 Nejoki ninye ninje: Irara ndai looitaa aten supati tʼengomom oo ltung'anak-- kake eyolo Engai iltauja linyi; amu enara kitok tiatua iltung'anak-- nera enkitirikata tʼengomom Engai."
Luke16:16 Etii nkitanapat o layolounok metabaiki Yohanes; neinosuni-- eiter te ina kata-- enkarsishu Engai-- nejing' oltung'ani pookin atua ninye tʼengolon."
Luke16:17 Elelek emuta shumata o enkop nelang' edoiyo oltili obo loo nkitanapat.
Luke16:18 Ore oltung'ani pookin oing'ua eng'oroyoni enye neamu engai-- near ninye enkidikikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni; o si ninye oloamaa enatung'aiye olmoruo lenye-- ear enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni."
Luke16:19 Etii oltung'ani adupani neishop olkila odo o olkila oibor-- neitaa eng'ida ngolong'i pookin naalioi."
Luke16:20 Netii olaisinani obo-- oji engarna enye Lasaros-- neiturrakini engalo kishomi enye neata mbaldakani"
Luke16:21 neyeu neraposho too mbelat naadoiyo tʼenaraa oladupani; metaa epuonu ildiain aamej mbaldakani enyena.
Luke16:22 Neaku nee olaisinani-- neilepie ilmalaikan ninye olgoo le Abraham. Nee si ninye oladuo adupani-- nenuki."
Luke16:23 Ore etii ninye atua ewueji enkima-- neapaa ngonyek enyena-- etii atua emion-- nedol Abraham tʼenelakwa o Lasaros tʼolgoo lenye."
Luke16:24 Neipot ninye nejo: Papa Abraham-- tokorduaki-- rriu Lasaros-- peitadoiki elukunya olkimojino lenye atua engare-- paarrinyoki olng'ejep lai-- amu aameikini tiatua ena kiwuwuoto."
Luke16:25 Nejo Abraham: Nakerai-- tadamu-- ajo inoto sidan inono tiatua empuan ino-- o Lasaros ntorrok; kake ore taata eilejilejitai ninye tene-- o iye-- nikintamei."
Luke16:26 Ore enalang kuna pookin-- otipikaki erishata kitok empolos ang' o ndai-- peiye ore lootii ene-- peyeu nelang'aki ndai-- nemeidim-- nemelang'u le ina alo enikitii yook."
Luke16:27 Nejo ninye: Akae-- aasai iye-- papa-- pirriwaki ninye engaji e papa lai;"
Luke16:28 amu aata lalashera imiet-- peijakenoki ninje-- pemepuonu si ninje atua ene wueji emion."
Luke16:29 Nejo Abraham: Eata ninje Mose o layolounok; njening' ninje!
Luke16:30 Nejo ninye: Me neijia-- papa Abraham! kake teni elo obo too lootuata enetii ninje-- nepuo aala."
Luke16:31 Nejoki ninye: Teni mening' ninje Mose o layolounok-- nemepuo aairuk baiki-- aajo epiu obo too lootuata."
Luke17:1 Nejoki ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena: Meata kata nemepuonu mbaak oo nkitarrikinot-- kake-- e kake aiya oloau ninje!"
Luke17:2 Eikash-- teni eenikini ninye osoit oituutishoreki emurt enye-- penang'akini ninye atua olbalbal-- nelang' eitarriki ninye nabo too kuna kutiti."
Luke17:3 Entagolie aten! Teni eitarruo olalashe lino-- toroja ninye; ore peala-- tung'aiki ninye."
Luke17:4 Ore pikintarruoki ninye iye kat napishana nabo olong'-- nikirrinyokino kat napishana nejo: Airridua! tung'aiki ninye!"
Luke17:5 Nejoki lairriwak Olaitoriani: Toponiki yook enkirukoto!
Luke17:6 Nejo Olaitoriani: Teni iatata enkirukoto anaa embeu e karadali nijokiki ele reteti: Tadotunye-- piun kion tʼolbalbal! anaata etoning'o ndai."
Luke17:7 Kang'ai too ndai loata olaisyayani oturisho arashu oirritisho nejing'u-- eing'ua enkuruma-- nejoki ninye:Wou asioki-- totona tʼenedaareki?"
Luke17:8 Kake me neijia ejoki ninye: Ntobira enanya-- terretenai nikisyayaki-- metabana nanya naok; ore tekurum nilanya nilaok si iye?"
Luke17:9 Kye-- keliki ninye ilo aisyayani oitobira naitanapaki-- baiki ashe? Majo nanu."
Luke17:10 Neijia baiki ndai; ore indipa aaitobira pookin naaitanapaki ndai-- entejo: Kira yook laisyayak leme toki; kintobira enemeata kata nimikintobir."
Luke17:11 Neaku etii engoitoi-- pelo Yerusalem-- eimita ninye empolos e Samaria o Galilaya."
Luke17:12 Ore pejing' ninye engang' nabo-- nenang'are leak tomon ooata enkea oo lbolot-- neitashe ninje tʼenelakwa"
Luke17:13 neapaa iltoiloi lenye nejo: Yesus-- Laitoriani-- tokordu yook!"
Luke17:14 Ore pedol ninye ninje-- nejoki ninje: Enjom-- entadua aten laidasak! Neaku ore epuoito ninje-- neisuji."
Luke17:15 Ore obo lenye otadua-- ajo eishiuwo-- nerrinyo-- eitadaraa Engai tʼoltoilo kitok--"
Luke17:16 nebatata aijululo too nkejek enyena-- eliki ninye ashe; nera ninye Osamareites."
Luke17:17 Nealu Yesus nejo: Mera tomon looisujaki? Kaji etii enturuj naa?
Luke17:18 Eitu etumi olotorrinyunye-- peisho Engai enkitook enye-- neme ele omoni?"
Luke17:19 Nejoki ninye: Nyototoi nno; enkirukoto ino nikintopua!
Luke17:20 Ore peikilikwan Ilfarisayoi ninye: Kanu elotu enkarsishu Engai? nealiki ninje nejo: Melotu enkarsishu Engai tʼemua nalio;
Luke17:21 nemelimuni: Ng'orai-- etii ene! arashu: idye! amu eng'orai-- etii enkarsishu Engai atua ndai."
Luke17:22 Nejoki ninye laiteng'enuok: Epuo aapuonu ngolong'i-- pipuopuo aayeu nidolidolo engolong' nabo Enkerai oltung'ani-- nimipuopuo aadol."
Luke17:23 Nepuo aaliki ninje ndai: Eng'orai ene! eng'orai idye! Emipuo-- emisuj!"
Luke17:24 Amu anaa peiwang' enkiwang'ata-- eing'ua shumata-- neijia elatiu Enkerai oltung'ani tʼengolong' enye."
Luke17:25 Kake meata kata nemeng'asi aaitame too nkumok-- neanyi tʼena kishon."
Luke17:26 Neijia anaa petaa too ngolong'i e Noa-- neijia eaku baiki too ngolong'i Enkerai oltung'ani:"
Luke17:27 nedaa ninje-- neokisho-- neamisho-- neamari-- metabaiki ena olong' natijing'ie Noa atua engalawa-- nelotu engare kitok neiminye pookin."
Luke17:28 Neijia anaa petaa too ngolong'i e Lot: edaa ninje-- neokisho-- neinyang'isho-- nemirisho-- neunisho-- neshetisho;"
Luke17:29 ore te ina olong' natupukuo Lot-- eing'ua Sodom-- nesha enkima o nkibiritini-- eing'ua shumata-- neiminye pookin."
Luke17:30 Neijia eaku baiki tʼengolong' nalioi Enkerai oltung'ani.
Luke17:31 Olotii te ina olong' shumata e keperaji netii masaa enyena atua aji-- njoo medou ninye-- peau nena. Neijia baiki olotii enkuruma-- njoo merrinyo kurum."
Luke17:32 Entadamutu eng'oroyoni e Lot!
Luke17:33 Oloing'oru-- peitopok oltau lenye-- nelaiminye ninye; ore oloiminye ninye-- neitopok."
Luke17:34 Aliki ndai: Nepuo aatii te ina kiarie aare atua erruat nabo; neng'amuni obo-- neing'uari olekai."
Luke17:35 Nepuo aatii are naaituutisho te nebo; neng'amuni nabo-- neing'uari engai."
Luke17:36 Netii aare enkurruna; neng'amuni obo-- neing'uari olekai."
Luke17:37 Nealu ninje nejoki ninye: Kaji-- Laitoriani? Nejoki si ninye ninje: Enetii empopong'-- neiturrurro ina alo baiki ilmotonyi."
Luke18:1 Neliki ninye ninje enkitanyanyukiet-- peiye edol ninje-- aajo meata kata nemesaisho oshi-- pemenaura--"
Luke18:2 nejo: Etii atua engang' nabo olaigwenani obo leitu eurei Engai nemeshilu oltung'ani.
Luke18:3 Netii atua ena ang' engoliai nabo-- nelotu enetii ninye nejo:Njooki enkigwena sidai tʼolaitang'oroni lai!"
Luke18:4 Neitu eyeu ninye te ina kata. Nejo tekurum tiatua kion: Ore teni maurei Engai namashilu oltung'ani--"
Luke18:5 kake tiaraki naaisho ena oliai enyamali naleng'-- nalaisho ninye enkigwena sidai-- pemaalotu tʼenkiting'oto aitanaur."
Luke18:6 Nejo Olaitoriani: Entoning' enajo ele aigwenani torrono!
Luke18:7 Ke-- meisho Engai enkigwena sidai lootegeluaki lenyena ooishiraki ninye dama o kiarie neng'iriaki ninye ninje tʼeanyunoto?"
Luke18:8 Aliki ndai: Elaisho ninye ninje enkigwena sidai nabokata. Kake-- teni elotu Enkerai oltung'ani — ketum sa ninye enkirukoto tʼenkop?"
Luke18:9 Nejoki ninye ematua oo ltung'unak lootejo tiatua aten-- aajo era supati-- nemen ilkulekai tung'anak-- ena kitanyanyukiet:"
Luke18:10 Eilepa iltung'anak aare aapuo engaji sinyati-- pesaisho; nera obo Olfarisayos o olekai olaoshoni le kodi."
Luke18:11 Neitashe Olfarisayos nesaisho tiatua kion nji: Engai-- aaliki iye ashe-- tiaraki namanyanyukie nanu kulekai tung'anak: sing'ouni-- laisilok-- laarak lʼenkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni arashu anaa ele aoshoni le kodi."
Luke18:12 Apukoo nanu aigil are tiatua enjuma naishooio ematua e tomon too pookin natum.
Luke18:13 Neitashe si ninye-- olaoshoni le kodi-- tʼenelakwa neitu eyeu neapaki ngonyek enyena shumata-- kake neosh olgoo lenye nejo: Engai-- tang'aduaki nanu-- olaitarruoni!"
Luke18:14 Aliki ndai: Etadoiye ele nelo engaji enye-- eitaaki supat-- nelang' ilo liare. Amu oltung'ani pookin loitaa kion kitok-- neitadouni ninye; ore oloitadou kion-- neitaai kitok."
Luke18:15 Nerikoki ninje ninye nkera kutiti-- peiye eporoo ninje. Ore pedol laiteng'enuok ena-- nebuaki ninje."
Luke18:16 Neipot Yesus ninje tʼenetii nejo: Einjoo nkera epuonu enatii-- emimitiki ninje; amu era enkarsishu Engai noo loonyanyukie ninje."
Luke18:17 Japa-- aliki ndai: Olemeng'amu enkarsishu Engai anaa enkerai-- nemejing' ninye atua tukul."
Luke18:18 Neikilikwan olkitok obo ninye nejo: Laiteng'enani sidai-- kainyo alaitobir-- palajung'u empuan nemeiting'?"
Luke18:19 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Ainyo pikijo sidai? Metii osidai neme obo-- nera Engai."
Luke18:20 Itayolo nkitanapat: Miar enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni; miar metua-- mipurrisho; minjakenu elejare; ntaa kituak minyi o ng'utunyi!"
Luke18:21 Nejo si ninye: Aibung'a nena pookin neba tʼenkitishu ai.
Luke18:22 Ore pening' Yesus kuna-- nejoki ninye: Kitong'orikia nabo; timira pookin niata-- pioriki laisinak-- nilaata masaa te shumata; ore pindip-- wou-- tusujaki!"
Luke18:23 Ore pening' ninye kuna-- neilish naleng'-- amu era oladupani naleng'."
Luke18:24 Ore pedol Yesus-- ajo eilisho ninye naleng'-- nejo: Oi egol-- pejing' looata masaa atua enkarsishu Engai!"
Luke18:25 Elelek eim endames eudoto esindano nelang' ejing' oladupani atua enkarsishu Engai.
Luke18:26 Nejo lootoning'o kuna: Ang'ai naa loidim atopua?
Luke18:27 Nejo si ninye: Enemeidim iltung'anak-- neidim Engai."
Luke18:28 Nejo Petros: Ng'orai-- kitung'aitie yook nkun ang' pookin nikisuj iye."
Luke18:29 Nejoki ninye ninje: Japa-- aliki ndai: Metii oltung'ani otung'aiye engaji arashu eng'oroyoni arashu lalashera arashu lootoiutuo ninye arashu nkera tʼolbae lʼenkarsishu Engai--"
Luke18:30 nemeng'amu aigil kumok t'ena kata o tiatua olmaa olotu empuan nemeiting'.
Luke18:31 Nerik ninye kulo tomon o are nejoki ninje: Eng'orai-- kilep aapuo Yerusalem-- neitabaiari pookin natisirakaki Enkerai oltung'ani too layolounok."
Luke18:32 Amu eitarasakini ninye loreren-- nekweniyeki nesuli nenotakini ngamulak--"
Luke18:33 near ninje ninye too nkeenda near metua-- nepiu ninye tʼengolong' e uni."
Luke18:34 Neitu eyolou ninje toki too kuna-- neaku etushumaki kulo rorei too ninje-- neitu eyolou enairoroki."
Luke18:35 Neaku ore penyikaki Yeriko-- netotona olmodooni obo tʼembata engoitoi-- eomonisho."
Luke18:36 Ore pening' ninye olorere oimita-- neikilikwanu: Kainyo ena?"
Luke18:37 Neitayolo ninje ninye: Yesus le Nasaret oimita.
Luke18:38 Neapaa ninye oltoilo nejo: Yesus-- nakerai e David-- tokorduaki!"
Luke18:39 Ore kulo looituruk nebuaki ninye-- pegira. Kake nepon ninye adar naleng': Nakerai e David-- tokorduaki!"
Luke18:40 Neitashe Yesus neitanapu-- perikuni ninye enetii ninye. Ore penyikaki ninye-- neikilikwan:"
Luke18:41 Ainyo iyeu naasaki iye? Nejo si ninye: Laitoriani-- padolishoi."
Luke18:42 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Tadolishoi! enkirukoto ino nikintopua.
Luke18:43 Nedolishoi ninye nabokata nesuj ninye-- eitadaraa Engai. Ore olorere pookin lotadua ina neisho Engai enkitadararoto."
Luke19:1 Nejing' ninye neim Yeriko.
Luke19:2 Naa ng'orai-- netii olee obo-- oji engarna enye Sakayos-- nera ninye olkitok loo laoshok le kodi naa oladupani."
Luke19:3 Neyeu ninye nedol Yesus-- ajo ng'ai neitu eidim tʼolbae lʼolorere-- amu dorrop entemata enye."
Luke19:4 Neituruk ninye akwet neilepaki olng'aboli-- petum atadua ninye; amu etayeuo ninye neim ena oitoi."
Luke19:5 Ore pebau Yesus ine wueji-- neimariri shumata nedol nejoki ninye: Sakayos-- tadou asioki-- amu meata kata namabik taata tiatua engaji ino."
Luke19:6 Nedou ninye asioki neng'amu ninye eng'ida.
Luke19:7 Ore pedol ltung'anak pookin ena-- neing'unyung'uny nejo: Etijing'a enetii olee aitarruoni-- pedaare."
Luke19:8 Neitashe Sakayos nejoki Olaitoriani: Ng'orai-- Laitoriani-- aisho laisinak ematua oo masaa ainei; ore pateleja oltung'ani-- narrinyoki ninye kat ong'wan."
Luke19:9 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Eewuo taata enkitopuata ena aji-- tiaraki nara si ninye enkerai e Abraham."
Luke19:10 Amu eewuo Enkerai oltung'ani peing'oru neitopok enaimina.
Luke19:11 Ore pening' ninje kuna-- nepon ajo ninye enkitanyanyukiet-- tiaraki natataanikia ninye Yerusalem nejo ninje-- aajo elalioi enkarsishu Engai nabokata;"
Luke19:12 akae-- nejo: Eshomo oltung'ani obo kitok olosho olakwa-- petumoki kion enkarsishu nerrinyo."
Luke19:13 Neipot ninye laisyayak lenyena oora tomon neisho ninje ngoshola mboreitin (mane) tomon nejoki ninje: Entobirishore-- metabana nalotu."
Luke19:14 Nemen iltung'anak lenyena ninye neirriwaa olkilikwai-- pesuj ninye nejo: Mikiyeu ele-- peitore yook."
Luke19:15 Neaku ore perrinyo ninye-- einoto enkarsishu-- neitanap-- peipotokini ninye kulo aisyayak looishoo ngoshola-- peyolou endupoto nainoto oltung'ani pookin."
Luke19:16 Nelotu ol elukunya nejo: Einoto emborei ino nabo mboreitin tomon.
Luke19:17 Nejoki ninye: Ee-- laisyayani sidai-- amu itaa supat tʼentoki kinyi-- ilaata engolon-- pintore ngang'itie tomon."
Luke19:18 Nelotu oliare nejo: Laitoriani-- einoto emborei ino nabo mboreitin imiet endupoto."
Luke19:19 Nejoki baiki ilo: niaku si iye Olaitoriani loo ngang'itie imiet.
Luke19:20 Nelotu olekai nejo: Laitoriani-- ng'orai-- nyena emborei ino naata natushuma t'olkila--"
Luke19:21 amu aaturia iye-- amu ira oltung'ani ogol-- idumu neitu ishum-- nisambu neitu iun."
Luke19:22 Nejoki ninye: Aaigwenaki tʼenkutuk ino-- laisyayani torrono. Itayolo iye-- ajo ara nanu oltung'ani ogol-- nadumu neitu ashum-- naisambu neitu aun."
Luke19:23 Ainyo naa peitu ipik iye ngoshola ainei atua engaji oo ngoshola-- petum endupoto? Ore palotu-- natum ninje o endupoto enye."
Luke19:24 Nejoki ninye kulo looitasheiki ninye: Entoorutu ninye ena borei nabo-- enjoo ele loata mboreitin tomon."
Luke19:25 Nejoki ninje ninye: Laitoriani-- eata ninye mboreitin tomon."
Luke19:26 Kake aliki nanu ndai: Eishori oltung'ani pookin loata-- neoruni ele lemeata baiki enaata."
Luke19:27 Kake entorikutu kulo mang'ati lainei ena alo leitu eyeu-- paitore ninje-- entaar ninje tʼengomom ai metuata."
Luke19:28 Ore peidip atejo ninye kuna-- neituruk alo ailep Yerusalem."
Luke19:29 Neaku ore penyikaki ninye Betfage o Betania metabaiki oldonyo oji Loo loirenito-- neirriwaa ninye aare too laiteng'enuok lenyena"
Luke19:30 nejo: Enjom enkiti ang' naitoriokinore ndai; ore pijing'ijing'i atua ninye-- nipuopuo aainepu enkurrarru osikiria naena-- neton eitu eilepaki oltung'ani o obo ninye tukul; entalakutu ninye-- entereakaki!"
Luke19:31 Ore peikilikwan oltung'ani ndai: Ainyo pilakuku ninye? entejo nji: Olaitoriani oyeu ninye.
Luke19:32 Nepuo looirriwaiyoki neinepu anaa petiaka ninje.
Luke19:33 Ore elakita ninje enkurrarru osikiria-- nejoki laitoriak lenyena ninje: Ainyo pilakuku ena kurrarru?"
Luke19:34 Nejo si ninje: Olaitoriani oyeu ninye.
Luke19:35 Nereu ninje ninye enetii Yesus neisalaashaki ilkilani lenye shumata enkurrarru osikiria-- neilepakinye Yesus."
Luke19:36 Ore eloito ninye-- neisalaash ninje ilkilani lenye tʼengoitoi."
Luke19:37 Ore penyikaki ninye-- epon etii enkururumoto Oldonyo loo loirienito-- neiter aang'ida esiamu pookin o laiteng'enuok lenyena neitoning'oo Engai tʼoltoilo kitok tʼolbae loo nkyasin kituak pookin naatadua--"
Luke19:38 ejo: Njeitadarari ololotu-- olkarsis-- tʼengarna Olaitoriani! Eseriani te shumata o enkitook te shumata naleng'!"
Luke19:39 Nejoki ematua oo Lfarisayoi tiatua olorere ninye: Laiteng'enani-- tabuaki laiteng'enuok linono!"
Luke19:40 Nealu ninye nejo: Aliki ndai: Teni epuo aagira kulo-- nepuo aadar isoito."
Luke19:41 Ore penyikaki nedol engang'-- neishiraki ninye"
Luke19:42 ejo: Ten emutu iyolo si iye tiatua ena olong' nara nʼe seriani ino! Kake etushumaki taata too ngonyek inono
Luke19:43 Amu kipuo aabaiki ngolong'i nikipuo aaikarru ilmang'ati linono nikiman nikigomu too mbat pookin
Luke19:44 nikirratanyaki enkop te nebo o nkera inono tiatua iye-- nemeing'ua tiatua iye osoit te shumata osoit-- tiaraki neitu iyolou iye enkata eleenoto ino."
Luke19:45 Ore pejing' ninye engaji sinyati-- neiter amir loomirisho o looinyang'isho tiatua"
Luke19:46 nejoki ninje: Etisiraki Era engaji ai engaji esayata-- nintaata ndai engapunet oo sing'ouni."
Luke19:47 Neaku eiteng'enisho ninye ngolong'i pookin tiatua engaji sinyati. Neing'oru laidasak kituak o layolok lʼesirata o laiturukok lʼolorere-- peiminye ninye--"
Luke19:48 neitu etum enaasaki-- amu eibung'are olorere pookin ninye einining'ito."
Luke20:1 Neaku nabo olong'-- eiteng'enita ninye olorere tiatua engaji sinyati-- einosu lomon lʼeng'ida-- neitashe laidasak kituak o layolok lʼesirata te nebo o laigwenak"
Luke20:2 neirorie ninye ejo: Tiaki yook-- ke ti aa golon intobirita kuna? arashu: Kang'ai likinjo ena golon?"
Luke20:3 Nealu ninye nejoki ninje: Aikilikwan si nanu ndai ororei obo-- pikilikiki."
Luke20:4 Keing'ua enkibatisa e Yohanes shumata arashu atua iltung'anak?
Luke20:5 Neibirribir ninje tiatua aten nejo: Teni kijo: Eing'ua shumata-- nejo si ninye: Ainyo naa peitu irukuruku ninye?"
Luke20:6 Teni kijo: Eing'ua atua iltung'anak-- nenang' olorere pookin yook too soito-- amu etayoloutuo-- aajo era Yohanes olayolounoni."
Luke20:7 Nealu ninje-- aajo meyolo eneing'ua."
Luke20:8 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Maliki si nanu ndai-- ke ti aa golon aitobirita kuna."
Luke20:9 Neiter aliki ninye olorere ena kitanyanyukiet: Etuuno oltung'ani obo enkuruma oo nkeek olmarua neitamany laturok nelo olototo lʼenkata naado.
Luke20:10 Neirriwaki ninye tʼenkata enye laturok olaisyayani obo-- peisho ninje ninye ematua oo lmomo loo nkeek olmarua. Near laturok ninye neitupuku-- meata toki."
Luke20:11 Nepon airriwaa olekai aisyayani; near ninje baiki ilo nesul neitupuku-- meata toki"
Luke20:12 Nepon airriwaa oli okuni; nepik ninje baiki ilo ilbaak nemir.
Luke20:13 Nejo Olaitoriani lʼenkuruma oo nkeek olmarua: Kaji aiko? Alairriwaki Oinoti lai lanyor; ajo nanu-- epuo aayanyit ninye."
Luke20:14 Ore pedol laturok ninye-- neibirribir oopeny nejo: Nyelido lora olajung'oni; mataar ninye metua-- petum ataa enjung'o enang'!"
Luke20:15 Nenang'aki ninje ninye oriong' enkuruma oo nkeek olmarua near ninye metua. Akae-- kainyo easaki ilo aitoriani lʼenkuruma oo nkeek olmarua ninje?"
Luke20:16 Elotu ninye neiminye lelo aturok neisho enkuruma enye oo nkeek olmarua kulekai. Ore pening ninje kuna-- nejo: Njepaash yook ina!"
Luke20:17 Neing'orong'oraa ninye ninje nejo: Kainyo ena naa natisiraki: Osoit otanyaita lashetak-- etaa ele osoit kitok lʼolpijata?"
Luke20:18 Ore oltung'ani pookin lourokino ilo soit-- negiligila; ore lourokino ninye-- neituut ilo."
Luke20:19 Neing'oru layolok lʼesirata o laidasak kituak-- peaki ninye ngaik te ina kata-- neurei ake olorere; amu etayoloutuo-- aajo eirorie ninje te ina kitanyanyukiet."
Luke20:20 Neing'oraa ninje ninye neirriwaa lairengesok-- peitaa aten supati-- peibung' ninye tʼororei lenye-- peitarasaki ninye enkitoria o engolon Olaitoriani lʼolosho."
Luke20:21 Neikilikwan ninje ninye nejo: Laiteng'enani-- kitayoloutuo-- aajo ilimu ninteng'enu enaitoriori niming'oraa entemet oltung'ani-- kake inteng'enu engoitoi Engai tʼesipata."
Luke20:22 Ke sidai-- teni kinjo kaisar kodi arashu me?"
Luke20:23 Neyolou ninye esungureishu enye nejoki ninje: Ainyo pikitemiteme?
Luke20:24 Entaduaki endenarion nabo! Ken e ng'ai ena mua o esirata? Nejo ninje: Ne kaisar.
Luke20:25 Nejoki ninje: Akae-- enjoo kaisar en e kaisar o Engai en Engai!"
Luke20:26 Neitu eidim ninje aaibung'a ninye tʼororei lenye tʼengomom olorere neiputukunyoki ealata enye negira.
Luke20:27 Nepuonu enetii ninye Sadukayoi ooje loojo-- aajo metii empiunoto oo lootuata-- neikilikwan ninye"
Luke20:28 nejo: Laiteng'enani-- etisiraka yook Mose-- ajo teni ee olalashe lʼoltung'ani loata eng'oroyoni nemeata ninye enkerai-- peamaa olalashe lenye ina ng'oroyoni peinyeyeki olalashe lenye olmuate."
Luke20:29 Akae-- etii lalashera oopishana. Ore ol elukunya eamaiye eng'oroyoni nee-- meata enkerai;"
Luke20:30 neamaa oliare ina ng'oroyoni-- nee si ninye-- meata enkerai;"
Luke20:31 neamaa oli okuni ninye; neijia eikuna pokira oopishana-- neitu eing'ua nkera-- nee."
Luke20:32 Ore tʼenkiting'oto nee si ninye-- ina ng'oroyoni."
Luke20:33 Akae-- ore tiatua empiunoto-- keaku eng'oroyoni e alo obo too ninje? Amu etaa eng'oroyoni oo kulo pokira oopishana."
Luke20:34 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninje: Eamisho neamari nkera ele maa--"
Luke20:35 kake looaku-- pebaia ilo maa o empiunoto oo lootuata-- meamisho ninje nemeamari."
Luke20:36 Amu meidim aainyaaki aatuata-- amu enyanyukie ilmalaikan-- nera nkera Engai-- tiaraki nara nkera empiunoto."
Luke20:37 Amu eitadamua baiki Mose tʼolodung'okino-- ajo epuo aapiu lootuata-- teni eimaki ninye Olaitoriani Engai e Abraham o Engai e Isaak o Engai e Yakoob."
Luke20:38 Mera Engai Engai oo lootuata-- kake noo looishiu; amu eishiuoki pookin ninye."
Luke20:39 Nealu layolok lʼesirata ooje nejo: Laiteng'enani-- itejo sidai."
Luke20:40 Neitu eitoki aaiteu ninje aaikilikwana ninye toki.
Luke20:41 Nejoki ninye ninje: Kaji eiko teni eimaki ninje Kristos-- aajo era enkerai e David?"
Luke20:42 Amu ejo David openy tiatua enkitabu oo singolioitin: Etiaka Olaitoriani Olaitoriani lai: Totona te tatene ai--"
Luke20:43 metabana napik ilmang'ati linono abori oo nkejek inono.
Luke20:44 Akae-- eipot David ninye Olaitoriani; kaji eiko naa teni era enkerai enye?"
Luke20:45 Ore pening' olorere pookin ninye-- nejoki ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena:"
Luke20:46 Entaduai aten too layolok lʼesirata ooyeu nelimana too lkilani adoru nenyor nkirorokinot too singiraitin o ntoneta elukunya tiatua ngajijik Engai o nkirragat elukunya tʼenedaareki--"
