Luke20:47 loonya ngajijik oo ngolia neitador sayat tʼenkitusupatuo. Nepuo aang'amu ninje enkigwena nalang'.
Luke21:1 Neitalang'aki ninye ngonyek nedol ladupak looitadoikitio nkishoorot enye atua eneitadoikini mpesai.
Luke21:2 Nedol ninye engoliai nabo aisinani-- naitadoikio naabebek are atua."
Luke21:3 Nejo ninye: Aliki ndai tʼesipata: Eitadoikio ena oliai aisinani nkumok nelang' kulekai pookin;
Luke21:4 amu eitadoikitio kulo pookin lekunot enkumoi oo masaa enye-- kake ore ena eitadoikio tʼesinaishu enye pookin nara erripet enye."
Luke21:5 Ore etejo looje tʼolbae lʼengaji sinyati-- aajo etakajaki ninye too soito sidan o too nkishorunot-- nejo ninye:"
Luke21:6 Epuonu ngolong'i nemeing'uari osoit te shumata osoit lemerratanyuni too kuna pookin nidolitata.
Luke21:7 Neikilikwan ninje ninye nejo: Laiteng'enani-- kanu naa eaku kuna? Kainyo olponoto-- teni epuo aabau kuna?"
Luke21:8 Nejo ninye: Eng'orai-- pemeitamanari ndai; amu epuo aapuonu ilkumok tʼengarna ai-- ejo: Ara nanu! o: Etinyikua enkata! Emisuj ninje!"
Luke21:9 Ore pipuopuo aaning' mbaak oo njorin o nkiposhiposhat-- eming'ayung'ayu! Meata kata nemeng'as aaku kuna-- kake melotu enkiting'oto nabokata."
Luke21:10 Tekurum nejoki ninye ninje: Eladumunye olorere aarare olekai orere-- o enkarsishu nabo aarare engai arsishu."
Luke21:11 Nepuo aaku nkikirikirat kituak enkop o nkeaitin o lameitin too wuejitin o wuejitin-- neaku baiki nkuretishuitin o ilponot kituak ooing'ua shumata."
Luke21:12 Ore eton eitu eaku kuna pookin-- neaki ninje ndai ngaik neisil ndai neitarasaki ndai atua ngajijik Engai o ngajijik eenata-- nerik ndai ngomomi oo lkarsisi o laiturukok tʼolbae lʼengarna ai."
Luke21:13 Neaku kuna enjakenishu too ndai.
Luke21:14 Akae-- entagoluoto too ltauja linyi-- pemiekenyanya-- kaji inkoko teni imitutu aten."
Luke21:15 Amu ayeu naisho nanu ndai enkutuk o eng'eno nemeidim aaisimu arashu aatigilunore laitang'orok linyi pookin.
Luke21:16 Kake epuo aaitarasaa ndai lootoiutuo ndai o lalashera o lʼenkishomi o iljorueta-- nepuo aar looje too ndai metuata."
Luke21:17 Niakuku looibaini too pookin tʼolbae lʼengarna ai.
Luke21:18 Nemeitoki aimin olpapitai lʼelukunya inyi tukul.
Luke21:19 Enting'iria too ltauja linyi!
Luke21:20 Akae-- teni idolidolo Yerusalem-- etamana iltimito-- entayolo te ina kata-- aajo etinyikua erruoroto enye."
Luke21:21 Ore olotii te ina kata atua Yudaya-- njekwetiki ildonyo; ore olotii atua aji-- njepuku aulo; ore olotii atua nkuruman-- njomejing' aji."
Luke21:22 Amu era ninje ngolong'i naalakieki esile-- peiye ebaia pookin naatisiraki."
Luke21:23 Oi-- osina linyi-- ndai naamena o naaitanakisho too nona olong'i! Amu eaku osina kitok tʼenkop o engoro tʼolorere."
Luke21:24 Nepuo aaurori ninje tʼempijan olalem-- neriki ninje-- peaku ilkyarunot tiatua loreren pookin; nepuoi aaroro Yerusalem too loreren-- metabana nebaia enkata oo loreren."
Luke21:25 Nepuo aaku ilponot tʼengolong' o olapa o lakir-- nejing' enkop olkirutoto loo loreren o enking'asiai-- neikurrukur olbalbal o enkiposhai enye--"
Luke21:26 nepuo aailiilaa iltung'anak tʼenkuretishu o tʼeanyunoto oo ntokitin naapuo aapuonu olmaa; amu epuo aaing'unung'un ngoloni e shumata.
Luke21:27 Nepuo aadol ninje te ina kata Enkerai oltung'ani-- elotu tʼerukenya tʼengolon o tʼenkitook kitok."
Luke21:28 Ore peiter aaku kuna-- emariria shumata-- entaaputu lukuny inyi-- tiaraki nanyiku elakunoto inyi."
Luke21:29 Neliki ninye ninje enkitanyanyukiet nabo: Eng'orai olng'aboli o iljanito pookin:
Luke21:30 teni edany ninje-- nidolidolo too ninje niyolouu-- aajo etaana enkata enkirowuaj."
Luke21:31 Neijia si ndai: teni idolidolo kuna naaku-- entayolou-- aajo etaa etaanu enkarsishu Engai."
Luke21:32 Japa-- aliki ndai: Memuta ena kishon tukul-- metabana neaku kuna pookin."
Luke21:33 Nepuo aamuta shumata o enkop-- kake mepuo aamuta rorei lainei tukul."
Luke21:34 Kake entaduai aten-- pemeiroshiu iltauja linyi tʼenkinosata o tʼemerai o too nkishilarot endaa-- pemeinepu ndai ina olong' nabokata--"
Luke21:35 amu elainepu pookin loomanya enkop anaa erreshet.
Luke21:36 Akae-- enjololoto tʼenkata pookin-- isaishosho-- pindimidimi aailanyai kuna pookin naapuo aaku-- pintasheshe t'engomom Enkerai oltung'ani."
Luke21:37 Neaku eiteng'enisho ninye too ndamaitin tiatua engaji sinyati-- nepuku too nkiarien nebik tʼoldonyo oipoti Loo loirienito."
Luke21:38 Nepuonu olorere pookin-- pepej ewuas-- enetii ninye atua engaji sinyati-- peiye einining' ninye."
Luke22:1 Netinyikutua ngolong'i kituak oo lmkaten lemeisiiio-- naaji pasaka."
Luke22:2 Neing'oru laidasak kituak o layolok lʼesirata eneiko-- peiminye ninye; kake eturia olorere."
Luke22:3 Kake eidipa atijing'a satan atua Yudas lora Iskariotes-- nera lʼesiana oo kulo tomon o are."
Luke22:4 Nelo ader oo laidasak kituak o ilkigeluni eneiko-- peitarasaki ninje ninye."
Luke22:5 Neng'ida ninje nedung'okino enkishooroto oo ngoshola.
Luke22:6 Neiruk ninye neing'oru enkata sidai naitarasarie ninye-- metii olorere."
Luke22:7 Eewuo engolong' oo lmkaten lemeisiijo naidasishoreki pasaka.
Luke22:8 Neirriwaa ninye Petros o Yohanes nejo: Embung'a engoitoi-- entobirakiti yook pasaka-- pikinya."
Luke22:9 Nejoki ninje ninye: Kaji iyeu nikipuo aaitobirie?
Luke22:10 Nejoki si ninye:Eng'orai-- ore pijing'ijing'i ndai atua engang'-- nelatumore ndai oltung'ani obo onapita emoti engare; entusuj ninye metabaiki engaji najing' ninye;"
Luke22:11 entiakiti olopeny engaji: Kitiaka Olaiteng'enani: Kodee engaji oo lomon-- panya te ina alo pasaka te nebo o laiteng'enuok lainei?"
Luke22:12 Nelaitadol ilo ndai olgilata kitok oitobirakaki ntoneta; entobira te ina alo.
Luke22:13 Nepuo neinepu anaa petiaka ninye ninje-- neitobir pasaka."
Luke22:14 Ore pebau enkata-- netoni o lairriwak tomon o are te nebo o ninye."
Luke22:15 Nejoki ninye ninje: Tʼeng'warrata atang'warra ainosa ena pasaka te nebo o ndai-- epon eitu aaisili."
Luke22:16 Amu aliki ndai: Maitoki anya ninye tukul metabana neitabaiari tiatua enkarsishu Engai.
Luke22:17 Neibung' ninye enkwaru neliki ashe nejo: Embung'a ena-- entoorikinoto tiatua ndai oopeny!"
Luke22:18 Amu aliki ndai: Maok tukul-- eiter taata tʼeishoi enjata olmarua-- metabana nelotu enkarsishu Engai."
Luke22:19 Neibung' olmkate nejo ashe nebelibel ninye neisho ninje nejo: Era ele osesen lai loishorunyeki ndai. Enkuna ena-- pikidamumu nanu."
Luke22:20 Naa neijia eibung'a ninye enkwaru-- eidipa endaa-- nejo: Era ena kwaru osotua ng'ejuk tiatua osarge lai oibukorieki ndai."
Luke22:21 Kake eng'orai-- etii engaina olaaitarasaa nanu-- e nebo o nanu tʼenaraa."
Luke22:22 Amu eloito Enkerai oltung'ani anaa petayeuoki-- kake-- ee-- kake aiya ilo tung'ani oitarasaa ninye!"
Luke22:23 Neiter ninje aaikilikwanaro tiatua aten-- ang'ai ele too ninje olaitobir ena."
Luke22:24 Neiter baiki enkitarrikino tiatua ninje-- kang'ai too ninje eikenari aa kitok."
Luke22:25 Nejoki ninye ninje: Eitorisho ilkarsisi loo loreren o looata engolon lenye eipoti laitobirak aripi.
Luke22:26 Kake me neijia ndai! Amu olkitoklinyi njeaku anaa olkinyi o olaiturukoni anaa olaisyayani.
Luke22:27 Amu kalo kitok-- oloton tʼendaata arashu oloisyaisho? Me oloton tʼendaata? Ara nanu tiatua ndai anaa oloisyaisho."
Luke22:28 Irara ndai lootobiko te nebo o nanu tiatua nkitasurot ainei.
Luke22:29 Naisho nanu ndai enkarsishu anaa paaishoo Papa lai nanu--"
Luke22:30 pipuopuo aanya niokioko tʼenaraa tiatua enkarsishu ai-- nipuopuo aatoni te shumata oo lorikaishi lʼenkitoria ningwenakiki ntipati tomon o are e Israel."
Luke22:31 Nejo Olaitoriani: Simon-- Simon-- ng'orai-- etayeuo satan nekut ndai anaa engano:"
Luke22:32 kake aatasayaka nanu iye-- pemeng'oru enkirukoto ino; ore piala iye-- ntagolo lalashera linono."
Luke22:33 Nejoki ninye: Laitoriani-- aidipakine nanu-- palo te nebo o iye atua eenata o enkea."
Luke22:34 Nejo si ninye: Petros-- aajoki iye: Epon eitu eorito taata olkikusieki-- nikilo amiki aigil uni-- ajo mikiyolo."
Luke22:35 Nejoki ninye ninje: Ore enkata nairriwaiye ndai-- miatata entutua arashu olbene arashu namuka-- ketong'orikia ndai toki? Nejo si ninje: Oi me!"
Luke22:36 Nejoki ninye ninje: Akae-- ore oloata taata entutua-- njeibung' ninye; neijia baiki olbene; ore lemeata toki njemir olkila lenye-- peinyang'u olalem."
Luke22:37 Amu aliki nanu ndai: Meata kata nemaitabaia nanu ena natisiraki: Eikenaiyoki te nebo o laitarruok. Amu enatisiraki te nanu-- neata enkitabaiaroto."
Luke22:38 Nejo si ninje: Laitoriani-- ng'orai-- etii ene lalema aare. Nejoki ninye ninje: Akae-- ebaiki."
Luke22:39 Nepuku nelo Oldonyo loo loirienito anaa petiu orregie lenye; nesuj laiteng'enuok ninye.
Luke22:40 Ore pebaia ine wueji-- nejoki ninje: Entasaishoto-- pemijing'ijing'i atua enkitasuroto."
Luke22:41 Neigut neing'ua ninje nelo enebaiki osoit negil kung' nesaisho
Luke22:42 nejo: Papa-- teni iyeu-- ntapaashaki ena kwaru; kake njoo meaku eyeunoto ai-- njeaku enino!"
Luke22:43 Nepukoki olmalaika ninye te shumata neitagol ninye.
Luke22:44 Ore eapare kion-- nepon asaisho tʼenyuata kitok. Neaku enkinyinyiret enye anaa ilkitong'at lʼosarge oodoiki enkop."
Luke22:45 Ore peinyototo ninye tʼesayata enye-- nelotu enetii laiteng'enuok lenyena neinepu ninje eirura tʼolbae lʼenkilishoto--"
Luke22:46 nejoki ninje: Ainyo pirurara? Enyoito-- entasaishoto-- pemijing'ijing'i atua enkitasuroto!"
Luke22:47 Ore epon eirorita ninye-- ng'orai-- eetuo olorere o oloipoti Yudas-- obo too kulo tomon o are-- oiturukie ninje-- nenyikaki ninye Yesus-- peiye eng'utut ninye."
Luke22:48 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Yudas-- intarasaa Enkerai oltung'ani tʼeng'ututata?"
Luke22:49 Ore pedol kulo looturubare ninye enaaku-- nejo: Laitoriani-- ke kiar ninje too lalema?"
Luke22:50 Near obo too ninje olaisyayani lʼolaidasani kitok nedung' enkiyok enye e tatene.
Luke22:51 Nealu Yesus nejo: Emimitiki ninje! neing'unye enkiyok enye neishiunye ninye.
Luke22:52 Nejoki Yesus laidasak kituak o ilkigeluni lʼengaji sinyati o laigwenak looetunye ninye: Ietuo ndai too lalema o too lkuman anaa loopuo aaibung' esing'ou.
Luke22:53 Aidipa atii e nebo o ndai ngolong'i pookin atua engaji sinyati-- neitu kielielie ngaik; kake enkata inyi ena o engolon enaimin."
Luke22:54 Neibung' ninje ninye aarik-- nerik engaji olaidasani kitok. Nesuj si ninye Petros tʼenelakwa--"
Luke22:55 Ore peinok ninje enkima tʼempolos e boo-- netoni te nebo; neton Petros tʼempolos enye."
Luke22:56 Nedol engaisyayani ninye-- eton tʼenedalita enkima-- nejur ninye nejo: Etaboitare si ele ninye."
Luke22:57 Nemiki ninye nejo: Nang'oroyoni-- mayolo nanu ninye."
Luke22:58 Ore tʼenkata kinyi nedol olekai ninye nejo: Ira si iye oliatua ninje. Nejo Petros: Letung'ani-- mara."
Luke22:59 Ore peishunye anaa esaa nabo-- nekurraki olekai ninye nejo: Esipa-- eturubare si ele ninye-- amu era ole Galilaya."
Luke22:60 Nejo Petros: Mayolo enijoito. Ore nabokata-- epon eirorita ninye-- neorito olkikusieki."
Luke22:61 Neibelekenya Olaitoriani neing'oraa Petros-- nedamu Petros rorei lʼOlaitoriani anaa petiaka ninye-- ajo epon eitu eorito taata olkikusieki-- nikilo amiki aigil uni."
Luke22:62 Nelo ninye aulo-- eishirita naleng'."
Luke22:63 Ore kulo leak looibung'a ninye-- nekweniye near ninye"
Luke22:64 neop ngonyek enyena near engomom enye neikilikwan ninye nejo: Tumusu olikitaara?
Luke22:65 Nemor ninje ninye too nkulie morot.
Luke22:66 Ore peaku dama-- neiturrurro enkigwena olorere-- laidasak kituak o layolok lʼesirata-- nerik ninje ninye atua enkigwena enye"
Luke22:67 nejo: Teni ira iye Kristos-- tiaki yook! Nejoki ninye ninje: Teni aliki ndai-- nimirukuruku tukul;"
Luke22:68 teni aikilikwan-- nimialulu tukul nimiking'uaikiki."
Luke22:69 Kake-- eiter taata-- elaton Enkerai oltung'ani te tatene engolon Engai."
Luke22:70 Nejo pookin: Akae-- ira iye naa Enkerai Engai? Nejoki ninye ninje: Ijojo ndai-- aajo ara nanu."
Luke22:71 Nejo ninje: Kainyo kintoki aayeunye enjakenishu? Amu kitoning'o oopeny tʼenkutuk enye.
Luke23:1 Neinyototo esiamu enye pookin nerik ninye enetii Pilatos.
Luke23:2 Neiter ninje aaitang'or ninye nejo: Kinoto ele eitoosh olorere lang' nemitiki aisho kaisar kodi nejo-- ajo era ninye Kristos-- olkarsis."
Luke23:3 Neikilikwan Pilatos ninye nejo: Ira iye olkarsis loo Yudayoi? Nealiki ninye nejo: Itejo iye.
Luke23:4 Nejoki Pilatos laidasak kituak o siamin: Matum entoki naitang'orieki ele tung'ani.
Luke23:5 Nekurraki ninje aajo: Eisisa ninye olorere-- eiteng'enisho tiatua Yudaya pookin-- eiter te Galilaya metabaiki ene."
Luke23:6 Ore pening' Pilatos ena-- neikilikwanu-- ten ake era ele tung'ani Olgalilayos."
Luke23:7 Ore pening' ajo era ninye lʼenkitoria e Herodes-- neirriwaki enetii Herodes lotii too nona olong'i Yerusalem."
Luke23:8 Ore pedol Herodes Yesus-- neng'ida naleng'-- amu eado eyeu nedol ninye-- tiaraki natoning'oiye mbaak enyena-- neanyu-- pedol olponoto oitobir ninye."
Luke23:9 Neikili-kwan ninye too rorei kumok; neitu ealiki ninye oo nyoo.
Luke23:10 Kake neitashe laidasak kituak o layolok lʼesirata nepon aaitang'or ninye naleng'.
Luke23:11 Nemen Herodes ninye o esiamu enye nekweniye ninye neishopoki ninye olkila oibor neitoki arrinyoki ninye enetii Pilatos.
Luke23:12 Neaku Herodes o Pilatos te ina olong' iljorueta-- amu era tʼenkata elukunya ilmang'ati."
Luke23:13 Neipot Pilatos te nebo laidasak kituak o ilkituak lʼolorere
Luke23:14 nejoki ninje: Kitorikokitio ele tung'ani anaa oloitoosh olorere-- naa eng'orai-- aigwenaka nanu ninye tʼengomom inyi-- neitu atum tʼele tung'ani entoki too kuna nintang'orierie;"
Luke23:15 eitu etum baiki Herodes; amu airriwaka ndai enetii ninye-- kake neitoki arrinyoki yook ninye; naa eng'orai-- metii entoki naitobira naarieki ninye metua."
Luke23:16 Akae-- aar ninye nalaku."
Luke23:17 Amu meata kata nemelaakini obo tʼorregie loo ngolong'i kituak.
Luke23:18 Neosh iltung'anak pookin olodoo te nebo nejo: Minye ninye! Talaaki yook Barabas!
Luke23:19 Nera ninye oltung'ani otanang'akaki atua engaji eenata tʼolbae lʼolarrabal otaa tiatua engang' o tʼolbae lʼearata metua.
Luke23:20 Neitoki aipot Pilatos ninje-- eyeu nelaku Yesus."
Luke23:21 Nedar ninje tʼoltoilo-- ejo: Tooshoki ninye esalaba! tooshoki ninye esalaba!"
Luke23:22 Nejoki ninye ninje en e uni: Amu nyoo-- kaa torroni eitobira ele? Eitu atum te ninye entoki naarieki metua: akae-- teni aidip ataara ninye-- nalaku."
Luke23:23 Nekurraki ninje too ltoiloi kituak neyeu neoshokini ninye esalaba. Netum iltoiloi lenye o loo laidasak kituak engolon.
Luke23:24 Neigwenu Pilatos-- peaku eyeunoto enye;"
Luke23:25 nelaku ele otanang'akaki atua engaji eenata tʼolbae lʼolarrabal o tʼolbae lʼearata metua-- ele lotayeutuo ninje: neitarasaki Yesus eyeunoto enye."
Luke23:26 Ore erikito ninye-- neibung' ninje Simon-- lora le Kirene-- oing'ua atua enkuruma-- nedumaki ninye esalaba-- penap aitusuj Yesus."
Luke23:27 Nesuj esiamu kitok olorere o noo ng'oroyok ninye naailishoki neishiraki ninye.
Luke23:28 Neibelekenyakino Yesus ninje nejo: Ndai natoiye e Yerusalem-- emikinjiraki nanu-- kake enjirakiti aten o nkera inyi!"
Luke23:29 Amu eng'orai-- epuonu ngolong'i naapuo aajoie: Teshi naaitashoito o ngoshuak neitu eisho o ilkinai leitu eitanakisho!"
Luke23:30 Nepuo aaiter ninje te ina kata aajoki ildonyo: Entuurokinoto yook! o ndonyo: Eopoi yook!
Luke23:31 Ore peitobirakini kuna oljani oshal-- keaku nyoo tiatua olotoiyo?"
Luke23:32 Nerik ninje baiki kulekai aitarruok aare-- peari metuata te nebo o ninye."
Luke23:33 Ore pepuonu ninje ewueji neipoti Emborbor-- neoshoki ninye te ine esalaba o kulo aitarruok te nebo o ninye-- obo te tatene o olekai te kedyanye."
Luke23:34 Nejo Yesus: Papa-- tung'aiki ninje-- amu meyolo enaitobirita! Neorikino ninje ilkilani lenyena neosh ol enkukuo."
Luke23:35 Neitashe olorere eing'orita. Nekweniye baiki ilkituak te nebo o ninje-- ejo: Eitopua ilkulekai; njeitopok kion-- teni era ele Kristos-- olotegeluaki lʼEngai."
Luke23:36 Nemor si ninje sikerin ninye-- nepuonu enetii ninye neaki ninye engare naitiming'anisho--"
Luke23:37 nejo: Teni ira iye olkarsis loo Yudayoi-- ntopua kion!"
Luke23:38 Netii baiki esirata shumata enye tʼenkutuk oo Lgrikini o noo Romayoi o noo Lhebrayoi: Era ele olkarsis loo Yudayoi.
Luke23:39 Ore obo too laitarruok ootiikaki-- nemor ninye: mira iye Kristos? Ntopua kion o yook!"
Luke23:40 Nealu olekai nebuaki ninye nejo: Miure baiki si iye Engai nitii atua ena arata?
Luke23:41 Neitoriori enang'-- amu kitum yook enaaku anaa pikitaasa; kake eitu eitobir ele enemeaku."
Luke23:42 Nejoki ninye Yesus: Laitoriani-- tadamuaki-- teni ijing' atua enkarsishu ino!"
Luke23:43 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Japa-- aaliki iye: Ilatii taata e nebo o nanu atua emparadis!"
Luke23:44 Neaku enkata oo saan ile-- nejing' enaimin enkop metabaiki saan enturuj--"
Luke23:45 neng'oru engolong' eong'an enye nepolosa olkarash lʼerishata engaji sinyati tʼempolos.
Luke23:46 Neipotisho Yesus tʼoltoilo kitok nejo: Papa-- ayaki Olmumua lai atua ngaik inono. Ore peidip atejo ena-- nedung'o tau."
Luke23:47 Ore pedol olkigeluni enataa-- neitadaraa Engai nejo: Esipa-- era ele tung'ani supat!"
Luke23:48 Ore peiturrurrokino siamin ena king'orare-- peing'oraa enataa-- nerrinyo eoshioshito ilgoon."
Luke23:49 Neitashe pookin lootayolore ninye tʼenelakwa o ng'oroyok naatusujutua ninye-- eing'ua Galilaya-- neing'oraa kuna pookin."
Luke23:50 Naa ng'orai-- etii olee obo-- oji engarna enye Yosef-- ora olkitok lʼenkigwena-- olee sidai naa supat--"
Luke23:51 — neitu eton ele te nebo o ninje tiatua enkigwena o tiatua nkitobirat enye; nera ninye le Arimatia-- engang' oo Yudayoi-- oloanyu enkarsishu Engai."
Luke23:52 Nelo ele enetii Pilatos aomonu osesen le Yesus;
Luke23:53 neitadou neirinaki ninye oikarash oibor-- nepik ninye atua enkurare natabatuaki tʼosoit-- nepon eitu eirragie o obo ina alo aikata."
Luke23:54 Neaku engolong' enkitobirakinore neiter akenyu engolong' naeng'ieng'areki.
Luke23:55 Etusuja ng'oroyok naaje naaing'ua Galilaya te nebo o ninye neing'oraa enkurare o eneikunaki teni epiki osesen lenye.
Luke23:56 Nerrinyo ninje neitobir ilat naarropil. Ore tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki neeng'ieng'a anaa petiu too nkitanapat.
Luke24:1 Ore tʼengolong' elukunya enjuma-- pepej ewuas-- nepuonu ninje enkurare-- enapita ilat naarropil naaitobira ninje."
Luke24:2 Neinepu osoit eibelekenyakaki enelakwa tʼengapunet--"
Luke24:3 nejing' atua neitu einepu osesen lʼOlaitoriani Yesus.
Luke24:4 Ore epon eitu eyolou eneiko-- naa ng'orai-- neitasheiki leak aare ninje ooishopito ilkarashi ooilang'isho."
Luke24:5 Neaku eureisho ninje neur lukuny aing'orie enkop; nejoki ninje: Ainyo ping'oruru oloishiu tʼewueji oo lootuata?
Luke24:6 Metii ninye ene-- kake etopiwuo. Entadamutu enatiaka ndai-- epon etii atua Galilaya--"
Luke24:7 ejo: Meata kata nemeitarasakini Enkerai oltung'ani atua ngaik oo ltung'anak aitarruok neoshokini esalaba nelapiu tʼengolong' e uni.
Luke24:8 Nedamu ninje rorei lenyena.
Luke24:9 Nerrinyo-- eing'ua enkurare-- peinosaki lelo tomon o obo o ilkulekai pookin kuna baak pookin."
Luke24:10 Netii Maria Magdalena o Yohana o Maria-- ng'otonye e Yakobos-- o nkulie te nebo o ninje naatiakitia lairriwak kuna."
Luke24:11 Etaliote kulo rorei too ninje anaa mbaak emodaishu neitu eiruk ninje.
Luke24:12 Kake nedumunye Petros nekwet alo enkurare neirrugo nejur nedol rasheta eper oopeny; neing'ua-- eing'asia tiatua kion tʼolbae lʼenataa."
Luke24:13 Naa ng'orai-- nepuo aare too ninje tʼena olong' engang'-- naji engama enye Emaus-- nalakwaniki Yerusalem stadia ntomoni ile (olototo loo saan are)."
Luke24:14 Neder ninje too mbaak oo kuna pookin naataa.
Luke24:15 Neaku ore ederrita-- eikilikwanaro ninje-- nenyikaki Yesus openy ninje nelo te nebo o ninje."
Luke24:16 Kake eitoriaki ngonyek enye-- pemeyolou ninye."
Luke24:17 Nejoki ninye ninje: Kakua rorei kulo linjangarrarra tʼempolos inyi-- ipuoitoto niatata nkirribon naasoto?"
Luke24:18 Nealu obo-- oji engarna enye Kleopas-- nejoki ninye: Ke iye ake openy olomoni te Yerusalem leitu eyolou nataa tiatua ninye too kuna olong'i?"
Luke24:19 Nejoki ninye ninje: Kakua baak? Nejoki si ninje ninye: Mbaak e Yesus le Nasaret otaa olee olayolounoni lʼengolon tʼenkyas o too rorei tʼengomom Engai o nʼolorere pookin;
Luke24:20 eneikuna teni eitarasaki laidasak kituak o ilkituak lang' ninye atua earata enkea neoshoki ninye esalaba.
Luke24:21 Kitejo yook-- aajo era ninye oloyeu nelaku Israel. Ore too kuna pookin etaa taata engolong' e uni-- neba netaa kuna."
Luke24:22 Etii baiki ng'oroyok atua yook naaing'asiaye yook naashomo engapunet-- pepej ewuas--"
Luke24:23 neitu einepu osesen lenye nepuonu nejo-- aajo etadua emua oo lmalaikan ootejo-- aajo eishiu ninye."
Luke24:24 Nepuo looje too kulo lootii e nebo o yook enkurare neinepu-- etiu neijia anaa petejo ng'oroyok; kake eitu edol ninje ninye."
Luke24:25 Nejoki ninye ninje: Oi-- irara ndai ilmoda o loo ltauja ooiroshi-- pirukuruku kuna pookin naatejo layolounok."
Luke24:26 Ke meata kata neitu eisili Kristos-- pejing' atua enkitook enye?"
Luke24:27 Neiter te Mose o too layolounok pookin neitayolo ninje too sirat pookin mbaak enyena.
Luke24:28 Nenyikaki ninje ena ang' napuoito; neitaa ninye kion anaa ololo lukunya.
Luke24:29 Nesai ninje ninye naleng' nejo: Tobiko te nebo o yook-- amu etaa naaku teipa netinyikaiye endama. Nejing' ninye-- pebik te nebo o ninje."
Luke24:30 Neaku ore eton ninye te nebo o ninje edaa-- neibung' ninye olmkate nejo ashe nebelibel ninye neoriki ninje."
Luke24:31 Neboli naa ngonyek enye neyolou ninye. Neimisori ninye neitu elioi too ninje.
Luke24:32 Nejokino ninje: Eitu eiwuwu iltauja lang' tiatua yook-- eirorie ninye yook tʼengoitoi neboloki yook sirat"
Luke24:33 Nedumunye ninje te ina kata nerrinyokino Yerusalem neinepu-- eiturrurro lelo tomon o obo o lelo ootaboitare ninje--"
Luke24:34 ootejo: Esipa-- etopiwuo Olaitoriani neipung'oki Simon."
Luke24:35 Neinosu si ninje mbaak engoitoi o eneikuna teni eyolouni ninye too ninje tʼembelibelata olmkate.
Luke24:36 Ore epon eirorita ninje kuna-- neitashe ninye openy tʼempolos enye nejoki ninje: Eseriani inyi!"
Luke24:37 Neing'asia ninje neaku eureisho nejo-- aajo edolita Olmumua."
Luke24:38 Nejoki ninye ninje: Ainyo piakuku looureisho? Naa ainyo peilepu kuna kibirribirrat too ltauja linyi?
Luke24:39 Eng'orai ngaik ainei o nkejek ainei-- aajo ara nanu openy. Errapirrapaki-- eng'orai-- amu meata Olmumua nkiri o loik anaa pidolidolo aata nanu."
Luke24:40 Ore ejo ena-- neitadol ninje ngaik o nkejek."
Luke24:41 Ore epon eitu eiruk ninje tʼolbae lʼeng'ida o enking'asiata-- nejoki ninje: Iatata endaa tene?"
Luke24:42 Neisho ninje ninye endung'oti osingirri otapejoki o enaisho oo njosho.
Luke24:43 Neibung' ninye nenya tʼengomom enye.
Luke24:44 Nejoki ninye ninje: Ninje rorei lainei latiaka ndai-- epon atii e nebo o ndai-- ajo meata kata nemebaia sirat pookin tiatua nkitanapat e Mose o tiatua layolounok o tiatua singolioitin tʼolbae lai."
Luke24:45 Neboloki ninye ninje te ina kata eng'eno-- petum aatayoloutu sirat--"
Luke24:46 nejoki ninje: Neijia etisiraki-- peiye eisili Kristos nepiu too lootuata tʼengolong' e uni--"
Luke24:47 peinosakini tiatua loreren pookin tʼengarna enye enkitaalata enkitaunoto oo nkitarruot-- eiteri te Yerusalem."
Luke24:48 Nirara ndai iljaken loo kuna pookin.
Luke24:49 Naa eng'orai-- alairriwaki shumata inyienkisiligata e Papa lai. Kake entotoni ndai tʼengang' Yerusalem-- metabana neitagoli ndai tʼengolon naing'ua shumata."
Luke24:50 Nerikoo ninje aulo metabaiki Betania-- neapu ngaik enyena nemayan ninje."
Luke24:51 Neaku emayanita ninye ninje-- nerishi o ninje-- neilepieki shumata."
Luke24:52 Ore peidip ninje aateserem ninye-- nerrinyokino Yerusalem tʼeng'ida kitok"
Luke24:53 netii oshi engaji sinyati-- eitadaraa Engai."
John1:1 Etii tʼenkiterata Ororei netii Ororei enetii Engai-- nera Engai ele Rorei."
John1:2 Netii ninye ele tʼenkiterata enetii Engai.
John1:3 Etaa pookin te ninye-- neitu eaku oo nyoo-- metii ninye."
John1:4 Netii atua ninye empuan nera empuan enkilang'et oo ltung'anak.
John1:5 Neilang'isho enkilang'et tiatua enaimin neitu eng'amu enaimin ninye.
John1:6 Etii oltung'ani obo oirriwuaki tʼEngai-- neji engarna enye Yohanes."
John1:7 Eewuo ninye-- peaku enjakenishu-- peiye eijakenu mbaak e ina kilang'et-- petum pookin aairuko te ninye."
John1:8 Eitu era ilo enkilang'et-- kake peijakenu mbaak enkilang'et."
John1:9 Era ninye enkilang'et nasipa nailang'aki oltung'ani pookin-- olotu atua ele maa."
John1:10 Etii atua olmaa-- etaa olmaa te ninye-- neitu eyolou olmaa ninye."
John1:11 Eewuo ninye atua enenye-- neitu eng'amu ilkulenyena ninye."
John1:12 Ore pookin lootang'amutua ninye-- neisho ninje engolon-- peaku nkera Engai-- ninje looiruk engarna enye--"
John1:13 leitu eiuni too sargeta neme tʼeyeunoto enkiring'o neme tʼeyeunoto olee-- kake tʼEngai."
John1:14 Neaku Ororei enkiring'o nemanya atua yook-- nikidol enkitook enye-- enkitook anaa nʼOinoti obo oing'ua Menye-- obore eng'adunoto o esipata."
John1:15 Eijakenu Yohanes mbaak enyena nedar nejo: Era ninye olairorua: olotu tekurum ai-- netii lukunya ai-- amu etii-- eitu atii nanu."
John1:16 Niking'amu yook pookin tʼemborei enye-- eng'adunoto o eng'adunoto."
John1:17 Amu eishooki nkitanapat te Mose; etaa eng'adunoto o esipata te Yesus Kristos.
John1:18 Neitu aikata edol oltung'ani o obo Engai; Oinoti obo otii engalo olgoo le Menye-- ilo loinosua."
John1:19 Nera ena enjakenishu e Yohanes-- te ina kata nairriwaitie Yudayoi laidasak o ilevites enetii ninye eing'ua Yerusalem-- peiye eikilikwan ninye: Ira iye ng'ai?"
John1:20 Neibalu ninye neitu emiki-- neibalu: Mara nanu Kristos."
John1:21 Neikilikwan ninje ninye: Ira naa ng'ai? Ira Eliya? Nejo: Mara. Ira iye olayolounoni? Nealu: Me.
John1:22 Akae-- nejoki ninje: Ira naa ng'ai? pikinjo aleta kulo looirriutua yook. Ijo aa te kion?"
John1:23 Nejo ninye: Ara nanu oltoilo lʼoloipotisho ti ang'ata: Entorioi engoitoi Olaitoriani! anaa petejo olayolounoni Yesaya.
John1:24 Era ninje looirriwaiyoki ematua oo Lfarisayoi.
John1:25 Neikilikwan ninje ninye nejoki: Ainyo naa pimbatisisho-- teni mira iye Kristos arashu Eliya arashu olayolounoni?"
John1:26 Nealiki Yohanes ninje nejo: Aibatis nanu tʼengare; neitashe tʼempolos inyi olimiyololo ndai--"
John1:27 ore olotu tekurum ai netii lukunya ai-- meaku te nanu-- palak enkeene enamuke enye."
John1:28 Etaa ena te Betania-- te lido kekun le Yordan-- enetii Yohanes eibatisishe."
John1:29 Ore tʼengolong' e are nedol Yohanes Yesus elotu enetii-- nejo: Ng'orai-- embalelo Engai nanapita nkitarruot olmaa."
John1:30 Era ninye ele lairorua nanu: Elotu tekurum ai olee lotii lukunya ai-- amu etii-- eitu atii nanu."
John1:31 Neitu ayolou si nanu ninye-- kake peiye elioi te Israel-- onaa aewuo nanu-- paibatisisho tʼengare."
John1:32 Neijakenu Yohanes nejo: Atadua Olmumua edou aing'ua shumata anaa olmaitai neton te shumata enye.
John1:33 Neitu ayolou si nanu ninye; kake olaairriwaiye-- paibatis tʼengare-- ninye laatiaka: Olidol edoiki Olmumua shumata enye nebik te shumata enye-- ninye ele oibatis tʼOlmumua Sinyati"
John1:34 Nadol si nanu naijakenu-- ajo era ninye Oinoti lʼEngai."
John1:35 Neitoki aitashe tʼengolong' e are Yohanes o are too laiteng'enuok lenyena--"
John1:36 nedol ninye Yesus elimana nejo: Ng'orai-- embalelo Engai!"
John1:37 Nening' kulo aiteng'enuok lenyena aare eirorita nesuj ninje Yesus.
John1:38 Neibelekenya Yesus nedol ninje esujita nejoki ninje: Kainyo ing'oruru? Nejoki si ninje: Rabi (ore enkitaalata enye: Olaiteng'enani)-- kaji ibikie?"
John1:39 Nejoki ninye ninje: Ewotu-- eng'orai! Nepuonu nedol enebikie-- nebik te ina olong' o ninye. Nera enkata oo saan tomon."
John1:40 Nera obo too kulo aare lootoning'o te Yesus nesuj ninye Andreas-- olalashe le Simon Petros."
John1:41 Neinepu ninye tʼenkata elukunya olalashe lenye Simon nejoki ninye: Kinoto Mesias (eji enkitaalata enye: Kristos).
John1:42 Nerikoki ninye enetii Yesus. Ore pedol Yesus ninye-- nejo: Ira iye Simon-- enkerai e Yona-- kimpoti iye Kefas (eji enkitaalata enye: Osoit)."
John1:43 Ore tʼengolong' e are neyeu Yesus nelo Galilaya neinepu Filipos nejoki ninye: Tusujaki!
John1:44 Nera Filipos ole Betsaida-- lʼengang' e Andreas o Petros."
John1:45 Neinepu Filipos Natanael nejoki ninye: Kinoto ele lotisiraka Mose atua nkitanapat nesir baiki layolounok-- Yesus-- enkerat e Yosef-- le Nasaret."
John1:46 Nejoki Natanael ninye: Keidim atupuku te Nasaret entoki sidai? Nejoki Filipos ninye: Wou-- ng'orai!"
John1:47 Nedol Yesus Natanael eyaaya ninye nejo tʼolbae lenye: Ng'orai-- Oisraeli osipa nemetii olosek atua ninye."
John1:48 Nejoki Natanael ninye: Ke ti aji kitayolo? Nealiki Yesus nejoki ninye: Ore epon eitu kimpot Filipos-- aatadua iye itii abori olng'aboli."
John1:49 Nealiki Natanael ninye: Rabi-- ira iye Oinoti lʼEngai-- ira iye olkarsis le Israel!"
John1:50 Nealiki nejoki Yesus ninye: Iruko iye-- tiaraki naatiaka iye-- ajo aatadua iye tiabori olng'aboli; iladol nalang' kuna."
John1:51 Nejoki ninye: Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Ore eiter taata ipuopuo aadol shumata ebolo-- neilep nedou ilmalaikan lʼEngai te shumata Enkerai oltung'ani."
John2:1 Ore tʼengolong' e uni neaku enkiama te Kana e Galilaya; netii ina alo ng'otonye e Yesus.
John2:2 Eipotoki baiki Yesus o laiteng'enuok lenyena tʼenkiama.
John2:3 Ore peishunye olmarua-- nejoki ng'otonye e Yesus ninye: Meata ninje olmarua."
John2:4 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Nang'oroyoni-- kainyo aataiye iye? Eton eitu enyiku enkata ai."
John2:5 Nejoki ng'otonye enye laisyayak: Ore enaliki ninye ndai — entobira.
John2:6 Netii ine motiok ile engare tʼorregie lʼenkisujare oo Yudayoi-- nejing' nabo ntemeta are arashu uni."
John2:7 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Enganya motiok engare! Neigany metabaiki mbiron.
John2:8 Nejoki ninye ninje: Entooku taata-- eakiti olkitok lʼenaraa! Neaki."
John2:9 Ore peinyorrinyor olkitok lʼenaraa engare nataa olmarua-- eitu eyolo eneing'ua-- kake etayolo lelo aisyayak enetookunye engare-- neipot olkitok lʼenaraa osanja"
John2:10 nejoki ninye: Eishoru oltung'ani pookin tʼenkata elukunya olmarua sidai-- ore peidip aatemerata-- neishoru olobebek-- kake imboo iye olmarua sidai metabaiki taata."
John2:11 Era ninye olponoto lʼelukunya oitobira Yesus te Kana e Galilaya neitalioio enkitook enye; neiruk laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye.
John2:12 Ore tekurum e ina nedoiyo Kapernaum-- ninye o ng'otonye enye o lalashera lenyena o laiteng'enuok lenyena-- netoni te ina alo ngolong'i neme kumok."
John2:13 Netaanu pasaka oo Yudayoi neilep Yesus alo Yerusalem--"
John2:14 neinepu tʼengaji sinyati etoni lamirak loo lmong'i o loo nkerra o loo lmaita o lagilak loo ngoshola--"
John2:15 neitobir enkeene too nkopit nemir pookin tiatua engaji sinyati-- nkerra o ilmong'i-- neibukoo mpesai oo lagilak loo ngoshola-- neibelekeny ilkitareta--"
John2:16 nejoki kulo oomirita ilmaita: Entautu kuna te ina alo-- emintaa engaji e Papa lai engaji enkinyang'a!"
John2:17 Nedamu laiteng'enuok lenyena-- aajo etisiraki: Aainosa engilata e tau engaji ino."
John2:18 Akae-- nealu Yudayoi: Kalo ponoto intadol yook-- tiaraki nintobir kuna?"
John2:19 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninje: Entigil ena aji sinyati-- naitasheye ninye too ngolong'i uni."
John2:20 Akae-- nejo Yudayoi: Eteshetaki ena aji too larin artam o ile-- nintasheye iye ninye too ngolong'i uni?"
John2:21 Kake etejo ninye mbaak engaji sinyati osesen lenye.
John2:22 Akae-- ore peidip atopiu tiatua lootuata-- nedamu laiteng'enuok lenyena-- aajo etolimuo ena-- neiruk esirata o rorei ootejo Yesus."
John2:23 Ore etii Yerusalem te pasaka-- too ngolong'i kituak-- neiruk ilkumok engarna enye edol ilponot lenyena ooitobira."
John2:24 Kake eitu eiruk Yesus ninje-- tiaraki natayolouo pookin--"
John2:25 neitu eyeunoi te ninye-- peijakenu o obo embae oltung'ani; amu etayolouo ninye openy enatii atua oltung'ani."
John3:1 Etii oltung'ani obo loo Lfarisayoi-- oji engarna enye Nikodemos-- olkitok loo Yudayoi;"
John3:2 nelotu ilo kiarie enetii ninye nejoki ninye: Laiteng'enani-- kiyolo-- aajo ira olaiteng'enani oewuo eing'ua Engai; amu metii o obo oidim aitobira kulo ponot lintobir iye-- teni metii Engai e nebo o ninye."
John3:3 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninye: Japa-- japa-- aaliki iye-- teni meiuni oltung'ani kat are-- meidim atadua enkarsishu Engai."
John3:4 Nejoki Nikodemos ninye: Kaji eikuni teni eiuni oltung'ani era moruo? Keidim ninye atijing'a atua engoshoke e ng'otonye eniare-- peiuni?"
John3:5 Nealu Yesus: Japa-- japa-- aaliki iye-- teni meiuni oltung'ani tʼengare o tʼOlmumua-- meidim atijing'a atua enkarsishu Engai--"
John3:6 Enatoiwuoki tʼenkiring'o nera enkiring'o; o enatoiwuoki tʼOlmumua nera Olmumua.
John3:7 Mimputukuny-- tiaraki naatiaka iye: Meata kata nemeiuni ndai kat are."
John3:8 Ekutisho olkutati tʼewueji nayeu-- nining' oltoilo lenye-- kake miyolo eneing'ua o enelo. Neijia etiu pookin lotoiwuoki tʼOlmumua."
John3:9 Nealu Nikodemos nejoki ninye: Kaji eiko teni eaku kuna?
John3:10 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninye: Ira iye olaiteng'enani le Israel nimiyolou kuna?
John3:11 Japa-- japa-- aaliki iye: Enikiyolo-- nikilimu-- o enikitadua-- nikinjakenu; niming'amumu ndai enjakenishu ang'."
John3:12 Ore painosaki ndai mbaak enkop-- nimirukuruku-- kaji inkoko teni irukuruku-- teni ainosaki ndai mbaak e shumata?"
John3:13 Nemetii o obo oilepa shumata neme ele lotadouo eing'ua shumata-- Enkerai oltung'ani-- natii shumata."
John3:14 Naa neijia anaa petaapaiye Mose olasurai ti ang'ata-- neijia meata kata nemeapari Enkerai oltung'ani--"
John3:15 peiye meimin pookin looiruk ninye-- kake peata empuan nemeiting'."
John3:16 Amu nji etonyorra Engai olmaa neishooio Oinoti lenye obo-- peiye meimin pokin looiruk ninye-- kake peata empuan nemeiting'."
John3:17 Amu eitu eirriu Engai Oinoti lenye atua olmaa-- peiye eigwenaki ninye olmaa-- kake petum atopua olmaa te ninye."
John3:18 Oloiruk ninye-- nemeigwenakini; olemeiruk ninye-- eidipaki aigwenaki-- amu eitu eiruk ninye Oinoti obo lʼEngai."
John3:19 Naa ena enkigwena-- ajo eewuo enkilang'et atua olmaa-- nenyorru iltung'anak enaimin nelang' enkilang'et; amu era nkyasin enye torrok."
John3:20 Amu pookin loitobir ntorrok-- neiba enkilang'et nemelotu enetii enkilang'et-- pemebuakini nkyasin enyena."
John3:21 Kake oloitobir esipata-- nelotu enetii enkilang'et-- peiye elioi nkyasin enyena; amu eitobirate ninje tʼEngai."
John3:22 Nelotu Yesus o laiteng'enuok lenyena tekurum oo kuna atua olosho Yudaya-- nebik te ina alo te nebo o ninje neibatisisho."
John3:23 Neibatisisho baiki Yohanes te Amon nataaniki Salem-- amu etii ngariak kumok ina alo; nepuonu ina alo iltung'anak neibatisi."
John3:24 Amu epon eitu enang'akini Yohanes atua engaji eenata.
John3:25 Akae-- neaku enkikilikwanaroto tiatua laiteng'enuok le Yohanes o Yudayoi tʼolbae lʼenkisujata."
John3:26 Nepuonu ninje enetii Yohanes nejoki ninye: Laiteng'enani-- ng'orai-- eibatisisho ele likitaboitare te lido kekun le Yordan-- linjakenoko iye-- nepuonu pookin enetii ninye."
John3:27 Nealu Yohanes nejo: Meidim oltung'ani atang'amu toki neme enaishooki ninye eing'ua shumata.
John3:28 Kinjakenokiki ndai oopeny-- aajo atejo: Mara nanu Kristos-- kake aajo aairriwaiyoki nanu-- paiturukie ilo."
John3:29 Oloata esanja-- nera osanja; kake ore oljore lʼosanja-- loitashe neinining' ninye-- neng'ida tʼeng'ida kitok tʼolbae lʼoltoilo lʼosanja. Akae-- eitabaiyoki ena ng'ida ai."
John3:30 Meata kata nemepona ninye-- nang'oru nanu."
John3:31 Ololotu te shumata-- nera shumata oo pookin. Oloing'ua enkop-- nera lʼenkop neiro ninye nʼenkop. Ololotu te shumata-- nera shumata oo pookin--"
John3:32 neijakenu ena natadua nening'; nemeng'amu o obo enjakenishu enye.
John3:33 Olong'amu enjakenishu enye-- neitagol ninye tʼolmishire-- ajo era Engai esipata."
John3:34 Amu oloirriua Engai-- nelimu ele rorei lʼEngai; amu meishoru Engai Olmumua tʼentemet."
John3:35 Nenyor Menye Oinoti neisho pookin atua engaina enye.
John3:36 Oloiruk Oinoti-- neata ele empuan nemeiting'; olemening' Oinoti-- nemeladol ninye empuan-- kake ebik engoro Engai te shumata enye."
John4:1 Akae-- ore peyolou Olaitoriani-- ajo etoning'o Ilfarisayoi-- aajo eitaa neibatis Yesus laiteng'enuok nelang' Yohanes--"
John4:2 — neitu eibatisishe Yesus openy-- kake laiteng'enuok lenyena ake-- —"
John4:3 neing'ua ninye Yudaya neitoki alo Galilaya.
John4:4 Kake meata kata nemeim Samaria.
John4:5 Akae-- nelotu ninye engang' nabo e Samaria-- naji Sukar-- nataaniki enkuruma naishoo Yakoob enkerai enye Yosef."
John4:6 Netii ine olkesimet le Yakoob. Akae-- ore penaura Yesus tʼolototo-- neton ninye te shumata olkesimet; nera enkata oo saan ile."
John4:7 Nelotu eng'oroyoni nabo e Samaria aoku engare. Nejoki Yesus ninye: Njooki enaok!
John4:8 Amu eshomo laiteng'enuok lenyena atua engang'-- peinyang'u ndaikin."
John4:9 Akae-- nejoki ena ng'oroyoni e Samaria ninye: Kaji inko teni kiomonu iye lira Oyudayos engare niok-- te nanu nara eng'oroyoni e Samaria? Amu mepororo Yudayoi o Samareites."
John4:10 Nealiki Yesus nejoki ninye: Ten emutu iyolou enkishooroto Engai o olora olikijoki: Njooki enaok! anaata isai ninye pikinjo engare naishiu.
John4:11 Nejoki eng'oroyoni ninye: Laitoriani-- miata eniokunye-- neasur olkesimet; kaji inotie naa engare naishiu?"
John4:12 Ira iye kitok nilang' papa lang' Yakoob loishoo yook ele kesimet neok te ninye ninye openy o nkera enyena o njoorei enyena?
John4:13 Nealiki Yesus nejoki ninye: Ore pookin look ena are-- neitoki alatum enkure;"
John4:14 kake olook engare nalaisho nanu ninye-- meitoki alatum enkure tukul nkatan pookin-- kake engare nalaisho nanu ninye neaku tiatua ninye olkesimet lʼengare neilepu metabaiki empuan nemeiting'."
John4:15 Nejoki eng'oroyoni ninye: Laitoriani-- njooki ena are-- pamalo atum enkure namalotu ene aoku!"
John4:16 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Nno-- mpoto olmoruo lino-- pilotu ene."
John4:17 Nealu eng'oroyoni nejo: Maata olmoruo. Nejoki Yesus ninye: Itaalua sidai: maata olmoruo--"
John4:18 amu indipa aata ilmoruak imiet-- ore ele liata taata-- mera olmoruo lino; itejo ina nesipa."
John4:19 Nejoki eng'oroyoni ninye: Laitoriani-- adol-- ajo ira olayolounoni."
John4:20 Etasaishote loopapa lang' tʼele donyo; nijojo ndai-- aajo meata kata nemera Yerusalem ewueji nesaishoreki."
John4:21 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Rukoki-- nang'oroyoni-- amu elotu enkata nipuopuo aasai Papa me tʼele donyo neme te Yerusalem."
John4:22 Isayesaya ndai enimiyololo-- kisai yook enikiyolo-- amu eing'ua enkitopuata atua Yudayoi;"
John4:23 kake elotu enkata netii baiki taata-- ajo epuo aasai loosaisho oosipa Papa tʼolmumua o tʼesipata-- amu eing'oru Papa kulo-- oosai ninye nji."
John4:24 Era Engai Olmumua-- ore loosai ninye-- meata kata nemesai tʼOlmumua o tʼesipata."
John4:25 Nejoki eng'oroyoni ninye: Ayolo-- ajo elotu Mesias oji Kristos; teni elotu ilo-- neinosaki ninye yook mbaak pookin."
John4:26 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Nanu ilo laairorie.
John4:27 Nepuonu te ina kata laiteng'enuok lenyena neiputukuny-- tiaraki nairorie eng'oroyoni; kake eitu ejo oltung'ani o obo: Kainyo inkilikwana arashu kainyo irorie ninye?"
John4:28 Akae-- neing'ua engoroyoni emoti enye nelo atua engang' nejoki iltung'anak:"
John4:29 Ewotu-- eng'orai oltung'ani laatiaka mbaak pookin naitobira; me ele lora Kristos?"
John4:30 Nepuku ninje tʼengang' nepuonu enetii ninye.
John4:31 Ore tʼerishata oo kuna nediding' laiteng'enuok ninye ejo: Laiteng'enani-- tadaai!"
John4:32 Nejoki ninye ninje: Era endaa ai nanya enimiyololo ndai.
John4:33 Akae-- nejokino laiteng'enuok: Keaka oltung'ani ninye endaa?"
John4:34 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Era endaa ai-- paitobir eyeunoto olaairriua nalaidip enkyas enye."
John4:35 Mijojo ndai oopeny: Eng'or lapaitin ong'wan-- pebau enkisambuare? Eng'orai nkuruman-- aajo eidipa aaiborrita tʼenkisambuare."
John4:36 Ore oloisambu-- neng'amu ninye olkwaje neiturrur eishoi-- peaku nʼempuan oo nkatan pookin-- peng'ida olaisuaroni te nebo o oladung'oni."
John4:37 Amu esipa ele rorei tiatua ena bae: Olekai loisuaia naa olekai lodung'u.
John4:38 Airriwaiye nanu ndai-- pidung'udung'u eneitu iekenyakinono; eteekenyate kulekai nijing'ijing'i ndai atua eekenyaroto enye."
John4:39 Neiruk ilkumok loo Samareites le ina ang' ninye tʼolbae loo rorei lʼeng'oroyoni naijakenishe: Aatiaka mbaak pookin naitobira.
John4:40 Akae-- ore pepuonu Samareites enetii ninye-- nesai ninje ninye-- pebik te nebo o ninje; nebik te ina alo ngolong'i are."
John4:41 Nepon aairuk ilkumok nelang' tʼolbae loo rorei lenyena--"
John4:42 nejoki ninje ina ng'oroyoni: Me tʼolbae lʼenitolimuo iye kiruko taata-- amu kitoning'o yook oopeny nikiyolou-- aajo era ninye tʼesipata Kristos-- Olaitopuani lʼolmaa."
John4:43 Ore peishunye ngolong'i are-- nepuku ninye te ina alo nelo Galilaya."
John4:44 Amu eijakenishe Yesus openy-- ajo meata olayolounoni enkitook tiatua olosho lenye."
John4:45 Akae-- ore pelotu ninye Galilaya-- neng'amu Ilgalilayoi ninye-- ootadua pookin naaitobira ninye te Yerusalem too ngolong'i kituak; amu eshomo si ninje ngolong'i kituak."
John4:46 Neitoki alotu Yesus Kana e Galilaya eneitaalie ninye engare-- peaku olmarua."
John4:47 Netii oltung'ani obo lʼolkarsis nemoi enkerai enye te Kapernaum; etoning'o ninye-- ajo eing'ua Yesus Yudaya nelotu Galilaya-- nelotu enetii ninye nesai-- pedoiyo aishiunye enkerai enye; amu etaa nae."
John4:48 Akae-- nejoki Yesus ninye: Teni midolidolo ilponot o nkiputukunyot-- nimirukuruku tukul."
John4:49 Nejoki oltung'ani lʼolkarsis ninye: Laitoriani-- tadoi epon eitu ee enkerai ai."
John4:50 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Nno-- eishiu enkerai ino! Eiruko oltung'ani ororei lotiaka Yesus ninye nelo."
John4:51 Ore epon edoiyo-- nenang'are laisyayak ninye nejo-- aajo eishiuwo enkerai enye."
John4:52 Akae-- neikilikwan ninye ninje esaa naikashunye; nejoki ninje ninye: Etung'aiye oltikana ninye ng'ole tʼesaa napishana."
John4:53 Akae-- neyolou menye-- ajo ina saa natiakinye Yesus ninye: Eishiu enkerai ino. Neiruk ninye o engaji enye pookin."
John4:54 Neitoki aaku ninye olponoto le are oitobira Yesus eing'ua Yudaya nelotu Galilaya.
John5:1 Ore peidipai kuna-- netii ngolong'i kituak oo Yudayoi-- neilep Yesus alo Yerusalem."
John5:2 Netii atua Yerusalem engalo kishomi oo ntare eluanata nabo naipoti tʼenkutuk oo Lhebrayoi Betesda-- neata nkitalani imiet."
John5:3 Neirrag tiatua ninje esiamu kitok oo ltamoiya: ilmodook-- lemeidim aashom-- looikang'a-- neanyu ninje-- peing'unung'un engare."
John5:4 Amu etadoikio olmalaika obo tʼenkata enye atua eluanata-- peing'unung'unye engare; ore olojing' tʼenkata elukunya-- eidipaki aaing'unung'unye engare-- neishiu tʼemoiyan pookin naata ninye."
John5:5 Netii oltung'ani obo ina alo loata emoiyan enye enkata oo larin osom o isiet.
John5:6 Nedol Yesus ninye eirrag-- ore peyolou ninye-- ajo etamoiya enkata naado-- nejoki ninye: Iyeu niaku bioto?"
John5:7 Nealiki oltamoiyai ninye: Laitoriani-- maata oltung'ani-- laaisho ajing' atua eluanata-- teni eing'unung'un engare; ore palotu nanu-- neiter ajing' olekai."
John5:8 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Nyototoi-- tudumu erruat ino-- pilo!"
John5:9 Neaku ilo tung'ani bioto nabokata nedumu erruat enye nelo. Nera ina olong' engolong' naeng'ieng'areki.
John5:10 Nejoki Yudayoi oloishiunyeki: Era taata engolong' naeng'iengareki-- meaku pinap erruat ino."
John5:11 Nealiki ninye ninje: Olaaitaa bioto-- ninye laatiaka: Tudumu erruat ino-- nno!"
John5:12 Neikilikwan ninje ninye: Ang'ai ilo likitiaka: Tudumu erruat ino-- nno?"
John5:13 Neitu eyolo oloishiunyeki-- ajo ang'ai ilo; amu eiwang'a Yesus tʼolbae lʼesiamu natii ine wueji."
John5:14 Ore peidipai nona-- neinepu Yesus ninye tʼengaji sinyati nejoki ninye: Ng'orai-- itaa bioto-- mintoki aitarruo-- pemikinepu entorroni nalang'."
John5:15 Nelo ilo tung'ani nejoki Yudayoi-- ajo Yesus oitaa ninye bioto."
John5:16 Onaa eing'oraitie Yudayoi Yesus t'entorroni neing'oru-- pear ninye metua-- tiaraki naitobira kuna tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki."
John5:17 Nealiki Yesus ninje: Eitobirisho Papa lai metabaiki taata-- naitobirisho si nanu."
John5:18 Akae-- nepon aayeu Yudayoi near ninye te ina bae metua-- tiaraki neitu eitaa engolong' naeng'ieng'areki toki-- kake etejo baiki-- ajo era Engai Menye-- neitaa kion anaa Engai."
John5:19 Akae-- nealiki Yesus nejoki ninje: Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Meidim aitobira Oinoti te kion toki-- teni medol enaitobir Menye; amu enaitobir ninye-- neitobir si ninye Oinoti neijia."
John5:20 Amu enyor Menye Oinoti neitadol ninye pookin naitobirita ninye openy-- nepon aitadol ninye nkyasin kituak naalang' kuna-- pipuopuo aaiputukuny ndai."
John5:21 Amu neijia anaa peinyeye Papa lootuata neitaa ninje looishiu-- neijia eitaa baiki Oinoti looyeu looishiu."
John5:22 Amu meigwenaki Papa oo obo-- kake eishoo enkigwena pookin Oinoti--"
John5:23 peitaa ninje pookin Oinoti kitok-- neijia anaa peitaa ninje Papa kitok. Olemeitaa Oinoti kitok-- nemeitaa Papa kitok loirriwaiye ninye."
John5:24 Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Oloning' rorei lainei neiruk olaairriua-- neata empuan nemeiting' nemelotu atua enkigwena-- kake eima eing'ua enkea nejing' empuan."
John5:25 Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai-- elotu enkata netii taata-- ajo epuo aaning' lootuata oltoilo lʼOinoti lʼEngai; ore looning' ninye-- nepuo aaishiu."
John5:26 Amu neijia anaa peata Papa empuan tiatua kion-- neijia eisho ninye baiki Oinoti lenye empuan-- peata tiatua kion--"
John5:27 neisho ninye engolon naitaaye enkigwena-- tiaraki nara Enkerai oltung'ani."
John5:28 Emimputukuny tʼena. Amu elotu enkata napuo aaning' pookin lootii atua nkuraren oltoilo lenye--"
John5:29 nepuo aapuku looitobira sidan peaku lʼempiunoto empuan-- kake looitobira ntorrok-- peaku lʼempiunoto enkigwena."
John5:30 Maidim nanu aitobira entoki te kion; neijia anaa paning'-- neijia aigwenu; ore enkigwena ai eitoriori-- amu maing'oru eyeunoto ai-- kake eyeunoto olaairriua."
John5:31 Teni aijakenoki nanu kion-- nemesipa enjakenishu ai."
John5:32 Netii olekai laaijakenoki-- nayolo-- ajo esipa enjakenishu naaijakenoki."
John5:33 Irriwaitie ndai enetii Yohanes-- neijakenisho ninye tʼesipata."
John5:34 Kake mang'amu nanu enjakenishu tʼoltung'ani; kake airo kuna pitumutumu aatopok.
John5:35 Nera ilo enkilang'et neiwuwu neilang'isho-- kake itayeutuo ndai nigalalulu tʼenkata kinyi tiatua enkilang'et enye."
John5:36 Kake enjakenishu naata nanu-- nera kitok nelang' ne Yohanes; amu aaijikenoki nkyasin naaishoo Papa-- paitabaia ninje-- kuna kyasin naitobir-- aajo aairriua Papa."
John5:37 Ore Papa lai laairriua-- ninye laaijakenoko; neitu ining'ining'i ndai aikata oltoilo lenye neitu idolidolo emua enye--"
John5:38 nimiatata rorei lenyena loobik tiatua ndai-- amu mirukuruku ndai ele loirriua ninye."
John5:39 Ing'oruru tiatua sirat-- amu ijojo ndai iatata empuan nemeiting' tiatua ninje-- naa nena naaijakenoki;"
John5:40 nimiyeuu nipuonunu enatii nanu-- peiye iatata empuan."
John5:41 Mang'amu nanu enkitook too ltung'anak--"
John5:42 kake atayolo ndai-- ajo miatata enyorrata Engai tiatua aten."
John5:43 Aewuo nanu tʼengarna e Papa lai-- neitu king'amumu; teni elotu olekai tʼengarna enye openy-- ning'amumu ilo."
John5:44 Kaji inkoko teni indimidimi ndai aairuko-- teni ing'amunororo enkitook niming'oruru enkitook naing'ua Engai Papa openy?"
John5:45 Emijo-- aajo aitang'or ndai tʼengomom e Papa; etii obo oloitang'or ndai-- Mose ling'idarere ndai."
John5:46 Amu ten emutu irukuruku Mose-- anaata kirukuruku si nanu; amu ninye otisira mbaak ainei."
John5:47 Kake teni mirukuruku sirat enyena-- kaji inkoko teni irukuruku rorei lainei?"
John6:1 Ore tekurum oo kuna nelo Yesus lido kekun lʼolbalbal le Galilaya-- tʼengalo e Tiberias."
John6:2 Nesuj esiamu kitok ninye-- tiaraki natadua ilponot looitobira ninye too loomoiyaa."
John6:3 Neilepaki Yesus oldonyo neton te ina alo te nebo o laiteng'enuok lenyena.
John6:4 Netaanu pasaka-- ngolong'i kituak oo Yudayoi."
John6:5 Akae-- neapu Yesus ngonyek nedol-- ajo elotu esiamu kitok enetii ninye-- nejoki ninye Filipos: Ke ti aji kipuo aainyang'u ilmkaten-- penya kulo?"
John6:6 Etejo ena-- petem ninye; amu etayolo ninye openy enatayeuo neitobir."
John6:7 Nealiki Filipos ninye: mebaiki ninje ilmkaten loo denaria iip are-- peng'amu oltung'ani pookin enkinyi."
John6:8 Nejoki ninye obo too laiteng'enuok oji Andreas-- olalashe le Simon Petros:"
John6:9 Etii olaiyoni obo ene loata ilmkaten imiet engano o singir aare; kake ke o nyoo kuna too kulo kumok nji?
John6:10 Nejo Yesus: Entotona iltung'anak! Netii olkujita kitok ine wueji. Akae-- netoni leak esiana nijo iip onom."
John6:11 Neibung' Yesus kulo mkaten nejo ashe neisho laiteng'enuok-- neoriki laiteng'enuok loototonitio; neijia baiki too kulo singir anaa petayeutuo."
John6:12 Ore peidip aataraposhoto-- nejoki ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena: Enturrurro mbelat naatelekutua-- pemeimin toki."
John6:13 Akae-- neiturrur mbelat oo lmkaten imiet lʼengano naatelekutua too looinosa-- neigany ilbenia tomon o are."
John6:14 Akae-- ore pedol kulo tung'anak ele ponoto loitobira ninye-- nejo ninje-- aajo era ninye olayolounoni tʼesipata olotu atua olmaa."
John6:15 Ore peyolou Yesus-- ajo eyeu nepuonu aaibung' ninye-- peitaa olkarsis-- negelari neitoki alo oldonyo ninye openy."
John6:16 Ore pemutu-- nedoiyo laiteng'enuok lenyena aapuo engalo olbalbal--"
John6:17 neilepaki engalawa nepuonu lido kekun lʼolbalbal metabaiki Kapernaum. Eidipa ataa enaimin-- nepon eitu elotu Yesus enetii ninje."
John6:18 Neiposha olbalbal tʼolkutati kitok otukutishe.
John6:19 Akae-- ore peidip aatinyikai enijo stadia (ng'ororot) tikitam o imiet arashu osom-- nedol ninje Yesus elimana ti oriong' olbalbal-- etaaniki engalawa-- neureishoi."
John6:20 Nejoki ninye ninje: Nanu-- emiureisho!"
John6:21 Akae neyeu neng'amu ninje ninye atua engalawa-- netii engalawa nabokata engalo olosho loshomo."
John6:22 Nedol tʼengai olong' esiamu naitashe tʼolkekun lʼolbalbal-- aajo metii ina alo engai alawa neme ena nabo natijing'a laiteng'enuok lenyena-- nedol eitu ejing' Yesus te nebo o laiteng'enuok lenyena atua engalawa-- kake eshomo laiteng'enuok lenyena oopeny ake."
John6:23 Kake eetuo nkulie alawani eing'ua Tiberias netaaniki ene wueji neinosie ninje ilmkaten lootejoiye Olaitoriani ashe.
John6:24 Akae-- ore pedol esiamu-- ajo metii Yesus ina alo nemetii laiteng'enuok lenyena-- nejing' si ninje atua ngalawani nepuonu Kapernaum-- eing'oru Yesus."
John6:25 Ore peinepu ninje ninye te lido kekun lʼolbalbal-- nejoki ninye: Laiteng'enani-- kanu itabaua ene?"
John6:26 Nealiki Yesus ninje nejo: Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Miking'oruru-- tiaraki nitadua ilponot-- kake tiaraki ninosa ilmkaten niraposhosho."
John6:27 Eming'oru endaa namuta-- kake endaa nalabik metabaiki empuan nemeiting'-- nalaisho ndai Enkerai oltung'ani; amu eitagolo Engai Papa ninye tʼolmishire."
John6:28 Akae-- nejoki ninje ninye: Kaji kinko-- pikintobir nkyasin Engai?"
John6:29 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninje: Ena enkyas Engai-- pirukuruku oloirriua ninye."
John6:30 Akae-- nejoki ninje ninye: Kalo ponoto naa intobir iye-- pikidol nikiruk iye? Kaa kyas intobir?"
John6:31 Einosa loopapa lang'mana ti ang'ata anaa petisiraki: Eishoo ninje meinosa olmkate oing'ua shumata.
John6:32 Akae-- nejoki Yesus ninje: Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Me Mose loishoo ndai olmkate oing'ua shumata-- kake Papa lai oishoo ndai olmkate osipa oing'ua shumata;"
John6:33 amu era olmkate lʼEngai ele lodou aing'ua shumata neisho olmaa empuan.
John6:34 Akae-- nejoki ninje ninye: Njoo yook oshi ilo mkate."
John6:35 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Ara nanu olmkate lʼempuan; ololotu enatii nanu-- nemetum olamei tukul-- o olaairuk nanu-- nemetum enkure aikata tukul."
John6:36 Kake atiaka ndai-- ajo kitadua nanu-- neitu kirukuruku."
John6:37 Ore pookin laaisho Papa-- nelotu enatii nanu; o si ninye ololotu enatii nanu-- namaiturraki boo tukul;"
John6:38 amu eitu adou aing'ua shumata-- paitobir eyeunoto ai-- kake eyeunoto olaairriua."
John6:39 Naa ena eyeunoto olaairriua-- pamaiminye pookin naaishoo ninye-- kake palaitopiu ninye tʼengolong' enkiting'oto."
John6:40 Amu era eyeunoto e Papa lai-- peata oltung'ani pookin odol Oinoti neiruk ninye-- empuan nemeiting' nalaitopiu nanu ninye tʼengolong' enkiting'oto."
John6:41 Akae-- neing'unyung'unyaki Yudayoi ninye-- tiaraki natejo: Ara nanu olmkate otadouo aing'ua shumata."
John6:42 Nejo ninje: Mera ele Yesus-- enkerai e Yosef-- likiyolo yook menye o ng'otonye? Kaji eiko teni ejo ninye: Atadouo aing'ua shumata?"
John6:43 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninje: Eming'unyung'unyakino tiatua ndai.
John6:44 Metii o obo oidim aeu enatii nanu-- eitu eyetu ninye Papa laairriua-- nalaitopiu nanu ninye tʼengolong' enkiting'oto."
John6:45 Etisiraki tiatua layolounok: Nepuo aaku pookin looiteng'ena Engai. Ore oltung'ani pookin loning' te Papa-- neiteng'enuo nelotu enatii nanu."
John6:46 Me tiaraki natadua o obo Papa-- neme oloing'ua Engai-- ninye otadua Papa."
John6:47 Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Olaairuk nanu-- neata empuan nemeiting'."
John6:48 Ara nanu olmkate lʼempuan.
John6:49 Einosa loominyi linyi mana ti ang'ata nee.
John6:50 Nera ele olmkate otadouo aing'ua shumata peiye olonya ninye-- nemee."
John6:51 Ara nanu olmkate oishiu otadouo eing'ua shumata; ore oltung'ani lonya ele mkate-- nelaishiu nkatan pookin; naa ore olmkate laishoru nanu-- nera enkiring'o ai nalaishoru tʼolbae lʼempuan olmaa."
John6:52 Akae-- neitarrikino Yudayoi tiatua aten nejo: Kaji eiko teni eidim ninye aishoo yook mainosa enkiring'o enye?"
John6:53 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Teni mipuopuo aanya enkiring'o Enkerai oltung'ani niokioko osarge lenye-- nimiatata empuan tiatua aten."
John6:54 Olonya enkiring'o ai neok osarge lai-- neata empuan nemeiting'-- nalaitopiu ninye tʼengolong' enkiting'oto."
John6:55 Amu era enkiring'o ai endaa nasipa nera osarge lai eokore nasipa.
John6:56 Olonya enkiring'o ai neok osarge lai-- nebik ninye tiatua nanu nabik si nanu tiatua ninye."
John6:57 Neijia anaa paairriua Papa loishiu naishiu si nanu tʼolbae le Papa-- neijia olaanya nanu-- nelaishiu ilo tʼolbae lai."
John6:58 Era ele olmkate otadouo aing'ua shumata-- me anaa peinosa loominyi linyi mana-- nee. Olonya ele mkate-- nelaishiu nkatan pookin."
John6:59 Etejo kuna tiatua engaji Engai-- eiteng'enisho te Kapernaum."
John6:60 Akae-- ore pening' ilkumok too laiteng'enuok lenyena kuna-- nejo: Egol kulo rorei; kang'ai oidim atoning'o ninje?"
John6:61 Ore peyolou Yesus tiatua kion-- ajo eing'unyung'uny laiteng'enuok lenyena tʼolbae lʼena-- nejoki ninje: Keitagor ndai ena?"
John6:62 Akae-- keaku naa nyoo-- teni ipuopuo aadol Enkerai oltung'ani eilep eneing'ua tʼenkata elukunya?"
John6:63 Nera Olmumua oloisho empuan-- mera enkiring'o o nyoo. Ore rorei latiaka ndai-- nera ninje Olmumua o empuan."
John6:64 Netii ematua too ndai lemeiruk. Amu etayolo Yesus tʼenkiterata: etii looje lemeiruk o oloje loitarasaa ninye.
John6:65 Nejo ninye: Onaa atiaka ndai: Metii oloidim aeu enatii nanu-- teni meisho Papa ninye."
John6:66 Onaa eshomo te ina ilkumok too laiteng'enuok lenyena aaing'ua ninye neitu eitoki aalimanare ninye.
John6:67 Akae-- nejoki Yesus kulo tomon o are: Ai iyeuu si ndai nipuopuo?"
John6:68 Nealiki Simon Petros ninye: Laitoriani-- pikipuo enetii ng'ai? Iata iye rorei lʼempuan nemeiting';"
John6:69 nikiruko yook nikitayoloutuo-- ajo ira iye Kristos-- Oinoti lʼEngai naishiu."
John6:70 Nealiki Yesus ninje: Eitu agelu nanu ndai tomon o are? Nera obo too ndai satan?
John6:71 Neimaki ninye Yudas Iskariotes le Simon; amu ele olaitarasaa ninye-- nera ninye obo too kulo tomon o are."
John7:1 Ore tekurum oo kuna nelimana Yesus te Galilaya; amu eitu eyeu nelimana te Yudaya-- tiaraki naing'oru Yudayoi ninye-- pear metua."
John7:2 Netaanu ngolong'i kituak oo Yudayoi-- ngolong'i oo ltomboitie loo lkujit."
John7:3 Nejoki lalashera ninye: Tung'ai ene-- pilo Yudaya-- peiye etum aatadol baiki laiteng'enuok linono nkyasin inono nintobir;"
John7:4 amu metii oloitobir entoki tiatua emikio neyeu nelioi tʼewuas. Teni intobir kuna-- ntadua kion olmaa."
John7:5 Amu eitu eiruk baiki lalashera lenyena ninye.
John7:6 Akae-- nejoki Yesus ninje: Epon eitu ebau enkata ai-- kake eidipakine oshi enkata inyi."
John7:7 Meidim olmaa atemena ndai-- kake aamen nanu-- tiaraki naijakenoki ninye-- ajo era torrok nkyasin enyena."
John7:8 Elepa ndai aapuo kuna olong'i kituak; epon mailep nanu alo kuna olong'i kituak-- tiaraki epon eitu ebaia enkata ai."
John7:9 Ore peidip atiaki ninje kuna-- nebik te Galilaya--"
John7:10 Ore peidip lalashera lenyena aailepa aapuo ngolong'i kituak-- neilep alo si ninye-- me tʼewuas-- kake tʼemikio."
John7:11 Akae-- neing'oru Yudayoi ninye too ngolong'i kituak nejo: Kaji etii ele?"
John7:12 Netii enking'unyung'uny kitok tʼolbae lenye atua siamin. Nejo ilkulekai: Era ninye supat; nejo ilkulekai: Me-- amu eitamanimanaa esiamu."
John7:13 Kake eitu eimaki oltung'ani o obo mbaak enyena tʼewuas tʼolbae lʼeuriata oo Yudayoi.
John7:14 Ore tʼempolos oo ngolong'i kituak neilep Yesus alo engaji sinyati neiteng'enisho.
John7:15 Akae-- neiputukuny Yudayoi nejo: Kaji etayolounye ele sirat neitu eiteng'enuo ninye?"
John7:16 Akae-- nealiki Yesus ninje nejo: Mera enkiteng'enare ai enai-- kake nʼolaairriua."
John7:17 Teni eyeu neitobir oltung'ani eyeunoto enye-- neyolou mbaak enkiteng'enare-- ten ake eing'ua Engai arashu ten ake alimu nanu te kion."
John7:18 Ololimu te kion-- neing'oru enkitook enye openy; oloing'oru enkitook oloirriua ninye-- nesipa ele nemetii entorroni atua ninye."
John7:19 Me Mose loishoo ndai nkitanapat? Nemetii o obo tiatua ndai loitobir nkitanapat. Ainyo piking'oruru aar matua?
John7:20 Nealu esiamu: Iata olmeneng'ani. Ang'ai liking'oru aar tua?
John7:21 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninje: Aitobira enkyas nabo nimputukunyunyu pookin.
John7:22 Onaa eishoo ndai Mose emurata-- me tiaraki naing'ua Mose-- kake loopapa; nimuratata ndai oltung'ani baiki tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki."
John7:23 Ore pemurati oltung'ani tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki-- pemeari nkitanapat e Mose — ainyo pikigorokiki-- tiaraki naitaa bioto oltungani olulung'a tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki?"
John7:24 Emingwenaki too ngonyek-- kake engwenakiti enkigwena supat."
John7:25 Akae-- nejo ematua oo le Yerusalem: Me ele eing'oru ninje-- pear metua?"
John7:26 Naa eng'orai-- eirorita ninye tʼewuas-- nemeliki ninje ninye toki. Akae-- ketayoloutuo ilkituak lang' tʼesipata-- aajo era ele Kristos?"
John7:27 Kake kiyolo yook ele eneing'ua; teni elotu Kristos-- metii oloyolo eneing'ua."
John7:28 Akae-- nedar Yesus tʼengaji sinyati-- eiteng'enisho nejo: Ee-- kiyololo ndai nanu niyololo enaing'ua-- neitu alotu te kion-- kake olosipa ele laairriua nanu-- limiyololo ndai;"
John7:29 kake ayolo nanu ninye-- amu aing'ua nanu ninye-- naa ele laairriua."
John7:30 Akae-- neing'oru ninje-- peibung' ninye-- kake eitu eaki oltung'ani o obo ninye engaina-- amu epon eitu ebau enkata enye."
John7:31 Neiruk ilkumok tiatua esiamu ninye nejo: Teni elotu Kristos-- keitobir ninye ilponot kumok oolang' kulo ooitobir ele?"
John7:32 Etoning'o Ilfarisayoi esiamu eing'oming'om kuna baak enyena-- neirriwaa laidasak kituak o Ilfarisayoi laisyayak-- peibung' ninye."
John7:33 Akae-- nejo Yesus: Epon atii enkiti kata e nebo o ndai-- nalo tekurum enetii olaairriua."
John7:34 Kipuopuo aaing'oru-- nimikitumutumu; ore enatii nanu-- nimindimidimi aaetu ndai."
John7:35 Akae-- nejokino Yudayoi tiatua aten: Keibung' ele engoitoi alo aji-- ajo mikintoki aatum ninye? kelo atua enkisardakata oo Lgrikini-- pelaiteng'en Ilgrikini?"
John7:36 Kalo rorei ele lotejo ninye: Kipuopuo aaing'oru-- nimikitumutumu-- o enatii nanu-- nimindimidimi aaetu ndai?"
John7:37 Ore tʼengolong' kitok enkiting'oto oo ngolong'i kituak neitashe Yesus nedar nejo: Oloata enkure njelotu enatii nanu-- peok."
John7:38 Olaairuk nanu anaa pejo esirata-- neiponyunye tʼosesen lenye moipoi engare naishiu."
John7:39 Eimaka ena aa mbaak Olmumua lopuo aang'amu looiruk ninve; amu epon metii Olmumua Sinyati-- tiaraki nepon eitu eitaai Yesus kitok."
John7:40 Akae-- ore pening' iltung'anak tiatua esiamu kulo rorei-- nejo: Esipa-- era ele olayolounoni."
John7:41 Nejo ilkulekai: Ele lora Kristos; nejo ilkulekai: Kelotu naa Kristos eing'ua Galilaya?
John7:42 Mejo esirata-- ajo elotu Kristos tiatua eishoi e David eing'ua Betlehem-- engang' natobikie David?"
John7:43 Akae-- nejing' atua olorere erishata tʼolbae lenye."
John7:44 Etayeutuo kulekai too ninje neibung' ninye; kake metii oltung'ani oaka ninye ngaik.
John7:45 Akae-- nepuonu laisyayak enetii laidasak kituak o Ilfarisayoi-- nejoki lelo ninje: Ainyo peitu irikuku ninye?"
John7:46 Nealu laisyayak: Eitu aikata eiro oltung'ani o obo neijia anaa peiro ele tung'ani.
John7:47 Akae-- nealiki Ilfarisayoi ninje: Keitamanimanaiyoki si ndai?"
John7:48 Kang'ai tiatua ilkituak arashu tiatua Ilfarisayoi loiruk ninye?
John7:49 Kake el orere ake lemeyolo nkitanapat-- njedeki ninje."
John7:50 Nejoki Nikodemos loewuo kiarie enetii ninye nera obo lenye ninje:
John7:51 Keigwenaki nkitanapat ang' oltung'ani-- epon eitu eng'asi aainining' ninye peyolouni enaitobira?"
John7:52 Nealu nejoki ninje ninye: Ing'ua si iye Galilaya? Tisipu-- ng'orai-- ajo mepuku olayolounoni aing'ua Galilaya."
John7:53 Neibung' oltung'ani pookin engoitoi nelo engaji enye.
John8:1 Nelo Yesus Oldonyo loo loirienito.
John8:2 Ore enasirie pepej ewuas-- neitoki alotu engaji sinyati-- nepuonu olorere pookin enetii ninye-- neton si ninye neiteng'en ninje."
John8:3 Nerikoki layolok lʼesirata o Ilfarisayoi ninye eng'oroyoni naibung'aki eitobirita mbaak eloloito-- neitasheye ninye tʼempolos--"
John8:4 nejoki ninye: Eibung'aki ena ng'oroyoni te ina kata ake naitobirita mbaak eloloito;
John8:5 kake eitanapa Mose yook too nkitanapat-- peari natiu nji too soito. Akae-- ijo aa iye?"
John8:6 Etolimutuo ena-- petem ninye-- petum enaitang'orie ninye. Kake eirruge Yesus nesir tʼolkimojino enkop."
John8:7 Ore eponita ninje aaikilikwan ninye-- neapunye nejoki ninje: Olemeata enkitarruoto too ndai-- njeiter anang' ninye tʼosoit."
John8:8 Neitoki airrugo nesir enkop.
John8:9 Ore pening' ninje kuna-- nepuku-- etigilua oltoilo lʼoltau ninje-- obo obo-- eiter too lmoruak metabaiki lʼenkiting'oto-- neleku ninye openy ake o ena ng'oroyoni natii empolos."
John8:10 Neapunye Yesus neitu edol oltung'ani neme ena ng'oroyoni nejoki ninye: Nang'oroyoni-- kaji etii kulo aitang'orok linono? Metii o obo likitaara?"
John8:11 Nejo si ninye: Metii o obo-- Laitoriani. Nejo Yesus: Maar si nanu iye; nno-- mintoki aitarruo eiter taata."
John8:12 Akae-- neitoki airorie Yesus ninje nejo: Ara nanu enkilang'et olmaa; olaasuj nanu-- nemelimana ninye tukul tiatua enaimin-- kake elaata enkilang'et empuan."
John8:13 Akae-- nejoki Ilfarisayoi ninye: Injakenoki iye kion; mesipa enjakenishu ino."
John8:14 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninje: Teni aijakenoki nanu kion-- nesipa enjakenishu ai-- amu ayolo enaing'ua o enalo."
John8:15 Ingwenunu ndai tʼentemet enkiring'o-- maigwenaki nanu oltung'ani o obo."
John8:16 Naa teni aigwenu nanu-- nera enkigwena ai esipata-- tiaraki namatii nanu openy-- kake nanu o Papa laairriua."
John8:17 Etisiraki baiki tiatua nkitanapat inyi-- ajo esipa enjakenishu oo ltung'anak aare."
John8:18 Ara nanu oloijakenoki kion-- naaijakenoki Papa laairriua."
John8:19 Akae-- nejoki ninje ninye: Kaji etii Minyi lino? Nealu Yesus: Mikiyololo nanu nimiyololo Papa lai: ten emutu kiyololo nanu-- anaata iyololo baiki Papa lai."
John8:20 Etolimuo Yesus kulo rorei tʼenetii eneitadoikini mpesai-- eiteng'enisho tiatua engaji sinyati; neitu eibung' oltung'ani o obo ninye-- amu epon eitu ebau enkata enye."
John8:21 Akae-- neitoki ninye ajoki ninje: Alo nanu-- niking'oruru ndai nipuopuo aae tiatua nkitarruot inyi. Enalo nanu mindimidimi ndai aaetu."
John8:22 Akae-- nejo Yudayoi: Kear kion metua-- tiaraki najo: Enalo nanu mindimidimi ndai aaetu?"
John8:23 Nejoki ninye ninje: Irara ndai liabori-- nara nanu le shumata; irara ndai lʼele maa-- namara nanu lʼele maa."
John8:24 Akae-- atiaka ndai-- ajo ipuopuo aae tiatua nkitarruot inyi; amu teni mirukuruku-- aajo ara nanu ilo-- nipuopuo aae tiatua nkitarruot inyi."
John8:25 Akae-- nejoki ninje ninye: Ira iye ng'ai? Nejoki Yesus ninje: Ore tʼenkata elukunya oloirorie ndai."
John8:26 Naata nkumok naimakinye ndai naigwenu; kake olaairriua nera esipata-- ore natoning'o nanu te ninye-- ninje alimu tiatua olmaa."
John8:27 Neitu eyolou ninje-- ajo eimakinye ninje Papa."
John8:28 Akae-- nejoki Yesus ninje: Teni ipuopuo aapu Enkerai oltung'ani-- nipuopuo aayolou te ina kata-- aajo ara nanu ilo-- namaitobir entoki naa kion-- kake anaa paaiteng'ena Papa lai-- nena alimu."
John8:29 Ore olaairriua-- netii e nebo o nanu; eitu aaing'ua Papa openy-- tiaraki naitobir oshi nanyor ninye."
John8:30 Ore eirorita ninye kuna-- neiruk ilkumok ninye."
John8:31 Akae-- nejoki Yesus Iyudayoi looiruko ninye: Teni ibikibiki ndai tiatua rorei lainei-- nirara laiteng'enuok lainei tʼesipata--"
John8:32 nipuopuo aayolou esipata nelalaku ndai esipata.
John8:33 Nealiki ninje ninye: Kira eishoi e Abraham neitu kisyayaki aikata o obo. Kaji inko teni ilimu iye-- ajo epuoi aalaku ndai?"
John8:34 Nealiki Yesus ninje: Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Ore oltung'ani pookin loitobir enkitarruoto-- nera osinga lʼenkitarruoto."
John8:35 Nemebik osinga ti aji nkatan pookin-- Oinoti obik nkatan pookin."
John8:36 Akae-- teni elalaku ndai Oinoti-- etalakuaki ndai tʼesipata."
John8:37 Ayolo nanu-- ajo irara eishoi e Abraham; kake king'oruru-- pikiariara matua-- tiaraki nemetum rorei lainei ewueji tiatua ndai."
John8:38 Airo kuna natadua te Papa lai; akae-- ore ndai nining'ining'i te minyi linyi-- nintobiribiri."
John8:39 Nealu nejoki ninje ninye: Era Abraham Papa lang'. Nejoki Yesus ninje: Teni irara nkera e Abraham-- entobira nkyasin e Abraham;"
John8:40 kake niking'oruru taata-- pikiariara matua-- oltung'ani lotiaka ndai esipata-- natoning'o tʼEngai. Eitu eitobir Abraham ena."
John8:41 Intobiribiri ndai nkyasin e minyi linyi. Etiakitia ninje ninye: Eitu eiu yook latalak-- kiata yook Papa obo-- ora Engai."
John8:42 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Ten emutu era Engai Minyi linyi-- anaata kinyorrinyorro nanu-- amu atupukuo nanu tʼEngai-- aewuo te ninye; amu eitu alotu te kion-- kake ninye laairriua."
John8:43 Ainyo pimiyolouu enkiroroto ai? Tiaraki nimindimidimi aatoning' rorei lainei.
John8:44 Ing'uang'ua ndai minyi linyi-- satan-- niyeuu nintobiribiri ilng'warraitin le minyi linyi. Era ninye olarani loo ltung'anak neba tʼenkiterata neitu eitashe ninye tiatua esipata-- amu metii esipata atua ninye. Teni elimu elejare-- nelimu enenye-- amu era ninye olalejani o menye lenye."
John8:45 Ore nanu-- tiaraki nalimu esipata-- nimikirukuruku."
John8:46 Kang'ai olinyi laaidim aitayolo enkitarruoto? Teni alimu esipata-- ainyo pimikirukuruku ndai?"
John8:47 Olora lʼEngai-- nening' rorei lʼEngai; onaa mining'ining'i ndai-- tiaraki nimirara lʼEngai."
John8:48 Nealu Yudayoi nejoki ninye: Mikijo yook sidai-- aajo ira iye Osamareites niata olmeneng'ani?"
John8:49 Nealu Yesus: Maata nanu olmeneng'ani-- kake aitaa kitok Papa lai-- nimikintaata ndai nanu kitok."
John8:50 Maing'oru nanu enkitook ai; etii obo oing'oru neigwenu.
John8:51 Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Teni eibung' oltung'ani rorei lainei-- nemeladol ninye enkea tukul nkatan pookin."
John8:52 Nejoki Yudayoi ninye: Kitayoloutuo taata-- aajo iata olmeneng'ani; etua Abraham o layolounok; nijo iye: Teni eibung' oltung'ani rorei lainei-- nemelainyorrinyor ninye enkea tukul nkatan pookin."
John8:53 Ira iye kitok nilang' papa lang' Abraham otua? Etuata baiki layolounok. Intaa kion ng'ai?
John8:54 Nealu Yesus: Teni aitaa nanu kion kitok-- mera enkitook ai toki. Etii Papa lai laaitaa kitok-- lijojo ndai-- aajo era Engai inyi;"
John8:55 nimiyololo ndai ninye-- kake ayolo nanu ninye. Ten emutu ajo: mayolo nanu ninye-- anaata aaku olalejani anaa ndai; kake ayolo nanu ninye naibung' rorei lenyena."
John8:56 Etagalale minyi linyi Abraham-- pedol engolong' ai: nedol neng'ida."
John8:57 Akae nejoki Yudayoi ninye: Epon miata larin onom-- nitadua iye Abraham?"
John8:58 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Epon eitu eiuni Abraham-- atii nanu."
John8:59 Nedumu soito-- penang' ninye. Neisudori Yesus nepuku neing'ua engaji sinyati neim empolos enye negiroo."
John9:1 Ore eimita Yesus nedol oltung'ani modooni neba tʼeiunoto.
John9:2 Neikilikwan laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye nejo: Laiteng'enani-- kang'ai loitarruoiye-- ke ninye arashu lootoiutuo ninye-- petoiwuoki ninye aa modooni?"
John9:3 Nealu Yesus: Eitu eitarruo ninye o lootoiutuo ninye-- kake pelioi nkyasin Engai te ninye."
John9:4 Meata kata namaitobir nkyasin olaairriua-- epon aa dama; elotu enkiarie nemeidim o obo aitobirishoi."
John9:5 Ore epon atii olmaa-- nara nanu enkilang'et olmaa."
John9:6 Ore peidip atejo kuna-- nenotaki ngamulak enkop neipurupuruj nkulupuok too ngamulak neelie olokidong'oi ngonyek--"
John9:7 nejoki ninye: Nno-- sujai tiatua eluanata Siloa (neji enkitaalata enye: Oloirriwaiyoki). Akae-- nelo aisuja nelotu edolisho."
John9:8 Ore lʼelatia o lootadua ninye tʼenkata elukunya-- aajo era olaomononi-- nejo: Me ele lototona eomonisho?"
John9:9 Nejo ilkulekai: Ninye. Nejo ilkulekai: Me-- ak enyanyukie ninye. Nejo ninye: Ee-- nanu."
John9:10 Akae nejoki ninje ninye: Kaji naa eikununo duo nebolo ngonyek inono?
John9:11 Nealu ninye: Oltung'ani oji Yesus oitobira olokidong'oi naaelie ngonyek naajoki: Nno eluanata Siloa-- sujai! Akae-- ashomo naisuja nadolishoi."
John9:12 Nejoki ninje ninye: Kaji etii ilo? Nejo: Mayolo.
John9:13 Nerik ninje ninye enetii Ilfarisayoi-- ilo lora tʼenkata elukunya olmodooni."
John9:14 Nera ina olong' engolong' naeng'ieng'areki naitobira Yesus olokidong'oi nebol ngonyek enyena.
John9:15 Akae-- neitoki naikilikwan si ninje Ilfarisayoi eneikuna ten edolisho. Nejoki ninye si ninje: Olokidong'oi aatipika-- naisuja nadolishoi."
John9:16 Akae-- nejo ematua oo Lfarisayoi: Mera ilo tung'ani lʼEngai-- amu meibung' engolong' naeng'ieng'areki. Nejo ilkulekai: Kaji eiko teni eidim aitobira oltungani aitarruoni ilponot kituak anaa kulo? Neaku erishata too ninje:"
John9:17 Akae-- neitoki aajoki ninje olmodooni: Ijo aa iye te ninye-- tiaraki natabolo ngonyek inono? Nejo: Olayolounoni."
John9:18 Neitu eiruk Iyudayoi mbaak enyena-- aajo era olmodooni netadolishe metabana neipot ninje lootoiutuo ninye otadolishe."
John9:19 Neikilikwan ninje nejo: Kera ninye enkerai inyi-- ijojo ndai-- etoiwuoki aa modooni? Kaji eiko teni edolisho ninye taata?"
John9:20 Akae-- nealu lootoiutuo ninye nejo: Kiyolo-- aajo era ele enkerai ang'-- netoiwuoki aa modooni."
John9:21 Ore eneikuna teni edolisho taata-- mikiyolo; arashu olotabolo ngonyek enyena-- mikiyolo; oltung'ani botor ninye-- enkilikwana ninye openy-- pelimu mbaak enyena."
John9:22 Etejo lootoiutuo ninye kuna-- tiaraki naturia Yudayoi; amu eidipa Yudayoi aatuun enjata-- aajo oltung'ani oibalu-- ajo era ninye Kristos-- neitauni ninye tʼenkisot."
John9:23 Te ina etejo lootoiutuo ninye: Oltung'ani botor ele-- enkilikwana ninye openy."
John9:24 Akae-- neitoki aaipot ninje ilo tung'ani lora opa modooni nejoki ninye: Njoo Engai enkitook! kiyolo yook-- aajo era ilo tung'ani olaitarruoni."
John9:25 Nealu ninye: Ten aa olaitarruoni-- mayolo; nabo ake ayolo-- ajo ara opa olmodooni nadolisho taata."
John9:26 Akae-- neitoki aajoki ninje ninye: Ainyo kintobiraka? Kaji eikuna teni ebol ngonyek inono?"
John9:27 Nealiki ninye ninje: Aidipa atiaki ndai — eitu ining'ining'i? Ainyo pintokiki aayeu nining'ining'i en e are? Iyeuu si ndai niakuku laiteng'enuok lenyena?
John9:28 Nebuaki ninje ninye nejo: Ira iye olaiteng'enuoni le ilo-- kira yook laiteng'enuok le Mose."
John9:29 Kiyolo yook-- aajo eirorie Engai Mose-- kake mikiyolo eneing'ua ilo."
John9:30 Nealu oltung'ani nejoki ninje: Eji era ninye entoki naiputukunyisho-- ajo miyololo ndai eneing'ua ninye-- naa ninye laatabolo ngonyek."
John9:31 Kiyolo yook-- aajo mening' Engai laitarruok-- kake teni eaku oltung'ani oloure Engai neitobir eyeunoto enye-- nening' ele."
John9:32 Eitu ening'i neba tʼenkiterata-- ajo etabolo oltung'ani ngonyek olotoiwuoki aa modooni."
John9:33 Ten emutu mera ilo lʼEngai-- anaata meidim aitobira toki."
John9:34 Nealu ninje nejoki ninye: Kitoiwuoki iye ilulung'a tiatua nkitarruot ninteng'en yook? Neitupuku ninye boo.
John9:35 Nening' Yesus-- ajo etupukutuo ninje ninye boo. Ore pedol ninye-- nejo: Iruk iye Oinoti lʼEngai?"
John9:36 Nealu ninye nejo: Kang'ai ilo-- Laitoriani-- patum airuko ninye?"
John9:37 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Itadua iye ninye-- naa ninye likirorie."
John9:38 Nejo: Airuk-- Laitoriani! neserem ninye."
John9:39 Nejo Yesus: Aewuo nanu atua ele maa-- paigwenu-- pedolishoi lemedolisho-- peaku modook loodolisho."
John9:40 Nening' kuna ematua oo Lfarisayoi lootii e nebo o ninye-- nejoki ninje ninye: Ke-- kira si yook ilmodook?"
John9:41 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Ten emutu irara modook-- anaata miatata enkitarruoto: kake ore pijojo taata: Kidolisho! nebik enkitarruoto inyi."
John10:1 Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Olemejing' emuatata oo ntare aim kishomi-- kake nelang' tʼengai wueji-- nera ninye olapurroni o olainyamoni."
John10:2 Kake olojing' aim kishomi nera olairritani loo ntare.
John10:3 Nebolu olarriponi le kishomi ninye-- nening' ntare oltoilo lenye neipot ngam oo ntare enyena nereu ninje aulo."
John10:4 Ore peidip aitupuku nkun enyena aulo-- nelo lukunya enye-- nesuj ntare ninye-- amu eyolo ninje oltoilo lenye."
John10:5 Mesuj ninje olomoni tukul-- kake ekwet ninye-- tiaraki nemeyolo ninje oltoilo lʼolomoni."
John10:6 Etiaka Yesus ninje ena kitanyanyukiet-- kake eitu emus ninje-- nara natiaka ninje."
John10:7 Akae-- neitoki ajo Yesus: Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Ara nanu kishomi oo ntare."
John10:8 Ore pookin laaiturukie nanu-- nera lapurrok o lainyamok; kake eitu ening' ntare ninje."
John10:9 Ara nanu kishomi; ore oltung'ani ojing' te nanu-- nepok-- nejing' ninye nepuku netum enkirrita."
John10:10 Melotu olapurroni neme tʼempurrore-- peyeng' neiminye ake; aewuo nanu-- peata ninje empuan o emborei."
John10:11 Ara nanu olairritani sidai. Eishooio olairritani sidai oltau lenye tʼolbae loo ntare.
John10:12 Ore olaishokoni-- lemera olairritani-- nemera olopeny ntare-- teni edol osuiyani elotu-- neing'ua ntare nekwet; nerreshu osuiyani ntare neisardakie."
John10:13 Nekwet olaishokoni nemepik mbaak oo ntare atua oltau lenye.
John10:14 Ara nanu olairntani sidai nayolo naara nkun ainei naayolo nkun ainei nanu--"
John10:15 neijia anaa paayolo Papa nanu nayolo si nanu Papa-- naishooio oltau lai tʼolbae loo ntare."
John10:16 Naata nkulie tare-- nemetii ninje ena muatata; meata kata namareu si ninje-- nepuo aaning' oltoilo lai-- nelaaku emboo nabo o olairritani obo."
John10:17 Onaa aanyor Papa-- tiaraki naishooio oltau lai-- paitoki ang'amu ninye kat are."
John10:18 Metii o obo oitau ninye te nanu-- kake nanu openy oishooio ninye. Aata engolon naishorie ninye-- naata engolon naitoki ang'amunye ninye. Atang'amua ena kitanapata te Papa lai."
John10:19 Neitoki aaku erishata tiatua Yudayoi tʼolbae loo kulo rorei.
John10:20 Nejo ilkumok too ninje: Eata ninye olmeneng'ani o oloirirua; ainyo pining'ining'i ninye?
John10:21 Nejo ilkulekai: Mera kulo rorei lʼoloata olmeneng'ani. Keidim olmeneng'ani atabolo ngonyek oo lmodook?
John10:22 Neaku ngolong'i esinyaroto engaji sinyati te Yerusalem-- naa enkata enkirobi."
John10:23 Nelimana Yesus tiatua engaji sinyati tʼolgilata le Salomo.
John10:24 Akae-- neman Iyudayoi ninye nejoki ninye: Metabaiki anu ing'asie iltauja lang? Teni ira iye Kristos-- tiaki yook abaraki."
John10:25 Nealiki Yesus ninje: Atiaka ndai neitu irukuruku; ore nkyasin naitobir nanu tʼengarna e Papa lai-- ninje naaijakenoki."
John10:26 Kake mirukuruku ndai-- tiaraki nimitiiti atua ntare ainei."
John10:27 Ening' ntare ainei oltoilo lai nayolo si nanu ninje naasuj ninje nanu--"
John10:28 naisho nanu ninje empuan nemeiting'-- nemepuo aaimin ninje nkatan pookin-- nemetii o obo laaoru ninje tʼengaina ai."
John10:29 Era Papa lai laaishoo ninje kitok nelang' pookin; nemetii o obo loidim atooru ninje tʼengaina e Papa lai.
John10:30 Ore nanu o Papa kira nabo.
John10:31 Neitoki aasotu Yudayoi soito-- penang'ie ninye."
John10:32 Nealiki Yesus ninje: Aitadua ndai nkyasin sidan kumok naaing'ua Papa lai; ke tʼolbae le aa kyas too kuna kinang'ieng'ie soito?
John10:33 Nealiki Yudayoi ninye: Mikinang' iye too soito tʼolbae lʼenkyas sidai-- kake tʼolbae lʼemoroto Engai-- tiaraki nintaa kion Engai-- nira oltung'ani."
John10:34 Nealiki Yesus ninje: Eitu esiri tiatua nkitanapat inyi: Atejo nanu: irara ngain?
John10:35 Teni ejo ninye ninje ngain-- lelo ootabaikia ororei lʼEngai — nemeidimi aataar esirata —--"
John10:36 nijokiki ndai ele loitaa Papa sinyati neirriwaki atua olmaa-- ajo emor Engai-- tiaraki natejo: Ara Oinoti lʼEngai?"
John10:37 Teni naaitobir nkyasin e Papa lai-- emikiruk;"
John10:38 teni aitobir-- baiki teni mikirukuruku nanu-- eruko kuna kyasin-- pitumutumu aatayolo nirukuruku-- aajo etii Papa atua nanu natii nanu atua Papa."
John10:39 Akae-- neitoki aaing'oru ninje-- peibung' ninye; nepuku ninye too ngaik enye."
John10:40 Neitoki alo lido kekun le Yordan metabaiki ene wueji netii Yohanes tʼenkata elukunya eibatisisho-- neton te ina alo."
John10:41 Nepuonu ilkumok enetii ninye nejo: Eitu eitobir Yohanes olponoto o obo-- kake ore mbaak pookin naatejo Yohanes tʼele-- nera esipata."
John10:42 Neiruk ilkumok ninye te ina alo.
John11:1 Netii oltung'ani obo lomoi oji Lasaros le Betania-- tʼengang' e Maria o ne Marta-- enganashe enye."
John11:2 Nera Maria ena naela Olaitoriani tʼeilata narropil nejut nkejek enyena too lpapit lenyena; nemoi olalashe lenye Lasaros.
John11:3 Akae-- neirriwaa nganashera olkilikwai enetii ninye nejo: Laitoriani-- ng'orai-- emoi olinyor."
John11:4 Ore pening' Yesus ena-- nejo: Mera ena moiyan nʼenkea-- kake nʼenkitook Engai-- peitaai Oinoti lʼEngai kitok te ninye."
John11:5 Etonyorra Yesus Marta o enganashe enye o Lasaros.
John11:6 Akae-- ore peidipa atoning'o-- ajo emoi-- nebik te ine wueji netii ngolong'i are."
John11:7 Nejoki tekurum laiteng'enuok lenyena: Mainyaaki aapuo Yudaya!
John11:8 Nejoki laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye: Laiteng'enani-- king'orutua Yudayoi-- pikinang' too soito-- nintoki alo ina alo?"
John11:9 Nealu Yesus: Me saan tomon o are eata endama? Teni elimana oltung'ani dama-- nemeikobi-- tiaraki nadolita enkilang'et ele maa;"
John11:10 Kake teni elimana oltung'ani tʼenkiarie-- neikobi-- amu metii enkilang'et atua ninye."
John11:11 Etejo kuna-- ore tekurum nejoki ninje: Eirure oljore lang' Lasaros; kake aibung' engoitoi-- palainyeye ninye."
John11:12 Akae-- nejoki laiteng'enuok lenyena ninye: Laitoriani-- teni eirure-- nelaishiu."
John11:13 Kake eimaka Yesus mbaak enkea enye-- nejo ninje-- aajo eimaka mbaak enkirragata oo njok."
John11:14 Akae-- nejoki Yesus ninje te ine abaraki: Etua Lasaros--"
John11:15 kake ang'ida tʼolbae linyi-- tiaraki neitu atii ina alo-- pitumutumu aairuko. Kake maapeti enetii ninye!"
John11:16 Akae nejoki Tomas-- oji Olmaoi-- kulekai aiteng'enuok: Maapeti si yook-- pikie te nebo o ninye."
John11:17 Akae-- ore pelotu Yesus-- neinepu ninye eidipa atobiko ngolong'i ong'wan tiatua enkurare."
John11:18 Netaaniki Betania Yerusalem anaa stadia tomon o imiet.
John11:19 Neetuo ilkumok too Yudayoi enetii Marta o Maria-- peiye eilejilej ninje tʼolbae lʼolalashe lenye."
John11:20 Akae-- ore pening' Marta-- ajo elotu Yesus-- nelanang'are ninye; neton Maria tiatua aji."
John11:21 Akae-- nejoki Marta Yesus: Laitoriani-- ten emutu itii ene-- anaata eitu ee olalashe lai!"
John11:22 Kake ayolo baiki taata-- ajo pookin niomonu Engai-- nikinjo Engai."
John11:23 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Elapiu olalashe lino.
John11:24 Nejoki Marta ninye: Ayolo-- ajo elapiu tʼenkitopiunoto engolong' enkiting'oto."
John11:25 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Ara nanu empiunoto o empuan; olaairuk nanu-- nelaishiu-- baiki teni ee;"
John11:26 naa pookin loishiu naairuk nanu-- nemee tukul nkatan pookin. Iruk ena?"
John11:27 Nejoki ninye: Ee-- Laitoriani-- airuko nanu-- ajo ira iye Kristos-- Oinoti lʼEngai-- oewuo atua olmaa."
John11:28 Ore peidip atejo kuna-- nelo neipot Maria-- enganashe enye-- tʼemikio nejo: Etabaua Olaitoriani-- kimpot."
John11:29 Ore pening' ninye ena-- nedumunye asioki alo enetii ninye;"
John11:30 amu epon eitu ebau Yesus engang'-- kake epon etii ene wueji netutumore Marta ninye."
John11:31 Akae-- ore pedol kulo Yudayoi-- lootii e nebo o ninye atua aji eilejilejita ninye-- Maria-- aajo etudumunye asioki nepuku-- nesuj ninje ninye ejo-- aajo eloito ninye enkurare-- peiye eishir te ina alo."
John11:32 Akae-- ore pebaia Maria ene wueji netii Yesus nedol ninye-- nebatatakino nkejek enyena nejoki ninye: Laitoriani-- ten emutu itii iye ene-- anaata eitu ee olalashe lai."
