John11:33 Akae-- ore pedol Yesus ninye eishirita o Yudayoi looiturrurrokinote ninye eishirita-- negoro ninye naleng' tʼolmumua neitang'aing'ai kion--"
John11:34 nejo: Kaji itipika ninye? Nejoki si ninje: Laitoriani-- wou-- ng'orai!"
John11:35 Neishir Yesus ilkiyo.
John11:36 Akae-- nejo Yudayoi: Eng'orai-- eneikuna teni enyor ninye."
John11:37 Nejo ematua enye: Eitu eidim ele lotabolo ngonyek olmodooni atomitiki ele-- pemee?"
John11:38 Akae-- neitoki Yesus agoro te kion nebaia enkurare. Nera engapunet netipikaki osoit shumata enye."
John11:39 Nejo Yesus: Entudumutu osoit! Nejoki Marta-- enganashe olotua-- ninye: Laitoriani-- eng'u taata-- amu engolong' e ong'wan etii."
John11:40 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Eitu aajoki iye-- ajo teni ilairuk-- niladol enkitook Engai?"
John11:41 Akae-- nedumu ninje osoit. Neapaki Yesus ngonyek shumata nejo: Papa-- aaliki iye ashe-- tiaraki nikitoning'o."
John11:42 Nayolo nanu-- ajo kining' oshi; kake atejo tʼolbae lʼesiamu namanita-- peiye eiruk-- aajo iye likirriua."
John11:43 Ore peidip atejo kuna-- nedar tʼoltoilo kitok: Lasaros-- tupuku boo!"
John11:44 Nepuku olotua eena nkejek o ngaik too rasheta enukare-- neirina engomom enye tʼerashet. Nejoki Yesus ninje: Entalaku ninye-- enjoo ninye elo."
John11:45 Akae-- neiruk ninye ilkumok too Yudayoi looetuo enetii Maria nedol enaitobira ninye."
John11:46 Nepuo ematua enye enetii Ilfarisayoi neliki ninje enaitobira Yesus.
John11:47 Akae-- neiturrur laidasak kituak o Ilfarisayoi enkigwena nejo: Kaji kinko? Amu eitobir ele tung'ani ilponot kumok."
John11:48 Teni kipal ninye nji-- nepuo aairuk pookin ninye-- nepuo aapuonu Romayoi neoru yook olosho o olorere."
John11:49 Nejoki Kayafas-- obo lenye lora olaidasani kitok te ilo ari-- ninje: Miyololo ndai toki;"
John11:50 nimimbirribirrirri-- aajo enaikash too yook-- teni elae oltung'ani obo tʼolbae lʼolorere-- pemeimin olorere olulung'a."
John11:51 Eitu elimu ninye ena te kion-- kake tiaraki nara olaidasani kitok te ilo ari-- neitayolou-- ajo elae Yesus tʼolbae lʼolorere--"
John11:52 neme tʼolbae lʼolorere ake-- kake peiturrur si nkera Engai naaisardaka-- peaku nabo."
John11:53 Akae-- ore eiter te ina olong'-- neigwena-- petum aataar metua."
John11:54 Akae-- neitu eitoki aibalunye Yesus kion tiatua Yudayoi-- kake eshomo ewueji netaaniki ang'ata metabaiki engang' naji Efrem-- neton te ina alo te nebo o laiteng'enuok lenyena."
John11:55 Netaanu pasaka oo Yudayoi neilep aapuo ilkumok Yerusalem-- eing'ua olosho-- epon eitu eaku pasaka-- peiye eisuj aten."
John11:56 Akae-- neing'oru ninje Yesus nejokino eitashe tʼengaji sinyati: Ijojo aa ndai-- melotu ninye tukul ngolong'i kituak?"
John11:57 Neishooitie laidasak kituak o Ilfarisayoi nkitanapat-- ajo teni eyolou oltung'ani enetii ninye-- njelotu alimu-- petum aaibung'a ninye."
John12:1 Akae-- ore eng'or ngolong'i ile-- epon eitu ebau pasaka-- nelotu Yesus Betania-- enetii Lasaros loitopiwuo Yesus too lootuata."
John12:2 Akae-- neitobiraki ninje ninye endaata te ina alo-- neisyaisho Marta; nera Lasaros obo too kulo loototonitio tʼendaata te nebo o ninye."
John12:3 Akae-- neibung' Maria entulet eilata narropil nara sidai naleng' negol enkinyang'a-- neelie Yesus nkejek nejut nkejek enyena too lpapit lenyena: neigany engaji erropili eilata."
John12:4 Nejo Yudas Iskariotes-- obo too laiteng'enuok lenyena-- loyeu neitarasaa ninye:"
John12:5 Ainyo peitu emiri ena ilata too denaria iip uni-- peishori laisinak?"
John12:6 Etejo ena-- me tiaraki naing'urrie ninye laisinak-- kake tiaraki nara olapurroni naa ninye olaibung'ani lʼenjumet oo ngoshola-- nenap natanang'akaki atua."
John12:7 Akae-- nejo Yesus: Entapal ninye-- amu etaa ena-- peaku nʼengolong' enukare ai;"
John12:8 amu iatata laisinak oshi tiatua ndai-- kake mikiatata nanu oshi."
John12:9 Akae-- neyolou esiamu kitok too Yudayoi-- aajo etii ina alo-- nepuonu me tʼolbae le Yesus ake-- kake peiye edol Lasaros loitopiwuo ninye tiatua lootuata."
John12:10 Neigwena laidasak kituak-- peiye ear baiki Lasaros metua--"
John12:11 amu eshomo tʼolbae lenye ilkumok tiatua Yudayoi neiruk Yesus.
John12:12 Eewuo tʼengai olong' esiamu kitok ngolong'i kituak; ore pening' ninje-- aajo elotu Yesus Yerusalem--"
John12:13 neibung' ilng'osil loo ltuka neipung' aapuo aanang'are ninye nedar: Hosiana! Njeitadarari ololotu tʼengarna Olaitoriani o olkarsis le Israel!
John12:14 Ore petum Yesus enkurrarru-- neilepaki ninye-- anaa petisiraki:"
John12:15 Miureisho-- nairo Sion-- ng'orai-- elotu olkarsis lino-- eton te shumata enkurrarru osikiria."
John12:16 Neitu eyolou laiteng'enuok lenyena tʼenkata elukunya kuna-- kake ore eitaaki Yesus kitok-- nedamu ninje te ina kata-- aajo kuna etisirakaki ninye naa kuna eitobirakitia ninje ninye."
John12:17 Akae-- neijakenu esiamu natii e nebo o ninye te ina kata naipoto Lasaros tʼenkurare neitopiu ninye too lootuata."
John12:18 Onaa etutumore esiamu ninye-- amu etoning'o-- aajo eitobira ninye ele ponoto."
John12:19 Akae-- nejokino Ilfarisayoi: Idolitata-- aajo mindimumu toki; eng'orai-- esuj olmaa pookin ninye."
John12:20 Netii Ilgrikini looje too kulo looileputua-- pepuo aasaisho too ngolong'i kituak;"
John12:21 akae-- nepuonu kulo enetii Filipos le Betsaida e Galilaya-- nesai nejo: Laitoriani-- kiyeu nikidol Yesus."
John12:22 Nelotu Filipos nejoki Andreas-- nepuonu Andreas o Filipos nejoki Yesus."
John12:23 Nealiki Yesus ninje nejo: Etabaua enkata-- peitaai Enkerai oltung'ani kitok."
John12:24 Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Teni medoiki embeu engano atua enkop nee-- nebik ninye openy ake; kake teni ee-- neiu ilmomo kumok."
John12:25 Olonyor empuan enye-- neiminye ninye; naa oloiba empuan tiatua ele maa-- nelarripoki ninye atua empuan nemeiting'."
John12:26 Teni eyeu naaisyayaki oltung'ani-- njaasuj ninye nanu; ore enatii nanu-- elatii ina alo baiki olaisyayani lai; olaaisyayaki nanu-- neitaa Papa ninye kitok."
John12:27 Etung'uyane taata Olmumua lai. Naa kainyo ajo? Papa-- ntopuaki te ina kata! Kake aewuo te ina atua ena kata."
John12:28 Papa-- ntaa engarna ino kitok! Akae-- nelotu oltoilo oing'ua shumata: Aidipa aitaa kitok naitoki alaitaa kitok."
John12:29 Akae-- nejo esiamu naitashe te ine nening' kuna: Etaa enkikurrukurroto. Nejo ilkulekai: Olmalaika oirorie ninye."
John12:30 Nealu Yesus nejo: Me tʼolbae lai etaa ele toilo-- kake tʼolbae linyi."
John12:31 Etii taata enkigwena ele maa; eiturrakini taata olkitok lʼele maa boo.
John12:32 Ore nanu-- teni aapuni tʼena kop-- nalayetu pookin enatii nanu."
John12:33 Kake etejo kuna-- peitayolo ke ti aa kea elae."
John12:34 Akae-- nealiki ninye esiamu: Kitoning'o yook tiatua nkitanapat-- aajo ebik Kristos nkatan pookin; naa kaji inko teni ijo iye: Meata kata nemeapuni Enkerai oltung'ani? Kang'ai ina kerai oltung'ani?"
John12:35 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Epon etii enkata kinyi enkilang'et empolos inyi. Entilimanata tʼena kata niatata enkilang'et-- pemelus ndai enaimin. Ololimana tiatua enaimin-- nemeyolo enelo."
John12:36 Ore tʼena kata niatata enkilang'et-- eruko enkilang'et-- pitumutumu aataa nkera enkilang'et."
John12:37 Etolimuo Yesus kuna nelo neisudori too ninje. Ore peidipa aitobira kulo ponot kumok nji tʼengomom enye-- neitu eiruk ninje ninye--"
John12:38 pebaia ororei lʼolayolouni Yesaya otejo: Kang'ai oiruk enkinosunoto ang'; Neitalioio engaina Olaitoriani te ng'ai?
John12:39 Onaa eitu eidim ninje aairuko-- amu einyaaka ajo Yesaya:"
John12:40 Eitaa ninye modook ngonyek enye neigen iltauja lenye-- pemedolisho too ngonyek nemeyolou too ltauja neibelekenya-- paishiunye ninje."
John12:41 Etejo kuna Yesaya-- tiaraki natadua enkitook enye nelimu mbaak enyena."
John12:42 Neijia eiruko baiki ilkumok too lkituak ninye: kake eitu eibalu ninje tʼolbae loo Lfarisayoi-- pemeitaini ninje tʼenkisot;"
John12:43 amu etonyorra ninje enkitook oo ltung'anak nelang' enkitook Engai.
John12:44 Nedar Yesus nejo: Olaairuk nanu-- maairuk nanu-- kake eiruk olaairriua nanu;"
John12:45 olaaing'oraa nanu-- neing'oraa olaairriua nanu."
John12:46 Aewuo nanu-- enkilang'et-- atua olmaa-- peiye mebik pookin laairuk nanu tiatua enaimin."
John12:47 Oloning' rorei lainei nemeibung' ninje-- maigwenaki nanu ninye; amu eitu alotu nanu-- paigwenaki olmaa-- kake paitopok olmaa."
John12:48 Olaaiturraa nanu nemeng'amu rorei lainei-- neata oloigwenaki ninye; neigwenaki ele rorei latolimuo nanu ninye tʼengolong' enkiting'oto."
John12:49 Amu eitu alimu nanu te kion-- kake Papa laairriua nanu-- ninye laaishoo enkitanapata enairorie o enalimunye."
John12:50 Nayolo-- ajo era enkitanapata enye empuan nemeiting'; akae-- enalimu nanu-- nalimu neijia anaa paatiaka Papa."
John13:1 Ore eitu eaku ngolong'i kituak e pasaka-- neyolou Yesus-- ajo etabaua enkata enye-- peiye eing'ua ele maa alo enetii Menye-- anaa petonyorra ilkulenyena tiatua olmaa-- nenyor metabaiki enkiting'oto."
John13:2 Ore peidipai endaata-- eidipa aishoo satan atua oltau le Yudas le Simon-- Iskariotes-- peitarasaa ninye--"
John13:3 eyolo-- ajo eishoo Menye ninye pookin atua ngaik-- naa ajo eing'ua Engai neitoki alo enetii Engai--"
John13:4 neinyototo tʼendaata neitau ilkilani lenyena neibung' erashet nerretenye empolos enye;
John13:5 nebukoki engare atua embongo neiter aisuj nkejek oo laiteng'enuok neitoi tʼerashet naterretenare ninye.
John13:6 Akae-- nelotu enetii Simon Petros; nejoki ilo ninye: Laitoriani-- ke iye likisuj nkejek?"
John13:7 Nealiki Yesus nejoki ninye: Ore enaitobirita nanu-- miyolo iye taata; kake ilayolou tekurum oo kuna."
John13:8 Nejoki Petros ninye: meaku nkatan pookin tukul-- pisuj iye nkejek ainei. Nejoki Yesus ninye: Teni maaisuj nanu iye-- miata enkidikidikoto o nanu."
John13:9 Nejoki Simon Petros ninye: Laitoriani-- me nkejek ainei ake-- kake baiki ngaik o elukunya."
John13:10 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Oloisujaki-- meaku peisuji neme nkejek ake-- amu eikishaan abaraki; inkishaanana ndai-- kake me pookin."
John13:11 Amu etayolo ninye oloitarasaa ninye; onaa etejo: Minkishaanana ndai pookin.
John13:12 Akae-- ore peidip aisuja nkejek enye-- neitoki aibung' ilkilani lenyena neton nejoki ninje: Iyololo enataasaka ndai?"
John13:13 Kimpotipoto ndai: Olaiteng'enani o Olaitoriani-- nijojo sidai-- amu ara:"
John13:14 Akae-- ore paisuja nanu-- Olaitoriani o Olaiteng'enani-- nkejek inyi-- meata kata nimisujaroro si ndai nkejek."
John13:15 Amu aidipa aishoo ndai enkiteng'enet-- pinkoko neijia anaa paikunaka nanu ndai."
John13:16 Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Me kitok olaisyayani nelang' Olaitoriani lenye nemera olairriwani kitok nelang' oloirriwaiye ninye."
John13:17 Teni iyololo kuna-- irara teshi-- teni intobiribiri kuna."
John13:18 Maimaki ndai pookin: Ayolo nanu lategelua; kake pebaia esirata: Olonya olmkate lai-- aataapaka entutunyo enye."
John13:19 Ore eba taata aliki ndai-- eitu eaku ena-- pitumutumu aairuko-- teni eaku-- ajo ara nanu."
John13:20 Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Olong'amu olairriwaa nanu-- naang'amu nanu; olaang'amu nanu-- neng'amu olaairriua."
John13:21 Ore peidip atejo Yesus kuna-- neng'uyana tʼolmumua neijakenu nejo: Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Aalaitarasaa obo linyi."
John13:22 Neing'oraro laiteng'enuok tʼempolos enye neing'arrirro aajo ang'ai eimaki.
John13:23 Neaku etonita obo too laiteng'enuok lenyena tʼengalo olgoo le Yesus-- nenyor Yesus ninye."
John13:24 Akae-- neroj Simon Petros ilo nejoki ninye: Tiaki-- kalo obo eimaka."
John13:25 Neurokino ninye olgoo le Yesus nejoki ninye: Laitoriani-- kang'ai ilo?"
John13:26 Akae-- nealu Yesus: Ilo lalo aitadoiki eonyoti naisho ninye. Akae-- neitadoiki eonyoti neisho Yudas le Simon-- Iskariotes."
John13:27 Ore tekurum eonyoti nejing' satan atua ninye. Akae-- nejoki Yesus ninye: Enintobir-- ntobira asioki!"
John13:28 Neitu eyolou ena o obo too kulo lootoni tʼendaata-- kainyo petiaka ninye ena."
John13:29 Etejo kulekai-- tiaraki nanapita Yudas enjumet oo ngoshola-- ajo etiaka Yesus ninye: Nyang'u enimikindim aatalaita too ngolong'i kituak-- arashu eisho laisinak toki."
John13:30 Akae-- ore peidip ninye atang'amu eonyoti-- nepuku nabokata. Naa kiarie."
John13:31 Akae-- ore pepuku ninye-- nejo Yesus: Eitaaki taata kitok Enkerai oltung'ani neitaai Engai kitok tiatua ninye."
John13:32 Teni eitaai Engai kitok tiatua ninye-- nelaitaa baiki Engai ninye kitok tiatua ninye openy-- neitaa ninye kitok nabokata."
John13:33 Nakera-- eng'or enkiti kata natii e nebo o ndai. Kipuopuo aaing'oru; naa anaa patiaka Yudayoi: Enalo nanu-- mindimidimi aaetu ndai-- najoki taata baiki ndai."
John13:34 Aisho ndai enkitanapata ng'ejuk-- pinyorrarra anaa patonyorra nanu ndai-- pinyorrarra si ndai."
John13:35 Te ina epuo aayolou pookin-- aajo irara laiteng'enuok lainei-- teni iatata enyorrata tʼempolos inyi."
John13:36 Nejoki Simon Petros ninye: Laitoriani-- kaji ilo? Nealiki Yesus ninye: Enalo nanu-- nimikindim taata atusuja-- kake kilasuj tekurum."
John13:37 Nejoki Petros ninye: Laitoriani-- ainyo pamaaidim atusuja iye taata nji? Ayeu naishooio empuan ai tʼolbae lino."
John13:38 Nealu Yesus: Kye-- injooio empuan ino tʼolbae lai? Japa-- japa-- aaliki iye: Meorito olkikusieki eitu kimiki kat uni."
John14:1 Nejoki ninye laiteng'enuok lenyena: Njoo neng'ayung'ayu iltauja linyi! Eruko Engai-- erukoki si nanu!"
John14:2 Etii engaji e Papa lai ntonat kumok; ten emutu metiu neijia-- anaata aliki ndai: Alo nanu-- paitobiraki ndai ewueji."
John14:3 Ore paidip ashomo naitobiraki ndai ewueji-- naitoki alotu nalarik ndai enatii nanu-- peiye ore enatii nanu-- nitiiti si ndai."
John14:4 Niyololo ndai enalo nanu niyololo baiki engoitoi.
John14:5 Nejoki Tomas ninye: Laitoriani-- mikiyolo enilo. Naa kaji kinko teni kiyolou engoitoi?"
John14:6 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Ara nanu engoitoi o esipata o empuan; melotu o obo enetii Papa neme te nanu.
John14:7 Ten emutu kiyololo nanu-- anaata iyololo si Papa lai. Iyololo ninye eba taata nidolitata ninye."
John14:8 Nejoki Filipos ninye: Laitoriani-- ntadua yook Papa-- nebaiki yook."
John14:9 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Atii enkata naba nji e nebo o ndai-- Filipos-- nimikiyololo nanu? Olaatadua nanu-- netadua Papa. Kaji inko teni ijo iye: Ntadua yook Papa?"
John14:10 Miruk iye-- ajo atii nanu atua Papa-- netii Papa atua nanu? Ore kulo rorei laliki nanu ndai-- maliki ndai te kion; kake Papa obik tiatua nanu-- neitobir nkyasin enyena."
John14:11 Erukoki nanu-- aajo atii nanu atua Papa-- netii Papa atua nanu; teni me neijia-- eruko tʼolbae loo kuna kyasin."
John14:12 Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Olaairuk nanu-- nelaitobir si ninye nkyasin naitobir nanu-- nelaitobir baiki nkituak naalang' kuna; amu alo enetii Papa;"
John14:13 ore eniomonunu lʼengarna ai-- nalaitobir ena-- peitaai kitok Papa tiatua Oinoti."
John14:14 Teni iomonunu entoki lʼengarna ai-- nalaitobir nanu."
John14:15 Teni kinyorrinyorro-- embung'a nkitanapat ainei!"
John14:16 Nayeu si nanu nasai Papa-- pelaisho ninye ndai olekai ailejilejani-- peiye etii e nebo o ndai nkatan pookin--"
John14:17 Olmumua lʼesipata lemeidim olmaa atang'amu-- amu medol nemeyolo ninye; iyololo ndai ninye-- amu ebik ninye te nebo o ndai netii atua ndai."
John14:18 Malaing'ua nanu ndai irara lokishin; alotu enitiiti.
John14:19 Eng'or enkiti kata-- namaaitoki adol olmaa-- kake kidolidolo ndai nanu-- amu aishiu nanu-- nipuopuo aaishiu si ndai."
John14:20 Nipuopuo aayolou te ina olong'-- aajo atii nanu atua Papa lai-- nitiiti ndai atua nanu o nanu atua ndai."
John14:21 Oloata nkitanapat ainei neibung' ninje-- nera ele olaanyor nanu; olaanyor nanu-- nenyorru Papa lai ninye-- nalanyor si nanu ninye nalaitayolou kion ninye."
John14:22 Nejoki Yudas ninye-- me Iskariotes: Laitoriani-- ketaa nyoo ena-- piyeu nintayolo kion yook neme olmaa?"
John14:23 Nealu Yesus nejoki ninye: Teni aanyor oltung'ani nelaibung' rorei lainei-- nelanyor Papa lai ninye-- nikipuonu enetii ninye nikipuo aaitobir entonata te ninye."
John14:24 Olemaanyor-- nemeibung rorei lainei; ore ororei lining'itoto-- mera olalai-- kake le Papa laairriua nanu."
John14:25 Atiaka ndai kuna-- epon atii e nebo o ndai."
John14:26 Kake ore olailejilejani-- Olmumua Sinyati-- lolairriu Papa Tengarna ai-- elaiteng'en ndai too pookin nelaitadamu ndai pookin natiaka ndai."
John14:27 Aing'uaiki ndai eseriani-- aisho ndai eseriani ai; maisho nanu ndai anaa peishoru olmaa. Njoo meng'aing'ayu iltauja linyi-- njoo meureisho."
John14:28 Itoning'o-- aajo atiaka ndai: Alo-- naitoki alotu enitiiti. Ten emutu kinyorrinyorro nanu-- anaata ing'idada-- tiaraki nalo enetii Papa; amu era Papa kitok naalang' nanu."
John14:29 Akae-- aidipa atiaki ndai-- epon eitu eaku-- pitumutumu aairuko-- teni eaku."
John14:30 Maitoki airorie ndai too nkumok-- amu elotu olkitok lʼele maa-- nemaataiye nanu toki;"
John14:31 kake peiye eyolou olmaa-- ajo anyor nanu Papa naitobir neijia anaa paaitanapa Papa: Enyoito-- maapeti aing'ua ene!"
John15:1 Ara nanu oljani lʼolmarua osipa nera Papa lai olaturoni.
John15:2 Ore olng'osila pookin liatua nanu lemeisho-- neitau ele; ore pookin loisho-- neikishaanye-- pepon aisho naleng'."
John15:3 Indipa ndai aaikishaana tʼolbae loo rorei latiaka ndai.
John15:4 Entobik tiatua nanu o nanu tiatua ndai. Neijia anaa pemeidim olng'osila atoishoi te kion-- teni mebik ninye tiatua oljani lʼolmarua-- neijia mindimidimi si ndai-- teni mibikibiki tiatua nanu."
John15:5 Ara nanu oljani lʼolmarua-- nirara ndai ilng'osil. Olobik tiatua nanu o nanu tiatua ninye-- neiu ele ilmomo kumok-- amu teni matii nanu-- nimindimidimi aaitobira toki."
John15:6 Olemebik tiatua nanu-- neiturrakini boo anaa olng'osila-- netoi-- neiturrur ninje nenang'aki atua enkima neiwuwu."
John15:7 Teni ibikibiki tiatua nanu-- nebik rorei lainei tiatua ndai-- ore pookin niyeuu niomonunu-- neitobirakini ndai."
John15:8 Eitaai Papa lai kitok te ina-- piiuu ilmomo kumok niakuku laiteng'enuok lainei."
John15:9 Neijia anaa paatonyorra Papa lai nanu-- neijia atonyorra si nanu ndai. Entobik tiatua enyorrata ai!"
John15:10 Teni imbung'ubung'u nkitanapat ainei-- nibikibiki tiatua enyorrata ai-- neijia anaa paibung'a nanu nkitanapat e Papa lai nabik tiatua enyorrata enye."
John15:11 Atiaka ndai kuna-- pebik eng'ida ai tiatua ndai nebaia eng'ida inyi."
John15:12 Nyena enkitanapata ai-- pinyorrarra anaa patonyorra nanu ndai."
John15:13 Metii Oloata enyorrata kitok nalang' ena naishooio oltung'ani oltau lenye tʼolbae loo ljorueta lenyena.
John15:14 Irara ndai iljorueta lainei-- teni intobiribiri enaitanap nanu ndai."
John15:15 Maitoki ajo-- irara ndai singan-- amu meyolo osinga entoki naitobir Olaitoriani lenye; aipoto ndai iljorueta-- amu pookin natoning'o te Papa lai aidipa aitayolo ndai."
John15:16 Me ndai likitegelutua nanu-- kake nanu otegelua ndai napik ndai-- pipuopuo aaiu ilmomo-- nebik ilmomo linyi-- peiye teni iomonunu Papa tʼengarna ai-- neisho ninye ndai."
John15:17 Kuna aitanap ndai-- pinyorrarra."
John15:18 Teni eibai olmaa ndai-- entayolo-- aajo aaitera aibai nanu-- epon meiba ndai."
John15:19 Ten emutu irara ndai lʼolmaa-- anaata enyor olmaa enenye; kake tiaraki nimirara lʼolmaa naa nanu otegelua ndai tʼolmaa-- onaa eiba olmaa ndai."
John15:20 Entadamutu ororei latiaka ndai: Metii osinga ora kitok nelang' Olaitoriani lenye. Ore aainyala ninje nanu-- nepuo aainyal baiki ndai; teni eibung'a rorei lainei-- nepuo aaibung' baiki kulinyi."
John15:21 Kake epuo aaitobiraki ndai kuna pookin tʼolbae lʼengarna ai; amu meyolo ninje ele laairriua nanu.
John15:22 Ten emutu eitu alotu nanu nairorie ninje-- anaata meata ninje enkitarruoto; kake meata ninje taata enalimu tʼolbae loo nkitarruot enye."
John15:23 Olaaibananu-- neiba baiki Papa lai."
John15:24 Ten emutu eitu aitobir nkitobirat tiatua ninje neitu eitobir olekai tung'ani o obo-- anaata meata ninje enkitarruoto; kake etadua ninje taata naaiba nanu o Papa lai."
John15:25 Kake peiye ebaia ororei lotisiraki tiatua nkitanapat enye: Aaibaitie pesho.
John15:26 Ore pelotu olailejilejani lalo airriwaki nanu ndai te Papa-- Olmumua lʼesipata-- lopuku te Papa-- nelaijakenu mbaak ainei--"
John15:27 nipuopuo aaijakenu si ndai-- tiaraki nitiiti e nebo o nanu neba tʼenkiterata."
John16:1 Atiaka ndai kuna-- pimirikaka."
John16:2 Nepuo aaitai ninje ndai tʼenkisot; kake ebau enkata-- pejo oltung'ani pookin oar ndai entuata-- ajo eisyayaki Engai."
John16:3 Nepuo aaitobir ninje kuna-- tiaraki nemeyolo Papa lai arashu nanu."
John16:4 Kake atiaka ndai kuna-- peiye-- teni elotu enkata-- pidamumu-- aajo atiaka ndai kuna; eitu aliki ndai kuna neba tʼenkiterata-- amu atii e nebo o ndai."
John16:5 Kake alo taata enetii olaairriua nanu-- nemetii o obo too ndai laaikilikwan: Kaji ilo?"
John16:6 Kake tiaraki natiaka ndai kuna-- neigany enkilishoto iltauja linyi."
John16:7 Kake aliki ndai esipata: Eaku too ndai-- teni alo nanu. Amu teni malo-- nemelotu olailejilejani enitiiti ndai; kake teni alo nanu-- nalairriwaki ninye ndai."
John16:8 Ore pelotu ninye-- neitayolo ninye olmaa mbaak enkitarruoto o nʼesupato o nʼenkigwena:"
John16:9 Mbaak enkitarruoto-- tiaraki nemaairuk nanu;"
John16:10 mbaak esupato-- tiaraki nalo enetii Papa nimikintokiki aadol nanu;"
John16:11 mbaak enkigwena-- tiaraki naigwenakini olkitok lʼele maa."
John16:12 Epon aata nkumok naliki ndai-- kake mindimidimi aatayolo taata."
John16:13 Kake teni elotu ninye-- Olmumua lʼesipata-- nerik ninye ndai atua esipata pookin; amu melalimu ninye te kion-- kake pookin naning' ninye-- nelalimu ninye-- neinosaki ndai mbaak naapuonu."
John16:14 Aalaitaa ninye kitok-- amu elang'amu naara nkun ainei-- neinosaki ndai."
John16:15 Ore pookin naata Papa-- nera nkun ainei. Onaa atejo: Elang'amu naara nkun ainei-- neinosaki ninye ndai."
John16:16 Eng'or peno-- nimikintokiki aadol nanu; neitoki ang'or peno-- nikidolidolo nanu-- amu alo enetii Papa."
John16:17 Akae-- nejokino ematua oo laiteng'enuok lenyena: Kainyo ena naliki ninye yook: Eng'or peno-- nimikintokiki aadol nanu; neitoki ang'or peno-- nikidolidolo nanu? o: Alo enetii Papa?"
John16:18 Akae-- nejo ninje: Kainyo ena najo ninye: peno? Mikiyolo enajoito."
John16:19 Neyolou-- ajo etayeutuo ninje neikilikwan ninye-- nejoki ninje: Inkilikwanaroro ndai ena tʼempolos inyi-- tiaraki natejo: Eng'or peno-- nimikintokiki aadol nanu; neitoki ang'or peno-- nikidolidolo nanu."
John16:20 Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Ipuopuo aaishir ndai nioshiosho enkiliyo-- nelang'ida olmaa; nepuoi aailishie ndai-- kake elo aala enkilishoto inyi aaku eng'ida."
John16:21 Teni eisho eng'oroyoni-- neata enkilishoto-- amu etabaua enkata enye; ore peidip atoiu enkerai-- nemeitoki adamu osina tʼolbae lʼeng'ida-- tiaraki natoikioki oltung'ani atua olmaa."
John16:22 Akae-- iatata ndai taata osina; kake aitoki aladol ndai-- nepuo aang'ida ltauja linyi-- nemetii o obo looru ndai eng'ida."
John16:23 Ore te ina olong' nimikipuopuo naikilikwan toki. Japa-- japa-- aliki ndai: Ore eniomonunu Papa lʼengarna ai-- nelaisho ninye ndai."
John16:24 Eitu iomonunu metabaiki taata toki lʼengarna ai. Entoomonutu-- nipuopuo aang'amu-- pebaia eng'ida inyi."
John16:25 Atiaka ndai kuna too loyoteni; ebau enkata namaitoki airorie ndai too loyoteni-- kake alainosaki ndai mbaak e Papa abaraki."
John16:26 Nipuopuo aaomonisho te ina olong' lʼengarna ai; majoki nanu ndai-- ajo alasai nanu Papa tʼolbae linyi;"
John16:27 amu enyor ndai Papa openy-- tiaraki nikitonyorra nanu nirukuruku-- aajo aewuo nanu aing'ua Engai."
John16:28 Atupukuo nanu te Papa nalotu atua olmaa; naitoki aing'ua olmaa nalo enetii Papa.
John16:29 Nejo laiteng'enuok lenyena: Ng'orai-- irorita taata tʼembarakinoto nimiro oloyote o obo."
John16:30 Kiyolo taata-- aajo iyolo pookin nemeaku te iye-- pikinkilikwan oltung'ani; onaa kiruk-- aajo iewuo ing'ua Engai."
John16:31 Nealiki Yesus ninje: Irukuruku taata?
John16:32 Eng'orai-- ebau enkata-- neidipa atabau-- pipuopuo aaisardakakino-- oltung'ani pookin ewueji enye-- niking'uang'ua nanu openy; kake matii openy ake-- amu etii Papa e nebo o nanu."
John16:33 Atiaka ndai kuna-- pitumutumu aata eseriani te nanu. Iatata osina tiatua olmaa; kake entagoluoto-- atigilua nanu olmaa."
John17:1 Eiroro Yesus kuna neapaki ngonyek enyena shumata nejo: Papa-- etabaua enkata. Ntaa kitok Oinoti lino-- pikintaa si ninye Oinoti kitok;"
John17:2 anaa pinjoo ninye engolon oo nkiri pookin-- peiye elaisho ninye pookin linjoo iye ninye-- empuan nemeiting'."
John17:3 Nera ena empuan nemeiting'-- pikiyolou iye ake-- Engai nasipa-- o Yesus Kristos lirriua."
John17:4 Aaitaa iye kitok tʼenkop naitahaia enkyas nikinjoo-- paitobir."
John17:5 Ore taata ntaaki iye nanu kitok-- Papa-- te iye tʼenkitook naata tʼengang' ino-- epon metii enkop."
John17:6 Aitayolo engarna ino iltung'anak likinjoo tiatua olmaa. Era ninje ilkulonono nikinjoo iye ninje-- neibung'a ninje rorei linono."
John17:7 Etayoloutuo ninje taata-- aajo ore pookin nikinjoo neing'ua enitii;"
John17:8 amu aishoo nanu ninje rorei likinjoo-- neng'amu si ninje neyolou tʼesipata-- aajo aewuo aing'ua engang' ino-- neiruk-- aajo iye likirriua."
John17:9 Asayaki nanu ninje; masayaki nanu olmaa-- kake kulo likinjoo; amu era ninje ilkulonono."
John17:10 Ore pookin naarankunainei-- naa nkunonono-- o naara nkunonono-- naa nkunainei-- naaitaai nanu kitok tiatua ninje."
John17:11 Namaitoki atii nanu atua olmaa; kake etii kulo atua olmaa-- nalotu nanu enitii iye. Papa sinyati-- torripo tʼengarna ino kulo likinjoo-- peiye eaku nabo anaa yook."
John17:12 Ore atii e nebo o ninje-- atorripo nanu ninje tʼengarna ino-- kulo likinjoo-- narrip ninje-- neitu eimin o obo too ninje-- neme enkerai enkiminata-- peiye ebaia esirata."
John17:13 Nalotu taata enitii nalimu kuna tiatua olmaa-- peiye ebaia eng'ida ai tiatua ninje oopeny."
John17:14 Aishoo nanu ninje rorei linono-- neibaiye olmaa ninje-- tiaraki nemera lʼolmaa-- neijia ana pamara si nanu lʼolmaa."
John17:15 Masaisho-- pintung'ua ninje olmaa-- kake pirrip ninje tʼoltorrono."
John17:16 Mera ninje lʼolmaa-- neijia anaa pamara lʼolmaa."
John17:17 Ntaa ninje sinyat tiatua esipata; nera ororei lino esipata.
John17:18 Anaa pikirriua nanu atua olmaa-- neijia airriwaki si nanu ninje atua olmaa."
John17:19 Nasinyaa nanu kion tʼolbae lenye-- peiye esinyari si ninje tiatua esipata."
John17:20 Me ninje ake asayaki-- kake baiki kulo laapuo aairuk nanu tʼolbae loo rorei lenye--"
John17:21 peaku pookin nabo-- anaa iye-- Papa-- tiatua nanu o nanu tiatua iye-- petii si ninje atua yook-- peiruk olmaa ajo iye likirriua."
John17:22 Ore enkitook nikinjoo nanu aidipa aishoo ninje-- peaku nabo anaa pikira yook nabo;"
John17:23 natii nanu atua ninje nitii iye atua nanu-- petum ninje aataa baiarot tiatua nabo-- peyolou olmaa-- ajo iye likirriua ninyorru ninje anaa pikitonyorra nanu."
John17:24 Papa-- ayeu netii ene wueji natii nanu kulo likinjoo e nebo o nanu-- pedol ninje enkitook ai nikinjoo-- amu kitonyorra eton eitu euni olmaa."
John17:25 Papa supat-- eitu kiyolou olmaa-- kake aatayolo nanu iye-- neyolo si kulo-- aajo iye likirriua."
John17:26 Naitayolo ninje engarna ino naitoki aitayolo-- peiye etii enyorrata nikitonyorrie nanu atua ninje-- natii si nanu atua ninje."
John18:1 Ore peidip Yesus atejo kuna-- nepuku ninye o laiteng'enuok lenyena aapuo lido kekun lʼengare Kidron-- netii ina alo enkuruma-- nejing' atua ninye o laiteng'enuok lenyena."
John18:2 Neyolo baiki Yudas loitarasaiye ninye ine wueji-- amu eiturrurrokino Yesus o laiteng'enuok lenyena aigil kumok ina alo."
John18:3 Akae-- neibung' Yudas oltim loo sikerin o laisyayak ooing'ua laidasak kituak o Ilfarisayoi nelotu ina alo too ndiararani o taai o nareta."
John18:4 Akae-- ore peyolou Yesus pookin naaku te ninye-- nepuku ninye nejoki ninje: Ang'ai ing'oruru?"
John18:5 Nealiki ninje ninye: Yesus le Nasaret. Nejoki Yesus ninje: Nanu ilo! Neitashe baiki Yudas loitarasaiye ninye te nebo o ninje.
John18:6 Akae-- ore pejoki Yesus ninje: Nanu ilo! nerrinyo ninje kurum nebatatakino enkop."
John18:7 Akae-- neitoki aikilikwan ninje: Ang'ai ing'oruru? Nejo si ninje: Yesus le Nasaret."
John18:8 Nealu Yesus: Atiaka ndai-- ajo nanu ilo. Akae-- teni king'oruru nanu-- entung'ai kulo-- pepuo--"
John18:9 peiye ebaia ororei lotejo ninye: Eitu aiminye o obo too kulo likinjoo.
John18:10 Akae-- neata Simon Petros olalem neshitu ninye neosh olaisyayani lʼolaidasani kitok nedung' enkiyok enye e tatene-- neji engarna olaisyayani Malkos."
John18:11 Akae-- nejoki Yesus Petros: Nyaaki olalem enjashur. Keaku-- pamaok enkwaru naaishoo Papa?"
John18:12 Akae-- neibung' oltim loo sikerin o olkigeluni o laisyayak loo Yudayoi Yesus neen ninye"
John18:13 neng'as aarik enetii Anas; amu era ninye olaputani le Kayafas lora olaidasani kitok le ilo ari.
John18:14 Nera Kayafas olotiaka Yudayoi-- ajo enaikash-- teni ee oltung'ani obo tʼolbae lʼolorere."
John18:15 Nesuj Simon Petros o olekai aiteng'enuoni Yesus. Neyoloi ilo aiteng'enuoni tʼolaidasani kitok-- nejing' ninye te nebo o Yesus atua engang' olaidasani kitok."
John18:16 Neitashe Petros tʼengalo kutukaji ti aulo. Akae-- nepuku olekai aiteng'enuoni oyoloi tʼolaidasani kitok neirorie engarriponi e kutukaji neriku Petros atua."
John18:17 Akae-- nejoki engaisyayani nara engarriponi e kutukaji Petros: Mira iye loo laiteng'enuok lʼele tung'ani? Nejo ninye: Me nanu!"
John18:18 Neitashe singan o laisyayak ooinua enkima oo nkuk-- amu etii enkirobi-- neij ninje enkima; netii si ninye Petros e nebo o ninje neitashe-- eijito enkima."
John18:19 Akae-- neikilikwan olaidasani kitok Yesus mbaak oo laiteng'enuok lenyena o mbaak enkiteng'enare enye."
John18:20 Nealiki Yesus ninye: Atabaraka nanu airorie olmaa; aiteng'enishe oshi tiatua engaji naiteng'enareki o tiatua engaji sinyati-- eneiturrurrokino Yudayoi pookin-- neitu alimu toki tʼemikio."
John18:21 Ainyo pikinkilikwan nanu? Nkilikwana lootoning'o ainyo atiaka ninje; ng'orai-- eyolo ninje natejo nanu."
John18:22 Ore peiro ninye kuna-- neosh obo too laisyayak ooitasheikitio Yesus tʼendap nejo: Ke nji ialiki olaidasani kitok?"
John18:23 Nealiki Yesus ninye: Teni airoro torrono-- njakenu enara torrono; teni aa sidai-- ainyo pikiosh?"
John18:24 Akae-- neirriwaki Anas ninye eena Kayafas-- olaidasani kitok."
John18:25 Netii Simon Petros eitashe eijito enkima. Akae-- nejoki ninje ninye: Mira si iye loo laiteng'enuok lenyena? Nemiki ninye nejo: Me nanu."
John18:26 Nejo obo loo singan lʼolaidasani kitok lʼenkishomi olotudung'o Petros enkiyok: Keitu aadol nanu iye tʼenkuruma te nebo o ninye?
John18:27 Akae-- neitoki amiki Petros-- neorito nabokata olkikusieki."
John18:28 Akae-- nerik ninje Yesus eing'ua Kayafas metabaiki engaji enkigwena. Nekenyu. Eitu ejing' ninje oopeny engaji enkigwena-- pemeidurukieki ninje-- kake peng'as aanya pasaka."
John18:29 Akae-- neipung'u Pilatos boo nejo: Kaa kitang'oroto iautua tʼele tung'ani?"
John18:30 Nealu nejoki ninje ninye: Ten emutu mera ele oloitobir entorroni-- anaata eitu kintarasaki iye ninye."
John18:31 Akae-- nejoki Pilatos ninje: Embung'a ndai ninye-- engwenakiti ninye too nkitanapat inyi. Nejoki Yudayoi ninye: Meaku too yook-- pikiar oltung'ani o obo metua."
John18:32 Pebaia ororei le Yesus otejo-- peitayolou ke ti aa kea elae."
John18:33 Akae-- neitoki ajing' Pilatos atua engaji enkigwena neipot Yesus nejoki ninye: Ira iye olkarsis loo Yudayoi"
John18:34 Nealu Yesus: Itolimuo ena maa kion openy arashu kitiakitia kulekai mbaak ainei?
John18:35 Nealu Pilatos: Kara nanu Oyudayos? Olorere lino o laidasak kituak laaitarasakitia. Kainyo itaasa?
John18:36 Nealu Yesus: Mera enkarsishu ai nʼele maa; ten emutu era enkarsishu ai nʼele maa-- anaata aamitoo laisyayak lainei-- pamaaitarasakini Yudayoi; kake ore taata mera enkarsishu ai nʼene."
John18:37 Akae-- nejoki Pilatos ninye: Ira naa iye olkarsis? Nealu Yesus: Itejo iye-- ajo ara olkarsis. Aatoiwuoki nanu tʼolbae le ina-- naa tʼolbae le ina aewuo atua olmaa-- paijakenoki esipata; ore pookin loora lʼesipata-- nening' oltoilo lai."
John18:38 Nejoki Pilatos ninye: Kainyo nara esipata? Ore peidip atejo ena-- neitoki aipung'oki Yudayoi nejoki ninje: Eitu atum nanu enkitang'oroto o nabo te ninye."
John18:39 Kake etii orregie too ndai-- palaaki nanu ndai oltung'ani obo te pasaka. Akae; iyeuu nalaaki ndai olkarsis loo Yudayoi?"
John18:40 Akae-- neitoki aadar nejo: Me ilo-- kake Barabas! Nera Barabas olaisimani."
John19:1 Akae-- neibung' Pilatos Yesus near too nkeenda."
John19:2 Neshetu sikerin olmarisian loo lkikarreta neishopoki ninye elukunya-- neishopoki ninye olkila odo"
John19:3 nejo: Supai-- lekarsis loo Yudayoi! near ninye too ndapi."
John19:4 Neitoki aipung'oki Pilatos boo nejoki ninje: Eng'orai-- arikoki ndai ninye te boo-- piyolouu-- aajo matum enkitang'oroto o nabo te ninye."
John19:5 Akae-- nepuku Yesus boo-- oishopito olmarisian loo lkikarreta o olkila odo. Nejoki ninye ninje: Eng'orai ele tung'ani!"
John19:6 Akae-- ore pedol laidasak kituak o laisyayak ninye-- nedar nejo: Tooshoki esalaba! Tooshoki esalaba! Nejoki Pilatos ninje: Embung'a ndai ninye-- entooshokiti esalaba; amu matum nanu enkitang'oroto te ninye."
John19:7 Nealiki Yudayoi ninye: Kiata yook nkitanapat-- ore too nkitanapat meata kata nemee ninye; amu eitaa kion Enkerai Engai."
John19:8 Akae-- ore pening' Pilatos ele rorei-- nepon aureisho--"
John19:9 neitoki ajing' engaji enkigwena nejoki Yesus: Kaji ing'ua iye? Neitu ealiki Yesus ninye ororei.
John19:10 Akae-- nejoki Pilatos ninye: Mikirorie? Miyolo-- ajo aata engolon naalakunye iye o engolon naaoshokinye iye esalaba?"
John19:11 Nealu Yesus: Anaata miata engolon e toki te nanu-- ten emutu eitu kinjori ninye te shumata; onaa olaaitarasaka nanu iye-- neata ninye enkitarruoto nalang'."
John19:12 Ore eiter te ina kata neing'oru Pilatos eneiko-- pelaku ninye. Kake nedar Yudayoi nejo: Teni ilaku ele-- nimira oljore le kaisar; ore pookin loitaa kion olkarsis-- nemen kaisar."
John19:13 Ore pening' Pilatos kulo rorei-- nerik ninye Yesus boo neton te shumata olorika lʼenkigwena tʼewueji neji „Enesipa oo soito“-- tʼenkutuk oo Lhebrayoi Gabata."
John19:14 Neaku enkitobirakinore e pasaka-- nera enkata anaa esaa ile. Nejoki ninye Yudayoi: Eng'orai-- era ele olkarsis linyi!"
John19:15 Akae-- nedar kulo: Minye-- minye ninye! Tooshoki ninye esalaba! Nejoki Pilatos ninje: kaoshoki olkarsis linyi esalaba? Nealiki laidasak kituak: Mikiata olkarsis-- neme kaisar ake."
John19:16 Akae-- neitarasaki te ina kata ninye ninje-- peoshokini ninye esalaba. Akae-- neibung' ninje nerik Yesus;"
John19:17 enapita ninye esalaba enye nelo metabaiki ewueji neji Emborbor-- ore tʼenkutuk oo Lhebrayoi Golgota."
John19:18 Neoshoki ninje ninye esalaba te ina alo o ilkulekai aare te nebo o ninye-- too mbat pokira are-- netii Yesus tʼempolos."
John19:19 Nesir Pilatos esirata nepik shumata esalaba; etisiraki: Yesus le Nasaret-- olkarsis loo Yudayoi."
John19:20 Akae-- neisoma ilkumok loo Yudayoi ena sirata-- amu etaaniki ene wueji netooshokinyeki Yesus esalaba engang'. Etisiraki tʼenkutuk oo Lhebrayoi o noo Romayoi o noo Lgrikini."
John19:21 Akae-- nejoki laidasak kituak loo Yudayoi Pilatos: Misir: Olkarsis loo Yudayoi-- kake ajo etejo ilo: Ara olkarsis loo Yudayoi."
John19:22 Nealu Pilatos: Enaidipa atisira-- atisira."
John19:23 Akae-- ore peidip isikerin aatooshokiti esalaba-- neibung' ninje ilkilani lenyena neitaa matuan ong'wan-- peata osikeri pookin ematua enye-- baiki emekiti. Nemeripa ena mekiti-- esheta tukul eiter te shumata."
John19:24 Akae-- nejokino ninje: Mikipolos ninye-- kake matooshokiti olenkukuo-- anake eaku en e ng'ai? pebaia esirata najo: Etoorikinote ninje ilkilani lainei tʼempolos enye neoshoki olenkukuo emekiti ai. Akae-- neitobir isikerin kuna."
John19:25 Neitashe tʼengalo esalaba e Yesus ng'otonye enye o enganashe e ng'otonye enye-- Maria-- eng'oroyoni e Kleopas-- o Maria Magdalena."
John19:26 Akae-- ore pedol Yesus ng'otonye o olaiteng'enuoni otonyorra-- eitasheikinore-- nejoki ninye ng'otonye: Nang'oroyoni-- ng'orai-- enkerai ino!"
John19:27 Tekurum nejoki olaiteng'enuoni: Ng'orai-- ng'utunyi ino! Ore eiter te ina kata nerik ele aiteng'enuoni ninye engang' enye."
John19:28 Ore tekurum ena etayolouo Yesus-- ajo eidipate pookin-- pebaia esirata-- nejo: Aata enkure!"
John19:29 Netii ina alo enaret nabore engare olodua. Akae-- neigany ninje enjutet engare olodua nepik shumata enjata neaki ninye alo enkutuk."
John19:30 Ore peidip Yesus atang'amu engare olodua-- nejo: Eidipe! neirrugie elukunya nedung'o tau."
John19:31 Akae-- tiaraki nara engolong' enkitobirakinore-- pemebik iseseni te shumata esalaba tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki-- nesai Yudayoi Pilatos-- pegili nkejek enye neitadouni."
John19:32 Akae-- nepuonu sikerin negil nkejek ol elukunya o ole are lootooshokoki esalaba te nebo o ninye."
John19:33 Ore pebaiki ninje Yesus-- nedol-- aajo eidipa atua-- neitu egil ninye nkejek--"
John19:34 kake etaremo obo too sikerin ninye eluboto tʼempere-- nepuku nabokata olpile."
John19:35 Ore olotadua ena-- neijakenu-- nesipa enjakenishu enye; neyolo ilo-- ajo elimu enasipa-- pitumutumu si ndai aairuko."
John19:36 Amu etaa kuna-- pebaia esirata: Megili oloito lenye."
John19:37 Neitoki ajo engai sirata: Epuo aaing'oraa lotaremo ninje.
John19:38 Ore peidipai kuna nesai Yosef le Arimatia Pilatos-- nera ninye olaiteng'enuoni le Yesus tʼemikio tʼolbae lʼenkuretishu oo Yudayoi-- peitai osesen le Yesus. Neisho Pilatos ninye meitai. Akae-- nelotu neitau osesen lenye."
John19:39 Nelotu baiki Nikodemos oewuo kiarie enetii ninye-- enapita enkitushulata oo ilat naarropil nijo ratilini iip."
John19:40 Akae-- neitadou ninje osesen le Yesus neen too rasheta naaibor te nebo o ilat naarropil anaa petiu tʼorregie lʼenukare oo Yudayoi."
John19:41 Netii ine wueji netooshokinyeki esalaba enkuruma-- netii atua enkuruma enkurare ng'ejuk-- neitu epiki aikata oltung'ani atua."
John19:42 Akae-- nepik ninje Yesus atua tʼolbae lʼengolong' enkitobirakinore oo Yudayoi-- amu etaana enkurare."
John20:1 Ore tʼengolong' elukunya enjuma nelotu Maria Magdalena enasirie-- epon emisimis-- enkurare-- nedol osoit eitaiyoki tʼenkurare."
John20:2 Akae-- nekwet nelo enetii Simon Petros o olekai aiteng'enuoni otonyorra Yesus-- nejoki ninje: Eitautuo ninje Olaitoriani tʼenkurare nimikiyolo yook enetipika ninje ninye."
John20:3 Akae-- nepuku Petros o olekai aiteng'enuoni neibung' engoitoi aapuo enkurare."
John20:4 Nekwet pokira are te nebo-- nekwet olekai aiteng'enuoni asioio nelang' Petros neiter abaia enkurare--"
John20:5 neirrugo arum-- nedol rasheta naaibor eper-- kake epon eitu ejing'."
John20:6 Akae-- nelotu baiki Simon Petros-- esujita ninye-- nejing' atua enkurare-- nedol rasheta naaibor eper"
John20:7 o erashet nairinyeki elukunya enye neitu eper te nebo o nkulie rasheta-- kake te bata-- egila tʼewueji enye openy."
John20:8 Akae-- nejing' te ina kata baiki olekai aiteng'enuoni lotabaiye aiter enkurare nedol neiruk;"
John20:9 amu epon eitu eyolou esirata-- aajo meata kata nemepiu ninye tiatua lootuata."
John20:10 Akae-- neitoki aapuo laiteng'enuok ngang'itie enye."
John20:11 Neitashe Maria tʼengalo enkurare te boo-- eishirita. Ore eishirita nji-- neirrugo arum atua enkurare--"
John20:12 nedol ilmalaikan aare lootoni eishopito ilkilani ooibor-- obo lukunya-- olekai nkejek te ine wueji neirragie osesen le Yesus."
John20:13 Nejoki ninje ninye: Nang'oroyoni-- ainyo pinjir? Nejoki ninye ninje: Etudumutua Olaitoriani lai namayolo enetipika ninye."
John20:14 Ore ejoito kuna-- nenang' silig nedol Yesus eitashe-- neitu eyolou-- ajo era Yesus."
John20:15 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Nang'oroyoni-- ainyo pinjir? Ang'ai ing'oru? Nejo ninye anai olaitobirani lʼenkuruma nejoki ninye: Laitoriani-- ten aa iye lotudumua ninye-- akae-- tiakaki enitipika-- paladumu nanu ninye."
John20:16 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Maria! Neibelekenya ninye nejoki ninye tʼenkutuk oo Lhebrayoi: Rabuni! neji: Laiteng'enani!
John20:17 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Miking'unye nanu-- amu eton eitu ailep enetii Papa-- kake nno enetii lalashera lainei-- tiaki ninje: Ailep enetii Papa lai o Minyi linyi o enetii Engai ai o Engai inyi."
John20:18 Nelotu Maria Magdalena neinosaki laiteng'enuok-- ajo etadua Olaitoriani-- neliki ninye kuna baak."
John20:19 Akae-- ore pemutu te ina olong' elukunya enjuma neena kutukajini enetii laiteng'enuok tʼolbae lʼenkuretishu oo Yudayoi-- nelotu Yesu neitashe tʼempolos enye nejoki ninje: Eseriani inyi!"
John20:20 Ore peidip atejo ena-- neitadol ninje ngaik o eluboto. Akae-- neng'ida laiteng'enuok-- edolita Olaitoriani."
John20:21 Neitoki ajoki Yesus ninje: Eseriani inyi! Neijia anaa paairriua Papa-- nairriwaa si nanu ndai."
John20:22 Ore peidip atejo ena-- nekutaki nejoki ninje: Entang'amutu Olmumua Sinyati!"
John20:23 Ore ling'uaikiki nkitarruot-- neing'uaikini ninje; ore lienikiki-- neenikini."
John20:24 Kake eitu etii Tomas-- obo too lelo tomon o are-- oipoti Olmaoi-- e nebo o ninje te ina kata naewuo Yesus."
John20:25 Akae-- nejoki ilkulekai aiteng'enuok ninye: Kitadua Olaitoriani. Nejoki si ninye ninje: Teni madol nanu tiatua ngaik enyena udot oo lmusomarini namapik olkimojino lai atua udot oo lmusomarini namaaki engaina ai atua eluboto enye-- mairuk tukul."
John20:26 Ore peishunye ngolong'i isiet neitoki aaiturrurro laiteng'enuok lenyena te nebo o Tomas; nelotu Yesus-- eena kutukajini-- neitashe tʼempolos enye nejo: Eseriani inyi!"
John20:27 Nejoki tekurum Tomas: Au olkimojino lino ene-- ng'orai ngaik ainei; au engaina ino-- eaki ninye eluboto ai-- miaku olemeiruk-- kake oloiruk."
John20:28 Nealiki Tomas nejoki ninye: Olaitoriani lai o Engai ai!
John20:29 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Iruko-- tiaraki nikitadua. Teshi looiruk-- eitu edol!"
John20:30 Akae-- eitobira Yesus kulekai ponot kumok tʼengomom oo laiteng'enuok lenyena-- leitu esiri tiatua ena kitabu;"
John20:31 Kake etisiraki kuna-- pitumutumu aairuko-- aajo era Yesus — Kristos-- Enkerai Engai-- peiye irukuruku-- iatata empuan tiatua engarna enye."
John21:1 Neitoki aitadol Yesus tekurum oo kuna kion laiteng'enuok tʼengalo olbalbal le Tiberias nelioi nji:
John21:2 Netii e nebo Simon Petros o Tomas-- oipoti Olmaoi-- o Natanael le Kana e Galilaya o nkera e Sebedayos o kulekai aare tiatua laiteng'enuok lenyena."
John21:3 Nejoki Simon Petros ninje: Alarresh singir. Nejoki ninje ninye: Kipuo si yook te nebo o iye. Nepuku ninje neilepaki engalawa-- neitu eibung' ninje te ina kiarie o toki."
John21:4 Ore pekenyu-- neitashe Yesus tʼembata olbalbal-- kake eitu eyolou laiteng'enuok-- aajo era Yesus."
John21:5 Akae-- nejoki Yesus ninje: Nakera-- miatata eninyanya? Nealiki ninje: Me."
John21:6 Nejoki si ninye ninje: Entanang'akiti erreshet ematua e tatene engalawa-- nipuopuo aatum. Akae-- nenang'aki-- neitu eidim aateyetu ninje tʼolbae lʼenkumoi oo singir."
John21:7 Akae nejoki ele aiteng'enuoni lotonyorra Yesus Petros: Era Olaitoriani! Akae-- ore pening' Simon Petros-- ajo era Olaitoriani-- neenikino olkila-- amu meishopo-- nenang'akino atua olbalbal."
John21:8 Kake eetuo kulekai aiteng'enuok tʼengalawa-- amu melakwaniki enetoiyo-- kake anaa entemet oo ngaik iip are-- neyetu erreshet oo singir."
John21:9 Akae-- ore peipung'oki enetoiyo-- nedol enkiturrurroto oo nkuk naaiwuwu-- netii shumata enye singir oopejo o olmkate."
John21:10 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Eautu ematua oo singir limbung'a taata!
John21:11 Neilep Simon Petros neyetu erreshet enetoiyo-- ebore singir kituak iip o onom o okuni; ore etii ilkumok looba nji-- neitu epolosa erreshet."
John21:12 Nejoki Yesus ninje: Ewotu-- entadaata! Metii o obo tiatua laiteng'enuok oitewuo aikilikwana ninye:Ira iye ng'ai? Amu etayoloito-- aajo era Olaitoriani."
John21:13 Nelotu Yesus neibung' olmkate neisho ninje-- neijia baiki singir."
John21:14 Era ena en e uni-- etalie Yesus too laiteng'enuok lenyena-- eidipa atopiu aing'ua lootuata."
John21:15 Akae-- ore peidip endaata-- nejoki Yesus Simon Petros: Simon le Yona-- ke kinyor nanu nilang' kulo? Nejoki ninye: Ee-- Laitoriani-- iyolo-- ajo aanyor iye. Nejoki ninye: Rrita mbalelon ainei!"
John21:16 Neitoki ajoki ninye en e are: Simon le Yona-- ke kinyor nanu? Nejoki ninye: Ee-- Laitoriani-- iyolo-- ajo aanyor iye. Nejoki ninye: Rrita ntare ainei!"
John21:17 Nejoki ninye en e uni: Simon le Yona-- ke kinyor nanu? Neilish Petros-- tiaraki natiaka ninye en e uni: Ke kinyor nanu? Nejoki ninye: Laitoriani-- iyolo iye pookin niyolo-- ajo aanyor iye. Nejoki Yesus ninye: Rrita ntare ainei!"
John21:18 Japa-- japa-- aaliki iye: Ore epon ira oti-- nien kion nilimaniki eniyeu. Kake teni ilaaku moruo-- nintorioo ngaik inono-- nikilaen olekai nikilarik enimiyeu nilo."
John21:19 Etejo ena-- peitayolo ninye-- ke ti aa kea elaitaa Engai kitok. Ore peidip atejo ena-- nejoki ninye: Tusujaki!"
John21:20 Neibelekenya Petros nedol olaiteng'enuoni onyor Yesus osujita-- ninye loirrugokine olgoo lenye tʼendaata nejo: Laitoriani-- kang'ai ele likintarasaa?"
John21:21 Akae-- ore pedol Petros ele-- nejoki Yesus: Laitoriani-- o ele naa?"
John21:22 Nejoki Yesus ninye: Teni ayeu nebik ninye metabana nalotu — kainyo iataiye? Tusujaki iye nanu!
John21:23 Akae-- nepuku ele rorei tiatua lalashera-- ajo melae ele aiteng'enuoni. Kake eitu ejoki Yesus ninye: Melae ninye! kake: Teni ayeu nebik ninye metabana nalotu — kainyo iataiye?"
John21:24 Era ele olaiteng'enuoni oijakenoki kuna nesir kuna-- nikiyolo-- aajo esipa enjakenishu enye."
John21:25 Etii baiki nkulie kumok naaitobira Yesus: ten emutu esiri ninje nabo nabo-- ajo nanu-- anaata meishaa enkop nkitabuni naapuoi aasir."
Acts1:1 Aidipa atisira-- Teofilos lanyor-- tiatua enkitabu elukunya mbaak pookin naaitera Yesus aitobir neiteng'enu"
Acts1:2 metabaiki ena olong' naidipa aitanapa tʼengolon Olmumua Sinyati lairriwak lootegelua neilepieki shumata;
Acts1:3 neitadol ninje kion eishiu eidipa osina lenye too rregiei kumok nelioi too ninje enkata oo ngolong'i artam neinosu nara nʼenkarsishu Engai.
Acts1:4 Ore peidip aiturrurro ninje-- neitanap ninje-- pemepuku te Yerusalem-- kake peanyu enkisiligata e Papa enitoning'o (nejo ninye) ndai te nanu;"
Acts1:5 amu eibatisishe Yohanes tʼengare-- kake eibatisi ndai tʼOlmumua Sinyati-- teni eishunye kuna olong'i kuti."
Acts1:6 Ore kulo ooiturrurrote neikilikwan ninye nejo: Laitoriani-- ke te ina kata ilarrinyoki Israel enkarsishu enye?"
Acts1:7 Nejoki ninye ninje: Me entoki inyi-- piyolouu enkopa arashu enkotata natipika Papa tiatua enkidimata enye;"
Acts1:8 kake ipuopuo aang'amu engolon Olmumua Sinyati olotu shumata inyi niakuku iljaken lainei tiatua Yerusalem o tiatua Yudaya o Samaria pookin o metabaiki enkiting'oto enkop.
Acts1:9 Ore peidip atejo kuna-- eing'orita kulo-- neapari neshum erukenya ninye too ngonyek enye."
Acts1:10 Ore eduaia ninje eloito ninye shumata-- ng'orai-- neitasheiki ninje leak aare looishopito ilkilani ooibor"
Acts1:11 ootejo: Ndai-- lelea le Galilaya-- ainyo pintasheshe nimaririri shumata? Ore ele Yesus oitung'aiyoki ndai nelo shumata eitoki alotu neijia anaa pitaduaitie eloito ninye shumata."
Acts1:12 Ore peidipai-- nerrinyo aapuo Yerusalem eing'ua oldonyo oji Loo loirienito-- otaaniki Yerusalem ebana olototo lʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki."
Acts1:13 Ore peidip aatijing'-- neilep shumaroto engaji netoni te ina alo Petros o Yohanes o Yakobos o Andreas o Filipos o Tomas o Bartolomayos o Matayos o Yakobos le Alfayos o Simon Selotes o Yudas le Yakobos."
Acts1:14 Ore kulo pookin neisyaisho tʼoltau obo tiatua esayata te nebo o ng'oroyok o Maria-- ng'otonye e Yesus-- o lalashera lenyena."
Acts1:15 Ore too nona olong'i neitashe Petros tʼempolos oo lalashera (ore esiana oo kulo looiturrurrote ebaia iip nabo o tikitam) nejo:
Acts1:16 Lelea-- lalashera-- meata kata nemeitabaiari esirata naitera alimu Olmumua Sinyati tʼenkutuk e David tʼolbae le Yudas lotaa olaiturukoni loo kulo ooibung'a Yesus."
Acts1:17 Amu eikenaiyoki te nebo o yook neng'amu enkyas ena kisyayare anaa yook.
Acts1:18 Neinyang'u ele enkuruma tʼolkwaje torrono nesulunye tʼengomom nedanya tʼempolos neitiakunye engoshoke pookin.
Acts1:19 Neyolou ena pookin ootii Yerusalem neipoti baiki ena kuruma tʼenkutuk enye Akeldama-- nera enkitaalata enye Enkuruma osarge."
Acts1:20 Amu etisiraki tiatua enkitabu oo Singolioitin: „Njeing'uari ntonat enyena-- njoo metii oltung'ani oton tiatua“-- ore kat are: „Njeng'amu olekai enkyas enking'orare enye“."
Acts1:21 Akae-- ore tiatua leak ootaboitare yook tʼenkata pookin natijing'a nepuku tʼempolos ang' Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos"
Acts1:22 eiter tʼenkibatisa e Yohanes metabaiki ina olong' naitung'aiyoki yook-- ore obo too lelo meata kata nemeaku oljakeni lʼempiunoto enye te nebo o yook."
Acts1:23 Neitasheye ninje aare: Yosef oipotoki Barsabas-- neata engai arna Yustos-- o Matias;"
Acts1:24 nesaisho nejo: Iye Laitoriani-- oyolo iltauja lenye pookin-- ntadolu obo Etegelua too kulo pokira are--"
Acts1:25 peng'amu ewueji ena kisyayare o enkirriwaroto natung'aiye Yudas nelo ewueji enye.
Acts1:26 Neosh olenkukuo netum enkukuo Matias neikenari ninye te nebo o lairriwak tomon o obo.
Acts2:1 Ore pebaia engolong' e Pentekoste netii pookin nabo wueji tʼoltau obo.
Acts2:2 Neaku nabokata oltoilo oing'ua shumata anaa lʼenkijape nakutisho tʼengolon neigany engaji pookin natonie.
Acts2:3 Nelioi etoorikiaki ninje ilng'ejepa anaa lʼenkima netonie shumata enye pookin obo obo.
Acts2:4 Neboreyu ninje pookin Olmumua Sinyati neiter aairo too nkulie kutukie neijia anaa peishoo Olmumua meiroro.
Acts2:5 Netii Yerusalem Yudayoi-- iltung'anak supati tiatua loreren pookin ootii enkop."
Acts2:6 Ore peibulaa ilo toilo-- neiturrurro siamin neirut-- amu etoning'o oltung'ani pookin eiro ninje tʼenkutuk enye."
Acts2:7 Neing'asia pookin neiputukuny nejokino ninje: Kye-- ore kulo pookin ooirorita me le Galilaya?"
Acts2:8 Anai ijo kining' yook oltung'ani pookin eiro tʼenkutuk ang' natoikioki yook?
Acts2:9 Ilpartoi o Ilmedoi o Elamitai o lootii Mesopotamia o Yudaya o Kapadokia o Pontos o Asia
Acts2:10 o Frigia o Pamfilia o Misri o matuan e Libia tʼembata e Kirene o lomon loora Romayoi
Acts2:11 o Yudayoi o ilkaponu o Ilkretes o Ilmarabu-- kining' kulo eiro too nkutukie ang' ntokitin kituak Engai."
Acts2:12 Neirut ninje pookin neing'arrirro nejokino: Kainyo eaku ena?
Acts2:13 Neitaa kulekai engalaa nejo: Etemerate tʼolmarua opi.
Acts2:14 Neitashe Petros o kulo tomon o obo neapaa oltoilo lenye nejoki ninje: Lelea loo Yudayoi o pookin litiiti Yerusalem-- entayolou kuna-- pinining'ung'u rorei lainei."
Acts2:15 Amu eitu emera kulo neija anaa pitejo ndai-- amu ore taata era esaa uni enasirie;"
Acts2:16 kake era kuna naatejo olayolounoni Yoel:
Acts2:17 Neaku too ngolong'i enkiting'oto-- neiro Engai-- nalabukoki Olmumua lai shumata oo nkiri pookin nepuo aainosu laiyok linyi o ntoiye inyi mbaak e akenya nepuo aadol ilbarnot linyi nduarot nepuo aata laigwenak linyi nkidetidetat;"
Acts2:18 nalabukoki too kuna olong'i shumata oo laisyayak lainei o ngaisyayak ainei Olmumua lai nepuo si ninje aainosu mbaak e akenya;
Acts2:19 naitaa nkiputukunyot te shumata o ilponot tiabori-- tʼenkop-- osarge o enkima o oloikuluo lʼempuruo;"
Acts2:20 Neala engolong' aaku enaimin-- neaku olapa osarge-- epon eitu elotu engolong' Olaitoriani nara kitok o nʼenkitalioroto;"
Acts2:21 neaku ore pookin oloipot engarna Olaitoriani-- nelapok."
Acts2:22 Lelea le Israel-- entoning' kulo rorei: Yesus le Nasaret-- oltung'ani oitadolua Engai tiatua ndai too nkitobirat engolon o too nkiputukunyot o too lponot ooitobira Engai tʼengaina enye tiatua ndai (anaa piyololo ndai oopeny)--"
Acts2:23 ele (loitarasuaki tʼenkigwena natootikio Engai o tʼeyolounoto enye neba opa) imbung'a ndai too ngaik oo ltorrok nisheshe niariara metua.
Acts2:24 Eitopiwuo Engai ninye nedung' mioitin enkea-- amu eitu eaku-- peibung' ninye."
Acts2:25 Amu eimaka David embae enye: Atadua nanu ngolong'i pookin Engai tʼengomom ai-- amu etii ninye engaina ai e tatene-- pamaing'unung'un."
Acts2:26 Onaa eiting'idaki te ina oltau lai neng'ida olng'ejep lai-- nelabik baiki osesen lai tiatua eanyunoto."
Acts2:27 Amu ming'ua Olmumua lai tiatua ewueji enkiminata niminjo Osinyati lino-- petum empurdata."
Acts2:28 Kinteng'ena engoitoi empuan; kilaigany eng'ida tʼengomom ino.
Acts2:29 Lelea-- lalashera-- enjooki-- pairo-- maureisho tʼengomom inyi mbaak olakui lang' David-- ajo etua nenuki netii enkurare enye enkop ang' metabaiki taata."
Acts2:30 Akae-- tiaraki nara olayolounoni neyolo-- ajo eisiliga Engai ninye tʼenkiturujata-- ajo eton tʼolorika lenye embeu eishoi enye--"
Acts2:31 neitera adol kuna neimaki empiunoto e Kristos-- ajo eitu epali Olmumua lenye tiatua ewueji oo lootuata neitu etum osesen lenye empurdata."
Acts2:32 Eitopiwuo Engai ele Yesus nikira yook pookin iljaken lenyena.
Acts2:33 Ore peidip ailepie Engai ninye tʼengaina enye e tatene-- neng'amu ninye enkisiligata Olmumua Sinyati tʼengaina e Menye-- ele otubukuo anaa pidolitata nining'itoto."
Acts2:34 Amu eitu eilep David shumata-- kake etejo openy: Etiaka Olaitoriani Olaitoriani lai: Totona te tatene ai--"
Acts2:35 metabana napik ilmang'ati linono abori oo ndapi oo nkejek inono.
Acts2:36 Njeyolou taata engaji pookin e Israel esipa-- ajo eitaa Engai ele Yesus litasho ndai-- peaku Olaitoriani o Kristos."
Acts2:37 Ore pening' ninje kuna-- nepejoi iltauja lenye nejoki ninje Petros o kulekai airriwaki Kaji kinko-- lelea-- lalashera?"
Acts2:38 Nejoki Petros ninje: Entaalata-- njeibatisi oltung'ani pookin too ndai atua engarna e Yesus Kristos-- petum enkitaunoto oo nkitarruot-- nipuopuo aang'amu enkishooroto Olmumua Sinyati."
Acts2:39 Amu era ena kisiligata eninyi o noo nkera inyi o noo pookin oolakwa oolaipot Olaitoriani-- Engai ang'."
Acts2:40 Neijakenisho neroj too kulekai rorei kumok nejo: Enjoo eitopoki ndai tʼena kishon naibelo.
Acts2:41 Ore kulo lootang'amutua rorei lenyena too ltauja-- neisho eibatisi; neponikini te ina olong' iltung'anak oobaia iip osom (elfun uni)."
Acts2:42 Nebik ninje tiatua enkiteng'enare oo lairriwak o tiatua enkidikidikoto o embelibelata olmkate o esayata.
Acts2:43 Nejing' enkuretishu atua iltauja pookin neaku nkiputukunyot o ilponot kumok too lairriwak.
Acts2:44 Netii pookin looiruko e nebo neaku eng'ara ntokitin pookin.
Acts2:45 Nemir masaa enye o naata neorikino pookin neijia anaa peata oltung'ani osina--"
Acts2:46 netoni ninje ngolong'i pookin tʼoltau obo tʼengaji sinyati ebelibel olmkate too ngajijik o ngajijik nenya endaa too ltauja oong'ida naleng' nemeata olosek
Acts2:47 neitadaraa Engai netum ninje eng'adunoto tʼolorere pookin; neponiki Olaitoriani esirit ngolong'i pookin iltung'anak ootopua.
Acts3:1 Akae-- neaku epuo Petros o Yohanes te nebo engaji sinyati tʼenkata nasaishoreki-- tʼesaa enturuj."
Acts3:2 Netii olee obo purpur eiter tʼengoshoke e ng'otonye otanapaki-- oitaperoki ngolong'i pookin te kutukaji engaji sinyati naipoti Sidai-- peomon kulo loojing' engaji sinyati nkishoorot empuris."
Acts3:3 Ore pedol ninye Petros o Yohanes ejing'ita engaji sinyati-- neomon ninje enkishooroto empuris."
Acts3:4 Neing'oraa ake Petros te nebo o Yohanes ninye nejoki: Ng'orai yook!
Acts3:5 Neing'oraa ninje neanyu-- peng'amu entoki too ninje."
Acts3:6 Neiro Petros: Maata ngoshola arashu sahabu-- ore enaata ninye aaisho: tʼengarna e Yesus Kristos le Nasaret ntasho-- tilimanai!"
Acts3:7 Neibung' engaina enye e tatene neapaa; netum nabokata ndapi enyena o rubat oo nkejek engolon--"
Acts3:8 neipirriu neitashe nelimana nejing' te nebo o ninje engaji sinyati nelo eityamityam eitadaraa Engai.
Acts3:9 Nedol olorere pookin ninye eloito eitadaraa Engai.
Acts3:10 Neyolou-- aajo ninye oloshi oton eomonu nkishoorot empuris te kutukaji sidai engaji sinyati-- neigany ninje nking'asiat o olputukuny too kuna naataa te ninye."
Acts3:11 Akae-- ore peidikidikore ele purpur loishiunyeki Petros o Yohanes-- neiturrurrokino olorere pookin enetii ninje atua enkitala naji ne Salomo-- eiputukuny."
Acts3:12 Ore pedol Petros ena-- nealiki olorere: Lelea le Israel-- ainyo pimputukunyokiki kuna? Arashu ainyo pikurrakiki yook ngonyek-- anai ijojo tʼengolon ang' arashu tʼesupato ang kinjoo ele-- pelimana?"
Acts3:13 Engai e Abraham o Isaak o Yakoob-- Engai oo lakuyani lang'-- ninye naitaa kitok Enkerai enye Yesus lintarasaitie ndai-- litomikio t'engomom e Pilatos te ina kata naigwenaka-- peing'uaiki ninye;"
Acts3:14 kake itomikio ndai ele Sinyati-- olopeny esupato-- nisaiyuyu-- peishori ndai oltung'ani otaara metua--"
Acts3:15 niariara Olkitok lʼempuan metua. Eitopiwuo Engai ilo aitung'ua lootuata nikira yook iljaken lenyena.
Acts3:16 Ore tʼenkirukoto e atua engarna enye eishooki ele lidolitata niyololo engolon tʼengarna enye; enkirukoto te ilo naishoo ninye ena biotishu tʼengomom inyi pookin.
Acts3:17 Akae-- lalashera-- ayolo-- ajo intobira kuna-- miyololo-- anaa peikuna si ninje-- ilkituak linyi."
Acts3:18 Kake eitisipa Engai kuna baak naatolimuo ninye opa tʼenkutuk oo layolounok lenyena pookin-- ajo eisili Kristos lenye."
Acts3:19 Ore taata-- entaalata-- embelekenyata-- pejutori nkitarruot inyi--"
Acts3:20 pepuonu nkatan eng'ieng'are tʼengomom Olaitoriani neirriu ninye Yesus Kristos oiteraki aainosaki ndai--"
Acts3:21 olemeata kata nemeng'amu enkitoria e shumata metabana neitobirakini mbaak pookin naairoro Engai t'enkutuk oo layolounok lenyena sinyat neba opa.
Acts3:22 Etejo baiki Mose: Elo aitopiwuoki ndai Olaitoriani Engai Olayolounoni tiatua lalashera linyi anaa nanu; entoning' ninye too pookin naaliki ndai.
Acts3:23 Elaaku ore oltung'ani pookin lemening' ilo ayolounoni-- neiminyeki ninye tukul tiatua olorere."
Acts3:24 Neinosu layolounok pookin eiter te Samuel o kulo lootusuja ninye-- kulo pookin ooiroro-- mbaak oo kuna olong'i."
Acts3:25 Irara ndai nkera oo layolounok o nʼosotua oitaa Engai o loominyi linyi te ina kata natiaka ninye Abraham: Emayani tʼeishoi ino ntipati pookin enkop.
Acts3:26 Eitopiwuoko ndai Engai tʼenkata elukunya enkerai enye Yesus neirriwaki ninye ndai-- pemayan ndai-- peibelekenyunye oltung'ani pookin aing'ua ntorrok enyena."
Acts4:1 Ore eton eirorie ninje iltung'anak-- nepuonu laidasak enetii ninje o olkitok lʼengaji sinyati o Sadukayoi"
Acts4:2 nerika-- tiaraki naiteng'en ninje olorere neinosu te Yesus enkitopiunoto too lootuata"
Acts4:3 neibung' ninje too ngaik neigenoo tiaji-- perripi metabaiki enasirie; amu etaa teipa."
Acts4:4 Ore ilkumok ootoning'o rorei lenye neiruk; neaku esiana oo leak iip onom.
Acts4:5 Ore peaku enasirie neiturrurro te Yerusalem ilkituak o laigwenak o layolok lʼesirata
Acts4:6 o Anas-- olaidasani kitok-- o Kayafas o Yohanes o Aleksandros o pookin loora lʼenkishomi oo laidasak kituak;"
Acts4:7 neitasheye ninje tʼempolos neikilikwan: Ke ti aa golon arashu ke ti aa arna intobira ndai kuna?
Acts4:8 Nejoki Petros eiganya Olmumua Sinyati ninje: Lekituak lʼolorere o laigwenak le Israel--"
Acts4:9 teni eigwenakini yook taata tʼembae sidai nainoto oltung'ani leyati-- ke ti aa bae etopua ninye--"
Acts4:10 entayolo ndai pookin o olorere pookin le Israel-- aajo tʼengarna e Yesus Kristos le Nasaret litooshokitio ndai esalaba-- loitopiwuo Engai aitung'ua lootuata-- te ninye eitashe ele aa bioto tʼengomom inyi."
Acts4:11 Nera ilo osoit linturraitie ndai-- lashetak-- etaa ninye osoit kitok lʼolpijata."
Acts4:12 Nemetii enkitopuata tʼolekai nemetii engai arna abori e shumata naishooki iltung'anak-- pikitum aatopok te ninye."
Acts4:13 Nedol ninje enjipai e Petros o en e Yohanes neitoki aayolou-- aajo era iltung'anak lemeyolo sirat-- eitu eiteng'eni-- neiputukuny-- neyolou baiki-- aajo etaboitare Yesus--"
Acts4:14 neitoki aadol ele tung'ani eishiunyeki eitashe te nebo o ninje-- neitu eata enaalu."
Acts4:15 Neitanapisho-- pepuku tʼenkigwena neigwena nejo:"
Acts4:16 Kainyo kintaas kulo tung'anak? Amu etayoloki ena kiputukunyoto naitobira ninje neibale too pookin oomanya Yerusalem-- nimikindim yook aatomiki."
Acts4:17 Kake pemepona-- pemeibulaa atua olorere-- maituria ninje osupatei-- pemeitoki aaimaki tʼoltung'ani o obo tʼena arna."
Acts4:18 Neipot ninje neitanapisho-- pemeitoki aairo tukul-- pemeiteng'enisho baiki tʼengarna e Yesus."
Acts4:19 Nealiki Petros o Yohanes nejoki ninje: Engwenakiti oopeny-- ten aa entoki sidai tʼengomom Engai-- pikining' ndai nikintalang' Engai."
Acts4:20 Mikindim yook aatapal eitu kiro enikitadua o enikitoning'o.
Acts4:21 Neitoki aaiture ninje neing'uaiki neitu etum entoki naitameiye ninje tʼolbae lʼolorere; amu eitadaraitie pookin Engai too kuna naataa.
Acts4:22 Amu etalang'a larin artam ele tung'ani oitobirakaki ena toki kitok enkishiunoto.
Acts4:23 Neing'uaikini nepuo enetii iltung'anak lenye neinosaki ninje naatiakitia ninje laidasak kituak o laigwenak.
Acts4:24 Ore pening' si ninje neilepie oltoilo tʼoltau obo-- pelo enetii Engai neiro: Lemagilani-- ira iye Engai naitobira shumata o enkop o ilbalbali o pookin naatii atua--"
Acts4:25 niroro tʼenkutuk e David-- olaisyayani lino-- tʼengolon Olmumua Sinyati: Ainyo peiula loreren neibirribir iltung'anak neme o nyoo?"
Acts4:26 Neitashe ilkarsisi lʼenkop neiturrurro ilkituak te nebo-- pear Olaitoriani o Kristos lenye."
Acts4:27 Amu esipa-- eiturrurrote tiatua ena ang' tʼolbae lʼOinoti lino sinyati Yesus liela iye-- Herodes o Pontios Pilatos te nebo o loreren o olorere le Israel--"
Acts4:28 peiye eitobir anaa petootikio engaina ino o enkigwena ino-- peaku neijia."
Acts4:29 Akae-- ng'orai taata-- Laitoriani-- nkituriat enye-- njoo laisyayak linono-- peiro lomon linono tʼenjipai pookin;"
Acts4:30 ntorioi engaina ino-- peaku nkishiunot o ntokitin kituak o nkiputukunyot tʼengaina Oinoti lino Yesus."
Acts4:31 Ore peidip aatasaishoto ninje neikirikira ewueji neiturrurrote ninje-- neigany pookin Olmumua Sinyati neiro lomon lʼEngai tʼenjipai."
Acts4:32 Neaku ake esiamu oo kulo looiruko oltau obo o Olmumua obo-- nemetii o obo otejo-- ajo era entoki naata ninye emasaita enye-- kake etang'ara ninje ntokitin pookin enye."
Acts4:33 Neijakenu lairriwak tʼengolon kitok empiunoto Olaitoriani Yesus-- neaku kitok eng'adunoto tiatua ninje pookin."
Acts4:34 Nemetii o obo too ninje oata elaunoto-- amu pookin ooata nkuruman arashu ngajijik nemir neau nainosie"
Acts4:35 nepik engalo oo nkejek oo lairriwak neorikini oltung'ani pookin neijia anaa peata elaunoto.
Acts4:36 Ore Yoses oipoto lairriwak Barnabas (ore enkitaalata enye: enkerai enkilejilejata)-- olevites otoiwuoki te Kupros--"
Acts4:37 neata enkuruma nemir neau ngoshola nepik engalo oo nkejek oo lairriwak.
Acts5:1 Netii oltung'ani obo oji Ananias nemir te nebo o eng'oroyoni enye naji Safira enaata
Acts5:2 neisudoki kion tʼesungureishu ematua oo ngoshola-- eyolo eng'oroyoni enye-- neau naatelekutua nepik engalo oo nkejek oo lairriwak."
Acts5:3 Nejoki Petros: Ananias-- ainyo pikinganya satan oltau lino-- pilej Olmumua Sinyati nisudoki kion tʼesungureishu ematua oo ngoshola enkuruma?"
Acts5:4 Ore eton memira-- mera entoki ino? Ore indipa atimira — me iye oitore? Ainyo pinjoo oltau lino meikuna nji? Me oltung'ani iteleja-- Engai."
Acts5:5 Ore pening' Ananias kulo rorei-- nebatata nee; neaku enkuretishu kitok too pookin lootoning'o kuna."
Acts5:6 Nedumunye ilbarnot neirin ninye nenap nenuk.
Acts5:7 Ore peishunye saan uni te ina kata-- nejing'u eng'oroyoni enye-- meyolo enataa."
Acts5:8 Nejoki Petros ninye: Tiakaki-- itimira ndai enkuruma te ina kinyang'a? Nejo: Ee-- te ina."
Acts5:9 Nejoki Petros ninye: Kaji inkuna teni iakuku nabo-- pitemiteme Olmumua lʼOlaitoriani? Ng'orai-- etii kutukaji nkejek oo kulo ootunuka olmoruo lino-- kipuo aanap si iye."
Acts5:10 Nebatata nabokata too nkejek enyena nee; nejing' ilbarnot nedol ninye etua-- nenap ninye nenuk te nebo wueji o olmoruo lenye."
Acts5:11 Netum esirit pookin enkuretishu kitok o pookin lootoning'o kuna.
Acts5:12 Neaku ntokitin kituak o nkiputukunyot kumok tiatua olorere too ngaik oo lairriwak; neboita pookin tʼoltau obo tiatua olgilata le Salomo:
Acts5:13 neitu eiteu o obo too lkulekai aidikidikore ninje-- kake eitadaraitie olorere ninje."
Acts5:14 Nepon eponari ake looiruko Olaitoriani-- leak kumok o ng'oroyok."
Acts5:15 Neitolok iltamoiya too ngoitoi neitepetaa shumata oo lonito o rruatin-- peiye-- teni elotu Petros-- eopoo oloip lenye ematua olorere."
Acts5:16 Nepuonu ilkumok eing'ua ngang'itie naamaniki Yerusalem-- enapita iltamoiya o looitame ilmeneng'a; neishiunyeki pookin."
Acts5:17 Neinyototo olaidasani kitok o pookin ooboitare ninye-- oora lʼenkiteng'enare oo Sadukayoi-- neigany enkiba--"
Acts5:18 neibung' lairriwak too ngaik nepik engaji oo looena.
Acts5:19 Kake etabolo olmalaika lʼOlaitoriani kiarie kutukaji engaji erripore neitupuku ninje nejo:
Acts5:20 Enjom-- pintasheshe-- pilimumu tiatua engaji sinyati lomon pookin lʼena puan."
Acts5:21 Ore peidip aatoning' kuna-- nepuo enasirie atua engaji sinyati neiteng'enisho. Nelotu olaidasani kitok o looboitare ninye neipot enkigwena o ilkituak pookin loo nkera Israel neirriwaa iltung'anak engaji erripore-- perikuni ninje."
Acts5:22 Ore pebaia lairriwak neitu edol ninje tʼengaji erripore-- nerrinyo neinosu mbaak"
Acts5:23 nejo: Kineputua engaji erripore aa bioto katukul neitashe larripok tʼeneishiaakinore kutukaji-- kake ore pikibol neitu kidol oltung'ani tiatua."
Acts5:24 Ore pening' olkitok lʼengaji sinyati o laidasak kituak kulo rorei-- neing'arrirro neitu eyolo kuna baak naataa."
Acts5:25 Nelotu oltung'ani obo neinosaki ninje mbaak nejo: Ore kulo tung'anak litipika ndai engaji erripore etii atua engaji sinyati-- eitashe neiteng'en olorere."
Acts5:26 Nelo olkitok te nebo o laisyayak neriku ninje-- kake me tʼengolon-- amu eturia olorere-- pemeaku enang' ninje too soito."
Acts5:27 Neriku neitasheye ninje tʼengomom enkigwena; neikilikwan olaidasani kitok ninje nejo:
Acts5:28 Eitu kintanap ndai tʼenkitanapata-- peminteng'enishosho tʼena arna? Ore ndai-- inganya Yerusalem enkiteng'enare inyi-- niyeuu niauu shumata ang' osarge le ilo tung'ani."
Acts5:29 Nealu Petros o kulekai airriwak nejo: Meata kata nimikining' Engai nelang' iltung'anak.
Acts5:30 Eitopiwuo Engai oo loopapa lang' Yesus litara metua niikiiki tʼenjata.
Acts5:31 Eitaa Engai ninye kitok tʼengaina enye e tatene-- peaku Olarikoni o Olaitopuani-- peisho Israel enkitaalata o enkitaunoto oo nkitarruot."
Acts5:32 Nikira yook ake iljaken loo kulo rorei o Olmumua Sinyati oishoo Engai kulo pookin looning' ninye.
Acts5:33 Ore pening' ninje kuna-- nepejoi iltauja lenye neigwena-- pear metuata."
Acts5:34 Neitashe obo tiatua enkigwena lora Olfarisayos-- neji engama enye Gamaliel-- olaiteng'enani loo nkitanapat-- neataiye olorere pookin oloip-- neitanapu-- periki lairriwak boo peno"
Acts5:35 nejoki ninje: Lelea le Israel-- entaduai aten too niasakiki kulo tung'anak."
Acts5:36 Amu ore too nona olong'i naaima einyotote Toidas nejo ninye era oltung'ani-- nesuj iltung'anak oobaia iip ong'wan; neari ilo metua-- ore pookin lootusuja ninye neisardakieki neitu eaku toki;"
Acts5:37 Ore tekurum enye nedumunye Yudas le Galilaya too ngolong'i enkikenare nerik iltung'anak ooje lootusuja ninye; neimin si ninye-- ore pookin lootusuja ninye neisardak."
Acts5:38 Akae-- ajoki ndai taata: Entapaashare kulo tung'anak-- entung'aikiti ninje! Amu teni era ena kigwena o ena kyas en oo ltung'anak-- nelarruoio ninye;"
Acts5:39 kake teni era en Engai-- mindimidimi aaitarruoi-- pimilioii anaa looarare Engai."
Acts5:40 Nening' ninye neipot lairriwak near ninje neitanap-- pemeitoki aairo tʼengarna e Yesus-- neing'uaiki."
Acts5:41 Nepuku tʼengomom enkigwena eng'ida-- aajo eishooki enkitook-- petum osina tʼolbae lʼengarna enye;"
Acts5:42 neitu epal too ngolong'i pookin tiatua engaji sinyati o too ngajijik eiteng'enu neinosu lomon le Yesus Kristos.
Acts6:1 Ore too kuna olong'i etoponate laiteng'enuok nejing' enking'unyung'unyata oo Lgrikini atua Yudayoi-- tiaraki neitu etum ngolia enye nkishoorot oo ngolong'i pookin abaraki."
Acts6:2 Neipot kulo tomon o are esiamu oo laiteng'enuok nejo: Meiting'idisho-- pikipal yook lomon lʼEngai-- peiye kisyayaki endaa."
Acts6:3 Onaa-- lalashera-- entegelutu too ndai iltung'anak oopishana looata enkitadararoto-- looiganya Olmumua. Sinyati o eng'eno-- pikipik ninje atua ena kyas."
Acts6:4 Kipuo aabik yook ake tiatua esayata o enkisyayare oo lomon.
Acts6:5 Neiting'idisho ilo rorei tʼesiamu pookin-- negelu Stefanos-- oltung'ani oiganya enkirukoto o Olmumua Sinyati-- o Filipos o Prokoros o Nikanor o Timon o Parmenas o Nikolaos-- olomoni le Antiokia--"
Acts6:6 neitasheye ninje tʼengomom oo lairriwak nesaisho neiteleiki ninje ngaik.
Acts6:7 Neibulaa lomon lʼEngai nepona naleng' esiana oo laiteng'enuok tiatua Yerusalem-- neiruk ilkumok too laidasak."
Acts6:8 Ore Stefanos-- obore enkirukoto o engolon-- neitobir nkiputukunyot o ntokitin kituak tiatua olorere."
Acts6:9 Neinyototo iltung'anak oora lʼesirit oo Libertinoi o Lkirenayoi o ne Aleksandria o ne Kilikia o Asia neikilikwanaro o Stefanos
Acts6:10 neitu eidim aatigilunore eng'eno o Olmumua oishoo meiroro.
Acts6:11 Neitijing' baiki leak ootejo: Kitoning'o ele eiroro rorei oomorie Mose o Engai.
Acts6:12 Neisusukie ninje olorere o laigwenak o layolok lʼesirata nenyikaki enetii neibung' nerik ninye atua enkigwena.
Acts6:13 Neitasheye iljaken lʼelejare ootejo: Eitu epal ele tung'ani emor ene wueji sinyati o nkitanapat;
Acts6:14 amu kitoning'o-- ejoito-- ajo elaar ele Yesus le Nasaret ene wueji neitaai rregiei ooishoo yook Mose."
Acts6:15 Nekurraki ninye ngonyek pookin lootii enkigwena nedol enyanyukie engomom enye en olmalaika.
Acts7:1 Nejo olaidasani kitok: Ke neija etiu?
Acts7:2 Nejo ninye: Lelea lalashera o loopapa-- entoning'! Eitadua kion Engai enkitook papa lang' Abraham te ina kata etii Mesopotamia-- epon eitu eton te Haran;"
Acts7:3 nejoki ninye: Tupuku tʼolosho lino o tʼenkishomi ino-- pilo olosho layeu naaitadol iye!"
Acts7:4 Nepuku te ina kata tʼolosho loo Lkaldayoi nemany Haran. Ore peidip atua menye lenye te ina alo-- neidurrunye Engai ninye metabaiki ele osho litiiti ndai taata--"
Acts7:5 neitu eisho ninye enjung'o tʼena alo metabaiki eneroro-- neisilig ninye-- ajo eisho-- metaa enenye o noo nkera enyena-- tekurum-- eton meata enkerai."
Acts7:6 Neiro nji Engai-- ajo eaku embeu enye engomom tʼolekai osho neitaai ninye osinga-- neitaasi ninye ntorrok te ina alo larin iip ong'wan."
Acts7:7 Ore olorere oitaa ninye osinga-- alaigwenaki nanu-- etejo Engai; ore peidipai kuna-- nelapuku naalaisyayaki nanu tʼene wueji."
Acts7:8 Neisho ninye enkitobirakinoto emurata; neiu ninye Isaak nemurat ninye tʼengolong' e isiet-- neiu Isaak Yakoob neiu Yakoob lakuyani tomon o are."
Acts7:9 Negil tau lakuyani nemir Yosef-- pelo olosho Misri; neboitare Engai ninye--"
Acts7:10 neitupuku ninye too sinaitin lenyena pookin neisho ninye eng'adunoto o eng'eno tʼengomom e Farao-- olkarsis le Misri; neitaa ninye olkitok le Misri o engaji enye pookin."
Acts7:11 Nelotu olamei atua olosho Misri pookin o atua olosho Kanaan-- o osina kitok-- neitu etum loopapa lang' endaa."
Acts7:12 Ore pening' Yakoob-- ajo etii endaa Misri-- neirriwaa loopapa lang' tʼenkata elukunya."
Acts7:13 Ore tʼengaigil e are neyolou lalashera Yosef-- neyolou Farao enkishomi e Yosef."
Acts7:14 Neirriwaa Yosef neipot Yakoob-- menye lenye-- o enkishomi enye pookin-- iltung'anak ntomoni naapishana o imiet."
Acts7:15 Nedoiyo Yakoob metabaiki Misri nee-- ninye o loopapa lang'--"
Acts7:16 nenapi ninye Sikem nenuki tiatua enkurare nainyang'ua Abraham tʼenkinyang'a oo ngoshola too nkera Emor te Sikem.
Acts7:17 Akae-- ore petaanu enkata enkisiligata naiturujaka Engai Abraham-- nepona olorere neaku kumok tʼolosho Misri--"
Acts7:18 metabana nejing' olekai karsis leitu eyolo Yosef.
Acts7:19 Neitobiraki ele olosek enkishomi ang' neitobiraki loopapa lang' ntorrok neisho eiturrari nkera enye kutiti-- pemebik eishiu."
Acts7:20 Neiuni te ina kata Mose neaku nenyorru Engai ninye neitotii enkata oo lapaitin okuni tʼengaji e menye;
Acts7:21 ore peiturrari-- nedumu ninye entito e Farao neitubulu ninye anaa enkerai enye."
Acts7:22 Neiteng'eni Mose tʼeng'eno pookin oo Lmisrin-- negolu too rorei o too nkyasin enyena."
Acts7:23 Ore peaku ninye loo larin artam-- nejing'aa atua oltau lenye-- peing'oraa lalashera lenyena-- nkera Israel."
Acts7:24 Nedol oltung'ani oisilitoi-- neing'araki neretoki oloinyalitai near Olmisri metua."
Acts7:25 Nejo-- ajo eyolou lalashera lenyena-- ajo eisho Engai ninje enkitopuata too ngaik enyena-- kake eitu eyolou ninje kuna."
Acts7:26 Ore tʼengolong' e are neipung'oki looara neitobiraki osotua nejo: Lelea-- irara ndai lalashera-- ainyo pintobirakinono ntorrok?"
Acts7:27 Ore oloisilito ol elatia enye neiponyaki ninye enelakwa nejo: Kang'ai likintaa iye olkitok o olarishani lang'?
Acts7:28 Iyeu nikiar matua anaa pitara ola ng'ole Misri?
Acts7:29 Neisik Mose te ilo rorei neaku olomoni tʼolosho Midian neiu te ina alo nkera are.
Acts7:30 Ore peishunye larin artam-- nelioi te ninye olmalaika lʼOlaitoriani ti ang'ata oldonyo Sinai tiatua enkiwuwuoto enkima tʼolodung'okino."
Acts7:31 Ore pedol Mose-- neiputukunyoki enatalie; ore penyikaki ninye-- peing'oraa-- nebaiki ninye oltoilo lʼOlaitoriani:"
Acts7:32 Ara nanu Engai oo loominyi linono-- Engai e Abraham o Engai e Isaak o Engai e Yakoob. Neikirikira Mose neitu eidim aing'orai."
Acts7:33 Nejoki Olaitoriani ninye: Talaku namuka too nkejek inono-- amu ore ene wueji nintasheiye era enkop sinyati."
Acts7:34 Enduata atadua osina loo ltung'anak lainei ootii Misri-- naning' ang'at enye nadou-- paitupuku ninje; onaa wou taata-- paairriwaa iye-- pilo Misri."
Acts7:35 Ele Mose otanyaita ninje nejoki: Kang'ai likintaa olkitok o olarishani lang? ninye eirriwaiye Engai-- peaku olkitok o Olaitopuani tʼengaina olmalaika otalie te ninye tiatua olodung'okino."
Acts7:36 Neitupuku ele ninje neitobir nkiputukunyot o ntokitin kituak tʼolosho Misri o tʼOlbalbal odo o tiatua ang'ata-- larin artam."
Acts7:37 Ninye ele Mose otiaka nkera Israel: Elainyeyeki ndai Olaitoriani Engai inyi olayolounoni tiatua lalashera linyi lijo nanu; entoning' ninye!
Acts7:38 Ninye ele otii atua esirit ti ang'ata te nebo o olmalaika oirorie ninye tʼoldonyo Sinai o loopapa lang'-- otang'amua rorei lʼempuan-- peisho yook;"
Acts7:39 neitu eiruk loopapa lang' aatoning' ninye neiponyaki enelakwa nerrinyo too ltauja Misri
Acts7:40 nejoki Aron: Ntobiraki yook ngain naaiturukie yook-- amu mikiyolo enataa tʼele Mose oitupukuo yook tʼolosho Misri."
Acts7:41 Neitobir olashe too nona olong'i neaki ena mua enkidasare neng'ida tʼolbae loo nkyasin oo ngaik enye.
Acts7:42 Neibelekenya Engai neisho ninje-- peisyayaki oltim le shumata anaa petisiraki tʼesirata oo layolounok: Ke kiakitia nanu yeng'unot o nkidasareitin larin artam tiatua ang'ata-- naaji e Israel?"
Acts7:43 Niapupu engaji olototo e Molok o olakira lʼengai inyi Romfa-- muain nintobira-- pisyayakiki ninje; nalaidurrie nanu ndai metabaiki idya matua e Babel."
Acts7:44 Neata loopapa lang' engaji olototo enjakenishu ti ang'ata anaa peitanapa ninye olotiaka Mose-- peshet aitanyanyukie ena mua natadua;"
Acts7:45 ore si ninje loopapa lang' ootang'amutua ninye neitijing' te nebo o Yosua atua olosho loo loreren ootimira Engai tʼengomom oo loopapa lang' metabaiki enkata e David
Acts7:46 loinoto eng'adunoto tʼengomom Engai neyeu netumoki ewueji natonie Engai e Yakoob.
Acts7:47 Neshetaki ake Salomo ninye engaji.
Acts7:48 Kake meton Olotii shumata tʼengaji nateshetaki too ngaik anaa pejo olayolounoni:
Acts7:49 Nera shumata olorika lai nera enkop enapik nkejek ainei: kaa aji iyeuu nikishetakiki? ejo Olaitoriani-- arashu kaa wueji nera ewueji eng'ieng'ata ai?"
Acts7:50 Me engaina ai naitobira kuna pookin?
Acts7:51 Ndai loo murto naagol-- lememurata too ltauja o too nkiyaa-- nitemumu ngolong'i pookin Olmumua Sinyati-- anaa loominyi neijia si ndai."
Acts7:52 Kalo ayolounoni eitu einyal loominyi? Etara metuata kulo loinosutua mbaak elotunoto ele oata esupato-- ele lintarasaitie niariara ndai metua."
Acts7:53 Itang'amutua ndai nkitanapat tʼenkirriunoto oo lmalaikan-- neitu imbung'ubung'u."
Acts7:54 Ore pening' ninje kuna-- nepejoi iltauja lenye neonyiki ninye lala."
Acts7:55 Ore peiganya ninye Olmumua Sinyati-- nekurraki ninye ngonyek enyena shumata nedol enkitook Engai o Yesus oitashe tʼengaina e tatene Engai"
Acts7:56 nejo: Eng'orai-- adolita shumata etabole neitashe Enkerai oltung'ani tʼengaina e tatene Engai."
Acts7:57 Neosh ninje olodoo naleng' nepising' nkiyaa enye neityamaki ninye tʼoltau obo
Acts7:58 neiponyaki aulo engan' nenang' too soito. Nepik iljaken ilkarashi lenye engalo oo nkejek olbarnoti obo oji Saulos.
Acts7:59 Nenang' ninje Stefanos too soito-- esaisho nejo: Laitoriani Yesus-- tang'amu Olmumua lai!"
Acts7:60 Negil kung' nedar tʼoltoilo lʼengolon: Laitoriani-- mishumaki ninje ena kitarruoto enye! Ore ejoito kuna nee."
Acts8:1 Nenyorru Saulos metaari ninye metua. Neaku too nona olong'i emirata kitok esirit natii Yerusalem; neisardakakino pookin atua olosho Yudaya o Samaria nemetii lairriwak.
Acts8:2 Nenuk leak looure Engai Stefanos neishiraki ninye naleng'.
Acts8:3 Neitobiraki Saulos esirit ntorrok naleng'-- ejing' ngajijik o ngajijik neikurtutaa leak o ng'oroyok apik engaji eenata."
Acts8:4 Ore looisardaka neim idye o idye-- einosu lomon lʼeng'ida."
Acts8:5 Nedoiyo Filipos nejing' engang' nabo e Samaria neinosaki ninje Kristos.
Acts8:6 Neinining' siamin tʼoltau obo mbaak naairoro Filipos nening' edolita ntokitin kituak naaitobira ninye.
Acts8:7 Amu etupukutuo ilmeneng'a eishirita tʼoltoilo kitok too lkumok ooitamioki; neishiu ilkumok ootununuko osupetai o looitong'ojin;
Acts8:8 neaku eng'ida kitok tiatua ena ang'.
Acts8:9 Netii oltung'ani obo oji engarna enye Simon oitobira ntasimi enyena oshi ake tiatua ena ang' neing'asiaye iltung'anak le Samaria neitaa kion olora kitok;
Acts8:10 neinining'u pookin ninye eiter tʼoloti metabaiki ilbotoro nejo: Eata ele tung'ani engolon kitok Engai.
Acts8:11 Neing'oraa ninye-- tiaraki naing'asiaye ninje ngolong'i kumok too ntasimi enyena."
Acts8:12 Ore peiruk ninje Filipos einosu mbaak enkarsishu Engai o engarna e Yesus Kristos-- neibatisi leak o ng'oroyok."
Acts8:13 Neiruk baiki Simon openy-- ore peibatisi ninye-- nerubare Filipos-- neiputukuny edolita ntokitin kituak o nkitobirat engolon naataa."
Acts8:14 Ore pening' si ninje-- lairriwak ootii Yerusalem-- aajo eiruko Samaria lomon lʼEngai-- neirriwaki ninje Petros o Yohanes."
Acts8:15 Ore pebaia ninje-- nesayaki ninje-- peng'amu Olmumua Sinyati--"
Acts8:16 amu eton eitu edoiki o obo too ninje-- eibatisaki ake tʼengarna Olaitoriani Yesus."
Acts8:17 Neiteleiki ninje ngaik enye neng'amu ninje Olmumua Sinyati.
Acts8:18 Ore pedol Simon-- ajo eishooki Olmumua Sinyati tʼenkiteleikinoto oo ngaik-- neitarasaki ninje ngoshola"
Acts8:19 nejo: Enjooki si nanu ena golon-- peaku ore pookin laiteleiki ngaik neng'amu Olmumua Sinyati."
Acts8:20 Nejoki Petros ninye: Njeimin ngoshola inono o iye-- tiaraki ijo iye-- ajo einyang'uni enkishooroto Engai too ngoshola."
Acts8:21 Miata eng'arata o ematua tiatua ele rorei-- amu meitoriori oltau lino tʼengomom Engai."
Acts8:22 Akae-- taalai tʼena torroni ino-- pisai Engai-- peiye-- ajo nanu-- piking'uaikini enkibirribirrata oltau lino;"
Acts8:23 amu adolita-- ajo kibore olodua nikienita ntorrok."
Acts8:24 Nealu Simon nejo: Entasayakaki tʼOlaitoriani-- pamaabaiki kuna baak nitejo ndai."
Acts8:25 Ore peidip ninje aaijakenutu o aainosutu lomon lʼOlaitoriani-- nerrinyo aapuo Yerusalem neinosu lomon lʼeng'ida too ngang'itie kumok e Samaria."
Acts8:26 Neirorie olmalaika lʼOlaitoriani Filipos nejoki: Nyototoi-- pilo-- abori metabaiki engoitoi nadoiyo eing'ua Yerusalem metabaiki Gasa-- nera ninye ang'ata."
Acts8:27 Nedumunye nelo. Naa ng'orai-- netii oltung'ani le Etiopia ogelema-- olkitok le Kandake-- enkarsis oo Laitiopoi-- ora olarriponi loo masaa enyena pookin-- eewuo ninye Yerusalem-- pesaisho;"
Acts8:28 neaku errinyo neton tiatua olgarri lenye-- eisomita olayolounoni Yesaya."
Acts8:29 Nejoki Olmumua Filipos: Nno enetaaniki-- teshepare ele garri."
Acts8:30 Nekwetiki Filipos ina alo nening' eisomita olayolounoni Yesaya neirorie: Itayolo enisomita?
Acts8:31 Nejo ninye: Kaji aiko teni aidim-- teni metii oltung'ani laaitayolo? Nediding' ninye Filipos-- peilepaki-- peton o ninye."
Acts8:32 Ore ewueji neisoma nera ena: Etereaki ninye anaa enker nayeng'i o anaa esuben e ker nemeorito tʼengomom oloisolito ilpapit-- neijia eitu ebol si ninye enkutuk enye."
Acts8:33 Neitauni tiatua enkitadounoto earata enye. Kang'ai loinosu entipat enye? Amu eitaiyoki empuan enye tʼenkop.
Acts8:34 Nealiki ninye Filipos nejoki: Aasai iye-- kang'ai eimaki olayolounoni too kuna baak? ke kion arashu olekai tung'ani?"
Acts8:35 Nebol Filipos enkutuk enye neinosaki ninye lomon lʼeng'ida le Yesus.
Acts8:36 Ore epuoito ninje tʼengoitoi-- nebaia enetii engare-- nejo Olarriponi loo masaa: Ng'orai-- nyena engare. Ainyo naamitiki-- pamaaibatisi?"
Acts8:37 Nejoki Filipos: Teni iruk tʼoltau pookin-- naa sidai. Nealu nejo: Airuk-- ajo era Yesus Kristos Oinoti lʼEngai."
