Acts8:38 Neitanapu-- peitashe olgarri-- nedoiki pokira are atua engare-- Filipos o olarriponi loo masaa-- neibatisi ninye."
Acts8:39 Ore pepuku ninje tiatua engare-- nea Olmumua lʼOlaitoriani Filipos neitu eitoki adol olarriponi loo masaa ninye-- kake eima ninye engoitoi enye eng'ida."
Acts8:40 Netumi Filipos te Asotos neim einosu lomon lʼeng'ida tiatua ngang'itie pookin metabana nebaia Kaisarea.
Acts9:1 Nedumakino Saulos aiture near metuata laiteng'enuok lʼOlaitoriani nelo enetii olaidasani kitok
Acts9:2 neyeu te ninye mbaruai-- penap Damaskos atua ngajijik Engai-- periku ninje Yerusalem eena-- teni etum iltung'anak lʼena oitoi-- leak arashu ng'oroyok."
Acts9:3 Ore etii olototo nenyikaki Damaskos-- neilang'aki ninye nabokata enkilang'et te shumata;"
Acts9:4 nebatatakino enkop nening' oltoilo ejoki ninye: Saul-- Saul-- ainyo pikimirita?"
Acts9:5 Nejo ninye: Laitoriani-- ira iye ng'ai? Nejoki ninye: Ara nanu Yesus likimirita iye; egol te iye-- piruaia olkikarret."
Acts9:6 Nejo ninye tʼenkikirikirata o tʼenkuretishu: Laitoriani-- ainyo iyeu naitobir? Nejoki Olaitoriani ninye: Tudumunye-- pijing' atua engang'-- kilikini te ina alo enintobir."
Acts9:7 Neitashe lʼemboitei enye aaitirring'a nening' oltoilo neitu edol oltung'ani.
Acts9:8 Nedumunye Saulos tʼenkop; ore pebol ngonyek enyena-- neitu edol toki; neibung' ninje engaina enye nerik ninye Damaskos."
Acts9:9 Neaku ngolong'i uni medolisho nemenya nemeok.
Acts9:10 Netii Damaskos olaiteng'enuoni oji engarna enye Ananias. Nejoki Olaitoriani ninye tiatua enduaroto: Ananias! Nejo: Nyele nanu-- Laitoriani!"
Acts9:11 Nejoki Olaitoriani ninye: Tudumunye-- pilo engoitoi naipoti Naitoriori-- pinkilikwanu L'engaji e Yudas oltung'ani oji Saulos le Tarsos; amu etii esaisho--"
Acts9:12 netadua si ninye tiatua enduaroto oltung'ani oji engarna enye Ananias-- ejing'ita neiteleiki ninye ngaik-- peishori edolisho."
Acts9:13 Nealu Ananias: Laitoriani-- atoning'o nanu mbaak ele tung'ani too lkumok-- eneikuna teni eitobiraki ntorrok isinyat linono lootii Yerusalem;"
Acts9:14 neitoki aata tene engolon too laidasak kituak naenie pookin looipot engama ino.
Acts9:15 Nejoki Olaitoriani ninye: Nno ake-- amu era ninye enaret nategelua nanu-- peea engarna ai atua loreren lemeata Engai o atua ilkarsisi o atua nkera Israel;"
Acts9:16 amu alaitadol ninye-- ajo elatum sinaitin kumok tʼolbae lʼengama ai."
Acts9:17 Nelo Ananias nejing' atu aji neiteleiki ninye ngaik nejo: Lalashe Saul-- aairriua Olaitoriani Yesus likimpang'aka tʼengoitoi niimua-- pikinjori idolisho-- pikingany Olmumua Sinyati."
Acts9:18 Nedou nabokata too ngonyek enyena ntokitin nijo ilpalak neitoki adolisho neinyototo neibatisi.
Acts9:19 Ore peidip atang'amu endaa-- netum engolon. Nebik Saulos te nebo o laiteng'enuok ootii Damaskos ngolong'i naaje."
Acts9:20 Neinosu ninye nabokata too ngajijik Engai lomon le Yesus-- ajo era ninye Oinoti lʼEngai."
Acts9:21 Ore pookin lootoning'o neiputukuny nejo: Me ele loiminye kulo te Yerusalem looipoto ena arna neotiki alotu ena alo-- perikoki laidasak kituak ninje looena?"
Acts9:22 Nepon atum Saulos engolon neapare Yudayoi ootii Damaskos agilu nenyok-- ajo era ele Kristos."
Acts9:23 Ore peim ngolong'i kumok-- neigwena Yudayoi-- pear metua;"
Acts9:24 kake etayolo Saulos olosek lenye; nerreshu dama o kiarie too kishomini-- pear ninye metua."
Acts9:25 Neibung' laiteng'enuok ninye kiarie neitadoiyo tʼesundai tʼolbene.
Acts9:26 Ore pebaia Saulos Yerusalem-- neyeu neidikidikore laiteng'enuok-- neurei pookin ninye-- neitu eiruk baiki-- ajo era olaiteng'enuoni."
Acts9:27 Neibung' Barnabas ninye nerik enetii lairriwak neinosaki eneikuna ninye nedol Olaitoriani tʼengoitoi oirorie ninye-- o eneikuna neiteng'enisho meureisho te Damaskos tʼengarna e Yesus."
Acts9:28 Nebik ninye te nebo o ninje te Yerusalem-- ejing' nepuku-- neiro tʼengarna Olaitoriani Yesus-- meureisho--"
Acts9:29 negilunore Ilgrikini-- neyeu si ninje near ninye metua."
Acts9:30 Ore peyolou lalashera kuna-- nerik ninye metabaiki Kaisarea neirriwaa ninye Tarsos."
Acts9:31 Akae-- netum esirit eseriani tiatua Yudaya pookin o Galilaya o Samaria-- neshetuni nepona nebik tiatua enkuretishu Olaitoriani o tiatua enkilejilejata Olmumua Sinyati."
Acts9:32 Ore eimita Petros wuejitin pookin-- nedoiki enetii sinyat ootobiko te Lida."
Acts9:33 Nedol te ina alo oltung'ani oji engarna enye Aineas oirraga tʼerruat larin isiet eseja osupetai.
Acts9:34 Nejoki Petros ninye: Aineas-- kinjiunye Yesus Kristos-- tudumunye-- pintobiraki kion erruat! Neinyototo nabokata."
Acts9:35 Nedol pookin ninye lootamanya Lida o Saron-- neibelekenyakino Olaitoriani."
Acts9:36 Netii Yope engaiteng'enuoni neji engarna enye Tabita-- ore enkitaalata enye: engoilii; neiganya ninye nkitobirat sidan o nkishoorot naaishooiye."
Acts9:37 Nesejai ninye too nona olong'i nee; neisuji ninye nepiki shumaroto.
Acts9:38 Netaaniki Lida Yope; ore pening' laiteng'enuok-- aajo etii Petros ina alo-- neirriwaa iltung'anak aare enetii ninye nediding'u-- pemeimutie elotu enetii ninje."
Acts9:39 Neinyototo Petros nerubare ninje; ore pebaia ninje nerik ninye shumaroto-- neitasheiki ninye ngolia pookin eishirita eitaduaia lokesenani o ilkarashi ooitobira Engoilii tʼena kata natii e nebo o ninje."
Acts9:40 Neitupuku Petros pookin negil kung' nesaisho-- neibelekenyakino empopong' nejo: Tabita-- nyototoi! Nebol ngonyek enyena; ore pedol ninye Petros-- neton."
Acts9:41 Neitarasaki ninye engaina enye neapaa ninye; ore peidip aipoto sinyat o ngolia-- neriku eishiu."
Acts9:42 Neyolouni ena tiatua Yope pookin-- neiruk ilkumok Olaitoriani."
Acts9:43 Neaku ebik ngolong'i kumok te Yope t'engang' oltung'ani obo oji engarna enye Simon-- oladotoni loo lonito."
Acts10:1 Etii oltung'ani obo atua Kaisarea neji engarna enye Kornelios-- olkitok lʼendung'oti empuoto naji Italia--"
Acts10:2 supat neure Engai te nebo o engaji enye pookin-- neisho olorere nkishoorot kumok nesai Engai ngolong'i pookin--"
Acts10:3 nedol tiatua enduaroto abaraki-- tʼenkata esaa enturuj dama-- ejing'aki olmalaika lʼEngai ninye tʼengaji enye nejoki ninye: Kornelios!"
Acts10:4 Neing'oraa ninye neureishoi nejo: Kainyo natii-- Laitoriani? Nejoki ninye: Eilepa sayat o nkishoorot inono engomom Engai nedamu ninje."
Acts10:5 Akae-- rriwai iltung'anak-- pepuo Yope neipot Simon oata engai arna enye Petros--"
Acts10:6 otii engang' oltung'ani oji engarna enye Simon-- ora oladotoni loo lonito-- etii engaji enye embata olbalbal; kilaliki ninye enintobir."
Acts10:7 Ore peidip ashomo ele malaika oirorie Kornelios-- neipot ninye laisyayak lenyena aare lʼengaji enye o osikeri lenye obo supat too kulo looisyayaki ninye oshi;"
Acts10:8 ore peidip ainosaki ninje mbaak pookin-- neirriwaa ninje-- pepuo Yope."
Acts10:9 Ore tʼengai olong'-- epon etii ninje engoitoi netaaniki engang'-- neilepaki Petros keper aji alo asaisho-- tʼenkata-- naunore engolong'."
Acts10:10 Netum olamei kitok neyeu nedaa-- kake ore epon eitobirakini endaa-- neururu tʼolmumua"
Acts10:11 nedol shumata etabole nedoiki engusa anaa erridata olkarash nateenaki too matuan ong'wan-- neitadouni enkop."
Acts10:12 Ore atua enye netii muain pookin oo ng'wesi naata nkejek ong'wan o iljang'it lʼosero o naaikurtutari o ntaritik e shumata.
Acts10:13 Nening' oltoilo ojoki ninye: Nyototoi-- Petros-- teyeng'a-- nosa!"
Acts10:14 Nejo Petros: Me neijia-- Laitoriani-- amu eitu aikata anya tukul enaiduruk o enemera sidai."
Acts10:15 Neitoki aning' ninye oltoilo en e are: Ore naaitisidana Engai-- mintaa iye torrok."
Acts10:16 Etaa kuna aigil uni; ore tekurum o kuna nerrinyori engusa shumata.
Acts10:17 Ore epon eitu eyolou Petros tʼoltau lenye eneiko tʼolbai lʼenduaroto natadua-- ng'orai-- neing'oru kulo tung'anak looirriwaiye Kornelios-- engaji e Simon-- neitashe te kishomi--"
Acts10:18 neipotisho neikilikwan anake etii Simon oata engai arna Petros ene anaa olomoni.
Acts10:19 Ore te ina kata eibirribirrita Petros enduaroto-- nejoki Olmumua ninye: Ng'orai-- etii iltung'anak okuni liking'oru;"
Acts10:20 tudumunye-- tadoi abori-- nno te nebo o ninje-- ming'arrirro-- amu nanu oirriua ninje."
Acts10:21 Nedoiki Petros kulo tung'anak ooirriwaka Kornelios enetii ninye nejoki: Eng'orai-- nanu ilo oling'oruru. Ke tʼolbae le nyoo itiiti ene?"
Acts10:22 Nejo ninje: Kornelios-- olkitok loo sikerin-- oltung'ani supat-- oloure Engai-- oata enkitadararoto sidai tiatua olorere pookin loo Yudayoi-- einoto ninye olkilikwai lʼolmalaika sinyati-- pikiriku engaji enye-- pikinining'u rorei linono."
Acts10:23 Neitijing' neitoomon ninje. Ore tʼengai olong' nedumunye te nebo o ninje nerubare ninye lalashera ooje ootii Yope.
Acts10:24 Ore tʼengolong' e are nejing' Kaisarea; neanyu Kornelios ninje eiturrurro enkishomi enye o iljorueta lenyena.
Acts10:25 Ore ejing'ita Petros-- nenang'are Kornelios ninye nebatatakino nkejek enyena neitaa ninye kitok."
Acts10:26 Neapu Petros ninye nejoki: Ntasho-- amu ara si nanu oltung'ani."
Acts10:27 Ore peidip airorie ninye-- nejing' nedol ilkumok ooiturrurrote."
Acts10:28 Nejoki ninje: Iyololo ndai-- aajo me sidai tʼoltung'ani lora Oyudayos-- teni eder arashu elotu enetii loora loo kulekai oreren; kake aaitadua Engai-- pamaipot oltung'ani o obo anaa oloiduruk arashu oltorrono."
Acts10:29 Onaa aewuo neitu aany aaipotoki. Akae-- aikilikwan taata: ke tʼolbae le nyoo kimpoto?"
Acts10:30 Nejo Kornelios: Engolong' e ong'wan taata eitu anya endaa metabaiki ena kata-- ore tʼesaa enturuj nasaisho tʼengaji ai-- naa ng'orai-- neitashe oltung'ani tʼengomom ai oata ilkarashi ooilang'isho--"
Acts10:31 nejo: Kornelios-- etoning'oki sayat inono nedamuni nkishoorot inono tʼengomom Engai."
Acts10:32 Akae-- rriwai iltung'anak-- pepuo Yope-- peipot te ine Simon oata engai arna Petros-- otii engaji e Simon-- oladotoni loo lonito-- natii embata olbalbal: teni elotu ninye-- nikilairorie."
Acts10:33 Nairriwaa nabokata enitii iye nintobira sidai iewuo. Akae-- kitii yook pookin taata ene engomom Engai-- pikining' mbaak pookin nikintanapa Engai."
Acts10:34 Nebol Petros enkutuk enye nejo: Esipa-- atayolo abaraki-- ajo meing'oraa Engai emua oo ltung'anak--"
Acts10:35 kake ore tiatua loreren pookin enyor oloure ninye o oloitobir esupato.
Acts10:36 Itayoloutuo ndai ele rorei loirriwaka Engai nkera Israel-- peinosu eseriani te Yesus Kristos ora Olaitoriani loo pookin--"
Acts10:37 oibulu atua Yudaya pookin neiter te Galilaya-- tekurum enkibatisa nainosua Yohanes--"
Acts10:38 ajo eela Engai Yesus le Nasaret tʼOlmumua Sinyati o tʼengolon-- oima idyalo o idyalo eitobir sidan-- eishiunye pookin looitamio satan-- amu etaboitare Engai ninye."
Acts10:39 Nikira yook iljaken loo mbaak pookin naaitobira ninye tiatua olosho loo Yudayoi o Yerusalem. Near ninje ninye metua neik tʼenjata.
Acts10:40 Eitopiwuo Engai ele tʼengolong' e uni neitadolu ninye tʼewuas--"
Acts10:41 me tʼolorere pookin-- kake too ljaken ooitera Engai agelu nera yook likitadaate nikiokisho te nebo o ninye-- eidipa atopiu too lootuata."
Acts10:42 Neitanap ninye yook-- pikinosaki olorere nikinjakenoki-- aajo ninye eitanapua Engai-- peaku olaigwenani loo looishiu o loo lootuata."
Acts10:43 Eijakenu te ninye layolounok pookin-- aajo eishori oltung'ani pookin loiruk-- enkitaunoto oo nkitarruot tʼengarna enye."
Acts10:44 Ore epon eirorita Petros kulo rorei-- nedoiki Olmumua Sinyati pookin ootoning'o ena bae."
Acts10:45 Neiputukuny kulo airukok lʼemurata ooetuo te nebo o Petros-- tiaraki natubukokoki baiki loreren lemeata Engai enkishooroto Olmumua Sinyati;"
Acts10:46 amu etoning'o eirorita ninje too nkutukie neitadaraa Engai. Nejo Petros:
Acts10:47 Keidim oltung'ani atomito engare-- pemeibatisi kulo lootang'amutua Olmumua Sinyati-- neijia ake anaa yook?"
Acts10:48 Neitanapisho-- peibatisi ninje tʼengarna e Yesus Kristos. Nesai ninye-- pebik ngolong'i naaje."
Acts11:1 Nening' lairriwak o lalashera ootii Yudaya-- aajo etang'amutua si ninje loreren lomon lʼEngai."
Acts11:2 Ore peilep Petros Yerusalem-- negilunore ninye loora lʼemurata"
Acts11:3 ejo: Itijing'a atua iltung'anak lememurata ning'arie endaa.
Acts11:4 Neiter Petros ainosaki ninje mbaak tʼolkereri ejo:
Acts11:5 Atobiko tiatua engang' Yope asaisho neururu Olmumua lai nadol enduaroto: nedou engusa anaa erridata olkarash-- neitadouni te shumata too mowuarak ong'wan-- nelotu enatii nanu;"
Acts11:6 ore pakurraki aing'oraa-- nadol ng'wesi lʼenkop naata nkejek ong'wan o iljang'it lʼosero o naaikurtutari o ntaritik e shumata."
Acts11:7 Naning' oltoilo laajoki: Nyototoi-- Petros-- teyeng'a-- nosa!"
Acts11:8 Najo si nanu: Me neijia-- Laitoriani-- amu ore entoki naiduruk arashu enemera sidai eton eitu ejing' enkutuk ai tukul."
Acts11:9 Naaitoki aliki nanu oltoilo oing'ua shumata: Ore naaitisidana Engai-- mintaa iye torrok."
Acts11:10 Neaku kuna aigil uni-- neitokini ailepie pookin shumata."
Acts11:11 Ore nabokata eitasheito iltung'anak okuni te boo engaji natii nanu laairriwakaki eing'ua Kaisarea.
Acts11:12 Naajoki ake Olmumua: Nno te nebo o ninje-- ming'arrirro! Nikiruba te nebo o kulo alashera ile nikijing' engaji e ilo lee."
Acts11:13 Neinosaki ninye yook eneikuna teni edol olmalaika oitasho tiatua engaji enye nejoki ninye: Rriwai iltung'anak-- pepuo Yope neipot Simon oata engai arna Petros--"
Acts11:14 likiliki rorei likintopok iye o engaji ino pookin.
Acts11:15 Ore paiter nanu airo-- nedoiki Olmumua Sinyati ninje anaa petadoikio yook tʼenkiterata."
Acts11:16 Nadamu te ina kata ororei lʼOlaitoriani otejo: Eibatisishe Yohanes tʼengare-- kake eibatisi ndai tʼOlmumua Sinyati."
Acts11:17 Akae-- ore peishoo Engai ninje ena kishooroto anaa yook looiruko Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos: kara nanu ng'ai oidim atomitiki Engai?"
Acts11:18 Ore pening' ninje kuna-- negira neitadaraa Engai nejo: Eishoo Engai baiki loreren lemeata ninye enkitaalata-- petum empuan."
Acts11:19 Ore kulo ooisardaka tʼolbae lʼosina otupukuo too mbaak e Stefanos-- nepuo metabaiki Foinike o Kupros o Antiokia neitu einosaki ororei olekai tung'ani neme Yudayoi ake."
Acts11:20 Etii ake ilkulekai ooje atua ninje-- leak le Kupros o le Kirene. Ore pebaia ninje Antiokia-- neirorie ninje baiki Ilgrikini neinosaki ninje Olaitoriani Yesus."
Acts11:21 Netii engaina Olaitoriani e nebo o ninje neiruk esiana kitok neibelekenyakino Olaitoriani.
Acts11:22 Nebaiki kuna baak nkiyaa esirit natii Yerusalem-- neirriwaa Barnabas-- pelo metabaiki Antiokia."
Acts11:23 Ore peidip atabai ninye nedol eng'adunoto naishorua Engai-- neng'ida nediding' pookin-- pebik ninje tiatua Olaitoriani osupatei too ltauja lenye."
Acts11:24 Amu era ninye oltung'ani supat nebore Olmumua Sinyati o enkirukoto. Nerikokini esiamu narrish Olaitoriani.
Acts11:25 Nepuku Barnabas alo Tarsos-- peing'oru Saulos--"
Acts11:26 ore petum ninye-- neriku Antiokia. Neaku eiturrurro ninje o esirit olari olulung'a neiteng'en esiamu narrish. Neipoti laiteng'enuok tʼenkata elukunya te Antiokia ilkristianoi."
Acts11:27 Nedou to kuna olong'i layolounok eing'ua Yerusalem nepuonu Antiokia.
Acts11:28 Neitashe obo too ninje oji engarna enye Agabos neitayolo ninye tʼenkidimata Olmumua-- ajo elotu olamei kitok atua olmaa pookin; neaku neijia too ngolong'i e kaisar Klaudios."
Acts11:29 Nenyorru aaitobira laiteng'enuok-- oltung'ani pookin anaa peidim-- enkishooroto-- peakini lalashera ootii Yudaya;"
Acts11:30 neiko nji neirriwaki laigwenak too ngaik e Barnabas o Saulos.
Acts12:1 Ore te ina kata neitorioo olkarsis Herodes ngaik enyena-- peitobiraki ntorrok iltung'anak lʼesirit."
Acts12:2 Near ninye Yakobos-- olalashe le Yohanes-- t'olalem metua."
Acts12:3 Ore pedol-- ajo eiting'ida Yudayoi-- nepon aibung' baiki Petros. Netii ngolong'i oo lmkaten lemeisiijo."
Acts12:4 Ore peidip aibung'a ninye-- nepik engaji erripore neitarasaki ilkamban ong'wan loo sikerin-- neata olkamba obo sikerin ong'wan-- perrip ninye neotiki arik engomom olorere-- eidipe pasaka."
Acts12:5 Akae-- nerripi Petros tʼengaji erripore; nesayaki esirit ninye Engai too sayat nemegira."
Acts12:6 Ore pebau engolong' nayeu Herodes neitupuku ninye boo-- neirrag Petros te ina kiarie tʼempolos oo sikerin aare-- eena too lpisia aare-- netii larripok kishomi-- perripi engaji erripore."
Acts12:7 Naa ng'orai-- nebau olmalaika lʼOlaitoriani neilang'isho enkilang'et tiatua olgilata neosh Petros laras neinyeye ninye ejoki; Tudumunye asioki! Nedoiyo ilpisia too ngaik enyena."
Acts12:8 Nejoki olmalaika ninye: Teenai-- njopo namuka! Neiko nji. Neitoki ajoki ninye: Njopo emekiti ino-- tusujaki!"
Acts12:9 Nepuku asuj neitu eyolou-- ajo esipa nena naaitobira olmalaika-- kake etejo ninye etadua enduaroto."
Acts12:10 Ore pelusoo erripoto elukunya o en e are-- nebaiki kishomi esekengei najing' engang'; nebolo openy. Nepuku neim engoitoi nabo-- neing'ua nabokata olmalaika ninye."
Acts12:11 Ore peitoki arrinyokino Petros kion-- nejo: Atayolo taata tʼesipata-- ajo eirriua Olaitoriani olmalaika lenye naaitopok nanu too ngaik e Herodes o tʼeanyunoto pookin olorere loo Yudayoi."
Acts12:12 Ore eibirribirrita kuna-- nelotu ninye engaji e Maria-- ng'otonye e Yohanes-- loata engai arna Markos-- naiturrurrore esiamu narrish esaisho."
Acts12:13 Ore peoshiosh Petros oldiripe le kutukaji-- nelotu engaisyayani nabo naji Rode-- peinining'."
Acts12:14 Ore peyolou oltoilo le Petros-- neitu ebol kutukaji tʼolbae lʼeng'ida-- nerrinyo asioio neinosu-- ajo eitashe Petros tʼengalo kishomi e boo."
Acts12:15 Nejoki ninje ninye: Iata oloirirua! Nenyok ajo: neijia etiu. Nejo ninje: Olmalaika lenye!
Acts12:16 Nepon Petros aoshiosh; ore pebol ninje-- nedol ninye neiputukuny."
Acts12:17 Ore peidip atoroja ninye tʼengaina-- pegira ninje-- neinosaki eneikuna teni eitai Olaitoriani ninye tiatua engaji erripore-- nejoki: Enosakiti kuna baak Yakobos o lalashera! Nepuku nelo engai wueji."
Acts12:18 Ore pekenyu-- neng'ayung'ayu sikerin naleng': ketaa nyoo Petros."
Acts12:19 Ore peing'oru Herodes ninye-- neitu etum-- neikilikwan ninye larripok neitanap-- periki aar; nedou eing'ua Yudaya nelo metabaiki Kaisarea neton te ina alo."
Acts12:20 Negoroki Herodes iltung'anak le Tiros o Sidon; nepuonu ninje enetii ninye tʼoltau obo-- eidipa aitau osotua o Blastos-- ora olarriponi lʼolgilata loirragieki lʼolkarsis-- neomon eseriani-- tiaraki naitoti olosho lʼolkarsis olenye."
Acts12:21 Ore tʼengolong' nategeluaki neishop Herodes ilkarashi lʼolkarsis netonie olorika lʼenkitook neirorie olorere.
Acts12:22 Neosh olorere olodoo nejo: Oltoilo lʼEngai-- mekure aa oltoilo lʼoltung'ani!"
Acts12:23 Neosh nabokata olmalaika lʼOlaitoriani ninye-- tiaraki neitu eisho ninye Engai enkitook; nenya ilkuru ninye nedung'o tau."
Acts12:24 Nebulu lomon lʼEngai nepona.
Acts12:25 Nerrinyo Barnabas o Saulos eing'ua Yerusalem-- eidipa aaitarasai nkishoorot-- erikito ninje Yohanes oata engai arna Markos."
Acts13:1 Netii Antiokia atua esirit layolounok o laiteng'enak-- Barnabas o Simeon oipotoki Niger o Lukios le Kirene o Manaen oitubuluaki te nebo o Herodes-- olkarsis lʼematua e ong'wan-- o Saulos."
Acts13:2 Ore peisyayaki ninje Olaitoriani neitupukoo aten-- neiro Olmumua Sinyati: Entegelakaki Barnabas o Saulos-- peitobir ninje ena kyas naipotoko nanu ninje."
Acts13:3 Neitupukoo aten nesaisho neiteleiki ninje ngaik neisho epuo.
Acts13:4 Ore kulo looirriwaiye Olmumua Sinyati nepuo metabaiki Seloikia nejing te ina alo engalawa nepuo Kupros;
Acts13:5 Ore etii engang' Salamis-- neinosu lomon lʼEngai tiatua ngajijik Engai oo Yudayoi; neata ninje baiki Yohanes loisyayaki ninje."
Acts13:6 Neim ninje oloigeruno pookin metabaiki Pafos nedol oltung'ani obo lora oloiboni o olayolounoni lʼelejare-- Oyudayos-- neji engarna enye Baryesus;"
Acts13:7 netii ninye te nebo o olaigwenani Sergios Paulos-- oltung'ani lʼeng'eno; eipoto ele Barnabas o Saulos neyeu nening' lomon lʼEngai."
Acts13:8 Negilunore Elimas ninje-- lora oloiboni-- amu nyena enkitaalata engarna enye-- neyeu neitapal olaigwenani enkirukoto."
Acts13:9 Kake ore Saulos-- oji baiki Paulos-- nebore Olmumua Sinyati-- nekurraki ngonyek shumata enye"
Acts13:10 nejo: Iye-- enkerai e satan-- nabore olosek o olduruki pookin-- olmang'atinda lʼesupato pookin-- mipal mishukushuk ngoitoi Olaitoriani naara sidan?"
Acts13:11 Akae-- ng'orai-- elotu engaina Olaitoriani shumata ino niaku modooni-- midol engolong' enkiti kata. Nedoiki ninye nabokata olairambai o enaimin-- nemanaa ninye neing'oru oloibung' engaina enye."
Acts13:12 Ore pedol olaigwenani enataa-- neiruk neiputukunyoki enkiteng enare Olaitoriani."
Acts13:13 Nejing' Paulos o lʼemboitei enye engalawa eing'ua Pafos nebaia Perge e Pamfilia; neing'ua Yohanes ninje nerrinyo Yerusalem.
Acts13:14 Neing'ua ninje Perge nebaia Antiokia e Pisidia nejing' tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki atua engaji Engai netoni.
Acts13:15 Ore peidipi aaisoma nkitanapat o layolounok-- neirriwaki ilkituak lʼengaji Engai aajoki ninje: Lelea-- lalashera-- teni etii obo too ndai loata ororei orojie olorere-- entolimu!"
Acts13:16 Neitashe Paulos neroj tʼengaina enye neiro: Lelea le Israel o ndai liurere Engai-- enining'o!"
Acts13:17 Etegelua Engai ele orere Israel loopapa lang' neitaa kitok olorere te ina kata nara lomon tʼolosho Misri-- nerik aitung'ua ninje tʼengaina enye nataapaiyoki."
Acts13:18 Eting'iriaka ninje larin artam ti ang'ata
Acts13:19 neiminye loreren oopishana tiatua olosho Kanaan neitujung' ninje olosho lenye.
Acts13:20 Ore tekurum neisho ninje larin iip ong'wan o onom laigwenak metabaiki olayolounoni Samuel.
Acts13:21 Tekurum neyeu ninje olkarsis-- neisho Engai ninje Saul-- enkerai e Kis-- oltung'ani lʼenkishomi e Benyamin-- larin artam."
Acts13:22 Ore peidip aitau ilo-- neunoki ninje David aitaa olkarsis lenye-- neijakenu te ninye nejo: Ainoto David le Isai (Yese)-- oltung'ani onyor oltau lai-- oloitobir pookin nayeu."
Acts13:23 Neunoki Engai Israel tiatua eishoi enye-- neijia anaa peisiligua-- Olaitopuani Yesus--"
Acts13:24 eidipa Yohanes aituruko ainosaki olorere pookin le Israel enkibatisa enkitaalata-- eton eitu elotu ninye."
Acts13:25 Ore peidip Yohanes olototo lenye-- nejo: Mara nanu ilo lijojo ndai-- kake eng'orai-- elotu tekurum ai ele lamaiteu nanu atalaku namuka oo nkejek enyena."
Acts13:26 Lelea-- lalashera-- nakera eishoi e Abraham o ndai liurere Engai-- eirriwakaki ndai ororei lʼena kitopuata."
Acts13:27 Ore kulo lootii Yerusalem o ilkituak lenye-- eitu eyolou ele arashu rorei loo layolounok ooisomai too ngolong'i pookin naaeng'ieng'areki neitabaia ninje tʼenkigwena enye."
Acts13:28 Ore peitu etum entoki naarie ninye metua-- nesai ninje ake Pilatos-- pear ninye metua."
Acts13:29 Ore peidip ninje pookin natisirakaki ninye-- neitadou ninye tʼenjata nepik atua engapunet."
Acts13:30 Neitopiu ake Engai ninye tiatua lootuata;
Acts13:31 nelioi ngolong'i kumok too kulo ooilepa o ninye eing'ua Galilaya metabaiki Yerusalem-- loora taata iljaken lenyena tiatua olorere."
Acts13:32 Kinosaki si yook ndai ena kisiligata nataa too loopapa lang'--"
Acts13:33 aajo eidipa aitisipai Engai ninye too yook-- nkera enye-- etopiwuo Yesus-- anaa petisiraki tiatua Osingolio le are: Ira iye Oinoti lai-- aatoiwuo iye taata."
Acts13:34 Ore tiaraki naitopiwuo ninye aitung'ua lootuata-- pemeala arruoio-- neiro nji: Ayeu naisho ndai eng'adunoto naisiliga David-- naibung' ninye osupatei."
Acts13:35 Onaa ejo tʼengai wueji: Minjooio osinyati lino-- pedol erruoroto."
Acts13:36 Amu ore David-- peidip tʼenkata enye aisyayaki eyeunoto Engai-- neirura ninye nepiki enetii loomenye nedol erruoroto;"
Acts13:37 kake eitu edol ele loitopiwuo Engai-- erruoroto."
Acts13:38 Akae-- njeyolouni too ndai-- lelea-- lalashera-- aajo einosakini ndai enkitaunoto oo nkitarruot tʼolbae lʼele."
Acts13:39 Neishori te ninye oltung'ani pookin loiruk ninye esupato neitu eidim aaishoo ndai nkitanapat e Mose.
Acts13:40 Eng'orai-- pemepuonu shumata inyi kuna naairoro layolounok:"
Acts13:41 „Eng'orai-- ndai lamenak-- emputukunyo niminimini! Amu aitobir nanu embae too ngolong'i inyi-- embae nimirukuruku-- teni einosaki oltung'ani ndai.“"
Acts13:42 Ore peidip ninje aatupukutu-- nesai iltung'anak ninje-- peitoki aaliki ninje kulo rorei tʼengai olong' naeng'ieng'areki."
Acts13:43 Ore peisardak esirit engaji Engai-- nesuj ilkumok loo Yudayoi o lʼemboitei oo Yudayoi looure Engai Paulos o Barnabas ooirorie nediding' ninje-- pebik tiatua eng'adunoto Engai."
Acts13:44 Ore tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki e are neiturrurro engang' pookin-- eng'or kuti ake-- pening' lomon lʼEngai."
Acts13:45 Ore pedol Yudayoi siamin-- neibung'aki ong'u neisimakinore enatejo Paulos nemorisho."
Acts13:46 Neiro Paulos o Barnabas meureisho ejo: Meata kata nemeng'asi aainosu ororei lʼEngai too ndai-- kake tiaraki nirrumokiki ninye enelakwa niming'oraara aten-- aajo iyeuu empuan nemeiting'-- eng'orai-- kimbelekenyakino loreren lemeata Engai."
Acts13:47 Amu neijia eitanapua yook Olaitoriani: Aatipika iye-- piaku enkilang'et oo loreren-- piaku iye enkitopuata metabaiki enkiting'oto enkop."
Acts13:48 Ore pening' loreren lemeata Engai kuna-- neng'ida neitadaraa ororei lʼOlaitoriani neiruk kulo ootushumaki-- pebaiki empuan nemeiting'."
Acts13:49 Neibulunyeki ororei lʼOlaitoriani atua ele osho pookin.
Acts13:50 Kake neiponyaa Yudayoi ng'oroyok naaure Engai naata enkitook o ilkituak lʼengang' neinyeye emirata namirie Paulos o Barnabas neitupuku ninje too mbatai enye.
Acts13:51 Neipiripiroo enterit oo nkejek enye-- pebaiki ninje-- nepuonu Ikonion."
Acts13:52 Neiganya laiteng'enuok eng'ida o Olmumua Sinyati.
Acts14:1 Neaku eiturrurro ninje te Ikonion tiatua engaji Engai oo Yudayoi neinosu nji-- aajo eiruko esiamu kitok oo Yudayoi o noo Lgrikini."
Acts14:2 Neiponyaa Yudayoi lemeiruk iltauja loo loreren metagoroki lalashera.
Acts14:3 Nebik te ina alo enkata naado peno neiteng'enu meureisho Olaitoriani-- oijakenoko lomon lʼeng'adunoto enye neisho metaa ntokitin kituak o nkiputukunyot too ngaik enye."
Acts14:4 Nerisha esiamu engang' nejing' kulekai ematua oo Yudayoi o kulekai ematua oo lairriwak.
Acts14:5 Neibung'aro loreren o Yudayoi o ilkituak lenye-- peitobiraki ninje ntorrok nenang' too soito--"
Acts14:6 neyolou ninje ena nekwetiki ngang'itie e Likaonia-- Listra o Derbe-- o olosho lotamana;"
Acts14:7 Netoni te ina alo neinosu lomon lʼeng'ida.
Acts14:8 Netii Listra oltung'ani obo-- menati nkejek-- leitu eidim ashomo eiter tʼengoshoke e ng'otonye-- eitu elo tukul."
Acts14:9 Neinining' ilo Paulos eirorita; nekurraki ninye ngonyek nedol-- ajo eata enkirukoto enkishiunoto--"
Acts14:10 neiro tʼoltoilo kitok ejo: Ntasho too nkejek inono aitoriori! Neipirriu ilo tung'ani shumata neiter alimana.
Acts14:11 Ore pedol isiamin enaitobira Paulos-- neapaa iltoiloi neiro tʼenkutuk e Likaonia: Etanyanyukie ngain iltung'anak nedoiki enikitii yook."
Acts14:12 Neipot Barnabas Tseus o Paulos Hermas-- amu ninye oljani loo rorei."
Acts14:13 Nereu olaidasani lʼengaji e Tseus natii aulo engang'-- ilmong'i o ilmarisiani loo ntapuka metabaiki kishomi neyeu neidas te nebo o siamin."
Acts14:14 Ore pening' lairriwak Barnabas o Paulos kuna-- nepolos ninje ilkilani lenye neityamaki siamin edarita"
Acts14:15 nejo: Lelea-- kainyo intobiritata te ina alo? Kira si yook iltung'anak loopuo aae anaa ndai-- kinosaki ndai-- pimbelekenyanya too kuna ain nemera o nyoo aapuo enetii Engai naishiu-- naitobira shumata o enkop o ilbalbali o pookin natii atua ninje;"
Acts14:16 neisho tʼenkopa naima loreren pookin epuo ngoitoi enye--"
Acts14:17 kake eitu epal ninje eijakenoki kion eitobir sidan-- neisho ndai enjan e shumata o nkatan eiunoto oo lmomo neigany iltauja linyi endaa o eng'ida."
Acts14:18 Ore ejoito kuna-- nemitiki siamin tʼosina-- pemeidasaki ninje."
Acts14:19 Nepuonu Yudayoi ooing'ua Antiokia o Ikonion neisis isiamin nenang' Paulos too soito neitupuku ninye aulo engang' nejo etua.
Acts14:20 Ore emanita laiteng'enuok-- neitashe nejing' atua engang' nelo tʼengolong' e are o Barnabas metabaiki Derbe."
Acts14:21 Neinosaki ninje ena ang' lomon lʼeng'ida neitaa ilkumok laiteng'enuok nerrinyo Listra o Ikonion o Antiokia.
Acts14:22 Neitagol iltauja loo laiteng'enuok ediding' pebik tiatua enkirukoto neitayolo ninje-- aajo meata kaata nimikijing' atua enkarsishu Engai too sinaitin kumok."
Acts14:23 Nerukoo sirito nepikaki ninje laigwenak-- esaisho nepukoo neitarasaki Olaitoriani oiruko ninye."
Acts14:24 Neim Pisidia nepuonu Pamfilia--"
Acts14:25 neinosu lomon te Perge nedou metabaiki Atalia
Acts14:26 nepuo te ine tʼengalawa Antiokia-- ene wueji netipikieki tʼeng'adunoto Engai enkyas naitabaitie."
Acts14:27 Ore pebaia ninje-- neiturrur esirit neinosaki enaitobira Engai too ninje-- ajo etaboloko Engai loreren lemeyolo ninye kutukaji enkirukoto."
Acts14:28 Nebik te ina alo enkata neme kiti te nebo o laiteng'enuok.
Acts15:1 Nedou iltung'anak ooje ooing'ua Yudaya neiteng'en lalashera nejo: Teni memurati ndai tʼorregie le Mose-- nimindimidimi aatopok."
Acts15:2 Ore peaku endung'o o enkitarrikino e Paulos o Barnabas o lelo-- neitanapaa ninje Paulos o Barnabas o kulekai tʼempolos enye-- pepuo tʼolbae lʼena kitarrikino Yerusalem enetii lairriwak o laigwenak."
Acts15:3 Neitare esirit ninje neim Foinike o Samaria neinosu enkitaalata oo loreren lemeata Engai neiting'id lalashera pookin naleng'.
Acts15:4 Ore pebaia ninje Yerusalem-- neng'amu esirit o lairriwak o laigwenak ninje-- neinosaa enkumoi oo mbaak naaitobira Engai too ninje."
Acts15:5 Neinyototo iltung'anak oora lʼematua oo Lfarisayoi ooiruko nejo: Meata kata nememurati ninje neitanapi-- peibung' nkitanapat e Mose."
Acts15:6 Neiturrurro lairriwak o laigwenak-- peleen ena bae."
Acts15:7 Ore peishangarra naleng'-- neitashe Petros nejoki ninje: Lelea-- lalashera-- iyololo-- aajo aategelua Engai opa tiatua ndai-- peiye ening' loreren lemeata Engai tʼenkutuk ai lomon lʼenkitopuata neiruk."
Acts15:8 Ore si ninye Engai nayolo iltauja neijakenoki kion too ninje neisho Olmumua Sinyati anaa yook--"
Acts15:9 neitu epik erishata empolos ang' o ninje neisuj iltauja lenye tʼenkirukoto.
Acts15:10 Akae-- ainyo pitemiteme taata Engai nipikipiki nkeek shumata oo murto oo laiteng'enuok neitu eidim aatanap loopapa lang' o yook?"
Acts15:11 Kake kiruk-- aajo kipok tʼeng'adunoto Olaitoriani Yesus-- naa neijia si ninje."
Acts15:12 Negira enkumoi pookin aainining' Barnabas o Paulos einosu ilponot o nkiputukunyot naaitobira Engai too ninje tiatua loreren lemeata Engai.
Acts15:13 Ore pegira kulo-- nealu Yakobos nejo: Lelea-- lalashera-- enining'oki!"
Acts15:14 Einosua Simeon eneikuna Engai tʼenkata elukunya ten egelu neng'amu olorere obo too loreren-- peata engarna enye."
Acts15:15 Etumo rorei loo layolounok o kulo-- neijia anaa petisiraki:"
Acts15:16 Alaibelekenyunye tekurum naitoki ashet engaji e David natuurori-- naitoki ashet nkun enyena naataaraki-- naitasheye ninje--"
Acts15:17 peiye eing'oru iltung'anak lootelekutua Olaitoriani-- o loreren pookin loipotieki engarna ai-- nejo Olaitoriani oitobir kuna."
Acts15:18 Eyolo Engai opa moitie nkitobirat enyena pookin.
Acts15:19 Onaa aalu nanu-- pemeitagolikini kulo looibelekenyakinote Engai tiatua loreren--"
Acts15:20 kake njesirakini ninje-- pepaash ilduruk loo nkulie ain o mbaak torrok oo nkiri o natagoroki o osarge."
Acts15:21 Amu eata Mose neba opa moitiei kulo looinosu mbaak enyena tiatua ngang'itie pookin neisomai ninye too ngolong i pookin naaeng'ieng'areki tiatua ngajijik Engai.
Acts15:22 Nejo lairriwak o laigwenak te nebo o esirit pookin-- aajo sidai-- teni egelu leak too ninje-- neirriwaa ninje-- pepuo Antiokia te nebo o Paulos o Barnabas o Yudas oipotoki Barsabas o Silas-- oora leak arikok tiatua lalashera."
Acts15:23 Nesir too ngaik enye nji: Kiroroki yook lairriwak o laigwenak likira lalashera ndai lalashera loo loreren ootii Antiokia o Siria o Kilikia.
Acts15:24 Tiaraki nikitoning'o yook-- aajo eing'arrirroitie ndai iltung'anak ooje too yook too nkiteng'enareitin neitarruo iltauja linyi-- eitu kintanap yook ninje entoki--"
Acts15:25 onaa kitadua yook likinturrurro tʼoltau obo-- aajo sidai-- pikirriwaki ndai leak ootegeluaki te nebo o likinyor-- Barnabas o Paulos--"
Acts15:26 iltung'anak looidipa aaishoo iltauja lenye tʼolbae Tengarna Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos.
Acts15:27 Nikirriu naa Yudas o Silas ooinosu oopeny ndai too rorei kuna baak.
Acts15:28 Amu eiting'ida Olmumua Sinyati o yook-- pemikipon aadumakindai rridat neme nona ake nemepalai--"
Acts15:29 pipaashipaasha nkiri enkidasare oo nkulie ain o osarge o natagoroki o mbaak torrok oo nkiri; teni imitikiki aten kuna-- nintobiribiri sidai. Esere naa!"
Acts15:30 Ore peishori meshomo-- nepuonu ninje Antiokia neiturrur enkumoi olorere neitarasaki empalai."
Acts15:31 Ore peidip aaisoma-- neng'ida te ina kilejilejata."
Acts15:32 Nediding' Yudas o Silas-- oora baiki layolounok-- lalashera too rorei kumok neitagol ninje."
Acts15:33 Ore peidip aatobik enkata naje-- neisho lalashera ninje meshomo tʼeseriani enetii looirriutua ninje."
Acts15:34 Nenyorru Silas atobiko te ine.
Acts15:35 Netoni Paulos o Barnabas te Antiokia eiteng'enisho neinosu lomon lʼOlaitoriani te nebo o kulekai kumok.
Acts15:36 Ore peishunye ngolong'i naaje-- nejoki Paulos Barnabas: Mainyaaki aamanaa-- pikiduare lalashera tiatua ngang'itie pookin nikinosunye lomon lʼOlaitoriani-- eneikununo."
Acts15:37 Neyeu Barnabas nerik te nebo o ninje Yohanes oji Markos.
Acts15:38 Kake etayeuo Paulos-- pemeriki ilo lotung'aiye ninje te Pamfilia neitu erubare ninje atua enkyas."
Acts15:39 Nejing' enkitarrikino metirishata; nerik Barnabas Markos nepuo tʼengalawa Kupros.
Acts15:40 Negelu Paulos Silas nepuo-- eidipa aaitarasakiti lalashera ninje eng'adunoto Engai."
Acts15:41 Neim ninje Siria o Kilikia neitagol sirito.
Acts16:1 Nebaia ninje Derbe o Listra. Naa ng'orai-- etii ina alo olaiteng'enuoni oji engarna enye Timoteos-- engerai eng'oroyoni nabo oo Yudayoi nairuko-- nera menye lenye Olgriki;"
Acts16:2 Neijakenu lalashera ootii Listra o Ikonion te ninye sidan.
Acts16:3 Neyeu Paulos-- perubare ele ninye-- neibung' nemurat ninye tʼolbae loo Yudayoi lootii atua kuna wuejitin-- amu etayolo pookin-- aajo era menye Olgriki."
Acts16:4 Ore peim atua ngang'itie-- neitarasaki kuna sipat-- naaitanaputua lairriwak o laigwenak ootii Yerusalem-- perrip ninje."
Acts16:5 Negolu sirito tiatua enkirukoto nepona aaku kumok too ngolong'i pookin.
Acts16:6 Neim Frigia o olosho Galatia nemitiki Olmumua Sinyati ninje einosu lomon tiatua Asia.
Acts16:7 Ore pebaia Misia-- netem aapuo Bitinia-- neitu eisho Olmumua le Yesus epuo;"
Acts16:8 neim Misia nebaia Troas.
Acts16:9 Nelioi enkitaduaroto kiarie te Paulos: etii oltung'ani obo le Makedonia oitashe nesai ninye nejoki: Talang'u Makedonia-- piretoki yook!"
Acts16:10 Ore peidip atadua ena kitaduaroto-- nikiyeu nabokata nikipuku aapuo Makedonia nikidol-- aajo esipa eipoto yook Olaitoriani-- pikinosaki ninje lomon lʼeng'ida."
Acts16:11 Nikidotu eenet te Troas nikibaia engoitoi naitoriori Samotrake o tʼengolong' e are Neapolis--"
Acts16:12 o te ina alo metabaiki Filipi nara engang' kitok olosho Makedonia-- engang' oo Romayoi. Nikitoni tiatua ena ang' ngolong'i naaje."
Acts16:13 Ore tʼengolong' naeng'ieng'areki nikipuku tʼengang' aapuo embata engare-- ewueji nasaishoreki-- nikitoni nikirorie ng'oroyok naaiturrurrote."
Acts16:14 Nening' eng'oroyoni nabo-- naji engarna enye Lidia-- engamirani oo lkarashi oodo-- nʼengang' Tiatira-- naure Engai; nebol Olaitoriani oltau lenye neibung' nairoro Paulos."
Acts16:15 Ore peibatisi ninye o engaji enye-- nesai yook nejo: Teni kitadua-- aajo ara engairukoni Olaitoriani-- entijing' engaji ai-- pitonini tiatua; nediding'aki yook!"
Acts16:16 Neaku ore pikipuo ewueji nesaishoreki-- neinepu yook engaisyayani nabo naata Olmumua loitayolo mbaak e akenya-- enainotoko laitoriak lenyena endupoto kitok tʼenkinosunoto oo mbaak e akenya."
Acts16:17 Nesuj ninye Paulos o yook neosh olodoo nejo: Era kulo leak laisyayak lʼEngai natii shumata neinosaki ndai engoitoi enkitopuata.
Acts16:18 Neiko neijia ngolong'i kumok. Negoro Paulos neibelekenya nejoki Olmumua: Aaitanap iye tʼengarna e Yesus Kristos-- pipuku te ninye. Nepuku te ninye te ina kata ake."
Acts16:19 Ore pedol laitoriak lenyena-- aajo eimina eanyunoto endupoto enye-- neibung' ninje Paulos o Silas neyetaki osingira engomom oo lkituak--"
Acts16:20 nerik ninje enetii larikok loo sikerin nejoki: Enyaul kulo tung'anak engang' ang' nera ninje Yudayoi--"
Acts16:21 neiteng'en irregiei lemeaku-- piking'amu aaitobir ninje-- tiaraki nikira Romayoi."
Acts16:22 Negoroki esiamu ninje-- neitanapu larikok loo sikerin-- peoruni ilkarashi lenye neari."
Acts16:23 Ore peidip aataara ninje naleng'-- nenang'aki ninje atua engaji erripore neitanap olarriponi lʼengaji-- perrip ninje naleng'."
Acts16:24 Ore peishori ninye ena kitanapata-- nenang'aki ninje atua engaji erripore-- olgilata liatua tukul-- neitirrish nkejek enye too nkeek."
Acts16:25 Ore tʼempolos e kiarie nesaisho Paulos o Silas neranyaki Engai-- neinining' ninje ilkulekai ooena."
Acts16:26 Neaku nabokata enkikirikirata kitok enkop neing'unung'un baiki entonata engaji erripore; nebolo nabokata kutukajini pookin nedoiyo eneta enye pookin.
Acts16:27 Ore pepiu olarriponi lʼengaji too njok nedol-- ajo etabolote kutukajini engaji erripore-- neshitu olalem neyeu near kion metua-- amu etejo-- ajo ekweta looena."
Acts16:28 Neapaa Paulos oltoilo tʼengolon nejoki: Miasaki kion entorroni-- amu kitii pookin ene!"
Acts16:29 Neyeu enkilang'et neilang'aki atua eikirikira-- nebatatakino Paulos o Silas"
Acts16:30 nerik ninje boo nejo: Laitoriak-- kaji aiko-- patum atopua?"
Acts16:31 Nejo ninje: Ruko Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos-- nipok iye o engaji ino."
Acts16:32 Neinosaki ninye lomon lʼOlaitoriani te nebo o pookin lootii atua engaji enye.
Acts16:33 Neitoomon ninje te ina kata e kiarie neisuj oshot enye-- neibatisi nabokata ninye o ilkulenyena pookin;"
Acts16:34 neriku ninje engaji enye neisho ninje endaa-- neng'ida ninye o engaji enye-- tiaraki nairuko Engai."
Acts16:35 Ore pekenyu-- neirriwaa ilkituak ilmurran lenye ejo: Metalaki kulo tung'anak meshomo!"
Acts16:36 Neinosaki olarriponi lʼengaji erripore Paulos lelo rorei: Eirriutua ilkituak-- pelakuni ndai. Akae-- enyoito taata-- pipuopuo tʼeseriani."
Acts16:37 Nejoki Paulos ninje: Etaaraki yook too ngonyek olorere-- eitu eigwenakini yook-- nikira yook Romayoi-- etanang'akitia yook engaji erriporej o taata neitupuku ninje yook tʼesungureishu? Me neijia! Njepuonu ake oopeny aarik yook boo!"
Acts16:38 Neliki ilmurran ilkituak kulo rorei. Neureishoi etoning'o-- aajo era ninje Romayoi--"
Acts16:39 nepuonu neirorie ninje-- nerik boo nesai-- pepuku tʼengang'."
Acts16:40 Nepuku tʼengaji erripore nepuo engaji e Lidia; ore pedol ninje lalashera-- neitagol ninje nepuku."
Acts17:1 Ore peidip aaima Amfipolis o Apolonia-- nebaia Tesalonike natii engaji Engai oo Yudayoi."
Acts17:2 Neijia anaa petamoo Paulos nejing'aki-- negilunore ninje too ngolong'i naaeng'ieng'areki uni too sirat--"
Acts17:3 neboloki neitayanaki ninje-- ajo meata kata nemeinosieki Kristos osina nepiu too lootuata; ore ele Yesus (etejo ninye) lainosaki ndai-- ninye Kristos."
Acts17:4 Neibelokino kulekai ninje nearakino ematua e Paulos o Silas-- baiki esiana kitok oo Lgrikini ooure Engai o ng'oroyok kituak neme kuti."
Acts17:5 Neibung'aki Yudayoi ong'u negelaki aten iltung'anak torrok tʼempolos oo lalimanak lʼengang' neitaa esiamu neng'uyan engang'; neitashe tʼengomom engaji e Yason neyeu neitupuku ninje boo engomom olorere.
Acts17:6 Ore pelau ninje-- neitupuku neyetu Yason o lalashera ooje engomom oo lkituak lʼengang' eoshito olodoo aajo: Kulo lootung'uyana olmaa eetuo baiki ene;"
Acts17:7 neitoomono Yason ninje; nemen kulo pookin nkitanapat e kaisar nejo: etii olekai karsis-- Yesus."
Acts17:8 Neng'uyan ninje esiamu o ilkituak lʼengang' lootoning'o kuna.
Acts17:9 Ore peidip aainoto entoki endung'okinoto e Yason o lʼemboitei enye-- neisho epuo."
Acts17:10 Neirriwaa lalashera nabokata Paulos o Silas kiarie metabaiki Beroia; ore pebaia-- nejing' atua engaji Engai oo Yudayoi."
Acts17:11 Eborraki ninje nelang'kulo le Tesalonike neng'amu ororei too ltauja ooitoriori neleen ngolong'i pookin sirat-- ten ake neijia etiu."
Acts17:12 Neiruk ilkumok too ninje o ng'oroyok oo Lgrikini naata enkitook o leak leme kuti.
Acts17:13 Ore peyolou Yudayoi le Tesalonike-- aajo einosu Paulos lomon lʼEngai te Beroia-- nebaia ina alo neibelibelie neing'unye baiki te ina alo siamin."
Acts17:14 Neirriwaa lalashera Paulos nabokata-- pelo metabaiki olbalbal-- kake etobiko Silas o Timoteos te ina alo."
Acts17:15 Ore kulo looturubare Paulos nerik ninye metabaiki Atenai; ore peidip aatang'amutu enkitanapata-- pepuonu Silas o Timoteos aasioki-- nepuo."
Acts17:16 Ore peanyu Paulos ninje te Atenai-- nepejoi atua ninye-- edol ajo ebore ena ang' enkisyayare oo nkulie ain."
Acts17:17 Neirorie ninye Yudayoi tiatua engaji Engai o kulo ooure Engai o tʼosingira ngolong'i pookin kulo ooinepua.
Acts17:18 Negilunore ninye ematua oo lang'eni ooji Epikureyoi o Istoikoi-- nejo ilkulekai: Kainyo eyeu nejo ele oiro pesho? Nejo ilkulekai: Enyanyukie oloinosu ngain omon. Amu einosua ninye lomon le Yesus o lʼempiunoto."
Acts17:19 Neibung'ninye nerik Areopagos ejo: Sidai-- teni kiyolou-- aajo kaa kiteng'enare ng'ejuk ena nirorita iye?"
Acts17:20 Amu iau iye mbaak omon atua nkiyaa ang'; kiyeu nikiyolou enkitaalata oo kuna baak.
Acts17:21 Amu ore iltung'anak pookin le Atenai o lomon ootii ine eitu eyeu neimaki lomon neme enkiroroto o ening'oto oo mbaak naara ng'ejuko.
Acts17:22 Neitashe Paulos tʼempolos e Areopagos nejo: Lelea le Atenai-- atadua ndai too mbaak pookin-- ajo iurere naleng' ngain."
Acts17:23 Amu ore paim-- naing'oraa wuejitin enkisyayare inyi nainepu baiki olkitaret obo lʼenkidasare losira: LʼEngai nemeyoloi! Ainosaki ndai taata ele lisyayakitia neitu iyolouu."
Acts17:24 Ninye Engai naitobira enkop o pookin natii atua-- era ninye Olaitoriani le shumata o lʼenkop-- mebik ninye tiatua ngajijik naaitobiraki too ngaik--"
Acts17:25 nemeisyayakini ninye too ngaik oo ltung'anak anaa ololau toki-- amu ninye oishoo pookin empuan o eang'an o pookin;"
Acts17:26 neitobir ninye t'osarge obo loreren pookin-- pemany ninje shumata enkop pookin nesir nkatan naaitanapaki o enebaiki ntonat enye--"
Acts17:27 peiye eing'oru ninje Olaitoriani eirrapirrapu-- petum; esipa-- melakwaniki ninye oltung'ani pookin too yook--"
Acts17:28 amu kinjiu tiatua ninye nikipuoiye nikitii atua ninye-- anaa pejo ilkulekai too ndai loosir singolioitin: Kira yook lʼeishoi Engai."
Acts17:29 Akae-- teni kira eishoi Engai-- meaku-- pikintanyanyukie Engai esahabu arashu ngoshola arashu osoit looitobiraki too nkyasin o tʼengarriyano oo ltung'anak."
Acts17:30 Eitu eing'oraa Engai nkatan emodaishu-- kake eitanap taata iltung'anak pookin too wuejitin pookin-- peala--"
Acts17:31 amu etipika engolong' naigwenakinye olmaa tʼesupato-- tʼolee obo oitanapua ninye neleen pookin tʼenkirukoto e atua ilo oidipa aitopiu aitung'ua lootuata."
Acts17:32 Ore pening' ninje mbaak enkitopiunoto oo lootuata-- nemor ilkulekai-- nejo ilkulekai: Kintoki aaning' iye too nona baak."
Acts17:33 Nepuku Paulos nji tʼempolos enye.
Acts17:34 Neibung'are ninye leak ooje neiruk-- netii atua kulo Dionisios-- olaigwenani obo Tene wueji-- o eng'oroyoni nabo naji engarna enye Damaris o ilkulekai te nebo o ninje."
Acts18:1 Neing'ua Paulos tekurum Atenai nelotu Korintos--"
Acts18:2 neinepu Oyudayos obo-- oji engarna enye Akwila-- otoiwuoki te Pontos-- oewuo too nona olong'i eing'ua Italia te nebo o eng'oroyoni enye Priskila-- amu eitanapishe kaisar Klaudios-- peing'ua Yudayoi pookin Roma; nejing'aki ninje."
Acts18:3 Tiaraki nang'ar enkyas nabo-- nebik tʼengaji enye neitobir nkyasin; amu ore enkyas enye — laitobirak loo ng'ajijik olototo."
Acts18:4 Neirorie ninye too ngolong'i naaeng'ieng'areki pookin tʼengaji Engai negilunore Yudayoi o Ilgrikini.
Acts18:5 Ore pebau Silas o Timoteos eing'ua Makedonia-- neisirkoni Paulos tʼolmumua-- peijakenoki Yudayoi-- ajo era ninye Kristos."
Acts18:6 Ore egilunore nemor ninje-- neipiripir ninye ilkilani lenyena nejoki ninje: Etii sargeta linyi shumata oo lukuny inyi! Maata eng'oki nanu-- ore eiter taata aibelekenyakino loreren lemeata Engai."
Acts18:7 Nedumunye te ine nelotu engaji oltung'ani oure Engai-- oji Titios Yustos-- otashare engaji enye engaji Engai."
Acts18:8 Neiruk Krispos-- olkitok lʼengaji Engai-- Olaitoriani-- o engaji enye pookin. Neinining' Ilkorintioi kumok neiruk neibatisi."
Acts18:9 Nejoki Olaitoriani Paulos kiarie tʼenkitaduaroto: Miureisho-- kake roro-- migira!"
Acts18:10 Amu aaboitare nanu iye nimikinyikaki oltung'ani-- pikinosie osina-- amu aata olorere kitok tiatua ena ang'."
Acts18:11 Nebik te ine olari obo o lapaitin ile-- eiteng'enu tiatua ninje lomon lʼEngai."
Acts18:12 Ore era Galion Olaitoriani le Akaya-- neitokitokakino Yudayoi tʼoltau obo Paulos nerik ninye enetii olorika lʼenkigwena"
Acts18:13 ejo: Eisis ele tung'ani olorere-- peisyayaki Engai t'engoitoi nemeishiaakinore nkitanapat ang'."
Acts18:14 Ore peyeu Paulos nebol enkutuk enye-- nejoki Galion Yudayoi: Loyudayoi-- ten emutu era ororei lʼenkisiloto arashu lʼenkyas torrono-- anaata ayeu naning' ndai abaraki--"
Acts18:15 kake tiaraki nara enkitarrikino enkiteng'enare o noo ngam o noo nkitanapat tiatua ndai-- entobirakinoto oopeny; mayeu naaku nanu olaigwenani loo nona baak."
Acts18:16 Nemir ninje tʼolorika lʼenkigwena enye.
Acts18:17 Neibung' Ilgrikini pookin Sostenes-- olkitok lʼengaji Engai-- near ninye tʼengomom olorika lʼenkigwena; neitu eshilaa Galion entoki o nabo too nona."
Acts18:18 Nebik Paulos te ine ngolong'i naaje-- neitanapare lalashera nejing' engalawa alo Siria te nebo o Priskila o Akwila-- eidipa atabarno elukunya-- amu eisiligishe."
Acts18:19 Nebaia Efesos neing'ua ninje te ina alo nejing' openy engaji Engai neirorioro o Yudayoi.
Acts18:20 Nesai ninje-- pebikoki ninje enkata naado-- kake eitu eiruk ninye."
Acts18:21 Neitanapare ninje ejo: Meata kata namatii kuna olong'i kituak naapuonu-- Yerusalem; aitoki arrinyokino ndai-- teni eyeu Engai. Neing'ua Efesos--"
Acts18:22 nebaia Kaisarea neilep (alo Yerusalem) neiroroki esirit nedou metabaiki Antiokia.
Acts18:23 Ore peidip atobiko enkiti kata-- nepuku nerukoo atua olosho Galatia o Frigia-- eitagol laiteng'enuok pookin."
Acts18:24 Nebaia Oyudayos obo Efesos-- oji engarna enye Apolos-- otoiwuoki te Aleskandria-- oltung'ani lʼeng'eno neaku shashaut too sirat."
Acts18:25 Eiteng'enaki ele tʼengoitoi Olaitoriani neiro tʼolmumua oiwuwu-- neiteng'enisho ninye naleng' too lomon le Yesus-- kake etayolo ninye enkibatisa e Yohanes ake."
Acts18:26 Neiter ninye airo-- metii enkuretishu-- tiatua engaji Engai. Ore pening' Priskila o Akwila ninye-- neitoomon ninye neitaaliki abaraki engoitoi Engai."
Acts18:27 Ore peyeu nelo ninye Akaya-- nesiraki nediding' lalashera laiteng'enuok-- peng'amu ninye. Ore pebaia ninye-- neretoki naleng' kulo looiruko tʼeng'adunoto;"
Acts18:28 amu etigilua oshi Yudayoi tʼengolon tʼengomom olorere pookin-- eitadolu too sirat-- ajo era Yesus Kristos."
Acts19:1 Neaku ore etii Apolos Korintos-- neim Paulos loshon le shumata nelotu Efesos neinepu laiteng'enuok ooje"
Acts19:2 nejoki ninje: Itang'amutua Olmumua Sinyati te ina kata niruko? Nealiki ninje ninye: Eitu aikata kining'-- ten ake etii Olmumua Sinyati."
Acts19:3 Nejo: Kang'ai eibatisieki ndai? Nejo: Enkibatisa e Yohanes.
Acts19:4 Nejo Paulos: Eibatisishe Yohanes t'enkibatisa enkitaalata-- ejoki olorere-- peiruk ololotu tekurum enye-- Yesus lora Kristos;"
Acts19:5 Ore pening' ninje kuna-- neisho eibatisi tʼengarna Olaitoriani Yesus;"
Acts19:6 neiteleiki Paulos ninje ngaik nelotu Olmumua Sinyati shumata enye neiro too nkulie kutukie neinosu mbaak e akenya.
Acts19:7 Neaku leak pookin loonyikaki tomon o are.
Acts19:8 Nejing' ninye atua engaji Engai neiro-- meata enkuretishu-- lapaitin okuni-- eiteng'enisho neitayolo ninje mbaak enkarsishu Engai."
Acts19:9 Ore peitagol ooje iltauja lenye neitu eiruk neimaki ena oitoi too ntorrok t'engomom esiamu-- nepuku ninye too ninje nerishu laiteng'enuok neiteng'enisho ngolong'i pookin tiatua engaji enkiteng'enare e Tiranos."
Acts19:10 Neaku kuna too larin aare-- nening' pookin lootii Asia lomon lʼOlaitoriani-- Yudayoi o Ilgrikini."
Acts19:11 Neitobir Engai ntokitin kituak naleng' too ngaik e Paulos--"
Acts19:12 neakini baiki rasheta enyena enkinyinyiret o nkimeitan enyena neibung'i te shumata oo loomoiyaa-- neing'ua moiyaitin ninje nepuku ilmeneng'a."
Acts19:13 Netem Yudayoi ooje ooyang'iyang'a oora loibonok-- aalimu te shumata oo kulo looata ilmeneng'a-- engarna Olaitoriani Yesus nejo; Kinturujaki ndai te Yesus oinosu Paulos."
Acts19:14 Netii leak oopishana-- nkera Oyudayos Skewas-- ora olaidasani kitok-- ooikuna nji."
Acts19:15 Nealiki olmeneng'ani nejoki ninje: Ayolo Yesus nayolo si Paulos-- kake irara ndai nyoo?"
Acts19:16 Neipirrioki ele tung'ani loata olmeneng'ani shumata negilu nerrek ninje-- metabana nekwet aaing'ua ena aji-- meata ilkilani-- eata ilbaak."
Acts19:17 Neyolou Yudayoi o Ilgrikini pookin ootii Efesos kuna baak-- nejing' enkuretishu atua ninje pookin-- neitaai kitok engarna Olaitoriani Yesus."
Acts19:18 Ore ilkumok too kulo ooiruko nepuonu-- neibalu neinosu nkitobirat enye."
Acts19:19 Ilkulekai ake looitobira mbaak nemeaku neau sirat enye nepej ninje too ngonyek oo pookin; neiken enkinyang'a enye netum ngoshola naaibor elfun onom.
Acts19:20 Neibulaa nji lomon lʼOlaitoriani tʼengolon anaa peidim.
Acts19:21 Ore peidip aaitaa kuna baak-- neibirribir Paulos tʼolmummua lenye-- ajo ore peidip aima Makedonia o Akaya nelo Yerusalem-- nejo: Ore atii ina alo-- meata kata namadol Roma."
Acts19:22 Neirriwaa iltung'anak aare too kulo ooisyayakitia ninye-- nera Timoteos o Erastos-- pepuo Makedonia; nebik ninye openy enkata naje te Asia."
Acts19:23 Neaku te ina kata enkipushoi kitok tʼolbae le ina kiteng'enare.
Acts19:24 Amu etii oltung'ani obo-- oji engarna enye Demetrios-- olkunoni loo ngoshola-- oitobira ngajijik oo ngoshola enkisyayare e Artemis-- netumoki lashetak endupoto neme kiti."
Acts19:25 Neiturrur ninye kulo te nebo o laretok loo nkyasin naanyanyukie nejoki: Lelea-- iyololo-- aajo kiata too kuna kyasin endupoto sapuk."
Acts19:26 Itadua ndai nining'ining'i-- aajo eisisita ele Paulos neitayolo iltung'anak kumok-- me te Efesos ake-- kake baiki te Asia pookin-- nejo-- ajo mera kuna naaitobiraki too ngaik-- ngain."
Acts19:27 Me entumoto ang' ake kiataiye osina naimin-- kake baiki engaji sinyati engai ng'oroyoni kitok ang' Artemis naikenari-- ajo me o nyoo-- neiminyeki enkitook enye-- naisyayaki iltung'anak le Asia pookin o lʼenkop."
Acts19:28 Ore pening' ninje kuna-- neigany engoro neosh olodoo ejo: Kitok Artemis oo Efesioi!"
Acts19:29 Neigany engang' pookin enking'oling'olata-- nepuo aasioio tʼoltau obo metabaiki ewueji oo nkiguraneitin-- newuap Gayos o Aristarkos-- iltung'anak le Makedonia-- lʼemboitei e Paulos."
Acts19:30 Ore peyeu Paulos nejing'aki olorere-- nemitiki laiteng'enuok ninye."
Acts19:31 Neirriwaki baiki ematua oo laigwenak le Asia-- loora iljorueta lenyena-- nediding' ninye-- pemelo ewueji oo nkiguraneitin."
Acts19:32 Akae-- neishir kulekai nji o kulekai nji-- amu eing'oling'olate iltimito nemeyolo ilkumok-- aajo kainyo peiturrurrote ninje."
Acts19:33 Neyetu kulekai Aleksandros errumoo Yudayoi ninye. Neroj Aleksandros tʼengaina neyeu nemitu kion tʼengomom olorere.
Acts19:34 Ore peyolou ninje-- aajo era ninye Oyudayos-- neosh ninje olodoo te nebo o pookin tʼenkata oo saan are-- eishirita: Kitok Artemis oo Efesioi!"
Acts19:35 Neitigir olasirani obo esiamu nejo: Lelea le Efesos-- kalo tung'ani lemeyolo-- ajo era engang' Efesos engashilaroni engai ng'oroyoni Artemis-- nʼemua natadouo te shumata?"
Acts19:36 Tiaraki nemeisimunoi nona-- onaa meata kata nimigirara ndai nimintobiribiri entoki enkisarisarata."
Acts19:37 Amu itorikutuo kulo tung'anak leitu epurroo ntokitin engaji engai neitu emor engai ng'oroyoni ang'.
Acts19:38 Akae-- teni eata Demetrios o laitobirak loo nkyasin looboitare ninye embae oltung'ani-- neatai nkigwenaitin o laigwenak. Njeitang'oro!"
Acts19:39 Teni iyeuu ororei loo nkulie baak-- nepuoi aal tʼoltumo oitoriokino."
Acts19:40 Amu kiureisho-- aajo eitang'ori yook tʼolbae lʼele arrabal le taata-- amu mikiata emitunoto tʼena kiposhai. Ore peidip atejo kuna-- neitanapaa enkigwena."
Acts20:1 Ore pegira enkiposhai-- neipot Paulos laiteng'enuok-- neilejilej neitanapare ninje nepuku-- pelo Makedonia."
Acts20:2 Ore peidip aima lelo oshon nediding' ninje too rorei kumok-- nebaia olosho loo Lgrikini."
Acts20:3 Nebik te ina alo lapaitin okuni. Ore peyeu Yudayoi near ninye tʼena kata nayeu nelo ninye tʼengalawa Siria-- nepuku eata ajo errinyo eimaa Makedonia."
Acts20:4 Nerubare ninye metabaiki Asia Sopatros le Piros te Beroia-- Aristarkos o Sekundos le Tesalonike-- Gayos le Derbe-- o Timoteos o Tukikos o Trofimos le Asia;"
Acts20:5 neituruk kulo neanyu yook te Troas.
Acts20:6 Nikipuo tʼengalawa eidipate ngolong'i oo lmkaten lemeisiijo-- king'ua Filipi nikibaiki ninje te Troas eishunyete ngolong'i imiet; nikibik te ina alo ngolong'i naapishana."
Acts20:7 Ore tʼengolong' Engai nikitumo-- pikigiligil olmkate-- neirorie Paulos ninje-- neyeu nelo enasirie olototo-- neitaador rorei lenyena metabaiki empolos e kiarie."
Acts20:8 Netii nkilang'eta kumok keper aji nikitutumore.
Acts20:9 Neton olbarnoti obo-- oji engarna enye Eutukos-- tʼelusiet neiroshiki njok-- epon eiro Paulos rorei kumok. Ore etalepoitie njok-- nesulakino kai e uni-- nedumuni etua."
Acts20:10 Nedou Paulos neurokino shumata enye-- nejap ninye nejo: Eminya osina-- etii empuan atua ninye."
Acts20:11 Neitoki ailep negil olmkate neinyorrinyor-- neiro naleng' metabaiki enasirie nepuku nji."
Acts20:12 Neriku ninje ele barnoti aa bioto-- neilejileja nelang' entemet."
Acts20:13 Nikinturuk yook tʼengalawa nikipuo metabaiki Asos-- nikiyeu niking'amu Paulos te ina alo; amu neijia eitanapua-- eyeu nelo openy too nkejek."
Acts20:14 Ore peinepu ninye yook te Asos-- nikintijing' ninye nikipuonu Mitilene."
Acts20:15 Nikijing' te ina alo engalawa nikibaiki tʼengolong' e are eneitoriokinore Kios; ore tʼengai olong nikijing' Samos nikibik tʼengang' Trogilion; ore tʼengolong' natusuja nikipuonu Miletos.
Acts20:16 Amu etayeuo neporoo Paulos tʼengalawa Efesos-- pemeimutie te Asia; amu etasioiye ninye anaa peidim-- ten ake eaku-- petii Yerusalem tʼengolong' e Pentekoste."
Acts20:17 Neirriwaa oltung'ani oing'ua Miletos-- pelo Efesos neipot laigwenak lʼesirit."
Acts20:18 Ore pepuonu enetii ninye-- nejoki ninje: Iyololo ndai enaikuna eiter tʼengolong' elukunya natabaua Asia-- naton tiatua ndai oshi--"
Acts20:19 aisyayaki Olaitoriani tʼenkitadounoto pookin o too lkiyo o too nkitasurot nainoto too losekin loo Yudayoi;
Acts20:20 neitu apal eitu adiding' ndai tʼengomom olorere o too ngajijik o ngajijik--"
Acts20:21 naijakenoki Yudayoi o Ilgrikini enkitaalata aaibelekenyakino Engai neiruk Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos.
Acts20:22 Akae-- eng'orai taata-- aateenaki tʼolmumua-- palo Yerusalem-- namayolo mbaak natum te ina alo;"
Acts20:23 kake aaijakenoki Olmumua Sinyati ejo too ngang'itie pookin-- ajo aanyu enat o sinaitin."
Acts20:24 Kake ore nona pookin nabo te nanu-- adol baiki-- ajo me entoki kitok empuan ai-- paidim aidipa olototo lai tʼeng'ida o enkisyayare naaishoo Olaitoriani Yesus-- paijakenu lomon lʼeng'adunoto Engai."
Acts20:25 Akae-- eng'orai-- ayolo-- ajo mikintokiki aadol engomom ai-- ndai pookin laimaiye ainosu enkarsishu Engai."
Acts20:26 Onaa aijakenoki ndai pookin taata-- ajo ara bioto tʼosarge linyi pookin;"
Acts20:27 amu eitu apal ainosaki ndai enkigwena pookin Engai.
Acts20:28 Entagolie aten o enjoo pookin natipika ndai Olmumua Sinyati anaa laing'orak-- entotio esirit Engai nainotoko kion t'osarge lenye openy."
Acts20:29 Amu ayolo kuna-- ajo ore paidip ashomo-- nejing'u suiyan malmalin atua ndai nemepal enjoo."
Acts20:30 Nepuku baiki tʼempolos inyi iltung'anak ooiro nemeitoriori-- pearaki laiteng'enuok ematua enye."
Acts20:31 Onaa enjololoto-- entadamutu-- ajo eitu apal tʼenkata oo larin okuni-- dama o kiarie-- adiding' oltung'ani pookin too lkiyo."
Acts20:32 Akae-- lalashera-- aitarasaki ndai taata Engai o lomon lenyena lʼeng'adunoto naidim atesheta neisho ndai enjung'o tiatua kulo pookin loora sinyat."
Acts20:33 Eitu ang'war too ndai ngoshola arashu sahabu arashu ilkilani;
Acts20:34 amu iyololo ndai oopeny-- aajo ore kuna aik ainei eisyayutua yeunot ainei o noo kulo laataboitare."
Acts20:35 Aitadua ndai pookin eninkoko-- teni intobiribiri nkyasin nji niretokiki lemeata engolon-- nidamumu rorei lʼOlaitoriani Yesus otejo: Sidai enkishooroto nelang' eng'amunoto."
Acts20:36 Ore peidip atejo kuna-- negil kung' nesaisho te nebo o ninje pookin."
Acts20:37 Neishir pookin naleng' neurokino ninje emurt e Paulos neng'utut ninye--"
Acts20:38 eilish naleng' tʼolbae lʼele rorei otejo-- ajo meitoki aadol engomom enye; neitare ninye metabaiki engalawa."
Acts21:1 Ore pikindip aatirishare ninje-- nikipuonu tʼengalawa tʼengoitoi naitoriori metabaiki Koos-- ore tʼengai olong' metabaiki Rodos; niking'ua ina alo metabaiki Patara."
Acts21:2 Nikidol engalawa naloito Foinike-- nikilepaki nikipuo."
Acts21:3 Akae-- ore pelioi Kupros-- niking'ua te kedyanye nikiim metabaiki Siria-- nikidou te Tiros-- amu te ina alo eyeu neitadounye masaa engalawa."
Acts21:4 Nikinepu laiteng'enuok nikibik te ina alo ngolong'i naapishana; nejoki ninje Paulos tʼenkidimata Olmumua-- pemeilep abaiki Yerusalem."
Acts21:5 Neaku ore pikintabaia yook nona olong'i-- nikidumunye nikipuo; neitare yook ninje pookin-- ng'oroyok o nkera-- metabaiki aulo engang'-- nikigil kung' tʼembata olbalbal nikisaisho."
Acts21:6 Ore pikintanaparo-- nikilepaki yook engalawa-- nerrinyo si ninje aapuo ang'."
Acts21:7 Ore pikindip olototo lang' king'ua Tiros-- nikibaia Ptolemais-- nikiroroki lalashera nikibik o ninje engolong' nabo."
Acts21:8 Ore tʼengolong' e are nikipuku yook loosujita Paulos-- nikibaia Kaisarea nikijing' engaji e Filipos oinosu lomon lʼeng'ida-- nera ninye obo too lelo oopishana-- nikibik tʼengaji enye."
Acts21:9 Neata ele ntoiye ong'wan neitu eamari-- naainosu mbaak e akenya."
Acts21:10 Ore pikipon aabik ngolong'i kumok-- nedou olayolounoni obo-- oji engarna enye Agabos-- tʼolosho Yudaya-- nelotu enikitii."
Acts21:11 Neibung' ninye enkimeita e Paulos neenye kion ngaik o nkejek nejo: Nji ejo Olmumua Sinyati: Neijia epuo aaen Yudayoi le Yerusalem olopeny ena kimeita neitarasaki atua ngaik oo loreren.
Acts21:12 Ore pikining' kuna-- nikisai yook o iltung'anak le ine wueji-- pemeilepaki Yerusalem."
Acts21:13 Nealu Paulos: Ainyo pinjirishiri nikigiligili oltau? amu aidipakine-- me paaeni ake-- kake paitoki ae te Yerusalem tʼolbae lʼengarna Olaitoriani Yesus."
Acts21:14 Ore eitu eisho yook mairorie-- nikigira kijo: Njeaku enayeu Olaitoriani Yesus!"
Acts21:15 Ore peishunye kuna olong'i-- nikintobirakino nikipuo Yerusalem."
Acts21:16 Nepuonu te nebo o yook baiki laiteng'enuok ooje le Kaisarea-- erikito yook enetii Mnason le Kupros-- olaiteng'enuoni le opa; nikipuo aabik tʼengang' enye."
Acts21:17 Ore pikibaia Yerusalem-- neng'amu yook lalashera tʼeng'ida."
Acts21:18 Nejing' Paulos te nebo o yook engaji e Yakobos; neiturrurro te ina alo ilpaiyani pookin.
Acts21:19 Ore peidip ninye airoroki ninje-- nelimu nabo nabo mbaak naitobira Engai tiatua loreren tʼenkisyayare enye."
Acts21:20 Ore pening' ninje ena-- neitadaraa Engai nejoki ninye: Idolita-- lalashe-- ke elfun aja naatii atua Yudayoi looiruk-- nera kulo pookin shashauti-- eibung' nkitanapat;"
Acts21:21 etolikioki ninje mbaak inono-- ajo inteng'enita Yudayoi pookin lootii atua loreren-- peing'ua Mose-- nijo-- pememurati nkera enye nemesuj orregie lenye."
Acts21:22 Akae-- kainyo ena? Meata kata nemeiturrurro esiamu-- amu epuo aaning' ninje-- aajo iewuo."
Acts21:23 Akae-- nyaaki-- ntobira enikijoki iye! Kiata iltung'anak ong'wan ooata enkisiligata;"
Acts21:24 mbung'a lelo-- tisinyai kion te nebo o ninje-- njoo ngoshola-- pebarn aten lukuny-- peyolou pookin aajo ore mbaak naatolikioki te iye me toki-- ore iye openy ishomo abaraki nimbung' nkitanapat."
Acts21:25 Ore lairukok too loreren kitisirakitia nikingwenu-- pemeibung' too nona entoki o nabo-- kake njepaash ake enkidasare oo nkulie ain o osarge o natagoroki o mbaak torrok oo nkiri."
Acts21:26 Neibung' Paulos kulo tung'anak nesinyaa kion o ninje tʼengolong' e are nejing' engaji sinyati aitaduaia enkitabaiaroto oo ngolong'i esinyaroto enye metabaiki neishori enkidasare tʼolbae lʼoltung'ani pookin lenye.
Acts21:27 Ore peaku eishunye ngolong'i naapishana-- nedol Yudayoi le Asia ninye etii atua engaji sinyati-- neisis olorere pookin-- neibung' ninye too ngaik nedar:"
Acts21:28 Lelea le Israel-- entaretishoto! Eiteng'en ele tung'ani iltung'anak pookin too wuejitin pookin neibelie olorere lang' o nkitanapat o ene wueji; neinyaaka si ariku Ilgrikini atua engaji sinyati neitaa ene wueji torrono."
Acts21:29 Amu etaduaki te nebo o ninye Trofimos le Efesos tiatua engang' nejo ninje-- Paulos otorikuo ninye atua engaji sinyati."
Acts21:30 Neng'ayung'ayu engang' pookin neiturrurro olorere-- neibung' ninje Paulos neyetaki boo engaji sinyati; neigen! nabokata kutukajini."
Acts21:31 Ore eing'oru eneiko-- pear ninye metua-- nebaiki mbaak olkitok lʼoltim-- ajo eing'ole Yerusalem pookin;"
Acts21:32 neipot ninye nabokata sikerin o ilkituak nekwet nedoiki ninje; ore pedol ninje olkitok o sikerin-- nepal ear Paulos."
Acts21:33 Nenyikaki olkitok neoru ninye neitanapisho-- peeni ninye too lpisia aare neikilikwanu: Kera ninye ng'ai? Kainyo etaasa?"
Acts21:34 Nejo kulekai tiatua esiamu kuna-- nejo ilkulekai nona; neitu eidim ainoto esipata tʼolbae lʼenkiposhai neitanapisho-- periki ninye engang' oo sikerin."
Acts21:35 Ore pebaia riot engaji-- nenap isikerin ninye tʼolbae lʼenkisimaroto olorere;"
Acts21:36 amu esujita esiamu olorere eishirita: Ntaiki ele enelakwa!
Acts21:37 Ore eitijing'itai engang' oo sikerin-- nejoki Paulos olkitok: Ke kinjo aairorie iye? Nejoki: Iyolo enkutuk oo Lgrikini?"
Acts21:38 Me iye le naarri Misri oaua enyaul too kuna olong'i nerik ang'ata le naarri tung'anak elfun ong'wan loora laarak?
Acts21:39 Nejo Paulos: Ara nanu oltung'ani Oyudayos lʼengang' Tarsos te Kilikia-- Oinoti lʼengang' nemera kinyi. Aasai-- pikinjo mairorie olorere."
Acts21:40 Neiruk. Neitashe Paulos te shumata oo riot engaji neroj olorere tʼengaina. Ore pegirai tukul-- neirorie tʼenkutuk oo Lhebrayoi nejo:"
Acts22:1 Lelea-- lalashera o loopapa-- enining'oki-- painosaki ndai emitunoto ai!"
Acts22:2 Ore pening' ninje-- aajo eirorie ninje tʼenkutuk oo Lhebrayoi-- nepon aagira. Nejo:"
Acts22:3 Ara nanu oltung'ani Oyudayos-- aatoiwuoki te Tarsos-- engang' e Kilikia-- naaitubuluni te ina ang'-- naaiteng'eni too nkejek e Gamaliel reriot oo loopapa lang' abaraki-- naaku olanyuani tʼEngai anaa ndai pookin taata;"
Acts22:4 Nainosie iltung'anak lʼena oitoi osina metabaiki enkea-- aen napik ninje-- leak o ng'oroyok-- engaji erripore--"
Acts22:5 anaa paaijakenoki olaidasani kitok o laigwenak-- kulo laaishoo mpala-- panap enetii lalashera nalo Damaskos-- pariku lootii ina alo eena metabaiki Yerusalem-- peitamei ninje."
Acts22:6 Ore aloito-- nabaia enetaaniki Damaskos-- euno engolong'-- naailang'aki nabokata lubot pookin enkilang'et kitok aing'ua shumata--"
Acts22:7 Nabatatakino enkop naning' oltoilo laajoki: Saul-- Saul-- ainyo pikimirita?"
Acts22:8 Naalu: Ira ng'ai-- Laitoriani? Naajoki: Ara nanu Yesus le Nasaret likimirita iye."
Acts22:9 Nedol kulo laataboitare nanu enkilang'et nejing' enkuretishu atua ninje-- kake eitu ening' oltoilo lʼele laairorie nanu."
Acts22:10 Najo: Kainyo alaitobir-- Laitoriani? Naajoki Olaitoriani: Tudumunye-- pilo Damaskos-- nikilikini te ina alo pookin nikintanapaki iye-- pintobir."
Acts22:11 Ore pamadolisho nanu tʼolbae lʼenkiwuwuoto ena kilang'et-- naaibung' laataboitare engaina ai nabaia Damaskos."
Acts22:12 Nelotu enatii Ananias-- oltung'ani supat too nkitanapat-- oijakenokoki too Yudayoi pookin ootii ina alo;"
Acts22:13 neitashe naajoki: Lalashe Saul-- tadolishoi! Nadol si nanu ninye te ina kata ake."
Acts22:14 Nejo: Kitegelua Engai oo loopapa lang'-- pitum atayolo enayeu ninye nidol olopeny esupato nining' oltoilo oing'ua enkutuk enye--"
Acts22:15 amu iaku oljakeni lenye too ltung'anak pookin too kuna nitadua nining'.
Acts22:16 Akae-- kainyo taata pimutie? Nyototoi-- pikimbatisi-- peisujari nkitarruot inono nimpot engarna Olaitoriani."
Acts22:17 Neaku ore paidip atorrinyoi Yerusalem nasaisho tʼengaji sinyati-- napurrupurru Olmumua lai nadol ninye"
Acts22:18 aajoki: Sarisara-- tupuku tasioi te Yerusalem! Amu meiruk ninje enjakenishu ino o mbaak ainei."
Acts22:19 Najo: Laitoriani-- etayoloutuo kulo-- aajo ateena nanu naar too ngajijik Engai kulo pookin likiruko iye."
Acts22:20 Ore peibukori osarge lʼoljakeni lino Stefanos-- atii nanu-- aitasheiki nairuk narripoki ninje looiminye ninye-- ilkilani lenye."
Acts22:21 Naajoki: Tudumunye-- amu aairiwaa nanu iye enelakwa atua loreren."
Acts22:22 Neinining' ninye metabaiki kulo rorei-- neapaa iltoiloi lenye nejo: Ntupuku ele tʼena kop! amu meaku-- peishiu."
Acts22:23 Ore eoshito olodoo-- neiturraki ilkilani lenye enelakwa neisuaki enterit shumata--"
Acts22:24 neitanapisho olkitok-- periki ninye engang' oo sikerin-- nejo-- petem aar too nkeenda-- peiye eyolou-- ajo kainyo peishiraki neijia."
Acts22:25 Ore eenita ninye too nkeenda-- peari-- nejoki Paulos olkigeluni obo oitasheiki ninye: Ke sidai too ndai-- piariara oltung'ani ora Oromayos-- eitu eigwenakini?"
Acts22:26 Ore pening' olkigeluni kuna-- nelo enetii olkitok neinosaki ninye mbaak ejo: Ainyo iyeu nintobir? Amu era ele tung'ani Oromayos."
Acts22:27 Nelotu olkitok nejoki ninye: Tolikioki-- ten ake ira Oromayos? Nejo: Ee!"
Acts22:28 Nealiki olkitok: Ainoto nanu aaku Oromayos too ngoshola kumok. Nejo Paulos: Tʼeiunoto nanu.
Acts22:29 Neing'uaiki ninye nabokata kulo lootayeutuo neikilikwan ninye. Neureishoi olkitok-- etayolouo ninye-- ajo Oromayos-- tiaraki nateena."
Acts22:30 Ore tʼengolong' e are eyeu neyolou esipata-- ainyo peitang'oro Yudayoi ninye-- nelaku ninye-- neitanapu-- peiturrurro laidasak kituak o enkigwena pookin-- nerik Paulos neitasheye tʼempolos enye."
Acts23:1 Nekurraki Paulos ngonyek enyena enkigwena nejoki: Lelea lalashera-- atobiko nanu tʼoltau sidai pookin tʼengomom Engai metabaiki ena olong' e taata."
Acts23:2 Neitanap olaidasani kitok Ananias looitashe o ninye-- peosh enkutuk enye."
Acts23:3 Nejoki Paulos: Kiar Engai iye-- enjewata engaji naelaki tʼenturoto! Amaa itotona aigwenaki nanu too nkitanapat nilau iye nintanapu-- paaoshi nanu?"
Acts23:4 Ore looitashe te nebo o ninye nejo: Imor olaidasani kitok lʼEngai?
Acts23:5 Nejo Paulos: Eitu ayolo-- lalashera-- ajo era olaidasani kitok-- amu etisiraki: Mirorie torrono olkitok lʼolorere lino!"
Acts23:6 Ore peyolou Paulos-- ajo era ematua Sadukayoi-- nera engai matua Ilfarisayoi-- neapaa oltoilo lenye tiatua enkigwena ajo: Lelea lalashera-- ara nanu Olfarisayos o enkerai Olfarisayos-- aaigwenakini nanu too mbaak eanyunoto o enkitopiunoto oo lootuata."
Acts23:7 Ore peidip airoro kuna-- neaku enkitarrikino too Lfarisayoi o Sadukayoi nerisha esiamu."
Acts23:8 Amu ejo Sadukayoi-- aajo metii enkitopiunoto-- metii ilmalaikan-- metii ilmumuan; neibalu Ilfarisayoi pokira are."
Acts23:9 Neaku olodoo kitok. Neinyototo layolok lʼesirata lʼematua oo Lfarisayoi negiluno nejo: Mikidol entorroni tiatua ele tung'ani-- kake teni eiroro Olmumua te ninye arashu olmalaika-- akae-- nikindim aaing'orutu olarrabal lʼEngai."
Acts23:10 Ore peaku enkitarrikino kitok-- neureishoi olkitok lʼoltim-- ajo epolos ninje Paulos-- neitanapu-- pedou oltim-- peitupuku ninye tʼengolon tʼempolos enye-- periki engang' oo sikerin."
Acts23:11 Ore enkiarie natusuja neitasheiki Olaitoriani ninye nejo: Ntagoluoi-- Paulos-- tʼoltau-- amu neijia anaa pikinjakenoko nanu te Yerusalem-- meata kata nimikinjakenoki neijia baiki te Roma."
Acts23:12 Ore pekenyu-- neitobirakino Yudayoi ooje nediaro nejo-- aajo menya nemeok metabana neidip aataar Paulos metua."
Acts23:13 Etalang'a artam looiturujakinote nji.
Acts23:14 Nepuonu ninje enetii laidasak kituak o laigwenak nejo: Kinturujakinote naleng'-- pimikinyorrinyor toki metabana nikiar Paulos metua."
Acts23:15 Akae-- ore ndai entiakiti olkitok lʼoltim o enkigwena-- perikuni ninye taisere enitiiti-- anaa ijo iyeuu niyolouu esipata oo mbaak enyena; ore si yook-- epon eitu enyiku nikintobirakino aar metua."
Acts23:16 Ore pening' enkerai enganashe e Paulos ele osek-- nelotu nejing' atua engang' oo sikerin neliki Paulos."
Acts23:17 Neipot Paulos olkigeluni obo nejo: Toriko ele barnoti enetii olkitok lʼoltim-- eata mbaak naainosaki ninye."
Acts23:18 Neibung' nerik enetii olkitok nejo: Aaipoto lido Paulos oena neyeu naarikoki ele barnoti-- amu eata ororei likiliki."
Acts23:19 Neibung' olkitok ninye engaina nerishunye nelo enkilepata neikilikwan ninye: Kakua baak iata-- pikinosaki?"
Acts23:20 Nejo: Etaa nabo Yudayoi-- pikisai iye-- pirik Paulos taisere atua enkigwena anaa ijo eyeu neikilikwanishore."
Acts23:21 Kake miruk iye ninje-- amu eoseku too ninje iltung'anak oolang' artam looiturujakinote-- pemenya nemeok metabana near ninye metua; eitobirakinote taata ninje neanyu enkitanapata ino."
Acts23:22 Neitanapare olkitok olbarnoti neitanap-- pemeliki oltung'ani-- ajo etolikio kuna."
Acts23:23 Neipot ilkigeluni aare nejo: Entobirakiti sikerin iip are oopuo Kaisarea o ntomoni naapishana lakedok loo mbartaishi o iip are loo remeta tʼesaa uni enkiarie;
Acts23:24 njeitobiraki ninje mbartaishi-- peilepakinye Paulos-- perik aa bioto enetii Olaitoriani lʼolosho Feliks."
Acts23:25 Nesir empalai nji:
Acts23:26 Airoroki nanu Klaudios Lisias Olaitoriani kitok lʼolosho-- Feliks."
Acts23:27 Eibung'a Yudayoi ele tung'ani neyeu near ninye metua. Nalotu nanu o oltim naitau ninye-- amu aatiakaki-- ajo Oromayos."
Acts23:28 Ore payeu nayolou enaitang'orie ninje-- narik ninye enkigwena enye--"
Acts23:29 nadol ajo eitang'oroki too nkitarrikinot oo nkitanapat enye nemetii enkitang'oro nanang' arashu naenyeki ninye.
Acts23:30 Ore paainosakini-- ajo eoseku Yudayoi ooje-- nairriu nabokata engang' ino-- naitanap looitang'oro ninye-- peiro mbaak enyena tʼengomom ino. Sere!"
Acts23:31 Akae-- nerik isikerin Paulos anaa peitanapaki ninje kiarie metabaiki Antipatris;"
Acts23:32 ore enasirie neisho lakedok loo mbartaishi erubare ninye-- nerrinyo ilkulekai engang' oo sikerin."
Acts23:33 Ore pebaia ninje Kaisarea-- neisho Olaitoriani lʼolosho empalai neitarasaki ninye baiki Paulos."
Acts23:34 Ore peidip Olaitoriani aisoma empalai-- neikilikwan-- ke oltung'ani li aa balbal ninye. Ore peyolou-- ajo era oltung'ani le Kilikia--"
Acts23:35 nejo: Aalaning' iye eetuo laitang'orok linono. Neitanapu-- perripi ninye tiatua engaji enkigwena e Herodes."
Acts24:1 Ore peishunye ngolong'i imiet-- nedou olaidasani kitok Ananias te nebo o laigwenak o olairoroni Tertulos; eetuo ninje enetii Olaitoriani lʼolosho-- peitang'or Paulos."
Acts24:2 Ore peipoti ninye-- neiter Tertulos aitang'or ninye nejo:"
Acts24:3 Tiaraki ninotoko yook eseriani kitok netaa mbaak sidan tʼele orere tʼenkishilaroto ino-- king'amu yook nona ngolong'i pookin too wuejitin pookin-- iye Feliks kitok-- te ashe naleng'."
Acts24:4 Kake pamapon aitanaur iye-- aasai-- pinining'u yook too nkuti tʼemborran ino."
Acts24:5 Kinoto ele tung'ani ekurro eitera enkiposhai tiatua Yudayoi pookin lootii atua olmaa nera olaiturukoni Tesiamu oo Lnasarayoi--"
Acts24:6 netem baiki aitarruo engaji sinyati-- nikimbung' nikiyeu nikingwenaki ninye too nkitanapat ang'."
Acts24:7 Kake eewuo olkitok Lisias neitau ninye tʼengolon kitok tiatua ngaik ang'
Acts24:8 neitanap laitang'orok-- pepuonu enitii iye; nindim si iye aikilikwanu openy ninye-- piyolou kuna pookin nikintang'orie ninye."
Acts24:9 Neitang'or baiki Yudayoi ninye ejo: Neijia etiu!
Acts24:10 Nealiki Paulos-- eidipa Olaitoriani lʼolosho atoroja ninye-- neiro: Tiaraki nayolo-- ajo itaa-- eiter too laritin kumok-- olaigwenani lʼele orere-- onaa ayeu namitu kion-- maureisho."
Acts24:11 Amu indim atayolo-- ajo melang' ngolong'i tomon o are neba nailepaki Yerusalem asaisho."
Acts24:12 Neitu aadol ninje tiatua engaji sinyati airorie oltung'ani arashu aing'oru enkisisa tʼesiamu arashu tʼengaji Engai arashu tʼengang'--"
Acts24:13 nemeidim aaitisipai naaitangorie ninje taata.
Acts24:14 Kake aibalu te iye ena-- ajo aisyayaki tʼena oitoi-- naipot ninje enkiteng'enare ng'ejuk-- Engai oo loopapa lang'-- nairuk pookin natisiraki tiatua nkitanapat o tiatua layolounok--"
Acts24:15 naata eanyunoto tʼEngai-- anaa peanyu si ninje oopeny-- ajo elaaku enkitopiunoto oo lootuata-- noo loora supati o noo lemera supati."
Acts24:16 Naitamok nanu kion-- paata eseriani oltau-- metii entibili tukul-- tʼengomom Engai o tʼengomom oo ltung'anak."
Acts24:17 Ore peishunye laritin kumok-- nalotu naaki olorere lai nkishoorot-- o nkidasareitin."
Acts24:18 Ore too nona naadol aaitisinyari tʼengaji sinyati-- metii esiamu nemetii olodoo-- kake Yudayoi ooje le Asia ootii;"
Acts24:19 meata kata nemetii ninje engomom ino-- paaitang'or nanu-- teni eata mbaak te nanu."
Acts24:20 Arashu njelimu kulo oopeny-- kaa kitarruoto etadua te nanu-- aitasho tʼengomom enkigwena--"
Acts24:21 neme ele rorei obo lairoro-- aitashe too ninje-- ajo: Too mbaak enkitopiunoto oo lootuata aaigwenakini nanu taata too ndai!"
Acts24:22 Ore peidip Feliks atoning'o nena-- neitaany enkigwena engai olong'-- amu etayolo abaraki ena oitoi-- nejo: Teni elalotu olkitok Lisias-- nadung' ororei linyi."
Acts24:23 Neitanap olkigeluni-- perrip Paulos-- pemeinosie ninye osina nememitiki oltung'ani ora olenye elotu enetii."
Acts24:24 Ore peishunye ngolong'i kuti-- nelotu Feliks te nebo o eng'oroyoni enye Drusila nara Eyudayos-- neipot Paulos nening' mbaak enkirukoto e atua Kristos Yesus."
Acts24:25 Ore peiro Paulos mbaak esupato o nʼemitikinoto oo mbaak oo nkiri o nʼenkigwena nalotu-- neureishoi Feliks nealiki: Nno taata-- ore pebau enkata nanyor-- naaitoki aipot iye."
Acts24:26 Neanyu ninye baiki-- ten ake eisho Paulos ninye ngoshola-- peiye elaku ninye; onaa etopona aipot neirorie ninye."
Acts24:27 Ore peishunye laritin aare-- neaku Porkios Festos olasujani le Feliks. Neyeu Feliks neiting'id Yudayoi neing'ua Paulos eena."
Acts25:1 Ore pebaia Festos embalbal enye-- neilep-- eishunyete ngolong'i uni-- alo Yerusalem eing'ua Kaisarea."
Acts25:2 Nepuonu laidasak kituak o Yudayoi kituak-- peitang'or Paulos-- neirorie ninye naleng'"
Acts25:3 neomon entoki empuris-- peisho elotu ninye Yerusalem; neoseku-- pear ninye tʼengoitoi metua."
Acts25:4 Nealu Festos-- ajo erripi Paulos te Kaisarea-- netaana-- peitoki alo ninye ang'."
Acts25:5 Nejo: Entadou looidim te nebo o nanu-- pintang'oring'oro ninye-- teni etii entorroni tʼele tung'ani."
Acts25:6 Ore peidip atobiko tʼempolos enye ngolong'i nemelang' isiet arashu tomon-- nedoiyo alo Kaisarea; neton tʼengai olong' tʼolorika lʼenkigwena neitanapu-- perikuni Paulos."
Acts25:7 Ore pelotu-- neitasheiki Yudayoi ootadoutuo eing'ua Yerusalem ninye-- neau nkitang'orot kumok naairoshi nemeidim aaitagolo--"
Acts25:8 amu etomituo Paulos kion nejo: Me tʼolbae loo nkitanapat oo Yudayoi neme tʼolbae lʼengaji sinyati neme tʼolbae le kaisar eitu aitarruo toki.
Acts25:9 Neyeu Festos neiting'id Yudayoi nealiki Paulos nejoki: Iyeu nilo iye Yerusalem-- pikingwenakini te ina alo tʼolbae loo kuna baak tʼengomom ai?"
Acts25:10 Nejo Paulos: Aitashe nanu tʼengomom olorika le kaisar-- ine wueji ake naaku-- paaigwenakinyeki. Eitu aitarruoki Yudayoi anaa piyolo si iye naleng'."
Acts25:11 Amu teni aitarruoiye arashu aitobira entoki nanang'-- maany ae; akae-- teni me toki aaitang'orie kulo-- maaidim oltung'ani aitarasaki ninje. Aipotie kaisar!"
Acts25:12 Ore peidip airorie Festos enkigwena-- nealu: Impotie kaisar-- ilo enetii kaisar."
Acts25:13 Ore peishunye ngolong'i naaje-- nebaia olkarsis Agripas o Bernike Kaisarea-- peiroroki Festos."
Acts25:14 Ore pebik ngolong'i kumok o ninye-- neitayolo Festos olkarsis mbaak e Paulos nejo: Etii oltung'ani obo otung aiye Feliks eena."
Acts25:15 Ore atii nanu Yerusalem-- nepuonu laidasak kituak o laigwenak loo Yudayoi engomom ai naaomonu earata enye."
Acts25:16 Naliki ninje-- ajo me orregie loo Romayoi-- peitarasari oltung'ani-- peari metua-- metii oloitang'oroki o looitang'or-- peing'oraro ngomomi-- neishori enkata namitunye kion too nena kitang'orot."
Acts25:17 Akae-- ore petumo te ine-- eitu aimutie-- naton tʼengolong' e are tʼolorika lʼenkigwena naitanapu-- perikuni ilo tung'ani;"
Acts25:18 neitasheiki ninye kulo looitang'oro ninye neitu elimu anaa paibirribirrua-- ororei torrono."
Acts25:19 Kake eata ake nkitarrikinot naaje te ninye nʼenkisyayare Engai enye o nʼoltung'ani obo Yesus lotua loimaka Paulos-- ajo eishiu."
Acts25:20 Ore peitu ayolo enaiko tʼolbae Perishare oo kuna kitarrikinot-- naikilikwan ninye-- ten ake eyeu nelo Yerusalem-- peigwenakini te ina alo too kuna baak."
Acts25:21 Kake ore peipotoki Paulos kion-- perripokini enkigwena e kaisar-- naitanapisho-- perripi metabana nairriwaa enetii kaisar."
Acts25:22 Nejoki Agripas Festos: Ayeu si nanu nainining' ele tung'ani. Nejo si ninye: Ilainining' taisere.
Acts25:23 Ore enasirie nepuonu Agripas o Bernike tʼenkitook kitok nejing' engaji enkigwena te nebo o ilkituak loo ltimito o ilkituak lʼengang'-- neitanapisho Festos-- perikuni Paulos."
Acts25:24 Nejo Festos: Olkarsis Agripas o ndai lelea pookin litiiti e nebo o yook-- idolitata ele tung'ani laatayeuokitio esiamu pookin oo Yudayoi enatii-- te Yerusalem o tʼene-- eapaa iltoiloi-- aajo meaku-- pepon aishiu."
Acts25:25 Ore padol si nanu-- ajo eitu eitobir ororei lonang' neipotoki ninye openy kion kaisar-- naigwenu-- pairriwaa ninye."
Acts25:26 Namaata mbaak enyena naaitoriori nasiraki olaitoriani. Onaa atorikuo ninye engomom inyi-- ore naleng' engomom ino-- olkarsis Agripas-- peiye ore peaku nkikilikwanat-- natum ororei pasir;"
Acts25:27 amu adol-- ajo meaku-- peirriwari oloena nemetii entoki naitang'orieki ninye."
Acts26:1 Nejoki Agripas Paulos: Kinjori pilimu rorei tʼolbae lino. Neitorioo Paulos engaina-- pemitu kion-- nejo:"
Acts26:2 Lekarsis Agripas-- ating'ide-- tiaraki naidim atomitu kion tʼengomom ino taata too mbaak pookin naaitang'orie Yudayoi--"
Acts26:3 nang'ida naleng'-- tiaraki niyolo iye rregiei o nkitarrikinot pookin atua Yudayoi; onaa aasai iye-- pikinining'u tʼemborran."
Acts26:4 Eyolo Yudayoi pookin empuan ai eiter tʼenkeraishu-- ati neba tʼenkiterata atua olorere lai te Yerusalem--"
Acts26:5 laatayoloutuo neba opa-- teni enyorru aaijakenutu; amu atobiko anaa Olfarisayos loibung' orregie ogol naleng' lʼenkisyayare Engai ang'."
Acts26:6 Ore taata aitashe naaigwenakini t'olbae lʼeanyunoto enkisiligata naishoo Engai loopapa lang'--"
Acts26:7 ore te ina eanyu nkishomitie ang' tomon o are nenyok aasaisho dama o kiarie peaku. Ore tʼolbae le ina anyunoto aaitang'or Yudayoi-- lekarsis."
Acts26:8 Ainyo pemeirukoi too ndai-- aajo eitopiu Engai lootuata?"
Acts26:9 Atejo nanu tiatua kion-- ajo meata kata namaitobir mbaak kumok-- pamit engarna e Yesus le Nasaret;"
Acts26:10 anaa paikuna te Yerusalem-- ateena sinyat kumok tʼengaji erripore-- aidipa ainoto engolon too laidasak kituak; atang'arie si nanu enkigwena-- earitai ninje metuata."
Acts26:11 Naitame ninje aigil kumok tiatua ngajijik Engai kumok naaraki ninje-- pemorisho; ore aareota engoro naleng'-- naar ninje baiki tiatua ngang'itie oo nkwapi."
Acts26:12 Ore te ina aloito Damaskos-- aata engolon o enkitanapata oo laidasak kituak--"
Acts26:13 euno engolong'-- lekarsis-- nadol tʼengoitoi enkilang'et naing'ua shumata nelang' enkilang'et engolong'-- naailang'aki nanu o lʼemboitei ai."
Acts26:14 Nikibatatakino yook pookin enkop-- naning' oltoilo laairorie nanu ojo too rorei lʼenkutuk oo Lhebrayoi: Saul-- Saul-- ainyo pikimirita? Egol te iye piruaia olkikarret."
Acts26:15 Najo nanu: Ira ng'ai-- Laitoriani? Nejo Olaitoriani: Ara nanu Yesus likimirita iye. Kake tudumunye-- pintashe too nkejek inono."
Acts26:16 Onaa aaipung'oko-- paaitaa iye olaisyayani o oljakeni loo kuna baak nitadua o nikipuoi aaitadol;"
Acts26:17 nayeu naaitopok iye tiatua ele orere o tiatua kulekai oreren-- naairriwaki iye taata enetii kulo--"
Acts26:18 pibol ngonyek enye nimbelekeny ninje-- peing'ua enaimin nebaiki enkilang'et-- peing'ua engolon e satan aapuo enetii Engai-- peng'amu enkitaunoto oo nkitarruot o enjung'o te nebo o kulo loosinyari tʼenkirukoto naairuk nanu."
Acts26:19 Neitu amen si nanu ena kitaduaroto e shumata-- lekarsis Agripas--"
