Acts26:20 kake ainosaka tʼenkata elukunya lootii Damaskos o Yerusalem o atua olosho pookin loo Yudayoi o too kulekai oreren-- peala neibelekenyakino Engai-- peitobir nkyasin sidan enkitaalata."
Acts26:21 Ore tʼolbae loo nona naaibung' Yudayoi tiatua engaji sinyati neyeu naar matua.
Acts26:22 Akae-- ore tʼeretokinoto Engai natii metabaiki ena olong' e taata naijakenisho too lkutiti o too lkituak namairo o nyoo neme enairo layolounok o Mose-- peaku neijia--"
Acts26:23 aajo eitamei Kristos neaku olaiturukoni tiatua empiunoto oo lootuata neinosaki olorere lenye o kulekai oreren mbaak enkilang'et.
Acts26:24 Ore emitu ninye kion nji-- nejo Festos tʼoltoilo kitok: Iata oloirirua-- Paulos! Kintaa eng'eno kitok-- pitum oloirirua."
Acts26:25 Nejo Paulos: Maata oloirirua-- Festos kitok-- kake alimu rorei lʼesipata o lʼentemet."
Acts26:26 Amu eyolo olkarsis kuna pookin nairo tʼengomom enye tʼeng'ida-- nayolo-- ajo meisudoroi te ninye ororei o obo too kulo-- amu eitu eaku kuna baak t'embata."
Acts26:27 Lekarsis Agripas-- iruk iye layolounok? Ayolo-- ajo iruk."
Acts26:28 Nejoki si ninye Agripas: Paulos-- ore too nkuti kisis si nanu-- paaku Olkristianos."
Acts26:29 Nejo Paulos: Ayeu tʼengomom Engai-- too nkuti arashu too nkumok-- peaku me iye ake-- kake pookin laainining'ito taata-- anaa nanu-- metii kuna eneta."
Acts26:30 Ore peidip airoro ninye kuna-- nedumunye olkarsis o Olaitoriani lʼolosho o Bernike o loototonitio te nebo o ninje--"
Acts26:31 nepuo embata neirorioro oopeny nejo: Eitu eitaas ele tung'ani entoki nanang' arashu enaenyeki.
Acts26:32 Nejoki Agripas Festos: Anaata elakuni ele tung'ani-- ten emutu eitu eipotoki kion kaisar."
Acts27:1 Ore peigwenakini-- pikipuo yook tʼengalawa metabaiki Italia-- neitarasakini Paulos o ilkulekai looena olkigeluni obo-- oji engama enye Yulios-- lʼoltim le kaisar."
Acts27:2 Nikilepaki engalawa e Adramiteno-- natayeuo nalo ngang'itie naatii embata e Asia; netii e nebo o yook Aristarkos le Makedonia-- lʼengang' Tesalonike."
Acts27:3 Ore tʼengolong' e are nikibaia Sidon; neitobiraki Yulios Paulos nʼemborran neisho ninye-- pelo enetii iljorueta lenyena-- pesaru ninye too yeunot."
Acts27:4 Ore pikindip aatung'ai ina alo-- nikiim abori e Kupros-- tiaraki narriny yook enkijape."
Acts27:5 Nikiim olbalbal le Kilikia o Pamfilia nikibaia engang' Mira e Likia.
Acts27:6 Nedol te ina alo olkigeluni engalawa e Aleksandria naloito Italia-- neilepakinye yook."
Acts27:7 Ore pikipuo akiti-- nikibaia too ngolong'i kumok tʼosina Knidos-- nemitiki yook enkijape-- nikiim abori e Krete nikibaia Salmone--"
Acts27:8 nikiporoo ninye tʼosina nikipuonu ewueji neji Enkutoto sidai-- netaaniki engang' Lasaya."
Acts27:9 Ore peishunye ngolong'i kumok neitoki aaku osina kitok kipuo tʼolbalbal-- eima enkata napukori-- neitayolo Paulos"
Acts27:10 nejoki ninje: Lelea-- adol-- ajo elaata elʼlototo lʼengalawa osina kitok-- me loo masaa o lʼengalawa ake-- kake baiki lʼempuan ang'."
Acts27:11 Kake eiruko olkigeluni olaiturukoni o olopeny engalawa nelang' kuna naairoro Paulos.
Acts27:12 Tiaraki neme sidai enkutoto-- pebik te ina alo tʼenkata enkirobi-- neyeu ilkumok neing'ua ina alo-- pebaia Foiniks-- pebik te ina alo tʼenkata enkirobi-- nera enkutoto e Krete natii erishata eunore o endoiyoroto engolong' o erishata endoiyoroto engolong' o shumata."
Acts27:13 Ore pekutishoi enkijape eunore engolong'-- nejo ninje einoto enatayeutuo-- nedotu eenet neim enetaaniki Krete naleng'."
Acts27:14 Ore tʼenkiti kata nekut enkijape nadumisho-- neitu edamu ninje-- naimua erishata enkilepunoto engolong' o shumata."
Acts27:15 Ore peibung'i engalawa neitu eidim aitoriokinore enkijape-- nikinjo metanapi yook."
Acts27:16 Nikipuo aasioki embata oloigeruno loji Klauda-- nikitum tʼosina aaibung'a embout--"
Acts27:17 nikidumu ninye-- peretoki yook-- nikien engalawa ang' abori too nkeenda; ore pikiurei-- aajo kidoiki atua Sirtis-- nikintadou rasheta enkijape-- nenapi yook neijia."
Acts27:18 Ore pekut yook enkijape naleng'-- neiter aaiturraa ninje tʼengolong' e are masaa."
Acts27:19 Ore tʼengolong' e uni nikinturraki too ngaik ang' nareta engalawa enelakwa.
Acts27:20 Neitu elioi engolong' o lakir too ngolong'i kumok neiposhita yook enkijape neme kiti-- neish osiligi lʼempuan too yook."
Acts27:21 Ore peitu enya ninje endaa ngolong'i kumok neitashe Paulos tʼempolos enye nejoki ninje: Lelea-- anaata kitoning'o nanu-- pimidotutu te Krete-- pikitum ele sina o enkiminata oo masaa."
Acts27:22 Kake ore taata-- adiding' ndai-- entagolo iltauja-- amu meimin o obo tiatua ndai-- neme engalawa ake."
Acts27:23 Amu aaitasheikio tʼena kiarie olmalaika lʼEngai nara olenye-- naa ninye oshi aisyayaki nanu--"
Acts27:24 nejo: Miureisho-- Paulos-- meata kata nimintashe tʼengomom e kaisar! Naa ng'orai-- kinyaaka aisho iye Engai pookin liboitare tʼolototo."
Acts27:25 Onaa-- lelea-- entagolo iltauja-- amu airuk Engai-- ajo eaku neijia anaa paatiakaki."
Acts27:26 Kake meata kata nimikibaiki oloigeruno obo.
Acts27:27 Ore pebau enkiarie e tomon o ong'wan-- nenapi yook ngaloli pookin tiatua olbalbal Adria-- nejo iltung'anak lʼengalawa tʼempolos e kiarie-- etaaniki olosho."
Acts27:28 Neitadou entemet-- netum ntemeta tikitam; ore penyikaa peno-- neitoki aitadou entemet-- netum ntemeta tomon o imiet."
Acts27:29 Neureishoi-- pemeitabaari yook enetii soito; neitadoiyo eneta ong'wan tekurum engalawa-- neyeu nekenyu."
Acts27:30 Ore peyeu iltung'anak lʼengalawa nekwet aaing'ua engalawa neitadoiki embout atua olbalbal anaa looyeu neitadoiki eenet lukunya engalawa--"
Acts27:31 nejoki Paulos olkigeluni o sikerin: Teni mebik kulo tiatua engalawa-- nimindimidimi aatopok ndai."
Acts27:32 Nedung' isikerin nkeenda embout neisho edoiyo.
Acts27:33 Ore pekenyu enasirie-- nediding' Paulos pookin-- penya endaa nejo: Era taata engolong' e tomon o ong'wan-- itaanyishote nitonini neitu inyanya endaa-- neitu intubutubu nkutukie."
Acts27:34 Onaa adiding' ndai-- pinyanya endaa-- amu eaku ena nʼenkitopuata inyi; amu medoiyo olpapita o obo too lukuny inyi."
Acts27:35 Ore peidip atejo kuna-- neibung' olmkate neliki Engai ashe tʼengomom oo pookin-- negiligil neiter anya."
Acts27:36 Negolu iltauja pookin nenya si ninje endaa.
Acts27:37 Nikiaku pookin looishiu tiatua engalawa iip are o ntomoni naapishana o ile.
Acts27:38 Ore peidip aataraposhoto-- neiteneneng' engalawa neiturraki endaa dorrop atua olbalbal."
Acts27:39 Ore pekenyu-- neitu eyolou ninje olosho-- kake etadua olkutoto loata embata sidai olosho-- neyeu neitijing' engalawa atua-- ten ake eaku."
Acts27:40 Nedung' eneta neing'ua tiatua olbalbal neitololong' nkeenda eriket engalawa neilepakinye olkarash lʼenkijape nepuoiye embata olosho.
Acts27:41 Ore pebaia ewueji neata too mbat pokira are olbalbal-- nenang'ari engalawa neitirrishi lukunya neitashe neitu eing'unung'un-- nedanya kurum tʼengolon enkiposhai."
Acts27:42 Neigwena sikerin-- peari looena metuata-- pemepor oltung'ani engare ailanyisho."
Acts27:43 Kake etayeuo olkigeluni neitopok Paulos nemitiki ninje-- pemeitobir enatayeutuo neitanapu-- penang'akino aang'as kulo olbalbal ooyolo aatapor engare-- pebaia olosho;"
Acts27:44 ore lootelekutua nejing' kulekai shumata oo mbaon o kulekai shumata oo nareta engalawa. Neaku nji netum aatabai pookin aa biot atua olosho.
Acts28:1 Ore pikindip aatopoku-- nikiyolou-- aajo eji engarna oloigeruno Melite."
Acts28:2 Neitobiraki yook loomanya nʼempuris enye oopeny: neinok enkima neitoomon yook pookin-- tiaraki natasha enjan o tʼolbae lʼenkirobi."
Acts28:3 Ore peiturrur Paulos orridati loo lkeek nepik atua enkima-- nepuku olasurai tʼenkirowuaj neibung' engaina enye."
Acts28:4 Ore pedol kulo tung'anak olasurai eililiokino engaina enye-- neirorioro oopeny: Esipa-- era ele tung'ani olarani-- etopokua tiatua olbalbal-- kake meisho elaata oo ntorrok-- peishiu."
Acts28:5 Nenang'aki ninye ake olowuaru atua enkima neitu etum entorroni.
Acts28:6 Neanyu kulo peiju arashu erria nabokata etua. Ore peidip aataanyu naleng'-- nedol-- aajo meaku toki-- neibelekenya nejo ninje-- aajo ninye Engai."
Acts28:7 Ore enemanita ene netii nkuruman olkitok lʼoloigeruno oji engarna enye Publios-- otang'amua yook neitaa yook lomon lenyena ngolong'i uni."
Acts28:8 Neaku eirraga menye le Publios tʼerruat neata oltikana nerotu osarge; nejing' Paulos enetii nesaisho neiteleiki ngaik neishiunye ninye.
Acts28:9 Ore peidip aataa kuna-- nepuonu ilkulekai loomoiyaa tiatua oloigeruno neishiunyeki."
Acts28:10 Neitaa ninje yook kituak tʼenkitook kitok. Ore pikipuo-- neilepakinye yook ntokitin naabaiki yook."
Acts28:11 Ore peishunye lapaitin okuni-- nikipuo tʼengalawa e Aleksandria natobiko-- tʼengalo oloigeruno tʼenkata enkirobi neata olponoto lenye: Ilmao."
Acts28:12 Ore pikipuonu Sirakusai-- nikibik ngolong'i uni."
Acts28:13 Nikimanaa king'ua ina alo nikibaia Region. Ore peishunye engolong' nabo-- nekutunye enkijape eunore engolong' nikipuonu tʼengolong' e are Puteoli."
Acts28:14 Nikinepu te ina alo lalashera nesai ninje yook-- pikibik ngolong'i naapishana. Nikibau tekurum Roma."
Acts28:15 Ore pening' lalashera le ina alo mbaak ang'-- nepuonu aatumore yook te Apioforum o Trestaberne. Ore pedol Paulos ninje-- neliki Engai ashe negolu."
Acts28:16 Ore pikibaia Roma-- neitarasaki olkigeluni looena olkitok lʼoltim. Neishori Paulos metotona tʼewueji enye openy te nebo o osikeri obo orripito."
Acts28:17 Ore peishunye ngolong'i uni-- neipot Paulos ilkituak loo Yudayoi. Ore pepuonu-- nejoki ninje: Lelea-- lalashera-- eitu aitobir entoki torrono tiatua olorere lang' arashu tʼorregie loo loopapa lang'-- naarikuni ake aena te Yerusalem naaitarasakini atua ngaik oo Romayoi."
Acts28:18 Ore paaidip aaikilikwana kulo-- neyeu naalaku-- amu metii entoki nanang' atua nanu."
Acts28:19 Kake ore peing'unyung'unyaki Yudayoi ninje-- naaitagolikini-- paipotoki kion kaisar-- me anaa Oloata ororei laitang'orie olorere lai."
Acts28:20 Onaa aipoto ndai-- paduare nairorie ndai; amu tʼolbae lʼeanyunoto e Israel aamanita ele pisiai."
Acts28:21 Nejoki lelo: Eitu king'amu yook empalai tʼolbae lino-- eing'ua Yudaya-- nemetii oltung'ani tiatua lalashera oewuo ene-- peinosaki neliki yook mbaak torrok te iye."
Acts28:22 Kake kinyor aatoning' te iye eniata-- amu kitayoloutuo te ina kiteng'enare ng'ejuk aajo eing'unyung'unyakini ninye too wuejitin pookin."
Acts28:23 Nedung'oki ninje ninye engolong' nepuonu ilkumok engaji enye natii-- neitayolo neijakenoki ninje enkarsishu Engai neinosaki mbaak e Yesus tiatua nkitanapat e Mose o tiatua layolounok-- eiter enasirie metabaiki teipa."
Acts28:24 Neiruk ematua enairoro ninye-- neitu eiruk kulekai."
Acts28:25 Ore peitarrikino ninje tʼempolos enye-- nepuo-- eidipa Paulos airoro ororei obo: Sidai enatiaka Olmumua Sinyati loopapa lang' tʼenkutuk olayolounoni Yesaya"
Acts28:26 nejo: Nno enetii ele orere-- piro: Ipuopuo aaning' too nkiyaa nimiyolouu-- nipuopuo aaing'oraa too ngonyek nimidolidolo;"
Acts28:27 amu epising'a oltau lʼele orere neiroshi nkiyaa enye tʼening'ore-- neiturukuny ngonyek enye-- pemepuo aadol too ngonyek nemening' too nkiyaa nemetum eng'eno too ltauja-- peala-- paitopok."
Acts28:28 Akae-- entayolo-- ajo eirriwakaki enkitopuata Engai loreren-- nepuo aaning' ninje."
Acts28:29 Ore eirorita kuna-- nepuo Yudayoi-- eata nkikilikwanat kumok tʼempolos enye."
Acts28:30 Nebik Paulos tʼengaji enye nainyang'ua emanyata enkata oo larin aare oolulung'a neng'amu pookin ootijing'a engaji enye--"
Acts28:31 neinosu enkarsishu Engai neiteng'enu tʼeng'ida pookin mbaak e Yesus Kristos nememitikini.
Romans1:1 Paulos-- osinga le Yesus Kristos-- oipotoki metaa olairriwani-- netegeluaki peinosu lomon sidan lʼEngai--"
Romans1:2 ootang'asa Engai aisilig too layolounok tiatua esirata sinyati--"
Romans1:3 tʼolbae lʼOinoti lenye-- otoiwuoki tʼeishoi e David tʼempukunoto oo nkiri--"
Romans1:4 neitaduaki tʼengolon-- ajo era Oinoti lʼEngai tʼempukunoto Olmumua osinyaa-- neba empiunoto too lootuata-- lora Yesus Kristos-- Olaitoriani lang'."
Romans1:5 Kinoto te ninye engaripo o enkirriwaroto-- penyor aairuko loolamita Engai pookin Tengarna enye--"
Romans1:6 nirara si ndai tiatua lelo ooipotuo Yesus Kristos: —
Romans1:7 enitiiti ndai pookin ootii Roma-- loonyor Engai-- ooipotoki metaa sinyat. Njebikie ndai eng'adunoto o eseriani naing'ua Engai Papa lang'-- o Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos."
Romans1:8 Ang'as aliki Engai ai ashe-- tiatua Yesus Kristos tʼolbae linyi pookin-- tiaraki nalikiori enkirukoto inyi tiatua olmaa pookin."
Romans1:9 Amu ore Engai naisyayaki tiatua Olmumua lai nalikioo lomon sidan lʼOinoti lenye-- naa ninye oljakeni lai-- padamu oshi ake ndai"
Romans1:10 tiatua sayat ainei-- naomonu anake eaku-- palotu enitiiti-- teni eyeu Engai."
Romans1:11 Amu ayeu naleng' nadol ndai-- patum aishoo ndai enkishooroto emumuaishu-- aitagol ndai--"
Romans1:12 eji paailejileji nanu te nebo o ndai tʼenkirukoto inyi o enai-- nikiatakino."
Romans1:13 Mayeu nimiyololo ndai-- lalashera-- ajo aibung'a aigil kumok alotu enitiiti-- naamitikini metabaiki taata-- patum ilmomo baiki tiatua ndai-- anaa baiki tiatua kulekai oreren."
Romans1:14 Aata nanu esile oo Lgrikini o noo nkwapi-- noo lang'eni o noo lemera lang'eni."
Romans1:15 Ore te nanu aitobirakine-- painosaki si ndai tiatua Roma lomon Peng'ida."
Romans1:16 Amu makurru nanu too lomon Peng'ida le Kristos; amu era ninje engolon Engai-- peaku enkitopuata oltung'ani pookin oiruk-- ang'as en Oyudayos neitoki en Olgriki."
Romans1:17 Amu eboluni tiatua ninje esupato Engai naing'ua enkirukoto nejing atua enkirukoto-- anaa petisiraki: Elaishiu osupat tʼenkirukoto."
Romans1:18 Amu etabolokoki engoro Engai naing'ua shumata entorroni pookin o empaashata esupato oo ltung'anak looibok esipata tiatua empaashata esupato--"
Romans1:19 amu enayolouni tʼEngai neibala too ninje; amu eitadua Engai ninje kuna.
Romans1:20 Amu eyolouni ntokitin enyena nemelio-- nera enkidimata enye oo nkatan pookin o engaishu-- tʼenkitobirata olmaa-- nelioi too nkyasin enyena; onaa-- meata ninje emitunoto."
Romans1:21 Tiaraki natayoloutuo Engai-- kake eitu eitadaraa ninye anaa Engai neitu eliki ashe; kake eibelekenyate tiatua ndamunot enye-- neitoipoki iltauja lenye aaku enaimin."
Romans1:22 Nejo aten aa ng'eni-- neaku ninje moda."
Romans1:23 Neibelekeny enkitook Engai nemeata erruoroto naitanyanyukie emua oltung'ani loata erruoroto-- o en oo ntaritik-- o en oo ng'wesi oo nkejek ong'wan-- o en oo ng'wesi naaikurtutari."
Romans1:24 Akae-- eitarasaka Engai ninje tiatua ilng'warrat loo ltauja lenye atua olduruki-- peitobir aten too seseni lenye nʼenkurruna."
Romans1:25 Amu ninje ooibelekenya esipata atua elejare-- neitaa kitok neisyayaki enkitobirata aaitalang' olaitobirani-- oitadarari nkatan pookin."
Romans1:26 Onaa-- eitarasaka Engai ninje atua ilng'warraitin lʼenkurruna-- amu ore ng'oroyok enye eibelekenya orregie oishiaakino aaitaa orregie lemeishiaakino;"
Romans1:27 neijia si eikuna leak-- etung'aitie orregie oitoriori te nebo o eng'oroyoni-- neinokino aten too lng'warraitin lenye-- leak o leak-- neas mbaak enkurruna-- netum olkwaje orisiore enkiminata enye."
Romans1:28 Neijia anaa petanyaita aatayolou Engai-- neijia eitarasaka Engai atua ndamunot naariwuo metaasa enemeitoriori--"
Romans1:29 neigany mesupato pookin o entalare o empiani o entorroni-- loobore olom-- earata metua-- enjangar-- olosek-- esayet-- enkisuro--"
Romans1:30 looiteeniki-- looiba Engai-- looitai loikop-- loowuasa-- looilash-- looiminye-- lemening' lootoiutuo ninje--"
Romans1:31 lootolo-- lemeibung' osotua-- lemeata enyorrata-- lemeing'uaikino-- lemeata engoshoke nanana."
Romans1:32 Eyolo ninje esupato Engai-- aajo ore kulo looas nona-- nenarikino enkea-- kake neme ninje oopeny ooas-- eshipakino baiki ilkulekai ooas."
Romans2:1 Onaa-- miata emitunoto-- oltung'ani pookin eigwenaki; amu eningwenakinye olekai-- ningwenakinye kion-- amu intobir kuna ningwenaki."
Romans2:2 Kake kiyolo-- aajo era enkigwena Engai esipata too kulo looiko neijia."
Romans2:3 Kake ijo aa iye-- letung'ani-- oigwenaki looitobir kuna nintobir si iye-- ijo ilakwet iye enkigwena Engai?"
Romans2:4 Arashu imen endupoto emborran enye o olng'iria o olgira? Miyolo-- ajo kirikoki emborran Engai enkirridunoto?"
Romans2:5 Kake inturrurroki iye kion tʼengogong'i ino o tʼoltau leitu eala engoro tʼengolong' engoro o embolunoto enkigwena supat Engai--"
Romans2:6 nalaisho oltung'ani pookin noo nkitobirat enyena:
Romans2:7 kulo looing'oru tʼolng'iria loo nkitobirat sidan empuan nemeiting'-- enkitadararoto o enkitaaroto enkitook;"
Romans2:8 kake kulo loora ilkiminjal lʼolarrabal nemening' esipata nening' nemera esupato-- engoro o enairowua."
Romans2:9 Enkilishoto o osina Olmumua pookin oitobir ntorrok-- ang'as lʼOyudayos-- baiki lʼOlgriki;"
Romans2:10 enkitadarraroto o enkitaaroto enkitook o eseriani oltung'ani pookin oitobir sidan-- ang'as Oyudayos-- baiki Olgriki."
Romans2:11 Amu meing'oraa Engai entemet oltung'ani.
Romans2:12 Amu ore lelo ooitarruoitie meata nkitanapat-- nepuo aaimin meata nkitanapat-- o lelo ooitarruoitie tiabori oo nkitanapat-- nepuoi aaigwenaki too nkitanapat."
Romans2:13 Amu me looning' nkitanapat era supati tʼengomom Engai-- kake looitobir ninje-- nepuo aaku supati."
Romans2:14 Amu teni eitobir loreren lemeyolo Engai-- lemeata nkitanapat-- tʼentonai enye openy nkitanapat-- neaku ninje-- lemeata nkitanapat-- nkitanapat enye oopeny--"
Romans2:15 neitadolu ninje-- aajo etisiraki enkyas oo nkitanapat tiatua iltauja lenye-- neijakenu oltoilo lʼoltau lenye-- baiki ndamunot naaitang'oro nemitikino;"
Romans2:16 te ina olong' naigwenakinye Engai nkisudorot oo ltung'anak te Yesus Kristos-- tʼerisioroto oo lomon lʼeng'ida lainei."
Romans2:17 Akae-- ng'orai-- iye likiji Oyudayos niimany nkitanapat ning'idare Engai--"
Romans2:18 niyolo eyeunoto enye; ore tiaraki nikindipaki aaiteng'ena tiatua nkitanapat-- nileen enara sidai-- peitobiri--"
Romans2:19 nijo indim ataa Olarikoni loo lmodook-- enkilang'et oo kulo ootoni tiatua enaimin--"
Romans2:20 olashukoni loo lʼmoda-- olaiteng'enani loo nkera naashal-- olotiu anaa jartani tiatua eyolounoto o esipata oo nkitanapat."
Romans2:21 Kake inteng'en olekai niminteng'en kion? Inosaki-- ajo mipurrisho-- nipurrisho iye openy?"
Romans2:22 Ijo-- miar enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni-- niar iye ninye? Ira iye oiba nkulie ain-- nioru enkitook Engai?"
Romans2:23 Iimany nkitanapat-- nintukurru Engai ipaashare nkitanapat?"
Romans2:24 Amu „tʼolbae linyi emori engarna Engai tiatua lemeata Engai“-- anaa petisiraki."
Romans2:25 Amu edupa emurata-- teni imbung' nkitanapat; kake teni mimbung' nkitanapat-- indipa ataa olememurata-- baiki teni kitumurataki."
Romans2:26 Ore teni eibung' olememurata esupato oo nkitanapat-- ke meikeni ninye-- ajo etumurataki?"
Romans2:27 Akae-- kilaigwenaki ele-- leitu emurati tʼosesen neibung' nkitanapat-- iye-- litii atua esirata o emurata nipaashare nkitanapat."
Romans2:28 Amu me ninye Oyudayos ora Oyudayos oriong'-- nemera ina emurata-- naitobiri too nkiri--"
Romans2:29 kake ilo-- lora Oyudayos tiatua-- naa ina emurata oltau-- naitobiri tʼolmumua-- me tʼesirata. Ore oloikununo nji-- neitadarari ninye tʼEngai-- me too ltung'anak."
Romans3:1 Kaa dupoto eata Yudayoi? Anai kedupa sa emurata nyoo?
Romans3:2 Edupa naleng' tʼorregie pookin. Ore tʼenkiterata-- eishooki ninje rorei lʼEngai."
Romans3:3 Kake teni eitu eiruk kulekai-- keibelekeny eanyata enye enkirukoto Engai?"
Romans3:4 Me neijia. Njoo Engai metisipai neaku oltung'ani pookin olalejani-- anaa petisiraki: pekintaai supat too rorei linono nigilu tʼenkata nikingwenakinyeki."
Romans3:5 Kake-- teni eitabaia mesupato ang' esupato Engai-- kijo nyoo? ke Engai nemera supat-- tiaraki nagoro? (Airo tʼorregie loo ltung'anak.)"
Romans3:6 Me neijia. Amu kaji eiko ten eidim Engai aigwenaki olmaa?
Romans3:7 Amu teni epon elejare ai esipata Engai neaku nʼenkitook enye-- ainyo paaigwenakini ade anaa olaitarruoni?"
Romans3:8 Meikash pekinko anaa pemori yook neimaki yook kulekai pekijo yook: maitobira ntorrok-- peaku ade sidan? ore earata natum ninje-- neitoriori."
Romans3:9 Ainyo naa? Kidupo yook aalang' ilkulekai? Me neijia katukul. Kitang'asa duo aaitadolu-- aajo etii pokira are-- Yudayoi o Ilgrikini-- tiabori oo nkitarruot--"
Romans3:10 anaa petisiraki: Metii olora supat o obo--"
Romans3:11 nemetii oltung'ani ng'en nemetii oloing'oru Engai.
Romans3:12 Amu etalamate pookin neaku pookin serserin-- nemetii oloitobir sidan o obo."
Romans3:13 Ore olgos lenye-- naa enkurare nabolo-- eiro too lng'ejepa lenye elejare-- netii esayet oo lasuria tiabori oo njonito oo nkutukie enye--"
Romans3:14 nebore enkutuk enye endiata o enduaran--"
Romans3:15 nekwet ngejek enye aaibukoo osarge--"
Romans3:16 netii enkiminata o osina ngoitoi enye--"
Romans3:17 nemeyolo engoitoi eseriani--"
Romans3:18 nemeata enkuretishu Engai tʼengomom oo ngonyek enye.
Romans3:19 Kiyolo-- aajo enalimu nkitanapat-- neliki kulo ootii atua nkitanapat-- peiye enuki enkutuk pookin-- neauni oltung'ani pookin atua enkigwena Engai;"
Romans3:20 Amuoretoo nkitobirat oo nkitanapat-- meitaai supat enkiring'o o nabo tʼengomom enye. Amu too nkitanapat elotu eyolounoto oo nkitarruot."
Romans3:21 Akae-- etalie taata esupato Engai-- metii nkitanapat-- naijakenuoki too nkitanapat o too layolounok--"
Romans3:22 esupato Engai nataa tʼenkirukoto e atua Yesus Kristos tiatua pookin looiruk. Amu metii ene erishata:
Romans3:23 eitarruoitie ninje pookin neitong'or enkitook Engai
Romans3:24 neaku supati pesho-- tʼeng'adunoto enye-- tʼelakunoto tiatua Kristos Yesus"
Romans3:25 loitera apik Engai-- peaku enkidasare enkitobirakinoto tʼenkirukoto tiatua osarge lenye-- peaku olponoto lʼesupato enye tʼenkitaunoto oo nkitarruot-- naatobiko metabaiki taata tiatua olng'iria lʼEngai--"
Romans3:26 peaku olponoto lʼesupato enye tʼena kata e taata-- peaku ninye supat neitaa supat oloiruk Yesus."
Romans3:27 Akae-- kaji etii enkitadararoto? Eitaiyoki. Ke ti aa kitanapata? Noo nkitobirat? Me neijia-- kake tʼenkitanapata enkirukoto."
Romans3:28 Onaa kijo yook-- aajo eitaai oltung'ani supat tʼenkirukoto-- metii nkitobirat oo nkitanapat."
Romans3:29 Ore Engai-- ke Engai oo Yudayoi ake? Me Engai oo loreren lemeyolo ninye si? Ee-- baiki noo lelo oreren."
Romans3:30 Tiaraki naa Engai nabo-- naitaa supat lʼemurata tiatua enkirukoto o lememurata tʼolbae lʼenkirukoto."
Romans3:31 Ke kinturraa nkitanapat tʼolbae lʼenkirukoto? Me neijia-- kake kintasheye nekua kitanapat."
Romans4:1 Akae-- kijo aa-- kainyo einoto Papa lang' Abraham tʼorregie lʼosesen?"
Romans4:2 Kijo nji: Teni eitaaki Abraham supat too nkitobirat-- neata enkitadararoto-- kake me tʼengomom Engai."
Romans4:3 Kake kejo aa esirata? Ejo: Eiruko Abraham Engai-- neikenakini ninye esupato."
Romans4:4 Kake ilo oas nkitobirat-- meikenakini olkwaje tʼempuris-- kake tʼenarikinoto."
Romans4:5 Ore ilo lemeitobirisho-- kake eiruk oloitaa supat olaitarruoni-- neikenakini enkirukoto enye esupato."
Romans4:6 Neijia anaa pejo si David-- ajo eata ilo tung'ani enteshishu-- oikenaki Engai esupato-- metii nkitobirat--"
Romans4:7 nejo: Teshi looitaikiaki ntorrok enye neopori nkitarruot enye.
Romans4:8 Tesh oltung'ani lemeikenaki Olaitoriani enkitarruoto.
Romans4:9 Ore ena teshishu-- ke en oo lekua oomurata ake-- arashu noo lememurata si? Meata kata nimikijo: eikenakaki Abraham enkirukoto enye esupato."
Romans4:10 Kanu eikenakaki? Kemurata arashu memurata? me tʼemurata-- kake eton eitu emurata."
Romans4:11 Etang'amua olponoto lʼemurata aaku olmishire lʼesupato naing'ua enkirukoto-- naata ninye eton eitu emurata-- peiye eaku ninye menye loo pookin looiruk lememurata-- neikenakini si ninje esupato;"
Romans4:12 peitoki aaku menye lʼemurata-- me loo lekua oomurata ake-- kake oopuoiye baiki roruat enkirukoto-- natii atua Papa lang' Abraham te ina kata eton eitu emurata."
Romans4:13 Amu eitu etum Abraham o eishoi enye ina kisiligata-- ajo eaku olajung'oni lʼolmaa-- too nkitanapat-- kake tʼesupato enkirukoto."
Romans4:14 Amu teni eitaai lekua ooata nkitanapat lajung'ok-- neitaai en e pesho enkirukoto-- ore enkisiligata-- nemekure aa enkisiligata."
Romans4:15 Amu eau nkitanapat engoro-- amu enemetii nkitanapat-- nemetii empaashata."
Romans4:16 Akae-- meata kata nemelotu esupato aing'ua enkirukoto-- peaku nʼeng'adunoto-- netum ataa ina kisiligata eata engolon tʼeishoi pookin-- me te ina ake natii abori oo nkitanapat-- kake baiki te ina naata enkirukoto anaa Abraham-- lora Papa lang' pookin"
Romans4:17 (anaa petisiraki: Aatipika iye-- piaku menye loo loreren kumok)-- tʼengomom Engai-- neiruk ninye eitopiu lootuata neipot nekua nemetii-- petii."
Romans4:18 Neiruko-- metii eanyunoto-- neanyu ajo elaaku menye loo loreren kumok tʼolbae lʼororei otiakaki ninye: Neijia eaku eishoi ino."
Romans4:19 Neitu eshalu tiatua enkirukoto-- neitu eing'oraa osesen lenye oidipe atua-- amu etaa enkitook enye anaa larin iip-- neitu eing'oraa si enkea engoshoke e Sara."
Romans4:20 Amu eitu eing'arrirrore enkisiligata Engai anaa lemeiruk-- kake einoto engolon tiatua enkirukoto neitaa Engai kitok--"
Romans4:21 neitagolieki naleng' te ina-- ajo eata Engai enkidimata naitobirie enaisiligishe."
Romans4:22 Onaa-- eikenakaki ninye esupato."
Romans4:23 Kake eitu esiri nona tʼolbae lenye ake-- ajo eikenakaki ninye--"
Romans4:24 kake baiki tʼolbae lang'-- peikenakini si yook-- teni kiruk ele-- oitopiwuo Yesus Kristos too lootuata--"
Romans4:25 loishoruaki tʼolbae loo nkitaruot ang' neitopiwuoki tʼolbae lʼesupato ang'.
Romans5:1 Akae-- ore peishooki yook esupato naing'ua enkirukoto-- nikiata eseriani o Engai tʼOlaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos--"
Romans5:2 nikiata te ilo tʼenkirukoto enyikakinoto e atua ena ng'adunoto nikintasheye-- nikintadaraa tiatua ena tʼolbae lʼeanyunoto enkitook Engai."
Romans5:3 Kake me tʼena ake-- kintadaraa baiki tiatua sinaitin-- tiaraki nikiyolo-- aajo eitaa osina olng'iria--"
Romans5:4 o olng'iria enkitagoluoto-- o enkitagoluoto eanyunoto--"
Romans5:5 nemeishoru eanyunoto enkutaroto; amu etubukokoki enyorrata Engai atua iltauja lang' tʼOlmumua Sinyati oishooki yook.
Romans5:6 Amu etua baiki Kristos-- eton kira yook menat-- tʼenkata enye tʼolbae loo lemeata Engai."
Romans5:7 Amu eton mee o obo tʼolbae lʼosupat; kake ajo nanu-- eiteu atua oltung'ani tʼolbae loo sidan."
Romans5:8 Kake eitadolu Engai enyorrata enye too yook-- ajo etua Kristos tʼolbae lang'-- eton kira laitarruok."
Romans5:9 Akae-- eitopuaki yook naleng' te ninye tʼengoro-- eishooki yook esupato tʼosarge lenye."
Romans5:10 Amu teni eitobirakaki yook o Engai tʼenkea Oinoti lenye-- eton kira ilmang'ati-- nelusoo naleng'-- eidipaki aaitobiraki yook-- nikipok tiatua empuan enye."
Romans5:11 Me te ina ake-- kake kintadaraa baiki tiatua Engai tʼOlaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos-- likinotie taata enkitobirakinoto."
Romans5:12 Onaa-- neijia anaa petijing'a enkitarruoto tʼoltung'ani obo atua olmaa o tʼenkitarruoto enkea-- neijia eima enkea baiki atua iltung'anak pookin looitarruoitie pookin tiatua ele obo."
Romans5:13 Amu etii enkitarruoto atua olmaa eton metii nkitanapat-- kake eitu eikenakini enkitarruoto opa ina kata metii nkitanapat."
Romans5:14 Kake eitoria enkea iltung'anak eiter te Adam metabaiki Mose-- baiki kulo leitu eitarruo tʼerisioroto empaashata e Adam-- lora enkitanyanyukiet e ilo otipikaki-- pelotu tekurum."
Romans5:15 Kake meikununo enkishooroto anaa enkitarruoto. Teni etuata ilkumok tʼolbae lʼenkitarruoto ele obo-- nelusoo naleng' eng'adunoto o enkishooroto Engai tiatua eng'adunoto oltung'ani obo-- Yesus Kristos-- natoponikiaki ilkumok."
Romans5:16 Nemetiu enkishooroto anaa idia kitarruoto nabo e lido oitarruoiye. Amu ore enkigwena naing'ua enkitarruoto nabo-- eaua enkiminata-- kake eitopok eng'adunoto too nkitarruot kumok o metabaiki esupato."
Romans5:17 Amu teni eitorishe enkea tʼolbae lʼenkitarruoto ele obo-- nepon naleng' neitorisho kulo loong'amu enkumoi eng'adunoto o enkishooroto naau esupato-- tiatua empuan tʼolbae le obo-- Yesus Kristos."
Romans5:18 Akae-- anaa peima enkea tʼolbae lʼenkitarruoto e obo atua iltung'anak pookin-- netum enkigwena nagol-- neijia-- tʼolbae lʼesupato e obo-- eima si esupato empuan atua iltung'anak pookin."
Romans5:19 Neijia anaa petaa tʼolbae lʼeanyata oltung'ani obo kumok laitarruok-- neijia epuo aaku tʼolbae lʼening'oto e obo ilkumok supati."
Romans5:20 Etijing'ua nkitanapat petum aatoponai nkitarruot. Kake anaa petoponaiye enkitarruoto-- netulusoiye apona eng'adunoto--"
Romans5:21 peiye-- neijia anaa peitorishe enkitarruoto tʼenkea-- neijia eitorisho si eng'adunoto metabaiki empuan nemeiting' tʼolbae le Yesus Kristos-- Olaitoriani lang'."
Romans6:1 Kijo aa yook? Kibik tiatua enkitarruoto-- pepona eng'adunoto?"
Romans6:2 Me neijia. Ore yook-- nikituatakitia enkitarruoto-- kaji kinko teni kintoki aaishiu tiatua ninye?"
Romans6:3 Miyololo ndai-- aajo eibatisaki yook pookin-- looibatisaki atua Kristos Yesus-- atua enkea enye?"
Romans6:4 Akae-- etunukaki yook te nebo o ninye tʼenkibatisa atua enkea-- peiye-- neijia anaa peitopiwuoki Kristos tiatua lootuata tʼenkitook e Menye-- neija kipuo aalimana si yook tiatua eng'ejukishu empuan."
Romans6:5 Amu teni enuki yook te nebo o ninye tʼenyanyukoroto enkea enye-- nikipuo aaku baiki lʼenyanyukoroto empiunoto enye."
Romans6:6 Kiyolo ena-- aajo etooshokoki oltung'ani lang' musana esalaba te nebo o ninye-- peiye eishunye osesen lʼenkitarruoto-- pemikintoki aaisyayaki yook enkitarruoto;"
Romans6:7 amu olotua-- eitaaki supat tʼenkitarruoto."
Romans6:8 Kake teni kituata te nebo o Kristos-- kiruk-- aajo kipuo aaishiu baiki te nebo o ninye--"
Romans6:9 nikiyolo-- aajo meitoki ae Kristos loitopiwuoki tiatua lootuata-- meitoki aitore enkea ninye."
Romans6:10 Amu enaidipa atua-- etuaka nkitarruot nabo kata; ore peishiu-- neishiuoki Engai."
Romans6:11 Neijia entejo si ndai-- aajo irara ndai lootuatakitia enkitarruoto-- ninjiuokiki Engai tiatua Kristos Yesus-- Olaitoriani lang'."
Romans6:12 Kake eminjo enkitarruoto meitoria atua osesen linyi otum enkea-- nining'ining'i ninye tiatua ilng'warraitin lenyena--"
Romans6:13 nimintarasakiki enkitarruoto rubat inyi anaa nareta entorroni-- kake entarasaki aten Engai anaa looishiu too lootuata-- o rubat inyi anaa nareta esupato."
Romans6:14 Amu melaitore enkitarruoto ndai-- amu mitiiti abori oo nkitanapat-- kake abori eng'adunoto."
Romans6:15 Ainyo naa? Kintarruo-- tiaraki nimikitii abori oo nkitanapat-- kake abori eng'adunoto? Me neijia."
Romans6:16 Miyololo-- aajo ore ilo-- lintarasakiki ndai aten singan nirukuruku-- nirara singan lenyena-- metaa irara lʼenkitarruoto aabaiki enkea-- arashu lʼening'oto aabaiki esupato?"
Romans6:17 Ashe-- Engai-- tiaraki nirara opa singan lʼenkitarruoto-- kake indipa aairuko taata too ltauja ilo aiturukoni lʼenkiteng'enare lining'ining'i ndai."
Romans6:18 Amu ore pitalakunote too nkitarruot-- niakuku singan lʼesupato."
Romans6:19 Airo tʼorregie lʼentung'anishu tʼolbae lʼemenatishu enkiring'o inyi. Amu anaa pinjoo rubat inyi eisyayaki olduruki o empaashata oo nkitanapat-- neijia enjoo taata rubat inyi-- peisyayaki esupato tiatua esinyaroto."
Romans6:20 Amu te ina kata nirara ndai singan loo nkitarruot-- nirara loolakuno tʼesupato."
Romans6:21 Akae-- kakua momo inoto te ina kata? Ore taata iatata sura tʼolbae loo nona; amu era enkiting'oto enye enkea."
Romans6:22 Kake itaa taata loolakuno too nkitarruot-- nisyayakiki Engai-- niatata ilmomo linyi-- piakuku sinyat-- niatata enkiting'oto nara empuan nemeiting'."
Romans6:23 Amu era enkea olkwaje lʼenkitarruoto-- kake era enkishooroto Engai empuan nemeiting' tiatua Kristos Yesus-- Olaitoriani lang'."
Romans7:1 Miyololo ndai-- lalashera-- (amu airorie kulo looyolo nkitanapat)-- aajo eitore nkitanapat oltung'ani enkata naishiuye?"
Romans7:2 Amu ore eng'oroyoni nayama olmoruo-- eteenikino o ninye too nkitanapat-- eton eishiu olmoruo lenye. Ore pee olmoruo-- netalakuaki tʼenkitanapata olmoruo."
Romans7:3 Kake eji engaarani enkidikidikoto enkiama-- teni eam olekai moruo ninye eton eishiu olmoruo. Ore pee olmoruo-- netalakuaki tʼenkitanapata-- nemeji engaarani enkidikidikoto enkiama-- teni ea olekai moruo ninye."
Romans7:4 Naa neijia itiuu si ndai-- lalashera lainei-- ituatakitia nkitanapat tiatua osesen le Kristos-- piakuku lʼolekai lora ilo oitopiwuoki too lootuata-- pekiiki Engai ilmomo."
Romans7:5 Amu te ina kata nikitii atua enkiring'o-- tʼolbae loo nkitanapat neasisho ilng'warraitin loo nkitarruot tiatua rubat ang' aaiki enkea ilmomo."
Romans7:6 Kake ore taata-- kitaa loolakuno too nkitanapat-- nikituatakitia ninje naateena yook-- pekisyaisho tʼeng'ejukishu Olmumua-- me tʼentiinoto musana esirata."
Romans7:7 Akae-- kijo aa? Kera nkitanapat enkitarruoto? Mera tukul. Kake eitu ayolou enkitarruoto neme too nkitanapat; amu anaata eitu ayolo olng'warra-- ten emutu eitu ejo nkitanapat: Ming'war!"
Romans7:8 Kake einoto enkitarruoto eretokinoto enkitanapata-- peinyeye tiatua nanu olng'warra pookin; amu teni metii nkitanapat-- netua enkitarruoto."
Romans7:9 Aishiuwo nanu enkata naje-- metii nkitanapat. Ore pelotu enkitanapata-- neishiu enkitarruoto--"
Romans7:10 kake atua nanu-- netumi-- ajo etaa enkitanapata nara nʼempuan-- te nanu nʼenkea."
Romans7:11 Amu einoto enkitarruoto eretokinoto enkitanapata naalej nanu naari matua te ninye.
Romans7:12 Nera nkitanapat sinyat-- nera si enkitanapata sinyati o supat o sidai."
Romans7:13 Akae-- ketaa enara sidai enkea te nanu? Me tukul. Kake etaa enkitarruoto-- pelioi anaa enkitarruoto-- tʼesidai enkea te nanu-- pepon aaku enkitarruoto torrono naleng' tʼenkitanapata."
Romans7:14 Amu kiyolo-- aajo era nkitanapat nʼe-mumuaishu-- nara ake nanu lʼenkiring'o-- laatimirakaki abori enkitarruoto."
Romans7:15 Amu mayolo enaitobir; amu maitobir enayeu-- kake enaiba-- ninye aitobir."
Romans7:16 Teni aitobir enamayeu-- nairuk nkitanapat-- ajo era sidan."
Romans7:17 Ore taata-- me nanu oitobir nona-- kake enkitarruoto natii atua nanu."
Romans7:18 Amu ayolo-- ajo memanya entoki sidai atua nanu-- eji tiatua enkiring'o ai. Aata eyeunoto-- kake matum aitobira sidan."
Romans7:19 Amu maitobir ena sidai nayeu-- kake enda torroni nemayeu-- aitobir."
Romans7:20 Ore paitobir enamayeu-- mekure aas nanu-- kake enkitarruoto natii atua nanu."
Romans7:21 Akae-- anyorriki-- ajo atii nanu oyeu neas enara sidai-- abori enkitanapata-- paitobir entorroni."
Romans7:22 Amu ashipakino nkitanapat Engai tiatua oltau lai.
Romans7:23 Kake adol nkulie kitanapat tiatua rubat ainei-- naarare nkitanapat eng'eno ai-- naaeniki-- paisyayaki nkitanapat enkitarruoto naatii atua rubat ainei."
Romans7:24 Oi-- ara nanu oltung'ani aisinani. Kang'ai laaitopok tʼosesen tʼena kea?"
Romans7:25 Kake ashe-- Engai-- tiatua Yesus Kristos-- Olaitoriani lang'. Onaa-- aisyayaki nanu openy tʼeng'eno ai nkitanapat Engai-- kake tʼenkiring'o nkitanapat enkitarruoto."
Romans8:1 Akae-- metii taata endiata o nabo atua kulo lootii atua Kristos Yesus-- lemelimana anaa peyeu enkiring'o-- kake anaa peyeu Olmumua."
Romans8:2 Amu aatalakutua nkitanapat Olmumua lʼempuan tiatua Kristos Yesus aitung'ua nkitanapat enkitarruoto o enkea.
Romans8:3 Amu enameidim nkitanapat-- tiaraki naa menat tʼolbae lʼenkiring'o-- neirriu Engai Oinoti lenye openy tiatua emua enkiring'o enkitarruoto o tʼolbae lʼenkitarruoto-- nedek enkitarruoto tiatua enkiring'o--"
Romans8:4 peitabaiari esupato oo nkitanapat tiatua yook lemikilimana anaa peyeu enkiring'o-- kake anaa peyeu Olmumua."
Romans8:5 Amu loora loo nkiri-- neibirribir noo nkiri-- kake loora lʼolmumua-- neibirribir nʼolmumua."
Romans8:6 Nera nkibirribirrat enkiring'o enkea-- kake era nkibirribirrat Olmumua empuan o eseriani."
Romans8:7 Amu era nkibirribirrat enkiring'o emang'atishu e atua Engai-- amu mening' ninye nkitanapat Engai-- nemeidim baiki."
Romans8:8 Meidim kulo lootii atua enkiring'o aaiting'ida Engai.
Romans8:9 Mitiiti ake ndai atua enkiring'o-- kake atua Olmumua-- ten ake emanya Olmuma lʼEngai atua ndai. Olemeata Olmumua le Kristos-- nemera olenye."
Romans8:10 Teni etii Kristos atua ndai-- netua osesen tʼolbae lʼenkitarruoto-- kake eishiu Olmumua tʼolbae lʼesupato."
Romans8:11 Teni emanya Olmumua le ilo-- oitopiwuo Yesus too lootuata-- atua ndai-- neitopiu ilo oitopiwuo Yesus tiatua lootuata-- si seseni linyi ooe-- tʼolbae lʼolmumua lenye omanya atua ndai."
Romans8:12 Akae-- lalashera-- kira yook loo silen-- me lʼenkiring'o-- pikisyayaki enkiring'o."
Romans8:13 Amu teni injiuu anaa peyeu enkiring'o-- nipuopuo aae; kake teni iariara nkitobirat osesen tʼOlmumua metuata-- nipuopuo aaishiu."
Romans8:14 Amu pookin loorik Olmumua-- nera ninje nkera Engai."
Romans8:15 Amu eitu ing'amumu Olmumua lʼesingaishu-- pintokiki aaureisho-- kake itang'amutua Olmumua lʼenkeraishu-- nikidarie ninye: Aba-- Papa!"
Romans8:16 Eijakenishe ele mumua te nebo o Olmumua lang'-- ajo kira nkera Engai."
Romans8:17 Teni kira nkera-- nikira lajung'ok-- lajung'ok lʼEngai-- loojung'isho te nebo o Kristos; teni eisili yook te nebo o ninye-- neitaai yook baiki kituak te nebo o ninye."
Romans8:18 Amu ajo nanu-- ajo menyanyuk nkisilot ena kata e taata o enkitook nalalioi too yook."
Romans8:19 Amu eanyu naleng' enkitobirata elioroto oo nkera Engai.
Romans8:20 Amu etii enkitobirata abori emutata-- me tʼeyeunoto enye-- kake tʼolbae lʼele-- lotipika ninye abori-- tʼeanyunoto."
Romans8:21 Amu epuoi aalaku baiki enkitobirata-- peing'ua enkisyayare erruoroto-- petum elakunoto enkitook oo nkera Engai."
Romans8:22 Amu kiyolo yook-- aajo eang' neata emion enkitobirata pookin te nebo o yook metabaiki taata."
Romans8:23 Me ninye ake-- kake baiki yook likiata enkishooroto elukunya Olmumua-- nikiang' tiatua aten nikianyu-- peitaai yook nkera nikitum elakunoto oo seseni lang'."
Romans8:24 Amu kitopua tʼeanyunoto. Ore eanyunoto nikidol-- mera ninye eanyunoto; amu olodol toki — kainyo peanyu?"
Romans8:25 Teni kianyu nimikidolita-- nikianyu tʼolng'iria."
Romans8:26 Nji eretoki baiki Olmumua emenatishu ang'; amu mikiyolo aatoomonu toki neijia anaa peitoriori-- amu etii Olmumua openy ewueji ang' too ang'an nemeiroroi."
Romans8:27 Kake eyolo ololeen iltauja ndamunot Olmumua-- amu eomonoki sinyat-- anaa penyor Engai."
Romans8:28 Kake kiyolo-- aajo eaku sidan ntokitin pookin too kulo loonyor Engai-- too kulo looipotoki tʼentootiki."
Romans8:29 Amu looiturukie ayolou-- etipika ninje-- perisyorei emua Oinoti lenye-- peaku ninye olkikau tiatua lalashera kumok."
Romans8:30 Ore lootipika ninye-- lelo eipoto; ore looipoto ninye-- lelo eitaa supati; ore looitaa supati-- lelo eitaa kituak."
Romans8:31 Akae-- ainyo kintoki aajo too kuna? Teni etii Engai ematua ang' — kang'ai loiteu atigilunore yook?"
Romans8:32 Neitu eshilu ninye baiki Oinoti lenye openy-- kake eitarasua ninye tʼolbae lang' pookin; meitoki aisho ninye yook te ninye ntokitin pookin?"
Romans8:33 Ang'ai oidim aitang'oro lootegeluaki lʼEngai? Etii Engai ene naitaa supat.
Romans8:34 Ang'ai oidim atedia? Etii Kristos Yesus ene lotua-- ore naleng' eitopiwuoki-- lotii engaina e tatene Engai-- nera baiki olosayaki yook."
Romans8:35 Ang'ai oidim atorishie yook enyorrata Engai? Enkilishoto arashu osina arashu emirare arashu olamei arashu engokishu arashu enkikirikirata arashu olalem?
Romans8:36 Anaa petisiraki: Eari yook dama pookin tʼolbae lino-- eikenari yook anaa nkerra naayeng'i."
Romans8:37 Kake kigilu nona pookin tʼele lotonyorra yook.
Romans8:38 Amu atayolo osupatei-- ajo meidim enkea arashu empuan arashu ilmalaikan arashu nkitoriaitin arashu naatii arashu naapuo aaku arashu ngoloni"
Romans8:39 arashu naatii shumata arashu engasuri arashu engai kitobirata pookin aatorishie yook enyorrata Engai natii atua Kristos Yesus-- Olaitoriani lang'."
Romans9:1 Airo esipata tiatua Kristos-- malejisho-- anaa paaijakenoki oltoilo lʼoltau lai tʼOlmumua Sinyati--"
Romans9:2 ajo aata osina kitok o emion nemeish tʼoltau lai.
Romans9:3 Amu anaata ak ayeu-- paadeki nanu openy aing'ua Kristos tʼolbae loo lalashera lainei laanyikita tʼempukunoto osesen;"
Romans9:4 loora loo Israel-- looinoto enkeraishu o enkitook o nkitanapat o enkisyayare Engai o nkisiligat--"
Romans9:5 neata si loopapa-- nepukunye Kristos ninje tʼemua enkiring'o-- nera ninye Engai too pookin-- neitadarari nkatan pookin."
Romans9:6 Majo nona-- tiaraki natabatate ororei lʼEngai. Amu mera pookin Israeli loora le Israel."
Romans9:7 Nemera pookin nkera e Abraham-- tiaraki nara eishoi enye-- kake: te Isaak kimpotieki eishoi ino."
Romans9:8 Eji mera nkera Engai nona naara nʼosesen-- kake nkera enkisiligata eikeni aaku eishoi."
Romans9:9 Amu ele ororei lʼenkisiligata teni ejo: Aitoki alotu tʼena kata-- netum Sara engaiyoni."
Romans9:10 Me ina ake-- kake ore pemenai Rebeka te ilo obo-- lora Isaak-- Papa lang'--"
Romans9:11 eton eitu eini nkera neitu eas entoki sidai arashu torrono — petum eotikinoto Engai aitasho tʼerisioroto engelunoto--"
Romans9:12 neme tʼerisioroto oo nkitobirat-- kake tʼolbae le ilo oipoto-- — netiakaki ninye (Rebeka): Eisyayaki olbotor oloti."
Romans9:13 Anaa petisiraki: Atonyorra Yakoob-- kake aibaiye Esau."
Romans9:14 Kijo aa yook? Ke me supat Engai? Me neijia.
Romans9:15 Amu etiaka Mose: Ang'adu ele lang'adu-- naing'urrie ele laing'urrie."
Romans9:16 Idol ta: me entoki e ilo oyeu anai okwet-- kake nʼEngai nang'adu oloyeu."
Romans9:17 Amu ejoki esirata Farao: Te ina aainyeye iye-- paitaduaya engolon ai te iye neitayolori engarna ai tiatua loshon pookin."
Romans9:18 Akae-- eng'adu ninye oloyeu-- neitagol oloyeu."
Romans9:19 Nikijoki iye nanu: Ainyo peitang'or ninye yook? Amu ang'ai oibelekeny eyeunoto enye?
Romans9:20 Iye-- letung'ani-- ira iye ng'ai-- pingwenare Engai? Amaa-- keikilikwan olokidong'oi oloitobir motiok: Ainyo pekintobira nji?"
Romans9:21 Meata oloitobir motiok engolon-- peitobir tʼolokidong'oi obo emoti nabo naata enkitook-- o engai naata enkurruna?"
Romans9:22 Akae-- ore peyeu Engai neitaduaya engoro enye neitayolou engolon enye-- nenap ninye tʼolng'iria kitok-- nkitobirat engoro enye naaitobiraka enkiminata--"
Romans9:23 peiye eitayolou enkumoi enkitook enye too nkitobirat eng'adunoto enye-- naatang'asa aitobir pebaiki enkitook--"
Romans9:24 naa yook-- ooipotuo ninye-- me ake too Yudayoi-- kake baiki too loreren lemeyolo Engai."
Romans9:25 Anaa peitoki ajo te Hosea: Aipot aitaa olorere lai lemera olorere lai-- ore eneitu anyor nanu-- naipot: enanyor ai."
Romans9:26 Neaku-- ore ine wueji netiakinyeki ninje: mirara olorere lai-- neipoti: nkera Engai naishiu."
Romans9:27 Neishiraki si Yesaya Israel-- ajo teni eaku eba nkera Israel anaa osunyai lʼolbalbal-- anaata epok ake olpisiai."
Romans9:28 Amu eaku ororei lʼenkitabaiaroto o endung'ore-- naa Olaitoriani oiko nji tʼenkop."
Romans9:29 Anaa petang'asa Yesaya ajo: Ten emut eitu eing'uaiki yook Olaitoriani loo ltimito eishoi-- anaata kitaa yook anaa Sodom neitanyanyukieki yook Gomora."
Romans9:30 Amaa-- kijo aa yook? Amu einoto loreren lemeyolo Engai esupato leitu eing'oru-- kake esupato naing'ua enkirukoto."
Romans9:31 Ore Israel otusuja nena kitanapat esupato-- neitu ebaiki ninje."
Romans9:32 Kainyo peitu ebaiki? Tiaraki neitu eing'oru tʼenkirukoto-- kake eing'orutua too nkitobirat oo nkitanapat. Eikobo aten tʼosoit lʼenkikoboto."
Romans9:33 Anaa petisiraki: Ng'orai-- apik te Sion osoit lʼenkikoboto o osoit lʼenkitirikata-- ore oloiruk ninye-- nemeitukurruni."
Romans10:1 Lalashera-- era eyeunoto oltau lai o esayata tʼEngai tʼolbae loo nkera Israel-- petum ninje enkitopuata."
Romans10:2 Amu aijakenoki ninje-- ajo eata enyuata tʼEngai-- kake me tʼeng'eno;"
Romans10:3 amu meyolou esupato Engai-- neing'oru naitasheye enenye oopeny-- neitu epik aten abori esupato Engai."
Romans10:4 Amu era Kristos embaiaroto oo nkitanapat-- petum oltung'ani pookin oiruk esupato."
Romans10:5 Amu esir Mose-- ajo elaishiu oltung'ani oitobir esupato naing'ua nkitanapat-- tiatua ninje;"
Romans10:6 kake eiro esupato naing'ua enkirukoto nji: Mijo tʼoltau lino: Kang'ai olailep shumata? neji ena-- perikuni Kristos enkop."
Romans10:7 Arashu: Kang'ai olodoiki atua engasuri? Neji ena-- ajo peilepunyeki Kristos tiatua lootuata."
Romans10:8 Kake kejo aa? Kitaaniki ororei tiatua enkutuk ino o tiatua oltau lino. Nera ele rorei lʼenkirukoto likinosu.
Romans10:9 Amu teni imbalu tʼenkutuk ino Olaitoriani Yesus niruk tiatua oltau lino-- ajo eitopiwuo Engai ninye too lootuata-- nilapok;"
Romans10:10 amu eiruki tʼoltau-- petumi esupato-- neibaluni tʼenkutuk-- petumi enkitopuata."
Romans10:11 Amu ejo esirata: Ore oltung'ani pookin oiruk ninye-- nemeitukurruni."
Romans10:12 Amu merisha ene Oyudayos o Olgriki; amu era ninye Olaitoriani loo pookin-- oladupani le atua pookin looipot ninye."
Romans10:13 Amu elapok oltung'ani pookin-- olaipot engarna Olaitoriani."
Romans10:14 Kake kaji eiko teni epuo aaipot oleitu eiruk? Naa kaji eiko teni epuo aairuk oleitu ening'? Na kaji eiko teni epuo aaning'-- meata olainosunoni?"
Romans10:15 Naa kaji eiko teni epuo aainosu-- teni eitu eirriwari ninje? Anaa petisiraki: Oi-- sidan nkejek oo looinosu eseriani o looinosu sidan."
Romans10:16 Kake me pookin ooiruk lomon lʼeng'ida. Amu ejo Yesaya: kang'ai oiruk enkinosunoto ang'?
Romans10:17 Onaa-- elotu enkirukoto tʼenkinosunoto-- nelotu enkinosunoto tʼororei lʼEngai."
Romans10:18 Kake aikilikwan: Eitu ening? Ee-- etoning'o. Amu etupukuo oltoilo lenye ajing'aa olmaa pookin-- nejing'aa rorei lenyena matuan pookin enkop."
Romans10:19 Kake aikilikwan: Eitu eyolou Israel? Tʼenkiterata ejo Mose: Aisho nanu ndai piataiyeye olom ilo orere lemera-- naitagoroki ndai olorere lemeata eng'eno."
Romans10:20 Neiteu Yesaya atejo: Aainotoki too lelo leitu aaing'oru-- natalioko lelo leitu aaikilikwanu nanu."
Romans10:21 Kake ejoki Israel: Aitorioko ngaik ainei engolong' pookin olorere lemening'isho neata engogong'i.
Romans11:1 Akae-- aikilikwan: Keiturraiye Engai olorere lenye? Me neijia. Amu ara si nanu ole Israel-- lʼeishoi e Abraham-- lʼenkishomi e Benyamin."
Romans11:2 Eitu eiturraa Engai olorere lenye otang'asa ninye ayolou. Arashu miyololo ndai enajo esirata te Eliya-- anaa pelotu enetii Engai tʼolbae le Israel ajo:"
Romans11:3 Olaitoriani-- etaara metuata layolounok linono netigilutua ilpereren lʼenkidasare linono; nanu ake otelekua-- naaing'oru Olmumua lai."
Romans11:4 Kake kainyo etaalikia Engai ninye? Aaiteliaka kion iltung'anak elfun naapishana leitu egilaki nkung' Baal.
Romans11:5 Neijia etiu si taata tʼena kata; etii lootelekutua tʼengelunoto eng'adunoto.
Romans11:6 Teni eaku tʼolbae lʼeng'adunoto-- nemekure tʼolbae loo nkitobirat-- amu anaata mekure aa eng'adunoto eng'adunoto. Kake teni eaku too nkitobirat-- nemekure etiu eng'adunoto toki-- amu anaata mekure aa enkitobirata enkitobirata."
Romans11:7 Ainyo naa? Ina naing'orua Israel eitu etum-- kake lʼengelunoto einoto; eitagoloki ilkulekai iltauja--"
Romans11:8 anaa petisiraki: Eishoo Engai ninje Olmumua loo njok naairoshi-- o ngonyek nemedolisho-- o nkiyaa nemening'isho metabaiki ena olong'."
Romans11:9 Nejo David: Njeaku endaaret enye erreshet o eloket o enkitapong'oroto o elaakinoto too ninje.
Romans11:10 Iopoki ngonyek enye enaimin-- pemedolisho-- nirrugie ngoriong'i enye oshi ake."
Romans11:11 Amaa-- keikobo ninje-- pebatata? Me neijia. Kake tʼembatatata enye etabaikia enkitopuata lemeata Engai-- penyok aasuj ninje."
Romans11:12 Amu teni era embatatata enye endupoto olmaa o enkitong'oroto enye endupoto oo lemeata Engai-- melusoo naleng'-- teni eitabaiari esiana enye?"
Romans11:13 Kake airorie ndai-- lemeata Engai-- tiaraki nara nanu olairriwani loo lemeata Engai-- nayeu naitadaraa enkisyayare ai--"
Romans11:14 anake atum aitonyua lʼenkiring'o ai-- pepok looje."
Romans11:15 Amu teni eaku enkiturraroto enye enkitobirakinoto olmaa-- me naleng' neaku eng'amunoto enye empiunoto too lootuata?"
Romans11:16 Ten aa sinyat ilmomo lʼenkiterunoto-- neijia si etiu empurpurjata nalulung'a; naa ten aa sinyati entonata-- neaku sinyat baiki ilng'osil."
Romans11:17 Kake teni etigilaki kulekai ng'osil aaitainye-- ore iye lora opa oloirien lʼentim nintijing'akinyeki tʼempolos ning'ar entonata o engare oloirien —"
Romans11:18 mintadaraa kion aibai ilng'osil. Ore teni intadaraa kion aibai ninje-- meata kata nimiyolo-- ajo me iye onap entonata-- kake entonata nikinap iye."
Romans11:19 Nialu iye: etigilaki ilng'osil aaitainye-- paapiki nanu atua. Sidai!"
Romans11:20 Tiaraki neitu eiruk ninje-- netigilaki-- nintashe iye tʼolbae lʼenkirukoto. Miwuasa-- kake tureisho."
Romans11:21 Amu teni eitu eing'urrie Engai lelo ng'osil oora-- nimiking'urrie si iye."
Romans11:22 Ng'orai taa emborran o empijan Engai-- empijan too kulo-- lootabatatate-- kake emborran te iye-- teni ibik tiatua emborran: pemikidung'i si iye."
Romans11:23 Naa neijia etiu lekua-- teni mebik eany enkirukoto-- nepuoi aaitijing'aki. Eitoki aidim Engai aitijing'aki ninje."
Romans11:24 Amu teni kitudung'oki iye aitainye oloirien lʼentim nikintijing'akini atua oloirien sidai-- kake omoni te iye-- ke me naleng' eitokini aaitijing'aki kulo ng'osil oora-- ootudung'uoki opa-- atua oloirien lenye openy?"
Romans11:25 Mayeu-- lalashera lanyor-- nimiyololo ena kisudoroto-- (pemiwuasasa)-- ajo etamodono Israel tʼematua-- metabana nejing' enkumoi oo lemeata Engai"
Romans11:26 nepok neijia Israel olulung'a-- anaa petisiraki: Elotu Olaitopuani aing'ua Sion-- neshurtaa entorroni e Yakob--"
Romans11:27 naa ilo osotua lai laitaa o ninje-- teni alaitau nkitarruot enye."
Romans11:28 Ore too lomon lʼeng'ida-- nera ninje ilmang'ati tʼolbae linyi-- kake tʼengelunoto era ninje lootonyorraki tʼolbae loo loopapa."
Romans11:29 Amu meinyaaia Engai nkishoorot o enkipototo enye.
Romans11:30 Neija anaa ndai opa eitu irukuruku Engai-- kake ekorduni taata ndai-- tiaraki neitu eiruk ninje;"
Romans11:31 neija meiruk taata si lekua enkordunoto ninoto ndai-- peiye etum si ninje enkordunoto."
Romans11:32 Amu eigenoiye Engai pookin pemeata enkirukoto-- petum atokordu ninje pookin."
Romans11:33 Oi-- engasuri endupoto o eng'eno o eyolounoto Engai! Meyolounoi nkigwenaitin enyena nemetumoi ngoitoi enyena!"
Romans11:34 Amu kang'ai lotayolo enkibirribirrata Olaitoriani? Arashu kang'ai lotaa olautakinoni lenye?
Romans11:35 Arashu kang'ai loituruko aisho ninye-- peitoki aisho arrinyoki ninye?"
Romans11:36 Amu eing'ua ninye neaku te ninye nejing' atua ninye pookin. Njeata ninye enkitook metabaiki nkatan pookin. Amen.
Romans12:1 Akae-- asai ndai-- lalashera-- tʼeng'adunoto Engai-- pinjoioio seseni linyi-- peaku enkidasare naishiu-- sinyati-- naiting'id Engai-- nera enkisyayare Engai naitoriori."
Romans12:2 Eminyanyukiei ele maa-- kake entaalata tʼeng'ejukishu oo nkibirribirrat inyi-- pindimidimi aataleen enara eyeunoto Engai sidai-- naiting'idisho-- enabaia."
Romans12:3 Amu ajoki tʼeng'adunoto Engai-- naaishooki nanu-- oltung'ani pookin lotii atua ndai-- pemeitaa ninye kion kitok too ndamunot nelang' olora-- kake njedamu mbaak enyena anaa nkuti-- oltung'ani pookin anaa petetemaka Engai ninye entemet enkirukoto."
Romans12:4 Amu neija anaa pekiata tiatua osesen obo rubat kumok nemeata rubat pookin enkyas nabo--"
Romans12:5 neijia kira yook ilkumok osesen obo tiatua Kristos-- nera tiatua yook obo erubata olekai."
Romans12:6 Nikiata nkishoorot nemenyanyukoro tʼeng'adunoto naishooki yook.
Romans12:7 Teni eata oltung'ani eyolounoto e akenya-- njeata t'entemet enkirukoto; ten aa enkisyayare-- njeisyaisho; ten aa oloiteng'enisho-- njeiteng'enisho;"
Romans12:8 ten aa olodiding'isho-- njediding'isho; ten aa olaishooroni-- njeishooio tʼoltau sidai; ten aa olaitasheikinoni-- njeitasheiki tʼenyuata; ten aa olang'adunoni-- jeng'adu tʼeng'ida."
Romans12:9 Njoo meata enyorrata enkitusupatuo. Embai enara torrono nimbung'arere enara sidai.
Romans12:10 Njeaku enyorrata oo lalashera tiatua ndai nʼoltau. Njeituruk obo aitaa olekai kitok.
Romans12:11 Emishalu tʼenyuata. Enjoo iatata enkima tiatua iltauja. Esyayakiti Olaitoriani.
Romans12:12 Enting'idata tiatua eanyunoto-- enting'iria tiatua osina-- entobik tiatua esayata."
Romans12:13 Entang'ar elaunoto oo sinyat. Entoomonishoto tʼeng'ida.
Romans12:14 Entamayan looisil ndai; entamayan-- emidek."
Romans12:15 Enting'idata te nebo o loong'ida-- enjira te nebo o looishir."
Romans12:16 Njoo idamumu tʼempolos inyi nabo. Emimbirribir ntokitin kituak-- kake embung'are enkitadounoto. Emiaku looitadaraa aten tʼen'geno."
Romans12:17 Emilaaki oltung'ani entorroni tʼentorroni. Embirribirrutu sidan tʼengomom oo ltung'anak pookin.
Romans12:18 Teni eaku-- embung'akinore iltung'anak pookin eseriani anaa pindimidimi ndai."
Romans12:19 Emilaakino-- lanyor-- ntorrok-- kake ewuang'ie engoro Engai-- amu esira: Enai elaata oo ntorrok-- alalak nanu-- ejo Olaitoriani."
Romans12:20 Akae-- teni etum olmang'atinda lino olamei-- ntotio ninye; teni etum enkure-- ntooko ninye; amu teni inko nji-- ninturrurroki nkuk enkima shumata elukunya enye."
Romans12:21 Minjo kigilu entorroni-- kake tigilu iye entorroni too sidan."
Romans13:1 Njening oltung'ani pookin ilkituak t'engolon. Amu metii engolon neme enaing'ua Engai; ore looata engolon-- Engai natipika ninje."
Romans13:2 Ore ologogong' tʼoloata engolon-- negogong'oki orregie lʼEngai; ore loogogong'-- neaki aten enkigwena."
Romans13:3 Amu mera ilkituak laituriak loo nkyasin sidan-- kake loo nkyasin torrok. Teni miyeu niurei Oloata engolon-- ntobira sidan-- nilaata enkitadararoto te ninye."
Romans13:4 Amu era ninye olaisyayani lʼEngai-- pitum iye sidan; kake teni intobir ntorrok-- tureishoi-- amu menapita ninye olalem pesho; era ninye olaisyayani lʼEngai-- pelaaki near oloitobir ntorrok."
Romans13:5 Onaa-- meata kata nemening'i ninye-- me tʼolbae lʼearata ake-- kake baiki tʼolbae lʼoltoilo lʼoltau."
Romans13:6 Onaa-- entalak baiki kodi-- amu era ninje laisyayak lʼEngai loonyamal te ina."
Romans13:7 Enjoo oltung'ani pookin esupato enye: le kodi — kodi-- olasotoni — esotore-- oloitureisho — enkuretishu-- lʼenkitook — enkitook."
Romans13:8 Njoo miatata esile oltung'ani o obo-- neme ake entonyorrata-- amu olonyor olekai-- eitabaiye nkitanapat."
Romans13:9 Amu enatejoki: miar enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni-- miar metua-- mipurrisho-- midung' ilmarenge-- ming'war-- arashu teni etii engai kitanapata nalang'-- etuumaki tiatua ele rorei: Tonyorra oltung'ani lʼelatia ino anaa pinyor kion."
Romans13:10 Meitobiraki enyorrata olʼelatia ntorrok. Akae-- era enyorrata enkitabaiaroto oo nkitanapat."
Romans13:11 Ore piyololo ena-- eji enkata-- ajo etabaua enkata-- pinyotototo too njok; amu etataanua enkitopuata ang' taata nelang' enikirukie--"
Romans13:12 etaa nalusoo enkiarie nenyiku endama; onaa maitau nkitobirat enaimin-- maishopo nareta enkilang'et."
Romans13:13 Matilimanata tʼorregie sidai anaa dama-- me tʼenkinosata o tʼemerai-- me tʼentalare o tʼenkimalimal-- me tʼenkitarrikino o tʼengilata e tau;"
Romans13:14 kake enjopo Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos-- ore enkishilaroto osesen eminko aainokie olng'warra."
Romans14:1 Entang'amutu olmenati lʼenkirukoto-- emingwenaki nkibirribirrat enyena."
Romans14:2 Eiruk obo-- ajo eidim ainosa pookin; olora menati-- nenya mbenek."
Romans14:3 Olonya-- minjo emen olemenya; minjo eigwenaki baiki olemenya olonya-- amu etang'amua Engai ninye."
Romans14:4 Ira iye ng'ai oloigwenaki olaisyayani omoni? Eitashe arashu ebatata ninye tʼOlaitoriani lenye openy; kake epuoi aaitasheye-- amu eidim aitasheye Engai ninye."
Romans14:5 Erishu obo engolong' tʼengai olong'-- neitoris olekai ngolong'i pookin; njegolu oltung'ani pookin too ndamunot enyena."
Romans14:6 Oloibung' ngolong'i-- neibung'aki Olaitoriani; olemeibung' ngolong'i-- nemeibung'aki Olaitoriani; olonya-- nenya tʼOlaitoriani-- amu eliki ninye Engai ashe; olemenya-- nemenya tʼOlaitoriani-- neliki Engai ashe."
Romans14:7 Amu meishiuoki o obo too yook kion-- nemeeki o obo kion;"
Romans14:8 amu teni kinjiu-- kinjiuoki Olaitoriani; teni kiee-- nikieeki Olaitoriani. Akae-- teni kinjiu-- teni kiee-- nikira lʼOlaitoriani."
Romans14:9 Amu etua Kristos te ina neishiu-- peiye eitore lootuata o looishiu."
Romans14:10 Kake iye-- ainyo pingwenaki olalashe lino? Ore iye olekai-- ainyo pimen iye olalashe lino? Amu epuoi aaitasheye yook pookin tʼengomom olorika lʼenkigwena le Kristos;"
Romans14:11 amu etisiraki: Aishiu-- ejo Olaitoriani-- meata kata nemaagilakini enkung'u pookin tʼengomom ai-- neibalu olng'ejep pookin Engai."
Romans14:12 Neijia elaisho pookin obo too ndai Engai ealet.
Romans14:13 Akae-- njoo mikintoki yook aaigwenaki obo olekai-- kake eikash-- teni ingwenarere-- pemeikob o obo olalashe lenye nemeitapong'oo ninye."
Romans14:14 Ayolo naitisipu-- ajo metii entoki nara torrono kion tiatua Olaitoriani; neaku ake torrono te ilo loikenaki ajo torrono."
Romans14:15 Kake teni eisinanu olalashe lino tʼolbae lʼendaa ino-- mekure ilimana iye tʼenyorrata. Miminye tʼendaa ino ilo otuaka Kristos ninye."
Romans14:16 Eminjo emori sidan inyi.
Romans14:17 Amu mera enkarsishu Engai endaa o eokoto-- kake esupato o eseriani o eng'ida tiatua Olmumua Sinyati;"
Romans14:18 amu oloisyayaki te ina Kristos-- neiting'id Engai nera kitok too ltung'anak."
Romans14:19 Akae-- matusuj mbaak eseriani neretokino obo olekai."
Romans14:20 Mintarruo tʼolbae lʼendaa enkyas Engai. Amu esmya entoki pookin-- kake eaku torrono te ilo onya tʼenkikoboto oltau lenye."
Romans14:21 Sidai-- teni minya nkiri-- nimiok olmarua-- nimintobir toki-- teni eikob arashu epong'ori arashu eshalu olalashe lino too ninje."
Romans14:22 Teni iata iye enkirukoto-- njoo iata kion t'engomom Engai. Tesh olemeata enkikoboto oltau tʼolbae lʼendaa nanya."
Romans14:23 Kake oloing'arrirro teni enya-- neigwenakini-- amu mepukunye enkirukoto. Kake enamepukunye enkirukoto-- naa enkitarruoto."
Romans15:1 Akae-- nenare taa too yook likira oogol-- pekinap enjalan oo looshal-- nimikintiship aten."
Romans15:2 Njeitiship oltung'ani pookin too yook ol elatia-- peaku sidai netum enkitagolioroto."
Romans15:3 Amu ore si Kristos eitu eitiship kion-- kake anaa petisiraki; Aatusulakinote nanu morot oo kulo likimor."
Romans15:4 Enatisiraki opa etisiraki-- peaku enkiteng'enare ang'-- pikitum eanyunoto tʼolng'iria o tʼenkilejilejata esirata."
Romans15:5 Njeisho ndai Engai olng'iria o enkilejilejata-- pidamumu tiatua ndai nabo anaa peyeu Kristos Yesus--"
Romans15:6 pitumutumu aaitadarai Engai o Menye lʼOlaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos-- tʼoltau obo o tʼenkutuk nabo."
Romans15:7 Onaa-- entang'amaroto anaa petang'amua yook Kristos-- peitaai Engai kitok."
Romans15:8 Kake ajo nanu-- etaa Yesus Kristos olaisyayani lʼemurata tʼolbae lʼesipata Engai-- peitagol nkisiligat naaishooki loopapa;"
Romans15:9 peiye eitadaraa loreren Engai tʼenkordunoto enye-- anaa petisiraki: Onaa aalaibalu iye tiatua loreren-- naranyaki engarna ino."
Romans15:10 Neitoki si ajo: Enting'idata-- loreren-- te nebo o olorere lenye!"
Romans15:11 Neitoki: Loreren pookin-- entadarai Olaitoriani-- njeiting'id ninye iltung'anak pookin!"
Romans15:12 Neitoki ajo Yesaya: Elaaku entonata e Yese o oloitashe-- peitore loreren; epuo aanyu loreren ninye."
Romans15:13 Njeigany ake ndai Engai eanyunoto tʼeng'ida pookin o tʼeseriani enkirukoto-- peitunyoi eanyunoto inyi tʼengolon Olmumua Sinyati."
Romans15:14 Ayolo si nanu-- lalashera lainei-- ajo eiganyi ndai emborran niboreii eyolounoto pookin-- pindimidimi aatorojaroto ndai aten."
Romans15:15 Kake aitewuo atisiraki ndai nkuti-- lalashera-- anake aitadamu ndai-- tʼolbae lʼemunyani naaishoo nanu Engai--"
Romans15:16 patum ataa olaisyayani le Kristos Yesus nalo enetii loreren lemeata Engai-- paitobir enkyas oo lomon lʼeng'ida osupatei-- neaku loreren enkidasare nashipakino Engai-- naa sinyati tiatua Olmumua Sinyati."
Romans15:17 Onaa aidim aitadarai kion tiatua Kristos Yesus-- ajo aisyayaki Engai."
Romans15:18 Anaata maiteu ainosu ororei-- ten emutu meitobir Kristos tiatua nanu pening'isho loreren-- tʼororei o tʼenkyas--"
Romans15:19 tʼenkidimata oo nkitaduarot o noo lponot-- o tʼenkidimata Olmumua lʼEngai-- netaa aiganya pookin aing'ua Yerusalem o mbat naamanimanaa metabaiki Ilirikon-- too lomon lʼeng'ida le Kristos."
Romans15:20 Atonyua baiki-- painosu euangelion too wuejitin neton eitu eipoti engarna e Kristos-- pemashet tʼentonata omoni--"
Romans15:21 kake anaa petisiraki: Meata kata nemedol lelo leitu einosuni lomon lenyena-- neyolou lelo leitu ening'."
Romans15:22 Neijia taa etiu-- paaiboiyoki aigil kumok alotu enitiiti ndai."
Romans15:23 Tiaraki namaata taata erishata too kuna kwapi-- natayeuo oshi ake kulo arin kumok nalotu enitiiti ndai--"
Romans15:24 onaa ayeu nalotu enitiiti-- teni aim too ndai alo Spania. Amu ajo nanu-- alatumore ndai tʼolototo lai-- nikintarere ndai nanu ine-- kindipa aaiting'ida peno enkata natii e nebo o ndai."
Romans15:25 Kake taata ang'as alo Yerusalem-- paisyayaki lelo sinyat."
Romans15:26 Amu etonyorra iltung'anak le Makedonia o Akaya-- pesotu eng'ara naje aaretoki sinyat aisinak ootii Yerusalem."
Romans15:27 Kake etonyorra-- nera si loo silen enye. Amu teni etang'ara loreren lemeata Engai ntokitin emumuaishu enye-- neitoriori-- peretoki si lelo ninje too mbaak oo seseni."
Romans15:28 Teni aidipa aitabai ena bae naeaki ninje kulo momo petum-- naimaa ndai alo Spania."
Romans15:29 Nayolo-- ajo teni alotu enitiiti-- alotu tʼemborei emayani e Kristos."
Romans15:30 Adiding' ndai-- lalashera-- tʼOlaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos o tʼenyorrata Olmumua-- pekiretokiki aatigilunore nikisayakiki nanu tʼEngai--"
Romans15:31 paakorduni too lelo lemeiruk te Yerusalem-- neshipakino lelo sinyat enkisyayare ai naiko te Yerusalem--"
Romans15:32 patum aeu tʼeng'ida enitiiti ndai tʼeyeunoto Engai naeng'ieng'a te nebo o ndai.
Romans15:33 Ore Engai eseriani metobiko te nebo o ndai pookin. Amen.
Romans16:1 Aitanapaki ndai enganashe ang' Foibe-- naa ninye engaisyayani esirit natii Kenkerea--"
Romans16:2 ping'amumu ninye tʼOlaitoriani anaa peaku too sinyat-- ninjosho eretokinoto too ngolati pookin naairishakinore ninye ndai. Amu etaretoko ilkumok-- naataretoko baiki nanu."
Romans16:3 Eroroki Priskila o Akwila-- laretok lainei tiatua Kristos."
Romans16:4 Amu etipika tʼolbae lʼempuan ai emurt enye; me nanu ake oliki ninje ashe-- kake eiko nji si sirito pookin naatii tiatua loreren lemeata Engai."
Romans16:5 Eroroki si esirit natii tʼengaji enye. Eroroki Epainetos olanyor lai-- lora olkikau le Kristos te Asia."
Romans16:6 Eroroki Maria natanyamala naleng' tʼolbae linyi.
Romans16:7 Eroroki Andronikos o Yunias lʼenkishomi ang' looteenaki te nebo o nanu-- neyolouni anaa lairriwak loora-- naaiturukie nanu aairuk Kristos."
Romans16:8 Eroroki Ampliatos olanyor lai tʼOlaitoriani.
Romans16:9 Eroroki Urbanos-- olaretoni lang' o Stakis-- olanyor lai."
Romans16:10 Eroroki Apeles-- otonyorraiyoki te Kristos."
Romans16:11 Eroroki Herodion lang'. Eroroki lelo loora lʼengang' e Narkisos tʼOlaitoriani.
Romans16:12 Eroroki Trifeena o Trifosa-- naatanyamala tʼOlaitoriani. Eroroki Perse enanyor-- natanyamala naleng' tʼOlaitoriani."
Romans16:13 Eroroki Rufus-- olotegeluaki tʼOlaitoriani-- o ng'otonye naa yeiyo ai."
Romans16:14 Eroroki Asinkritos o Flegon o Hermas o Patrobas o lalashera ootii e nebo o ninje.
Romans16:15 Eroroki Filologus o Yulia-- Nereus o enganashe enye-- o Olimpas o sinyat pookin te nebo o ninye."
Romans16:16 Erorokinoto ndai aten tʼeng'ututata sinyati. Eiroroki ndai sirito le Kristos.
Romans16:17 Kake adiding' ndai-- lalashera-- ping'oraara lelo ooau rishat o nkitapong'orot nemeishiaakino ina kiteng'enare ninteng'enuote ndai-- nipaasharere aaing'ua ninje."
Romans16:18 Amu meisyayaki looba nji-- Olaitoriani-- kake engoshoke enye-- nelej si iltauja loo lemera torrok too rorei lenye oobor naa sidan."
Romans16:19 Amu eibale enkirukoto inyi too ltung'anak pookin. Onaa-- ashipakino ndai-- nayeu niakuku ng'eni tiatua mbaak supati-- kake turua tiatua mbaak torrok."
Romans16:20 Ore Engai eseriani-- metororuaki satan abori oo nkejek inyi asioki. Njebik eng'adunoto Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos te nebo o ndai."
Romans16:21 Eiroroki ndai Timoteos-- olaretoni lai-- o Lukios o Yason o Sosipater lʼenkishomi ang'."
Romans16:22 Airoroki ndai-- nanu Tertius-- otisira ena palai-- tʼOlaitoriani."
Romans16:23 Eiroroki ndai Gayos-- olaaitoomono nanu o esirit nalulung'a. Eiroroki ndai Erastos-- olopeny masaa engang'-- o Kwartos-- olalashe."
Romans16:24 Njebik eng'adunoto Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos te nebo o ndai.
Romans16:25 Ore Engai-- naidim aitagolo ndai tʼerisioroto oo lomon lʼeng'ida lainei o nkinosunot e Yesus Kristos-- naaibalu emikio naisudoiyoki neba tʼenkiterunoto olmaa--"
Romans16:26 kake etaboluoki neitayolouni taata tiatua sirat oo layolounok-- tʼenkitanapata Engai oo nkatan pookin-- peuni ening'oto enkirukoto tiatua loreren pookin:"
Romans16:27 Njeata Engai nara openy ake ng'en-- enkitook nkatan pookin metabaiki nkatan pookin. Amen."
1Corinthians1:1 Paulos oipotoki-- peaku olairriwani le Yesus Kristos tʼeyeunoto Engai-- o Sostenes-- olalashe lang':"
1Corinthians1:2 en esirit Engai natii Korintos ena palai-- noo lelo ootisinyaiyoki tiatua Yesus Kristos-- isinyat ooipotoki-- te nebo o pookin ooipot engarna Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos-- too wuejitin enye o nkunang' pookin."
1Corinthians1:3 Njeboitare ndai eng'adunoto o eseriani naing'ua Engai Papa lang' o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos.
1Corinthians1:4 Aliki Engai ashe oshi tʼolbae lʼeng'adunoto Engai naishooki ndai tiatua Kristos Yesus--"
1Corinthians1:5 tiaraki nitudupore ndai ntokitin pookin tiatua ninye-- enkiteng'enare pookin o eyolounoto pookin--"
1Corinthians1:6 neijia anaa petagolo enjakenishu e Kristos tiatua ndai--"
1Corinthians1:7 neijia eitu ing'oruru tʼenkishooroto o nabo nianyunyu embolunoto Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos
1Corinthians1:8 oloitagol baiki ndai metabaiki enkiting'oto-- perneitang'ori ndai tʼengolong' Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos."
1Corinthians1:9 Supat Engai naipotokinyeki ndai atua enkidikidikoto Oinoti lenye Yesus Kristos-- Olaitoriani lang'."
1Corinthians1:10 Adiding' ndai-- lalashera-- tʼolbae lʼengarna Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos-- piroro pookin entoki nabo-- nimiatata orot tiatua ndai-- kake embung'aroto tʼoltau obo o tʼendamunoto nabo."
1Corinthians1:11 Amu aatolikitio mbaak inyi-- lalashera lainei-- lekua lʼengaji e Kloe-- aajo etii enjangar atua ndai."
1Corinthians1:12 Ajo nanu ele rorei-- njere ejo pookin too ndai: Ara nanu ole Paulos-- nara nanu ole Apolos-- nara nanu ole Kefas-- nara nanu ole Kristos."
1Corinthians1:13 Amaa-- ketoore Kristos? Ketooshokoki Paulos esalaba tʼolbae linyi? Arashu keibatisaki ndai lʼengarna e Paulos?"
1Corinthians1:14 Aliki Engai ashe-- amu eitu aibatis oltung'ani obo too ndai neme Krispos o Gayos."
1Corinthians1:15 Nemetii oltung'ani o obo oidim atejo eibatisaki lʼengarna ai.
1Corinthians1:16 Kake aibatisa si lʼengaji e Stefanos. Teni me lelo-- madamu ajo aibatisa kulekai."
1Corinthians1:17 Amu eitu aainiwaa Kristos-- paibatis-- kake painosu lomon lʼeng'ida-- neme too rorei ng'eni-- pemeiturrari esalaba e Kristos."
1Corinthians1:18 Amu ore ororei lʼesalaba-- nera emodaishu too lelo ooimin-- kake ore too yook ooitopuaki-- naa engolon Engai."
1Corinthians1:19 Amu etisiraki: Aiminye eng'eno oo lang'eni-- naiturraa eng'eno oo looyolo."
1Corinthians1:20 Kodee olng'en? Kodee olayoloni loo sirat? Kodee lang'eni lʼele maa? Keitu eitaa Engai eng'eno ele maa emodaishu?
1Corinthians1:21 Amu tiaraki neitu eyolou olmaa tʼeng'eno enye Engai tiatua eng'eno enye-- etonyorrua Engai aitopua tʼenkinosunoto emodaishu kulo looiruk."
1Corinthians1:22 Amu eing'oru Yudayoi ilponot-- neing'oru Ilgrikini eng'eno--"
1Corinthians1:23 kake kinosu yook Kristos otooshokoki esalaba-- nera too Yudayoi erikai o too loreren emodaishu--"
1Corinthians1:24 kake too kulo looipotoki-- too Yudayoi o too Lgrikini-- nera Kristos engolon Engai o eng'eno Engai."
1Corinthians1:25 Amu era emodaishu Engai ng'en nelang' iltung'anak-- neata emenatishu Engai engolon nelang' iltung'anak."
1Corinthians1:26 Amu eng'orai-- lalashera-- enkipototo inyi-- metii atua ndai kumok loora lang'eni nemetii kumok lʼengolon nemetii kumok looata enkitook;"
1Corinthians1:27 kake etegelua Engai naara moda olmaa-- peiye eitukurru lang'eni-- o naara menat olmaa etegelua Engai-- peiye eitukurru naara nʼengolon;"
1Corinthians1:28 etegelua Engai nemeata enkitook olmaa o natemenaki-- nemera toki-- peiye eiturraa nara toki-- peiye pemeitaa toki nara toki--"
1Corinthians1:29 pemeitadaraa kion enkiring'o pookin tʼengomom Engai.
1Corinthians1:30 Ing'uang'ua si ndai atua ninye tiatua Kristos Yesus-- lotaa too yook eng'eno naing'ua Engai-- esupato o esinyaroto o elakunoto--"
1Corinthians1:31 peiye anaa petisiraki; Oloitadaraa kion-- njeitadaraa kion tiatua Olaitoriani."
1Corinthians2:1 Ore si nanu-- lalashera-- eitu alotu enitiiti ndai tʼenkishaa ororei arashu eng'eno ainosaki ndai enjakenishu Engai."
1Corinthians2:2 Amu eitu aikenaki kion payolo toki too ndai neme Yesus Kristos otooshokoki esalaba.
1Corinthians2:3 Natii nanu atua ndai tʼenjalan o tʼenkuretishu o tʼenkikirikirata naleng'.
1Corinthians2:4 Ore ororei lai o enkinosunoto ai-- nemera ororei sidai lʼeng'eno oo ltung'anak-- kake ol enkitaduaroto Olmumua o tʼengolon--"
1Corinthians2:5 peiye eunokino enkirukoto inyi-- me tʼeng'eno oo ltung'anak-- kake tʼengolon Engai."
1Corinthians2:6 Kake kilimu eng'eno too lootabaitie-- me eng'eno ele maa-- neme en oo lkituak lʼele maa-- loopuo aamuta--"
1Corinthians2:7 kake kilimu eng'eno Engai tiatua emikio-- natushumaki-- natipika Engai tʼenkiturukoto e opa moitie-- peaku enkitook ang';"
1Corinthians2:8 neitu eyolou ninye o obo loo lkituak lʼele maa; amu ten emutu etayoloutuo-- anaata eitu eoshoki esalaba Olaitoriani lʼenkitook;"
1Corinthians2:9 kake anaa petisiraki: Neitu edol engong'u-- neitu ening' enkiyok-- neitu ejing' atua oltau lʼoltung'ani-- ninje eitobiraka Engai kulo loonyor ninye."
1Corinthians2:10 Kake etaboloko yook Engai ena tʼOlmumua lenye; amu eirengesu Olmumua mbaak pookin-- baiki ngasurin Engai."
1Corinthians2:11 Amu kang'ai too ltung'anak loyolo nʼoltung'ani neme Olmumua lʼoltung'ani otii atua ninye? Neijia meyolo o obo nʼEngai-- neme Olmumua lʼEngai."
1Corinthians2:12 Eitu king'amu yook Olmumua lʼele maa-- kake Olmumua oing'ua Engai-- pikitum aatayolou ng'adunot naaishoo yook Engai;"
1Corinthians2:13 nikilimu baiki ninje-- me too rorei looiteng'enu eng'eno oo ltung'anak-- kake looiteng'enu Olmumua-- nikingwenaki mbaak emumuaishu tʼemumuaishu."
1Corinthians2:14 Meyolo oltung'ani lʼenkop mbaak Olmumua lʼEngai-- amu era te ninye emodaishu-- nemeidim atayolou-- amu eigwenuni ninje tʼemumuaishu."
1Corinthians2:15 Kake eigwenu ol Olmumua mbaak pookin-- nemeigwenaki o obo ninye."
1Corinthians2:16 Amu kang'ai lotayolouo nkibirribiirat Olaitoriani? Kang'ai elaiteng'en ninye? Kake kiata yook nkibirribirrat e Kristos.
1Corinthians3:1 Neitu aidim nanu airorie ndai-- lalashera-- anaa lʼOlmumua-- kake itiuu anaa lʼenkiring'o-- anaa nkera kutiti tiatua Kristos."
1Corinthians3:2 Aitotio ndai too kule-- me tʼendaa nagol; amu eton eitu indimumu. Baiki taata eton mindimumu."
1Corinthians3:3 Amu eton irara lʼenkiring'o. Amu teni etii atua ndai olom o olarrabal o enjangar-- keton mirara lʼenkiring'o nipuoiyeye mbaak oo ltung'anak?"
1Corinthians3:4 Amu teni ejo obo: Ara ole Paulos-- nejo lekai: Ara nanu ole Apolos — mirara ndai loo ltung'anak?"
1Corinthians3:5 Kang'ai Apolos? naa kang'ai Paulos? Me laisyayak lootaretokitio ndai-- pitumutumu enkirukoto-- kake anaa peishoo Olaitoriani oltung'ani pookin."
1Corinthians3:6 Atuuno nanu-- neitook Apolos-- kake Engai naitubulua."
1Corinthians3:7 Akae-- ore oloun-- me toki-- neme oloitook-- kake Engai naitubulu."
1Corinthians3:8 Kake ore oloun o oloitook-- naa obo; kake etum pookin olkwaje lenye tʼerisioroto enkyas enye."
1Corinthians3:9 Amu kira yook laitobirak lʼenkyas te nebo o Engai-- nirara ndai enkuruma-- neitoki enjetata Engai."
1Corinthians3:10 Ore tʼeng'adunoto Engai naaishooki nanu-- anaa olashetani arriya atipika enkitamanyunoto-- neshet olekai tung'ani shumata. Njeing'oraa oltung'ani pookin-- eneiko teni eshetaki shumata e ina."
1Corinthians3:11 Amu meidim atipika o obo engai kitamanyunoto neme ena natipikaki-- nera Yesus Kristos."
1Corinthians3:12 Teni eshetaki oltung'ani shumata ena kitamanyunoto sahabu-- ngoshola-- soito lʼenkinyang'a nagol-- ilkeek-- olkujita-- ndung'ot olperesi--"
1Corinthians3:13 nelaibalai enkyas oltung'ani pookin; amu elaibalie engolong'-- amu eboluni tʼenkima-- nelaleen ena kima enkyas oltung'ani pookin eneikununo."
1Corinthians3:14 Teni ebik enkyas oltung'ani natesheta ninye-- nelatum olkwaje;"
1Corinthians3:15 teni eiku enkyas oltung'ani-- nelatum elaunoto-- elapok ake ninye openy-- kake anaa tʼenkima."
1Corinthians3:16 Miyololo ndai-- aajo irara engaji Engai-- nemanya Olmumua lʼEngai atua ndai?"
1Corinthians3:17 Teni eitarruo oltung'ani engaji Engai-- neitarruo Engai ele; amu sinyati engaji Engai-- nirara ndai."
1Corinthians3:18 Njoo melej oltung'ani kion; olojo too ndai-- ajo era ng'en tiatua ele maa-- njeaku olmodai-- petum ataa ng'en."
1Corinthians3:19 Amu era eng'eno ele maa emodaishu tʼEngai. Amu etisiraki: Erresh ninye lang'eni tiatua olosek lenye.
1Corinthians3:20 Neitoki: Eyolo Engai ndamunot oo lang'eni-- aajo mera toki."
1Corinthians3:21 Onaa-- njoo meitadaraa o obo kion too ltung'anak! Amu era pookin nkun inyi:"
1Corinthians3:22 ten aa Paulos-- ten aa Apolos-- ten aa Kefas-- ten aa olmaa-- ten aa empuan-- ten aa enkea-- ten aa naatii-- ten aa naapuo aaku-- — nkun inyi pookin--"
1Corinthians3:23 kake irara ndai le Kristos-- nera Kristos lʼEngai."
1Corinthians4:1 Nji njeikenaki yook oltung'ani pookin-- ajo kira laisyayak le Kristos o laitasheikinok loo njumat Engai."
1Corinthians4:2 Akae-- meing'oruni toki too laitasheikinok neme ak etumi aa supati."
1Corinthians4:3 Mera toki te nanu-- teni aaigwenakini too ndai arashu tʼengolong' oo ltung'anak; namaigwenaki baiki nanu kion."
1Corinthians4:4 Amu mayolo toki te nanu-- kake maaitaai te ina supat; era Olaitoriani-- olaaigwenaki nanu."
1Corinthians4:5 Onaa-- emingwenu toki eitu ebau enkata enye-- metabana nelotu Olaitoriani ololo ailang'u njumat enaimin neitalioio yeunot oo ltauja; netum te ina kata oltung'ani pookin enkitadararoto tʼEngai."
1Corinthians4:6 Ore kuna baak-- lalashera-- airo te kion ai o Apolos tʼolbae linyi-- pinteng'enuonuo too yook-- pemilang'ilang'a nona naatisiraki-- pemetii obo linyi owuasare olekai tʼolbae lʼolekai."
1Corinthians4:7 Amu kang'ai likintooruo iye nikintalang' olekai? Ainyo iata neitu itum? Kake ten aa inoto iye ninye-- ainyo pintadaraa kion-- anake eitu itum?"
1Corinthians4:8 Indipa aataraposhoto-- indipa aataa ladupak-- nintorishosho mikitii yook. Eaku ten emut intorishosho-- peiye kintorisho si yook te nebo o ndai."
1Corinthians4:9 Kake ajo nanu-- eitaduaia yook Engai anaa looti naleng'-- ooitarasakaki enkea-- amu kitaa yook enking'orare olmaa o noo lmalaikan o noo ltung'anak."
1Corinthians4:10 Kira ilmoda tʼolbae le Kristos-- kake irara ndai ng'eni tiatua Kristos; kishal yook-- nigoligolo ndai; neanyiti ndai-- nemenari yook."
1Corinthians4:11 O metabaiki ena saa kiata olamei o enkure-- nimikinjopo-- neoshi yook isederi-- nimikiata ang'--"
1Corinthians4:12 nikinyamalu-- nikintobir enkyas too ngaik ang' aten; teni emori yook-- nikimayan; naa teni einyali yook-- niking'iri;"
1Corinthians4:13 teni eiteenikini yook-- nikisaisho; eitaaki yook anaa endiata olmaa-- anaa oloirerio loo pookin oo taata."
1Corinthians4:14 Eitu asir kuna baak-- paitukurru ndai-- kake padiding' ndai-- nkera ainei nanyor."
1Corinthians4:15 Amu ten emut iatata ndai laiteng'enak iip kat iip tiatua Kristos-- anaata miatata loominyi kumok. Amu ore te Yesus Kristos atoiwuo nanu ndai too lomon lʼeng'ida."
1Corinthians4:16 Onaa adiding' ndai: Entaa lasujak lainei!
1Corinthians4:17 Te ina airriwaiye enitiiti ndai Timoteos-- ora enkerai ai nanyor naa supat tiatua Olaitoriani-- paitadamu ndai rregieita lang' ootii atua Kristos-- anaa paiteng'enisho too wuejitin pookin tiatua esirit pookin."
1Corinthians4:18 Ewuasa kulekai-- aajo malotu nanu enitiiti;"
1Corinthians4:19 kake alotu asioki-- teni eyeu Olaitoriani-- nayolou nanu me rorei loo loowuasa-- kake engolon."
1Corinthians4:20 Amu ore enkarsishu Engai meitashe tʼororei-- kake tʼengolon."
1Corinthians4:21 Ainyo iyeuu? kalotu tʼeng'udi arashu tʼenyorrata o oltau lʼemborran?
1Corinthians5:1 Eitoning'oro ororei ajo etii entalare atua ndai-- anaa pemeba nji tiatua lemeata Engai-- neji eama obo eng'oroyoni e menye lenye."
1Corinthians5:2 Niwuasasa ndai-- neme injirishiri-- peitupukuni olotaasa ina tiatua ndai?"
1Corinthians5:3 Kake ore nanu-- lematii tʼosesen e nebo o ndai kake tʼolmumua-- aidipa aigwenaki anaa Olotii ilo otaasa nji--"
1Corinthians5:4 peiye-- teni itumomo lʼengarna Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos-- eitarasakini ninye tʼolmumua lai o tʼengolon Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos satan--"
1Corinthians5:5 aitarruo enkiring'o-- kake pepok Olmumua tʼengolong' Olaitoriani Yesus."
1Corinthians5:6 Me sidai-- neijia anaa pintadaraara aten. Miyololo ndai-- aajo eisiijie enkiti kisiijoi entapa pookin?"
1Corinthians5:7 Akae-- entau tiatua ndai ina kisiijoi musana-- pitumutumu aataa entapa ng'ejuk-- neijia anaa pemekure etii enkisiijoi atua ndai. Amu eidasaiyeki embalelo e pasaka ang'-- nera Kristos."
1Corinthians5:8 Onaa-- maitaa ngolong'i kituak-- me tiatua enkisiijoi musana-- neme tiatua enkisiijoi emalmalishu o entorroni-- kake tiatua neitu eisiijoi esidano o esipata."
1Corinthians5:9 Atisiraka ndai tiatua empalai-- pimimbung'arere looas mbaak torrok oo nkiri."
1Corinthians5:10 Majo ina tukul too looas mbaak torrok oo nkiri lʼele maa-- arashu too lʼempiani o laisimak o looisyayaki muain-- amu te ina meata kata niming'uang'ua olmaa."
1Corinthians5:11 Kake atisiraka taata ndai-- pimimbung'arere oltung'ani oipoti olalashe-- teni era ninye oloas mbaak torrok oo nkiri-- ana ol empiani-- ana oloisyayaki muain-- ana olamoroni-- ana olaisimani. Eming'arie oloba nji endaa si."
1Corinthians5:12 Ara nanu ng'ai-- paigwenaki lootii boo? Nimingwenakiki lootii atua?"
1Corinthians5:13 Ore kulo ootii boo-- neigwenaki Engai. Ore si ndai entau oltung'ani torrono tʼempolos inyi."
1Corinthians6:1 Teni eataiye oltung'ani too ndai olekai embae-- kaji eiko teni eiteu aing'oru enkigwena too lemera supati-- neme too sinyat?"
1Corinthians6:2 Arashu miyololo ndai-- aajo epuo aaigwenaki sinyat olmaa? Teni ipuopuo aaigwenaki olmaa-- midupapa aaigwenaki mbaak kutiti?"
1Corinthians6:3 Miyololo ndai-- aajo kingwenaki yook ilmalaikan? Me naleng' sii mbaak ena kishon?"
1Corinthians6:4 Kake ore ndai-- teni iororo tʼolbae loo ntokitin ena kishon-- ning'oruru kulo lemeata enganyit tiatua esirit-- nipikipiki ninje aaku laigwenak?"
1Corinthians6:5 Atiaka ndai kuna aitukurru ndai. Metii atua ndai oltung'ani o obo ora ng'en oidim atirisha olalashe o olalashe?
1Corinthians6:6 Kake eishangarra olalashe o olekai-- baiki tʼengomom oo lemeiruk?"
1Corinthians6:7 Mekure eitoriori-- teni injangarrarra tʼempolos inyi. Ainyo piminjosho eikunakini ndai entorroni? Ainyo piminyorrurru aatalaita endupoto?"
1Corinthians6:8 Kake ndai oopeny looitobir ntorrok neisimisho-- naa too lalashera."
1Corinthians6:9 Amaa miyololo-- aajo mejung'u iltorrok enkarsishu Engai? Emilej aten. Mepuo aajung'u looas mbaak torrok oo nkiri o looisyayaki nkulie ain o looar enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni o lʼenjalan torrono o looisokorisho"
1Corinthians6:10 o lapurrok o lang'warrak o lamerak o lamorok o laisimak enkarsishu Engai.
1Corinthians6:11 Ore kulekai tiatua ndai-- naa nji opa etiu. Kake eisujaki ndai neitaai ndai sinyat tiatua engarna Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos o tiatua Olmumua lʼEngai ang'."
1Corinthians6:12 Aidimakino pookin-- kake meitoriori pookin; aidimakino pookin-- kake mayeu naaen o nyoo."
1Corinthians6:13 Endaa tʼengoshoke o engoshoke tʼendaa; kake eitarruo Engai pokira are: engoshoke o endaa. Kake ore osesen-- me oloo mbaak torrok oo nkiri-- kake ol Olaitoriani-- neitoki Olaitoriani ol osesen."
1Corinthians6:14 Eitopiwuo Engai Olaitoriani nelaitopiu si yook tʼengolon enye.
1Corinthians6:15 Arashu miyololo ndai-- aajo era seseni linyi rubat e Kristos? Kaitaa rubat e Kristos rubat esindani? Me neijia."
1Corinthians6:16 Arashu miyololo ndai-- aajo olorubare esindani-- naa osesen obo o ninye. Amu ejo: Eaku pokira are enkiring'o nabo."
1Corinthians6:17 Kake oloibung'are Olaitoriani-- neaku Olmumua obo o ninye."
1Corinthians6:18 Enkwet mbaak torrok oo nkiri! Etii enkitarruoto pookin naitobir oltung'ani-- oriong' osesen-- kake oloitobir mbaak torrok oo nkiri-- neitarruoki osesen lenye openy."
