1Corinthians6:19 Anai miyololo-- aajo era osesen linyi engaji Olmumua Sinyati otii atua ndai-- linoto tʼEngai nimirara kul inyi oopeny?"
1Corinthians6:20 Amu einyang'uaki ndai tʼenkinyang'a nagol. Onaa entadarai Engai tʼosesen linyi o tʼolmumua linyi oora lʼEngai.
1Corinthians7:1 Ore too kuna baak nikitisirakitia nanu ndai-- ajo nanu-- eikash-- teni meporoo oltung'ani eng'oroyoni."
1Corinthians7:2 Kake tʼolbae loo mbaak torrok oo nkiri-- njoo olee metaa eata engoroyoni enye kion-- njeata si eng'oroyoni olmoruo lenye kion."
1Corinthians7:3 Ore olee-- njeisho eng'oroyoni enye enanare-- njoo si eng'oroyoni meikunaki neijia olee lenye."
1Corinthians7:4 Meata enaidim eng'oroyoni tʼosesen lenye kion-- kake olee-- neijia si etiu olee-- meata enaidim tʼosesen lenye kion-- kake eng'oroyoni."
1Corinthians7:5 Emimitikino ndai aten-- neme teni irukuruku pokira are tʼenkata naje-- pitumutumu erishata oo sayat-- nintokiki aatumo-- pemeitasur ndai satan tʼolbae lʼolduruki linyi."
1Corinthians7:6 Kake ajo ena-- paitadol ndai-- maitanap."
1Corinthians7:7 Amu ayeu iltung'anak pookin netiu anaa nanu enaikununo. Kake eata oltung'ani pookin enkishooroto naishoo Engai ninye-- obo ena-- olekai enda."
1Corinthians7:8 Kake ajoki leitueamaro o ngolia: sidai too ninje-- teni ebik anaa nanu enaikununo."
1Corinthians7:9 Kake teni meidim ninje aatobik meama-- njeama. Amu eikash-- teni eama nelang' empejoto."
1Corinthians7:10 Ore lekua ooamishote-- naitanap-- kake me nanu-- kake Olaitoriani-- pemeing'ua eng'oroyoni olmoruo lenye-- —"
1Corinthians7:11 kake teni eing'ua-- njebik meama-- ana eitobirakinore olmoruo lenye-- — nemeing'ua olmoruo eng'oroyoni enye."
1Corinthians7:12 Ore ilkulekai ajoki nanu ndai-- me Olaitoriani: Teni eata olalashe eng'oroyoni nemeiruk-- neyeu ina neboitare ninye-- njoo mepal ninye."
1Corinthians7:13 Ore si eng'oroyoni-- teni eata olmoruo lemeiruk-- neyeu ilo neboitare ninye-- njoo mepal ninye."
1Corinthians7:14 Amu etisinyaiyoki olmoruo lemeiruk tʼeng'oroyoni-- neitokini aasinyaa eng'oroyoni nemeiruk tʼolmoruo. Teni me neijia-- anaata era duruk nkera inyi-- kake etaa sinyat taata."
1Corinthians7:15 Kake teni erisha lido lemeiruk-- njerisha. Teni eikununo nji-- meeni olalashe arashu enganashe; kake eipotie Olaitoriani yook eseriani."
1Corinthians7:16 Ti aji iyolo iye-- eng'oroyoni-- an ake intopok olmoruo lino? Anai ti aji iyolo iye-- olmoruo-- an ake intopok eng'oroyoni ino?"
1Corinthians7:17 Kake anaa petoorikia Olaitoriani-- anaa peipotoko Engai-- njelimana oltung'ani pookin neijia."
1Corinthians7:18 Teni eipotoki oltung'ani emurata-- nemetiu anaa olememurata. Naa teni eipotoki oltung'ani memurata-- nememurati."
1Corinthians7:19 Me toki emurata-- ana teni mimurata me toki-- kake teni imbung' nkitanapat Engai."
1Corinthians7:20 Njebik oltung'ani pookin tʼenkipototo naipotieki.
1Corinthians7:21 Inyorriki ai kimpotoki tʼesingaishu? Miekenyakinore. Kake teni indim atalakunye-- tonyorra aikuna nji."
1Corinthians7:22 Amu oloipotoki tʼOlaitoriani anaa osinga-- nelakuno tʼOlaitoriani; neijia si etiu oloipotoki elakuno-- nera osinga le Kristos."
1Corinthians7:23 Einyang'uaki ndai tʼenkinyang'a nagol; akae-- emiaku singan loo ltung'anak."
1Corinthians7:24 Lalashera lainei-- njebikie oltung'ani pookin eneipotieki te nebo o Engai."
1Corinthians7:25 Kake ore tʼolbae loo ntoiye-- maata enkitanapata Olaitoriani-- kake aisho ndai enkigwena ai anaa oltung'ani oinoto eng'adunoto Engai-- pabik tiatua enkirukoto."
1Corinthians7:26 Akae-- ajo nanu: Sidai tʼolbae lʼosina otii-- teni eikununo oltung'ani pookin nji:"
1Corinthians7:27 Teni kiteenaki eng'oroyoni-- naing'oru elakunoto. Teni ilakunore eng'oroyoni-- ming'oru eng'oroyoni."
1Corinthians7:28 Kake teni iamisho-- mintarruo; naa teni eami entito-- nemeitarruo; kake eata looba nji enyamali tʼosesen-- anaata ayeu naibooio ndai te ina."
1Corinthians7:29 Kake ajo nji-- lalashera-- amu dorrop enkata. Ore nkulie mbaak-- naa kuna: looata ng'oroyok-- njetiu anaa lemeata; ore looishir-- netiu anaa lemeishir;"
1Corinthians7:30 ore looshipa-- netiu anaa lemeshipa; ore looinyang'u-- netiu anaa lemeata toki;"
1Corinthians7:31 ore looitobirishore ena kop-- netiu anaa lemeitobirishore t'entorroni: amu emuta mbaak ena kop."
1Corinthians7:32 Ak ayeu ndai pimiekenyanya. Ore olemeama-- neshilaa mbaak Olaitoriani-- peitiship Olaitoriani;"
1Corinthians7:33 ore oloamishe-- neshilaa mbaak ena kop-- peitiship eng'oroyoni."
1Corinthians7:34 Kake etii enaor eng'oroyoni nayama o entito. Ore enda nemeama-- neshilaa mbaak Olaitoriani-- petum ataa sinyati tʼosesen o tʼoltau; kake ore enda nayama-- neshilaa mbaak ena kop-- anaa peitiship olmoruo lenye."
1Corinthians7:35 Atejo kuna-- peaku endupoto inyi-- neme erreshet apik ndai-- kake peitoriori-- nisyayakiki ndai Olaitoriani osupatei-- meiboiyori ndai."
1Corinthians7:36 Kake teni ejo oltung'ani meidim aiboo entito enye enganyit-- tiaraki nataa botor-- nenare peaku neijia-- njeitobir enanyorru-- meitarruo: njeami."
1Corinthians7:37 Kake ore ilo oibung'a tiatua oltau lenye-- tiaraki naa ninye oitore nemeata earakinoto-- netayeuo si tʼoltau lenye-- peibok entito enye-- neiko sidan."
1Corinthians7:38 Akae-- ore oloamaki entito enye-- neitobir sidan-- ore olemeamaki-- neitobir sidan nelang'."
1Corinthians7:39 Eibooki eng'oroyoni too nkitanapat-- eton eishiu olmoruo lenye; kake teni ee olmoruo-- neishori meama elde oyeu; tiatua Olaitoriani ake."
1Corinthians7:40 Kake era ninye tesh nelang'-- teni ebik nji-- anaa paigwenu nanu; amu ajo aata si nanu Olmumua lʼEngai."
1Corinthians8:1 Ore too ntokitin naayeng'akini nkulie ain aaitaa nkidasareitin-- nikiyolo-- amu kiata pookin eyolounoto. Eyolounoto-- naitaa sapuk elukunya-- kake eshet enyorrata."
1Corinthians8:2 Teni ejo oltung'ani eyolo toki-- neton eitu eyolo anaa pemeata kata nemeyolo."
1Corinthians8:3 Kake ore oltung'ani onyor Engai-- ninye eyolouni tʼengomom enye."
1Corinthians8:4 Akae-- kiyolo mbaak endaa oo nkidasareitin naayakini nkulie ain-- aajo mera engai omoni toki tiatua olmaa-- nikintoki aayolo-- aajo metii engai Ai neme nabo ake."
1Corinthians8:5 Naa ten ake etii nkulie naaji ngain te shumata arashu tʼenkop (anaa petii ngain kumok o laitoriak kumok)--"
1Corinthians8:6 kake ore yook-- nikiata Engai nabo ake-- ninye Papa-- nepukunye ntokitin pookin te ninye-- nikitii yook atua ninye-- o Olaitoriani obo-- Yesus Kristos-- te ninye etaa ntokitin pookin o yook te ninye."
1Corinthians8:7 Kake meata iltung'anak pookin ena yolounoto. Kake eton esuj kulekai o taata nkulie ain-- nenya ntokitin naateyeng'akaki ninje-- aajo noo nena-- neidurukieki nji ndamunot enye-- tiaraki nashal."
1Corinthians8:8 Kake meitudupaki yook endaa tʼEngai. Teni mikinya-- nemeng'oriki yook toki-- naa teni kinya-- nimikilang'."
1Corinthians8:9 Kake eng'orai-- pemeaku ena lakunoto inyi enkikoboto oo looshal."
1Corinthians8:10 Amu ten emutu kidol olekai tung'ani iye-- liata eyolounoto-- inya endaa tʼengaji oo nkulie ain-- meisisi tʼoltau lenye naa ten ake eshal-- penya enateyeng'akaki nkulie ain?"
1Corinthians8:11 Neimin neijia tʼeyolounoto ino olalashe oshal-- otuaiye Kristos ninye."
1Corinthians8:12 Kake teni intarruokiki neijia lalashera niariara ndamunot enye naashal-- nintarruokiki si Kristos."
1Corinthians8:13 Akae-- teni eitapong'oo endaa olalashe lai-- namanyankiri ai kata-- pemaitapong'oo olalashe lai."
1Corinthians9:1 Ke malakuno nanu? Mara nanu olairriwani? Keitu adol Yesus. Olaitoriani lang'? Mirara ndai enkyas ai tiatua Olaitoriani?
1Corinthians9:2 Teni mara nanu olairriwani too lkulekai-- kake ara too ndai. Amu ore olponoto-- ajo ara olairriwani-- nirara ndai tiatua Olaitoriani."
1Corinthians9:3 Ena emitunoto ai too lelo laaikilikwan.
1Corinthians9:4 Amaa-- mikiata engolon-- pekinya arashu pekiok?"
1Corinthians9:5 Mikiata engolon nikiea enganashe aaku eng'oroyoni anaa ilkulekai airriwak-- o lalashera lʼOlaitoriani-- o Kefas?"
1Corinthians9:6 Arashu nanu ake openy o Barnabas lemeata engolon nimikipalie enkyas?
1Corinthians9:7 Kalo sikeri oisyaisho nkatitin pookin nemetum olkwaje? Ana kang'ai oun enkuruma oo njanito olmarua nemenya ilng'anayok lenyena? Ana kang'ai oirrita enjoo nemeok kule e inajoo?
1Corinthians9:8 Kajo kuna anaa oltung'ani? Ana mejo nkitanapat neijia?
1Corinthians9:9 Amu etisiraki too nkitanapat e Mose aajo: Mien olkiteng' enkutuk eidong' ilpaik. Ke ilmong'i eshilaa Engai?
1Corinthians9:10 Arashu eitu ejo tʼolbae lang' katukul? Kake etisiraki tʼolbae lang'-- amu ore olotur enkuruma-- njetur tʼeanyunoto-- ore oloituutisho-- njeituutisho tʼeanyunoto-- peiye eng'arie ninye tʼenkata enye."
1Corinthians9:11 Teni kituunokitio yook ndai ntokitin emumuaishu-- ke entoki sapuk-- teni kisambu yook ntokitin enkop inyi?"
1Corinthians9:12 Ten aa eaku kulekai eng'ar ndai kuna baak-- mikilusoo yook? Kake eitu yook kisuj ena golon-- kake kiting'iria nkumok-- pemikimbooio euangelion e Kristos."
1Corinthians9:13 Miyololo ndai-- aajo ore looitobirisho tʼengaji sinyati-- nenya ne ina aji-- o looidasisho tʼolperere lʼenkidasare-- nenyaiye olperere."
1Corinthians9:14 Neijia si eitanapua Olaitoriani-- peata kulo ooinosu euangelion-- embaikinoto enye tʼeuangelion."
1Corinthians9:15 Kake eitu asuj entoki o nabo too nena. Neitu asir nanu kuna baak-- peaku neijia te nanu. Amu enare nae nanu-- pemeitai oltung'ani enkitadararoto ai."
1Corinthians9:16 Amu teni ainosu lomon lʼeng'ida-- namaata enkitadararoto. Amu meata kata namainosu. Ee-- kake aiya-- teni mainosu lomon lʼeng'ida."
1Corinthians9:17 Amu teni aiko kuna tʼenyorrata-- natum olkwaje-- teni me tʼenyorrata-- naaishooki ake ena kisyayare."
1Corinthians9:18 Kainyo naa olkwaje lai? Nyele painosu lomon lʼeng'ida aiko nji pesho tʼempuris ake-- namaitarruo engolon naata tiatua lomon lʼeng'ida."
1Corinthians9:19 Amu alakuno too ltung'anak pookin-- kake aaua kion atua esingaishu oltung'ani pookin-- patum kumok too ninje."
1Corinthians9:20 Too Yudayoi naaku Oyudayos-- patum Yudayoi-- o too lelo ootii abori oo nkitanapat naaku anaa abori oo nkitanapat-- ten ake matii openy abori oo nkitanapat-- patum lootii abori oo nkitanapat."
1Corinthians9:21 Too lelo lemeata nkitanapat-- natiu anaa maata nkitanapat-- (kake me anaa maata nkitanapat tʼEngai-- kake aata nkitanapat tiatua Kristos)-- patum lemeata nkitanapat."
1Corinthians9:22 Too looshal nataa anaa oloshal-- patum looshal. Ataa anaa iltung'anak pookin too mpukunot pookin-- patum too ngoitoi pookin aitopua iltung'anak."
1Corinthians9:23 Naitobir nanu pookin tʼolbae loo lomon lʼeng'ida-- peiye atum atang'ara ninje."
1Corinthians9:24 Miyololo ndai-- aajo ore lookwet tiatua eneikarruno-- nekwet ninje pookin-- kake eng'amu obo ake en engilunoto? Neijia enkwet si ndai-- pitumutumu aatang'amu."
1Corinthians9:25 Ore oltung'ani pookin logilunore-- neitore kion too pookin; akae-- eng'amu lelo enkaja namuta-- ore yook enememuta."
1Corinthians9:26 Akae-- akwet si nanu nji-- me anaa oltung'ani lemeyolo enelo; aara nji-- me anaa oloar enkijape."
1Corinthians9:27 Kake aibooio osesen lai naisingan ninye-- pamainosaki kulekai naaku openy oloiturrari."
1Corinthians10:1 Amu mayeu-- pemiyololo ndai-- lalashera-- aajo etii loopapa lang' pookin abori erukenya neim pookin atua olbalbal--"
1Corinthians10:2 neibatisi pookin atua Mose tiatua erukenya o tiatua olbalbal--"
1Corinthians10:3 nenya pookin endaa nabo emumuaishu--"
1Corinthians10:4 neok pookin eokoto nabo emumuaishu-- amu etooko tʼosoit lʼemumuaishu lotusujare ninje-- nera ele soit Kristos."
1Corinthians10:5 Kake eitu eng'ida Engai too lkumok lenye-- amu etaraki ninje ti ang'ata."
1Corinthians10:6 Etaa nena entoki enkiteng'enare too yook-- pimikiaku yook lang'warrak loo ntorrok-- anaa petang'warrishote lelo."
1Corinthians10:7 Emiaku baiki laisyayak loo nkulie ain-- anaa petaa looje too ninje-- anaa pesira: Etotonitio olorere aadaa neokisho neinyototo-- peiguran."
1Corinthians10:8 Njoo mikintobir mbaak torrok oo nkiri anaa peitobira looje too ninje-- nerara tʼengolong' nabo elfun tikitam o uni."
1Corinthians10:9 Njoo mikintasur baiki Olaitoriani-- anaa peitasuro looje too ninje-- neimin ninje too lasuria."
1Corinthians10:10 Eming'unyung'uny baiki anaa peing'unyung'unya looje too ninje-- neimin tʼolaiminieni."
1Corinthians10:11 Etaa nena pookin-- peaku entoki enkiteng'enare oo lelo-- nesiri-- peaku erojata too yook looinepua emutata enkop."
1Corinthians10:12 Onaa-- olojo eitashe-- peing'oraa-- pemebatata."
1Corinthians10:13 Eitu einepu ndai enkitasuroto neme nʼentung'anishu; kake era Engai supat nemeisho eitasuri ndai nalang' enindimidimi-- kake eitaa tʼenkitasuroto empukunoto-- pindimidimi aatanap ninye."
1Corinthians10:14 Akae-- lalashera lainei-- elanya enkisyayare oo nkulie ain."
1Corinthians10:15 Airorie ndai anaa iltung'anak ng'eni; entetem enalimu.
1Corinthians10:16 Ore enkwaru emayani nikimayan-- mera ninye enkidikidikoto osarge le Kristos? Ore olmkate likibelibel yook-- mera ninye enkidikidikoto osesen le Kristos?"
1Corinthians10:17 Tiaraki nara olmkate obo-- nikira si yook ilkumok osesen obo-- amu king'ar yook pookin olmkate obo."
1Corinthians10:18 Eng'orai Israel eneikununo too mbaak osesen. Ore kulo ooinos nkidasareitin-- meidikidikore ninje si olperere?"
1Corinthians10:19 Kajo aa? Kajo entoki nateyeng'akaki nkulie ain-- ninye toki?"
1Corinthians10:20 Kake ajo: Ore ntokitin naaidasishore loreren lemeata Engai-- neidasaki loiriruani-- me Engai; namayeu nanu ndai ping'aring'ara loiriruani."
1Corinthians10:21 Mindimidimi ndai aatook enkwaru Olaitoriani o enkwaru oo loiriruani-- nimindimidimi aatang'ar enaraa Olaitoriani o enaraa oo loiriruani."
1Corinthians10:22 Arashu king'elaki Olaitoriani? Ke kiata yook engolon aalang' ninye?
1Corinthians10:23 Aidimakino pookin-- kake me pookin naisho endupoto; naidimakino pookin-- kake me pookin nashet."
1Corinthians10:24 Njoo meing'oru oltung'ani nkun enyena-- kake baiki nʼolekai."
1Corinthians10:25 Entoki pookin natii tʼenemirishoreki-- entaam-- niminkilikwanunu tʼolbae loo ndamunot."
1Corinthians10:26 Amu: En Engai enkop o emborei enye.
1Corinthians10:27 Kake ore teni eipot ndai obo too lemeiruk-- pinyanya endaa te nebo o ninje-- niyeuu nipuopuo-- entaam pookin naisho ndai-- niminkilikwanunu tʼolbae loo ndammunot."
1Corinthians10:28 Naa teni ejoki ndai oltung'ani: eteyeng'akaki kuna kiri nkulie ain-- eminya-- tʼolbae le ilo otiaka ndai o pimitutu ndamunot."
1Corinthians10:29 Kake me ndamunot inono-- ajo ndamunot olekai. Ainyo peigwenakini elakunoto ai too ndamunot olekai?"
1Corinthians10:30 Teni anya aliki ashe-- ainyo paamori tʼolbae loo nena natejoiye ashe?"
1Corinthians10:31 Akae-- teni inyanya arashu iokioko arashu intobiribiri toki-- entobira pookin-- peaku nʼenkitook Engai."
1Corinthians10:32 Eminjo enkikoboto Yudayoi-- ana Ilgrikini-- ana esirit Engai--"
1Corinthians10:33 neijia anaa paitiship si nanu iltung'anak pookin-- namaing'oru endupoto ai-- kake en oolkumok-- petum aatopok."
1Corinthians11:1 Entaa ndai lasujak lainei-- neijia anaa para nanu olasujani le Kristos."
1Corinthians11:2 Aitadaraa ndai-- lalashera-- tiaraki nikidamumu nanu too ntokitin pookin nimbung'arere rregieita laishoo ndai."
1Corinthians11:3 Nayeu ndai niyololo-- aajo era elukunya olee pookin Kristos-- ore elukunya eng'oroyoni-- naa olmoruo-- ore elukunya e Kristos-- naa Engai."
1Corinthians11:4 Ore olee pookin osaisho arashu oitayolou mbaak e akenya-- teni eitoip elukunya-- nemepik elukunya enye enganyit."
1Corinthians11:5 Ore eng'oroyoni pookin nasaisho arashu naitayolou mbaak e akenya-- teni meitoip elukunya-- nemepik elukunya enye enganyit; netiu anaa etabarnoki."
1Corinthians11:6 Teni eitu eitoip eng'oroyoni elukunya-- njebarni ninye. Kake tiaraki nemeaku tʼeng'oroyoni-- teni edung'i ilpapit ana ebarni-- njeitoip elukunya."
1Corinthians11:7 Kake ore olee-- njoo meitoip elukunya-- tiaraki naa ninye emua o enkitook Engai. Kake ore eng'oroyoni-- naa enkitook olmoruo."
1Corinthians11:8 Amu eitu eing'ua olee atua eng'oroyoni-- kake eng'oroyoni natung'aiye atua olee."
1Corinthians11:9 Neitu eitobiri olee tʼolbae reng'oroyoni-- kake eng'oroyoni tʼolbae lʼolee."
1Corinthians11:10 Onaa-- eikash-- teni eata engolon tʼelukunya tʼolbae loo lmalaikan."
1Corinthians11:11 Kake eikununo nji: mera eng'oroyoni metii olmoruo-- nemera olmoruo metii eng'oroyoni tiatua Olaitoriani."
1Corinthians11:12 Amu anaa eng'oroyoni eing'ua olee-- neija etii olee tʼeng'oroyoni; kake eing'ua pookin Engai."
1Corinthians11:13 Engwenare ndai oopeny: Keitoriori-- teni esai eng'oroyoni Engai eitu eitoip elukunya?"
1Corinthians11:14 Arashu meiteng'en ndai enkitobirunoto ajo ore teni eata olee ilpapit ooado-- neaku enkurruna te ninye--"
1Corinthians11:15 neija teni eata eng'oroyoni ilpapit ooado-- naa enkitook te ninye? amu eishooki ilpapit aaku eopet enye."
1Corinthians11:16 Teni etii oltung'ani onyor enjangar-- mikiata yook orregie oba nji-- nemeata si sirito Engai."
1Corinthians11:17 Ore aisho ndai ena kitanapata-- maitadaraa ndai-- tiaraki nimitumomo tʼorregie oikash-- kake tʼorregie torrono nelang'."
1Corinthians11:18 Ore en enkiterata-- teni itumomo tʼesirit-- natoning'o ajo etii rishat atua ndai-- nairuk ematua oo nona."
1Corinthians11:19 Amu meata kata nemeaku rishat tiatua ndai-- peibaluni loora supati tiatua ndai."
1Corinthians11:20 Kake teni itumomo-- nemenyai endaa Olaitoriani."
1Corinthians11:21 Amu teni iyeuu ninyanya endaa sinyati-- neng'as pookin anya endaa enye openy-- neata olekai olamei-- nemera olekai."
1Corinthians11:22 Amaa-- miatata ngajijik inyi ninyayeye niokioko? Arashu imenimene ndai esirit Engai nintukurrurru kulo lemeata toki? Kajoki aa ndai? Kaitadaraa ndai? Tʼolbae loo nona maitadaraa ndai."
1Corinthians11:23 Amu atang'amua nanu tʼOlaitoriani enaishoo ndai-- ajo eibung'a Olaitoriani Yesus te ina kiarie naitarasarieki ninye-- olmkate"
1Corinthians11:24 nejo ashe nebelibel ejo: Enkoito-- entaam! Era ele osesen lai logilieki ndai; enkuna ena-- pekidamumu nanu."
1Corinthians11:25 Neijia eibung'a baiki enkwaru-- eidipa endaata-- ejo: Era ena kwaru osotua ng'ejuk tiatua osarge lai; enkuna ena oshi-- teni iokioko-- pekidamumu nanu."
1Corinthians11:26 Amu oshi-- teni inyanya ele mkate niokioko ena kwaru-- enosutu enkea Olaitoriani-- metabana nelotu ninye."
1Corinthians11:27 Ore olonya olmkate neok enkwaru Olaitoriani-- meitobirakino-- nelatumoki kion earata osesen o osarge lʼOlaitoriani."
1Corinthians11:28 Akae-- njeleen oltung'ani kion-- petum ainosa nji ele mkate neok ena kwaru."
1Corinthians11:29 Amu olonya neok-- meitobirakino-- nenya neokoki kion enkigwena-- tiaraki nemeitaa kitok osesen lʼOlaitoriani."
1Corinthians11:30 Onaa-- etii atua ndai ilkumok loora menat o loomoiyaa neirura ematua kitok."
1Corinthians11:31 Amu teni kingwenaki aten-- nemeigwenakini yook."
1Corinthians11:32 Ore peigwenaki yook Olaitoriani-- neitubuluni yook-- pemedeki yook te nebo o olmaa."
1Corinthians11:33 Onaa-- lalashera lainei-- teni itumomo te nebo aanya endaa-- entaanyunoto ndai aten."
1Corinthians11:34 Ore teni eata obo olamei-- nenya tʼengaji enye-- pemeaku oltumo linyi ol enkigwena. Ore nkulie naatong'oro-- teni alotu naitobir."
1Corinthians12:1 Mayeu-- lalashera-- pimiyololo mbaak emumuaishu."
1Corinthians12:2 Iyololo-- aajo itang'asa aaku lemeata Engai-- nipuopuo enetii muain nemeiro-- anaa petorikoki ndai."
1Corinthians12:3 Onaa-- aitayolo ndai-- ajo metii oltung'ani loiro tiatua Olmumua lʼEngai ojo: Njedeki Yesus! Nemetii oloidim atejo: Olaitoriani Yesus! neme tʼOlmumua Sinyati."
1Corinthians12:4 Etii rishat oo nkishoorot-- kake etii Olmumua obo;"
1Corinthians12:5 netii rishat oo nkisyayareitin-- kake etii Olaitoriani obo;"
1Corinthians12:6 netii rishat oo nkitobirat-- kake etii Engai nabo naitobir pookin tiatua pookin."
1Corinthians12:7 Eishori oltung'ani pookin enkitaduaroto Olmumua-- peaku endupoto oo pookin."
1Corinthians12:8 Amu eishori oltung'ani obo tʼOlmumua ororei lʼeng'eno-- o olekai ororei lʼeyolounoto-- tʼele Mumua ake--"
1Corinthians12:9 o olekai enkirukoto tiatua ele Mumua-- o olekai nkishoorot enkishiunoto tiatua Olmumua obo--"
1Corinthians12:10 o olekai enkidimata oo ngoloni-- o olekai eyolounoto e akenya-- o olekai enkitooroto oo lmumuan-- o olekai nkutukie kumok-- o olekai enkitaalata oo nkutukie."
1Corinthians12:11 Neitobir kuna pookin Olmumua obo orisio neoriki oltung'ani pookin anaa peyeu ninye.
1Corinthians12:12 Amu neijia anaa pera obo osesen neata rubat kumok naa rubat pookin nʼosesen obo-- teni era ninje baiki kumok-- naa n'osesen obo ake: neijia baiki Kristos."
1Corinthians12:13 Amu eibatisaki yook pookin tʼOlmumua obo-- pekiaku osesen obo-- ten aa Yudayoi-- ana Ilgrikini-- ana singan-- ana loolakuno-- neitooki pookin atua Olmumua obo."
1Corinthians12:14 Ore si osesen-- nemera erubata nabo-- kake rubat kumok."
1Corinthians12:15 Teni ejo enkeju: mara engaina-- akae-- mara en osesen-- — ainyo-- me en osesen ninye?"
1Corinthians12:16 O teni ejo enkiyok: mara engong'u-- akae-- mara en osesen-- — ainyo-- me en osesen ninye?"
1Corinthians12:17 Ten aa osesen olulung'a engong'u-- kodee ening'oto? Ten aa osesen ening'oto katukul-- ti aji eing'uaya?"
1Corinthians12:18 Kake etipika Engai rubat pookin tiatua osesen-- anaa petayeuo."
1Corinthians12:19 Teni era rubat pookin erubata nabo-- kodee osesen?"
1Corinthians12:20 Kake etaa taata rubat kumok-- kake osesen obo."
1Corinthians12:21 Nemeidim engong'u atiaki engaina: Mikitumoki nanu; arashu meidim elukunya atiaki nkejek: Mikitumokiki nanu.
1Corinthians12:22 Kake enare kuna rubat osesen naalio eshalu naleng'-- neyeuni naleng'--"
1Corinthians12:23 o nena rubat osesen nikijo etong'orikitia enganyit too nkulie-- nikinjo enganyit naleng'; o nena naaitukurru yook-- nikintaa kituak aaitulusoo."
1Corinthians12:24 Amu ore nena rubat supati ang'-- nemelaita enkitadararoto. Kake eitushula Engai osesen-- neisho enganyit idia rubata natong'orikia--"
1Corinthians12:25 pemeaku eoroto tiatua osesen-- kake peshilaro pookin aten."
1Corinthians12:26 Naa teni emoi erubata nabo-- neme nkulie pookin te nebo; ore teni eitaai kitok erubata nabo-- neng'idakino nkulie pookin."
1Corinthians12:27 Kake irara osesen le Kristos o rubat enyena anaa perisiore oltung'ani pookin.
1Corinthians12:28 Netipika Engai iltung'anak tiatua esirit; ore lʼenkiterata lairriwak-- ore liare layolounok-- ore li okuni laiteng'enak-- ore tekurum looitobir nkidimat-- ore tekurum nkishoorot naaishiunyeki loomoi-- o laretok-- o looitorisho-- o nkutukie naaoro."
1Corinthians12:29 Ke-- lairriwak pookin? Ana layolounok pookin? Ana laiteng'enak pookin? Ana nkidimat pookin?"
1Corinthians12:30 Ana keata pookin enkishooroto naishiunye loomoi? Ana keiro pookin too kulekai ng'ejepa? Ana keitaal pookin ninje?
1Corinthians12:31 Kake entonyok-- pitumutumu nkishoorot kituak naleng'-- napon aitadol ndai engoitoi naikash naleng'."
1Corinthians13:1 Ten emutu airo too lng'ejepa loo ltung'anak o loo lmalaikan-- namaata enyorrata-- anaata ara olduala oorito o elil naoru."
1Corinthians13:2 Ten emutu aata eyolounoto nayolo mikiot pookin o eng'eno pookin-- ten emutu aata enkirukoto pookin-- paidurrie ildonyo-- namaata enyorrata-- namara toki."
1Corinthians13:3 Ten emutu aoriki laisinak masaa ainei pookin naishooio osesen lai-- peikie enkima-- namaata enyorrata-- namaaku toki."
1Corinthians13:4 Eng'iri enyorrata-- ebor enyorrata-- megil tau-- meyang'iyang' enyorrata-- meikarrikar--"
1Corinthians13:5 melau enganyit-- meing'oru enara enenye-- meitagoroi-- meiken entorroni--"
1Corinthians13:6 meng'idakino enemeitoriori-- kake eng'idakino esipata;"
1Corinthians13:7 enyuakino pookin-- eiruk pookin-- neanyu pookin-- eng'iriakino pookin."
1Corinthians13:8 Meitoki amuta enyorrata. Teni aa yolounot-- nepuo aamuta; teni aa nkutukie-- nepuo aaiting'; teni aa eng'eno-- nelamuta."
1Corinthians13:9 Amu kiata eng'eno ematua ake-- nikiyolou ne akenya ematua ake."
1Corinthians13:10 Teni ebau embaiaroto-- nelaishunye nʼematua."
1Corinthians13:11 Ore opa ara enkerai-- airoro anaa enkerai-- naata eng'eno anaa enkerai-- aaibirribir anaa enkerai; ore ataa olee-- naing'ua enkeraishu."
1Corinthians13:12 Amu kidolita taata tiatua enking'oret anaa tʼoloyote; ore te ina kata engomom tʼengomom. Atayolo taata ematua-- kake alayolou te ina kata naleng'-- anaa paatayolouoki si nanu."
1Corinthians13:13 Akae-- ebik taata enkirukoto-- eanyunoto-- enyorrata-- kuna uni; kake era enyorrata kitok too kuna nelang'."
1Corinthians14:1 Entusuj enyorrata-- ninyokinyoko aaing'oru nkishoorot emumuaishu-- enaikash teni intayolouu ne akenya."
1Corinthians14:2 Amu ore ilo oiro tʼolekai ng'ejep-- nemeirorie iltung'anak-- kake Engai; nemening' olekai-- eiro ninye ake mikiot tʼOlmumua."
1Corinthians14:3 Kake oloitayolou ne akenya-- neirorie iltung'anak-- peaku nʼenjetakinoto o nʼendiding'aroto o nʼenkilejilejata."
1Corinthians14:4 Ore oloiro tʼolekai ng'ejep-- neshet kion; kake oloitayolou ne akenya-- neshet esirit."
1Corinthians14:5 Kake ayeu taata ndai pookin niroro too lng'ejepa-- o naleng'-- teni intayolouu ne akenya. Amu ore oloitayolou ne akenya-- nelang' oloiro too lng'ejepa-- teni meitaai ninye ninje-- peiye etum esirit enjetakinoto."
1Corinthians14:6 Onaa-- lalashera-- ten emut eaku alotu enitiiti-- airo too lng'ejepa-- kaa dupoto itumutumu te nanu-- teni mairorie ndai tʼembolunoto ana tʼeyolounoto ana tʼenkitayolounoto ana tʼenkiteng'enare?"
1Corinthians14:7 Neijia etiu ntokitin nemeishiu naaisho oltoilo-- anaa enkisulet arashu enkinanda; teni meisho ninje iltoiloi ooro-- kaji eikuni teni eyolouni enaoshi tʼenkisulet arashu tʼenkinanda?"
1Corinthians14:8 Arashu teni eoshi emowuo tʼoltoilo lemeyolounoi-- kang'ai oitobirakinore enjore?"
1Corinthians14:9 Neijia si itiuu ndai-- teni iroro too lng'ejepa nimiatata rorei ooyolounoi-- kaji eiko teni eyolo iltung'anak-- enilimumu? Amu iroro anaa atua enkijape."
1Corinthians14:10 Etii iltoiloi loo muain kumok tiatua olmaa-- kake metii nemeyolounoi."
1Corinthians14:11 Teni mayolou enkutuk enye-- naaku omoni tʼele oiro-- neaku ilo oiro-- olomoni te nanu."
1Corinthians14:12 Neijia si ndai liyeuu nkishoorot emumuaishu-- entonyok aaing'oru enkumoi oo nkishoorot nishetietie esirit."
1Corinthians14:13 Akae-- ore oloiro too lng'ejepa-- njesaisho nji-- peitaai si."
1Corinthians14:14 Amu teni asaisho too lng'ejepa-- nesai Olmumua lai-- kake meaki eng'eno ai ilmomo oltung'ani o obo."
1Corinthians14:15 Ainyo naa enaikash? Ayeu nasai tʼolmumua lai naitoki asai tʼeng'eno ai. Arany singolioitin lʼEngai tʼolmumua lai-- narany tʼeng'eno ai si."
1Corinthians14:16 Kake teni imayan tʼolmumua-- kaji eiko teni eiruk ele otii ewueji oo laning'ok ajo: Amen-- tʼelikinoto ashe ino-- teni meyolo eniroro?"
1Corinthians14:17 Esipa-- iliki iye ashe naleng'-- kake eitu eitagoli olekai te ina."
1Corinthians14:18 Aliki Engai ashe-- tiaraki nairo too lng'ejepa nalang' ndai pookin;"
1Corinthians14:19 kake tiatua esirit-- ayeu nairo rorei imiet ake tʼeng'eno ai-- paiteng'en ilkulekai-- nelang' airo rorei iip kat iip too lng'ejepa."
1Corinthians14:20 Lalashera-- emiaku nkera tiatua eng'eno inyi; kake tiatua ntorrok entaa nkera-- kake entaa baiarot tiatua eng'eno inyi."
1Corinthians14:21 Etisiraki tiatua nkitanapat: Ayeu nairorie ele orere too kulekai ng'ejepa o too nkutukie oo lomon-- nemaaning' ninje nanu-- etejo Olaitoriani."
1Corinthians14:22 Akae-- era ilng'ejepa ilponot loo lemeiruk-- neme loo looiruk-- kake era enkitayoloto e akenya en oo looiruk-- neme noo lemeiruk."
1Corinthians14:23 Ten emutu etumo esirit nalulung'a tʼewueji nebo neiro pookin too lng'ejepa-- neitoki aapuonu iltung'anak leme ng'eni ana lemeiruk-- anaata mejo iatata oloirirua?"
1Corinthians14:24 Kake ten eaku eitayolou pookin lomon lʼEngai-- nelotu olemeiruk ana olemeyolo toki-- nediding' neigwenaki pookin ninye;"
1Corinthians14:25 ore mbaak oltau lenye naaisudori-- neibalunyeki-- nebatata tʼengomom enye aserem Engai-- neiruk ajo etii Engai atua ndai esipa."
1Corinthians14:26 Ainyo naa-- lalashera? Teni itumomo ndai-- niatata pookin isingolioitin lʼEngai-- enkiteng'enare-- embolunoto-- ilng'ejepa-- enkitaalata; enjoo ntokitin pookin meidipata nʼenjetata."
1Corinthians14:27 Teni eiro oltung'ani too lng'ejepa-- njoo metaa aare-- ana teni elusoo-- neaku okuni-- kake tʼolkereri-- ninjosho obo-- peitaalu."
1Corinthians14:28 Naa teni metii oloitaal-- njegira ilo tiatua esirit-- neirorie kion o Engai."
1Corinthians14:29 Enjoo layolounok loo lomon lʼEngai eiro aare arashu okuni-- ninjosho ilkulekai metirisha."
1Corinthians14:30 Kake teni etum olekai oton tene embolunoto-- negira ol enkiterata."
1Corinthians14:31 Amu indimidimi ndai pookin aatayolou-- me obo ake-- peiteng'enuo pookin nediding! pookin."
1Corinthians14:32 Ore ilmumuan loo layolounok-- nening' layolounok."
1Corinthians14:33 Amu ore Engai-- me Engai enjangar-- kake en eseriani."
1Corinthians14:34 Anaa tiatua sirito pookin oo sinyat-- enjoo egira ng'oroyok tiatua esirit. Amu eitu eishori ninje-- peirorie-- kake pening' anaa enatejo nkitanapat."
1Corinthians14:35 Naa teni eyeu neiteng'enuo toki-- njoo meikilikwana ilmoruak lenye too ngajijik-- amu enkurruna tʼeng'oroyoni-- teni eiro tʼesirit."
1Corinthians14:36 Ainyo-- ai ndai eing'ua ororei lʼEngai-- ana ndai etabaikia ake?"
1Corinthians14:37 Ore oltung'ani pookin oiken kion ajo olayolounoni arashu ol Olmumua-- njeyolou nona baak nasiraki ndai-- amu nkitanapat Olaitoriani."
1Corinthians14:38 Naa ten eaku emoda oltung'ani-- njemoda."
1Corinthians14:39 Akae-- lalashera lainei-- entonyok piakuku layolounok-- emimitiki eiro too lng'ejepa."
1Corinthians14:40 Enjoo ntokitin pookin eitoriori neaku tʼorregie sidai.
1Corinthians15:1 Aitayolo ndai-- lalashera-- lomon lʼeng'ida lainosaka ndai-- ning'amumu baiki nintasheshe tiatua ninje--"
1Corinthians15:2 ipokipoko baiki too ninje-- teni imbung'ubung'u ele rorei anaa painosaka ndai; ten emutu me-- anaata iruko pesho."
1Corinthians15:3 Amu aitarasaka ndai tʼenkata elukunya kuna natang'amua si nanu openy-- ajo etua Kristos tʼolbae loo nkitarruot ang' anaa pejo sirat--"
1Corinthians15:4 ajo etunukaki neitopiuni tʼengolong' e uni-- anaa pejo sirat--"
1Corinthians15:5 ajo etalie te Kefas-- tekurum too lelo tomon o are."
1Corinthians15:6 Tekurum nelioi too lalashera loolang' iip imiet te nebo-- neishiu ilkumok lenye metabaiki taata-- neirurate ilkulekai."
1Corinthians15:7 Nelioi tekurum te Yakobos-- tekurum too lairriwak pookin."
1Corinthians15:8 Ore tekurum oo pookin nelioi baiki te nanu anaa lʼeiunoto neitu ebaia.
1Corinthians15:9 Amu ara nanu olkiti loo lairriwak nemeaku paaipoti nanu olairriwani-- amu atimira esirit Engai."
1Corinthians15:10 Kake ara tʼeng'adunoto Engai olara-- neitu eaku eng'adunoto Engai pesho tiatua nanu-- amu atopona anyamalu nalang' ninje pookin-- me nanu baiki-- kake eng'adunoto Engai naarubare nanu."
1Corinthians15:11 Kake ten aa nanu arashu ninje-- neijia kinko teni kinosu lomon-- naa neija iruko."
1Corinthians15:12 Kake teni einosuni Kristos-- ajo etopiwuo too lootuata-- kejo aa kulekai too ndai-- aajo meatai empiunoto oo lootuata?"
1Corinthians15:13 Teni metii empiunoto oo lootuata-- eitu epiu baiki Kristos."
1Corinthians15:14 Teni eitu epiu Kristos-- akae-- era enkinosunoto ang' en e pesho naa ne pesho enkirukoto inyi."
1Corinthians15:15 Netumi baiki yook anaa iljaken lʼelejare lʼEngai-- tiaraki nikinjakenokitio Engai empaashata-- aajo eitopiwuo ninye Kristos leitu eitopiu-- teni mepiu lootuata;"
1Corinthians15:16 amu teni mepiu lootuata-- neitu epiu baiki Kristos."
1Corinthians15:17 Teni eitu epiu Kristos-- nera enkirukoto inyi pesho-- nepon itiiti atua nkitarruot inyi."
1Corinthians15:18 Akae-- neimina si ninje looirurate tiatua Kristos."
1Corinthians15:19 Teni kianyu Kristos tiatua ena puan ake-- nikira yook laisinak too ltung'anak pookin."
1Corinthians15:20 Ore taata etopiwuo Kristos too lootuata nera ol elukunya loo looirura.
1Corinthians15:21 Amu oltung'ani obo oaua enkea-- naa oltung'ani obo oaua empiunoto oo lootuata."
1Corinthians15:22 Amu anaa petuata ninje pookin te Adam-- neijia epuoi aaitopiu pookin te Kristos."
1Corinthians15:23 Kake oltung'ani pookin tʼerisioroto enye: Ol elukunya Kristos-- tekurum loora le Kristos tʼelotunoto enye--"
1Corinthians15:24 tekurum enkiting'oto-- teni eitarasaki ninye Engai o Papa enkarsishu-- neidip enkitoria pookin o engolon o enkidimata pookin."
1Corinthians15:25 Meata kata nemeitorisho ninye metabana nepik ilmang'ati lenyena pookin abori oo nkejek enyena.
1Corinthians15:26 Ore olmang'atinda obaiye opuoi aaidip-- naa enkea."
1Corinthians15:27 Amu etipika pookin abori oo nkejek enyena. Teni ejo-- etipikaki pookin abori-- neibalunye ajo nemetii ilo otipika pookin abori enkitoria enye."
1Corinthians15:28 Kake teni etii pookin abori enkitoria enye-- te ina kata nening' si Oinoti ilo otipika pookin abori enkitoria enye-- peiye eaku Engai pookin tiatua pookin."
1Corinthians15:29 Anai kaji eiko lelo ooibatisi tʼolbae loo lootuata-- teni mepiu lootuata katukul? Ainyo peibatisi tʼolbae lenye?"
1Corinthians15:30 Nikitii yook enemeserian ngolong'i pookin?
1Corinthians15:31 Esipa-- tʼenkitadararoto naata te Kristos Yesus-- Olaitoriani lang'-- ae engolong' pookin."
1Corinthians15:32 Ten aa tʼempukunoto oo ltung'anak ataarare lowuarak te Efesos-- kaa dupoto aata te ina? Teni mepiu lootuata: „Mataam nikiok-- amu kituata taisere!“"
1Corinthians15:33 Eminjo eimalimalie ndai. Eitarruo ilderrat torrok rregieita sidan.
1Corinthians15:34 Enyeito osupatei-- emias ntorrok! Amu etii kulekai lemeyolo Engai oo toki; ajo ena aitukurru ndai."
1Corinthians15:35 Ore eikilikwan oltung'ani: Kaji eikuni teni eitopiuni lootuata? Kalo sesen epuonunye?
1Corinthians15:36 Iye-- lemodai-- enisuaia mepiu-- teni mee."
1Corinthians15:37 Ore enisuaia-- mera ninye osesen-- oaku tekurum-- kake embeu ake-- anaa en entapa arashu nabo oo nkulie pookin."
1Corinthians15:38 Kake Engai naisho osesen anaa peyeu ninye openy-- neisho pookin nabo too mbeun osesen lenye."
1Corinthians15:39 Nkiri pookin mera enkiring'o nabo; kake engai en oo ltung'anak-- engai en oo ntaritik-- engai en oo singir."
1Corinthians15:40 Netii seseni le shumata o seseni lʼenkop.
1Corinthians15:41 Eata engolong' engai kilang'et-- neata olapa engai kilang'et; kake epaasha olakira obo tʼolekai tʼenkilang'et."
1Corinthians15:42 Neija eaku empiunoto oo lootuata. Eisuari tiatua entiinoto narruoio neitopiuni tiatua entiinoto nemerruoio.
1Corinthians15:43 Eisuari tiatua entiinoto emenata-- neitopiuni tiatua entiinoto enkitook. Eisuari tiatua enjalan-- neitopiuni tiatua engolon."
1Corinthians15:44 Eisuari osesen lʼenkishon-- neitopiuni osesen lʼemumuaishu. Ten etii osesen lʼenkishon-- netii si osesen lʼemumuaishu."
1Corinthians15:45 Anaa petisiraki: Etaa oltung'ani lʼenkiterata Adam oltau oishiu; neaku ilo Adam lʼenkiting'oto Olmumua loisho empuan.
1Corinthians15:46 Kake mera osesen lʼemumuaishu ol enkiterata-- kake ol enkishon-- nesuj ol emumuaishu."
1Corinthians15:47 Ore oltung'ani lʼenkiterata eing'ua enkop naa ol enterit; ore oltung'ani liare-- neing'ua shumata."
1Corinthians15:48 Anaa peikununo ele lʼenterit-- neijia si etiu lʼenterit; eneikununo ele le shumata-- neijia si eikununo kulo le shumata."
1Corinthians15:49 Anaa peitanapa emua e ilo lʼenterit-- neijia si kipuo aanap emua e ilo le shumata."
1Corinthians15:50 Kake ajo ele rorei-- lalashera: meidim nkiri o osarge aatujung'u enkarsishu Engai; nemejung'u naarruoio nena nemerruoio."
1Corinthians15:51 Eng'orai-- aliki ndai emikio: Mikipuo pookin aairura-- kake epuoi aaitaal yook pookin;"
1Corinthians15:52 neaku neijia nabokata anaa tʼenkirriabata engong'u-- teni eoshi emowuo enkiting'oto. Amu eru emowuo neinyototo lootuata eata empuan nemerruoio-- neitaali yook."
1Corinthians15:53 Amu meata kata nemeishop ena narruoio enemerruoio-- ore ena nae-- neishop ina nemee."
1Corinthians15:54 Teni eishop ena narruoio enemerruoio nelaishop ena nae enemee-- nelaaku ororei etisiraki:"
1Corinthians15:55 Etoijoiyoki enkea tiatua engilunoto. Kaji etii-- enkea-- engilunoto ino? Kaji etii-- enkea-- olkikarret lino?"
1Corinthians15:56 Kake era olkikarret lʼenkea enkitarruoto-- nera engolon enkitarruoto nkitanapat."
1Corinthians15:57 Ashe Engai naisho yook engilunoto tʼOlaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos!
1Corinthians15:58 Onaa-- lalashera lainei lanyor-- entuunoto-- eming'unung'un-- entopon naleng' aaitobir oshi enkyas Olaitoriani-- iyololo-- aajo mera enyamali inyi en e pesho tiatua Olaitoriani."
1Corinthians16:1 Ore tʼolbae lʼesotore oo ngoshola-- peishori sinyat-- enkuna neijia anaa paitanapa si sirito naatii Galatia."
1Corinthians16:2 Tʼengolong' elukunya enjuma pookin-- njepik pookin too ndai neshumaki kion enanyorru-- pemetii enkitaunoto oo ngoshola-- teni alotu."
1Corinthians16:3 Ore teni abau-- nairriwaa lelo ligelulu ndai oopeny-- te nebo o mpala-- peaki ninje nkishoorot inyi Yerusalem."
1Corinthians16:4 Ore teni enare nalo si nanu-- nepuo ninje te nebo o nanu."
1Corinthians16:5 Kake alotu enitiiti ndai-- teni aimua Makedonia-- amu aimu Makedonia."
1Corinthians16:6 Abik too ndai enkiti kata arashu si enkata oloirujuruj-- pekintarere ndai nanu ewueji enalo nanu."
1Corinthians16:7 Amu mayeu naduare ndai taata tʼolototo lai-- kake ajo nanu alabik enkata naje te nebo o ndai-- teni enyorru Olaitoriani."
1Corinthians16:8 Kake abik te Efesos metabaiki Pentekoste--"
1Corinthians16:9 amu aatabolokoki enkishomi kitok naau ilmomo kumok-- netii si ilmang'ati."
1Corinthians16:10 Teni elotu Timoteos-- eng'orai-- peton te nebo o ndai metii enkuretishu; amu eitobir enkyas Olaitoriani anaa nanu openy."
1Corinthians16:11 Njoo memen o obo ninye. Entario ninye tʼeseriani-- pelotu enatii; amu aanyita ninye te nebo o lelo alashera."
1Corinthians16:12 Ore tʼolbae le Apolos-- olalashe lang'-- entayolo-- aajo atididing'a ninye naleng'-- pelotu enitiiti ndai te nebo o lalashera; kake eitu eyeu nelotu taata-- kake elotu teni etumoki."
1Corinthians16:13 Enjololoto-- entasheito tʼenkirukoto-- nitiuu anaa leak-- entagol!"
1Corinthians16:14 Entobira ntokitin pookin tʼenyorrata.
1Corinthians16:15 Aitadamu ndai-- lalashera-- piyolouu engaji e Stefanos-- amu ninje ilmomo lʼelukunya te Akaya nepik aten atua enkisyayare oo sinyat."
1Corinthians16:16 Entoning' ninje ooba nji o pookin looitobir enkyas nenyamalu te nebo.
1Corinthians16:17 Ang'ida tʼolbae lʼelotunoto e Stefanos o Fortunatos o Akaikos; amu ore pookin natong'oro too ndai-- eitabaitie ninje."
1Corinthians16:18 Amu eeng'ieng'ie Olmumua lai o ilmumuan linyi; akae-- entayolou ootiu neijia."
1Corinthians16:19 Eiroroki ndai sirito naatii Asia. Eiroroki ndai naleng' tiatua Olaitoriani Akwila o Priskila te nebo o esirit tʼengaji enye.
1Corinthians16:20 Eiroroki ndai lalashera pookin. Erorokinoto ndai aten tʼeng'ututata sinyati.
1Corinthians16:21 Ore nanu-- Paulos-- airoroki ndai tʼengaina ai."
1Corinthians16:22 Ore oltung'ani pookin lemenyor Olaitoriani-- njeaku anatema. Maran ata (eji: njedeki. Wou-- Olaitoriani lang'.)"
1Corinthians16:23 Njeboitare ndai eng'adunoto Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos.
1Corinthians16:24 Ore enyorrata ai-- njeboitare ndai pookin tiatua Kristos Yesus. Amen."
2Corinthians1:1 Paulos-- olairriwani le Yesus Kristos tʼeyeunoto Engai-- o olalashe Timoteos: en esirit Engai natii Korintos ena palai-- te nebo o sinyat pookin tiatua Akaia nalulungʼa."
2Corinthians1:2 Njeboitare ndai engʼadunoto o eseriani naingʼua Engai-- Papa lang'-- o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos."
2Corinthians1:3 Njeitadarari Engai o Menye lʼOlaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos-- lora Papa lʼeng'adunoto o Engai enkilejilejata."
2Corinthians1:4 Eilejilej yook tiatua enkilishoto ang' pookin-- pikindim aailejileja si yook kulo lootii atua enkilishoto pookin tʼenkilejilejata nailejilejie Engai yook."
2Corinthians1:5 Amu anaa pepona sinaitin le Kristos too yook-- neijia nepona si enkilejilejata nailejilejie yook Kristos."
2Corinthians1:6 Teni kitum yook enkilishoto-- neaku enkilejilejata o enkitopuata inyi; teni eilejileji yook-- neaku enkilejilejata inyi-- teni ing'iriri lelo sinaitin anaa pking'iri si yook."
2Corinthians1:7 Nikiata eng'idaroto nagol tʼolbae linyi-- tiaraki nikiyolo-- aajo anaa ping'aring'ara nkisilot-- neijia si enkilejilejata."
2Corinthians1:8 Amu mikiyeu nimiyololo-- lalashera-- mbaak osina lang' nikinoto te Asia-- njere einepua yook olemikindimaa-- peking'arrirrore empuan ang' si--"
2Corinthians1:9 nikiata yook enkigwena enkea tiatua aten. Etaa nona-- pemiking'idare yook aten-- kake Engai naitopiu lootuata;"
2Corinthians1:10 eitopua yook tʼenkea naba nji-- neton eitopok yook engolong' pookin; nikianyita ninye ajo elaitopok yook baiki akenya--"
2Corinthians1:11 tʼeretokinoto inyi-- teni isayakiki yook-- peliki iltung'anak kumok ashe tʼolbae lʼeng'adunoto naishooki yook."
2Corinthians1:12 Ore enkitadararoto ang' naa ina: eijakenu oltoilo lʼoltau lang'-- aajo tʼesinyatishu o tʼesipata Engai-- neme tʼeng'eno entung'anishu-- kake tʼeng'adunoto Engai-- kitilimanate tiatua ele maa-- naleng' too ndai."
2Corinthians1:13 Amu eitu kisiraki ndai nkulie neme nena nisomama ana niyolouu-- nairuk ajo ipuopuo aatayolou yook metabaiki enkiting'oto-- neijia anaa pitayoloutuo yook tʼematua."
2Corinthians1:14 Amu kira yook enkitadararoto inyi-- neijia anaa pirara si ndai enkitadararoto ang' atua engolong' Olaitoriani Yesus."
2Corinthians1:15 Ore tiatua ena ng'idaroto najo te ina kata alotu enitiiti-- pintokiki aatum enkishooroto--"
2Corinthians1:16 naimaa ndai alo Makedonia-- naitoki arrinyokino ndai aing'ua Makedonia-- pikintarere aaitabaiki Yudaya."
2Corinthians1:17 Ore adamu nena-- kaing'ashaiye? Arashu ketaa noo nkiri natayeuo? Me neijia. Kake era ee ee-- ore me naa me-- te nanu."
2Corinthians1:18 Kake supat Engai-- tiaraki neitu eaku nikirorie ndai ee o me--"
2Corinthians1:19 kake ore Oinoti lʼEngai likinosutua nanu o Silvanos o Timoteos too ndai-- neitu eaku ee o me-- kake etaa ee tiatua ninye."
2Corinthians1:20 Amu era nkisiligat Engai pookin ee te ninye-- neaku Amen te ninye-- peitadarari Engai tʼolbae lang'."
2Corinthians1:21 Kake Engai ninye naitagolo yook te nebo o ndai tiatua Kristos-- neel yook--"
2Corinthians1:22 nepik ninye yook olmishire neisho yook enkiterunoto Olmumua tiatua iltauja lang'.
2Corinthians1:23 Naipot nanu Engai-- peaku oljakeni te shumata oltau lai-- ajo aing'urrie ndai-- tiaraki neitu aitoki alotu enitiiti ndai engalo Korintos."
2Corinthians1:24 Neme-- pikintore yook enkirukoto inyi-- kake kira laretok Eng'ida inyi-- amu intasheshe ndai tiatua enkirukoto."
2Corinthians2:1 Kake atejo-- paiko neijia-- pamaitoki alotu tʼenkilishoto enitiiti ndai."
2Corinthians2:2 Amu teni ailishie nanu ndai-- ang'ai laaiting'id nanu-- teni me ilo lailishie?"
2Corinthians2:3 Onaa-- atisiraka ndai nona-- peiye-- teni alotu-- matum enkilishoto too lelo lemeata kata namang'idare ninje; amu airukore ndai pookin-- ajo ore eng'ida ai-- naa eng'ida inyi si."
2Corinthians2:4 Amu tʼosina kitok o emion oltau atisiraka ndai-- o too lkiyo kumok: neme pitumutumu ndai enkilishoto-- kake piyolouu enyorrata kitok naata too ndai."
2Corinthians2:5 Ore teni eishoo oltung'ani enkilishoto-- neitu aailishie nanu-- kake eilishie tʼematua-- — pamairoshiye — ndai pookin."
2Corinthians2:6 Kake ebaiki oltung'ani otiu neijia-- teni einoto ninye earata naba nji too ltung'anak kumok;"
2Corinthians2:7 enaikash-- teni iponipono aapalaki ndai ninye nilejilejeje oltau lenye pemeimisori ninye tiatua enkilishoto nalang'."
2Corinthians2:8 Akae-- adiding' ndai-- pintokiki ndai aanyor ninye."
2Corinthians2:9 Amu atisiraka ndai-- patum atujurro ndai-- ten aa iruko ndai tiatua mbaak pookin."
2Corinthians2:10 Ore ele ling'uaikiki ndai toki-- naing'uaiki si nanu. Amu ore nanu-- teni aing'uaiki oltung'ani toki-- naing'uaiki tʼolbae linyi tʼengomom Olaitoriani;"
2Corinthians2:11 pemegilu yook satan; amu metiu-- ajo mikiyolou yeunot enyena."
2Corinthians2:12 Ore palotu Troas ainosu euangelion e Kristos-- aatabolokoki kutukaji tiatua Olaitoriani--"
2Corinthians2:13 neitu aeng'ieng'a tʼolmumua lai-- tiaraki neitu atum Titos-- olalashe lai; kake kintanapate o ninje-- naing'ua ninje ajing' Makedonia."
2Corinthians2:14 Nikiliki Engai ashe naisho yook oshi ake engilunoto tiatua Kristos-- nebolu erropili eyolounoto enye too yook too wuejitin pookin."
2Corinthians2:15 Amu tʼEngai kira yook erropili sidai e Kristos tiatua lelo oopok o tiatua lelo ooimin:
2Corinthians2:16 Too kulo kira erropili naing'ua enkea atua enkea-- kake too lekua erropili naing'ua empuan atua empuan. Naa ang'ai oidipakine too kuna baak?"
2Corinthians2:17 Amu mikitiu yook anaa ilkumok-- ooitarruo ororei lʼEngai-- kake kinosu anaa lʼesipata ooing'ua Engai nikitii tʼengomom Engai atua Kristos."
2Corinthians3:1 Ke kitang'asa aaitoki aaitadaraa aten? Arashu kiyeu anaa looje-- mpala enkitadararoto too ndai?"
2Corinthians3:2 Ndai empalai ang' natisiraki tiatua iltauja lang'-- nayoloi neisomai too ltung'anak pookin;"
2Corinthians3:3 tiaraki neibalunyeki ndai-- aajo irara empalai e Kristos naitobiraki tʼenkisyayare ang'; eitu esiri tʼerokan-- kake tʼOlmumua lʼEngai naishiu-- me tiatua soito dapashi oogol-- kake tiatua soito loo nkiri loo ltauja."
2Corinthians3:4 Kiata eng'idaroto naba nji te Kristos atua Engai--"
2Corinthians3:5 me tiaraki nikira toki te aten nikidamu anaa te aten-- kake eing'ua enkidimata ang' Engai"
2Corinthians3:6 naishoo yook maidimai anaa laisyayak lʼosotua ng'ejuk-- me lʼesirata-- kake lʼOlmumua; amu ear esirata metua-- kake eisho Olmumua empuan."
2Corinthians3:7 Kake teni eata enkisyayare enkea tiatua sirat-- natabatuaki too soito-- enkitook-- neitu eidim baiki nkera Israel aaing'orai engomom e Mose tʼolbae lʼenkitook namuta engomom enye--"
2Corinthians3:8 me naleng' eitoki aata enkisyayare Olmumua enkitook?
2Corinthians3:9 Amu teni eata enkisyayare endiata enkitook-- me naleng' epon aata enkisyayare esupato enkitook?"
2Corinthians3:10 Amu meikeni enkitook e ina matua naitaai opa kitok tʼolbae lʼena kitook nalang' tukul.
2Corinthians3:11 Amu teni eata enda naiting'-- enkitook-- me naleng' eata ena nabik-- enkitook?"
2Corinthians3:12 Akae-- ore pikiata eanyunoto naba nji-- meata kata nimikiata enkiteunoto kitok--"
2Corinthians3:13 nimikintobir neijia anaa Mose-- lotipika eopet shumata engomom enye-- pemeing'oraa nkera Israel enkiting'oto ena naiting';"
2Corinthians3:14 kake eitiming'anaki ndamunot enye-- amu ebik metabaiki ena olong' e taata ena opet shumata enkisoma osotua musana-- neitu eboluni-- amu eiting'ieki tiatua Kristos;"
2Corinthians3:15 kake ebik metabaiki taata-- oshi teni eisomai Mose-- eopet shumata oo ltauja lenye."
2Corinthians3:16 Kake oshi-- teni eibelekenyakino oltung'ani Olaitoriani-- neitauni eopet."
2Corinthians3:17 Nera Olaitoriani Olmumua; ore enetii Olmumua lʼOlaitoriani-- naa ine etii elakunoto."
2Corinthians3:18 Kake king'oraa yook pookin tʼengomom nemeata eopet enkitook Olaitoriani anaa tʼenking'oret-- nepuoi aaitaal yook te ina mua enkitook atua enkitook-- anaa tʼOlaitoriani ora Olmumua."
2Corinthians4:1 Tiaraki nikiata ena kisyayare-- anaa pikinoto eng'adunoto-- nimikinaura--"
2Corinthians4:2 kake kiany nekua baak emikio naaitukurru-- nimikintobir tʼolosek-- nimikintaal ororei lʼEngai tʼelejare; kake tʼembolunoto esipata kintadol aten oltoilo loo ltauja loo ltung'anak pookin tʼengomom Engai."
2Corinthians4:3 Akae-- teni eisudori lomon lʼeng'ida ang'-- neisudori too kulo loopuo aaimin--"
2Corinthians4:4 neitamodono engai ele maa eng'eno oo lemeiruk-- pemeilang'aki ninje enkilang'et oo lomon lʼeng'ida o lʼenkitook e Kristos-- lora emua Engai."
2Corinthians4:5 Amu mikinosu yook aten-- kake Kristos Yesus-- lora Olaitoriani-- nikira yook laisyayak linyi te Yesus."
2Corinthians4:6 Amu Engai najo: Njeilang'isho enkilang'et tʼenaimin-- ninye nailang'ishe tiatua iltauja lang'-- aisho eong'an nikiyolounye enkitook Engai tiatua engomom e Kristos."
2Corinthians4:7 Kake kiata kuna masaa kiroteti too ntokitin esarng'ab-- peaku enkidimata naitobirisho en Engai-- neme enang'."
2Corinthians4:8 Kitum osina too ngaloli pookin-- kake miking'ashaa; niking'aing'ai-- kake mikipalaa;"
2Corinthians4:9 eitamei yook-- kake merikinoi yook; enang'ari yook enkop-- kake mikiimin."
2Corinthians4:10 Kinap enkata pookin tʼosesen lang' enkea Olaitoriani Yesus-- peibalunye empuan Olaitoriani Yesus tʼosesen lang'."
2Corinthians4:11 Amu ore yook likinjiu-- neishori yook enkata pookin-- matuata tʼolbae le Yesus-- petum si aibalunye empuan e Yesus tiatua seseni lang' ooe."
2Corinthians4:12 Akae-- eitobirisho enkea tiatua yook-- kake empuan tiatua ndai."
2Corinthians4:13 Ore pikiata Olmumua obo lʼenkirukoto-- anaa petisiraki: Airuko-- tiaraki nairo-- nikiruk nikintoki aairo."
2Corinthians4:14 Nikiyolo ele oitopiwuo Olaitoriani Yesus-- neitopiu si yook te Yesus-- neitasheye yook te nebo o ndai."
2Corinthians4:15 Amu eaku pookin tʼolbae linyi-- peitadaraa eng'adunoto kitok Engai-- eliki ilkumok Engai ashe."
2Corinthians4:16 Akae-- mikinaura-- kake ten ake eimin oltung'ani lang' li oriong'-- neitaai ng'ejuk oli atua ngolong'i pookin."
2Corinthians4:17 Ore enkilishoto ang' nanyanyukie enkirriabata nelelek-- neitaa pikitum yook enkitook oo nkatan pookin naa kitok naleng'--"
2Corinthians4:18 yook limiking'oraa nalio-- kake nemelio. Amu eim nalio-- nebik nemelio nkatan pookin."
2Corinthians5:1 Kake kiyolo yook-- aajo teni erratanyi engaji ang' olototo ena kop-- kiata enjetata natesheta Engai-- engaji oo nkatan pookin te shumata-- neitu eitobiri too ngaik."
2Corinthians5:2 Amu kiang' si yook te ina niking'war-- peishopokini yook entonata' e shumata;"
2Corinthians5:3 ore baiki-- teni eishopokini yook-- pimikilioi mikinjopo."
2Corinthians5:4 Amu ore pikitii atua engaji olototo-- nikiang' eiroshikini yook; mikiyeu neoruni yook tiatua ninye ilkilani-- kake peitokini aaishopoki yook-- peimisori nʼenkea tiatua empuan."
2Corinthians5:5 Ore oloitobira yook tiatua ina-- nera Engai-- naishoo yook errimata Olmumua."
2Corinthians5:6 Akae-- kintagoluo yook oshi naleng' too ltauja nikiyolo-- aajo teni kimany atua osesen-- nimikimany atua Olaitoriani;"
2Corinthians5:7 amu kilimana yook tʼenkirukoto-- me tʼenking'orare;"
2Corinthians5:8 kake kintagoluo too ltauja nikinyor nelang'-- kimanyisho mikitii atua osesen-- pikimanyisho tʼenetii Olaitoriani."
2Corinthians5:9 Onaa-- kinyok-- kimanyisho arashu kindur-- peng'ida ninye too yook."
2Corinthians5:10 Amu meata kata nimikipuo aalioi tʼengomom olorika lʼenkigwena le Kristos-- peiye ea oltung'ani pookin naaitobira ninye tʼenkata empuan osesen-- naara sidan arashu ntorrok."
2Corinthians5:11 Kake tiaraki nikiyolo euriata Olaitoriani-- niking'urrie iltung'anak-- kake kimbalunye tʼEngai. Ang'idare-- ajo kimbalunye baiki tiatua oltoilo loo ltauja linyi."
2Corinthians5:12 Mikintoki aaitadaraa aten too ndai-- kake kinjo ndai entumokinoto-- pindimidimi aaitadarai aten tʼolbae lang'-- niatata enialikiki lelo ooitadararie aten naalio-- neme tʼoltau."
2Corinthians5:13 Amu teni kintalang'-- naa tʼolbae lʼEngai; ten aa kira ng'eni-- tʼolbae linyi."
2Corinthians5:14 Amu eisirkonoo yook enyorrata e Kristos; kingwenu ena-- aajo etua obo tʼolbae loo pookin-- akae-- etuata ninje pookin;"
2Corinthians5:15 etua ninye tʼolbae loo pookin-- peiye meishiuoki looishiu aten-- kake ele lotua tʼolbae lenye nepiu."
2Corinthians5:16 Neijia mikiyolo yook-- eiter taata-- oltung'ani o obo tʼenkiring'o; teni kitayoloutuo baiki Kristos tʼenkiring'o-- kake mikintoki aayolou taata."
2Corinthians5:17 Neijia-- teni etii oltung'ani atua Kristos-- etaa enkitobirata ng'ejuk; eima musan-- ng'orai-- etaa pookin ng'ejuko."
2Corinthians5:18 Kake eing'ua pookin Engai naitobirakinye yook kion te Kristos-- neisho yook enkisyayare enkitobirakinoto;"
2Corinthians5:19 amu etii Engai atua Kristos neitobirakinye kion olmaa nemeikenaki ninje lang'at enye-- nepik atua yook ororei lʼenkitobirakinoto."
2Corinthians5:20 Akae-- kira yook taata lairriwak tʼewueji e Kristos-- amu Engai nadiding'isho too yook; kisaisho tʼewueji e Kristos: Enjoo eitobirakini ndai o Engai."
2Corinthians5:21 Amu eitaa ninye ele lemeyolo enkitarruoto-- enkitarruoto-- tʼewueji ang'-- pikiaku yook esupato Engai tiatua ninye."
2Corinthians6:1 Kididing' ndai anaa loong'ar enkyas inyi-- piming'amumu pesho eng'adunoto Engai--"
2Corinthians6:2 amu ejo: Aatoning'o iye tʼenkata sidai naataretoko iye tʼengolong' enkitopuata. Eng'orai-- etaa taata enkata sidai. Eng'orai-- etaa taata engolong' enkitopuata."
2Corinthians6:3 Mikinjo yook oltung'ani o obo enkikoboto o nabo-- pemesuli enkyas ang'--"
2Corinthians6:4 kake kintadol aten tʼentoki pookin anaa laisyayak lʼEngai: tiatua olng'iria kitok-- tiatua nkilishot-- tiatua sinaitin-- tiatua nkatan naagol--"
2Corinthians6:5 tiatua arat-- tiatua ienat-- tiatua nkiposhiposhat-- tiatua nkyasin naagol-- tiatua njololot-- tiatua mpukorot--"
2Corinthians6:6 tiatua enkishaa-- tiatua eyolounoto-- tiatua enyuakinoto-- tiatua emborran-- tiatua Olmumua Sinyati-- tiatua enyorrata nemeitusupatuo--"
2Corinthians6:7 tiatua ororei lʼesipata-- tiatua engolon Engai-- too nareta esupato oo ntatenia o nkedyanyia--"
2Corinthians6:8 tʼenkitook o tʼemenata-- tʼeimakinoto torrono o tʼeimakinoto sidai-- anaa laitapaashak-- kake anaa lasipak--"
2Corinthians6:9 anaa lemeyoloi-- kake anaa looyolouni; anaa looe-- kake kinjiu; anaa looari-- kake mearai metuata;"
2Corinthians6:10 anaa looilish-- kake loong'ida oshi; anaa laisinak-- kake looitudup ilkumok; anaa lemeata toki-- kake looata pookin."
2Corinthians6:11 Oi ndai Ilkorintioi-- etabolokoki ndai nkutukie ang'-- elala iltauja lang'."
2Corinthians6:12 Eitu eironyi ndai tiatua yook-- kake eironyi ndai tiatua iltauja linyi oopeny."
2Corinthians6:13 Airorie ndai anaa nkera ainei-- pinkoko anaa yook neboli si iltauja linyi."
2Corinthians6:14 Emiaku looeni te nebo o lemeiruk too nemeitoriori. Amu kaa kidikidikoto eata esupato o empaashata oo nkitanapat? Kaa kidikidikoto eata eong'an o enaimin?
2Corinthians6:15 Kaa kitushulata eata Kristos o Belial? Arashu kaa ng'arata eata oloiruk o olemeiruk?
2Corinthians6:16 Kaa risioroto eata engaji sinyati Engai o muain? Amu irara ndai engaji sinyati Engai naishiu anaa pejo Engai: Alamany atua ninje nalalimana tʼempolos enye-- nepuo aaku ninje olorere lai."
2Corinthians6:17 Onaa: Entupukutu tʼempolos enye-- entirishunye-- ejo Olaitoriani-- emiporoo nemeisuja; nalang'amu nanu ndai--"
2Corinthians6:18 nalaaku too ndai Minyi-- nipuopuo aaku ndai te nanu laiyok lainei o ntoiye ainei-- ejo Olaitoriani tʼengolon pookin."
2Corinthians7:1 Akae-- ore pikiata kuna kisiligat-- lanyor-- maisuja aten tʼentibilishu pookin enkiring'o o en olmumua-- pikibaiki esinyatishu tiatua enkuretishu Engai."
2Corinthians7:2 Entang'amu yook. Eitu kintarriki oltung'ani-- neitu kiony olekai-- neitu kinkonyu olekai."
2Corinthians7:3 Majo nena aigwenaki ndai. Atang'asa duo ajo-- njere itiiti atua iltauja lang'-- pikie anai kipok te nebo."
2Corinthians7:4 Airorie ndai tʼenjipai kitok; naata nkitadararot kumok tʼolbae linyi; aaiganya enkilejilejata-- napon aata eng'ida naleng' tiatua osina lang' pookin."
2Corinthians7:5 Amu ore kietuo yook atua Makedonia-- eitu eata enkiring'o ang' eng'ieng'ata tukul-- kake eilishieki yook too ngaloli pookin: etii boo arat netii atua nkuretishuitin."
2Corinthians7:6 Kake eilejileja yook Engai nailejilej looitadou aten-- tʼembaunoto e Titos;"
2Corinthians7:7 me t'embaunoto enye ake-- kake baiki tʼenkilejilejata nailejilejieki ninye too ndai-- neinosaki ninye yook errimata inyi-- enkishirata inyi-- enyuata inyi tʼolbae lai-- napon baiki ang'ida."
2Corinthians7:8 Amu teni ailishie ndai tiatua embarua-- mairridu; ten ake airridu-- tiaraki nadol-- ajo eilishie ndai ina barua enkiti kata ake--"
2Corinthians7:9 nang'ida taata-- me tiaraki nilisho-- kake tiaraki nilisho pialala; amu eilishieki ndai anaa peyeu Engai-- peiye mitumutumu entorroni o nabo too yook."
2Corinthians7:10 Amu eishoru enkilishoto anaa peyeu Engai enkitaalata e atua enkitopuata nemeirriduni; kake eishoru enkilishoto olmaa enkea.
2Corinthians7:11 Eng'orai-- tiaraki neilishieki ndai anaa peyeu Engai-- keba aa enyuata natupukunye-- te nebo o emitikinoto-- o engoro o enkuretishu o errimata o engilata e tau o elaakinoto; intadua ndai aten aa supati tukul tʼena bae."
2Corinthians7:12 Ore patisiraka ndai-- eitu asiraki ndai tʼolbae le ilo oitarruoiye-- anai tʼolbae le ilo otemenaiyoki-- kake peibalunye enyuata inyi tʼolbae lang' tʼengomom Engai;"
2Corinthians7:13 too nona baak eilejilejaki yook iltauja lang'. Tʼenkilejilejata ang' etopone eng'ida ang' tʼolbae lʼeng'ida e Titos; amu eeng'ieng'ieki Olmumua lenye too ndai pookin.
2Corinthians7:14 Amu ore enaitaa ndai kituak te ninye-- neitu akurru; kake anaa esipata pookin natolikio nanu ndai-- neijia eitisipaki si enkitadararoto ang' tʼengomom e Titos."
2Corinthians7:15 Ore enyorrata oltau lenye-- naa kitok naleng' atua ndai-- teni edamu ninye enkirukoto inyi pookin-- enitang'amutua ninye tʼenkuretishu o tʼenkikirikirata."
2Corinthians7:16 Ang'ida-- amu aanyunye ndai ntokitin sidan pookin."
2Corinthians8:1 Aitadamu ndai-- lalashera-- eng'adunoto Engai naishooki tiatua sirito e Makedonia."
2Corinthians8:2 Ten ake etaa sapuk osina otetemieki ninje-- nepona naleng' eng'ida enye; ore ten aa ninje aisinak loora-- neishooio nkumok tʼesupato."
2Corinthians8:3 Aijakenoki ninje-- ajo tʼenkidimata enye-- kake enalang' enkidimata enye-- eitobirakinote--"
2Corinthians8:4 nesai yook tʼenkilejilejata kitok-- peking'amu enkishooroto o eng'arata enkisyayare-- naitobirakitia sinyat."
2Corinthians8:5 Neme anaa pikitaanyutua-- kake etang'asa aaishooio aten Olaitoriani-- ore tekurum yook-- tʼeyeunoto Engai."
2Corinthians8:6 Onaa-- nikididing' Titos-- peiye-- anaa petang'asa asotu too ndai-- eitabaia si ina kishooroto."
2Corinthians8:7 Kake neijia anaa piatata enkumoi oo mbaak pookin-- tiatua enkirukoto o ororei o eyolounoto o enyuata o enyorrata inyi too yook-- neijia entonyok piponana si tʼena munyani."
2Corinthians8:8 Mairo aitanapu toki-- kake tiaraki natonyua ilkulekai-- natem si enyorata inyi-- anake eitoriori."
2Corinthians8:9 Amu iyololo eng'adunoto Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos-- ajo ninye adupani-- kake etaa aisinani tʼolbae linyi-- piakuku adupak tʼesinaishu enye."
2Corinthians8:10 Nyena eng'eno ai naliki ndai-- amu etumoki ndai-- tiaraki ninterutua tʼolari le ng'ole pokirare: me enkitobirata ake-- baiki eyeunoto."
2Corinthians8:11 Ore taata-- entabai enkitobirata inyi; anaa pitonyorra opa aatayeu-- neijia entaas si tʼerisioroto oo masaa inyi."
2Corinthians8:12 Amu teni enyorru oltung'ani-- neshipakinoi te ina naata-- me te ina nemeata."
2Corinthians8:13 Majo ena-- peiteneneng'i ilkulekai neiroshieki ndai-- kake perisioi."
2Corinthians8:14 Onaa-- enjoo etumoki endupoto inyi enang'oriki ninje ena kata-- petumoki si akenya endupoto enye enyorrata inyi-- perisioroi--"
2Corinthians8:15 anaa petisiraki: Ore ele oiturrurro nkumok-- nemeata enaleku; ore elde oiturrurro nkuti-- nemeng'oriki toki."
2Corinthians8:16 Ashe Engai naishorua enyuata naba nji tiatua oltau le Titos too ndai.
2Corinthians8:17 Amu etang'amua ninye eutata ang'-- kake eisarisara tʼenyorrata enye openy-- pelotu enitiiti ndai."
2Corinthians8:18 Kirriwaitie olalashe te nebo o ninye-- oitadarari tʼolbae lʼeuangelion tiatua sirito pookin."
2Corinthians8:19 Neme neijia ake-- kake etegelutua sirito ninye-- perubare yook t'olototo lang' tʼolbae lʼena munyani nikintobir-- peitaai Engai kitok nelioi olokiyo lang'."
2Corinthians8:20 Nikimitiki te ina-- pemeduaki oltung'ani yook ntorrok tʼolbae lʼena sotore nikintobir."
2Corinthians8:21 Amu king'as aadamu mbaak sidan-- neme tʼengomom Olaitoriani ake-- kake tʼengomom oo ltung'anak si."
2Corinthians8:22 Kirriwaitie te nebo o ninje ilo alashe lang'-- likitujurro too mbaak kumok aigil kumok-- aajo enyokita naleng'-- kake epon taata anyok."
2Corinthians8:23 King'idare ndai naleng'-- ten aa tʼolbae le Titos ora lʼemboitei ai neretoki ndai te nebo o nanu-- arashu tʼolbae loo lalashera lang' oora lairriwak loo sirito-- naa enkitook e Kristos."
2Corinthians8:24 Akae-- entaduai ninje enaibalunye enyorrata inyi o enkitadararoto ang' tʼolbae linyi-- baiki too ngomomitie oo sirito."
2Corinthians9:1 Ore mbaak e ina kisyayare naitaasi sinyat-- mayeu nasiraki ndai."
2Corinthians9:2 Amu ayolo eyeunoto inyi sidai-- naitadararie too kulo le Makedonia-- ajo ebik eitobirakino Akaia olari le ng'ole; neisis enyuata inyi ilkumok."
2Corinthians9:3 Nairriwaa lalashera-- pemeaku enkitadararoto ang' tʼolbae linyi en e pesho te ina toki-- nintobirakinono ndai anaa pairorie tʼolbae linyi;"
2Corinthians9:4 pemeaku-- teni epuonu iltung'anak le Makedonia te nebo o nanu-- nedol ndai-- aajo eitu ianyishosho-- nikikurru yook (pamajo; ndai) te ina kitadararoto."
2Corinthians9:5 Akae-- atejo-- meata kata namadiding' lalashera-- peiturukie aabaiki ndai neitobir ena mayani nitang'asa ndai aaisilig opa-- peidipakino anaa emayani-- neme anaa empiani."
2Corinthians9:6 Ajo nanu ena: Oloisuaia eng'or-- nelaisambu eng'or; oloisuaia osupatei-- nelaisambu osupatei."
2Corinthians9:7 Njeisho oltung'ani pookin anaa penyor tʼoltau-- me tʼenkilishoto arashu tʼengolon; amu enyor Engai olaishooroni oshipa."
2Corinthians9:8 Eidim aitaa Engai-- petii eng'adunoto pookin atua ndai-- peiye iatata oshi embaikinoto pookin tʼentoki pookin-- niponana naleng' tʼenkyas sidai pookin--"
2Corinthians9:9 anaa petisiraki: Eitarasaiye ninye naleng' neisho laisinak-- ebik esupato enye nkatan pookin."
2Corinthians9:10 Oloitarasaki embeu olaisuaroni-- nelaitarasaki baiki endaa nainosi-- nepon embeu inyi nelaitubulu ishot esupato inyi--"
2Corinthians9:11 pidupaii tiatua entoki pookin e atua emborrakinoto-- naitaaki Engai ashe too yook."
2Corinthians9:12 Amu ore enkisyayare ena sotore nemeidip ake enang'oriki sinyat-- kake epon si ina-- peliki ilkumok Engai ashe tʼolbae lʼena kisyayare supat--"
2Corinthians9:13 amu eitaa ninje Engai kitok tʼolbae lʼening'oto inyi nimbalunyenye euangelion e Kristos-- o tʼolbae lʼemborrakinoto e ina ng'arata ninjosho ninje o pookin;"
2Corinthians9:14 neng'war ndai tʼengomono enye neomonoki ndai tʼolbae lʼenkumoi emunyani Engai too ndai.
2Corinthians9:15 Njeishori Engai ashe t'enkishorunoto enye nemeimakinoi.
2Corinthians10:1 Ore nanu-- Paulos-- adiding ndai tʼengaripo o tʼemborran e Kristos-- lara oti-- teni atii e nebo o ndai-- kake ore alamita ndai-- napi too ndai."
2Corinthians10:2 Kake asai ndai-- emikisis-- papiju atii e nebo o ndai-- naiteunore te ina golon naaikenaki nanu iltung'anak-- looje-- loojo kilimana anaa peyeu nkiri."
2Corinthians10:3 Amu ten ake kipuo tiatua nkiri-- nimikiara too nareta oo nkiri."
2Corinthians10:4 Amu ore nareta ang'-- nemera noo nkiri-- kake eata engolon tʼEngai-- pikirratanyie naaikarraro."
2Corinthians10:5 Kintadou ndamunot o engadoro pookin naapare eyolounoto Engai-- nikiaru eng'eno pookin aitaa singan-- pening' Kristos."
2Corinthians10:6 Kindipakino-- pikilaaki eanyata pookin-- teni etabaiye ening'oto inyi."
2Corinthians10:7 Amaa-- ing'oraara ndai mbaak naatii oriong'? Teni etii oltung'ani ong'idare kion ajo ninye le Kristos-- njeitoki adamu si ninye ena-- ten aa ole Kristos ninye-- nikira si yook."
2Corinthians10:8 Ore ten emutu apon aitadararie kion engolon ang' naishoo yook Olaitoriani mateshet ndai neme tʼenkiminata-- anaata makurru;"
2Corinthians10:9 pamatiu anake ayeu naiture ndai too mpala.
2Corinthians10:10 Amu-- ejo-- eiroshi mpala enyena-- neitoki aata engolon; kake teni etii ninye tʼosesen-- neshal nemeata enaidim ororei lenye."
2Corinthians10:11 Ore olotiu neijia-- njedamu ena-- ajo anaa pikinkununo too rorei oo mpala teni mikitii-- naa neijia si kitiu yook tʼenkyas ang'-- ten aa kitii."
2Corinthians10:12 Amu mikinteu aatipik aten esiana oo lelo ooitadaraa aten nimikintorisiore ninje-- amu tiaraki naitorisiokino aten o aten neiken aten anaa iltung'anak loora-- nemeyolou toki."
2Corinthians10:13 Ore yook-- mikintadaraa aten aalang' entemet-- kake anaa perisiore entemet e ilo rregie otetemaka Engai yook-- pekibaiki si enitiiti ndai."
2Corinthians10:14 Amu mikilusoo yook naleng'-- anake eitu kibaiki enitiiti ndai. Kindipa aatabaiki ndai tʼeuangelion e Kristos."
2Corinthians10:15 Nimikintadaraa aten aalang' entemet tiatua nyamalareitin oo lkulekai-- nikiruk-- aajo teni ebulu enkirukoto inyi tiatua ndai-- pekipon yook tʼorregie lang'--"
2Corinthians10:16 nikinosaki euangelion si kulo oomanya idya matua too ndai-- nimikintadararie aten nona naaitobiraki tʼorregie loo lkulekai."
2Corinthians10:17 Kake ore Oloitadaraa kion-- njeitadaraa tiatua Olaitoriani."
2Corinthians10:18 Amu mera ele supat-- loitadaraa kion-- kake teni eitadaraa Olaitoriani ninye."
2Corinthians11:1 Eikash-- ten emutu ing'iriri peno emodaishu te nanu-- kake ajo-- ing'iriri sa."
2Corinthians11:2 Amu anyokita tʼolbae linyi tʼenyuata Engai. Amu atasayaka olmoruo obo-- patum atoriko entito supat ayaki Kristos."
2Corinthians11:3 Kake aureisho-- peiye-- anaa peteleja olopa asurai Eva tʼesungureishu enye-- eiminyeki si ndamunot inyi aaing'ua emborrakinoto e atua Kristos."
2Corinthians11:4 Amu ten emutu elotu obo-- neinosu olekai Yesus leitu kinosu yook-- arashu ing'amumu olekai mumua leitu ing'amumu-- arashu engai euangelion neitu eishori ndai-- anaata igirara."
2Corinthians11:5 Kake aiken nanu kion-- ajo maang'oriki toki too lelo airriwak „kituak“."
2Corinthians11:6 Ore ten aa mara ng'en too rorei-- namara neijia tiatua eyolounoto-- kake aibalunye too ndai tiatua mbaak pookin."
2Corinthians11:7 Kaitarruoiye-- tiaraki naitadouo kion-- peitaai ndai kituak? Amu ainosaka ndai euangelion Engai pesho--"
2Corinthians11:8 naoru nkulie sirito ang'amu olkwaje too ninje-- painosaki ndai."
2Corinthians11:9 Ore eton atii opa e nebo o ndai tʼeng'oroto ai-- eitu aek olekai tung ani; amu ore pepuonu lalashera aaing'ua Makedonia-- aataretokitio eng'oroto ai; o tiatua mbaak pookin atorripo kion-- pamairoshiki ndai-- narrip kion aiko neijia."
2Corinthians11:10 Anaa esipata natii atua nanu-- metii oltung'ani oidim aiboi enkitadararoto ai naata tiatua loshon le Akaia."
2Corinthians11:11 Tʼolbae le nyoo? Tiaraki namanyor nanu ndai? Eyolo Engai.
2Corinthians11:12 Kake enayeu naitobir-- alaitobir-- padung' ororei loo lelo ooing'oru entoki naitadararie-- aajo etiu ninje anaa yook."
2Corinthians11:13 Amu ore iltung'anak ooba nji-- oora lairriwak lʼelejare naa laitobirak looata olosek-- neitaai aten aaku lairriwak le Kristos."
2Corinthians11:14 Nemeiputukunyisho; amu eitaai kion satan openy aaku olmalaika lʼenkilang'et.
2Corinthians11:15 Onaa-- mera entoki sapuk-- teni eitaai aten laisyayak lenyena aatiu anaa lainosunok lʼesupato; neaku enkiting'oto enye tʼerisioroto oo nkitobirat enye."
2Corinthians11:16 Aitoki ajo-- njere njoo mejo oltung'ani ajo amoda; teni me-- entang'amuaki anaa olmodai-- peiye si nanu aitadaraa kion peno."
2Corinthians11:17 Ore enajo taata-- malimu anaa tʼOlaitoriani-- kake anaa tʼemodaishu-- amu kitabaitie enkitadararoto."
2Corinthians11:18 Tiaraki naitadaraa ilkumok aten tʼolbae lʼenkiring'o-- nayeu naitadaraa kion si nanu."
2Corinthians11:19 Amu ing'iriakiki ilmoda tʼeng'ida-- nirara ndai ng'eni."
2Corinthians11:20 Ing'iriri-- teni eitaa ndai oltung'ani singan-- arashu teni einyal ndai-- arashu teni earaa ndai-- arashu teni egogong'oki ndai-- arashu teni ear ndai engomom inyi."
2Corinthians11:21 Airo tʼengilata enganyit-- anaa teni kishal yook. Ore entoki naimany oltung'ani-- (airo tʼemodaishu)-- naimany si nanu."
2Corinthians11:22 Kera Ilhebrayoi ninje? ara si nanu. Ke Israeli ninje? ara si nanu. Kera eishoi e Abraham? ara si nanu.
2Corinthians11:23 Kera laisyayak le Kristos? airo tʼemodaishu-- alusoo nanu. Atanyamala alang'; aataaraki aaitalang'; atii aigil kumok atua sinaitin enkea; aateenaki aaitalang;"
2Corinthians11:24 too Yudayoi atang'amua aigil imiet oshot artam neng'oru nabo;
2Corinthians11:25 naataaraki too lkikarreta aigil uni; naataaraki too soito kat nabo. Etigile embout natii aigil uni. Dama o kiarie atobiko tiatua enaiposha.
2Corinthians11:26 Tiatua lotot aigil kumok-- tiatua osina loo lkejek-- tiatua osina loo laisimak-- tiatua osina tʼentipat ai-- tiatua osina too lemeata Engai-- tiatua osina too ngang'itie-- tiatua osina ti ang'ata-- tiatua osina tʼolbalbal-- tiatua osina loo lalashera lʼelejare;"
2Corinthians11:27 tiatua nyamalareitin o nkyasin-- tiatua erripore aigil kumok-- tiatua olamei o enkure-- tiatua mpukorot kumok-- tiatua enkirobi o maishopo;"
2Corinthians11:28 metii nona tokitin neitu aipot-- naa enkyas naaek ngolong'i pookin o enkishilaroto oo sirito pookin."
2Corinthians11:29 Ang'ai oshal-- namashal nanu? Ang'ai oitapong'ori-- namairowua nanu?"
2Corinthians11:30 Teni meata kata namaitadaraa-- naitadaraa kion tʼolbae lʼenjalan ai."
2Corinthians11:31 Eyolo Engai o Menye lʼOlaitoriani Yesus-- otamayanaki nkatan pookin-- ajo malejisho."
2Corinthians11:32 Tiatua Damaskos etorripo olaigwenani kitok lʼolkarsis Aretas engang oo Ldamaskoi-- paaibung' nanu;"
2Corinthians11:33 naaitadoiyori tʼelusiet tiatua oltutua tʼesundai engang'-- napok ailany ngaik enyena."
2Corinthians12:1 Medupa-- paitadaraa kion-- kake ainosu peno nduarot o mbolunot Olaitoriani."
2Corinthians12:2 Ayolo oltung'ani tiatua Kristos-- neba too larin tomon o ong'wan — ten aa tiatua osesen-- mayolo; Engai nayolo — etanapaki ele metabaiki shumata e uni."
2Corinthians12:3 Nayolo ele tung'ani — ten aa tiatua osesen-- ten aa metii atua osesen-- mayolo; Engai nayolo —--"
2Corinthians12:4 ajo etanapaki atua emparadis nening' rorei lemeiroroi-- lemeidim oltung'ani aimaki."
2Corinthians12:5 Aitadaraa kion tʼele-- kake maitadaraa kion te nanu-- neme tʼemenatishu ai."
2Corinthians12:6 Amu ten emut ayeu naitadaraa kion-- anaata mamoda-- anaata alimu esipata; kake aitore kion-- pamaaitaa o obo kitok nelang' enadolita te nanu arashu enaning'ito te nanu."
2Corinthians12:7 Ore pamaikarrikar tʼolbae lʼenkumoi oo mbolunot-- aaishooki olkikarret tiatua osesen-- olmalaika le satan-- paaar too ndapi-- pamatum aikarrikarra."
2Corinthians12:8 Ore te ilo aidipa atasaya Olaitoriani aigil uni-- paaing'ua ninye nanu."
2Corinthians12:9 Naajoki ninye nanu: Kibaiki eng'adunoto ai-- amu ebaia engolon ai tiatua emenatishu. Onaa-- eikash naleng'-- teni aitadarrarie kion emenatishu ai-- pemany engolon e Kristos atua nanu."
2Corinthians12:10 Onaa-- ang'ida tiatua menatishuitin-- tiatua menat-- tiatua nkisilot-- tiatua mirat-- tiatua sinaitin-- tʼolbae le Kristos. Amu teni aaku menati-- naata te ina kata engolon."
2Corinthians12:11 Ataa olmodai tʼenkitadararoto-- nikiarakiki ndai nanu. Kake anaata eikash-- paaitaai kitok too ndai. Amu mara oti too lelo airriwak „kituak“-- ten ake mara toki."
2Corinthians12:12 Amu eitobiraki ilponot lʼolairriwani tiatua ndai tʼolng'iria pookin-- o too nkitaduat-- o too nkiputukunyot-- o too nkidimat."
2Corinthians12:13 Ainyo natong'orikia ndai too nona kulie sirito-- neme ilo rorei ake-- ajo eitu airoshiki ndai? Entung'aiyoki nanu ena torroni."
2Corinthians12:14 Eng'orai-- aidipakino palotu enkata e uni enitiiti ndai-- namairoshiki nanu ndai. Amu maing'oru nkun inyi-- kake ndai oopeny. Amu meiteng'elaki nkera lootoiutuo masaa sidan-- kake lootoiutuo nkera enye."
2Corinthians12:15 Nayeu naishooio ntokitin ainei naitoki aishooio nanu kion t'eng'ida kitok tʼolbae lʼenkishui inyi; ten aa anyor nanu ndai naleng'-- nikinyorrinyorro nanu aaitong'or."
2Corinthians12:16 Kake njeaku neijia-- peitu aek nanu ndai; kake tiaraki nara osunguroi-- aibung'a ndai tʼolosek."
2Corinthians12:17 Arashu kaikonyaiye entoki oltung'ani tʼengaina e obo loo kulo lairriwaka ndai?
2Corinthians12:18 Atididing'a Titos nairriwaa olalashe obo te nebo o ninye. Keikonyarie Titos ndai toki? Eitu kilimana tʼolmumua obo? Ana eitu kipuoiye eroruata nabo?
2Corinthians12:19 Intokiki aajo ndai-- njere kimitu yook too ndai? Kirorie tiatua Kristos tʼengomom Engai; kake eaku kuna pookin-- lanyor lainei-- pesheti ndai."
2Corinthians12:20 Amu aureisho-- teni alotu-- pamainepu ndai anaa payeu-- nimikinepupu si ndai nanu anaa piyeuu: netii too ndai enjangar-- olom-- engoro-- enkitarrikino-- enkurrata-- elikioroto-- olwuasa-- enkiposhiposhata;"
2Corinthians12:21 neaku-- teni aitoki alotu enitiiti-- naaitadou Engai ai too ndai-- natum ailishoki ilkumok looitarruoitie opa neitu eala aaing'ua olduruki o entalare o enkimali-mal naataasa."
2Corinthians13:1 Alotu taata enkata e uni enitiiti ndai. Tʼenkutuk oo ljaken aare arashu okuni njeitashe ororei pookin.
2Corinthians13:2 Atang'asa aliki-- naitoki aliki ndai-- neijia anaa patiaka ndai atii enkata e are-- nasiraki si taata matii-- lelo ooitarruoitie opa o ilkulekai pookin: Teni aitoki alotu-- namaing'urrie."
2Corinthians13:3 Tiaraki ning'oruru enkitisipunoto-- ajo eiro Kristos tiatua nanu-- lemeshal tiatua ndai."
2Corinthians13:4 Amu etooshokoki esalaba tʼenjalan-- kake eishiu tʼengolon Engai. Ore peaku kishal yook tiatua ninye-- nikinjiu te nebo o ninye tiatua engolon Engai enitiiti ndai."
2Corinthians13:5 Entetem ndai aten-- ten aa itiiti atua enkirukoto-- entujur ndai aten. Arashu miyolouu ndai aten-- aajo etii Kristos atua ndai? Anake etaa irara turua."
2Corinthians13:6 Naanyu piyolouu-- aajo mikira yook turua."
2Corinthians13:7 Asai Engai-- pemintobiribiri entorroni o nabo-- me pikilioi yook anaa supati-- kake pintobiribiri ndai naishiaakino-- nikitiu yook anaa turua."
2Corinthians13:8 Amu mikindim yook aaitobira entoki nemeishiaakinore esipata-- kake naponiki esipata."
2Corinthians13:9 Amu king'ida ina kata teni kishal yook nigoligolo ndai; naa ena kiyeuoki ndai-- pintabaiaia."
2Corinthians13:10 Akae-- asiraki ndai kuna baak eton atioyo-- peiye-- teni alotu-- maiko empijan tʼerisioroto engolon naaishoo Olaitoriani-- pashet neme paiminye."
2Corinthians13:11 Ore tʼenkiting'oto-- lalashera-- enting'idata-- entabai-- elejileja ndai aten-- embirribirra nabo-- embung'a eseriani-- nelarubare ndai Engai enyorrata o en eseriani."
2Corinthians13:12 Erorokinoto ndai tʼeng'ututata sinyati! Eiroroki ndai sinyat pookin.
2Corinthians13:13 Ore eng'adunoto Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos o enyorrata Engai o enkidikidikoto Olmumua Sinyati-- njebik too ndai pookin. Amen."
Galatians1:1 Paulos-- olairriwani-- (neme loo ltung'anak-- neme too ltung'anak-- kake te Yesus Kristos o Engai Papa oitopiwuo ninye too lootuata)"
Galatians1:2 o lalashera pookin ootii e nebo o nanu: En oo sirito naatii Galatia ena palai.
Galatians1:3 Njebikie ndai eng'adunoto o eseriani naing'ua Engai Papa o Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos--"
Galatians1:4 oishooiye kion tʼolbae loo nkitarruot ang'-- peitopok yook tʼele maa torrono e taata anaa peyeu Engai naa Papa lang'--"
Galatians1:5 oitaai kitok nkatan pookin oo nkatan pookin. Amen.
Galatians1:6 Aiputukuny-- tiaraki nitapaashare aasioki ele oipotoko ndai atua eng'adunoto e Kristos nimbelekenyakinono engai euangelion;"
Galatians1:7 kake metii engai-- neme etii looje ooyeu neitang'aing'ai ndai neibelekeny euangelion e Kristos."
Galatians1:8 Kake ten eaku yook arashu olmalaika le shumata oinosaki ndai engai euangelion nimikinosakitia yook ndai-- njedeki ilo."
Galatians1:9 Anaa pikintera aajo-- naitoki ajo taata: Teni einosaki ndai oltung'ani euangelion neme nitang'amutua-- njedeki ilo."
Galatians1:10 Eton aisyayaki iltung'anak tʼenkinosunoto arashu Engai? Arashu ijojo-- ayeu naitiship iltung'anak? Ten emut ayeu naitiship iltung'anak-- anaata eitu aaku osinga le Kristos."
Galatians1:11 Kake aitayolo ndai-- lalashera-- ore ena euangelion nainosu nanu-- nemera en oo ltung'anak."
Galatians1:12 Amu eitu ang'amu neitu aiteng'enuo ninye tʼoltung'ani o obo-- kake tʼembolunoto e Yesus Kristos."
Galatians1:13 Ajo nanu-- indipa aatoning'-- anaa paikununo opa eton asuj orregie loo Yudayoi-- amu atimira naleng' esirit Engai naiminye ninye--"
Galatians1:14 naponaa tiatua rregieita loo Yudayoi nalang' ilkumok lʼolosho lang' o lʼolporror lai-- amu atonyua naleng' too nena naatang'amutua loopapa."
Galatians1:15 Ore penyorru Engai naategelua opa tʼengoshoke e yeiyo naaipot tʼeng'adunoto enye--"
Galatians1:16 aitayolo Oinoti lenye tiatua nanu-- painosaki lomon lenyena loreren lemeata Engai: akae-- atudumunye nabo kata neitu aigwena o looata enkiring'o o osarge--"
Galatians1:17 neitu ailep alo Yerusalem enetii lelo ootang asa aaku lairriwak-- kake ashomo Arabia naitoki arrinyunye Damaskos."
Galatians1:18 Ore peishunye larin okuni-- nabaiki Yerusalem-- padol Petros-- nabik ngolong'i tomon o imiet te nebo o ninye."
Galatians1:19 Too lkulekai airriwak eitu adol o obo-- neme Yakobos-- olalashe lʼOlaitoriani."
Galatians1:20 Kake enasiraki ndai-- ng'orai-- eyolo Engai-- malejisho."
Galatians1:21 Ore tekurum nalotu atua enkop e Siria o Kilikia.
Galatians1:22 Neton eitu aayolouni engomom ai too sirito tiatua Kristos naatii Yudaya.
Galatians1:23 Eidipa ake aatoning'-- aajo ore ilo otang'asa amir yook opa-- neinosu taata ena kirukoto naiminye opa--"
Galatians1:24 neitadaraa Engai te nanu.
Galatians2:1 Ore tekurum-- peishunye larin tomon o ong'wan-- naitoki ailep alo Yerusalem te nebo o Barnabas narik si Titos te nebo o nanu."
Galatians2:2 Kake ailepa alo tʼolbae lʼembolunoto naaishooki-- nairorie o ninje mbaak euangelion nainosu too loreren lemeata Engai-- naigwena naleng' o lelo ooikenaki-- aajo etaa eanyitai-- pemeaku akwet pesho."
Galatians2:3 Kake ore Titos otii e nebo o nanu-- lora Olgriki-- neitu earakini pemurati."
Galatians2:4 Amu ore pejing'u tʼenkisudoroto lalashera lʼelejare aaikeernu elakunoto ang' nikiata tiatua Kristos-- petum aaitaa yook isingan--"
Galatians2:5 neitu kinjo yook ewueji meitoria ninje yook-- peitashe esipata euangelion too ndai."
Galatians2:6 Kake ore lekua ooata enkitook-- — anaa petotiutuo ninje opa-- me toki te nanu-- amu meing'oraa Engai engomom oltung'ani — amu ore lelo ooata enkitook-- eitu aaponiki nanu toki--"
Galatians2:7 kake ore pedol-- aajo aaishooki nanu euangelion too lememurata-- anaa peishooki Petros too lelo oomurata--"
Galatians2:8 (amu ore ilo oitaa Petros olairriwani too lelo oomurata-- naa ninye si laaitaa nanu too lemeata Engai)--"
Galatians2:9 ore peyolou ninje ena ng'adunoto naaishooki nanu-- Yakobos o Kefas o Yohanes-- ooikenaki aa ng'apeta-- naaishoo nanu o Barnabas engaina e tatene neiruk-- pikipuo yook enetii loreren lemeata Engai-- nepuo ninje enetii loomurata."
Galatians2:10 Naa ororei obo ake-- eyeu nikidamu laisinak-- naa ina atonyua si nanu paitobir."
Galatians2:11 Kake ore pelotu Petros Antiokia-- naitasheikio nanu engomom enye-- amu eitang'oroki ninye."
Galatians2:12 Amu ore eton eitu epuonu iltung'anak ooing'ua Yakobos-- neaku eng'arie ninye endaa lemeata Engai; kake ore pepuonu-- nepal neorunye-- amu eure ninye lelo oomurata--"
Galatians2:13 o metabaiki ilkulekai Yudayoi eibelekenyate te nebo o ninye-- nerikori si Barnabas tʼesungureishu enye."
Galatians2:14 Kake ore padol-- ajo eitu eitoriokino esipata euangelion-- najoki Petros tʼengomom oo pookin: Teni ira Oyudayos-- ninjiu tʼorregie loo lemeata Engai neme tʼoloo Yudayoi-- ainyo piaraki lemeata Engai-- peikununo anaa Yudayoi?"
Galatians2:15 Kira yook Yudayoi tʼempukunoto ang'-- nimikira laitarruok ooing'ua loreren lemeata Engai."
Galatians2:16 Kake tiaraki nikiyolo-- aajo meitaai oltung'ani supat too nkitobirat oo nkitanapat-- kake tʼenkirukoto e atua Yesus Kristos-- nikiruk si Yesus Kristos-- peitaai yook supati tʼenkirukoto e atua Kristos-- neme too nkitobirat oo nkitanapat; amu ore too nkitobirat oo nkitanapat meitaai supat enkiring'o o nabo."
Galatians2:17 Kake ten emut eaku edoli yook ooing'oru esupato tiatua Kristos-- kira laitarruok-- anaata mera Kristos olaisyayani loo nkitarruot? Njoo meaku!"
Galatians2:18 Amu teni aitoki ashet ina natigila-- naitaa nanu kion olalang'ani."
Galatians2:19 Kake aidipa atuaki nkitanapat-- paishiuoki Engai. Aatooshokoki esalaba te nebo o Kristos."
Galatians2:20 Aishiu-- kake me nanu-- amu Kristos oishiu tiatua nanu; ore enaishiu taata tiatua enkiring'o-- naishiu tiatua enkirukoto Oinoti lʼEngai laatonyorra nanu neishooio kion tʼolbae lai."
Galatians2:21 Maiturraa eng'adunoto Engai; amu teni elotu esupato aing'ua nkitanapat-- netua Kristos pesho."
Galatians3:1 Ndai Ilgalatai lemeng'enu-- ang'ai eibelekenya ndamunot inyi nimirukuruku esipata? Amu eitaduaki ndai Kristos anaa etooshokoki esalaba enitiiti ndai."
Galatians3:2 Ayeu nikintayololo nanu ele rorei ake: Itang'amutua Olmumua too nkitobirat oo nkitanapat-- arashu tʼenkinosunoto enkirukoto?"
