Galatians3:3 Miatata eng'eno aaiko nji? Itang'asa tʼolmumua-- niyeuu taata nintabaiaia tʼenkiring'o?"
Galatians3:4 Ke-- iting'iria nkitamiot kumok naaba nji pesho? Ten aa neija-- naa pesho."
Galatians3:5 Ore ele oisho ndai Olmumua neas nkitobirat naaba nji tiatua ndai-- amaa-- keas too nkitobirat oo nkitanapat-- arashu tʼenkinosunoto enkirukoto?"
Galatians3:6 Neijia anaa peiruko Abraham Engai neikenakini ninye ina esupato.
Galatians3:7 Akae-- niyololo-- aajo kulo lʼenkirukoto-- naa ninje nkera e Abraham."
Galatians3:8 Etang'asa adol esirata-- ajo eitaa Engai loreren lemeata ninye-- supati tʼenkirukoto; onaa etiaka Abraham: Epuoi aamayan loreren pookin te iye."
Galatians3:9 Onaa-- eaku emayani looata enkirukoto te nebo o Abraham ora airukoni."
Galatians3:10 Amu ore lelo pookin ooirishakino nkitobirat oo nkitanapat-- netii abori endiata. Amu etisiraki: Edia oltung'ani pookin lemebik tiatua mbaak pookin-- naatisiraki tʼenkitabu oo nkitanapat-- peitobir ninje."
Galatians3:11 Eibala taata-- ajo metii oltung'ani oaku supat too nkitanapat-- amu: Elaishiu osupat tʼenkirukoto;"
Galatians3:12 Mera nkitanapat nʼenkirukoto; kake „ore oltung'ani oitobir ninje-- neishiu“."
Galatians3:13 Etalakua Kristos yook tʼendiata oo nkitanapat etaaiye yook endiata-- amu esira: „Edia oltung'ani pookin oika tʼenjata“--"
Galatians3:14 petum aeu emayani e Abraham shumata oo loreren lemeata Engai pookin te Yesus Kristos-- niking'amu nji Olmumua oisiligaki tʼenkirukoto."
Galatians3:15 Lalashera lainei-- airo anaa iltung'anak. Meiturrari osotua lʼoltung'ani-- oidipaki aitagolo-- nemeponikini toki."
Galatians3:16 Ore taa nkisiligat-- neisiligakaki Abraham o eishoi enye. Mejo „too ishoreitin“-- anaa kumok; kake etiu anaa nabo-- eji: „tʼeishoi ino“-- naa ninye Kristos."
Galatians3:17 Kake ajo nji: Ore ele sotua otang'asa Engai aitagolu peaku te Kristos-- nemeiturrari-- nemeiting'ie nkitanapat enkisiligata; amu eishooki nkitanapat-- eidipate aatulusoi larin iip ong'wan o osom eiter ninye."
Galatians3:18 Amu ten emut etumi enjung'o too nkitanapat-- anaata eitu eishori tʼenkisiligata; kake eishoo Engai Abraham tʼenkisiligata pesho."
Galatians3:19 Ainyo naaku nkitanapat? Etoponikiaki tʼolbae loo nkitarruot-- metabana nelotu eishoi-- naishooki enkisiligata-- netipikaki too lmalaikan t'engaina olaidikidikoni."
Galatians3:20 Mera olaidikidikoni oli obo-- kake nabo Engai."
Galatians3:21 Amaa-- kearare nkitanapat nkisiligat Engai? me neija. Ore ten emutu eishooki nkitanapat naaidim aaishoo empuan-- anaata elotu esupato aing'ua nkitanapat."
Galatians3:22 Kake eigenoiye esirata pookin tiabori enkitarruoto-- peishori enkisiligata enkirukoto e atua Kristos kulo looiruk."
Galatians3:23 Ore eton eitu ebau enkirukoto-- etorripoki yook abori oo nkitanapat-- neigenori yook tiatua enkirukoto napuoi aabolu."
Galatians3:24 Nji etaa nkitanapat ngarikok-- perik yook enetii Kristos-- peitaai yook supati tʼenkirukoto."
Galatians3:25 Ore peidip aeu enkirukoto-- nimikintoki aatii abori oo ngarikok."
Galatians3:26 Amu irara ndai pookin nkera Engai tʼenkirukoto e atua Kristos Yesus.
Galatians3:27 Ore ndai pookin looibatisaki atua Kristos-- injopo baiki Kristos."
Galatians3:28 Metii ene Oyudayos arashu Olgriki-- metii ene osinga arashu olakuno-- metii ene olee arashu eng'oroyoni; amu itaa ndai pookin obo tiatua Kristos Yesus."
Galatians3:29 Ore pirara ndai le Kristos-- itaa eishoi e Abraham o lajung'ok-- anaa pejo nkisiligat."
Galatians4:1 Kake ajo nanu-- meata olajung'oni te ina kata nara enkerai kinyi erishata o osinga-- baiki teni era Olaitoriani lʼenjung'o;"
Galatians4:2 kake etii ninye abori oo laing'orak o laitasheikinok metabaiki enkata natipika menye.
Galatians4:3 Neija baiki yook-- ore te ina kata nikira nkera kunyinyi-- nikira looisyaisho tiabori oo nkiteng'enareitin ele maa."
Galatians4:4 Ore peidip atabau embaiaroto enkata-- neirriu Engai Oinoti lenye-- neiu eng'oroyoni ninye nepiki abori oo nkitanapat--"
Galatians4:5 pelaku kulo lootii abori oo nkitanapat-- peiye king'amu enkeraishu."
Galatians4:6 Akae-- tiaraki nitaa nkera-- onaa eirriwaka Engai Olmumua lʼOinoti lenye atua iltauja linyi-- lodar: Aba-- Papa!"
Galatians4:7 Akae-- mekure ira osinga-- kake enkerai; teni ira enkerai-- nira olajung'oni lʼEngai te Kristos."
Galatians4:8 Kake ore idia kata eitu iyolouu Engai-- nisyayakiki kulo lemera ngain tʼempukunoto."
Galatians4:9 Kake ore taata-- indipa aatayolou Engai niponana aayolounoi tʼEngai-- ainyo pintokiki ndai aarrinyokino nkitaduat tashala o sasi niyeuu aaku kat are singan lenye?"
Galatians4:10 Imbung'ubung'u naleng' ngolong'i o lapaitin o rishat o larin.
Galatians4:11 Aureisho tʼolbae linyi-- pemeaku aisyayaka ndai pesho."
Galatians4:12 Entotiu anaa nanu enatiu; amu atiu si nanu anaa ndai; lalashera-- asai ndai. Eitu kiasakiki entoki torrono."
Galatians4:13 Iyololo-- aajo tiatua enjalan osesen lai ainosaka ndai euangelion tʼenkata elukunya."
Galatians4:14 O nkitasurot ainei naata tʼosesen-- eitu imenimene neitu ianyianya; kake kitang'amutua nanu anaa olmalaika lʼEngai-- anaa Kristos Yesus openy."
Galatians4:15 Kaa teshishu iatata te ina kata? Amu ara oljakeni too ndai-- ten emut eidimai-- anaata itadotutuo ngonyek inyi nikinjosho nanu."
Galatians4:16 Kataa olmang'atinda linyi-- tiaraki naitadol ndai esipata?"
Galatians4:17 Ore enyuata enye tʼolbae linyi-- me sidai; kake eyeu nikipaasharere nanu-- pinyokitata tʼolbae lenye."
Galatians4:18 Kake eikash-- teni inyokinyoko oshi tiatua mbaak sidan-- me ena kata ake atii e nebo o ndai."
Galatians4:19 Nakera ainei-- naiu kat are tʼemion-- metabana nelioi emua e Kristos tiatua ndai:"
Galatians4:20 Ak ayeu naboitare ndai naitaai oltoilo lai; amu mayolo anaa pitiuu ndai.
Galatians4:21 Entolikioki nanu ndai-- liyeuu nibikibiki abori oo nkitanapat: Eitu ining'ining'i ndai nkitanapat?"
Galatians4:22 Amu etisiraki-- ajo eata Abraham laiyok aare-- etoiwuo obo esinga-- neiu olekai enalakuno."
Galatians4:23 Kake ore ilo otoiwuo esinga-- etoiwuoki too mbaak enkiring'o-- ore ilo otoiwuo enalakuno-- naa tʼengolon oo nkisiligat."
Galatians4:24 Ore kuna baak etiu anaa nkitanyanyukieta. Amu ninje sotuan aare-- eing'ua obo oldonyo Sinai-- oiki esingaishu-- naa ninye Hagar."
Galatians4:25 Naa ore Hagar-- eipoti tʼenkop oo Lmarabu oldonyo Sinai-- neishiaakinore Yerusalem-- naatai tʼena kata-- netii atua esingaishu te nebo o nkera enyena."
Galatians4:26 Kake ore Yerusalem natii shumata-- elakuno-- naa ninye yeiyo ang pookin."
Galatians4:27 Amu etisiraki: Ting'idai-- engolupi nemeisho-- Taapu oltoilo ninjir-- en eitu ening' emion eishoi. Amu ore nkera e ina naton openy-- naa kumok-- nelang' nʼena naata olmoruo."
Galatians4:28 Ore taata yook-- lalashera-- kira nkera oo nkisiligat tʼolbae le Isaak."
Galatians4:29 Kake anaa te ina kata petimira ele otoiwuoki too mbaak enkiring'o lido otoiwuoki tʼOlmumua-- naa neijia etiu si taata."
Galatians4:30 Kake ketejaa sirat? Taarai ena singa o engaiyoni enye; amu mejung'u engaiyoni esinga te nebo o engaiyoni enalakuno.
Galatians4:31 Akae-- lalashera-- mikira yook nkera esinga-- kake kira nkera enalakuno."
Galatians5:1 Akae-- entobik tiatua elakunoto natalakunye yook Kristos-- emintoki aajing' atua enjata esingaishu."
Galatians5:2 Eng'orai-- nanu Paulos aliki ndai-- ajo teni emurati ndai-- miduporere toki Kristos."
Galatians5:3 Naitoki aijakenoki oltung'ani pookin lomurati-- ajo meata kata nemeitabaia nkitanapat pookin."
Galatians5:4 Imina ndai te Kristos-- loojo-- eitaai supati too nkitanapat-- itusulunyete tʼeng'adunoto."
Galatians5:5 Kake kimaririu yook tʼOlmumua eanyunoto esupato naing'ua enkirukoto--"
Galatians5:6 Amu meata tiatua Kristos emurata engolon arashu memurata-- kake enkirukoto naitobirisho tʼenyorrata."
Galatians5:7 Ikweta sidai. Ang'ai lotomitikio ndai-- pimisujusuju esipata?"
Galatians5:8 Eitu epukunye ena kisisa oloipoto ndai.
Galatians5:9 Ore enkisiijoi kinyi neisiijie enkitushulata pookin.
Galatians5:10 Airuk nanu ndai tiatua Olaitoriani-- ajo mipuopuo aaibirribir engai toki. Ore oloitang'arrir ndai-- nelaea enkigwena-- lora enara."
Galatians5:11 Ore nanu-- lalashera-- teni epon ainosu emurata-- ainyo pepon aaisili? Anaata eishunye erikai esalaba."
Galatians5:12 Edupa-- teni eiturrari kulo looibelie ndai."
Galatians5:13 Kake eipotokoki ndai-- lalashera-- elakunoto. Njoomeaku ake elakunoto inyi eng'asiata enkiring'o-- kake esyayakinoto tʼenyorrata--"
Galatians5:14 amu eitobirai nkitanapat pookin tʼororei obo-- tʼele: Tonyorra ol elatia ino anaa pinyor kion!"
Galatians5:15 Kake teni ionyororo ninosaroro-- eng'orai-- pimimutaroro."
Galatians5:16 Ajo ake: Entilimanata tʼolmumua-- pemintobiribiri baiki olng'warra lʼenkiring'o."
Galatians5:17 Amu eng'war enkiring'o agilunore Olmumua negilunore Olmumua enkiring'o-- amu eara ninje pokira are-- pemintobiribiri kuna niyeuu ndai."
Galatians5:18 Kake teni erik ndai Olmumua-- mitiiti abori oo nkitanapat."
Galatians5:19 Eibala nkitobirat enkiring'o naara: earata enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni-- entalare-- olduruki-- enkimalimal--"
Galatians5:20 enkisyayare oo muain-- enkibonore-- mang'atishuitin-- enkitarrikino-- engilata e tau-- ngoroitin-- nkiminjalishuitin-- rishat osotua-- njangarrin-- nkibaroitin--"
Galatians5:21 earata metua-- meraitin-- nkinosareitin o nanyanyukye kuna-- naiturukie aliki ndai naitoki aiturukie alimu-- ajo mepuo aajung'u looitobir kuna enkarsishu Engai."
Galatians5:22 Kake era ilmomo lʼOlmumua: enyorrata-- eng'ida-- eseriani-- olng'iria-- emborran-- esidano-- enkirukoto-- olgira sidai-- emitikinoto oo mbaak oo nkiri."
Galatians5:23 Megilunore nkitanapat kuna.
Galatians5:24 Ore kulo loora le Kristos Yesus-- neoshoki enkiring'o enye esalaba te nebo o yeunot torrok o ilng'warraitin."
Galatians5:25 Teni kinjiu tʼOlmumua-- matilimanata baiki tʼOlmumua."
Galatians5:26 Njoo mikiaku looing'oru enkitadararoto e pesho-- looisisiuno-- looibaro."
Galatians6:1 Lalashera-- teni ebatatari oltung'ani tʼenkitarruoto nabo-- entaretokiti-- ndai lʼemumuaishu-- ele tʼolmumua obor-- niduaia kion-- pimikintasuri si iye."
Galatians6:2 Entanapakinoto irridat-- pipuopuo aaitabaia nji nkitanapat e Kristos."
Galatians6:3 Amu teni ejo oltung ani-- era toki-- nemera o nyoo-- nelej kion."
Galatians6:4 Njeleen oltung'ani pookin enkyas enye openy-- neata ninye te ina kata enkitadararoto te kion openy neme tʼolekai tung'ani."
Galatians6:5 Amu elanap oltung'ani pookin orridati lenye openy.
Galatians6:6 Oloiteng'eni tʼororei-- njeng'arie sidan pookin oloiteng'en ninye."
Galatians6:7 Emimbel-- memoroi Engai! Amu enaun oltung'ani-- naa ninye elaisambu."
Galatians6:8 Amu oloun tʼenkiring'o enye-- nelaisambu tʼenkiring'o erruoroto; oloun tʼOlmumua-- nelaisambu tʼOlmumua empuan nemeiting'."
Galatians6:9 Njoo mikinaura kintobir sidan-- amu kipuo aaisambu tʼenkata enye nimikiishu."
Galatians6:10 Akae-- teni kintoki aatum enkata-- maitobira sidan too ltung'anak pookin-- kake tʼenkata elukunya too loong'ar enkirukoto."
Galatians6:11 Idolitata ndai-- aajo keba aa kulo rorei latisiraka ndai tʼengaina ai."
Galatians6:12 Ore kulo looyeu neshipakinoi ndai tʼenkiring'o-- nearaki ndai metumurati ndai-- pemetum emirata tʼolbae lʼesalaba e Kristos."
Galatians6:13 Amu ore si ninje oomurata-- nemeibung' nkitanapat-- kake eyeu nemurati ndai-- petum aaitadararie seseni linyi."
Galatians6:14 Kake njaapaash ena kitadararoto-- neme en esalaba Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos; te ilo aatooshokoki nanu olmaa esalaba-- neoshokini olmaa esalaba te nanu."
Galatians6:15 Amu tiatua Kristos medupa emurata arashu memurata-- kake enkitobirata ng'ejuk nadupa."
Galatians6:16 Ore kulo pookin oopuoiye ilo rregie-- njebik eseriani o enking'urroto shumata enye o shumata Israel lʼEngai."
Galatians6:17 Eiter taata njoo maaitoki oltung'ani aitanyamal; amu anapita ilponot lʼOlaitoriani ootipikaki osesen lai.
Galatians6:18 Metobikie eng'adunoto Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos Olmumua linyi-- lalashera lainei. Amen."
Ephesians1:1 Paulos-- olairriwani le Yesus Kristos tʼolbae lʼeyeunoto Engai: too sinyat ootii Efesos o too lairukok le atua Kristos."
Ephesians1:2 Metobikie ndai eng'adunoto o eseriani naing'ua Engai Papa o Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos!
Ephesians1:3 Njeitadarari Engai o Menye lʼOlaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos! Etamayana ninye yook tʼemayani pookin emumuaishu te shumata tiatua Kristos.
Ephesians1:4 Etegelua ninye yook tiatua Kristos-- eton eitu epiki entonata olmaa-- pikiaku sinyat nimikiata ntibil tʼengomom enye tiatua enyorrata."
Ephesians1:5 Neituruk apik yook-- pekitum enkeraishu e atua ninye te Yesus Kristos-- tʼenyorrata eyeunoto enye--"
Ephesians1:6 peitadarari enkitook eng'adunoto enye natang'adunye ninye yook tiatua Olotonyorra.
Ephesians1:7 Nikiata tiatua ninye elakunoto tʼosarge lenye-- enkitaunoto oo nkitarruot tʼendupoto eng'adunoto enye"
Ephesians1:8 natoponikia ninye yook tiatua eng'eno pookin o enjartano.
Ephesians1:9 Neitayolo ninye yook emikio eyeunoto enye tʼenyorrata enye naiturukie aotiki tiatua ninye--"
Ephesians1:10 peitobiri tʼembaiaroto oo nkatan-- neiturrur pookin tiatua Kristos-- ntokitin naatii shumata o naatii enkop."
Ephesians1:11 Kinoto tiatua ninye enjung'o-- yook lootipikaki tʼentootiki enye loitaa ntokitin pookin tʼenkigwena eyeunoto enye--"
Ephesians1:12 pekiaku yook enkitadararoto enkitook enye-- yook likinturuko aanyu Kristos."
Ephesians1:13 Itiiti si ndai atua ninye-- indipa aatoning' lomon lʼesipata-- euangelion enkitopuata inyi; eitagoloki baiki ndai lairukok tiatua ninye tʼOlmumua Sinyati lʼenkisiligata--"
Ephesians1:14 ora eng'asiata enjung'o ang'-- pekitum elakunoto nikiaku masaa enyena-- neaku enkitadararoto enkitook enye."
Ephesians1:15 Onaa baiki nanu-- aidipa atoning'o enkirukoto too ndai tiatua Olaitoriani Yesus o enyorrata e atua sinyat pookin--"
Ephesians1:16 mapal eitu ajo ashe tʼolbae linyi nadamu ndai too sayat ainei--"
Ephesians1:17 peisho ndai Engai Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos-- Menye lʼenkitook-- Olmumua lʼeng'eno o embolunoto tiatua eyolounoto enye"
Ephesians1:18 o ngonyek oo ltauja linyi naailang'akaki-- piyolouu ndai enara eanyunoto enkipototo enye o enara endupoto enkitook enjung'o enye tiatua sinyat"
Ephesians1:19 o enara enkitook nemetemai engolon enye e atua yook likiruk tʼenkidimata engolon enye kitok--"
Ephesians1:20 naitaa ninye tiatua Kristos te ina kata naitopiwuo ninye too lootuata neitoton ninye te tatene enye e shumata--"
Ephesians1:21 peaku shumata enkitook pookin o engolon o enkidimata o enkitoria o engarna pookin naimakini-- me tiatua ele maa ake-- kake baiki tiatua ololotu;"
Ephesians1:22 nepik ntokitin pookin abori oo nkejek enyena neisho-- peaku ninye elukunya oo pookin tʼesirit"
Ephesians1:23 nara osesen lenye nera emborei naigany pookin tiatua pookin.
Ephesians2:1 ishoo empuan si ndai ootuata tʼolbae loo lang'at o nkitarruot--"
Ephesians2:2 ipuoiyeye opa tʼerisioroto orregie lʼele maa o lʼoloata engolon tʼolng'inai-- ora Olmumua oitobirisho tiatua iltung'anak lemeiruk."
Ephesians2:3 Amu te nebo o ninje kitilimanate si yook opa tiatua ilng'warraitin lʼenkiring'o ang' nikintobir eyeunoto enkiring'o o en eng'eno-- nikira si yook nkera engoro tʼempukunoto ang'-- neijia anaa ilkulekai."
Ephesians2:4 Kake ore Engai nara adupani tʼenkordunoto-- tʼenyorrata enye kitok natonyorrie ninye yook--"
Ephesians2:5 neishoo yook empuan te nebo o Kristos te ina kata nikituata too nkitarruot-- — eitopuaki ndai tʼempuris-- —"
Ephesians2:6 neitopiu neitoton yook te nebo o ninye tiatua wuejitin e shumata tiatua Kristos Yesus--"
Ephesians2:7 peiye elaitadolu tiatua nkatan naapuonu akenya enkitook endupoto empuris enye tiatua emborran too yook tiatua Kristos Yesus.
Ephesians2:8 Amu eitopuaki ndai tʼempuris tʼenkirukoto-- ena me too ndai-- era ninye enkishooroto Engai:"
Ephesians2:9 me too nkitobirat-- pemeitadaraa oltung'ani kion."
Ephesians2:10 Amu kira yook enkyas enye-- eitobiraki yook tiatua Kristos Yesus-- pekintobir nkyasin sidan naaituruko aitobir Engai-- pekilimana tiatua ninje."
Ephesians2:11 Akae-- entadamu-- aajo ore pirara ndai opa lemeata Engai t'enkiring'o ooipotoki lememurata too kulo ooji emurata tʼenkiring'o-- naitobiri tʼengaina--"
Ephesians2:12 niakuku te ina kata lemeata Kristos-- oolakwaniki enkarsishu e Israel-- nirara lomon loo sotuaitin o loo nkisiligat-- leitu eata eanyunoto neitu eata Engai tiatua olmaa."
Ephesians2:13 Kake ore taata-- ndai ootii atua Kristos neaku enelakwa opa-- nitinyikutua tʼolbae lʼosarge le Kristos."
Ephesians2:14 Amu ninye eseriani ang'-- oitaa yook pokira are nabo-- netigila erishata natii tʼempolos-- eitai emang'atishu tʼenkiring'o enye--"
Ephesians2:15 nara nkitanapat naatipikaki neum naaitanapishoteki-- petum aitaa kulo are oltung'ani obo ng'ejuk te ninye kion neitobir eseriani--"
Ephesians2:16 neitobirakinye pokira are tiatua osesen obo Engai tʼesalaba-- eidipa atara emang'atishu te ninye openy."
Ephesians2:17 Eewuo ninye neinosaki tʼeuangelion eseriani ndai ootii enelakwa-- o yook ootataana."
Ephesians2:18 Amu tiatua ninye eishori yook pokira are-- pikijing' Engai tʼOlmumua obo."
Ephesians2:19 Akae-- mekure irara taata lomon o ilkaponu-- kake irara loopeny te nebo o sinyat o loong'ar engaji Engai--"
Ephesians2:20 ooteshetakaki entonata oo lairriwak o layolounok-- nera Yesus Kristos osoit lʼolpijata lenye;"
Ephesians2:21 ore tiatua ninye eidikidikoki enjetata pookin nebulu-- peaku engaji sinyati tiatua Olaitoriani--"
Ephesians2:22 eteshetakaki baiki ndai shumata enye-- piakuku emanyata Engai tiatua Olmumua."
Ephesians3:1 Akae-- ara nanu-- Paulos-- oloena le Kristos Yesus tʼolbae linyi lemeata Engai--"
Ephesians3:2 anaa pitoning'o ndai lomon lʼenkisyayare eng'adunoto Engai-- naaishooki nanu tʼolbae linyi."
Ephesians3:3 Amu aaitayolouoki ena mikio tʼembolunoto-- anaa patisira shumata too looti rorei--"
Ephesians3:4 peiye-- teni isomama ndai-- nejing'aa ndai eyolounoto ai ena mikio e Kristos."
Ephesians3:5 Eitu eitayoloi too lkulekai porrori loo nkera oo ltung'anak-- anaa petabolokoki taata tʼOlmumua lairriwak o layolounok--"
Ephesians3:6 aajo ore loreren lemeata Engai eaku loong'ar enjung'o-- naa rubat osesen obo-- neng'ar nkisiligat e atua Kristos tʼeuangelion--"
Ephesians3:7 naaitaai nanu olaisyayani lenye tʼerisioroto enkishooroto eng'adunoto Engai naaishoo nanu tʼengolon enye naidimari.
Ephesians3:8 Ara nanu oti naleng' tiatua sinyat pookin-- kake aaishooki ena ng'adunoto-- painosu tiatua loreren lemeata Engai endupoto nemetemai e Kristos--"
Ephesians3:9 nailang'aki oltung'ani pookin aitayolo keba aa eng'arata emikio natushumaki tʼenkiterata olmaa tiatua Engai-- naitaa ntokitin pookin tiatua Yesus Kristos--"
Ephesians3:10 petum aatayolou taata nkitoriaitin o ngoloni e shumata tʼesirit eng'eno oo muain kumok Engai--"
Ephesians3:11 tʼerisioroto eotikinoto enye oo nkatan pookin-- naitadua tiatua Kristos Yesus-- Olaitoriani lang'--"
Ephesians3:12 nikiata tiatua ninye enkiteunoto o enyikakinoto tiatua eng'idaroto tʼenkirukoto e atua ninye.
Ephesians3:13 Onaa-- asai ndai-- pimishalulu too nkisilot ainei natum tʼolbae linyi-- nera ninje enkitook inyi."
Ephesians3:14 Onaa agilaki kung' ainei Menye lʼOlaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos--"
Ephesians3:15 eing'ua ninye empapaishu pookin naipoti te shumata o tʼenkop--"
Ephesians3:16 peiye eisho ninye ndai tʼemborei enkitook enye-- pigolulu tʼolmumua linyi tiatua oltung'ani le atua--"
Ephesians3:17 pemany Kristos atua iltauja linyi tʼenkirukoto-- ipikipiki ntonat neuni ndai tiatua enyorrata--"
Ephesians3:18 pindimidimi aatayoloutu te nebo o sinyat pookin enara endapasho o engadoro nairag o engadoro naitashe o engasuri--"
Ephesians3:19 piyolouu baiki enyorrata e Kristos nalang' eyolounoto pookin-- peiganyi ndai tʼenkiganyata pookin Engai."
Ephesians3:20 Ore ele loidim aitobira nelang' naleng' pookin-- enikiomonu arashu enikimbirribirru-- tʼenkidimata naitobirisho ninye tiatua yook--"
Ephesians3:21 njeishori ele enkitook tiatua esirit o tiatua Kristos Yesus too ishoreitin pookin enkata pookin o nkatan pookin. Amen.
Ephesians4:1 Akae-- adiding ndai-- nanu oloena tiatua Olaitoriani-- pilimanana anaa peaku tʼenkipototo naipotieki ndai--"
Ephesians4:2 tʼenkitadounoto pookin o tʼemborran o tʼolng'iria-- pinapakinono tiatua enyorrata--"
Ephesians4:3 ninyokinyoko aaibung' enaboishu Olmumua tiatua eenet eseriani.
Ephesians4:4 Etii osesen obo ake o Olmumua obo-- anaa peipotokoki baiki ndai tiatua eanyunoto nabo enkipototo inyi;"
Ephesians4:5 netii Olaitoriani obo-- enkirukoto nabo-- enkibatisa nabo--"
Ephesians4:6 Engai nabo o Menye loo pookin-- Olotii shumata oo pookin o too pookin o tiatua pookin."
Ephesians4:7 Kake eishooki pooki tung'ani lang' eng'adunoto narisiore entemet enkishooroto e Kristos.
Ephesians4:8 Onaa ejo: Eilepaka shumata neibok engaji oo looena neisho iltung'anak nkishoorot.
Ephesians4:9 Ore peilepaka shumata-- meji si ena ajo etang'asa adou atua wuejitin e abori naleng' enkop?"
Ephesians4:10 Ore ninye otadouo-- naa ninye si oloilepa alo shumata alang' wuejitin pookin-- peigany ntokitin pookin."
Ephesians4:11 Eishoo ninye-- peaku ematua lairriwak o ilkulekai layolounok o ilkulekai lainosarok loo lomon lʼeng'ida o ilkulekai lairritak o laiteng'enak--"
Ephesians4:12 peaku sinyat looidim aaitobira enkyas enkisyayare-- pesheti osesen le Kristos--"
Ephesians4:13 metabana nikilep yook pookin atua enaboishu enkirukoto o eyolounoto Oinoti lʼEngai-- pikiaku leak ootabaitie nikibaiki entemet embotoro nalulung'a e Kristos--"
Ephesians4:14 pimikintoki aaku nkera-- pemerikiriki yook idye o idye tʼolkutati pookin lʼenkiteng'enare tiatua olosek loo ltung'anak o tiatua esungureishu-- peaku emputokinoto enkitamanimanaroto--"
Ephesians4:15 kake pikiata esipata tiatua enyorrata nikibulu tiatua ninye lora elukunya-- Kristos-- too mbaak pookin;"
Ephesians4:16 neidikidikoki te ninye osesen pookin neibung'aro too rubat pookin-- peretokino ematua nabo o engai t'entemet enkidimata neitaa-- pebulu osesen metaa enjetakinoto enye openy tiatua enyorrata."
Ephesians4:17 Ajo ena naijakenu tiatua Olaitoriani: Emintoki ndai aalimana anaa ilkulekai lemeata Engai tʼempesho oo ndamunot enye.
Ephesians4:18 Eidipaki aatipik enaimin ndamunot enye nelam empuan naing'ua Engai-- tiaraki nemetii eng'eno tiatua ninje-- etaa modook iltauja lenye."
Ephesians4:19 Naa torrok ninje neishooio aten atua mbaak torrok oo nkiri neas nʼolduruki te nebo o empiani.
Ephesians4:20 Kake ore ndai eitu inteng'enuonuo Kristos neijia--"
Ephesians4:21 ten aa itoning'o lomon lenyena neiteng'eni ndai tiatua ninye-- anaa petii esipata tiatua Yesus."
Ephesians4:22 Onaa-- entautu oltung'ani musana tʼorregie lenye lʼelukunya-- loiminye kion tʼolng'warra lʼeng'uyan--"
Ephesians4:23 niakuku ng'ejuko tiatua Olmumua loo ndamunot--"
Ephesians4:24 ninjopishopo oltung'ani ng'ejuk oitobiraki tʼemua Engai tiatua esupato o esinyatishu o esipata.
Ephesians4:25 Onaa enturrai elejare-- eroro esipata-- oltung'ani pookin tʼol elatia enye-- amu kira rubat tiatua yook."
Ephesians4:26 Emigoro-- pemintarruoruo; eminjo edoiyo engolong'-- iatata engoro!"
Ephesians4:27 Eminjo si satan eng'asiata!
Ephesians4:28 Olotupurrishe-- njoo meitoki apurrisho-- kake njepon anyok aitobir too ngaik enyena sidan-- peiye etum aata enaisho Oloata elaunoto!"
Ephesians4:29 Njoo mepuku olderra torrono tʼenkutuk inyi-- kake enara sidai-- peaku enjetakinoto neisho looning' enjipai!"
Ephesians4:30 Emilishie Olmumua Sinyati lʼEngai lotipikieki ndai olmishire lʼengolong' elakunoto!
Ephesians4:31 Njelakwaniki ndai erokan e oshoke pookin o olmurai le oshoke o engoro o enjangar o emoroto te nebo o entorroni pookin!
Ephesians4:32 Entaa tiatua ndai oopeny loobor-- looata ngoshuak naanana-- looing'uaikino anaa petung'aikia Engai ndai tiatua Kristos."
Ephesians5:1 Akae-- entaa lasujak lʼEngai anaa nkera naanyorri--"
Ephesians5:2 entilimanata tiatua enyorrata anaa petonyorra yook Kristos neishooio kion tʼolbae lang'-- peaku enkishooroto o enkidasare-- nara erropili sidai tʼEngai."
Ephesians5:3 Njoo meimakini too ndai tukul mbaak torrok oo nkiri o olduruki pookin o engong'u oo masaa-- anaa pemeata kata nemeaku too sinyat--"
Ephesians5:4 baiki nemeata sura o olderra lʼemodaishu o enkitakwenishoto torrono nemeaku too ndai-- kake entopon elikinoto e ashe."
Ephesians5:5 Amu meata kata nimiyololo ena-- aajo meata enjung'o tiatua enkarsishu e Kristos o Engai oloitobir mbaak torrok oo nkiri arashu lʼolduruki arashu lʼengong'u oo masaa-- lora olaisyayani loo nkulie ain."
Ephesians5:6 Eminjo eitamanimanaa ndai oltung'ani o obo too rorei le pesho; amu elotu tʼolbae loo kuna engoro Engai shumata oo ltung'anak lemeiruk.
Ephesians5:7 Akae-- emiaku lang'arak o ninje."
Ephesians5:8 Amu irara opa enaimin-- kake itaa taata enkilang'et tiatua Olaitoriani."
Ephesians5:9 Entobik anaa nkera enkilang'et-- amu etii ilmomo lʼenkilang'et atua esidano o esupato o esipata pookin;"
Ephesians5:10 entaleen enashipakinoi tʼOlaitoriani.
Ephesians5:11 Eming'ar nkyasin enaimin nemeata ilmomo-- kake eaku-- pingwenakiki ninje."
Ephesians5:12 Amu enaitobir ninje tʼemikio-- neata si enkurruna."
Ephesians5:13 Kake ore kuna pookin eibalunye-- teni eigwenaki enkilang'et ninje; amu pookin naibalunye-- naa enkilang'et."
Ephesians5:14 Onaa ejo: Nyototoi oloirura-- topiu tiatua lootuata nikilailang'aki Kristos."
Ephesians5:15 Akae-- eng'orai-- pilimanana aabaraki-- me anaa ilmoda-- kake anaa lang'eni--"
Ephesians5:16 ilakuku enkata-- amu etaa ngolong'i torrok."
Ephesians5:17 Onaa emiaku ilmoda-- kake loodamu enara eyeunoto Olaitoriani!"
Ephesians5:18 Emimera tʼolmarua lotii enkibor oo ngonyek-- kake njebore ndai Olmumua!"
Ephesians5:19 Erorioroto too singolioitin lʼengauo o too singolioitin lʼenkitadararoto o too singolioitin sidan lʼemumuaishu niranyakiki nintadaraara Olaitoriani too ltauja linyi--"
Ephesians5:20 nilikiki Engai o Papa oshi ashe tʼolbae loo ntokitin pookin tʼengarna Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos--"
Ephesians5:21 ining'ororo too ndai tiatua enkuretishu e Kristos.
Ephesians5:22 Njening' ng'oroyok ilmoruak lenye anaa Olaitoriani--"
Ephesians5:23 amu era olmoruo elukunya eng'oroyoni-- anaa pera Kristos elukunya esirit nera ninye Olaitopuani lʼosesen."
Ephesians5:24 Neijia anaa pening' esirit Kristos-- neijia njening' ng'oroyok ilmoruak too pookin."
Ephesians5:25 Lemoruak-- entonyor ng'oroyok inyi anaa petonyorra Kristos esirit neishooio kion tʼolbae lenye--"
Ephesians5:26 pesinyaa ninye eikishaanye tʼenkisujata engare tiatua ororei--"
Ephesians5:27 petum aeaki ninye kion esirit enkitook nemeata entibili arashu esototo arashu pookin nijo kuna-- kake peaku sinyati o nemeata eleyata."
Ephesians5:28 Neijia meata kata nemenyor ilmoruak ng'oroyok enye anaa seseni lenye oopeny. Olonyor enkitok enye-- nenyor kion--"
Ephesians5:29 amu eitu ai kata eibai o obo osesen lenye; kake eitoti neramat ninye-- neijia anaa si Kristos esirit enye."
Ephesians5:30 Amu kira yook rubat osesen lenye-- lʼenkiring'o enye o loo loik lenyena."
Ephesians5:31 Onaa elaing'ua oltung'ani menye o ng'otonye neibung'are eng'oroyoni enye-- neaku pokira are osesen obo."
Ephesians5:32 Kitok ena mikio; kake alimu mbaak e Kristos o nʼesirit.
Ephesians5:33 Neijia si ndai-- njoo oltung'ani pookin too ndai enyor enkitok enye anaa kion; ore enkitok-- njeure olmoruo."
Ephesians6:1 Nakera-- entoning' lootoiutuo ndai tiatua Olaitoriani; amu eitoriori ena."
Ephesians6:2 „Ntaa kituak minyi o ng'utunyi!“ era ena enkitanapata elukunya naata enkisiligata--"
Ephesians6:3 „pitum sidan nibik enkata naado tʼenkop.“
Ephesians6:4 Ore ndai-- loomenye-- emintagor nkera inyi-- kake entubulu ninje tʼenkiteng'enare o tʼendiding'are Olaitoriani!"
Ephesians6:5 Laisyayak-- entoning' loora laitoriak linyi loo seseni tʼenkuretishu o tʼenkikirikirata too ltauja linyi oosipa anaa Kristos--"
Ephesians6:6 me tʼenkisyayare oo ngonyek anaa looiting'id iltung'anak-- kake anaa laisyayak le Kristos nintobiribiri eyeunoto Engai too ltauja--"
Ephesians6:7 tʼolokiyo sidai isyayakiki ninje anaa looisyayaki Olaitoriani-- neme iltung'anak--"
Ephesians6:8 niyololo-- aajo ore oltung'ani pookin oitobir sidan-- nelang'amu kuna tʼOlaitoriani-- ten aa osinga arashu ololakuno."
Ephesians6:9 Ore ndai-- laitoriak-- enkunakiti si ninje neijia-- entapal enkituriata-- iyololo-- aajo etii shumata Olaitoriani lenye o linyi-- nemeing'oraa ninye entemet oltung'ani."
Ephesians6:10 Ore tʼenkiting'oto-- lalashera lainei-- entagolito tiatua Olaitoriani o tiatua enkidimata engolon enye."
Ephesians6:11 Enjopo nareta pookin Engai-- pitumutumu aaitashoito too losekin le satan;"
Ephesians6:12 amu mikiarare osarge o enkiring'o-- kake ilkituak o looata engolon o laitoriak lʼolmaa lʼena aimin o ilmumuan torrok ootii abori e shumata."
Ephesians6:13 Onaa-- embung'a nareta pookin Engai-- peiye indimidimi aaitashoito tʼengolong' torrono-- naa teni itigilutua pookin-- nintasheshe."
Ephesians6:14 Akae-- entashoito-- iteenikinote esipata too mpolosi ninjopishopo esupato tʼolgoo--"
Ephesians6:15 ninjopitoto namuka tiabori oo nkejek anaa looidipakinote too lomon lʼeng'ida o eseriani.
Ephesians6:16 Ore too kuna pookin embung'a elong'o enkirukoto nindimiemie aailiilarie mbaa naaiwuwu oltorrono--"
Ephesians6:17 nimbung'ubung'u erripet esekengei elukunya naisho enkitopuata o olalem lʼolmumua lora lomon lʼEngai.
Ephesians6:18 Entasaishoto tʼenkata pookin tiatua Olmumua tʼesayata o tʼeomonoto pookin ninjolololo baiki tʼenyuata pookin nisayakiki sinyat pookin--"
Ephesians6:19 nikisayakiki si nanu-- paaishori abolu enkutuk ai maureisho naitayolou emikio euangelion--"
Ephesians6:20 amu ninye ataaiye olaisyayani oena-- peiye anyokita tʼeng'ida nairo anaa pemeata kata namaiko."
Ephesians6:21 Onaa-- piyolouu-- anaa paikununo-- enaas-- elaitayolo ndai mbaak pookin Tukikos-- olalashe onyorri o olaisyayani supat tiatua Olaitoriani--"
Ephesians6:22 lairriwaka ndai-- piyolouu anaa paikununo-- neilejilej ninye iltauja linyi."
Ephesians6:23 Metobiko eseriani too lalashera-- o enyorata te nebo o enkirukoto naing'ua Engai Papa o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos!"
Ephesians6:24 Metobiko eng'adunoto too pookin loonyor Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos oshi ake. Amen.
Philippians1:1 Paulos o Timoteos-- isingan le Yesus Kristos: too sinyat pookin tiatua Yesus Kristos ootii engang' e Filipi-- te nebo o laing'orak o laisyayak."
Philippians1:2 Njeboitare ndai eng'adunoto o eseriani naing'ua Engai Papa lang' o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos!
Philippians1:3 Aliki oshi Engai ai ashe-- teni adamu ndai--"
Philippians1:4 ngolong'i pookin-- too sayat ainei pookin tʼolbae linyi pookin-- nasaisho tʼeng'ida--"
Philippians1:5 tʼolbae lʼenkidikidikoto inyi tiatua lomon lʼeng'ida-- eiter tʼengolong' elukunya metabaiki taata--"
Philippians1:6 nayolo ena toki nabo-- ajo oloitera tiatua ndai enkyas sidai-- nelaitabaia metabaiki engolong' e Kristos Yesus--"
Philippians1:7 anaa peitoriori te nanu-- paibirribirraki ndai pookin-- tiaraki naata ndai tiatua oltau lai tiatua ienat ainei o tiatua emitunoto o enkitagoloto oo lomon lʼeng'ida-- amu irara ndai pookin ling'aring'ara te nebo o nanu eng'adunoto."
Philippians1:8 Amu era Engai oljakeni lai-- ajo aataiye ndai pookin esing'ati tʼenkordunoto e Yesus Kristos."
Philippians1:9 Nasayu ena-- pepona abulu enyorrata inyi oshi tiatua eyolounoto o tiatua enkitagoluoto pookin--"
Philippians1:10 pindimidimi aataleen enaaku-- piakuku berleli-- lemeitirikisho metabaiki engolong' e Kristos--"
Philippians1:11 iborere too lmomo lʼesupato lootaa te Yesus Kristos-- peaku enkitook o enkitadararoto Engai."
Philippians1:12 Ayeu ake niyolouu ndai-- lalashera-- ajo ore mbaak nainoto-- eaku ninje emponata enkibularoto oo lomon lʼeng'ida--"
Philippians1:13 neijia ajo etaliote ienat ainei tiatua Kristos tʼengaji enkigwena pookin o too lkulekai pookin--"
Philippians1:14 netum lalashera kumok tiatua Olaitoriani enkitagoloto too ienat ainei-- nepon naleng' aaiteu aairoro lomon lʼEngai-- metii enkuretishu."
Philippians1:15 Kake einosu looje Kristos tʼolbae lʼengilata e tau o enkitarrikino-- ore ilkulekai tʼoltau sidai."
Philippians1:16 Einosu lelo Kristos tʼenkitarrikino nemebaraki-- amu ejo eponiki ienat ainei enkilishoto;"
Philippians1:17 ore ilkulekai tʼenyorrata-- amu eyolo-- aajo abik ene tʼolbae lʼemitunoto oo lomon lʼeng'ida."
Philippians1:18 Ainyo si? Njeinosuni Kristos tʼorregie pookin-- tʼenkitaduaroto arashu tʼesipata-- nang'ida tiatua ina naitoki alang'ida;"
Philippians1:19 amu ayolo-- ajo elaaku ena te nanu enkitopuata tʼolbae lʼesayata inyi o tʼolbae lʼenkitarasunoto Olmumua le Kristos--"
Philippians1:20 anaa paibartu naleng' naanyu-- ajo makurru tʼentoki o nabo-- kake eitadarari Kristos tʼenjipai pookin anaa oshi o taata tiatua osesen lai-- ten eaku tʼempuan arashu tʼenkea."
Philippians1:21 Amu aishiye nanu Kristos naeiye endupoto.
Philippians1:22 Kake tiaraki naitobir enkyas ai ilmomo-- ten aishiu tʼosesen-- namayolo enagelu."
Philippians1:23 Aairony kuna baak pokira are: Aata olng'warra lʼelakunoto-- patii e nebo o Kristos-- naa sidai ena naleng';"
Philippians1:24 kake meata kata namabik tʼosesen tʼolbae linyi.
Philippians1:25 Ore Eng'idaroto kitok ayolo-- ajo alabik naitoki aboitare ndai pookin-- pitumutumu enjetakinoto o eng'ida enkirukoto--"
Philippians1:26 nindimidimi aaitadarai aten tʼolbae lai-- teni aitoki alotu enitiiti ndai."
Philippians1:27 Embung'a ake orregie sidai anaa peyeu lomon lʼeng'ida le Kristos-- peiye-- ten alotu nadol ndai arashu matii naning' mbaak inyi-- intasheshe tiatua Olmumua obo o tiatua oltau obo nigilunono te nebo o yook tʼolbae lʼenkirukoto oo lomon lʼeng'ida--"
Philippians1:28 niminjosho eiture ndai ilmang'ati linyi tʼentoki o nabo-- nera ena too ninje olponoto oibala lʼenkiminata-- kake too ndai lʼenkitopuata-- neing'ua ena Engai;"
Philippians1:29 amu eishooki ndai tʼolbae le Kristos-- me pirukuruku ake atua ninye-- kake peisili ndai baiki tʼolbae lenye--"
Philippians1:30 niatata ina araroto anaa pitadua te nanu nining'ining'i taata te nanu.
Philippians2:1 Akae-- ten etii atua ndai enkilejilejata tiatua Kristos-- ten etii enkitigiraroto enyorrata-- ten etii enkidikidikoto Olmumua-- ten etii ngoshuak naanana o nkordunot--"
Philippians2:2 enganyutu eng'ida ai-- piatata ndamunot naanyanyuk-- niatata enyorrata nanyanyuk-- niatata oltau obo-- nidamumu nabo--"
Philippians2:3 nimintobiribiri toki tʼenkitarrikinoto o enkitook e pesho-- kake entaaroto kituak tiatua aten tʼenkitadounoto;"
Philippians2:4 Njoo meing'oraa oltung'ani nkun enyena ake-- kake baiki mbaak oo lkulekai."
Philippians2:5 Embung'a nkibirribirrat tiatua ndai-- anaa peata ninje Kristos Yesus--"
Philippians2:6 lotii atua emua Engai-- neitu eing'oraa anaa nkyarunot-- perisiore Engai--"
Philippians2:7 kake eitoroka kion neibung' emua osinga-- neaku anaa iltung'anak nelioi tʼorregie anaa oltung'ani;"
Philippians2:8 neitadou kion nening'ishoi metabaiki enkea-- metabaiki enkea esalaba."
Philippians2:9 Onaa-- eitaa Engai ninye kitok naleng' neisho ninye engarna nalang' nkulie arn pookin--"
Philippians2:10 pegila Tengarna e Yesus enkung'u pookin natii shumata o enkop o abori enkop--"
Philippians2:11 peibalu olng'ejep pookin-- ajo era Yesus Kristos Olaitoriani-- peitaa kitok Engai Menye."
Philippians2:12 Akae-- lanyor lainei-- anaa pitoning'o oshi-- neme enkata ake natii-- kake naleng' taata matii-- entaa enkitopuata inyi tʼenkuretishu o tʼenkikirikirata."
Philippians2:13 Amu Engai naitobir tiatua ndai eyeunoto o enkitabaiaroto tʼenyorrata enye.
Philippians2:14 Entaas pookin metii enking'unyung'unyata o enking'arrirro--"
Philippians2:15 piakuku nkera Engai nemeata entioto ana esungureishu-- nemetii embuakinoto-- tiatua ena kishon torrono nariwuo; ore tiatua ninje ilang'ishosho anaa nkilang'eta olmaa--"
Philippians2:16 tiaraki nimbung'arere ororei lʼempuan-- paaitadarari tʼengolong' e Kristos anaa oleitu ekwet pesho-- neitu eitobirisho pesho."
Philippians2:17 Ten ake aaibukori shumata enkidasare o enkisyayare enkirukoto inyi-- ang'ida nang'ida te nebo o ndai pookin."
Philippians2:18 Enting'idata si ndai too nena-- o te nebo o nanu."
Philippians2:19 Kake aisilig tʼOlaitoriani Yesus-- ajo airriwaki ndai Timoteos asioki-- patum si nanu enjipai-- ten ayolou enitiuu."
Philippians2:20 Amu maata olekai laanyanyukie nanu-- oshilaa tʼolbae linyi tʼenyorrunoto naba nji."
Philippians2:21 Amu eing'oru pookin nkun enye-- me en e Kristos."
Philippians2:22 Kake iyololo ndai-- aajo ninye supat; amu aataretoko anaa enkerai menye too lomon lʼeng'ida."
Philippians2:23 Ninye aisilig-- ajo airriwaa nabo kata-- teni ayolou mbaak ainei eneikunari."
Philippians2:24 Kake ang'idare Olaitoriani-- ajo alotu si nanu asioki."
Philippians2:25 Kake ajo eishiaakino-- teni airriwaki ndai Epafroditos ora olalashe lai neitobir enkyas te nebo o nanu-- na osikari lʼematua ai-- neitoki aa olairriwani linyi-- peisyayaki ngolati ainei."
Philippians2:26 Amu eataiye ndai esing'ati neimuntut naleng'-- tiaraki nitoning'o ndai-- aajo etamoiya."
Philippians2:27 Amu etamoiya naleng' o metinyikaki enkea-- kake etang'adua Engai ninye; neme ninye ake-- kake si nanu-- pamatum osina aitaalie olekai sina."
Philippians2:28 Onaa-- airriwaiye ninye aitasioki-- peiye-- ten intokiki aadol ninye-- ing'idada ndai-- neitong'ori si osina lai."
Philippians2:29 Akae-- entang'amutu tiatua Olaitoriani tʼeng'ida pookin nintaata kituak iltung'anak ooba nji."
Philippians2:30 Amu tʼolbae lʼenkyas e Kristos etinyikaka enkea nemerrip empuan enye-- peitabaia enatong'oro tʼenkisyayare inyi tʼolbae lai."
Philippians3:1 Enyaaki-- lalashera lainei-- enting'idata tiatua Olaitoriani. Teni asiraki ndai il oshi rorei-- namaaitanaur ina-- kake eitagol ndai."
Philippians3:2 Eng'orai ildiain-- eng'orai laasak torrok-- eng'orai loodung'isho!"
Philippians3:3 Amu kira yook emurata-- nikisyayaki Engai tʼolmumua-- nikintadaraa aten tʼolbae le Kristos-- nimiking'idare enkiring'o--"
Philippians3:4 ten ake aata si nanu-- pang'idare enkiring'o. Teni ejo olekai tung'ani-- eidim ating'idare enkiring'o-- nalang' nanu naleng':"
Philippians3:5 Aatumurataki tʼengolong e isiet-- nara lʼolorere le Israel-- lʼentipat e Benyamin-- Olhebrayos oing'ua Ilhebrayoi; tʼempukunoto oo nkitanapat ara Olfarisayos--"
Philippians3:6 tʼenyuata-- atimira esirit-- ore t'esupato naing'ua nkitanapat-- namaata entibili."
Philippians3:7 Kake enataa endupoto te nanu-- aikena aa enkiminata tʼolbae le Kristos."
Philippians3:8 Eton aiken nona pookin aa enkiminata-- amu kitok naleng' eyolounoto Olaitoriani lai Yesus Kristos; ore tʼolbae lenye aikena pookin ajo enkiminata-- naitoki aiken aa olduruki-- patum Kristos--"
Philippians3:9 nalio nanu tiatua ninye-- ajo maata esupato naing'ua nkitanapat-- kake eing'ua enkirukoto e atua Kristos-- naa ninye esupato naikenaki Engai enkirukoto--"
Philippians3:10 patum atayolo ninye o enkidimata empiunoto enye o eng'arata oo nkisilot enyena-- panyanyukie enkea enye--"
Philippians3:11 nabaiki enkitopiunoto oo lootuata.
Philippians3:12 Me neijia-- ajo aidipa ainoto arashu aitabaiye; kake akwetiki-- anake atum aibung'a ina-- tiaraki naaibung'a Yesus Kristos nanu."
Philippians3:13 Lalashera-- maiken kion-- ajo aidipa aibung'a; kake aas nabo toki: arikino enatii kurum-- naitoriokinore enda natii lukunya--"
Philippians3:14 nanyok aisarisar-- pabaiki idya rishata o emasaita sidai-- naaitadolu enkipototo e shumata Engai tiatua Kristos Yesus."
Philippians3:15 Kake ore yook pookin lootabaitie-- matadamutu ina-- naa teni idamumu ndai engai bae-- enjoo eboloki Engai ndai ena--"
Philippians3:16 kake pikipuoiye ake ilo rregie likitang'amutua.
Philippians3:17 Entaa lasujak lainei-- lalashera-- eng'orai kulo loolimana neijia anaa piatata too yook enkitanyanyukiet."
Philippians3:18 Amu elimana ilkumok anaa patiaka ndai aigil kumok nalimu taata aishirita-- ajo era ninje ilmang'ati lʼesalaba e Kristos--"
Philippians3:19 nera enkiting'oto enye enkiminata-- nera engai enye engoshoke-- neata enkitook tiatua enkurruna enye-- neibirribir ntokitin enkop."
Philippians3:20 Amu etii entonata ang' shumata nikianyu te inalo Olaitopuani o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos
Philippians3:21 olaitaal osesen lang' lʼenkitadounoto-- petum atanyanyukie osesen lenye lʼenkitook-- tʼenkidimata naidimie ninye atipika ntokitin pookin abori enye."
Philippians4:1 Akae-- lalashera lainei lanyor-- laataiye esing'ati-- lirara eng'ida o enkaja ai-- entashoito tiatua Olaitoriani-- lanyor lainei."
Philippians4:2 Asai Evodia-- nasai Sintike-- peata endamunoto nabo tiatua Olaitoriani."
Philippians4:3 Ee-- aasai si iye-- ol emboitei ai-- taretoki nena kituak naataarare tʼolbae loo lomon lʼeng'ida te nebo o nanu-- o Klemens o ilkulekai aretok lainei ootii ngam enye enkitabu empuan."
Philippians4:4 Enting'idata tiatua Olaitoriani oshi ake! Naitoki ajo: Enting'idata!
Philippians4:5 Njeyolouni emborran inyi too ltung'anak pookin! Etaanu Olaitoriani.
Philippians4:6 Emiekenya te toki-- kake enjoo-- peyolou Engai oshi yeunot inyi tʼesayata o tʼeropare te nebo o elikinoto e ashe."
Philippians4:7 Ore eseriani Engai nalang' eng'eno pookin-- njerrip iltauja linyi o ndamunot inyi tiatua Kristos Yesus."
Philippians4:8 Ore tʼenkiting'oto-- lalashera-- entoki pookin nasipa-- naata enkitook-- naata esupato-- naata eshaatishu-- naiting'idisho-- elimunoto sidai-- enara orregie sidai-- enaitadarari — ninje embirribirra!"
Philippians4:9 Nona baak nintengenuote ning'amumu nining'ining'i nidolidolo te nanu-- entobira-- nebik Engai eseriani te nebo o ndai."
Philippians4:10 Ang'ida naleng' tiatua Olaitoriani-- tiaraki ninyaakitia aapiu-- pikishilaala nanu. Esipa-- itishilaitie oshi ake-- kake eitu itumutumu erishata."
Philippians4:11 Majo ena tʼolbae lʼeng'oroto; amu aiteng'enue-- paabaiki mbaak pookin natii atua."
Philippians4:12 Amu ayolo enaikununo-- teni aang'oriki toki arashu teni ebore ntokitin. Aidipakino ewueji pookin o too mbaak pookin: teni ataraposhe arashu teni aata olamei-- teni aata enkumoi arashu elaunoto."
Philippians4:13 Aidimu pookin tʼolbae le ilo-- laaidimunye-- lora Kristos."
Philippians4:14 Kake itaasa enaishiaakino-- tiaraki nikitaretokitio tiatua osina lai."
Philippians4:15 Niyololo si ndai-- le Filipi-- aajo ore tʼenkiterata euangelion-- neba enkata natupukuo Makedonia-- nemetii esirit naatang'arie esiana enkishooroto o eng'amunoto-- neme ndai ake."
Philippians4:16 Amu baiki tiatua Tesalonike kirriwakitia nanu enkata elukunya o enkata e are enataa naatumoki nanu.
Philippians4:17 Metiu ajo aing'oru enkishooroto-- kake aing'oru ilmomo-- pebore tiatua enkikenata inyi."
Philippians4:18 Amu aata pookin-- naata emborei. Aata tʼenkumoi aidipa atang'amu te Epafroditos enaing'ua ndai-- erropili sidai-- enkidasare nashipakino Engai."
Philippians4:19 Njeigany Engai ai naang'or too ndai pookin tʼerisioroto endupoto enye tiatua enkitook te Yesus Kristos.
Philippians4:20 Njeata Engai-- Papa lang'-- enkitook eiter nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin."
Philippians4:21 Eroroki sinyat pookin tiatua Kristos Yesus. Eiroroki ndai lalashera ootii e nebo o nanu.
Philippians4:22 Eiroroki ndai sinyat pookin-- naleng' lelo lʼengaji e kaisar."
Philippians4:23 Ore eng'adunoto Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos-- njebik too ndai pookin. Amen."
Colossians1:1 Paulos-- olairriwani le Yesus Kristos-- tʼeyeunoto Engai-- o olalashe Timoteos:"
Colossians1:2 Too sinyat ootii engang' e Kolosai-- o enetii lalashera airukok tiatua Kristos. Njeboitare ndai eng'adunoto o eseriani naing'ua Engai Papa lang' o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos."
Colossians1:3 Kiliki yook Engai o Menye lʼOlaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos ashe nikisayaki ndai oshi--"
Colossians1:4 kindipa aatoning' enkirukoto inyi e atua Kristos o enyorrata niatata ndai too sinyat pookin--"
Colossians1:5 tʼolbae lʼeanyunoto naitaanyaki ndai te shumata-- nindipa aatoning' opa tʼororei lʼesipata tiatua euangelion."
Colossians1:6 Eewuo enitiiti ndai-- anaa atua olmaa pookin neiu ilmomo anaa si tiatua ndai-- eiter te ina olong' nitoning'o niyolouu eng'adunoto Engai tiatua esipata;"
Colossians1:7 anaa pinteng'enuote te Epafras-- ol emboitei ang'"
Colossians1:8 etaboloko yook enyorrata inyi tʼOlmumua.
Colossians1:9 Onaa-- mikigira si yook nikisayaki ndai-- eiter te ina olong' nikitoning'o ena-- nikisai-- peiganyi ndai eyolounoto eyeunoto enye tiatua eng'eno pookin o eyolounoto emumuaishu--"
Colossians1:10 pilimanana anaa peaku tʼOlaitoriani-- metaa enting'idata pookin-- piiuu ilmomo tiatua enkitobirata sidai pookin--"
Colossians1:11 niponana tʼeyolounoto Engai nigolulu tʼengolon pookin-- tʼentemet engolon enkitook enye-- pitumutumu olng'iria pookin o olgira tʼeng'ida--"
Colossians1:12 ilikiki Papa ashe loidimunye yook eng'arata enjung'o oo sinyat tiatua enkilang'et--"
Colossians1:13 loitopua yook tiatua engolon enaimin neitobik yook tiatua enkarsishu Oinoti lʼenyorrata enye--"
Colossians1:14 nikiata tiatua ele elakunoto tʼosarge lenye-- nera enkitaunoto oo nkitarruot."
Colossians1:15 Naa ninye emua Engai nemeduai-- olkikau loo nkitobirat pookin."
Colossians1:16 Amu te ninye eitobiraki ntokitin pookin naatii shumata o naatii enkop-- naalio o nemelio-- ten aa lorikaishi loo looitore-- arashu nkitoriaitin-- arashu nkarsishuni-- arashu ngoloni; pookin eitobiraki te ninye o tʼolbae lenye."
Colossians1:17 Netii ninye tʼenkiterata oo ntokitin pookin-- netii pookin atua ninye."
Colossians1:18 Nera ninye elukunya osesen-- eji nʼesirit; ninye ora enkiterunoto o olkikau oing'ua lootuata-- peiturukie tiatua pookin."
Colossians1:19 Amu etishipakine-- pemany emborei pookin atua ninye;"
Colossians1:20 neitobirakinye pookin kion-- naatii enkop arashu naatii shumata-- tiaraki naitaa eseriani tʼosarge tʼesalaba enye tʼengalo enye openy."
Colossians1:21 Ore ndai-- lirara opa lomon o ilmang'ati tiatua ndamunot inyi tʼolbae loo asat inyi torrok--"
Colossians1:22 einotoko ndai enkitobirakinoto tʼosesen enkiring'o enye tʼenkea-- peitasheye ndai irara sinyat nimiatata entioto arashu entibili tʼengomom enye--"
Colossians1:23 ten aa ipuoiyeye enkirukoto niunokinono ninye nigoligolo-- niminjosho eibelekenyari ndai aaitung'ua eanyunoto euangelion-- nitoning'o ndai-- nainosuaki tiatua nkitobirat pookin naatii abori e shumata-- neaku ataa nanu-- Paulos-- olaisyayani lenye."
Colossians1:24 Ashipa taata tiatua sinaitin lainei tʼolbae linyi naitahaia tʼenkiring'o ai enang'oriki nkisilot e Kristos tʼosesen lenye-- lora esirit;"
Colossians1:25 naa ninye aaitaaki nanu olaisyayani lenye tʼerisioroto enkisyayare Engai-- naaishooki tiatua ndai-- paitabaia naleng' ororei lʼEngai--"
Colossians1:26 naa ninye emikio natushumaki too nkatan o lajijik le opa-- kake etabolokoki sinyat lenyena taata."
Colossians1:27 Amu etonyorra Engai aitayolo enara enkumoi sidai e ina mikio tiatua loreren lemeata Engai-- naa ninye Kristos tiatua ndai-- lora eanyunoto enkitook."
Colossians1:28 Nikinosu yook ninye nikididing' iltung'anak pookin tʼeng'eno pookin-- pikintasheye oltung'ani pookin etaa baiaroti tiatua Kristos Yesus;"
Colossians1:29 nanyamalaki nanu ina kyas nanyok tʼentemet enkidimata e ilo oitobirisho tiatua nanu tʼengolon.
Colossians2:1 Amu ayeu niyololo-- ajo keba aa eaparoto naata tʼolbae linyi o lelo le Laodikea o pookin leitu edol engomom ai tʼosesen--"
Colossians2:2 peilejileji iltauja lenye neitushuli te nebo tiatua enyorrata-- petum endupai pookin enkitabaiaroto eng'eno-- aatayolou emikio Engai Papa o ne Kristos;"
Colossians2:3 ore tiatua ninye eisudori masaa sidan pookin eng'eno o eyolounoto.
Colossians2:4 Najo kuna-- pemelej ndai oltung'ani too rorei sidan."
Colossians2:5 Amu teni matii tʼosesen-- natii e nebo o ndai tʼolmumua-- nang'ida-- teni adol orregie linyi o enkirukoto inyi nagol e atua Kristos."
Colossians2:6 Anaa pitang'amutua Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos-- neijia entilimanata tiatua ninye--"
Colossians2:7 niunokinono-- nishetakinono tiatua ninye tʼenkirukoto nagol-- neijia anaa peiteng'enaki ndai-- niponana aaliki ashe te ina."
Colossians2:8 Eng'orai-- pemeitamanimanaa ndai oltung'ani tʼenkiteng'enare arashu tʼempesho elejare tʼerisioroto eng'amunoto oo ltung'anak-- o noo rregieita lʼolmaa-- neme tʼeyeunoto e Kristos."
Colossians2:9 Amu emanya tiatua ninye emborei pookin engaishu anaa osesen.
Colossians2:10 Nirara ndai baiarot tiatua ninye lora elukunya enkitoria o engolon pookin.
Colossians2:11 Ore tiatua ninye etumurataki ndai tʼemurata neitu eitobiri too ngaik-- kake etushurtaki osesen oata nkitarruot tiatua enkiring'o-- eji tʼemurata e Kristos."
Colossians2:12 Etunukaki ndai te nebo o ninye tʼenkibatisa; ore te ninye itopiutuo si ndai tʼenkirukoto naitobir Engai-- naitopiwuo ninye too lootuata."
Colossians2:13 Einyeye si ndai te ina kata nituata tiatua nkitarruot o tiatua enkiring'o inyi nememurata-- neisho ndai empuan te nebo o Kristos-- etapalaka yook nkitarruot pookin--"
Colossians2:14 nejut esirata naitang'oro yook-- nataa too nkitanapat neibok yook; kake etoshoroiye ninye nesheiki esalaba--"
Colossians2:15 neitau enkishopo oo nkitoriaitin o looata engolon-- neitaduaia tʼewuas-- nerik ninje anaa nkyarunot-- eidipa atigilu ninje."
Colossians2:16 Eminjo eigwenakinye ndai oltung'ani endaa arashu enaoki arashu ngolong'i kituak naaje arashu lapaitin lʼenkibor arashu ngolong'i e sabato;
Colossians2:17 ore kuna baak-- naa oloip loo ntokitin e akenya; kake ole Kristos osesen."
Colossians2:18 Eminjo eiwang'ie ndai oltung'ani enjunet-- lora oloito anaa peyeu openy tʼenkitadounoto o tʼesupato oo lmalaikan-- neitu edol hoo nabo too nena-- neitaa sapuk elukunya pesho tiatua ndamunot naaing'ua enkiring'o enye--"
Colossians2:19 nemeibung'are elukunya-- naa ninye naret osesen olulung'a neisho eidikidiko te nebo neibung'aro tʼengalo oo rubat o ieneta enyena-- nebulu nji-- petum emponaroto Engai."
Colossians2:20 Teni ituata te nebo o Kristos nipalipala rregieita lʼolmaa-- ainyo pisujusuju rregieita lʼolmaa anaa loopon aaishiu tiatua olmaa?"
Colossians2:21 Ejo: mimbung' ena-- niminyorrinyor ena-- nimiporoo ena--"
Colossians2:22 naa pookin ntokitin naamuta ake tiabori oo ngaik oo ltung'anak-- nera nkitanapat o nkiteng'enareitin oo ltung'anak--"
Colossians2:23 naatiu anaa eng'eno tʼolbae lʼesinyatishu nageluno o enkitadounoto-- tiaraki nemeing'urrie osesen nemeshilaa enkiring'o-- peata ngolati enyena."
Colossians3:1 Akae-- teni itopiutuo ndai te nebo o Kristos-- eng'orutu ne shumata-- enetii Kristos lotonita te tatene Engai."
Colossians3:2 Embirribirra nara ne shumata-- me nara nʼenkop."
Colossians3:3 Amu ituata ndai netushumaki empuan inyi te nebo o Kristos tiatua Engai.
Colossians3:4 Teni elalioi Kristos-- empuan ang'-- nipuopuo aalioi si ndai te nebo o ninye tiatua enkitook."
Colossians3:5 Akae-- entaar metuata rubat inyi naatii enkop: mbaak torrok oo nkiri o olduruki o enkima o olng'warra torrono o engong'u oo masaa-- nara enkisyayare oo nkulie ain."
Colossians3:6 Tʼolbae loo kuna baak elotu engoro Engai shumata oo ltung'anak lemeiruk.
Colossians3:7 Naa tiatua ninje itilimanate si ndai opa injiuyeye ninje.
Colossians3:8 Kake ore taata-- entautu pookin too ndai: engoro o enkiba o entorroni o emoroto o ilderrat torrok tʼenkutuk inyi."
Colossians3:9 Emilejaro tiatua ndai aten! Entautu oltung'ani musana te nebo o nkyasin enyena--"
Colossians3:10 ninjopishopo oltung'ani ng'ejuk-- oitaai ng'ejuk tʼeyolounoto-- tʼerisioroto emua e ilo oitobira ninye;"
Colossians3:11 nemetii ene Olgriki arashu Oyudayos arashu omurata arashu lememurata arashu olmeeki arashu Oskite arashu osinga arashu ololakuno-- kake era Kristos pookin netii atua pookin."
Colossians3:12 Akae-- enjopo anaa lootegeluaki lʼEngai-- sinyat o loonyorri-- iltauja lʼenkordunoto-- emborran-- enkitadounoto-- enkirobi-- olng'iria--"
Colossians3:13 ninapakinono-- ning'uaikinono-- teni eata oltung'ani enkitang'oroto tʼolekai; neijia anaa petung'aikia Olaitoriani ndai-- neijia si ndai!"
Colossians3:14 ore too kuna pookin-- enjopo enyorrata nara eenet enkitabaiaroto."
Colossians3:15 Njeitorisho eseriani e Kristos tiatua iltauja linyi-- ndai looipotokoki atua ninye tiatua osesen obo-- niakuku loobore ashe."
Colossians3:16 Njebik ororei le Kristos tiatua ndai tʼemborei-- ninteng'enaroro nididing'aroro tʼeng'eno pookin-- niranyakiki Engai too ltauja linyi too singolioitin lʼengauo o too singolioitin lʼenkitadararoto o too singolioitin sidan lʼolmumua."
Colossians3:17 Ore pookin nintobiribiri tʼororei arashu tʼenkyas-- entobira kuna pookin tʼengarna Olaitoriani Yesus-- pilikiki ashe Engai Menye te ninye."
Colossians3:18 Ndai-- nang'oroyok-- entoning' ilmoruak linyi-- anaa peitoriori tʼOlaitoriani."
Colossians3:19 Ndai-- lemoruak-- entonyor ng'oroyok inyi-- emiaku pushunot too ninje."
Colossians3:20 Ndai-- nakera-- entoning' lootoiutuo ndai too ntokitin pookin; amu ena naiting'id Olaitoriani."
Colossians3:21 Ndai loomenye-- emintagor nkera inyi-- pemeaku kureti."
Colossians3:22 Ndai-- laisyayak-- entoning' loora laitoriak linyi loo seseni too pookin-- me tʼenkisyayare oo ngonyek anaa looiting'id iltung'anak-- kake too ltauja lemeata olosek niurere Olaitoriani."
Colossians3:23 Ore pookin enintobiribiri-- too ltauja entobirakiti anaa Olaitoriani-- me anaa iltung'anak--"
Colossians3:24 niyololo-- aajo ipuopuo aatum elaakinoto enjung'o tʼOlaitoriani; amu isyayakiki Olaitoriani Kristos."
Colossians3:25 Kake ore oloitobir entorroni-- nelang'amu entorroni naitobira; amu meing'oraa Engai entemet oltung'ani."
Colossians4:1 Ore ndai-- laitoriak-- enkunakiti laisyayak linyi naaishiaakino o naarisiore-- niyololo aajo-- iatata si ndai Olaitoriani te shumata."
Colossians4:2 Entonyok tʼesayata-- ninjolololo tʼenkishooroto e ashe--"
Colossians4:3 niomonokiki si yook pookin-- peboloki yook Engai kutukaji ororei-- nikilimu emikio e Kristos-- amu ina aateenyeki--"
Colossians4:4 paibalunye ninye neija anaa pemeata kata namalimu.
Colossians4:5 Entilimanata tʼeng'eno tʼengomom oo kulo lootii aulo ninyang'unyenye enkata.
Colossians4:6 Enjoo eborru ororei linyi netipikaki emakat pejing'aa tʼenkata pookin-- piyololo eninkoko-- pindimidimi aaishoo ealet naitoriori oltung'ani pookin."
Colossians4:7 Eitayolo ndai Tukikos mbaak ainei pookin-- naa ninye olalashe lanyor o olaisyayani supat o osinga te nebo o nanu tiatua Olaitoriani--"
Colossians4:8 lairriwaka ndai-- peyolou-- eninkununono-- neilejilej nediding' iltauja linyi--"
Colossians4:9 te nebo o Onesimos-- olalashe supat naa kirotet-- lora obo linyi. Eitayolo ndai mbaak pookin naataa tʼene."
Colossians4:10 Eiroroki ndai Aristarkos loena anaa nanu-- o Markos-- ol enganashe e Barnabas-- lora ninye itang'amarie nkitanapat naaje; teni elotu enitiiti ndai-- entang'amutu ninye--"
Colossians4:11 o Yesus oji Yustos-- loora lʼemurata. Nera ninje ake laretok lainei tiatua enkyas enkarsishu Engai-- nainoto enkilejilejata too ninje."
Colossians4:12 Eiroroki ndai Epafras-- lora obo linyi-- naa osinga le Kristos-- osayaki ndai oshi tʼenyuata-- pintasheshe aa baiarot neiganyaki ndai tʼeyeunoto pookin Engai."
Colossians4:13 Aijakenoki ninye-- ajo enyamalaki ndai naleng' o kulo lootii Laodikea o Hierapolis."
Colossians4:14 Eiroroki ndai Lukas-- olabaani likinyor-- o Demas si."
Colossians4:15 Eroroki lalashera ootii Laodikea o Nimfa si-- o esirit natii engaji enye."
Colossians4:16 Ore teni eidipaki aaisoma ena palai too ndai-- ninjoioio-- peisomai si tʼesirit e Laodikea-- nisomama ndai en e Laodikea--"
Colossians4:17 nijokiki Arkipos: Ng'orai enkisyayare nitang'amua tiatua Olaitoriani-- ntabai iye."
Colossians4:18 Enkirorokinoto ai Paulos-- tʼengaina ai. Entadamutu ienat ainei. Metobikie eng'adunoto ndai. Amen."
1Thessalonians1:1 Paulos o Silvanos o Timoteos: en esirit oo Ltesalonikes ena palai tiatua Engai Papa o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos. Njebikie ndai eng'adunoto o eseriani naing'ua Engai Papa lang' o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos.
1Thessalonians1:2 Kiliki Engai ashe oshi too ndai pookin nikimpot ndai tiatua sayat ang'
1Thessalonians1:3 nikidamu mikipal enkyas enkirukoto o enyamali enyorrata o olng'iria lʼeanyunoto-- nara ninye Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos tʼengomom Engai o Papa lang'."
1Thessalonians1:4 Amu kiyolo-- lalashera oonyor Engai-- anaa petegelua ndai Engai;"
1Thessalonians1:5 amu eitu ebaiki euangelion ang' ndai tʼororei ake-- kake baiki tʼengolon o tiatua Olmumua Sinyati o tʼenkitisipunoto kitok; niyololo-- neijia anaa pikinkununo too ndai tʼolbae linyi;"
1Thessalonians1:6 itaa ndai lasujak lang' o lʼOlaitoriani-- nitang'amutua ororei tiatua sinaitin kumok tʼeng'ida tiatua Olmumua Sinyati"
1Thessalonians1:7 niakuku larikok loo pookin ooiruko te Makedonia o te Akaia.
1Thessalonians1:8 Amu eibulaiye oltoilo lʼororei lʼOlaitoriani aing'ua ndai; neyolounoi enkirukoto inyi e atua Engai-- me tiatua Makedonia o Akaia ake-- kake baiki too wuejitin pookin-- nemeyeuni nikipon yook ororei."
1Thessalonians1:9 Amu eitayolo ninje oopeny eneikunakine ororei lang' too ndai te ina kata kijing' atua ndai-- anaa eninkuna ndai-- pimbelekenyakinono Engai-- nipalipala muain nemera Engai-- nisyayakiki Engai naishiu nasipa--"
1Thessalonians1:10 nianyunyu Oinoti lenye aing'ua shumata oitopiwuo ninye too lootuata-- Yesus-- loitopok yook aitung'ua engoro nalotu."
1Thessalonians2:1 Amu iyololo si ndai-- lalashera-- enjing'ata ang' te ina kata kietuo enitiiti-- ajo eitu eaku pesho;"
1Thessalonians2:2 amu ten ake kindipa aatang'amutu nkisilot o morot kumok te Filipi-- anaa eniyololo ndai-- nikiata empijan kitok tiatua Engai ang'-- pikinosaki ndai lomon lʼeng'ida kiata enara kitok."
1Thessalonians2:3 Amu ore enkitaduaroto ang' eitu eaku tʼenkitapong'oroto arashu tʼolduruki arashu tʼolosek;
1Thessalonians2:4 kake anaa peishoo yook Engai-- pikinosu lomon lʼeng'ida-- neijia kilimu; neme pikintiship iltung'anak-- kake Engai naleen oltau lang'."
1Thessalonians2:5 Amu eitu ai kata kiimaki rorei lʼolosek-- anaa piyololo-- arashu kiata empiani naisudoro-- — Engai oljakeni lang' —;"
1Thessalonians2:6 neitu king'oru enkitadararoto too ltung'anak-- neme too ndai-- neme too kulekai."
1Thessalonians2:7 Amu eaku-- ten emutu kiroshikitio ndai anaa lairriwak le Kristos; kake kitoborrita yook too ndai-- anaa engaibung'ani naitoti nkera enyena."
1Thessalonians2:8 Neijia kitishipakinote ndai naleng' nikitonyorra yook aaishoo ndai-- me lomon lʼeng'ida ake-- kake iltauja lang' si-- tiaraki nikitonyorra ndai naleng'."
1Thessalonians2:9 Ajo nanu idamumu-- lalashera-- enyamali o enyuata ang'; amu kintobira enkyas dama o kiarie-- pemikiek oltung'ani too ndai nikinosu too ndai lomon lʼeng'ida lʼEngai."
1Thessalonians2:10 Irara ndai iljaken-- naa si ninye Engai-- enikinkunari too ndai tʼesinyatishu o t'esupato-- nimikiata entioto--"
1Thessalonians2:11 niyololo-- aajo anaa eikunaki menye nkera enyena-- neijia kitididing'a nikilejilej"
1Thessalonians2:12 nikinjakenoki si yook oltung'ani pookin too ndai-- pilimanana ndai aaitoriokino Engai-- naipotoko ndai enkarsishu o enkitook enye."
1Thessalonians2:13 Onaa kiliki Engai ashe mikipal-- amu ore ping'amumu ororei lʼEngai likinosakitia yook ndai-- neitu ing'amumu anaa ororei loo ltung'anak-- kake anaa ororei lʼEngai-- anaa pera tʼesipata-- naitobirisho tiatua ndai liruko."
1Thessalonians2:14 Amu ore ndai-- lalashera-- itaa lasujak loo sirito naatii Yudaya tiatua Kristos Yesus-- tiaraki ninoto si ndai enkisiloto too ltung'anak lʼenkishomi inyi-- anaa peinoto ninje too Yudayoi."
1Thessalonians2:15 Etara Olaitoriani Yesus o layolounok ootupukutuo too ninje-- nemir si yook-- nemeitiship Engai neapare iltung'anak pookin--"
1Thessalonians2:16 nemitiki ninje yook kirorie lemeata Engai-- pepok-- neitabaia nkitarruot enye wuejitin pookin. Amu eton elotu engoro shumata enye metabaiki enkiting'oto."
1Thessalonians2:17 Kake ore yook-- lalashera-- peoruni yook ndai nimikiduare enkiti kata tʼengomom-- kake me too ltauja-- nikisarisara naleng'-- pikidol engomom inyi tʼesing'ati kitok."
1Thessalonians2:18 Akae-- kitayeutuo nikipuo enitiiti ndai (nanu Paulos)-- aigil are-- kake etomitikio satan yook."
1Thessalonians2:19 Amu kang'ai ora eanyunoto o eng'ida o enkaja ang' enkitadararoto? Mirara si ndai tʼengomom Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos tʼelotunoto enye?
1Thessalonians2:20 Amu irara ndai enkitook o eng'ida ang'.
1Thessalonians3:1 Ore peaku mekure kindim aating'iria-- nikinyor-- aajo eing'uaikini yook oopeny te Atenai"
1Thessalonians3:2 nikirriwaa Timoteos-- olalashe lang' o olaisyayani lʼEngai-- naa olaretoni lang' too lomon lʼeng'ida le Kristos-- peitagol neilejilej ndai tʼenkirukoto inyi--"
1Thessalonians3:3 pemenanau oltung'ani tiatua kulo sinaitin; amu iyololo-- aajo etipikaki yook nona."
1Thessalonians3:4 Ore en opa kata nikitii e nebo o ndai-- kitolikitio yook ndai tʼenkiterata-- aajo kipuo aatum sinaitin-- anaa petaa niyololo si ndai."
1Thessalonians3:5 Tiaraki nemekure aidim ating'iria-- nairriwaa olkilikwai-- payolou enkirukoto inyi-- pemeaku eitasur ndai olaitasuroni neaku enkyas ang' en e pesho."
1Thessalonians3:6 Kake ore pelotu Timoteos aing'ua ndai enikitii neliki yook enkirukoto inyi o enyorrata inyi-- nidamunyenve yook oshi ake too sidan niyeuu naleng' nidolidolo yook-- anaa si yook kiyeu nikidol ndai:"
1Thessalonians3:7 akae-- eilejilejaki yook-- lalashera-- tʼolbae linyi tiatua emion ang' pookin o osina lang' tʼenkirukoto inyi;"
1Thessalonians3:8 amu kinjiu yook taata-- teni intasheshe ndai tiatua Olaitoriani."
1Thessalonians3:9 Amu kaa ashe kindim aatalaaki Engai tʼolbae linyi tʼena ng'ida pookin niking'ida too ndai tʼengomom Engai ang'?
1Thessalonians3:10 Kiomon Engai naleng' dama o kiarie-- pikidol ngomomi inyi nikitum aaitobira ina natong'oro tʼenkirukoto inyi."
1Thessalonians3:11 Ore Engai Papa lang' openy o Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos-- njeitorioo ngoitoi ang' maetu enitiiti."
1Thessalonians3:12 Metoponai Olaitoriani enyorrata tiatua ndai aten o too ltung'anak pookin-- anaa eniki-tiu yook too ndai--"
1Thessalonians3:13 peitagoli iltauja linyi nemeata entibili tiatua esinyatishu tʼengomom Engai o Papa lang' metabaiki elotunoto Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos te nebo o sinyat lenyena pookin.
1Thessalonians4:1 Akae-- eng'or-- lalashera-- kisai nikididing' ndai tiatua Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos-- peiye (anaa pitang'amutua too yook-- pibikibiki tʼorregie oitoriori ninting'iding'idi Engai) iponipono aapona."
1Thessalonians4:2 Amu itayolo nkitanapat nikinjoo yook ndai tʼOlaitoriani Yesus.
1Thessalonians4:3 Amu era ena eyeunoto Engai-- esinyaroto inyi-- pipaasharere mbaak torrok oo nkiri--"
1Thessalonians4:4 peyolou oltung'ani pookin atoriku enaret enye tʼesinyaroto o too nganyiti--"
1Thessalonians4:5 me tʼenkima olng'warra anaa loreren lemeyolo Engai--"
1Thessalonians4:6 pemeitarruo oltung'ani nemelej olalashe lenye tʼenkinyang'a-- amu elalaaki Olaitoriani entorroni oo kuna pookin-- anaa pekinturuko aaliki ndai nikinjakenu."
1Thessalonians4:7 Amu eitu eipotoki yook Engai olduruki-- kake esinyaroto."
1Thessalonians4:8 Akae-- olomen ena-- memen oltung'ani-- kake Engai naishoo atua ndai Olmumua lenye Sinyati."
1Thessalonians4:9 Ore tʼenyorrata oo lalashera meaku-- pasiraki ndai-- amu eiteng'ena Engai ndai openy-- pinyorrara--"
1Thessalonians4:10 amuneijia intobirakiki baiki lalashera tiatua Makedonia pookin. Kake adiding' ndai-- lalashera-- entopon enalang';"
1Thessalonians4:11 ninyokinyoko aagira aaitobir nkun inyi nintobiribiri nkyasin inyi too ngaik inyi-- anaa pikintanapa ndai--"
1Thessalonians4:12 peiye ilimanana tʼorregie oitoriori too kulo loora le boo niming'oruru toki too ninje.
1Thessalonians4:13 Mikiyeu-- lalashera-- pimiyololo mbaak oo looirura-- pimilishilishi anaa kulekai lemeata eanyunoto."
1Thessalonians4:14 Amu teni kiruk-- aajo etua Kristos nepiu-- neijia elariku Engai te Yesus baiki kulo looirurate te nebo o ninye."
1Thessalonians4:15 Amu kiliki ndai ena tiatua ororei lʼOlaitoriani-- aajo mikipuo aaiturukie yook likinjiu-- likitelekutua te ina kata nalotu Olaitoriani-- kulo looirurate."
1Thessalonians4:16 Amu eladou te shumata ninye-- Olaitoriani-- tiatua enkipototo sapuk-- tʼoltoilo lʼolmalaika kitok-- tiatua eorunoto esekegwa Engai-- nepuo aapiu tʼenkata elukunya lootuata tiatua Kristos--"
1Thessalonians4:17 tekurum nepuoi aailepie tiatua rukenyan yook likinjiu-- likitelekutua-- te nebo o ninje-- pikipuo aanang'are Olaitoriani tʼolng'inai-- pikipuo aatii nji e nebo o Olaitoriani nkatan pookin."
1Thessalonians4:18 Elejilejaroto nji too kulo rorei.
1Thessalonians5:1 Kake ore nkatan o rishat-- lalashera-- meyeuni nasiraki ndai."
1Thessalonians5:2 Amu iyololo ndai oopeny-- aajo ore engolong' Olaitoriani elotu anaa olapurroni olotu te kiarie."
1Thessalonians5:3 Amu ore ejo ninje: osotua neserian-- nelotu entorroni nabo kata shumata enye-- anaa peinepu emion eng'oroyoni namena-- nemeidim aailanyishoi ninje."
1Thessalonians5:4 Kake ore ndai-- lalashera-- mirara ndai lʼenaimin-- peinepu ndai ina olong' anaa olapurroni."
1Thessalonians5:5 Irara ndai pookin nkera eong'an o nkera endama; mikira yook lʼenkiarie arashu lʼenaimin.
1Thessalonians5:6 Akae-- njoo mikirura anaa ilkulekai-- kake maishololoto nikitum eng'eno."
1Thessalonians5:7 Amu ore kulo ooirura-- kiarie eirura; ore loomera-- nemera kiarie."
1Thessalonians5:8 Kake ore yook likira lʼendama-- maishololoto tʼeng'eno ang'-- kinjopo elong'o enkirukoto o enyorrata-- o olkaranda lʼesekengei lʼeanyunoto nabaiki enkitopuata."
1Thessalonians5:9 Amu eitu epikaki yook Engai engoro-- kake pikitum enkitopuata tiatua Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos"
1Thessalonians5:10 otuaka yook-- peiye-- teni kinjololo arashu kirura-- kinjiu te nebo o ninye."
1Thessalonians5:11 Akae-- elejilejaroto tiatua ndai aten nishetakinono obo o olekai-- anaa eninkoko."
1Thessalonians5:12 Kake kisai yook ndai-- lalashera-- piyolouu kulo ooitobiraki ndai enkyas-- oorikito ndai tiatua Olaitoriani nediding' ndai."
1Thessalonians5:13 Entopon entonyor ninje tʼolbae lʼenkyas enye; entobik iataiyeye ninje eseriani.
1Thessalonians5:14 Kake kididing' ndai-- lalashera-- enteng'ena lemeibung' orregie oitoriori-- entagolo looshal-- entanapakinore ilmenat-- enting'iriakiti iltung'anak pookin."
1Thessalonians5:15 Eng'orai-- pemelaaki oltung'ani olekai tung'ani entorroni tʼentorroni-- kake entusuj oshi sidan-- too ndai oopeny o too ltung'anak pookin."
1Thessalonians5:16 Enting'idata oshi!
1Thessalonians5:17 Entasaishoto oade!
1Thessalonians5:18 Entejo ashe tʼentoki pookin! amu ninye eyeunoto Engai tiatua Kristos Yesus too ndai.
1Thessalonians5:19 Emiliilarie Olmumua!
1Thessalonians5:20 Emimenu eyolounoto e akenya!
1Thessalonians5:21 Entaleen pookin-- emboo si naara sidan!"
1Thessalonians5:22 Entapaashare emua entorroni pookin!
1Thessalonians5:23 Kake ore ninye-- Engai eseriani-- njesinyaa ndai tukul-- njerripoki elulung'ata inyi-- Olmumua o oltau o osesen-- meata entibili-- elotunoto Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos!"
1Thessalonians5:24 Supat oloipot ndai-- nelaitobir baiki ninye."
1Thessalonians5:25 Ndai-- lalashera lanyor-- entoomonoki yook Engai!"
1Thessalonians5:26 Eroroki lalashera pookin tʼeng'ututata sinyati!
1Thessalonians5:27 Aitanapa ndai tʼOlaitoriani-- peisomai ena palai too lalashera sinyat pookin."
1Thessalonians5:28 Ore eng'adunoto Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos-- njeboitare ndai pookin. Amen."
2Thessalonians1:1 Paulos o Silvanos o Timoteos: en esirit oo Ltesalonikes ena palai-- tiatua Engai-- Papa lang' o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos."
2Thessalonians1:2 Njeboitare ndai eng'adunoto o eseriani naing'ua Engai-- Papa lang' o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos."
2Thessalonians1:3 Meata kata nimikiliki oshi Engai ashe tʼolbae linyi-- lalashera-- anaa peaku; amu ebulu enkirukoto inyi naleng'-- nepona enyorrata oltung'ani pookin tiatua ndai pookin--"
2Thessalonians1:4 neijia ajo kintadaraa aten tʼolbae linyi tiatua sirito Engai tʼolng'iria linyi o tʼenkirukoto inyi tiatua nkisilot inyi pookin o tiatua sinaitin liting'iria--"
2Thessalonians1:5 nera olponoto lʼenkigwena supat Engai-- peiye intobirakinono aajing' enkarsishu Engai-- eitameitoi ndai baiki tʼolbae lenye--"
2Thessalonians1:6 anaa peitoriori tʼEngai-- pelaaki tʼosina kulo looisilisil ndai--"
2Thessalonians1:7 o ndai looisilisili-- eng'ieng'ata te nebo o yook-- te ina kata nalalioi Olaitoriani Yesus eing'ua shumata te nebo o ilmalaikan lʼengolon enye--"
2Thessalonians1:8 tiatua enkiwuwuoto enkima-- peisho elaata kulo lemeyolou Engai o kulo lemening' euangelion Olaitoriani lang' Yesus--"
2Thessalonians1:9 loopuo aaning' earata o erruoroto oo nkatan pookin-- nemetii engomom Olaitoriani-- nemetii enkitook engolon enye--"
2Thessalonians1:10 teni elalotu neitadarari tiatua sinyat lenyena neiputukunyokini tiatua lairukok pookin-- te ina olong-- amu eirukoki enjakenishu ang' too ndai."
2Thessalonians1:11 Onaa-- kiomonoki yook ndai Engai ang'-- peisho ninye ndai intobirakinorere ena kipototo-- neitabaia enjipakinoto pookin emborran o enkyas enkirukoto tiatua engolon--"
2Thessalonians1:12 peitadarari too ndai engarna Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos-- o ndai te ninye-- tʼeng'adunoto Engai ang' o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos."
2Thessalonians2:1 Ore tʼolbae lʼelotunoto Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos o enkiturrurroto ang' enetii ninye-- kisai ndai-- lalashera lanyor--"
2Thessalonians2:2 eminjo eiposhiposhi ndai aasioki aaing'ua ndamunot inyi-- niminjosho eiturei ndai-- neme tʼolmumua-- neme tʼororei-- neme tʼempalai natiu eing'ua yook-- ajo etabaua engolong' e Kristos."
2Thessalonians2:3 Eminjo elej ndai oltung'ani tʼorregie o obo-- amu melotu ina olong'-- neme empaashata nang'as alotu-- neboluni ele tung'ani lʼenkitarruoto-- enkerai enkiminata--"
2Thessalonians2:4 lora olmang'atinda-- neilepie kion te shumata oo pookin naji Engai arashu enda naseremi-- peitoton kion anaa Engai atua engaji sinyati Engai neitaduaia kion-- ajo ninye Engai."
2Thessalonians2:5 Midamumu-- aajo ore opa eton aboitare ndai-- atolikio ndai kuna baak?"
2Thessalonians2:6 Niyololo taata si ina naibooio ninye-- petum aibalunye tʼenkata enye."
2Thessalonians2:7 Amu eitera aitobirisho emikio entorroni-- kake etii obo oibooio taata ninye o metabana neitaini."
2Thessalonians2:8 Te ine neboluni ilo torrono-- oar Olaitoriani tʼolmumua lʼenkutuk enye-- nelaidip ninye-- teni elioi tʼelotunoto enye--"
2Thessalonians2:9 naa ilo oata elotunoto tʼerisioroto enkyas e satan te nebo o nkidimat oo muain kumok o ilponot o nkitaduat elejare--"
2Thessalonians2:10 o tʼenkitamanimanaroto atua mesupato too kulo looimin-- tiaraki neitu eng'amu enyorrata aanyor esipata neitopoki ninje."
2Thessalonians2:11 Onaa-- eirriwaki Engai ninje engolon enkitapong'oroto-- peiruk elejare--"
2Thessalonians2:12 peiye eigwenakini lemeiruk esipata-- kake eshipakino mesupato."
2Thessalonians2:13 Kake ore yook-- meata kata nimikiliki oshi Engai ashe tʼolbae linyi-- lalashera lang' kiroteti tiatua Olaitoriani-- tiaraki nategelua Engai ndai tʼenkiterunoto-- pitumutumu enkitopuata tʼesinyaroto Olmumua o tʼenkirukoto esipata;"
2Thessalonians2:14 naa ina eipotoko ndai tʼeuangelion ang'-- piakuku masaa enkitook Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos."
2Thessalonians2:15 Akae-- lalashera-- entashoito nimbung'ubung'u nena nitang'amutua-- naatolikioki ndai-- ten aa tʼororei arashu tʼempalai ang'."
2Thessalonians2:16 Ore ninye-- Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos o Engai Papa lang'-- otonyorra yook neisho enkilejilejata oo nkatan pookin o eanyunoto sidai tiatua eng'adunoto:"
2Thessalonians2:17 njediding' ninye iltauja linyi neitagol ndai tiatua enkiteng'enare o nkyasin sidan pookin.
2Thessalonians3:1 Ore enang'or-- lalashera-- entasayaki yook-- pesioki ororei lʼOlaitoriani aponari-- neitadarari anaa too ndai--"
2Thessalonians3:2 neng'adieki yook iltung'anak moda o torrok; amu me en oo lkumok enkirukoto.
2Thessalonians3:3 Kake supat Olaitoriani! elaitagol nerrip ndai tʼentorroni.
2Thessalonians3:4 Kiruk tiatua Olaitoriani ndai-- aajo enikintanap ndai-- ninkoko nipuopuo aaiko."
2Thessalonians3:5 Njeitorioki Olaitoriani iltauja linyi enyorrata Engai o olng'iria le Kristos.
2Thessalonians3:6 Kake kintanap ndai-- lalashera-- tʼengarna Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos-- pipaasharere olalashe pookin lemeibung' orregie oitoriori neme tʼenkiteng'enare nitang'amutua too yook."
2Thessalonians3:7 Amu iyololo ndai oopeny eninkoko-- pisujusuju yook; amu eitu kimposha too ndai--"
2Thessalonians3:8 neitu kinya endaa oltung'ani o obo pesho-- kake kintobira dama o kiarie nkyasin tʼenyamali o tʼosina-- pimikiroshiki obo linyi--"
2Thessalonians3:9 me-- tiaraki nimikiata engolon-- kake pikinjo ndai enkiteng'enare-- pisujusuju yook."
2Thessalonians3:10 Amu te ina kata nikitii atua ndai-- kintanapa ndai ena-- ajo teni meyeu neitobir oltung'ani enkyas-- njoo medaa."
2Thessalonians3:11 Amu kining'-- aajo etii atua ndai looibung' orregie lemeitoriori nemeitobir enkyas-- kake eitobir mbaak nemeaku."
2Thessalonians3:12 Kake kintanap lelo nikididing' ninje tiatua Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos-- peitobir enkyas tʼolgira nenya endaa enye openy."
2Thessalonians3:13 Ndai-- lalashera-- eminaura intobiribiri sidan."
2Thessalonians3:14 Teni etii oltung'ani lemening' ororei lang'-- entayolo ele tung'ani nimiatata eng'arata o ninye-- pekurru ninye."
2Thessalonians3:15 Kake eminkenaki ninye anaa olmang'atinda-- kake entididing' anaa olalashe linyi."
2Thessalonians3:16 Ore ninye-- Olaitoriani lʼeseriani-- njeisho ndai eseriani oshi too ngoitoi kumok. Njebik Olaitoriani te nebo o ndai!"
2Thessalonians3:17 Enkirorokinoto tʼengaina ai nanu Paulos; naa ilo olponoto lai tiatua mpala pookin; asir aiko nji.
2Thessalonians3:18 Njebik eng'adunoto Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos tiatua ndai pookin. Amen.
1Timothy1:1 Paulos-- olairriwani le Yesus Kristos tʼenkitanapata Engai-- Olaitopuani lang'-- o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos lora eanyunoto ang':"
1Timothy1:2 en ino-- Timoteos-- enkerai ai nasipa tʼenkirukoto-- eng'adunoto o enkordunoto o eseriani naing'ua Engai-- Papa lang'-- o Yesus Kristos-- Olaitoriani lang'."
1Timothy1:3 Anaa idya naaitanapa iye-- pibik te Efesos enkata nalo Makedonia-- nintanap kulekai-- pemeiteng'en nkulie baak--"
1Timothy1:4 nemening' natinin e opa o noo lmakui nemeata enkiting'oto-- naayau nkilikwanat nelang' enjetakinoto e atua Engai tiatua enkirukoto."
1Timothy1:5 Kake enkitabaiaroto oo nkitanapat-- naa enyorrata naing'ua oltau oibor o oltoilo sidai lʼoltau o enkirukoto nemeata esungureishu."
1Timothy1:6 Ore kulekai etapaasha nona neibelekenyakino ororei le pesho--"
1Timothy1:7 neyeu neaku laiteng'enak lʼesipata-- nemeyolo enalimu arashu enaitasheye."
1Timothy1:8 Kake kiyolo-- aajo sidan nkitanapat-- teni eitobir oltung'ani abaraki--"
1Timothy1:9 neyolou ena-- ajo eitu epiki tʼoltung'ani supat-- kake etipikaki too looitobir ntorrok o lemening'isho-- too lemeure Engai o laitarruok-- too lemesinyari o looimaki engarna Engai pesho-- too lootara menye o lootara ng'otonye-- o laarak metuata--"
1Timothy1:10 o looitobir mbaak torrok oo nkiri-- o looisokorisho-- o loopur iltung'anak-- o lalejak-- o looituruj elejisho-- o teni etii olekai bae lemenyanyukie enkiteng'enare naishiuniisho--"
1Timothy1:11 tʼerisioroto euangelion kitok Engai tesh-- naaishooki nanu-- painosu."
1Timothy1:12 Aliki ashe Kristos Yesus-- Olaitoriani lang'-- Aaitagolo-- amu aatadua ara airukoni naapik atua enkisyayare--"
1Timothy1:13 lara tʼenkata elukunya olamoroni o olamirani o olaotikinoni loo ntorrok; kake aaibung'akaki engoshoke nanana-- amu aitobira opa nena mayolo-- maata enkirukoto."
1Timothy1:14 Kake etaa kitok naleng' empuris Olaitoriani lang' te nebo o enkirukoto o enyorrata natii atua Kristos Yesus.
1Timothy1:15 Esipa ele rorei neaku-- peng'amu pookin-- ajo eewuo Kristos Yesus atua olmaa-- peitopok laitarruok-- naa nanu ol elukunya lenye."
1Timothy1:16 Kake te ina aaibung'akaki engoshoke nanana-- peitadolu Yesus Kristos tʼenkata elukunya tiatua nanu olng'iria pookin-- peaku entoki enkiteng'enare oo kulo loopuo aairuk ninye-- petum empuan oo nkatan pookin."
1Timothy1:17 Njetum olkarsis loo nkatan pookin o Engai nabo ng'en-- nemerruoio-- nemelio-- enganyit o enkitook nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin."
1Timothy1:18 Ena enkitanapata naaisho iye-- enkerai ai Timoteos-- tʼerisioroto oo nkitayolounot nitang'asa atum-- piarare enjore sidai tiatua ninje--"
1Timothy1:19 niata enkirukoto o oltoilo sidai lʼoltau-- naa ninje eiturraitie kulekai-- netigile emeili enkirukoto enye."
1Timothy1:20 Ore too lelo naa Humenayos o Aleksandros-- laitarasaka satan-- peiboiori nememorisho."
1Timothy2:1 Akae-- adiding'isho-- peitaai tʼenkata elukunya oo ntokitin pookin omonot-- sayat-- sayakinot-- ashen too ltung'anak pookin--"
1Timothy2:2 too lkarsisi o too pookin looata engolon-- pekiata empuan girati o nʼeseriani tʼorregie lʼEngai o tʼenkishaa pookin."
1Timothy2:3 Amu sidai ena neiting'idisho tʼengomom Engai-- Olaitopuani lang'--"
1Timothy2:4 loyeu nepok iltung'anak pookin nepuonu atua eyolounoto esipata.
1Timothy2:5 Amu etii Engai nabo netii olaidikidikoni obo lʼEngai o loo ltung'anak-- oji oltung'ani Kristos Yesus--"
1Timothy2:6 loishooiye kion-- peaku elakunoto too pookin-- enjakenishu too nkatan enye;"
1Timothy2:7 te ina aaitaaki olkilikwai o olairriwani-- (airo esipata-- malejisho) o olaiteng'enani loo loreren lemeata Engai tiatua enkirukoto o esipata."
1Timothy2:8 Akae-- ayeu nesaisho leak tʼewueji pookin neilepie ngaik sinyat-- metii engoro o enking'arrirroto."
1Timothy2:9 Neija si ng'oroyok-- njekaj aten tʼolkila oikishaan te nebo o nganyiti o eng'eno bioto-- neme tʼenjetata oo lpapit o tʼeikare e sahabu o noo lulu arashu tʼenkishopoto oo lkilani oogol enkinyang'a--"
1Timothy2:10 kake anaa peaku too ng'oroyok naaibalu enkuretishu Engai too nkitobirat sidan.
1Timothy2:11 Ore eng'oroyoni-- njeiteng'enuo tʼolgira o tʼening'oto."
1Timothy2:12 Maisho eng'oroyoni eiteng'enisho-- arashu eitore olee-- kake njegira."
1Timothy2:13 Amu Adam etang'asaki aaitobir-- neitokini Eva."
1Timothy2:14 Eitu eleji Adam-- kake eng oroyoni etelejaki-- neau enkitarruoto."
1Timothy2:15 Kake eitopoki tʼeishoi oo nkera-- teni ebik ninje tiatua enkirukoto o enyorrata o esinyatishu te nebo o eng'eno bioto."
1Timothy3:1 Esipa ele rorei: teni eyeu oltung'ani enkyas olaing'orani lʼesirit-- nesuj enkyas sidai."
1Timothy3:2 Ore si ninye olaing'orani-- njoo meata eleyata-- neaku olmoruo lʼeng'oroyoni nabo-- lememera-- loata eng'eno aitabaia-- lobaraki-- olaitinyikunoni loo lomon-- oloyolo aiteng'enisho--"
1Timothy3:3 me olaokoni lʼolmarua-- me olaarani-- me olong'oroki kion too ntorrok-- kake olobor-- olgirati-- lemenyor ngoshola--"
1Timothy3:4 loitasheiki engaji enye sidai-- neata nkera naaning'isho tʼenganyit pookin."
1Timothy3:5 Teni eaku meidim oltung'ani aitasheiki engaji enye-- kaji eiko teni eitasheiki esirit Engai?"
1Timothy3:6 nemeaku olng'ejuk lʼenkirukoto-- pemeitaa sapuk elukunya nebatata atua enkigwena e satan."
1Timothy3:7 Meata kata nemeata si enjakenishu sidai too kulo lootii boo-- pemebatata atua emoroto neitoki atua erreshet e satan."
1Timothy3:8 Neijia si laisyayak lʼesirit-- njeaku loobor-- lemeata ilng'ejepa aare-- nemeok enaisho naleng'-- nemeata olorok loo masaa--"
1Timothy3:9 looata emikio enkirukoto tiatua ndamunot naaibor.
1Timothy3:10 Ore kulo njeng'asi aaleen-- peishori tekurum enkisyayare-- teni enyorrikini meata eleyata."
1Timothy3:11 Neijia si ng'oroyok enye-- njeata nganyiti-- nemekurrisho-- nerrip aten-- naara supati too ntokitin pookin."
1Timothy3:12 Ore laisyayak-- njeaku pookin obo olmoruo lʼeng'oroyoni nabo-- naa looitasheiki nkera enye o ngajijik enye aabaraki."
1Timothy3:13 Ore looisyaisho sidai-- netumoki aten enkitook sidai neata enkiteunoto sapuk tʼenkirukoto e atua Kristos."
1Timothy3:14 Aatisiraka iye kuna baak nairuk-- ajo alotu enitii asioki."
1Timothy3:15 Kake teni aimutie naleng'-- pitum atayolo orregie limbung' tiatua engaji Engai-- naa ninye esirit Engai naishiu-- eng'apet o entonata esipata."
1Timothy3:16 Naa kitok naleng' peinosuni ena mikio engaishu: Ninye oloibalunyeki tiatua osesen-- neitaaki supat tʼolmumua-- nelioi too lmalaikan-- neinosuni tiatua loreren lemeata Engai-- neiruki tʼolmaa-- neng'amari te shumata."
1Timothy4:1 Kake ejo Olmumua aibalunye-- ajo tiatua nkatan enkiting'oto epuo aarrinyo kulekai aaing'ua enkirukoto-- neibung'are ilmumuan enkitamanimanaroto o nkiteng'enareitin oo loiriruani."
1Timothy4:2 Amu etelejaki tʼolosek loo kulo ooiro elejare-- ootapejoki olmishire tiatua ndamunot enye--"
1Timothy4:3 nemitiki iltung'anak eamisho-- nemitiki enya ndaikin naaitobira Engai-- peng'amu lairukok o looyolou esipata ninje te ashe."
1Timothy4:4 Amu era enkitobirata Engai pookin sidai-- nemetii enaiturrari nang'amuni te ashe;"
1Timothy4:5 amu esinyari tʼororei lʼEngai o tʼesayata.
