1Timothy4:6 Teni intanap lalashera kuna-- niaku olaisyayani sidai le Kristos Yesus oitubuluaki too rorei lʼenkirukoto o lʼenkiteng'enare sidai nitusuja oshi."
1Timothy4:7 Tapaasha natinin e pesho oo ntasati. Ntamoo kion orregie lʼEngai.
1Timothy4:8 Amu eishoru emokunoto osesen endupoto kinyi-- kake eata emokunoto Engai endupoto too ntokitin pookin-- neata enkisiligata empuan e taata o enalaaku."
1Timothy4:9 Esipa ele rorei neaku penyorruni naleng'.
1Timothy4:10 Amu kinyamal te ina nikinyok aang'idare Engai naishiu-- ora Olaitopuani loo ltung'anak pookin-- naleng' loo lairukok."
1Timothy4:11 Ntanapa kuna-- nteng'enu!"
1Timothy4:12 Minjo eiba oltung'ani enkitishu ino! kake taa enkiteng'enare too lairukok tiatua ororei-- tiatua orregie-- tiatua enyorrata-- tiatua Olmumua-- tiatua enkirukoto-- tiatua eshaatishu."
1Timothy4:13 Metabana nalotu-- tonyua tʼenkisoma-- tʼendiding'aroto-- tʼenkiteng'enare!"
1Timothy4:14 Mirikino enkishooroto nikinjooki tʼenkitayolounoto-- kinteleikitia ilpaiyani ngaik."
1Timothy4:15 Nena tishilarie-- tamokunore-- pipona tiatua ntokitin pookin aibalunye."
1Timothy4:16 Torripo kion o enkiteng'enare; tobikie nena baak. Amu teni inko neijia-- nintopok kion o kulo likining'."
1Timothy5:1 Milepilepaki olpaiyan-- kake tididing'a ninye anaa minyi lino-- o ilmurran anaa lalashera--"
1Timothy5:2 nkituak tasati anaa noo yeiyo-- nkutiti anaa nganashera inono tʼeshaatishu pookin."
1Timothy5:3 Ntaa kituak ngolia naara!
1Timothy5:4 Kake teni eata engoliai nkera arashu nkera oo ltoiye lenye-- njeng'as ninje aaiteng'enuo aten-- peyolo aaitadua enkisyayare Engai too ngajijik enye nelaaki lootoiutuo ninje too sidan-- amu ina sidai tʼengomom Engai neiting'id ninye."
1Timothy5:5 Enara oliai-- nebik openy neanyu Engai-- nebik tiatua eomonoto dama o kiarie."
1Timothy5:6 Amu enabik tiatua olng'warra-- netua eishiu."
1Timothy5:7 Ntanapa kuna baak-- pebik meata eleyata!"
1Timothy5:8 Teni meshilaa oltung'ani ilkulenyena o naleng' kulo l'engaji enye-- eisimua ele enkirukoto naa torrono nelang' olemeiruk."
1Timothy5:9 Minjo egeluni engoliai neitu ebaiki larin ntomoni ile-- natii opa eng'oroyoni olmoruo obo--"
1Timothy5:10 neijakenoki nkyasin sidan ninye-- teni eitubulua nkera-- neitoomon lomon-- neisuj isinyat nkejek-- neretoki looata osina-- nesuj enkyas sidai pookin-- peitobir."
1Timothy5:11 Kake ore ngolia kutiti-- tapala-- amu teni ewuasare Kristos-- neyeu neami--"
1Timothy5:12 neata enkigwena-- ajo eiturraitie en opa kirukoto elukunya."
1Timothy5:13 Neitoki aaku turua nemoku emanaa too ngajijik. Neme turua ake-- kake era si noopeny olderra o rorei loo nkurrat-- neiro mbaak nemeaku."
1Timothy5:14 Akae-- ayeu ngolia kutiti neami-- neiu nkera-- neing'oraa ngajijik enye-- nemeisho ele mang'atinda eng'asiata namorishore."
1Timothy5:15 Amu eidipa kulie aatorrinyoto aatusuj satan.
1Timothy5:16 Kake teni eata olairukoni arashu engairukoni ngolia-- njeshilaa ninje-- nemeisho eek esirit-- petum nena olia naara-- enabaiki."
1Timothy5:17 Njoo eitaai kituak aigil are kulo aigwenak looitasheiki sidai-- naleng' kulo loonyok tʼororei o tʼenkiteng'enare."
1Timothy5:18 Amu ejo esirata: meenai enkutuk olkiteng' loidong'isho; neitoki: Eaku-- petum olaitobirani olkwaje lenye."
1Timothy5:19 Teni eitang'ori olaigwenani-- ming'amu ena kitang'oroto-- neme teni etii iljaken aare arashu okuni."
1Timothy5:20 Ore looitarruo-- ngwenaki tʼengomom oo pookin-- peureisho si ilkulekai."
1Timothy5:21 Aijakenu tʼengomom Engai o Kristos Yesus o ilmalaikan gelunot lʼEngai-- pimbung' nena baak-- miata enyorunoto arashu enkitooroto."
1Timothy5:22 Minteleiki oltung'ani ngaik asioki! Ming'ar nkitarruot oo lkulekai tung'anak! Torripo kion-- pibik aa shaat!"
1Timothy5:23 Mintoki taata aok engare-- kake tooko enkiti aisho tʼolbae lʼengoshoke ino-- tiaraki nimoi aigil kumok."
1Timothy5:24 Ore nkitarruot oo kulekai tung'anak edoli nabokata-- netum earata tʼenkiterata; nelioi nkitarruot oo kulekai tekurum."
1Timothy5:25 Neijia etiu si nkitobirat sidan oo kulekai edoli tʼenkiterata-- nemeidim aaisudoroto nkulie."
1Timothy6:1 Ore singan pookin ootii abori enjata-- njeiken laitoriak lenye tʼenganyit pookin-- pememori engarna Engai o enkiteng'enare."
1Timothy6:2 Ore lelo-- looata laitoriak ooiruk-- nememenaa tiaraki nara lalashera; kake eikash-- teni epon ninje aaisyayaki ninje-- amu era ninje lairukok naa kiroteti oong'ar emunyani. Nteng'ena kuna baak nididing'!"
1Timothy6:3 Teni eiteng'en oltung'ani nkulie baak nemebik tiatua rorei ooi-shiuniisho lʼOlaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos o tiatua enkiteng'enare narisiore orregie lʼEngai--"
1Timothy6:4 neiteija ilo elukunya pesho-- nemeyolo toki-- neata emoiyan naaunye nkikilikwanat o njangarrin-- naapukunye engilata e tau-- enkitarrikino-- emoroto-- elapo torrono--"
1Timothy6:5 olarrabal loo ltung'anak ooitarruoitie eng'eno enye netooruoki esipata-- loodamu-- aajo orregie lʼEngai etumie endupoto. Tapaashare looba nji!"
1Timothy6:6 Kake era emokunoto Engai o engiraishu oo naatai-- engong'u sapuk endupoto;"
1Timothy6:7 amu eitu kiau toki atua olmaa-- eibala-- ajo mikindim aaea toki."
1Timothy6:8 Ore pikiata ndaikin o ilkilani-- matigirata too nena."
1Timothy6:9 Ore kulo looyeu neaku ladupak-- neurokino atua enkitasuroto o erreshet o ilng'warraitin kumok lʼemodaishu o looata enkitameito looitadoiki iltung'anak atua erruoroto o enkiminata."
1Timothy6:10 Amu era enyorrata oo ngoshola entonata oo ntorrok pookin-- neng'war kulekai ena neimalimal neing'ua enkirukoto nepej aten too mioitin kumok."
1Timothy6:11 Kake iye-- letung'ani lʼEngai-- kweta kuna! Tonyoku esupato-- emokunoto Engai-- enkirukoto-- enyorrata-- olng'iria-- emborran!"
1Timothy6:12 Taarai tʼearata sidai enkirukoto-- mbung'a empuan oo nkatan pookin nikimpotieki nimbalu enkibalunoto sidai tʼengomom oo ljaken kumok."
1Timothy6:13 Aaitanap iye tʼengomom Engai naisho pookin enkishui-- o tʼengomom e Yesus Kristos oijakenuo tʼengomom e Pontius Pilatos enkibalunoto sidai;"
1Timothy6:14 mbung'a enkitanapata-- metii entibili nemetii enkitadiata-- metabana neaku elioroto Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos--"
1Timothy6:15 naitadol tʼenkata enye ilo lora tesh-- naa ninye oata engolon pookin ake-- ora olkarsis loo lkarsisi pookin o Olaitoriani loo laitoriak pookin--"
1Timothy6:16 naa ninye ake lemee-- omany tiatua eong'an enemeidim atijing'a oltung'ani-- neitu edol oltung'ani ninye nemeidim atadua; enenye enkitook o enkarsishu oo nkatan pookin. Amen."
1Timothy6:17 Ntanapa ladupak lootii atua ele maa-- pemewuasa-- pemeiruk masaa naaibelibel-- kake Engai naishiu-- naitarasaki yook pookin tʼenkumoi-- pekisotu tʼeng'ida--"
1Timothy6:18 peitobir ninje sidan-- netum endupai oo nkitobirat sidan-- neishooio tʼeng'ida-- neretisho--"
1Timothy6:19 neiturrur aten masaa naaku entonata sidai e idya nalotu-- neibung' empuan nasipa."
1Timothy6:20 Iye-- Timoteos-- torripo kuna nikinjooki-- tanya rorei le pesho lʼentung'anishu o njangarrin eyolounoto elejare--"
1Timothy6:21 amu etusuja kulekai nena neiminye enkirukoto. Njoo kiboitare eng'adunoto. Amen.
2Timothy1:1 Paulos-- olairriwani le Yesus Kristos tʼeyeunoto Engai tʼerisioroto enkisiligata empuan tiatua Kristos Yesus:"
2Timothy1:2 en ino-- Timoteos-- enkerai ai nanyor-- eng'adunoto o enkordunoto o eseriani naing'ua Engai Papa o Kristos Yesus-- Olaitoriani lang'."
2Timothy1:3 Aliki Engai ashe naomon neba opa tʼentonai oo lakuyani lang' too ndamunot sidan-- anaa enaadamu iye namapal dama o kiarie--"
2Timothy1:4 nayeu naadol iye-- teni adamu ilkiyo linono-- paaigany eng'ida;"
2Timothy1:5 amu adamu enkirukoto ino nasipa natii atua iye-- naitera opa amany tiatua koko ino Lois o tiatua ng'utunyi Oinike-- nayolo-- ajo tiatua iye si."
2Timothy1:6 Te ina bae aaitadamu iye-- pinyeye enkishooroto Engai natii atua iye tʼenkiteleikinoto oo ngaik ainei."
2Timothy1:7 Amu eitu eisho Engai yook Olmumua lʼenkuretishu-- kake Olmumua lʼengolon o lʼenyorrata o lʼenkitoriokinoto."
2Timothy1:8 Onaa-- mining' enkurruna te nanu-- oloena lenye-- kake ting'iria too nkisilot tʼolbae lʼeuangelion-- anaa nanu-- tʼerisioroto engolon Engai--"
2Timothy1:9 naitopua neipotoki yook tʼenkipototo sinyati-- me tʼolbae loo nkitobirat ang'-- kake tʼeotikinoto enye o eng'adunoto naishooki yook tiatua Kristos Yesus-- eton eitu eiteruni olmaa;"
2Timothy1:10 neibalunyeki taata tʼelioroto Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos-- oiminye engolon enkea neitupukoki atua enkilang'et empuan o entiinoto nemerruoio tʼeuangelion--"
2Timothy1:11 naatipikaki nanu-- mataa olainosunoni o olairriwani o olaiteng'enani loo loreren lemeata Engai."
2Timothy1:12 Te ilo bae atum kuna kisilot; kake maning' enkurruna too ninje-- amu ayolo olairuk-- naaitisipuni-- ajo aaidim atorripoki nena naaishooki-- metabaiki ina olong'."
2Timothy1:13 Mbung'a naleng' enkiteng'enare oo rorei ooishiuniisho Etoning'o te nanu-- tiatua enkirukoto o enyorrata natii atua Kristos Yesus."
2Timothy1:14 Ina kishooroto sidai torripo tʼeretokinoto Olmumua Sinyati-- omany tiatua yook."
2Timothy1:15 Iyolo ele rorei-- ajo aatalamare nanu pookin ootii Asia; naa too ninje si Filipos o Ermogenes."
2Timothy1:16 Metokordu Olaitoriani engaji e Onesiforos-- amu aaitishipa aigil kumok neitu ening' enkurruna too nkeenda ainei;"
2Timothy1:17 kake ore etii Roma-- aaing'orua naleng' naainoto."
2Timothy1:18 Njeisho Olaitoriani-- petum ninye enkordunoto tʼOlaitoriani te ina olong'; iyolo si iye-- keba aa nkyasin aaisyayaka te Efesos."
2Timothy2:1 Ore iye-- nakerai ai-- tagolo tiatua eng'adunoto e atua Kristos Yesus."
2Timothy2:2 Kuna limot nitoning'o te nanu too ljaken kumok-- njoo kulekai tung'anak supati-- ooata eyolounoto-- peiteng'en si ilkulekai."
2Timothy2:3 Tang'ara enkisiloto te nebo o nanu anaa olmurrani supat le Yesus Kristos.
2Timothy2:4 Metii osikari olo enjore oitushulaki kion mbaak ena kop-- amu eyeu neitiship ilo otisiraka ninye enkyas osikari."
2Timothy2:5 Ore tʼenkiguran-- baiki teni eapare oltung'ani-- nemetum enkaja-- neme teni eapare osupatei."
2Timothy2:6 Meata kata nemetum olaturoni lotur enkuruma-- ilmomo tʼenkiterata. Tumuso naleng' enajo!"
2Timothy2:7 Amu kinjo Olaitoriani eng'eno tiatua mbaak pookin.
2Timothy2:8 Tadamu Yesus Kristos-- otopiwuo too lootuata-- lʼeishoi e David-- tʼeuangelion ai;"
2Timothy2:9 naaisilieki ena metabaiki too nkeenda anaa oloitobira ntorrok-- kake meenai ororei lʼEngai."
2Timothy2:10 Onaa-- ang'iriaki pookin tʼolbae loo lootegeluaki-- peiye etum si ninje enkitopuata tiatua Kristos Yesus te nebo o enkitook oo nkatan pookin."
2Timothy2:11 Esipa ele rorei: Teni kie te nebo o ninye-- nikipuo aaishiu te nebo o ninye--"
2Timothy2:12 teni kimiki-- nelamiki si ninye yook;"
2Timothy2:13 teni mikiruk-- nebik ninye aa supat-- amu meidim ninye atomikio kion."
2Timothy2:14 Ntadamu iltung'anak kuna baak-- ninjakenu tʼengomom Olaitoriani-- pemeishangarrare rorei-- amu medupai-- neibelekenyari ake kulo looning'."
2Timothy2:15 Tonyua aitadol kion tʼEngai anaa olaitobirani supat lemeata eleyata-- looriki ororei lʼesipata abaraki."
2Timothy2:16 Ntalama kion mbaak enderrare oo mpeshoi entung'anishu; amu epon ina ake orregie torrono--"
2Timothy2:17 nenya ilo rorei anaa enkea nayeng'i; tiatua kulo etii Humenayos o Filipos--"
2Timothy2:18 ootapong'ori aaing'ua esipata-- nejo eidipa ataa empiunoto oo lootuata-- neibelekenya enkirukoto oo kulekai tung'anak."
2Timothy2:19 Kake ebik entonata nagol Engai neata ele ponoto: Eyolo Olaitoriani loora ilkulenyena — o: Njepaash entorroni oltung'ani pookin oipot engarna Olaitoriani.
2Timothy2:20 Ore tʼengaji kitok-- metii ake ntokitin e sahabu arashu nʼosuiai oibor-- kake baiki noo nkeek o nʼesarng'ab-- neata kulie enganyit-- neata kulie enkurruna."
2Timothy2:21 Kake teni eisuja oltung'ani apaash nona-- neaku entoki sinyati naata enganyit-- netumoki olopeny-- neidipakinore enkyas pookin sidai."
2Timothy2:22 Lanya ilng'warraitin torrok enkitishu! kake tusuja esupato-- enkirukoto-- enyorrata-- eseriani te nebo o pookin ooipot Olaitoriani tʼoltau oibor."
2Timothy2:23 Tanya nkikilikwanat naatii emodaishu nemedupa; amu iyolo-- ajo eiu ake olarrabal."
2Timothy2:24 Kake ore olaisyayani lʼOlaitoriani-- me sidai-- teni eilepilep-- kake meata kata nemebor too ltung'anak pookin-- neyolo aiteng'enisho-- neng'iriaki iltorrok--"
2Timothy2:25 odiding' tʼemborran lelo ooata engogong'i-- an ake eisho Engai ninje enkitaalata-- peyolou esipata--"
2Timothy2:26 neng'enu neidim aatupukutu tiatua erreshet e satan-- oteena ninje-- peitobir enayeu ninye."
2Timothy3:1 Kake tayolou ele rorei-- ajo too ngolong'i enkiting'oto-- nepuonu nkatan nemeserian."
2Timothy3:2 Amu eaku iltung'anak loonyor aten-- nenyor masaa-- looilash-- newuasa-- nemorisho-- nemening' lootoiutuo ninje-- nemeliki ashe-- nemeure Engai--"
2Timothy3:3 nemeata enyorrata-- nemeing'uaikino-- nekurrisho-- nemera shaati-- nera pushunot-- nemeata emborran--"
2Timothy3:4 neitarasaki-- neitobir mbaak torrok-- neitaa sapuk elukunya pesho-- nenyor olng'warra torrono nelang' Engai--"
2Timothy3:5 neitanyanyukie aten enyor Engai-- kake eany engolon enye. Talama iye iltung'anak ooba nji."
2Timothy3:6 Amu tiatua lelo ninje epuku oojing' ngajijik nerresh ng'oroyok naanap orridati loo nkitarruot-- erikito atua ilng'warraitin loo muain kumok--"
2Timothy3:7 naa ninje ooiteng'enuo oade-- nemeidim aainoto eyolounoto esipata."
2Timothy3:8 Kake anaa etanyaita Yanes o Yambres eiruk Mose-- neijia etiu si ninje neany esipata; nera ninje iltung'anak ootarruoitie ndamunot-- lemeidimunye tiatua enkirukoto."
2Timothy3:9 Kake meidim aashom lukunya oade; amu eibalunye emodaishu enye too ltung'anak pookin-- neijia anaa opa peibalunye emodaishu oo lelo."
2Timothy3:10 Kake itusuja iye enkiteng'enare ai-- orregie lai-- eotikinoto ai o enkirukoto o enkitirring'a o enyorrata o olng'iria lai--"
2Timothy3:11 o mirat ainai o nkisilot ainei nainoto te Antiokia-- Ikonion o Listra. Keba aa nkisilot nating'iria te ine! Kake aatang'adua Olaitoriani aitung'ua pookin."
2Timothy3:12 Ore pookin ooyeu neibung'are orregie sidai tiatua Yesus Kristos-- netum emirata."
2Timothy3:13 Kake ore kulo tung'anak torrok oolejisho-- nelusoo aaku torrok-- neitapong'oo neitapong'ori."
2Timothy3:14 Kake tobiko iye tiatua nena ninteng'enue nikintanapaki.
2Timothy3:15 Ore tiaraki niyolo esirata sinyati neba enkata ira enkerai-- nikindim ninye aiteng'ena iye-- pitum enkitopuata tiatua enkirukoto e atua Kristos Yesus."
2Timothy3:16 Amu ore esirata pookin nara enkutunoto Engai-- netumoki ataa enkiteng'enare o enkigwena o enkitoriokinoto o enkitubulunoto tiatua esupato--"
2Timothy3:17 peaku oltung'ani lʼEngai oljartan oidimu enkyas sidai pookin.
2Timothy4:1 Onaa-- aijakenu tʼengomom Engai o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos-- olotu aigwenaki looishiu o lootuata tʼelioroto enye o tʼenkarsishu enye:"
2Timothy4:2 Nosu ele rorei-- tonyua tʼenkata sidai o neme sidai-- ngwenaki-- ntureishoi-- tuutu tʼolng'iria pookin o tʼenkiteng'enare."
2Timothy4:3 Amu elotu enkata nemeyeu ninje enkiteng'enare naishiuniisho-- kake tʼerisioroto oo lng'warraitin lenye oopeny eing'oru laiteng'enak ootiu anaa peyeu nening' nkiyaa enye--"
2Timothy4:4 neibelekeny nkiyaa enye pemening' esipata-- neibelekenyakino natinin elejare."
2Timothy4:5 Ore iye-- torripo kion too pookin-- ting'iria too ntorrok-- ntobira enkyas olainosunoni loo lomon lʼeng'ida-- ntabai enkisyayare ino!"
2Timothy4:6 Amu atioyo aidasishoreki netinyikua enkata elakunoto ai.
2Timothy4:7 Atigilunore engilunoto sidai-- aidipa enkwetata-- aiboiye enkirukoto;"
2Timothy4:8 eng'or aarripokini olkaranda tʼesupato-- laalaisho Olaitoriani te ina olong'-- olaigwenani supat-- neme nanu ake-- kake pookin lootonyorra elioroto enye."
2Timothy4:9 Tonyua naleng'-- tasioku enatii nanu!"
2Timothy4:10 Amu natung'aiye Demas-- nenyor mbaak ele maa-- neshomo Tesalonike-- neshomo Kreskens Galatia-- neshomo Titos Dalmatia."
2Timothy4:11 Lukas ake openy otii e nebo o nanu. Iao Markos enitii-- toriku ene wueji-- amu ninye laaretoki nanu enkisyayare."
2Timothy4:12 Amu airriwaiye Tukikos meshomo Efesos.
2Timothy4:13 Au ele kila liopore latung'aiye te Troas too ngaik e Karpos-- teni ilotu-- o nkitabuni-- naleng' nena naaitobiraki too ndapan."
2Timothy4:14 Ore Aleksandros-- ele kunoni-- aaikunaka ntorrok kumok; njelaaki Olaitoriani ninye-- anaa perisiore nkyasin enyena."
2Timothy4:15 Kake torripo si iye kion naleng' te ninye-- amu etanya rorei lang' naleng'."
2Timothy4:16 Tʼemitunoto ai elukunya eitu aaitasheiki o obo engalo ai-- kake aatung'aitie pookin. Njoo meikenakini ninje."
2Timothy4:17 Kake aaitasheikio Olaitoriani naaitagolie-- peitabaiari enkinosunoto te nanu-- nening' lemeata Engai pookin; naatang'adieki nanu enkutuk olng'atuny--"
2Timothy4:18 Aalo ang'adie Olaitoriani enkyas torrono pookin naalo aitopok tiatua enkarsishu enye e shumata. Njeishori ninye enkitook nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin. Amen.
2Timothy4:19 Roroki Priska o Akwila o engaji e Onesiforos.
2Timothy4:20 Etobiko Erastos te Korintos; ore Trofimos atung'aiye ninye te Miletos emoi.
2Timothy4:21 Tasioku wou eton eitu ebau enkata enkirobi. Kiroroki Oibulos o Prudens o Linos o Klaudia o lalashera pookin.
2Timothy4:22 Njebik Olaitoriani te nebo o Olmumua lino. Njebik eng'adunoto te nebo o ndai. Amen.
Titus1:1 Paulos-- osinga lʼEngai o olairriwani le Yesus Kristos-- tʼerisioroto enkirukoto oo lootegeluaki lʼEngai o eyolounoto esipata nabaiki enkisyayare Engai--"
Titus1:2 tiatua eanyunoto empuan nemeiting'-- naisiliga Engai nemelejisho-- eton eitu ebau nkatan enkop;"
Titus1:3 kake tʼenkata enye etaboluo ororei lenye tʼenkinosunoto naaishooki nanu tʼenkitanapata Engai-- Olaitopuani lang':"
Titus1:4 te Titos-- enkerai ai nasipa tiatua enkirukoto niking'ar yook pokira are. Njoo kiboitare eng'adunoto o enkordunoto o eseriani naing'ua Engai Papa o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos-- Olaitopuani lang'."
Titus1:5 Te ina aatung'aiye iye te Kreta-- pintabaia nena baak naatong'oro-- nipik laigwenak too ngang'itie pookin-- anaa enaaitanapa iye."
Titus1:6 Ten etii olemeata entibili-- olmoruo lʼeng'oroyoni nabo-- olopeny nkera naairuk nemeimakini aajo era ninje naaiminye arashu nemening'isho."
Titus1:7 Amu njoo meata olaing'orani (bishop) eleyata-- anaa olaramatani lʼengaji Engai-- nemeaku oltung'ani ogol ong'u-- nemeaku ologoro asioki-- neme olaokoni lʼolmarua-- neme olaarani-- me olong'oroki kion too ntorrok--"
Titus1:8 kake olorik lomon aji-- Oloata emborran-- Oloata eng'eno nabore-- olora supat o sinyati o shaat--"
Titus1:9 oloibung'are ele rorei osipa tʼensioroto enkiteng'enare-- oloyolo aiteng'enisho-- peata engolon nadiding'ie tʼenkiteng'enare naishiuniisho neigwenaki looata engogong'i."
Titus1:10 Amu etii laderrak o laitasurok kumok lemening'isho ooata rorei le pesho-- kake naleng' kulo lʼemurata."
Titus1:11 Meata kata nemenuki nkutukie enye-- amu eibelekeny ngajijik naalulung'a-- neiteng'en nemeitoriori tʼolbae lʼendupoto enye torrono."
Titus1:12 Etejo obo too ninje-- oloiboni lenye openy ajo: Era Ilkretes oshi lalejak-- lowuarak torrok o ngoshuak turua."
Titus1:13 Esipa ena jakenishu. Tiaraki natiu neijia-- ngwenaki ninje tʼempijan-- peidim aataa supati tʼenkirukoto--"
Titus1:14 nemesuj natinin oo Yudayoi o nkitanapat oo ltung'anak oolam esupato.
Titus1:15 Sidan ntokitin pookin too loora sidan-- kake metii entoki sidai too lduruki o lemeiruk-- kake eidurukieki eng'eno o oltoilo lʼoltau lenye."
Titus1:16 Ejo ninje eyolo Engai; kake too nkitobirat enye-- nemiki ninye-- neata ntorrok-- nemening'isho-- neru tiatua enkyas sidai pookin."
Titus2:1 Kake ore iye-- roro lomon anaa perisiore enkiteng'enare naishiuniisho."
Titus2:2 Tiaki ilpaiyani-- pememera-- neata enganyit o eng'eno-- neaku biot tʼenkirukoto-- tʼenyorrata-- tʼolng'iria;"
Titus2:3 neija si ntasati-- peata orregie oaku too sinyat-- nemeaku naakurrisho arashu naaok enaisho sapuk-- neaku ngaiteng'enak sidan--"
Titus2:4 aaiteng'enu nkituak kutiti-- penyor ilmoruak lenye o nkera enye--"
Titus2:5 neitore aten-- neaku shaati-- neramat ngajijik enye-- neata emborran-- nening' ilmoruak lenye-- pememori ororei lʼEngai."
Titus2:6 Neijia tididing'a leak ooti-- peitore aten."
Titus2:7 Kake tiatua ntokitin pookin-- tang'asa ntadua kion anaa enkitanyanyukiet oo nkitobirat sidan-- tʼenkiteng'enare nemeshula nkulie baak-- tʼesinyatishu--"
Titus2:8 tʼororei oishiuniisho lemeata eleyata-- pekurru olmang'atinda torrono nemetum enaimaki yook tʼentorroni."
Titus2:9 Njening' laisyayak laitoriak lenye neiting'id ninje too pookin-- nemeing'unyung'uny--"
Titus2:10 nemepurrisho-- kake peitadolu esupato pookin sidai-- peiye ekaj enkiteng'enare Engai-- Olaitoriani lang'-- too mbaak pookin."
Titus2:11 Amu etaliokine eng'adunoto Engai naitopokisho iltung'anak pookin--"
Titus2:12 eiteng'enita yook-- pikiany empaashata Engai o ilng'warran lʼolmaa-- pikinjiu tiatua ele maa tʼeng'eno o tʼesupato o tʼenkuretishu Engai--"
Titus2:13 nikimaririu eanyunoto tesh o enkitadolunoto enkitook Engai kitok o Olaitopuani lang' Yesus Kristos--"
Titus2:14 oishorua kion tʼolbae lang'-- pelaku yook tʼempaashata pookin oo nkitanapat neisujaki kion olorere lemeata entemakino nenyok nkyasin sidan."
Titus2:15 Roro kuna baak nididing' ningwenaki tʼempijan sidai. Niminjo oltung'ani obo kiany.
Titus3:1 Ntadamu ninje-- pening' laitoriak o looata engolon neiruk-- neidipakino tʼenkyas pookin sidai--"
Titus3:2 nememor iltung'anak-- nemeata olarrabal-- neaku aripi-- neitaduaia emborran pookin too ltung'anak pookin."
Titus3:3 Amu ore si yook opa nimikiata eng'eno-- neitu kining'-- nikimanimanaa-- nikisyayaki ilng'warraitin o ng'idaitin torrok oo muain kumok-- nikipuoiye entorroni o olkikainit-- neibai yook nikimbaro tiatua aten."
Titus3:4 Kake etalie emborran o enyorrata Olaitopuani lang'-- Engai-- too ltung'anak--"
Titus3:5 me tʼolbae loo nkitobirat esupato nikintobira yook-- kake eitopua ninye yook tʼenkordunoto enye-- tʼenkisujata eiunoto e are o tʼenkitaaroto ng'ejuk tʼOlmumua Sinyati--"
Titus3:6 lotubukoko yook tʼemborei te Yesus Kristos-- Olaitopuani lang'--"
Titus3:7 pekiaku supati tʼempuris e ilo o lajung'ok lʼempuan nemeiting' tʼeanyunoto.
Titus3:8 Esipa ele rorei-- nayeu ninteng'en akurraki-- peiye edoli kulo ooiruk Engai-- aajo etii eitobirita nkitobirat sidan. Naa sidai ina neretoki iltung'anak."
Titus3:9 Tanya nkikiliwanat emodaishu o noo lmakui-- o enjangar o enara tʼolbae loo nkitanapat; amu medupa ninje naa pesho."
Titus3:10 Ore oltung'ani orishari-- talama-- teni eidipaki aitaduai aigil nabo arashu are--"
Titus3:11 niyolo-- ajo eibelekenye oltung'ani oba nji neitarruo-- neigwenaki kion."
Titus3:12 Teni aairriwaki iye Artemas arashu Tukikos-- tasioku wou Nikopolis enatii-- amu ayeu nabik te ine enkata enkirobi."
Titus3:13 Rriwai Senos-- ele ayoloni loo nkitanapat-- o Apolos-- peitobir olototo lenye naleng'-- pemeng'oriki toki."
Titus3:14 Njeiteng'enuo si iltung'anak lang'-- peitobirita nkitobirat sidan-- aaitaa ngolati naayeuni-- pemeaku loolau ilmomo."
Titus3:15 Kiroroki pookin ootii e nebo o nanu. Roroki pookin oonyor yook tʼenkirukoto. Njebik eng'adunoto too ndai pookin. Amen.
Philemon1:1 Paulos-- oloena le Yesus Kristos-- o Timoteos-- olalashe: te Filemon olikinyor o olaitobirani lʼenkyas te nebo o yook--"
Philemon1:2 o te Apia-- enganashe-- o te Arkipos-- olong'ar enjore te nebo o yook-- o tʼesirit natii atua engaji ino."
Philemon1:3 Njeboitare ndai eng'adunoto o eseriani naing'ua Engai-- Papa lang'-- o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos."
Philemon1:4 Aliki Engai ai ashe enkata pookin-- teni aadamu iye tʼeomonoto ai--"
Philemon1:5 teni aning' mbaak enyorrata ino o enkirukoto niata tiatua Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos o too sinyat pookin--"
Philemon1:6 petum enkirukoto ino niking'ar-- engolon tʼeyolounoto oo ntokitin pookin sidan nikiata tiatua Kristos Yesus."
Philemon1:7 Kake kiata eng'ida kitok o enkilejilejata tʼenyorrata ino; amu intaraposho iltauja loo sinyat-- lalashe lai."
Philemon1:8 Onaa-- ten ake aata enkiteunoto pookin tiatua Kristos-- paaitanap iye mbaak naaku--"
Philemon1:9 aadiding' iye tʼenyorrata ake-- nanyanyukie Paulos olpaiyan-- ore taata ara si oloena le Yesus Kristos."
Philemon1:10 Aadiding' iye tʼolbae lʼenkerai ai natoiwuo tiatua nkeenda-- Onesimos--"
Philemon1:11 neitu kitumoki opa-- kake ore taata aaretoki nanu o iye."
Philemon1:12 Amu airriwaa ninye meeu enitii iye-- tang'amu ninye anaa ijo oltau lai openy."
Philemon1:13 Amu atayeuo nebik ninye te nebo o nanu-- paaisyayaki tʼewueji ino tiatua nkeenda oo lomon lʼeng'ida;"
Philemon1:14 kake eitu ayeu neitobir ninye toki-- metii enyorrata ino-- pemetiu anaa eikonyuni sidan inono-- kake pinyor iye openy."
Philemon1:15 Ebaiki te ina kitoorunyeki tʼenkiti kata-- piata ninye nkatan pookin--"
Philemon1:16 nemekure enyanyukie osinga-- kake elusoo tʼosinga-- anaa olalashe kirotet-- naa olalai o naleng' olino-- too pokira are-- tʼosesen o tiatua Olaitoriani."
Philemon1:17 Onaa-- teni kinkenaki nanu olora liking'ar-- tang'amu ninye anaa nanu kion."
Philemon1:18 Kake teni kintarruoiye toki arashu eata entoki esile-- tipika atua esiana ai."
Philemon1:19 Nanu-- Paulos-- otisiraka tʼengaina ai openy-- ajo alak nanu; pamaajoki iye-- ajo iye openy laa esile ai."
Philemon1:20 Ee-- lalashe lai-- njooki mainoto eng'ida tʼolbae lino tiatua Olaitoriani; eng'ieng'ie oltau lai tiatua Kristos!"
Philemon1:21 Aatisiraka iye-- amu airuk ajo kining' iye nanu-- nayolo-- ajo intobir iye nalang' enajo."
Philemon1:22 Kake te nebo o nona-- ntobirakaki ewueji nabikie; amu airuk ajo tʼolbae loo omonot inyi-- naaishori nanu ndai."
Philemon1:23 Kiroroki Epafras-- oloena te nebo o nanu tiatua Yesus Kristos--"
Philemon1:24 o Markos o Aristarkos o Demas o Lukas-- looisyaisho te nebo o nanu."
Philemon1:25 Njebik eng'adunoto Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos tʼolmumua linyi. Amen.
Hebrews1:1 Ore peidip airorie Engai opa loopapa too layolounok aigil kumok o too muain kumok--"
Hebrews1:2 neirorie ninye yook tʼenkiting'oto oo kuna olong'i tʼOinoti-- lotipika-- peaku olajung'oni loo pookin-- eitobirieki baiki ninye enkop;"
Hebrews1:3 olora enkibor enkitook o erisioroto entiunoto enye-- loirishiu ntokitin pookin tʼororei lʼenkidimata enye-- eidipa aitaa enkisujata oo nkitarruot ang' neton te tatene enkitook natii shumata--"
Hebrews1:4 etaa sidai naleng' nelang' ilmalaikan nejung'u engarna kitok nelang' enenye.
Hebrews1:5 Amu kalo too lmalaikan etiaka ninye aikata: Ira iye Oinoti lai-- nanu laatoiwuo iye taata? Neitoki: Alaaku nanu Menye lenye te ninye-- nelaaku ninye Oinoti te nanu?"
Hebrews1:6 Neitoki ajo te ina kata nariku olkikau lenye atua olmaa: Nepuo aaserem ninye ilmalaikan lʼEngai pookin.
Hebrews1:7 Ore tʼolbae loo lmalaikan ejo: Eitaa ilmalaikan lenyena metotiu anaa ilkutat o laisyayak lenyena metotiu anaa ilng'ejepa lʼenkima;
Hebrews1:8 kake tʼolbae lʼOinoti ejo nji: Olorika lino-- iye Engai-- obik nkatan pookin; ore eng'udi enkarsishu ino naa eng'udi enkitoriokinoto."
Hebrews1:9 Itonyorra iye esupato nimbai mesupato. Onaa Engai-- kielie iye Engai ino eilata eng'ida-- nikintalang' iljorueta linono."
Hebrews1:10 O: Iye-- Olaitoriani-- otuuno tʼenkiterunoto enkop; ore shumata-- naa nkitobirat oo ngaik inono."
Hebrews1:11 Neaku erruoio ninje-- nibik iye oshi; nepuo aamusanu anaa enkila--"
Hebrews1:12 nintaal ninje anaa olkila-- nepuo aawala; kake itiu iye anaa oshi ake-- nemepuo aaiting' larin linono."
Hebrews1:13 Kake kalo too lmalaikan etiaka aikata: Totona iye te tatene ai-- metabana napik ilmang'ati linono abori oo nkejek inono?"
Hebrews1:14 Mera ninje pookin ilmumuan aisyayak looirriwaiyoki tʼolbae lʼenkisyayare oo kulo loopuo aajung'u enkitopuata?
Hebrews2:1 Akae-- meata kata nimikinyok kimbung' ororei likitoning'o-- pemikimin ai wueji."
Hebrews2:2 Amu ten aa ele rorei oiroro ilmalaikan-- meibelekenya-- ore elang'ata o eanyata pookin netum elaakinoto enye--"
Hebrews2:3 kaji kinko teni kilany yook-- teni mikinyor enkitopuata naba nji-- natang'asa Olaitoriani alimu-- neakitia yook kulo ootoning'o--"
Hebrews2:4 neaku si Engai oljakeni lenye te nebo o ninje-- too lponot o nkiputukunyot kumok o nkidimat oo muain kumok-- neoriki Olmumua Sinyati tʼerisioroto eyeunoto enye."
Hebrews2:5 Amu eitu epik ilmalaikan meitoria olmaa olotu-- likiimaki yook."
Hebrews2:6 Kake eijakenu obo aibalunye ajo: Ainyo oltung'ani metaa idamu ninye-- o enkerai oltung'ani metaa ishilaa ninye?"
Hebrews2:7 Nintaa iye ninye oti too lmalaikan enkiti kata-- ninjopoko ninye enkaja enkitadararoto o nʼenkitook-- ninjoo ninye eitore nkitobirat oo ngaik inono--"
Hebrews2:8 nipik ntokitin pookin abori oo nkejek enyena. Tiaraki natipika pookin abori enye-- neitu epal o nyoo neitu epiki abori enye. Kake ore taata-- eton eitu kidol ntokitin pookin etipikaki abori enye."
Hebrews2:9 Kake kidol ele-- oitaaki oti too lmalaikan enkiti kata-- Yesus-- tʼolbae lʼenkitamioto enkea-- eishopokoki enkaja enkitadararoto o nʼenkitook-- peiye-- tʼeng'adunoto Engai-- einyorrinyor enkea tʼolbae loo pookin."
Hebrews2:10 Amu enare ilo-- lotii ntokitin pookin tʼolbae lenye-- oitobira ntokitin pookin-- netorikoko nkera kumok enkitook-- peitabaia olkitok lʼenkitopuata enye too nkitamiot."
Hebrews2:11 Amu ore ele osinyaa o kulo oosinyari-- neing'ua pookin atua obo; onaa mekurru ninye-- teni eipot ninje lalashera--"
Hebrews2:12 nejo: Ainosaki engarna ino lalashera lainei-- o tiatua esirit aranyaki engarna ino."
Hebrews2:13 Neitoki: Ayeu nang'idare ninye. Neitoki: Ng'orai-- nanu o nkera naaishoo Engai nanu."
Hebrews2:14 Ore petaa nkera etang'ara enkiring'o o osarge-- neng'arie si ninye nena-- peiminye tʼenkea enkidimata e ilo loata engolon enkea-- naa ninye satan--"
Hebrews2:15 petum atalaku kulo loora tʼolbae lʼenkuretishu enkea singan ngolong'i enye pookin.
Hebrews2:16 Amu meramat ninye ilmalaikan-- kake eishoi e Abraham eramat."
Hebrews2:17 Akae-- meata kata nemenyanyukie ninye lalashera lenyena too ntokitin pookin-- peaku ninye olobore enkordunoto o olaidasani kitok-- oitabaia ntokitin pookin tʼEngai-- netum olorere enkitaunoto oo nkitarruot."
Hebrews2:18 Amu ina einotie ninye emion o enkitasuroto-- peidim ataretoki kulo ooitasuri."
Hebrews3:1 Onaa-- lalashera lainei sinyat-- oong'ar enkipototo e shumata-- entayolou olairriwani o olaidasani kitok likirabalu-- naa ninye Kristos Yesus--"
Hebrews3:2 oata enkirukoto te ilo oitaa ninye-- anaa si Mose tiatua engaji enye pookin."
Hebrews3:3 Kake meata kata nemetum ele enkitook nelang' Mose-- neijia anaa pelang' enkitook olaitobirani lʼengaji enkitook engaji."
Hebrews3:4 Amu ore engaji pookin-- iltung'anak ooitobira; kake Engai-- naitobira ntokitin pookin."
Hebrews3:5 Esipa-- eata Mose embaiaroto tʼengaji enye pookin anaa osinga-- neaku enjakenishu oo kuna baak naaishooki pelimu."
Hebrews3:6 Kake ore Kristos etaa anaa enkerai neitore engaji enye; ore engaji enye-- nikira yook-- teni kimbung' aakurraki eng'idaroto o enkitook eanyunoto metabaiki enkiting'oto--"
Hebrews3:7 Akae-- anaa pejo Olmumua sinyati: Taata-- teni ining'ining'i oltoilo lenye--"
Hebrews3:8 emintagol iltauja linyi-- anaa petaa tʼenkitagoroto tʼengolong' enkitasuroto ti ang'ata--"
Hebrews3:9 paaitasurokitio loo minyi linyi-- naatem-- nedol nkitobirat ainei larin artam."
Hebrews3:10 Neijia patagorokine ina kishon najo: Epong'ori oshi too ltauja. Kake eitu eyolou ngoitoi ainei--"
Hebrews3:11 paituruj tʼengoro ai ajo: mepuo aajing' eng'ieng'ata ai.
Hebrews3:12 Eng'orai-- lalashera lainei-- pemeaku obo too ndai-- oata oltau torrono lemeiruk nelam Engai naishiu;"
Hebrews3:13 kake entididing'aroto aten ngolong'i pookin eton eipoti: taata-- pemeaku obo too ndai oitagol oltau lenye tʼelejata enkitarruoto."
Hebrews3:14 Amu etaa king'ar Kristos-- teni kimbung' aakurraki entiunoto nikintera-- metabaiki enkiting'oto."
Hebrews3:15 Ore teni eji: Taata-- teni ining'ining'i ndai oltoilo lai-- emintagol iltauja linyi anaa petaa tʼenkitagoroto:"
Hebrews3:16 Kakua naa lelo ootoning'o neitaa enkitagoroto? Me ninje pookin-- ootupukutuo aaing'ua Misri te Mose?"
Hebrews3:17 Naa kakua lelo ootagorokine ninye larin artam? Me ninje ooitarruoitie-- netuata seseni lenye ti ang'ata?"
Hebrews3:18 Arashu kakua eiturujaka ninye ajo: mejing' atua eng'ieng'ata enye-- neme kulo lemeiruk?"
Hebrews3:19 Nikidol yook aajo eitu eidim ninje aatijing'-- amu eitu eiruk."
Hebrews4:1 Onaa-- matureisho yook-- pemikilau kijing' atua eng'ieng'ata enye naisiliga ninye-- pemetii obo too yook otioyo."
Hebrews4:2 Amu einosakaki si yook lomon ooitopokisho anaa lekua; kake ore ilo rorei lʼenkinosunoto eitu eretoki ninje-- tiaraki neitu eiruk lootoning'o--"
Hebrews4:3 (amu yook ootaa eiruk-- kijing' atua eng'ieng'ata) anaa petejo: Kake aituruja tʼengoro ai-- mepuo aajing' eng'ieng'ata ai. Ore peidipaki aaitobira nkitobirat opa tʼenkiterunoto enkop--"
Hebrews4:4 nejo engai wueji tʼengolong' e napishana nji: Neeng'ieng'a Engai tʼengolong' e napishana too nkitobirat enyena pookin.
Hebrews4:5 Neitoki ene wueji: Mepuo aajing' eng'ieng'ata ai.
Hebrews4:6 Te ina eng'or ajo etii loojing' ine-- o lelo ootang'asaki aainosaki-- eitu etum aatijing-- amu eitu eiruk;"
Hebrews4:7 neitoki apik ninye engolong'-- eidipa atulusoi enkata naado naba nji-- nejo te David: Taata-- anaa petejoki opa-- taata-- teni ining'ining'i oltoilo lenye-- emintagol iltauja linyi."
Hebrews4:8 Amu ten emut eeng'ieng'ie Yosua ninje-- anaata eitu eitoki ninye aimaki ai olong'."
Hebrews4:9 Onaa-- eng'or eng'ieng'ata tʼolorere lʼEngai."
Hebrews4:10 Amu olotijing'a atua eng'ieng'ata enye-- neeng'ieng'a ninye too nkyasin enyena-- anaa Engai too nkun enyena."
Hebrews4:11 Akae-- matonyok-- pekijing' atua ena eng'ieng'ata-- pemedoiki o obo atua ilo rregie lʼeanyata."
Hebrews4:12 Amu eishiu ororei lʼEngai neitobirisho nedung'isho nelang' olalem pookin opi mbat pokira are nerish empuan o Olmumua o rubat o ntolo neigwenaki ndamunot o nkibirribirrat oltau.
Hebrews4:13 Nemetii enkitobirata o nabo nemelioi tʼengomom enye-- kake etii eor netaboluoki pookin too ngonyek enyena. Kilimu te ina."
Hebrews4:14 Akae-- ore pekiata olaidasani kitok-- Yesus Kristos-- Oinoti lʼEngai-- oilepa shumata-- maibung'a enkibalunoto."
Hebrews4:15 Amu mikiata olaidasani kitok lemeidim atoning'oki yook emion too menatishuitin ang'-- kake eitasuroki ninye too pookin anaa yook-- metii ake enkitarruoto."
Hebrews4:16 Akae-- matinyikaki tʼenjipai olorika lʼeng'adunoto enye-- peking'amu enkordunoto nikitum eng'adunoto naau eretokinoto tʼenkata nanare."
Hebrews5:1 Amu ore olaidasani kitok pookin oitayoki tiatua iltung'anak-- nepiki tʼolbae loo ltung'anak tiatua nena naaishiaakinore Engai-- peaki nkishoorot o nkidasareitin tʼolbae loo nkitarruot;"
Hebrews5:2 oloidim aing'urrie kulo lemeyolo o loomanimanaa-- tiaraki naman enjalan si ninye."
Hebrews5:3 Onaa-- meata kata nemeidasisho si tʼolbae loo nkitarruot enyena openy-- anaa tʼolbae loo nkitarruot olorere."
Hebrews5:4 Nemetii oltung'ani ong'amu kion enkitook-- kake Engai naipotoki ninye-- anaa Aron."
Hebrews5:5 Neijia si Kristos-- eitu epik kion atua enkitook-- peaku olaidasani kitok-- kake ilo otiaka ninye; Ira iye Oinoti lai; taata aatoiwuo iye."
Hebrews5:6 Anaa pejo si engai wueji: Ira iye olaidasani nkatan pookin tʼorregie le Melkisedek.
Hebrews5:7 Ore too ngolong'i enkiring'o enye-- eaka omonot o sayat te nebo o enkishirata sapuk o ilkiyo ilo oidim aitopua ninye tʼenkea; netoning'uoki ninye-- tiaraki naitaa Engai kitok."
Hebrews5:8 Ten aa Oinoti lʼEngai ninye-- neiteng'enuo tiatua sinaitin-- pebik tiatua ening'oto."
Hebrews5:9 Ore peidipi aitabai-- neaku ninye olaretoni loo pookin ooiruk ninye-- petum ninje enkitopuata nemeiting'--"
Hebrews5:10 neipot Engai ninye olaidasani kitok tʼorregie le Melkisedek.
Hebrews5:11 Te ina eng'or mbaak kumok-- pekirorie ndai-- kake egol-- tiaraki nirara ndai yetuti tʼening'oto."
Hebrews5:12 Kake eikash-- ten emut indipa aataa laiteng'enak-- ore taata nintokiki aayeu neiteng'eni ndai sirat lʼenkiterunoto tiatua rorei lʼEngai; nirara ndai oonare kule-- lemeidim endaa nagol."
Hebrews5:13 Amu ore oltung'ani leton eok kule-- netiu anaa olemeyolo naleng' ororei lʼesipata; amu era enkerai kiti."
Hebrews5:14 Kake endaa nagol en oo ltung'anak kituak-- ooitamoo eng eno enye too nkyasin engolon-- petum aaitooro sidan o ntorrok."
Hebrews6:1 Akae-- matapal taata kiimaki en opa kiteng'enare enkiterunoto e Kristos-- nikinyok-- pekibaiki embaiaroto-- nimikintoki aaitobir entonata enkitaalata aing'ua nkitobirat enkea-- o en enkirukoto e atua Engai--"
Hebrews6:2 o en enkibatisa-- o en enkiteng'enare-- o en enkiteleikinoto oo ngaik-- o en empiunoto oo lootuata-- o en enkigwena oo nkatan pookin."
Hebrews6:3 Kiyeu nikintobir si nena-- teni eisho Engai pekias."
Hebrews6:4 Amu ore kulo ooidipaki aailang'aki neinyorrinyor enkishooroto e shumata neng'ar Olmumua Sinyati
Hebrews6:5 neinyorrinyor ororei obor lʼEngai o engolon olmaa olotu--"
Hebrews6:6 teni elam-- nemeidimai peitokini aaitaa ng'ejuko neala; amu ore lelo neitoki aaoshoki Oinoti lʼEngai esalaba tiatua aten-- nepik ninye enkurruna metalioi."
Hebrews6:7 Amu ore enkop natooko enjan nashaiki aigil kumok shumata enye-- neiu ilmomo sidan ooret kulo ootuturo ninye-- neng'amu emayani naing'ua Engai."
Hebrews6:8 Kake teni eiu ilkeko o ntulele entim-- nemedupa-- nenyikita endiata-- ore enkiting'oto enye-- epejori."
Hebrews6:9 Kake-- lanyor lainei-- kianyu enaikash too ndai-- petaana enkitopuata-- baiki ten ake kiro neijia."
Hebrews6:10 Amu supat Engai-- merikino enkitobirata inyi o enkyas enyorrata nintaduaitie lʼengarna enye-- amu isyayakitia sinyat-- nepon ake isyayakiki."
Hebrews6:11 Nikiyeu neitaduaia oltung'ani pookin too ndai ina nyuata-- pimbung'ubung'u eanyunoto metabaiki enkiting'oto--"
Hebrews6:12 pemiakuku ilturua-- kake lasujak loo kulo oojung'u tʼenkirukoto o olng'iria nkisiligat."
Hebrews6:13 Amu ore peisho Engai Abraham enkisiligata-- pemeidim aituruja tʼolikai kitok alang' ninye-- neituruj te ninye kion--"
Hebrews6:14 nejo: Esipa-- ayeu naamayan iye naapon iye."
Hebrews6:15 Neijia eting'iria netum enkisiligata.
Hebrews6:16 Eiturujisho iltung'anak tʼolkitok olang' ninje-- neidip enkiturujata enjangar pookin o metipika engolon."
Hebrews6:17 Neijia eikuna Engai-- peyeu neitadolu lajung'ok enkisiligata akurraki-- ajo neing'unung'un eyeunoto enye-- neponiki enkiturujata;"
Hebrews6:18 nikitum yook too ntokitin are nemeing'unung'un-- (amu meidimai nelejisho Engai)-- enkilejilejata nagol-- teni kikwetiki nikimbung' eanyunoto nairragieki tʼengomom ang'--"
Hebrews6:19 nikiata anaa enkibung'et supat nagol oltau lang' najing' si atua ine wueji naigaraa ilo karash--"
Hebrews6:20 enetijing'a olaiturukoni tʼolbae lang'-- lora Yesus-- otaa olaidasani kitok nkatan pookin tʼorregie le Melkisedek."
Hebrews7:1 Amu ore ele Melkisedek-- naa olkarsis le Salem-- olaidasani lʼEngai natii shumata naleng'-- otanang'are Abraham-- peshukunye aing'ua enjore naarare lelo karsisi--"
Hebrews7:2 nemayan ninye-- netoorikia Abraham ninye ematua e tomon oo ntokitin pookin. Ore tʼenkiterata neitaali ninye neji: olkarsis lʼesupato; tekurum nera si olkarsis le Salem-- eji: olkarsis lʼeseriani--"
Hebrews7:3 lemeata menye-- nemeata ng'otonye-- nemeata enkishomi-- nemeata enkiterata oo ngolong'i enyena arashu enkiting'oto enkishui enye. Kake eitanyanyukieki Oinoti lʼEngai nebik olaidasani nkatan pookin."
Hebrews7:4 Eng'orai-- keba aa enkitook naata ilo loishoo si Abraham lora olakui lang' kitok-- ematua e tomon oo nena tokitin naataarua."
Hebrews7:5 Ore lelo ooing'ua atua nkera e Levi-- netum enkisyayare enkidasare-- eata engolon nang'amunye ematua e tomon oo lalashera lenye tʼerisioroto oo nkitanapat-- ten aa etupukutuo si ninje tʼolopoli le Abraham."
Hebrews7:6 Kake ore ilo lemeipoti ishoreitin o lakuyani lenyena ootupukuo ninye-- nea ematua e tomon e Abraham-- nemayan ele oishooki nkisiligat."
Hebrews7:7 Kake meatai enjangar-- ajo emayani oloti tʼolkitok."
Hebrews7:8 Naa ene-- iltung'anak lʼenkea-- ootang'amutua ematua e tomon-- kake ine obo oata enjakenishu ajo eishiu-- otang'amua."
Hebrews7:9 Onaa-- pajo nji: Eishooio si Levi ong'amu ematua e tomon-- ematua e tomon tʼolbae le Abraham."
Hebrews7:10 Amu eton etii opa olopoli le Abraham lora menye-- penang'are Melkisedek ninye."
Hebrews7:11 Kake ten etaa enkitabaiaroto tʼenkisyayare enkidasare e Levi (amu te ina einotie olorere nkitanapat)-- kainyo naa peyeuni olekai aidasani kitok oinyototo tʼorregie le Melkisedek-- nemeikeni ninye tʼorregie le Aron?"
Hebrews7:12 Amu teni eitaali enkisyayare enkidasare-- meata kata nemeitaali si nkitanapat."
Hebrews7:13 Amu ore ilo oimakinyeki kuna baak-- naa ol lekai orere-- leitu aikata epukunye ninye oltung'ani oitobira enkyas olperere lʼenkidasare."
Hebrews7:14 Amu eibala ajo-- atua Yuda etupukuo Olaitoriani lang'-- naa entipat neitu eimakinye Mose ororei o obo tʼenkisyayare enkidasare."
Hebrews7:15 Neibalunye naleng'-- ten eaku einyototo olekai aidasani tʼorregie le Melkisedek--"
Hebrews7:16 ajo eitaaki olaidasani me tiatua nkitanapat naata engolon enkiring'o-- kake tiatua enkidimata empuan nemeiting'."
Hebrews7:17 Amu eijakenu ajo: Ira iye olaidasani loo nkatan pookin tʼorregie le Melkisedek.
Hebrews7:18 Neijia ejuti nkitanapat naaiturukie-- tiaraki nashal nemedupa--"
Hebrews7:19 (amu eitu eidim nkitanapat aaitabai toki)-- neauni eanyunoto naikash naleng'-- naa ninye kinyikakinye Engai."
Hebrews7:20 Neaku emponaroto ajo etipikaki ninye melai enkiturujata. Amu eitaaki lelo laidasak metii enkiturujata--"
Hebrews7:21 kake ore ninye tʼenkiturujata e ilo otiaka: Eituruja Olaitoriani nemeinyaku ninye ena: Ira iye olaidasani loo nkatan pookin tʼorregie le Melkisedek.
Hebrews7:22 Neijia etaa Yesus olaramatani lʼosotua sidai naleng'.
Hebrews7:23 Ore lelo naa ilkumok ootaa laidasak-- tiaraki natomitikio enkea ninje ebik."
Hebrews7:24 Kake ore ninye obik nkatan pookin-- eata enkisyayare enkidasare nemeiting'."
Hebrews7:25 Onaa-- eidim aitopua oshi ake kulo oopuonu enetii Engai-- ten eimaa ninye-- amu eishiu oshi neomonoki ninje."
Hebrews7:26 Amu eikash too yook-- teni kiata olaidasani kitok oba nji-- ajo era sinyati nemeata entorroni-- nemeata entibili-- otirishunye too laitarruok-- netii ninye shumata naleng'--"
Hebrews7:27 lemenare ninye anaa lelo aidasak-- peng'as aidasisho ngolong'i pookin tʼolbae loo nkitarruot enyena oopeny-- neitoki aidasisho tʼolbae loo nkitarruot olorere; amu eikuna nji enkata nano-- eidasaiye kion."
Hebrews7:28 Amu ore nena kitanapat neitaa iltung'anak ooshal-- peaku laidasak kituak. Kake ore ele rorei lʼenkiturujata otusuja nkitanapat-- etipika Oinoti baiaroti obik nkatan pookin."
Hebrews8:1 Ore eumata oo kuna nikiimaki-- naa ena: Kiata olaidasani laijo ele oton te tatene olorika lʼenkitook e shumata--"
Hebrews8:2 naa olaisyayani lʼewueji sinyati o lʼengaji nasipa naitobira Engai neme oltung'ani.
Hebrews8:3 Amu ore olaidasani kitok pookin nepiki-- peidas too nkishoorot o nkidasareitin. Onaa-- meata kata nemeata si ele entoki naidas."
Hebrews8:4 Ten emut etii ninye ena kop-- anaata mera ninye olaidasani-- amu ene etii laidasak ooyaki nkishoorot tʼerisioroto oo nkitanapat."
Hebrews8:5 Eisyayaki lelo enkitanyanyukiet o oloip loo nena tokitin naatii shumata-- neijia anaa peirorie ealet Engai Mose: Ngorai-- etejo-- pintobir pookin aitanyanyukie ina mua nikintaduaki tʼoldonyo."
Hebrews8:6 Kake einoto ninye enkisyayare naikash naleng'-- tiaraki naa ninye olaramatani lʼosotua olusoo tʼesidano-- otuunokino nkisiligat sidan naleng'."
Hebrews8:7 Amu ten emut eitu eata ol enkiterata eleyata-- anaata eitu eing'oruni ole are."
Hebrews8:8 Amu eikok ninye ninje ejo: Ng'orai-- epuonu ngolong'i-- ejo Olaitoriani-- nayeu naitaa o engaji Israel o engaji Yuda osotua ng'ejuk;"
Hebrews8:9 me anaa ilo sotua naitaa o loopapa lenye te ina olong' naibung' engaina enye-- parik aitung'ua enkop e Misri. Amu eitu ninje ebik tiatua osotua lai; onaa-- eitu ayeu nashilaa ninje-- ejo Olaitoriani."
Hebrews8:10 Amu ele osotua laitaa o engaji Israel-- eishunye kuna olong'i: Ayeu naisho nkitanapat ainei atua endamunoto enye-- nasir atua oltau lenye-- nayeu naaku Engai enye-- neaku ninje olorere lai."
Hebrews8:11 Nemeiteng'en obo ol elatia enye-- arashu olalashe lenye: Tayolou Olaitoriani! amu aapuo nanu aayolou pookin-- eiter oloti metabaiki olbotor."
Hebrews8:12 Amu alaing'urrie mesupato enye-- nemaitoki adamu nkitarruot enye."
Hebrews8:13 Ore petejo: ng'ejuk-- neitaa musana ol enkiterata; amu enataa musana o moruo-- netinyikaka emutata."
Hebrews9:1 Eata si ele sotua lʼenkiterata rregieita lʼenkisyayare o ewueji sinyati enkop.
Hebrews9:2 Amu eteshetaki olgilata oiteru-- ore tiatua netipikieki enkilang'et o emesa o olperere loo lmkateni. Neji ine wueji esinyati."
Hebrews9:3 Ore tekurum olekai karash lʼerishata netii olgilata oji: esinyati naleng'--"
Hebrews9:4 enetii emoti nairishoreki e sahabu o osanduku lʼosotua otapetieki esahabu katukul; ore atua etii oloti le sahabu oigany mana-- ele mkate le shumata-- o eng'udi e Aron natubulakitia mbenek-- o soito lʼosotua."
Hebrews9:5 Ore shumata e ilo sanduku netii ilkerubin lʼenkitook-- ooitoipito olorika lʼenkordunoto-- naa ntokitin nemeimakinyeki taata."
Hebrews9:6 Kake ore peidipaki aaitobira kunda tokitin-- neng'as laidasak aajing' atua ilo gilata lʼenkiterata ngolong'i pookin-- peitobir enkisyayare Engai."
Hebrews9:7 Kake ore tiatua ele gilata le are-- nejing' olaidasani kitok openy-- tʼolari obo nabo kata ake-- nemejing' ninye meata osarge oitainye nkitarruot enyena o nʼolorere."
Hebrews9:8 Neijia eitayolo Olmumua Sinyati ajo-- ore ena oitoi narik atua ewueji sinyati-- eton eitu eibalunyeki ina kata naitasheye olgilata lʼenkiterata."
Hebrews9:9 Naa ina enkitanyanyukiet naitadol ena kata e taata-- tʼeneidasieki nkishoorot o nkidasareitin nemeidim aaitaa supat tiatua ndamunot enyena ele oisyayakinye ninje Engai."
Hebrews9:10 Amu mebaiki endaa o eokoto o nkisujat naaorioro o esinyatishu e oriong' naaitanapaki metabaiki enkata naitobiri eng'ejuk.
Hebrews9:11 Kake eewuo Kristos-- peaku olaidasani kitok loo sidan naapuonu-- neim engaji olototo nara kitok nabaia nelang'-- neitu eitobiri too ngaik-- eji ena mera nʼena kitobirata--"
Hebrews9:12 nejing' nabo kata atua olgilata sinyati-- me tʼosarge loo lkineji o loo lasho-- kake tʼosarge lenye openy-- eidipa ainoto elakunoto oo nkatan pookin."
Hebrews9:13 Amu teni esinyaa osarge loo lkineji o loo lmong'i o nkuruon entauo naaisuakaki ilduruk-- peaku enkisujare enkiring'o--"
Hebrews9:14 me naleng' eisuj osarge le Kristos-- loitarasaka kion Engai-- meata eleyata-- tʼOlmumua loo nkatan pookin-- iltauja lang'-- peking'ua nkitobirat nemeishiu-- pekisyayaki Engai naishiu."
Hebrews9:15 Onaa era ninye tʼolbae le ina olaidikidikoni lʼosotua ng'ejuk-- peiye eng'amu tʼenkea nataa elakunoto oo ntorrok kulo-- lootii abori osotua lʼelukunya-- looipotokoki enkisiligata enjung'o oo nkatan pookin."
Hebrews9:16 Amu tʼenetii enkitanapata enjung'o-- meata kata nemeng'as enkea e ilo oitanapishie."
Hebrews9:17 Amu eata enkitanapata enjung'o enkidimunoto tʼenkea. Meidimu enkata neton eishiu oloitanapishie.
Hebrews9:18 Onaa-- ele sotua lʼelukunya eitu eitobiri metii osarge."
Hebrews9:19 Amu ore opa-- peidip Mose aimaki nkitanapat pookin aliki olorere olulung'a-- neibung' osarge loo lasho o loo lkineji aitushulaki engare o ilpapit oonyokio loo nkerra o oljani oji isop-- neisuaki shumata enkitabu o olorere pookin--"
Hebrews9:20 ejo: Ele osarge lʼosotua-- oitanapa ndai Engai."
Hebrews9:21 Neijia si eikuna engaji olototo o ntokitin pookin enkisyayare aisuaki osarge--"
Hebrews9:22 naa ore tʼorregie loo nkitanapat-- etaana ntokitin pookin eisuji tʼosarge; naa ten eitu eibukori osarge-- nemetii enkitaunoto oo nkitarruot."
Hebrews9:23 Akae-- meata kata nemeisuji nkitanyanyukieta oo ntokitin e shumata too nkidasareitin anaa nena. Kake ore ninje oopeny-- kuna tokitin e shumata-- meata kata nemetum nkidasareitin naalusoo too nekua."
Hebrews9:24 Amu eitu ejing' Kristos ewueji sinyati naitobiraki too ngaik-- (nara oloip le ine nesipa)-- kake etijing'a te shumata-- nedoli taata tʼengomom Engai tʼolbae lang'--"
Hebrews9:25 neme peidas kion aigil kumok-- anaa pejing olaidasani kitok atua ewueji sinyati olari pookin tʼosarge omoni."
Hebrews9:26 Amu ten aa neijia-- anaata enarikino ninye-- neitamei aigil kumok eiter enkiterunoto olmaa; kake ore taata-- tʼenkitabaiaroto oo nkatan-- etalie nabo kata-- petum aitau nkitarruot tʼenkidasare enye kion."
Hebrews9:27 Anaa petipikakaki iltung'anak-- pee nabo kata-- nelotu tekurum enkigwena--"
Hebrews9:28 neijia eidasaki Kristos nabo kata-- aitau nkitarruot oo lkumok. Ore ninye lemeata nkitarruot nelalioi enkata e are too kulo ooanyu ninye-- petum enkitopuata."
Hebrews10:1 Amu ore nkitanapat-- eata oloip loo ntokitin sidan naapuonu-- me entiinoto oo ntokitin oopeny. Meata kata nemeidasi nkidasareitin naanyanyuk larin pookin-- nemeidim aaitabai kulo ooidasisho."
Hebrews10:2 Amu ten emutu mekure eata kulo ooisyayaki Engai-- oltoilo torrono lʼoltau-- tʼolbae loo nkitarruot-- ten eidipaki aaisuja nabokata-- anaata eiting'o enkyas enkidasare."
Hebrews10:3 Kake ore tiatua kuna kidasareitin etii ake enkitadamunoto oo nkitarruot larin pookin.
Hebrews10:4 Amu meidim osarge loo lmong'i o loo lkineji aitau nkitarruot.
Hebrews10:5 Onaa etejo-- pelotu atua olmaa: Eitu iyeu nkidasareitin o nkishoorot-- kake kintobiraka osesen lai."
Hebrews10:6 Ore lasari oopejori o nkidasareitin oo nkitarruot-- nimikintiship."
Hebrews10:7 Akae-- atejo: Ng'orai alotu-- (tiatua enkitabu etisiraki te nanu)-- paitobir-- Engai-- eniyeu iye."
Hebrews10:8 Ore pejo shumata: Ore nkidasareitin o nkishoorot-- lasari oopejori o nkishoorot tʼolbae loo nkitarruot-- neitu iyeu-- neitu kintiship (naa ninje ooishoori tʼorregie loo nkitanapat)"
Hebrews10:9 neitoki ajo: Ng'orai-- alotu-- Engai-- paitobir eniyeu iye-- — neiwang'ie ilo lʼelukunya-- pepik oli are."
Hebrews10:10 Te ina yeunoto etisinyaiyoki yook nabo kata tʼenkidasare osesen le Yesus Kristos.
Hebrews10:11 Ore olaidasani pookin-- eitashe peitobir enkisyayare ngolong'i pookin-- neishooio in oshi kidasareitin nemeidim katukul aaitau nkitarruot."
Hebrews10:12 Kake ore ninye-- peidipa aidasa tʼenkidasare nabo tʼolbae loo nkitarruot-- nadupa nkatan pookin-- neton taata te tatene Engai--"
Hebrews10:13 eanyu metabana nepiki ilmang'ati lenyena abori oo nkejek enyena.
Hebrews10:14 Amu tʼenkidasare nabo eitabaiye too nkatan pookin kulo ootisinyaiyoki.
Hebrews10:15 Eijakenoki yook si Olmumua Sinyati. Amu ore peidip atang'asa ajo:
Hebrews10:16 Nyele osotua-- laitaa o ninje-- eishunye kuna olong'i-- nejo Olaitoriani: Ayeu naisho nkitanapat ainei atua iltauja lenye nasir atua ndamunot enye--"
Hebrews10:17 namaitoki adamu nkitarruot o ntorrok enye.
Hebrews10:18 Kake ten eitauoki nona-- nemekure etii nkidasareitin tʼolbae loo nkitarruot."
Hebrews10:19 Akae-- lalashera-- ore pekiata enkiteunoto nikiimie enjing'ata ewueji sinyati tʼosarge le Yesus--"
Hebrews10:20 naitobiraka ninye yook-- peaku engoitoi ng'ejuk naishiu tʼolkarash lʼerishata-- neji-- tʼenkiring'o enye--"
Hebrews10:21 nikiata olaidasani kitok loitore engaji Engai:
Hebrews10:22 matinyikaki tʼoltau osipa tiatua emborei enkirukoto-- looisuaki iltauja nimikiata oltoilo torrono loo ltauja neisujaki seseni tʼengare sidai;"
Hebrews10:23 maibung'a enkibalunoto eanyunoto-- metii enking'unung'unata-- amu era ninye supat loisiligishe;"
Hebrews10:24 maibirribirrakinoto tʼenyuata nʼenyorrata o noo nkitobirat sidan--"
Hebrews10:25 njoo mikipal oltumo lang' anaa peiko looje-- kake mati diding'aroto niponipono ina naleng'-- amu idolidolo-- aajo etinyikua engolong'."
Hebrews10:26 Amu teni kintarruo aaotiki-- kindipa aatang'amu eyolounoto esipata-- nimikintoki aata engai kidasare tʼolbae loo nkitarruot--"
Hebrews10:27 kake te idye eanyu enkigwena naitureisho o empijan enkima napej laanyak.
Hebrews10:28 Ore oloany nkitanapat e Mose-- meata kata nemee metii olng'ur-- too ljaken aare arashu okuni."
Hebrews10:29 Naa inyorrikiki-- keba aa enkigwena e ilo oany Oinoti lʼEngai-- neiken ele sarge lʼosotua oisujieki-- aa torrono-- nemor Olmumua lʼeng'adunoto?"
Hebrews10:30 Amu kiyolo ilo ojo: Enai elaata oo ntorrok-- nanu olaaki; neitoki: Elaigwenaki Olaitoriani olorere lenye."
Hebrews10:31 Olbae torrono oitureisho-- teni ibatata tiatua ngaik Engai naishiu."
Hebrews10:32 Kake entadamutu ngolong'i enkiterata niting'iriakitia-- eilang'akaki ndai-- earata kitok oo nkisilot--"
Hebrews10:33 ematua nabo-- tʼolbae lʼemenata o loo nkisilot itaa emoroto-- o engai matua-- ping'arierie kulo looikunakaki nji."
Hebrews10:34 Amu itoning'o nkisilot oo looteenaki-- ning'iriakiki enkisimaroto oo masaa inyi tʼeng'ida-- iyololo-- aajo iatata te shumata masaa sidan naalang' naabik."
Hebrews10:35 Akae-- eminturraa eng'idaroto inyi-- naata ninye olkwaje kitok."
Hebrews10:36 Amu eaku-- piatata olng'iria-- peiye intobiribiri eyeunoto Engai-- nitumutumu enkisiligata."
Hebrews10:37 Amu epon eng'or enkiti-- pelotu ololotu-- nemeimutie ninye baiki;"
Hebrews10:38 Nelaishiu osupat lai tʼenkirukoto-- kake olorrinyo tekurum-- nemeshipakino oltau lai."
Hebrews10:39 Kake mikira yook loorrinyo tekurum neimin-- kake looata enkirukoto naitopok iltauja."
Hebrews11:1 Era enkirukoto entonai oo nikianyu o esiparoto oo kuna tokitin nimikidol.
Hebrews11:2 Te ina einoto iltung'anak le opa enjakenishu.
Hebrews11:3 Tʼenkirukoto kiyolo-- aajo ore enkop eitobiraki tʼororei lʼEngai-- neitu eaku kuna nikidol tʼentoki nalio."
Hebrews11:4 Tʼenkirukoto eaka Abel Engai enkidasare kitok nelang' Kain; naa te ina einoto enjakenishu-- ajo era supat-- tiaraki naijakenuo Engai tʼenkishooroto enye; naa te ina neton eiro o taata-- etua."
Hebrews11:5 Tʼenkirukoto eitainyeki Henok-- pemetum enkea-- neitu edoli-- amu Engai naitaia ninye; amu ore eton eitu eitaini-- neata enjakenishu ajo enyorruni tʼEngai."
Hebrews11:6 Amu teni metii enkirukoto-- meidimai penyorruni too ngonyek Olaitoriani. Amu ore oloyeu nelo enetii Engai-- meata kata nemeiruk-- ajo etii ninye neisho kulo ooing'oru ninye-- olkwaje."
Hebrews11:7 Tʼenkirukoto eitaa Noa Engai kitok-- petum ororei lʼEngai too mbaak neitu edoli-- neitobir engalawa naaku enkitopuata engaji enye; te ina eigwenaka olmaa neaku olajung'oni lʼesupato naing'ua enkirukoto."
Hebrews11:8 Tʼenkirukoto etoning'o Abraham peipoti metupuku alo ilo osho otiakaki ajo elajung'u; nepuku alo meyolo enebaia.
Hebrews11:9 Tʼenkirukoto etaa ninye olomoni te idya kop naisiligaki anaa me enenye-- nemanya atua ilng'oborri te nebo o Isaak o Yakoob-- ootaa te nebo o ninye lajung'ok le ina kisiligata--"
Hebrews11:10 amu etaanyutua ina ang' naata enkitamanyunoto-- amu ore olashetunoni o olaitobirani-- naa Engai."
Hebrews11:11 Tʼenkirukoto etang amua Sara enkidimata nemenai tʼeishoi ina kata etaa moruo netulusoiye larin lenyena-- amu eikena aa supat ilo oisiliga."
Hebrews11:12 Akae-- etoiwuoki tʼosesen obo-- ten aa etiu anaa otua-- ilkumok-- loorisiore lakir le shumata tʼenkumoi-- netiu anaa osunyai lʼembata olbalbal lemeikenai."
Hebrews11:13 Netuata kulo pookin tʼenkirukoto neitu opa ninje etum nkisiligat-- kake etadua tʼenelakwa neilejilej aten too nona-- nenyorru neibalu-- aajo era ninje lomon o ilkaponu tʼenkop."
Hebrews11:14 Amu lelo oojo neijia-- eibalu aajo eing'oru olosho lora."
Hebrews11:15 Naa ten ak einyaakitia aadamu ilo osho otung'uaitie-- anaata einoto erishata narrinyore."
Hebrews11:16 Kake eyeu taata ninje olosho oikash-- naa shumata ilo. Te ina bae mekurru Engai-- teni eji Engai enye-- amu eitobiraka ninje engang."
Hebrews11:17 Tʼenkirukoto eidasa Abraham Isaak-- peitasuri-- neishooio Oinoti lenye obo-- eidipa atang'amu nkisiligat--"
Hebrews11:18 naa ninye otiakaki: Te Isaak kimpoti eishoi ino--"
Hebrews11:19 neiken ajo eidim Engai aitopiu si too lootuata; onaa-- einyaaka atum ninye anaa enkitanyanyukiet."
Hebrews11:20 Tʼenkirukoto etamayana Isaak Yakoob o Esau too ntokitin naapuonu akenya.
Hebrews11:21 Tʼenkirukoto etamayana Yakoob-- pee-- nkera pokira are e Yosef-- nesai airishakino elukunya eng'udi enye."
Hebrews11:22 Tʼenkirukoto-- penyikaki Yosef enkea-- nelimu ninye ororei lʼempukunoto oo nkera Israel-- neisho enkitanapata tʼolbae loo loik lenyena."
Hebrews11:23 Tʼenkirukoto-- peini Mose-- neisudoo lootoiutuo ninye-- tiaraki natadua-- aajo enkerai sidai-- neitu eure ninje enkitanapata olkarsis."
Hebrews11:24 Tʼenkirukoto-- pebulu Mose-- etanya eipoti ajo enkerai entito e Farao--"
Hebrews11:25 nenyor ategelu osina te nebo o olorere lʼEngai nelang eng'ida ele maa naing'ua enkitarruoto--"
Hebrews11:26 neiken ajo era emoroto e Kristos endupoto kitok nelang' masaa sidan e Misri; amu eing'oraiye ninye olkwaje.
Hebrews11:27 Tʼenkirukoto etung'aiye ninye Misri nemeure engoro olkarsis-- amu eibung'are ilo leitu edol anaa olodolita."
Hebrews11:28 Tʼenkirukoto eibung'a pasaka o idya kisuakinoto osarge-- pemeporoo ilo oiminie ilkikaunot-- ilkulenye."
Hebrews11:29 Tʼenkirukoto eima ninje tʼempolos Olbalbal Odo anaa tʼenkop natoiyo; netem Ilmisrin aajo kinko neijia-- nemut ninje engare."
Hebrews11:30 Tʼenkirukoto etuurori isunda e Yeriko-- peidip aataman ngolong'i naapishana."
Hebrews11:31 Tʼenkirukoto eitu eimin Rahab-- idya naibor onyek-- te nebo o kulo leitu eiruk-- amu etang'amua lelo aikitalak tʼeseriani."
Hebrews11:32 Naa kainyo apon ajo? Amu mebaiki enkata-- ten alimu lomon le Gideon o le Barak o le Simson o le Yefta o le David-- o le Samuel-- o loo layolounok--"
Hebrews11:33 ootigilutua nkarsishuni tʼenkirukoto-- neitobir esupato-- netum nkisiligat-- nenuk ilgoso loo lng'atunyo--"
Hebrews11:34 near engolon enkima-- neilany empijan olalem-- netum enkidimata tiatua enjalan-- negolu ninje t'enjore-- nemir njoreitin oo lmangati--"
Hebrews11:35 neitoki aatum ng'oroyok lootuata lenye eitopiwuoki aaitung'ua enkea. Ore kulekai etaaraki tʼemion-- neany elakunoto-- peiye etum ninje enkitopiunoto nara."
Hebrews11:36 Ore kulekai eting'kiakitia emoroto o arat-- te nebo o nkeenda o enkibooroto;"
Hebrews11:37 netaaraki too soito-- netudung'oki tʼolmusumeno-- netaremoki-- netaraki tʼolalem; nemanimanaa eishopito ndapan oo ntare o ndapan oo nkineji-- lemeata toki-- netum osina o enkinyala--"
Hebrews11:38 (lemenarikino enkop)-- netaa ninje loomanimanaa ti ang'ata-- o too ldonyo-- o too ngapunia-- o tiatua ngumot enkop."
Hebrews11:39 Ore kulo pookin einoto enjakenishu tʼenkirukoto-- neitu eng'amu enkisiligata--"
Hebrews11:40 amu etang'asa Engai aitaany yook entoki nadupa-- pemeitabaiari ninje neme te nebo o yook."
Hebrews12:1 Akae si yook-- likiata erukenya naba nji oo ljaken looman yook-- maitapero orridati pookin oiroshi o enkitarruoto naibung'are yook-- makwetiki tʼolng'iria engilunoto natipikaki yook lukunya--"
Hebrews12:2 maimariria Yesus ora olaiturukoni o olaitabaiani lʼenkirukoto-- oting'iriaka esalaba tʼewueji eng'ida natii engomom enye-- neitu eshilaa enkurruna-- neton te tatene olorika lʼenkitoria lʼEngai."
Hebrews12:3 Entadamutu oloting'iriaka engogong'i naba nji oo laitarruok tiatua kion-- peiye minaurara nimileporiri too ltauja linyi."
Hebrews12:4 Eton eitu iariara meeu osarge igilunorere enkitarruoto--"
Hebrews12:5 nitorikinote enkilejilejata nairorie ndai anaa nkera: Nakerai ai-- mimenu earata Olaitoriani-- nimiliilaa-- teni kiar ninye!"
Hebrews12:6 Amu olonyor Olaitoriani-- ninye ear; near ninye enkerai pookin nang'amu ninye."
Hebrews12:7 Teni ing'iriri earata-- neiken Engai ndai anaa nkera; amu Kaa kerai mear menye?"
Hebrews12:8 Naa ten eitu itumutumu earata natang'ara pookin-- nitaa ndai iyat-- me iinot."
Hebrews12:9 Ore pekiata yook loopapa lʼosesen lang'-- ootaara yook-- nikianyit ninje-- meaku pekipon aaning' ilo menye loo lmumuan-- pekinjiu?"
Hebrews12:10 Amu too nkuti olong'i etaara ninje yook-- anaa petadua aajo sidai-- kake ore ninye tʼeretokinoto-- pekitum aatang'amu esinyaroto enye."
Hebrews12:11 Ore earata pookin tʼena kata natii-- melio ajo era eng'ida-- kake enkilishoto; elaisho ake tekurum ilmomo lʼeseriani o lʼesupato kulo looiteng'enaki te ninye."
Hebrews12:12 Onaa-- entorioi ngaik naatuurori o nkung' naatalepori--"
Hebrews12:13 entaa ngoitoi naaitoriori oo nkejek inyi-- pemeiwang'iwang' o obo anaa olng'ojine-- kake peikashu aishiu."
Hebrews12:14 Enkwetiki eseriani too ltung'anak pookin o esinyaroto-- amu medol o obo Olaitoriani metii ena."
Hebrews12:15 Eng'orai-- pemeng'oru o obo tʼe-ng'adunoto Engai-- pemebulu entonata o nabo nadua naitirik ndai-- neidurukieki ilkumok te ina."
Hebrews12:16 Njoo mera o obo olaitobirani loo mbaak torrok oo nkiri arashu osuuji anaa Esau otimira tʼolbae lʼendaa nabo enkikaushu enye.
Hebrews12:17 Amu entayolo-- aajo ore petayeuo ninye tekurum nejung'u emayani-- etemenaki-- amu eitu etum ninye eng'adata enkitaalata-- baiki eing'oraa naleng' too lkiyo."
Hebrews12:18 Amu eitu ipuonunu enetii oldonyo oirrapirrapuni-- oiwuwu tʼenkima-- o emiso o enaimin o enkutishoto kitok enkijape"
Hebrews12:19 o eorunoto esekegwa o oltoilo loo rorei lotanyaita kulo-- lootoning'o-- pemeponikini ninje ororei;"
Hebrews12:20 amu eitu eidim aatanapakinore enaitanapaki: Baiki ten eporoo olowuaru oldonyo-- nepuoi aanang' too soito arashu tʼempere metua;"
Hebrews12:21 eitureishe baiki neijia ena kitaduaroto metejo Mose: Aaibung'a enkuretishu neikirikira.
Hebrews12:22 Kake ietuo ndai oldonyo Sion o engang' Engai naishiu-- Yerusalem natii shumata-- o iip nkujit oo lmalaikan-- o enkiturrurroto kitok olorere--"
Hebrews12:23 o esirit oo lkikauni lootisiraki te shumata-- o Engai-- olaigwenani loo pookin-- o ilmumuan loo supati looitabaiyoki--"
Hebrews12:24 o olaidikidikoni lʼosotua ng'ejuk-- Yesus-- o osarge lʼenkisuaroto loiro sidai nelang' le Abel."
Hebrews12:25 Eng'orai-- emiany ele olimu. Amu ten eitu edany lelo ootanyaita oloiroro tʼenkop-- ke melusoo pe mikilany-- teni kiany ilo oiro aing'ua shumata?"
Hebrews12:26 Ore te ina kata eikirikirie oltoilo lenye enkop-- kake ore taata eisiligishe-- ajo: o nabo kata alaing'unung'unye me enkop ake-- kake shumata si."
Hebrews12:27 Kake ore kulo rorei „o nabo kata“ eitayolou aajo-- epuoi aaitaal naaing'unung'un-- eji nena naaitobiraki-- peiye ebik nemeing'unung'un."
Hebrews12:28 Akae-- tiaraki nikitum enkarsishu nemeing'unung'un-- kiata eng'adunoto nikisyayakinye Engai-- nikintiship ninye tʼenganyit o tʼenkuretishu."
Hebrews12:29 Amu era Engai ang' enkima napejisno.
Hebrews13:1 Njebik enyorrata oo lalashera.
Hebrews13:2 Emirikino enkitoomonoto oo lomon; amu eitoomono ilkulekai-- meyolo-- ilmalaikan."
Hebrews13:3 Entadamutu looteenaki anaa looteenaki te nebo o ninje-- o kulo looisilitoi-- anaa litiiti ndai oopeny atua iseseni."
Hebrews13:4 Njeata enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni too pookin enkitook-- njoo meata enkirragata entibili. Amu eigwenaki Engai laitobirak loo mbaak torrok oo nkiri o laarak lʼenkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni--"
Hebrews13:5 Njoo metii orregie lʼenyorrata oo masaa-- entigirata too ntokitin naatai; amu ninye otejo: Maapal iye namaaing'ua;"
Hebrews13:6 kinteu baiki yook aatejo: Era Olaitoriani olaretoni lai namalo aureisho. Kainyo aasaki oltung'ani?
Hebrews13:7 Entadamutu laiturukok linyi-- looinosakitia ndai lomon lʼEngai-- eng'orai enkiting'oto empuan enye-- entusuj enkirukoto enye."
Hebrews13:8 Yesus Kristos ng'ole o taata o ninye ilo metabaiki nkatan pookin.
Hebrews13:9 Eminjo peimalimali ndai too nkiteng'enareitin oo muain kumok o ngomon; amu sidai ten egolu oltau tʼeng'adunoto-- me too ndaikin nemeitudup kulo loonyamal too ninje."
Hebrews13:10 Kiata olperere lʼenkidasare lemeaku kulo ooramat ena aji-- neinos."
Hebrews13:11 Amu ore lelo shang'it-- ooaki olaidasani kitok osarge lenye atua ewueji sinyati-- nepej ori seseni lenye tʼenkima ti aulo enkirragata."
Hebrews13:12 Onaa si ninye Yesus-- pesinyaa olorere tʼosarge lenye openy-- neaku oinoto enkisiloto ti aulo engalo kishomi."
Hebrews13:13 Akae-- maapeti si yook aaing'ua enkirragata-- enetii ninye-- pekinap emoroto enye."
Hebrews13:14 Amu mikiata tene engang' nabik-- kake king'oru engai nalotu."
Hebrews13:15 Onaa-- mayaki Engai enkidasare enkitadararoto oshi tiatua ninye-- naa ilmomo loo njonito oo nkutukie naaibalu engarna enye."
Hebrews13:16 Emirikino aaitobira sidan ning'aring'ara-- amu eiting'id kuna kidasareitin Engai."
Hebrews13:17 Entoning' laiturukok linyi-- entusuj ninje-- amu eishololo ninje tʼolbae loo lmumuan linyi anaa loopuoi aaikilikwan-- petum aaitobira tʼeng'ida meang'iang'-- amu meisho ndai ena endupoto."
Hebrews13:18 Entoomonoki yook. King'idare ena-- pekiata oitoilo sidai lʼoltau nikinyok aaibung' orregie sidai too pookin."
Hebrews13:19 Adiding' ndai naleng' pinkoko nji-- patum atorrinyoi enitiiti ndai asioki."
Hebrews13:20 Ore Engai eseriani-- natorikuo aitung'ua too lootuata ele shokut kitok loo ntare-- tʼosarge lʼosotua loo nkatan pookin-- ninye Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos--"
Hebrews13:21 njeitaa ndai looitabaia enkyas sidai pookin-- pitumutumu aataas enayeu ninye-- neas tiatua ndai enaitiship ninye te Yesus Kristos; enenye enkitook nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin. Amen."
Hebrews13:22 Kake adiding' ndai-- lalashera lainei-- entang'amutu ele rorei lʼendiding'aroto-- amu atisiraka ndai too lkuti rorei."
Hebrews13:23 Entayoloito-- aajo eidipaki aatalaku olalashe lang' Timoteos. Ten elotu asioki-- naladol ndai te nebo o ninye."
Hebrews13:24 Eroroki laiturukok linyi pookin o sinyat pookin. Eiroroki ndai lalashera ootii Italia.
Hebrews13:25 Njebik eng'adunoto te nebo o ndai pookin. Amen.
James1:1 Yakobos-- osinga lʼEngai o lʼOlaitoriani Yesus Kristos: eninyi ena palai-- ndai kuna tipati tomon o are naaisardakakinote nkwapi. Entasupai!"
James1:2 Enkena aajo eng'ida nabore-- lalashera lainei-- ten ibatatakinono atua nkitasurot oo mpukunot kumok--"
James1:3 niyololo-- aajo eitaa enkirukoto inyi-- ten eitoriori-- olng'iria."
James1:4 Ore olng'iria-- meata kata nemebik egol metabaiki enkiting'oto-- piakuku lbaiarot oolulung'a lemeng'oriki toki."
James1:5 Ten etii oltung'ani linyi otong'orikia eng'eno-- njesai ninye Engai naisho oltung'ani pookin tʼenkumoi nemeisikong'aki-- neaku eishori ninye."
James1:6 Kake njoo metasaya tʼenkirukoto-- meata enking'arrirroto. Amu oloing'arrirro nenyanyukie lopir lʼenaiposha-- ooreota neiposhiposh enkijape."
James1:7 Njoo mejo ilo tung'ani-- ajo elang'amu ninye toki tʼOlaitoriani;"
James1:8 ore oltung'ani orisha oltau-- nemeitoriori too ngoitoi enyena pookin."
James1:9 Ore olalashe lora oti-- njeitadaraa kion tʼenkitook enye--"
James1:10 ore oladupani-- njeitadaraa kion tʼenkitadounoto enye-- amu elusoo anaa entapukai oo nkujit."
James1:11 Eilepu engolong' te nebo o enkirowuaj-- netoi nkujit-- nerarunye entapukai enye-- neimin enkishaa enkitobirata enye. Neijia si etiu oladupani-- einaaia too nkyasin enyena pookin."
James1:12 Tesh oltung'ani oting'iria tʼenkitasuroto-- amu ore etaa etaleenoki-- nelang'amu enkaja empuan naisiliga Olaitoriani kulo loonyor ninye."
James1:13 Njoo mejo o obo loitasuri: aaitasur Engai. Amu meitasuri Engai too ntorrok-- nemeitasur ninye openy oltung'ani o obo."
James1:14 Eitasuri oltung'ani pookin tʼolng'warra lenye openy-- loroju neisis ninye."
James1:15 Ore tekurum eidipa atang'amu olng'warra neiu ninye enkitarruoto-- ore petabaiye enkitarruoto neiu ninye enkea."
James1:16 Emimanimanaa-- lalashera lainei lanyor!"
James1:17 Eing'ua enkishooroto pookin sidai o enkishooroto nabaia shumata-- edou eing'ua enetii Menye loo nkilang'eta-- nemetii enetii ninye enkitaalata arashu oloip lʼenkibelekenyata."
James1:18 Etoiwuo ninye yook tʼeyeunoto enye-- tʼororei lʼesipata-- pekiaku yook enkiterata oo nkitobirat enyena."
James1:19 Onaa-- lalashera lainei lanyor-- njeaku oltung'ani pookin losioki ainining'u-- lemesioki agoro;"
James1:20 amu meitobir engoro oltung'ani enaaku tʼEngai.
James1:21 Onaa-- entautu olduruki pookin o enkumoi entorroni-- ning'amumu tʼemborran ororei-- lotuunoki atua ndai-- loidim aitopua iltauja linyi."
James1:22 Entaa laitobirak lʼororei-- me laning'ok ake-- pemilejileje aten."
James1:23 Amu teni era oltung'ani olaning'oni lʼororei nemera olaitobirani-- nenyanyukie ninye oltung'ani loing'oraa engomom osesen lenye tʼenking'oret."
James1:24 Ore peidip aing'orai-- nelo nerikino nabo kata enetiu."
James1:25 Ore loturuma atua nkitanapat naabaia elakunoto-- nemera olaning'oni lorikinisho-- kake olaitobirani lʼenkyas-- neaku ninye tesh tiatua enkitobirata enye."
James1:26 Teni ejo oltung'ani-- ajo era olaisyayani lʼEngai-- nemeitore olng'ejep lenye-- kake elej oltau lenye-- nera enkisyayare enye ne pesho."
James1:27 Ore enkisyayare sidai nemeata eleyata tʼengomom Engai-- Papa-- era ena: Enking'orare oo lokishin o en oo ngolia tiatua enkilishoto enye-- o erripore e kion tʼolmaa-- pemeata entibili."
James2:1 Lalashera lainei-- eminken-- aajo eing'oraa enkirukoto e atua Yesus Kristos-- Olaitoriani lʼenkitook lang'-- entemet oltung'ani."
James2:2 Amu ten emut ejing'u oltumo linyi oltung'ani oishopo olgisoi le sahabu o olkila sidai-- neitoki alotu olaisinani oishopito olkila duruki--"
James2:3 ning'oring'oro ndai ele oishopo olkila sidai-- nijokiki ninye: Totona tʼene wueji sidai-- nintokiki aajoki ele aisinani: Ntasho iye tʼende-- arashu: Totona ene abori olorika loo nkejek ainei:"
James2:4 anaata eitu intoorioro tiatua ndai aten-- niakuku laigwenak oosuj ndamunot torrok?"
James2:5 Entoning'oki nanu-- ndai-- lalashera lainei lanyor-- keitu egelu Engai laisinak lʼena kop loora ladupak lʼenkirukoto o lajung'ok lʼenkarsishu-- naisiligaka kulo oonyor ninye?"
James2:6 Kake ore ndai-- itemenaitie oltung'ani aisinani. Me ladupak ooek ndai neyetu ndai tʼengomom enkigwena enye?"
James2:7 Ke-- memor ninje engarna sidai naipotieki ndai?"
James2:8 Ten intabaiaia enkitanapata olkarsis-- anaa pejo esirata: Tonyorra oltung'ani lʼelatia ino anaa kion-- ninkoko sidai--"
James2:9 kake ten ing'oraara entemet oltung'ani-- nintarruorruo-- neaku nkitanapat iljaken-- aajo irara lalang'ak."
James2:10 Amu teni eibung' oltung'ani nkitanapat pookin neitarruoki nabo-- etaa oloitarruoko pookin."
James2:11 Amu olotejo: „Miar enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni!“ etejo baiki: „Miar metua!“ Akae-- teni eitu iar enkidikidikoto olmoruo o eng'oroyoni-- kake itaara metua-- itaa olalang'ani loo nkitanapat."
James2:12 Eroro nji-- enkuna nji-- anaa loopuoi aaigwenaki too nkitanapat elakunoto."
James2:13 Amu etum enkigwena-- metii eng'adunoto-- lemenana oshoke; neitadaraa kion enanai e oshoke-- meure enkigwena."
James2:14 Kaa dupoto ena-- lalashera-- teni ejo oltung'ani-- ajo eata enkirukoto nemeata nkitobirat? Keidim aitopua enkirukoto ninye?"
James2:15 Teni meishopo olalashe arashu enganashe nelau embaikinoto endaa--"
James2:16 nejoki obo linyi ninje: Esere naa-- erowuajie aten-- entaraposhoto! niminjosho ninje launot osesen: kaa dupoto ena?"
James2:17 Neijia baiki enkirukoto-- teni meata nkitobirat-- netua tiatua kion openy."
James2:18 Kake ebaiki oltung'ani ejo: Iata iye enkirukoto-- naata nanu nkitobirat. Ntaduaki enkirukoto ino metii nkitobirat-- nayeu naaitadol iye too nkitobirat ainei enkirukoto ai."
James2:19 Iruk iye-- ajo etii Engai nabo. Itaasa sidai; neiruk si ninje loiriruani-- neikirikira."
James2:20 Ke-- iyeu niyolou-- oltung'ani oilash-- ajo etua enkirukoto nemeata nkitobirat?"
James2:21 Keitu eitaai Abraham-- Papa lang'-- supat tʼolbae loo nkitobirat-- peidas Oinoti lenye Isaak tʼolperere lʼenkidasare?"
James2:22 Idol taa-- ajo eitobirishore enkirukoto nkitobirat enyena-- neitabaiyoki enkirukoto too nkitobirat;"
James2:23 nebaia esirata najo: Eiruko Abraham Engai-- neikenakini ninye ena esupato-- neipoti: oljore lʼEngai."
James2:24 Itadua ndai-- aajo eitaai oltung'ani supat tʼolbae loo nkitobirat-- me tʼolbae lʼenkirukoto ake."
James2:25 Neija si etiu Rahab-- enda sindani: Keitu eitaai si ninye supat too nkitobirat-- peng'amu lelo aikitalak-- neisho epuku aulo tʼengai oitoi?"
James2:26 Amu anaa petua osesen-- metii Olmumua-- neijia si etua enkirukoto-- metii nkitobirat."
James3:1 Eminjo eyeu oltung'ani pookin too ndai neaku olaiteng'enani-- lalashera lainei-- niyololo-- aajo eigwenakini yook enkigwena nalang'."
James3:2 Amu kintadiak pookin too mbaak kumok. Ore oltung'ani pookin lemeitadiak tʼororei obo-- ninye oltung'ani baiaroti-- neidim si aiboo osesen lenye pookin-- anaa peiboori olbarta opiki esekengei enkutuk."
James3:3 Ng'orai-- kimbooio ilbartan too sekenge aagoliki-- pening' ninje yook-- nikintamanaa seseni lenye pookin."
James3:4 Ng'orai si imeilin-- ten aa sapuki naleng'-- nereo ilkutat oogol ninje-- kake eitamanaa ninje enkiti kitamanet ewueji eneyeu oloreota."
James3:5 Neijia si etiu olng'ejep-- era enkiti rubata osesen-- neas mbaak kituak. Ng'orai-- enkiti kima-- kake keba aa entim nainok ninye?"
James3:6 Neijia si olng'ejep-- naa enkima-- neitoki enkop nabore mesupato. Neijia etiu olng'ejep tiatua rubat ang'-- nepik osesen olulung'a ntibil-- neinok orregie lang' pookin-- teni epuku enkiwuwuoto enye aing'ua ewueji e satan."
James3:7 Amu eitamokuni mpukunot pookin oo ng'wesi o noo ntaritik o noo ng'wesi naaikurtutari o noo ng'wesi naatii atua enaiposha-- neitamoku iltung'anak ninje."
James3:8 Kake meidim oltung'ani aitamoku olng'ejep-- entorroni nemegirai-- nabore esayet nadua."
James3:9 Ninye kintadararie Engai Papa-- naa ninye kimorie oltung'ani-- oitobiraki tʼemua Engai."
James3:10 Nepuku tʼenkutuk nabo enkitadararoto o endiata. Njoo meaku neijia-- lalashera lainei."
James3:11 Keitupuku oljorro tʼeululu nabo engare namelok o engare nadua?
James3:12 Keidim-- lalashera lainei-- olng'aboli atoiu ngululu oloirien-- anai enjani olmarua ilng'abolo? Neijia meidim si oljorro oisukut aishoo engare namelok."
James3:13 Kang'ai ora ng'en o jartan too ndai? Njeitaduaia tʼorregie lenye sidai nkitobirat enyena tʼemborran o enʼgeno.
James3:14 Kake teni iatata olom odua o enjangar tiatua iltauja linyi-- emilash nimile jishosho aaibooio esipata."
James3:15 Amu ina me eng'eno nalotu aing'ua shumata-- kake en enkop-- o en oo ltung'anak-- o en oo loiriruani."
James3:16 Amu enetii olom o enjangar-- ine etii enking'oling'olata o enkyas pookin enkurruna."
James3:17 Kake ore eng'eno naing'ua shumata-- era tʼenkiterata shaat-- neitoki aata eseriani-- neborr-- nelelek ening'oto-- nebore enkordunoto o ilmomo sidan-- nemeata enyorrakinoto o esungureishu."
James3:18 Ore olmomoi lʼesupato-- neisuakini tʼeseriani kulo ooitobir eseriani."
James4:1 Kaji eing'ua enjore o olarrabal tiatua ndai? Meing'ua ilng'warraitin linyi ooara tiatua rubat inyi?
James4:2 Ing'warring'warra ndai-- nimitumutumu; imbaroro ndai niatata olom-- niming'amumu; iariara ndai tʼenjore; miatata toki-- amu eitu iomonunu."
James4:3 Iomonunu niming'amumu-- tiaraki niomonunu too ntorrok-- pinosishosho tiatua ilng'warraitin linyi."
James4:4 Ndai-- laitobirak loo mbaak torrok oo nkiri-- miyololo-- aajo era enjoruetishu olmaa emang'atishu Engai? Ore oloyeu neaku oljore lʼolmaa-- neaku ninye olmang'atinda lʼEngai."
James4:5 Arashu ijojo-- ak eiro esirata pesho ojo: Ore Olmumua omany atua ndai-- neng'war nenyokisho?"
James4:6 Kake eisho eng'adunoto nalang'; onaa-- ejo esirata: Eany Engai loowuasa-- kake eisho ninye eng'adunoto looitadou aten."
James4:7 Akae-- entoning' Engai-- nianyianya satan-- neaku eipirri aing'ua ndai."
James4:8 Entinyikaki ndai Engai-- nenyikaki si ninye ndai. Esuja ngaik-- ndai laitarruok-- entaa iltauja linyi shaati-- ndai looing'arrirro."
James4:9 Entoning' osina-- nilishosho-- ninjirishiri; enjoo enkwenia inyi eitaali aaku enkishirata-- o eng'ida inyi neaku enkilishoto."
James4:10 Entadou aten tʼengomom Engai-- nelailepie ndai."
James4:11 Eminteenikino ndai-- lalashera lainei. Ore oloiteeniki olalashe lenye neigwenaki ninye-- neiteeniki ilo neigwenaki nkitanapat. Kake teni ingwenaki nkitanapat-- nimira olaitobirani loo nkitanapat-- kake olaigwenani."
James4:12 Etii obo oishoru nkitanapat neigwenaki-- oloidim aitopua neiminye. Ira iye ng'ai oigwenaki ol elatia ino?"
James4:13 Akae-- aiya-- ndai loojo: Kipuo taata arashu taisere atua ena arashu atua enda ang'-- nikipuo aabik te ina alo olari obo nikintaa enkinyang'a-- pekitum endupoto--"
James4:14 nimiyololo enaaku taisere. Amu kainyo empuan inyi? Nera empuruo nalio enkiti kata-- tekurum neitoki aimisori."
James4:15 Eaku pijojo te ina: Teni elayeu Olaitoriani nikipuo aaishiu-- nikipuo aaitobir ena arashu ina."
James4:16 Kake intadaraara taata aten tiatua olwuasa linyi. Ore enkitadararoto anaa ena nera torrono.
James4:17 Ore oloyolo aitobira sidan-- nemeitobir-- nera te ninye enkitarruoto."
James5:1 Akae-- aiya-- ndai ladupak-- enjira nilishilishi tʼolbae lʼosina olotu shumata inyi."
James5:2 Etobobua endupoto inyi-- nenya laing'ur ilkilani linyi."
James5:3 Ore esahabu inyi o ngoshola inyi etadoro einosa enkop-- ore endoron enkinosata enkop-- neijakenu-- nenya nkiri oo seseni linyi anaa enkima. Inturrurro masaa too ngolong'i naatulusoitie."
James5:4 Ng'orai-- ore olkwaje loo laitobirak ooisambutua nkuruman inyi litomito ndai tʼenkikonya-- ninye oishir; etijing'a enkishirata oo laisambuak atua nkiyaa Olaitoriani loo ltimito."
James5:5 Inosa ndai olkar tʼenkop-- nitonini tiatua naaitiship osesen-- nintotiti iltauja linyi tʼengolong' eyeng'are."
James5:6 Ingwenakitia olora supat niariara-- neitu eany ninye ndai."
James5:7 Enting'iria ndai-- lalashera-- metabau elotunoto Olaitoriani. Eng'orai olaturoni lʼenkuruma eanyu ilmomo sidan lʼenkop-- neng'iri metabana netum enjan elukunya o en e tekurum."
James5:8 Enting'iria si ndai-- nintagoligolo iltauja linyi; amu etinyikua elotunoto Olaitoriani."
James5:9 Emiang'iang'akino obo o olekai-- lalashera lainei-- pemeigwenakini ndai. Ng'o rai-- eitashe olaigwenani te kutukaji."
James5:10 Entusuj-- lalashera lainei-- enkisiloto o olng'iria loo layolounok-- ooirorie tʼengarna Olaitoriani."
James5:11 Ng'orai-- kijo ninje teshi looting'iria. Itoning'o olng'iria le Iyob-- nitadua enkiting'oto Olaitoriani; amu eata Olaitoriani engoshoke nanana-- naa ninye oata enking'urroto."
James5:12 Kake enang'or-- lalashera lainei-- eminturuj-- me te shumata-- neme tʼenkop-- neme tʼengai kiturujata. Njeaku ororei linyi: ee-- ora ee-- o: me-- ora me-- pemibatatata abori enkigwena."
James5:13 Ore peisili obo too ndai-- njesaisho! Ore peng'ida oltung'ani-- njerany singolioitin lʼengauo!"
James5:14 Ore pemoi obo too ndai-- njeipot ninye laigwenak lʼesirit-- pesayaki ninje ninye-- neelie eilata tʼengarna Olaitoriani."
James5:15 Nelaitopok esayata enkirukoto oltamoiyai-- neapaa Olaitoriani ninye; naa teni eitobira nkitarruot-- nepuoi aaitaiki ninje."
James5:16 Akae-- embalakinoto nkitarruot-- entasayakinoto-- pitumutumu aaishiutu. Eidim esayata engolon osupat nkumok."
James5:17 Nera Eliya oltung'ani onyanyukie yook-- nesaisho tʼesayata-- pemesha enjan-- neitu eshaiki enjan enkop laritin okuni o lapaitin ile;"
James5:18 neitoki asaisho-- neishoru shumata enjan-- neiu enkop ilmomo lenyena."
James5:19 Lalashera lainei-- teni eimalimal obo linyi neing'ua esipata-- neibelekenya oltung'ani ninye--"
James5:20 njeyolou ele-- ajo ooibelekenya olaitarruoni tʼengoitoi enye naimalimalie-- nelaitopok ninye empuan enye tʼenkea neopoo enkumoi oo nkitarruot."
1Peter1:1 Petros-- olairriwani le Yesus Kristos: too lomon ootegeluaki-- ooisardakakinote Pontus o Galatia o Kapadokia o Asia o Bitinia--"
1Peter1:2 loora gelunot lʼEngai Papa tʼeyolounoto enye neba opa-- o tiatua esinyaroto Olmumua Sinyati metabaiki ening'oto o enkisuakinoto osarge le Yesus Kristos. Metoponari eng'adunoto o eseriani Engai too ndai!"
1Peter1:3 Njeitadarari Engai o Menye lʼOlaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos-- lotoiwuo yook kat are tʼenanai enye kitok e oshoke-- pekitum eanyunoto naishiu tʼempiunoto e Yesus Kristos too lootuata--"
1Peter1:4 pekitum enjung'o nemerruoio-- nemeata entibili-- nemeinaaia-- natorripokoki ndai te shumata--"
1Peter1:5 ndai loorripi tiatua engolon Engai tʼenkirukoto-- pitumutumu enkitopuata naitobirieki-- peboluni tʼenkata enkiting'oto."
1Peter1:6 Nipuopuo aagalalu te ina kata-- baiki teni meata kata nemeilishieki ndai enkiti kata too nkitasurot oo muain kumok--"
1Peter1:7 petumi enkirukoto inyi enataleenoki neata enkinyang'a kitok nelang' esahabu namuta naleeni tʼenkima-- neaku enkitadararoto o enkitook o enganyit tiatua embolunoto e Yesus Kristos--"
1Peter1:8 leitu idolidolo ninyorrinyorro nirukuruku ninye nimidolitata taata-- nipuopuo aagalalu tʼeng'ida nemeiroroi o enaitadarari--"
1Peter1:9 nipuopuo aaea enkiting'oto enkirukoto inyi-- nera enkitopuata oo ltauja linyi."
1Peter1:10 Ore ina kitopuata-- eing'orutua neikeernu layolounok ooitayolo ena ng'adunoto nipuopuo aatum ndai."
