1Peter1:11 Eikeernutuo-- aajo kaa kata arashu kaa pukunoto natuutua Olmumua le Kristos otii atua ninje-- netang'asa aijakenu nkisilot e Kristos o enkitook nasuju tekurum."
1Peter1:12 Etabolokoki ninje metayolo; amu eitu eisyayaki aten-- kake ndai-- tiatua nena baak naainosakitia taata ndai lelo ooakitia ndai euangelion tʼOlmumua Sinyati-- oirriuaki aitung'ua shumata-- naa mbaak naang'war si ilmalaikan pedol."
1Peter1:13 Onaa-- enteen mpolosi oo ndamunot inyi-- enjololoto-- enting'idare metabaiki enkiting'oto empuris nayakini ndai tiatua embolunoto e Yesus Kristos--"
1Peter1:14 anaa nkera naaning'isho-- emimbung' orregie loo lng'warraitin linyi lʼenkata elukunya litonyorra miyololo--"
1Peter1:15 kake anaa peyeu oloipoto ndai-- ora sinyati-- entaa si ndai sinyat tiatua orregie pookin--"
1Peter1:16 amu etisiraki: njoo irara sinyat-- amu ara nanu sinyati."
1Peter1:17 Naa tiaraki nimpotipoto ninye Papa oigwenaki oltung'ani pookin anaa petiu enkyas enye-- meing'oraa entemet enye-- entilimanata tiatua enkuretishu tʼenkata inyi nitiiyeiye ene--"
1Peter1:18 iyololo-- aajo eitu elakuni ndai too naarruoio-- too ngoshola arashu tʼesahabu-- tʼemokunoto inyi musana nitang'amutua too loominyi--"
1Peter1:19 kake tʼosarge ogol enkinyang'a anaa lʼembalelo neitu eitarruo nemeata entibili-- le Kristos--"
1Peter1:20 loiturukieki ayolou-- eton eitu epiki entonata olmaa-- kake loitalioiyoki tʼenkiting'oto oo nkatan tʼolbae linyi--"
1Peter1:21 ndai liruko te ninye Engai-- naitopiwuo ninye tiatua lootuata neisho ninye enkitook-- peiye iatata enkirukoto inyi o eanyunoto e atua Engai."
1Peter1:22 Esuja iltauja linyi tiatua ening'oto esipata tʼolmumua-- piatata enyorrata oo lalashera nemeitusupatuo-- entonyorrata too ltauja naleng'--"
1Peter1:23 anaa lootoiwuoki kat are-- me tʼembeu erruoroto-- kake te nemerruoio-- tʼororei lʼEngai naishiu obik nkatan pookin."
1Peter1:24 Amu Era enkiring'o pookin anaa olkujita-- o enkitook enye pookin anaa entapukai olkujita; etoiyo olkujita nerarunye entapukai;"
1Peter1:25 kake ebik ororei lʼOlaitoriani nkatan pookin. Nera ninye ele rorei loinosuaki too ndai.
1Peter2:1 Akae-- enturrai entorroni pookin o olosek pookin o enkitusupatuo o engilata e tau o elikioroto pookin;"
1Peter2:2 entang'warr anaa nkera naa eneiunyeki kule eng'eno nemeata olosek-- pipuopuo aabulaki too kuna atua enkitopuata--"
1Peter2:3 teni inyorrinyorra-- aajo ebor Olaitoriani."
1Peter2:4 Ipuonunu enetii ninye anaa osoit oishiu loiturraitie iltung'anak-- kake lotegelua Engai negol enkinyang'a."
1Peter2:5 Enteshet si ndai aten anaa soito looishiu-- piakuku engaji emumuaishu-- nipuopuo aaitobir enkyas sinyati olaidasani-- ninjoioio nkidasareitin emumuaishu naaiting'id Engai te Yesus Kristos."
1Peter2:6 Onaa etisiraki tiatua esirata: Ng'orai-- apik atua Sion osoit kitok lʼolpijata otegeluaki negol enkinyang'a-- naa oloiruk ninye-- nemelakurru."
1Peter2:7 Akae-- nera ninye too ndai looiruk-- lʼenkinyang'a nagol; kake etaa ele soit-- loiturraitie lashetak neaku olkitok lʼolpijata lʼengaji-- too lemeiruk"
1Peter2:8 osoit lʼenkikoboto o osoit lʼenkitarrikino; nepuo aaikob ninje aten tiatua ororei nemening'isho-- etipikaki ninje baiki atua ena."
1Peter2:9 Kake irara ndai eishoi nategeluaki-- enkyas olaidasani olkarsis-- olorere sinyati-- olorere lenye-- pitumutumu aainosutu sidan oloipotoko ndai tʼenaimin atua enkilang'et enye naiputukunyi;"
1Peter2:10 leitu irara opa olorere-- kake irara taata olorere lʼEngai-- leitu eibung'akini ndai engoshoke nanana-- kake eibung'akaki taata."
1Peter2:11 Lanyor-- adiding' ndai anaa lomon o iltung'anak lʼolototo-- pipaasharere ilng'warraitin loo nkiri looarare Olmumua"
1Peter2:12 niatata orregie sidai tiatua loreren-- pedol kulo looimaki ndai anaa laitobirak loo ntorrok-- nkyasin inyi sidan neitadaraa Engai tʼengolong' eleenoto."
1Peter2:13 Entipik aten abori enkitoria pookin oo ltung'anak tʼolbae lʼOlaitoriani-- ten aa olkarsis lolang' kulekai--"
1Peter2:14 ten aa larikok looirriua ninye-- pelaaki laitobirak loo ntorrok neitadaraa laitobirak loo sidan."
1Peter2:15 Amu era ena eyeunoto Engai-- pipising'ing'i nkutukie o emodaishu oo ltung'anak lemeata eng'eno-- intobiribiri sidan;"
1Peter2:16 anaa loolakuno-- nimintaata elakunoto anaa enaopoo entorroni-- kake anaa laisyayak lʼEngai."
1Peter2:17 Entaa kituak iltung'anak pookin-- entonyor lalashera-- enturia Engai-- enjoo olkarsis enkitook."
1Peter2:18 Laisyayak-- entoning laitoriak tʼenkuretishu pookin-- me isidan o loobor ake-- kake baiki lemebor--"
1Peter2:19 Amu era ena empuris-- teni eng'iriaki oltung'ani nkisilot tʼolbae lʼoltoilo lʼoltau edamu Engai-- netum osina pesho."
1Peter2:20 Kaa kitadararoto ena-- teni ing'iriri neari ndai intarruorruo? Kake teni intobiribiri sidan neisili ndai ning'iriri-- era ena empuris tʼengomom Engai."
1Peter2:21 Amu eipotoki ndai te ina-- amu eisiloki baiki Kristos tʼolbae linyi neing'uaiki ndai olponoto-- pisujusuju rregiei lenyena;"
1Peter2:22 leitu eitobir enkitarruoto o nabo neitu etumi olmarengei o obo tiatua enkutuk enye;
1Peter2:23 leitu emorisho-- etamoroki ninye; neitu eitureishe-- eisiloki ninye; kake eitarasaka pookin ele loigwenaki aitorio;"
1Peter2:24 olotanapa nkitarruot ang' tiatua osesen lenye shumata enjata-- pikinjiuoki esupato-- kituatakitia nkitarruot; injiutuo too lbaak lenyena."
1Peter2:25 Amu nanyanyukie ntare naaisardaka-- kake etorrinyokoki ndai taata olairritani o olaing'orani loo lmumuan linyi."
1Peter3:1 Entotiu neijia-- na ng'oroyok-- entoning' ilmoruak linyi-- pe-- teni etii lemeiruk ororei-- etumi tʼorregie loo ng'oroyok enye-- metii rorei--"
1Peter3:2 tiaraki nadol ninje orregie linyi shaat tʼenkuretishu.
1Peter3:3 Njoo meaku enkaja inyi en e boo tʼenjetata oo lpapit o tʼeikare esahabu o tʼenkishopoto oo lkilani--"
1Peter3:4 kake enkaja tiatua-- enememuta emborran-- Olmumua ogira nebor; nera sidai naleng' tʼengomom Engai."
1Peter3:5 Amu neijia opa etakaja ng'oroyok sinyat aten-- naa Engai etipika eanyunoto enye-- nening' ilmoruak lenye--"
1Peter3:6 anaa petoning'o Sara Abraham neipot ninye Olaitoriani lenye; nitaa ndai nkera enyena-- teni intobiribiri sidan nimiureishosho nimiruturutu too pookin."
1Peter3:7 Entotiu si neijia-- ndai le moruak-- entushulare ninje tʼeng'eno-- enjoo eng'oroyoni anaa enaret nemeata engolon enkitook-- anaa naajung'u te nebo o ndai eng'adunoto empuan-- pememitikini sayat inyi."
1Peter3:8 Ore tʼenkiting'oto-- njoo iatata pookin ndamunot naanyanyuk-- nirara loong'ar nkisilot-- loonyor lalashera-- looata ngoshuak naanana-- looitadou aten."
1Peter3:9 Emilak entorroni tʼentorroni-- arashu enkilepilepata tʼenkilepilepata-- kake entamayanishoto-- amu iyololo-- aajo eipotoki ndai te ina-- pipuopuo aajung'u emayani."
1Peter3:10 Amu oloyeu nenyor empuan enye nedol ngolong'i sidan-- njerishie olng'ejep lenye entorroni o njonito enkutuk enye-- pemelimu olosek."
1Peter3:11 Njeibelekenya tʼentorroni neitobir sidan-- njeing'oru eseriani nesuj ninye;"
1Peter3:12 amu etii ngonyek Olaitoriani shumata oo supati-- nening' nkiyaa enyena omonot enye-- kake eiba engomom Olaitoriani looitobir ntorrok."
1Peter3:13 Naa kang'ai oidim aitobiraki ndai ntorrok-- teni irara ndai lanyuak loo sidan?"
1Peter3:14 Naa teni iatata nkisilot tʼolbae Mesupato-- nirara teshi. Emiurei enkituriata enye-- emiirut!"
1Peter3:15 Kake entisinyai Olaitoriani Kristos tiatua iltauja linyi. Entobirakinoto-- pialulu oltung'ani pookin oikilikwan ndai ororei tʼolbae lʼeanyunoto natii atua ndai--"
1Peter3:16 kake tʼemborran o tʼenkuretishu o tʼoltoilo sidai lʼoltau-- peaku ore kulo ooimaki ndai anaa looitobir ntorrok-- neitukurruni-- tiaraki natamoro orregie linyi sidai tiatua Kristos."
1Peter3:17 Enaikash teni eitamei oltung'ani eas sidan-- ten aa eyeunoto Engai-- alang' teni eitamei eas ntorrok."
1Peter3:18 Amu etua baiki Kristos nabo kata tʼolbae loo nkitarruot ang'-- osupat tʼolbae loo lemeata esupato-- peiye erik yook enetii Engai; etaaraki metua tʼosesen meitaai eshiu tʼolmumua;"
1Peter3:19 eshomo baiki te ilo peinosaki ilmumuan tʼenkibooroto--"
1Peter3:20 leitu opa ening'isho eton eanyisho olng'iria lʼEngai too nkatan e Noa naaitobiritai emeili-- naa ina naitopokieki ilkuti ake tauja-- oora isiet-- tʼengare."
1Peter3:21 Naa engare naitopok si yook taata tʼenkibatisa naitanyanyukieki te ina-- nemera enjororoto oloirerio lʼosesen-- kake osotua lʼoltoilo sidai lʼoltau oitoriokinore Engai tʼolbae lʼempiunoto e Yesus Kristos--"
1Peter3:22 oilepa shumata neton te tatene Engai: ore ilmalaikan o nkitoriaitin o nkidimat-- naa nʼenkitoria enye."
1Peter4:1 Tiaraki nating'iriaka Kristos yook nkisilot osesen-- akae-- enterreten si ndai aten te ina otikinoto-- amu ore ilo oitamioki osesen-- etung'aiye nkitarruot--"
1Peter4:2 pemekure eishiuoki ninye ilng'warraitin loo ltung'anak tʼerishata nepon ebikie osesen-- kake eyeunoto Engai."
1Peter4:3 Amu ebaiki-- ajo kintobira tʼenkata empuan ang' natulusoiye-- yeunot oo loreren oolamita Engai-- kipuoiye mbaak torrok oo nkiri-- ilng'warraitin-- emerai-- enkinosishore-- eokishore-- nkisyayareitin oo nkulie ain."
1Peter4:4 Ore pemishularere ndai ninje tiatua ele rregie torrono lemeitoriori-- neaku eing'asia nesukeny ndai."
1Peter4:5 Kake epuo aaisho ealet ilo eitobirakino-- peigwenaki looishiu o lootuata."
1Peter4:6 Te ilo bae-- einosakaki si lootuata euangelion-- peigwenakini tʼosesen anaa iltung'anak-- kake neishiuoki Engai tʼolmumua."
1Peter4:7 Etinyikua enkiting'oto oo ntokitin pookin.
1Peter4:8 Akae-- enteng'enuoto-- enjololoto-- pisaishosho. Ore enaiturukie pookin-- njoo iatata enyorrata kitok tiatua ndai-- amu eopoo enyorrata enkumoi oo nkitarruot--"
1Peter4:9 Entoomonoto-- metii enking'unyung'unyata."
1Peter4:10 Esyayakinoto-- oltung'ani pookin anaa petang'amua enkishooroto-- anaa laing'orak sidan loo ng'adunot kadami Engai."
1Peter4:11 Teni eiro oltung'ani-- njeiro anaa rorei lʼEngai; teni eisyaisho oltung'ani-- njeisyaisho anaa tʼenkidimata naisho Engai ninye-- peiye eitadarari Engai tiatua ntokitin pookin te Yesus Kristos-- oata enkitook o enkitoria metabaiki nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin."
1Peter4:12 Lanyor lainei-- eminjo eitomonokino ndai enkima naleenyeki ndai-- anaa entoki omoni nataa too ndai;"
1Peter4:13 kake enting'idata-- tiaraki ning'aring'ara nkisilot e Kristos-- peiye ing'idada nigalalulu tʼenkata embolunoto enkitook enve--"
1Peter4:14 Irara teshi-- teni eitemenetari ndai tʼolbae lʼengarna e Kristos-- amu eeng'ieng'akino shumata inyi Olmumua lʼenkitook o lʼEngai; emori ninye tiatua ninje-- neitadarari tiatua ndai."
1Peter4:15 Kake njoo meisili o obo too ndai anaa olotaara metua arashu olapurroni arashu olaitobirani loo ntorrok arashu oloitijing' kion enkyas olekai.
1Peter4:16 Kake teni eisili-- tiaraki nara Olkristianos-- njoo metum enkurruna-- kake njeitaa Engai kitok te ina arna."
1Peter4:17 Amu etabaua enkata-- peiter enkigwena tʼengaji Engai. Teni eng'as too yook — kaa kiting'oto naaku too kulo lemeiruk lomon lʼeng'ida lʼEngai?"
1Peter4:18 Teni epok osupat tʼosina — ke ti aji elioi olemeure Engai o olaitarruoni?
1Peter4:19 Akae-- ore looisili tʼeyeunoto Engai-- njeitarasaki ninje iltauja lenye olaitobirani supat tiatua nkitobirat sidan."
1Peter5:1 Ore loora ilpaiyani tiatua ndai-- adiding' nanu lara si olpaiyan anaa ndai o oljakeni loo nkisilot e Kristos-- ong'ar ena kitook naapuoi aabolu:"
1Peter5:2 Errita enjoo e Kristos natii atua ndai-- ning'oraara-- neme tʼearakinoto-- kake tʼenyorrrunoto; anaa penyor Engai; niming'oruru endupoto torrono-- kake tʼenyorrata oltau--"
1Peter5:3 neme anaa laitoriak lʼolorere-- kake anaa laiturukok lʼenjoo."
1Peter5:4 Ore peibalunye ele airritani kitok-- neishori ndai enkaja enkitook nemeinaaia."
1Peter5:5 Neijia si entotiu ndai looti-- entoning' ilpaiyani. Entoning'oroto pookin tiatua ndai-- embung'akinoto pookin aten enkitadounoto; amu eibooio Engai loowuasa-- kake eisho eng'adunoto looitadou aten."
1Peter5:6 Akae-- entadou aten tiabori engaina nagol Engai-- petum ailepunye ninye ndai tʼenkata enye."
1Peter5:7 Entanang'akiti nkishilarot inyi pookin shumata enye-- amu ninye oshilaa ndai."
1Peter5:8 Enteng'enuoto-- enjololoto-- amu eman ndai olmang'atinda linyi-- satan-- anaa olng'atuny oipurrito neing'oru olonya;"
1Peter5:9 enteunore ninye tʼenkirukoto nagol-- iyololo-- aajo etabaikitia si lalashera linyi ootii olmaa nena kisilot."
1Peter5:10 Ore Engai eng'adunoto pookin naipotoko ndai-- looisili enkata kinyi-- atua enkitook enye oo nkatan pookin tiatua Kristos Yesus-- ninye olaitorioki ndai engoitoi nelairishiu nelaitagol neitasheye ndai."
1Peter5:11 Njeata ninye enkitook o enkitoria metabaiki nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin! Amen.
1Peter5:12 Tʼengaina e Silvanos-- olalashe linyi supat (enajo nanu)-- atisiraka ndai too lkuti rorei-- padiding' ndai naijakenu-- ajo ina eng'adunoto nasipa Engai; entasheiye ina."
1Peter5:13 Eiroroki ndai kulo ootegeluaki te nebo o ndai-- ootii Babilon-- o enkerai ai Markos."
1Peter5:14 Erorokinoto ndai obo olikai tʼeng'ututata enyorrata. Njebik eseriani too ndai pookin ootii atua Kristos. Amen.
2Peter1:1 Simon Petros-- osinga o olairriwani le Yesus Kristos: too lelo ooinoto ena nabo kirukoto kirotet te nebo o yook-- tiatua esupato naisho Engai ang' o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos."
2Peter1:2 Njeisho Engai ndai eng'adunoto o eseriani kitok tʼeyolounoto Engai o Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos.
2Peter1:3 Tiaraki naidipaki aaishoo yook tʼeyolounoto oloipoto yook tʼenkitook o tʼenkishaa enye engolon pookin engaishu enye naeaki yook empuan o enkuretishu Engai--"
2Peter1:4 naishorieki yook nkisiligat naaikishaan naa kituak naleng'-- peiye itumutumu aatang'ar too nona entiunoto Engai-- ikwetikwete olng'warra lʼerruoroto lotii enkop:"
2Peter1:5 onaa entonyok te ina naleng'-- pintaduaiaia tiatua enkirukoto inyi enkishaa o tiatua enkishaa eyolounoto"
2Peter1:6 o tiatua eyolounoto emitikinoto o tiatua emitikinoto olng'iria o tiatua olng'iria enkuretishu Engai
2Peter1:7 o tiatua enkuretishu Engai enyorrata oo lalashera o tiatua enyorrata oo lalashera enyorrata oo pookin.
2Peter1:8 Ore piatata nona osupatei-- meisho ninje ndai ishalulu nimiatata ilmomo tiatua eyolounoto Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos;"
2Peter1:9 kake olemeata nona-- nera modooni neirrapirrapisho nerikino enkisujata oo nkitarruot enyena e opa."
2Peter1:10 Onaa-- lalashera-- entopon aanyok-- pintagoligolo enkipototo o engelunoto inyi; amu teni intobiribiri nona-- nimipuopuo aaitoki aaikobo."
2Peter1:11 Amu nji epuoi aadup aaisho ndai enjing'ata e atua enkarsishu oo nkatan pookin Olaitoriani lang' naa Olaitopuani Yesus Kristos.
2Peter1:12 Akae-- mayeu napai-- paitadamu ndai oshi kuna baak-- ten aa iyololo neitagolieki ndai tiatua esipata natii."
2Peter1:13 Nadol ajo eitoriori-- eton atii atua ena aji-- paitadamu nainyeye ndai;"
2Peter1:14 amu ayolo-- ajo meata kata namaitau engaji ai asioki-- anaa enaaitadua Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos."
2Peter1:15 Kake ayeu nanyokita-- peiye-- teni aidipa ashomo-- itumutumu aatadamutu kuna baak."
2Peter1:16 Amu eitu kisuj yook natinin eng'eno te ina kata nikintayolo ndai engolon o elotunoto Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos-- kake kitadua too ngonyek ang' enkitook enye--"
2Peter1:17 te ina kata nainoto ninye tʼEngai Menye enganyit o enkitook tʼoltoilo oakaki ninye eing'ua enkitook kitok: Nyele Oinoti lai lanyor oshipakino oltau lai.
2Peter1:18 Kitoning'o yook ele toilo lotaa eing'ua shumata-- kiboitare ninye tʼoldoinyo sinyati."
2Peter1:19 Nikiata si ororei ogol lʼeyolounoto-- nintobiribiri sidai-- teni ing'oraara ninye anaa enkilang'et nailang'isho tiatua ewueji emiso-- metabana neiter endama neilepu olakira lʼengakenya tiatua iltauja linyi."
2Peter1:20 Meata kata niming'asing'asa aayolou ena-- aajo meaku eyolounoto o nabo esirata tʼenkitaalata enye openy;"
2Peter1:21 amu eitu eauni eyolounoto o nabo tʼeyeunoto oltung'ani-- kake eiroro iltung'anak sinyat lʼEngai-- eutakini tʼOlmumua Sinyati."
2Peter2:1 Kake etaa opa si layolounok lʼelejare tiatua olorere-- neijia anaa peaku si tiatua ndai laiteng'enak lʼelejare-- oopuo aaiteru orot enkiminata-- nemiki Olaitoriani oinyang'ua ninje-- neaki aten enkiminata asioki."
2Peter2:2 Nepuo aasuj ilkumok enkiminata enye; ore tʼolbae lenye neimakini engoitoi esipata too ntorrok.
2Peter2:3 Tʼempiani o too rorei lʼolosek epuo aaing'oru endupoto too ndai. Kake meimutie enkigwena enye e opa-- nemeirura enkiminata enye."
2Peter2:4 Amu eitu eing'urrie Engai ilmalaikan ooitarruoitie-- kake too ngameta enaimin etanang'aka ninje atua easuroto-- peitaanyitai enkigwena;"
2Peter2:5 neitu eing'urrie olmaa li opa-- kake etorripo Noa-- olainosunoni lʼesupato-- te nebo o kulekai oopishana-- peau ninye oloirrag lʼengare kitok shumata enkop-- natii kulo torrok."
2Peter2:6 Neibelekeny ngang'itie Sodom o Gomora metaa nkuruon-- neigwenaki ninje tʼenkigwena ogol-- nepikaki enkiteng'enet iltung'anak torrok oopuonu tekurum;"
2Peter2:7 neitopok Lot-- ele supat-- lora ninye eisilo kulo tung'anak torrok tʼorregie lenye lʼolduruki;"
2Peter2:8 amu tiaraki natamanya ninye ora supat-- te nebo o ninje-- nening' nedol enataasa-- neitamio ninje ngolong'i kumok Olmumua le ilo supat too nkyasin enye nemeishiaakino."
2Peter2:9 Eyolo Olaitoriani atang'adu looure ninye tiatua nkitasurot-- neitaany looas ntorrok atua engolong' enkigwena-- petum earata--"
2Peter2:10 naleng' kulo oolimana anaa peyeu nkiri tiatua olng'warra duruki-- neany nkitoriaitin-- looata olwuasa-- looata engogong'i-- lemeikirikira teni emor ninje ngoloni enkitook;"
2Peter2:11 kake too nona pookin eitu eau ilmalaikan oolusoo tʼenkidimata o tʼengolon-- emoroto torrono aaigwenaki ninje tʼengomon Olaitoriani."
2Peter2:12 Kake etiu lelo anaa ng'wesi nemeata endamunoto-- naatoinyeki neba empukunoto peibung'i neyeng'i-- naa ninje oomorisho-- nepuo aaimin tiatua orregie lenye torrono--"
2Peter2:13 netum olkwaje loo nkyasin enye torrok. Eiken aajo naa olkar-- teni esuj mbaak emerai endama-- loora ntibil o ntiot enkurruna-- neinosisho tʼenedaareki teni eng'arie ndaikin inyi--"
2Peter2:14 neata ngonyek oobore mbaak torrok oo nkiri-- lemeiboiori too ntorrok-- nelej iltauja ooshal-- neata oltau otamoo ngoitoi oo lng'warraitin-- naa nkera endiata."
2Peter2:15 Etung'aitie engoitoi naitoriori-- nemanimanaa eibung' engoitoi e Bileam-- enkerai e Beor-- otonyorra olkwaje le mesupato--"
2Peter2:16 kake einoto earata elang'ata enye-- neirorie esikiria nemeidim airoro tʼoltoilo loo ltung'anak-- neibooio emodaishu oloiboni."
2Peter2:17 Ore ninje naa iljorroi lemetii engare-- ng'atambo naareo olkutati-- neitaanyitai ninje erokan enaimin nkatan pookin."
2Peter2:18 Amu elimu ninje rorei lʼolwuasa-- neitasur too mbaak torrok oo nkiri-- peiwuwu ilng'warraitin torrok loo nkiri tiatua kulo ootang'asa aailany lelo oomanimanaa tʼelejare;"
2Peter2:19 neisiligaki ninje elakunoto-- kake era ninje oopeny singan lʼenkiminata; amu teni egiluni oltung'ani-- neaku osinga le ilo otigilua ninye."
2Peter2:20 Amu ore peidip ninje aailanya oloirerio lʼolmaa tʼeyolounoto Olaitoriani o Olaitopuani Yesus Kristos-- nerreshi negiluni kat are-- neaku too ninje mbaak enye enkiting'oto torrok nelang' nʼenkiterata."
2Peter2:21 Enaikash too ninje-- ten emut eitu eyolou engoitoi esupato-- alang' teni eyolou neitoki aalam tʼenkitanapata sinyati naishooki ninje."
2Peter2:22 Neaku too ninje asipai ena tepe: Eitoki anya oldia enaturrugumna-- neitoki aing'olare olbitir oisuja olokidong'oi."
2Peter3:1 Ena empalai e are nasiraki ndai-- lanyor lainei-- naitadamunye ndai nainyeye ndamunot inyi sidan--"
2Peter3:2 pidamumu kulo rorei ootang'asa aaliki ndai layolounok sinyat-- o enkitanapata ang'-- likira lairriwak lʼOlaitoriani o Olaitopuani."
2Peter3:3 Entayolo tʼenkata elukunya ena-- aajo epuo aapuonu too ngolong'i enkiting'oto lamorok tiatua emoroto luopuoito anaa peyeu ilng'warraitin lenye oopeny--"
2Peter3:4 nejo: „Kaji etii enkisiligata elotunoto enye? Amu neba eiruate loopapa etobiko pookin anaa tʼenkiterata enkitobirata“.
2Peter3:5 Kake eshuma too kulo loojo ena-- ajo etii shumata neba opa o enkop nataa tʼengare nepuku tʼengare tʼororei lʼEngai;"
2Peter3:6 Onaa neiminyeki enkop te ina kata tʼoloirrag lʼengare.
2Peter3:7 Neijia eitaanyitai shumata e taata o enkop tʼororei lenye-- nerripokini enkima metabaiki engolong' enkigwena o enkiminata oo ltung'anak lemeure Engai"
2Peter3:8 Njoo meshumakini ndai-- loonyorri-- ena nabo-- ajo enyanyukie engolong' nabo tʼOlaitoriani anaa laritin iip tomon-- o laritin iip tomon anaa engolong' nabo."
2Peter3:9 Moimutie Olaitoriani eitabaia enkisiligata enye-- anaa pejo looje enkimutioto-- kake eng'iri too yook nemeyeu-- peimin oltung'ani-- kake pebaiki pookin enkitaalata."
2Peter3:10 Kake elalotu engolong' Olaitoriani anaa olapurroni te kiarie-- nepuo aamuta shumat tʼoriri-- nepuo aashola ntokitin tʼeikan-- nepuo aamuta enkop o nkitobirat naatii atua--"
2Peter3:11 Ore pelolong'u kuna pookin-- kaji inkoko teni meata kata nimimbung'ubung'u orregie sinyati o orregie lʼenkuretishu Engai--"
2Peter3:12 pianyunyu nikwetikiki elotunoto engolong' Engai-- napuoi aamutie shumat tʼenkima nepuoi aasholie neikieki ntokitin!"
2Peter3:13 Kake kianyu yook shumata ng'ejuk o enkop ng'ejuk tʼenkisiligata enye namanyie esupato.
2Peter3:14 Onaa-- loonyorri-- entonyok ianyunyu kuna-- pedoli ndai tʼeseriani t'engomom enye miatata ntibil o entorroni--"
2Peter3:15 ninkenikene olng'iria lʼOlaitoriani lang' enkitopuata inyi-- anaa petisira si olalashe lang' likinyor Paulos tʼeng'eno enye naishooki ninye--"
2Peter3:16 anaa peirorie nona tiatua mpala enyena pookin; ore tiatua ninje etii kulie baak naagol nemeyolounoi-- naaitaai kulo lemeyolo nemeunokino-- neijia anaa nkulie sirat-- neaku nʼenkiminata enye."
2Peter3:17 Kake ore ndai-- loonyorri-- tiaraki niyololo nona tʼenkiterata-- entorrip aten-- pemerikori ndai tʼenkitapong'oroto oo ltung'anak torrok te nebo o ninje-- mbatatata aaing'ua ewueji inyi neikarraro."
2Peter3:18 Kake entubul tiatua eng'adunoto o eyolounoto Olaitoriani lang o Olaitopuani Yesus Kristos. Njeata ninye enkitook taata o metabaiki ngolong'i oo nkatan pookin. Amen.
1John1:1 Enataa neba tʼenkiterata-- enikitoning'o-- enikitadua too ngonyek ang'-- eniking'oraitie neirrapirrap ngaik ang'-- mbaak ororei lʼempuan-- —"
1John1:2 etalie empuan nikitadua nikinjakenu nikinosaki ndai ena puan nemeiting'-- enataboitare Menye nelioi too yook —:"
1John1:3 kinosaki ndai enikitadua-- enikitoning'o-- peiye ing'aring'ara si ndai o yook; nera eng'arata ang' nabo o Papa o Oinoti lenye Yesus Kristos."
1John1:4 Nikisir yook nona-- peiganyi eng'ida ang'."
1John1:5 Nyena enkinosunoto nikitoning'o yook naing'ua ninye-- nikinosaki ndai-- aajo era Engai eong'an-- nemetii enaimin atua ninye katukul."
1John1:6 Teni kijo yook-- aajo kiata eng'arata te nebo o ninye nikipuo tiatua enaimin-- nikilejisho nimikintobir esipata."
1John1:7 Kake teni kipuo tiatua eong'an anaa petii ninye atua eong'an-- nikiata yook eng'arata tiatua aten-- neisuj osarge le Yesus Kristos-- Oinoti lʼEngai-- yook too nkitarruot pookin."
1John1:8 Teni kijo-- mikiata enkitarruoto-- nikilej aten-- nemetii esipata atua yook."
1John1:9 Teni kimbalu nkitarruot ang'-- nera ninye airukoni naa supat-- peiye eitaiki yook nkitarruot neikishaanye yook tʼentorroni pookin."
1John1:10 Teni kijo-- eitu kintarruo-- nikintaa ninye olalejani-- nemetii ororei lenye atua yook."
1John2:1 Nakera ainei-- asiraki ndai kuna-- peiye mintarruorruo; naa teni eitarruo obo-- kiata olomitu yook te Papa-- Yesus Kristos-- ora supat."
1John2:2 Nera ninye enkitobirakinoto too nkitarruot ang'-- neme too nkitarruot ang' ake-- kake too nʼolmaa pookin."
1John2:3 Ena nikiyolounye-- aajo kiyolou ninye-- teni kimbung' nkitanapat enyena."
1John2:4 Ore olojo: Ayolo ninye-- nemeibung' nkitanapat enyena-- naa olalejani-- nemetii esipata atua ninye."
1John2:5 Kake ore oloibung' ororei lenye-- neitabaiyoki enyorrata Engai tiatua ninye-- esipa. Ina kiyolounye-- aajo kitii atua ninye."
1John2:6 Ore olojo-- ebik tiatua ninye-- meata kata nemelimana neijia anaa petilimane ninye."
1John2:7 Lanyor lainei-- eitu asiraki ndai enkitanapata ng'ejuk-- kake enkitanapata musana-- niatata neba tʼenkiterata. Ore enkitanapata musana-- naa ilo rorei Etoning'o tʼenkiterata."
1John2:8 Naitoki asiraki ndai enkitanapata ng'ejuk-- nasipa tiatua ninye o tiatua ndai; amu etinyikaiye enaimin-- neilang'isho eong'an nasipa."
1John2:9 Ore olojo-- etii atua eong'an neiba olalashe lenye-- neton etii ninye atua enaimin."
1John2:10 Ore olonyor olalashe lenye-- nebik tiatua eong'an nemetii enkitapong'oroto atua ninye."
1John2:11 Ore oloiba olalashe lenye-- netii ninye atua enaimin nelimana tiatua enaimin nemeyolo-- enelo; amu eitamodono enaimin ngonyek enyena."
1John2:12 Asiraki ndai-- nakera kutiti-- ajo eitaikiaki ndai nkitarruot tʼolbae lʼengarna enye."
1John2:13 Asiraki ndai-- loopapa-- ajo Itayoloutuo ele lora neba tʼenkiterata. Asiraki ndai-- le murran-- ajo itigilutua oltorrono."
1John2:14 Atisiraka ndai-- nakera-- ajo itayoloutuo Minyi. Atisiraka ndai-- loopapa-- ajo itayoloutuo ele lora neba tʼenkiterata. Atisiraka ndai-- le murran ajo irara ndai oogol nebik lomon lʼEngai tiatua ndai nitigilutua oltorrono."
1John2:15 Eminyor olmaa-- baiki naatii atua olmaa. Teni enyor oltung'ani olmaa-- metii enyorrata e Menye atua ninye."
1John2:16 Amu ntokitin pookin naatii atua olmaa: olng'warra lʼenkiring'o o olng'warra loo ngonyek o olwuasa lʼempuan-- mera naaing'ua Menye-- kake era naaing'ua olmaa."
1John2:17 Nelamuta olmaa o olng'warra lenye; kake oloitobir eyeunoto Engai-- ninye lobik nkatan pookin."
1John2:18 Nakera kutiti-- esaa enkiting'oto ena; anaa enitoning'o ndai-- aajo elotu olmang'atinda le Kristos-- neijia eetuo ilmang'ati le Kristos kumok. Te ina kiyolou-- aajo etaa esaa enkiting'oto."
1John2:19 Eshomo ninje aaing'ua atua yook-- kake me ilkulalang' ninje. Amu ten emut aa ninje ilkulalang'-- anaata etobiko te nebo o yook. Kake meata kata nemeibalunye-- ajo me ilkulalang' pookin."
1John2:20 Eelieki ndai eilata te ilo ora Sinyati niyololo ndai mbaak pookin.
1John2:21 Eitu asiraki ndai anaa lemeyolo esipata-- kake iyololo ninye-- nintokiki aayolo-- aajo meing'ua elejare esipata."
1John2:22 Kang'ai olalejani-- leme elde omiki-- ajo era Yesus ele Kristos? Naa ilo olmang'atinda le Kristos omiki Menye o Oinoti."
1John2:23 Ore olomiki Oinoti-- netomikio si Menye; ore oloibalu Oinoti-- neata si Menye."
1John2:24 Ore nena nitoning'o tʼenkiterata-- njebik tiatua ndai. Teni ebik tiatua ndai-- enitoning'o tʼenkiterata-- nipuopuo aabik si ndai te nebo o Oinoti o Menye."
1John2:25 Naa ena enkisiligata naishoo ninye yook: empuan nemeiting'.
1John2:26 Kuna baak atisiraka ndai tʼolbae loo lelo oorik ndai aaitapong'oo.
1John2:27 Ore eelare nitang'amutua ndai te ninye-- nebik tiatua ndai-- nimiyeuu olekai tung'ani-- peiteng'en ndai; kake enaiteng'ena ndai eelare pookin-- nesipai nemetii elejare; ore anaa peiteng'ena ndai-- entobik tiatua ninye."
1John2:28 Ore taata-- nakera ainei kutiti-- entobik tiatua ninye-- pekiata enkiteunoto-- teni eboluni ninye-- nimikikurru tʼelotunoto enye."
1John2:29 Teni iyololo-- aajo ninye supat-- nintokiki aayolou-- aajo ore oloitobir esupato-- naa ilo etoiwuo ninye."
1John3:1 Eng'orai eneba enyorrata naishoo yook Papa-- peipoti yook nkera Engai-- nikira. Onaa meyolo yook olmaa-- amu meyolo ninye."
1John3:2 Akae-- lanyor-- kira yook nkera Engai-- neton eitu elioi enikipuo aaku. Kake kiyolo-- aajo teni elalioi-- nikipuo aaku anaa ninye-- amu kipuo aadol ninye anaa petiu."
1John3:3 Ore pookin loataiye ninye ena anyunoto-- neisuj kion anaa pera ilo loisuja."
1John3:4 Ore oltung'ani pookin loitobir nkitarruot-- nepaashare nkitanapat-- naa nkitarruot empaashata oo nkitanapat."
1John3:5 Niyololo-- aajo etalie ninye-- peitai nkitarruot ang'-- nemetii enkitarruoto atua ninye."
1John3:6 Ore oltung'ani pookin lobik tiatua ninye-- nemeitarruo; ore pookin oitarruo-- eitu edol neitu eyolou ninye."
1John3:7 Nakera kutiti-- eminjo oltung'ani metoriko ndai aitapong'oo. Ore oloitobir esupato-- naa supat ilo-- anaa pera ninye supat."
1John3:8 Ore oloas enkitarruoto-- naa satan eing'ua. Amu eitarruo satan neba tʼenkiterata. Te ina etalie Oinoti lʼEngai-- peiminye nkitobirat e satan."
1John3:9 Ore pookin otoiwuoki tʼEngai-- nemeitarruo-- amu ebik eishoi enye te nebo o ninye; meidim ninye aitarruoi-- amu etoiwuoki tʼEngai."
1John3:10 Too kuna baak eibalunye nkera Engai o nkera e satan: ore pookin lemeitobir esupato-- nemeing'ua Engai-- o ele lemenyor olalashe lenye."
1John3:11 Amu nyena enkinosunoto litoning'o tʼenkiterata-- ajo pekinyorra aten."
1John3:12 Me anaa Kain-- otupukuo tʼentorroni-- near olalashe lenye metua. Ainyo petaara ninye metua? Tiaraki nara nkitobirat enyena torrok-- kake supati nʼolalashe lenye."
1John3:13 Emimputukuny-- lalashera lainei-- teni eibai ndai olmaa."
1John3:14 Kiyolo yook-- aajo kiima atua enkea nikijing' atua empuan-- amu kinyor yook lalashera; olemenyor olalashe lenye-- nebik tiatua enkea."
1John3:15 Ore oltung'ani pookin loibai olalashe lenye-- nera olaarani oar oltung'ani metua-- niyololo ndai-- aajo meata olarani lʼoltung'ani empuan nemeiting' tiatua ninye nabik."
1John3:16 Kitayoloutuo te ina enyorrata-- tiaraki naishooiye ilo oltau lenye tʼolbae lang'; meata kata nimikinjooio si yook iltauja lang' tʼolbae loo lalashera."
1John3:17 Ore Oloata masaa ele maa-- nedol olalashe lenye loata elaunoto-- neitagoloki ninye engoshoke enye nanana — kaji eiko teni ebik enyorrata Engai tiatua ninye!"
1John3:18 Nakera kutiti-- eminyor tʼororei arashu tʼolng'ejep-- kake tʼenkyas o tʼesipata."
1John3:19 Te ina kiyolou-- aajo kira lʼesipata nikindim aaitigira oltau lang' tʼengomom enye--"
1John3:20 ore teni eigwenaki yook oltau lang'-- nera Engai kitok nelang' oltau lang' neyolou ntokitin pookin."
1John3:21 Lanyor lainei-- teni meigwenaki yook oltau lang'-- nikiata enkiteunoto nikintoriokinore Engai--"
1John3:22 ore enikiomonu-- nikipuo aang'amu te ninye; amu kimbung' nkitanapat enyena-- nikintobir-- enaitiship ninye."
1John3:23 Naa ena enkitanapata enye-- peiye kiruk engarna Oinoti lenye-- Yesus Kristos-- nikinyorra tʼempolos ang'-- anaa peishoo ninye yook enkitanapata."
1John3:24 Ore oloibung' nkitanapat enyena-- nebik tiatua ninye o elde tiatua ninye. Te ina kiyolou yook-- aajo ebik tiatua yook-- tʼOlmumua oishoo ninye yook."
1John4:1 Lanyor lainei-- emiruk ilmumuan pookin-- kake entaleen ilmumuan-- ten ake Engai eing'ua-- amu etijing'a laiteng'enak kumok lʼelejare atua olmaa."
1John4:2 Meata kata nimiyolouu ndai Olmumua lʼEngai tʼena: Ore Olmumua pookin oibalu-- ajo eewuo Yesus Kristos tʼosesen-- naa ninye Engai eing'ua;"
1John4:3 ore Olmumua pookin lemeibalu-- ajo eewuo Yesus Kristos tʼosesen-- nemeing'ua ninye Engai. Naa ele Olmumua lʼolmang'atinda le Kristos litoning'o ninye-- ajo elotu-- neidipa taata aeu atua olmaa."
1John4:4 Irara ndai l'Engai-- nakera kutiti-- nitigilutua lelo; amu ore oloti! atua ndai-- nera kitok nelang' ele otii atua olmaa."
1John4:5 Naa lʼolmaa ninje-- onaa elimu nʼolmaa-- nening' olmaa ninje."
1John4:6 Kira yook lʼEngai-- ore oloyolou Engai-- nening' yook; ore olemeing'ua Engai-- nemening' yook. Te ina kiyolou Olmumua lʼesipata o Olmumua lʼenkitapong'oroto."
1John4:7 Lanyor lainei-- matonyorrata tiatua aten; amu ore enyorrata-- Engai eing'ua-- o olonyor-- netoiwuoki tʼEngai neyolo Engai."
1John4:8 Olemenyor-- nemeyolo Engai-- amu era Engai enyorrata."
1John4:9 Etalie enyorrata Engai tiatua ena too yook-- ajo eirriwaka Engai Oinoti lenye obo atua olmaa-- pekipuo aaishiutu yook te ninye."
1John4:10 Etii enyorrata atua ena: me tiaraki nikitonyorra yook Engai-- kake tiaraki natonyorra ninye yook neirriu Oinoti lenye-- peaku enkitobirakinoto too nkitarruot ang'."
1John4:11 Lanyor-- teni etonyorra yook Engai neijia-- meata kata nimikinyorra si yook."
1John4:12 Eitu edol aikata oltung'ani o obo Engai. Teni kinyorra yook-- nebik Engai tiatua yook-- neitabaiyoki enyorrata enye tiatua yook."
1John4:13 Kiyolou tʼena-- ajo kibik tiatua ninye nebik ninye tiatua yook-- tiaraki naishoo ninye yook nʼOimumua lenye."
1John4:14 Nikitadua yook nikinjakenu-- ajo eirriua Menye Oinoti lenye-- peaku Olaitopuani lʼolmaa."
1John4:15 Ore oloibalu-- ajo Oinoti lʼEngai Yesus-- nebik Engai tiatua ninye-- o si ninye tiatua Engai."
1John4:16 Nikindipa aatayolou nikiruk enyorrata naata Engai too yook. Era Engai enyorrata; ore olobik tiatua enyorrata-- nebik tiatua Engai o Engai tiatua ninye."
1John4:17 Te ina eitabaiari enyorrata too yook-- pekiata eng'idaroto tʼengolong' enkigwena; amu neijia anaa petii ninye-- nikitii si yook atua ele maa."
1John4:18 Metii enkuretishu atua enyorrata-- kake eiturraki enyorrata natabaiye enkuretishu boo-- amu eata enkuretishu emion. Oloureisho-- neitu ebaia tiatua enyorrata."
1John4:19 Matonyor yook ninye-- amu ninye loitera anyor yook."
1John4:20 Teni ejo oltung'ani; „Anyor Engai“-- neiba olalashe lenye-- nera olalejani. Amu olemenyor olalashe lenye lodol — kaji eiko ten eidim ninye atonyorra Engai nemedol?"
1John4:21 Ore ena kitanapata kiata te ninye peiye olonyor Engai-- nenyorru si olalashe lenye."
1John5:1 Ore oltung'ani pookin loiruk Yesus-- ajo ninye Kristos-- etoiwuoki ninye tʼEngai. Ore oltung'ani pookin lonyor olotoiwuo ninye-- nenyor baiki olotoiwuoki te ninye."
1John5:2 Kiyolo te ina-- ajo kinyor nkera Engai-- teni kinyor Engai nikintobir nkitanapat enyena."
1John5:3 Amu nyena enyorrata Engai-- pikimbung' nkitanapat enyena-- nemegol nkitanapat enyena."
1John5:4 Ore pookin natoiwuoki tʼEngai-- negilu olmaa; nera enkirukoto ang' engilunoto natigilua olmaa."
1John5:5 Ang'ai lora Ologilu olmaa neme oloiruk-- ajo era Yesus Oinoti lʼEngai?"
1John5:6 Ele ninye olotu tʼengare o tʼosarge-- Yesus Kristos; me tʼengare ake-- kake tʼengare o tʼosarge. Naa Olmumua-- oijakenu; amu era Olmumua esipata."
1John5:7 Amu etii okuni ooijakenu: Olmumua o engare o osarge;
1John5:8 netii pokira okuni atua obo.
1John5:9 Teni king'amu enjakenishu oo ltung'anak-- nera enjakenishu Engai kitok nalang'; amu enjakenishu Engai ena naijakenuo tʼOinoti lenye."
1John5:10 Ore oloiruk Oinoti lʼEngai-- neata ina jakenishu tiatua ninye. Ore olemeiruk Engai-- neitaa ninye olalejani-- amu meiruk ninye enjakenishu naijakenu Engai tʼOinoti lenye."
1John5:11 Naa ena enjakenishu-- ajo eishoo yook Engai empuan nemeiting'-- netii ena puan atua Oinoti lenye."
1John5:12 Ore Oloata Oinoti lʼEngai-- neata empuan; ore olemeata Oinoti lʼEngai-- nemeata ninye empuan."
1John5:13 Atisiraka ndai kuna baak-- piyololo-- aajo iatata empuan nemeiting' nirukuruku engarna Oinoti lʼEngai."
1John5:14 Naa ena eng'idaroto nikiataiye ninye-- teni kiomonu toki tʼeyeunoto enye-- nening' ninye yook."
1John5:15 Teni kiyolo yook-- aajo ening' yook enikiomonu-- nikiyolo-- aajo kiata omonot nikitoomonutuo ninye."
1John5:16 Teni edol oltung'ani olalashe lenye eitarruo enkitarruoto neme en enkea-- njeomonoki; neaku eisho Engai empuan kulo lemeitarruo nʼenkea. Etii enkitarruoto narik enkea; eitu aliki-- peomonoki oltung'ani ena."
1John5:17 Era mesupato pookin enkitarruoto-- nemera kulie kitarruot nʼenkea."
1John5:18 Kiyolo yook-- aajo ore olotoiwuoki tʼEngai-- nemeitarruo; kake olotoiwuoki tʼEngai-- nerrip kion nemeporroo ninye ele torrono."
1John5:19 Kiyolo yook-- aajo kira lʼEngai-- neton olmaa pookin tiatua entorroni."
1John5:20 Kake kiyolo-- aajo eewuo Oinoti lʼEngai neisho yook eng'eno-- pekiyolou olosipa-- nikitii yook atua olosipa-- atua Oinoti lenye Yesus Kristos. Ninye Engai nasipa o empuan nemeiting'."
1John5:21 Nakera kutiti-- entorrip aten too nkulie ain. Amen."
2John1:1 Olpaiyan osiraki eng'oroyoni nategeluaki o nkera enyena-- nanyor tiatua esipata-- neme nanu ake-- kake enyor si kulo pookin ootayoloutuo esipata--"
2John1:2 tʼolbae lʼesipata nabik tiatua yook nelabik te nebo o yook nkatan pookin:
2John1:3 Njeboitare ndai eng'adunoto o enkordunoto o eseriani naing'ua Engai Papa o Olaitoriani Yesus Kristos-- Oinoti le Papa-- tiatua esipata o enyorrata."
2John1:4 Ating'ide naleng'-- tiaraki nainoto too nkera inono kulie-- naalimana tiatua esipata-- anaa kitang'amutua enkitanapata e Papa."
2John1:5 Onaa-- aasai iye taata-- nakitok-- me anaa aasiraki iye enkitanapata ng'ejuk-- kake ina nikiata tʼenkiterata-- pekinyorra."
2John1:6 Naa ena enyorrata-- pekilimana anaa peyeu enkitanapata enye; nyena enkitanapata-- anaa pitoning'o tʼenkiterata-- peiye ilimanarere ina."
2John1:7 Amu kumok lalejak ooetuo atua olmaa-- lemeibalu Yesus Kristos-- aajo eewuo tʼenkiringʼo. Ninye olalejani-- naa olmang'atinda le Kristos."
2John1:8 Entaduai ndai aten-- pemiiminyenye kunda nikintobira-- kake pikitum olkwaje olulung'a."
2John1:9 Ore pookin opaash nemebik tiatua enkiteng'enare e Kristos-- nemeata ninye Engai. Ore olobik tiatua enkiteng'enare e Kristos-- neata pokira are-- Papa o Oinoti."
2John1:10 Teni elotu oltung'ani atua ndai nemeau ena kiteng'enare-- eminjo ejing' engaji inyi ana irorokiki."
2John1:11 Amu ore oloiroroki ninye-- neng'arie nkitobirat enyena torrok."
2John1:12 Aata ntokitin kumok nayeu nasiraki ndai-- nemayeu nasiraki tʼenkaratasi arashu tʼerokan-- kake aanyu metabana nalotu enitiiti ndai-- airorie tʼenkutuk-- peborei eng'ida inyi."
2John1:13 Kiroroki iye nkera enganashe ino nategeluaki. Amen.
3John1:1 Olpaiyan osiraki Gayos-- oljore lai-- lanyor tiatua esipata."
3John1:2 Olanyor lai-- aayeuoki iye piserian tiatua mbaak pookin niata embiotishu-- neijia anaa peserian Olmumua lino."
3John1:3 Atishipe naleng'-- pepuonu lalashera aaijakenu esipata ino-- anaa pilimana tiatua esipata."
3John1:4 Maata ai ng'ida kitok nalang' ena-- teni atoning'o mbaak oo nkera ainei naapuoiye esipata."
3John1:5 Olanyor lai-- iasita tʼesupato tʼentoki pookin nintobiraki lalashera o lelo oora lomon--"
3John1:6 ooijakenutuo enyorrata ino tʼengomom esirit; nintoki aas sidan-- teni irriwaa ninje eitobirakinote osupatei tʼengomom Engai."
3John1:7 Amu etupukutuo ninje tʼolbae lʼengarna enye nemeng'amu toki too lemeata Engai.
3John1:8 Onaa-- meata kata nemeking'amu lootiu anaa lelo-- pekiaku te nebo o ninje laitobirak lʼena sipata."
3John1:9 Atisiraka esirit; kake ore Diotrefe-- oyeu neaku olkitok too ninje-- eitu eng'amu yook."
3John1:10 Onaa-- teni alotu-- ayeu naitadamu ninye nkitobirat naaitobir-- amu eimaki yook too rorei torrok. Nemebaiki ina ake-- kake meng'amu ninye lalashera-- nemitiki lelo ooyeu neng'amu ninje-- neitoki aitai tʼesirit."
3John1:11 Olanyor lai-- misuj entorroni-- kake esupato. Oloitobir esupato-- neing'ua Engai."
3John1:12 Eata Demetrios enjakenishu oltung'ani pookin o en esipata-- nikinjakenu si yook; niyolo iye enjakenishu ang' ajo esipa."
3John1:13 Aata mbaak kumok nayeu naasiraki-- kake mayeu naasiraki iye tʼerokan o tʼenjata nasirishoreki."
3John1:14 Kake aanyu-- ajo aadol iye asioki-- nikiro yook too nkutukie."
3John1:15 Njoo kibikie eseriani. Kiroroki iye iljorueta. Roroki iljorueta too ngam enye.
Jude1:1 Yudas-- osinga le Yesus Kristos-- olalashe le Yakobos: too lelo ooipotoki-- loonyorri tiatua Engai Papa lang'-- nerripi tiatua Yesus Kristos."
Jude1:2 Njeponari enkordunoto o eseriani o enyorrata too ndai.
Jude1:3 Lanyor lainei-- ore pashilaa naleng' asiraki ndai tʼolbae lʼenkitopuata ang' niking'ar-- nemeata kata namadiding' ndai-- peiye iaparere aamitu enkirukoto-- naishooki nabo kata sinyat."
Jude1:4 Amu etii kulekai tung'anak ooetuo aaisudunye-- naa ninje ootisirieki neba opa ena kigwena-- ajo era ninje lemeure Engai-- neibelekeny eng'adunoto Engai eas entorroni-- nemiki Engai-- Olkitok obo-- o Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos."
Jude1:5 Kake ayeu naitadamu ndai-- oo ten aa iyololo mbaak pookin-- ajo ore ena kata nabo eitopua Olaitoriani olorere aitungʼua olosho le Misri-- near enkata e are kulo leitu eiruk."
Jude1:6 Eibooko ninye baiki ilmalaikan leitu ebik tiatua enkitoria enye openy-- kake lootung'aitie entonata enye-- enkigwena engolong' kitok-- peen ninje too ienat oo nkatan pookin tiabori enaimin."
Jude1:7 Neijia si Sodom o Gomora o ngang'itie naataanikino-- naataasa mbaak torrok oo nkiri nesuj engai kiring'o-- eitaaki ninje enkiteng'enet-- petum enkisiloto enkima oo nkatan pookin."
Jude1:8 Neijia etiu si kulo aidetidetak oopik eng'iring'o ntibil-- neany enkitoria-- nemor looata enkitook."
Jude1:9 Kake ore Mikael-- ele malaika kitok-- peishangarra o satan neirorie tʼolbae lʼosesen le Mose-- nemeiteu atudung'o enkigwena emoroto shumata enye-- kake etejo: Njoo kilaaki Olaitoriani!"
Jude1:10 Kake ore lelo oomor pookin nemeyolo; ore enayolou ninje tʼempukunoto enye anaa ng'wesi nemeata eng'eno-- te ina erruoio."
Jude1:11 Kake aiya ninje-- amu esujita ninje engoitoi e Kain-- nebatatakino enkitapong'oroto e Bileam tʼolbae lʼendupoto-- neimin tʼenkiposhiposharoto e Kora."
Jude1:12 Naa ninje ooata empiani too ndaikin enyorrata inyi-- neinosisho meureisho-- neitoti aten-- netiu ninje anaa ng'atambo nemeata engare naanap ilkutat-- nera iljanito oorony lukuny lemeata ilmomo-- ootuata kat are-- nedotuni too ntonat--"
Jude1:13 naa ninje anaa lopir pushunot lʼenaiposha ooiponyu enkurruna enye oopeny-- lakir oopuaiya-- ooitaanyaki erokan enaimin oo nkatan pookin."
Jude1:14 Kake eibonishe si too lootiu nji Henok-- ole opishana neba Adam-- nejo: Ng'orai-- elotu Olaitoriani te nebo o iip tomon kumok oo sinyat lenyena--"
Jude1:15 peigwenaki pookin neitalak lemeure Engai pookin tʼolbae loo nkitobirat pookin orregie lenye torrono naaitarruoitie o tʼolbae loo mbaak naagol pookin naaimakitia laitarruok torrok ninye.
Jude1:16 Naa kulo ninje ooing'unyung'uny neishir oshi ake-- nelimana too lng'warraitin lenye-- neiro nkutukie enye mbaak sapuki olwuasa-- nenyorraki aten too ltung'anak tʼolbae lʼendupoto ele maa."
Jude1:17 Kake ore ndai-- lanyor lainei-- entadamutu kulo rorei ootang'asa aalimu lairriwak lʼOlaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos--"
Jude1:18 enetiakitia ndai-- aajo tʼenkata enkiting'oto epuo aatii lamorok oolimana too lng'warraitin lʼorregie lenye torrono."
Jude1:19 Naa kulo ooau rishat nesuj mbaak osesen-- nemeata nʼolmumua."
Jude1:20 Kake ore ndai-- lanyor lainei-- enteshetakinoto enkirukoto inyi sinyati naleng' tiatua Olmumua Sinyati-- nisaishosho--"
Jude1:21 nirripirripi aten tiatua enyorrata Engai-- nianyunyu enkordunoto Olaitoriani lang' Yesus Kristos narik atua empuan nemeiting'."
Jude1:22 O kulekai looing'arrirro-- eng'urrie-- o kulekai-- entopua iwuapupu ninje tiatua enkima-- ning'urrierrie kulekai tʼeuriata; nimbaii si olkila otipikaki oloirerio lʼenkiringʼo."
Jude1:23 
Jude1:24 Ore ninye naidim atorripo ndai-- miatata entibili-- neitasheye ndai tʼengomom enkitook enye-- miatata eleyata-- tʼeng'ida kitok--"
Jude1:25 naa ninye Engai nabo-- Olaitopuani lang' te Yesus Kristos-- Olaitoriani lang': njeishori ninye enkitook o emagilanishu o engolon o enkidimata taata oo metabaiki nkatan pookin. Amen."
Revelation1:1 Embolunoto e Yesus Kristos naishoo Engai ninye meitadua singan lenyena mbaak nemeata kata nemeaku aasioki-- neutaki neirriwaki tʼolmalaika lenye osinga lenye Yohanes--"
Revelation1:2 oijakenuo ororei lʼEngai o enjakenishu e Yesus Kristos natadua.
Revelation1:3 Teshi oloisoma o looning' ororei lʼenkitayolounoto nerrip enatisira tiatua; amu etinyikua enkata.
Revelation1:4 Yohanes: too kuna sirito naapishana naatii Asia. Njebik eng'adunoto te nebo o ndai o eseriani naing'ua ilo otii taata-- naa ninye opa otii-- naa ninye olotu-- neing'ua kulo mumuan oopishana ootii tʼengomom olorika lenye--"
Revelation1:5 neing'ua Yesus Kristos lora oljakeni supat o olkikau loo lootuata o olkitok loo lkarsisi tʼenkop. Ninye otonyorra yook neisuj yook too nkitarruot tʼosarge lenye--"
Revelation1:6 neitaa yook ilkarsisi o laidasak tʼengomom Engai o Menye lenye-- oishori enkitook o engolon nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin. Amen."
Revelation1:7 Ng'orai-- elotu too ng'atambo e shumata-- nepuo aadol ninye ngonyek pookin o lootaremo ninye; nepuo aaishir tʼolbae lenye njomito pookin enkop. Ee-- esai!"
Revelation1:8 Ara nanu A o O-- ejo Olaitoriani Engai otii taata-- naa ninye opa otii-- naa ninye olotu-- tʼengolon pookin."
Revelation1:9 Nanu Yohanes-- lora si olalashe linyi ong'arie ndai osina o enkarsishu o olng'iria le Yesus Kristos-- atii napari oloigeruno lʼenaiposha oji Patmos-- tʼolbae lʼororei lʼEngai o lʼenjakenishu e Yesus Kristos."
Revelation1:10 Natii atua Olmumua tʼengolong' Olaitoriani naning' tekurum ai oltoilo sapuk laijo ol emowuo--"
Revelation1:11 ojo: Ara nanu A o O-- ol enkiterata o ol enkiting'oto: Tisira nena nidolita tiatua enkitabu nirriwaki nekua sirito naapishana naatii Asia-- atua Efesos o Smirna o Pergamos o Tiatira o Sardes o Filadelfia o Laodikea."
Revelation1:12 Nashuko nanu-- ajo paing'oraa ilo toilo laairorie. Ore paidip atushukoi-- nadol nkilang'eta naapishana e sahabu--"
Revelation1:13 o tʼempolos oo nekua kilang'eta naapishana obo-- onyanyukie Oinoti lʼoltung'ani-- oishopo olkila oado-- nerretena enkimeita e sahabu olgoo lenye."
Revelation1:14 Ore elukunya o ilpapit lenyena neibor anaa enaileri naibor-- anaa esiret-- netiu ngonyek anaa ilng'ejepa lʼenkima."
Revelation1:15 Netiu nkejek enyena anaa suia ooika tʼenkima-- naijo oltoilo lenye oloo ngariak kituak;"
Revelation1:16 neata lakir oopishana tʼengaina enye e tatene-- nepuku tʼenkutuk enye olalem opi ngaloli pokira are-- neilang'isho engomom enye anaa engolong' nailiil."
Revelation1:17 Ore padol ninye-- nabatata too nkejek enyena anaa olotua; naaiteleiki ninye engaina enye e tatene-- naajoki: Miureisho-- ara nanu ol enkiterata o ol enkiting'oto"
Revelation1:18 o oloishiu. Ataa olotua-- o ng'orai-- aishiu nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin naata ieneta enkea o ine wueji enkima."
Revelation1:19 Tisira naa kuna baak nitadua-- o naatii o naapuo aaku akenya."
Revelation1:20 Ore emikio oo lelo akir oopishana litadua t'engaina ai e tatene o nena kilang'eta naapishana e sahabu: Ore lakir oopishana-- naa ilmalaikan loo sirito naapishana; ore nkilang'eta naapishana nitadua-- naa sirito naapishana."
Revelation2:1 Tisiraki olmalaika lʼesirit natii atua Efesos: Kuna ejo oloibung'ita kulo akir oopishana te tatene enye-- olimana tʼempolos oo kuna kilang'eta e sahabu naapishana:"
Revelation2:2 Ayolo nkitobirat inono o enkyas ino o olng'iria lino-- nimindim atanapa iltung'anak torrok-- nitetema kulo ooipot aten lairriwak-- nemera ninje-- nitadua si ajo lalejak;"
Revelation2:3 niata olng'iria ninyok tʼolbae lʼengarna ai-- neitu inauru."
Revelation2:4 Kake aataiye embae nabo-- ajo itung'aiye enyorrata elukunya."
Revelation2:5 Tadamu-- kaji itusulari-- taalai nintobir nkitobirat enkiterata! Teni me-- nalotu asioki enitii naoshoo enkilang'et ino tʼewueji enye-- teni miala."
Revelation2:6 Kake iata ele rorei-- ajo imbai nkitobirat oo Lnikolaitin-- naibai si nanu."
Revelation2:7 Oloata enkiyok-- njening enajoki Olmumua sirito. Ologilu-- naisho ninye meinosa tʼoljani lʼempuan otii atua emparadis Engai."
Revelation2:8 Tisiraki olmalaika lʼesirit natii atua Smirna: Kuna ejo ol enkiterata o ol enkiting'oto-- otaa olotua neitoki apiu:"
Revelation2:9 Ayolo nkitobirat inono o osina lino o esinaishu ino — kake ira iye oladupani — o emoroto oo looipot aten Yudayoi-- nemera-- kake era lʼesirit e satan."
Revelation2:10 Miurei nikipuoi aaisilie! Ng'orai-- elanang'aki satan kulekai linyi engaji eenata-- peleeni ndai-- nipuopuo aata enkisiloto ngolong'i tomon. Taa airukoni metabaiki enkea-- naalaisho iye enkaja enkitook empuan."
Revelation2:11 Oloata enkiyok-- njening' enajoki Olmumua sirito. Ologilu-- nemeinosie enkea e are ninye osina."
Revelation2:12 Tisiraki olmalaika lʼesirit natii atua Pergamos: Kuna ejo Oloata olalem opi ngaloli pokira are:
Revelation2:13 Ayolo enintobir o ewueji enimanya-- enetii olorika le satan. Nimbung' engarna ai neitu imiki enkirukoto ai baiki too nena olong'i naataarieki metua Antipas-- oljakeni lai supat-- too ndai-- enetii satan."
Revelation2:14 Kake aataiye nkuti baak-- amu iata iltung'anak ooibung'a enkiteng'enare e Bileam oigwena Balak-- peuni enkitadiata tʼengomom oo nkera Israel-- ajo meinosa nkiri oo nkidasareitin naateyeng'akaki nkulie ain neas mbaak torrok oo nkiri."
Revelation2:15 Niata si iye kulekai ooibung'a enkiteng'enare oo Lnikolaitin; aiba ina.
Revelation2:16 Taalai! Teni me-- nalotu asioki enitii-- naarare ninje tʼolalem lʼenkutuk ai."
Revelation2:17 Oloata enkiyok-- njening' enajoki Olmumua sirito. Ologilu-- naisho ninye meinosa mana naisudori-- naisho ninye osoit oibor netisiraki shumata ele soit engarna ng'ejuk nemeyolo oltung'ani neme ilo ong'amu ninye."
Revelation2:18 Tisiraki olmalaika lʼesirit natii atua Tiatira: Kuna ejo Oinoti lʼEngai oata ngonyek anaa ilng'ejepa lʼenkima netiu nkejek enyena anaa suia:
Revelation2:19 Ayolo nkitobirat inono o enyorrata ino o enkirukoto ino o enkisyayare ino o olng'iria lino-- nayolo-- ajo etalang'a nkitobirat inono enkiting'oto nena enkiterata."
Revelation2:20 Kake aataiye embae nabo-- tiaraki ninjo ena ng'oroyoni Isebel naipot kion engayolounoni-- eiteng'en neitapong'oo singan lainei-- peitobir mbaak entalare nenya nkiri oo nkidasareitin naateyeng'akaki nkulie ain."
Revelation2:21 Naishoo ninye enkata naalare tʼolbae lʼentalare enye; nemeala.
Revelation2:22 Ng'orai-- anang'aki ninye atua erruat-- o kulo ootaara te nebo o ninye enkidikidikoto enkiama-- atua osina kitok-- teni meala tʼolbae loo nkitobirat enye--"
Revelation2:23 naar nkera enyena metuata-- peyolou sirito pookin-- aajo nanu oleen lairakuji o iltauja; naisho oltung'ani pookin too ndai tʼerisioroto oo nkitobirat inyi."
Revelation2:24 Naliki ndai ilkulekai ootii Tiatira lemeata enkiteng'enare naijo ena-- neitu eyolou ngasurin e satan (anaa pejo): Manang'aki shumata inyi olekai rridati."
Revelation2:25 Kake eniatata-- embung'a-- metabana nalotu."
Revelation2:26 Ologilu nerrip nkitobirat ainei metabaiki enkiting'oto-- naisho ninye engolon-- peitore ninye lemeata Engai--"
Revelation2:27 neirrita ninje tʼeng'udi esekengei nedany anaa motiok esarng'ab--"
Revelation2:28 anaa enatang'amua si nanu te Papa; naisho ninye olakira lʼengakenya.
Revelation2:29 Oloata enkiyok-- njening' enajoki Olmumua sirito."
Revelation3:1 Tisiraki olmalaika lʼesirit natii atua Sardes: Kuna ejo Oloata ilmumuan oopishana lʼEngai o lakir oopishana: Ayolo nkitobirat inono-- amu iata engarna ajo injiu-- nitua iye."
Revelation3:2 Topiu nintagol nkulie naataa ee. Amu eitu adol nkitobirat inono etabaitie tʼengomom Engai.
Revelation3:3 Onaa-- tadamu enitang'amua nitoning'o-- torripo taalai! Teni minjololo-- nalotu shumata ino anaa olapurroni-- nimiyolo ina saa nalotunye enitii."
Revelation3:4 Kake iata kulie arn te Sardes neitu epik oloirerio nkilani enye; nepuo ninje aalimana te nebo o nanu-- amu eaku too ninje;"
Revelation3:5 Ologilu-- nemeata kata nemeishopokini ilkilani ooibor-- namajut nanu engarna enye tʼenkitabu empuan-- nayeu naibalu engarna enye tʼengomom e Papa lai o ilmalaikan lenyena."
Revelation3:6 Oloata engiyok-- njening' enajoki Olmumua sirito."
Revelation3:7 Tisiraki olmalaika lʼesirit natii atua Filadelfia: Kuna ejo ele Sinyati olosipa-- oata eenet e David-- obolu nemetii oigen-- oloigenoo nemetii obolu:"
Revelation3:8 Ayolo nkitobirat inono. Ng'orai-- aishoo tʼengomom ino kutukaji nabolo-- nemetii oloidim aigeno; amu iata iye enkiti golon-- nimbung'a ororei lai neitu imiki engarna ai."
Revelation3:9 Ng'orai-- aisho kulekai loora lʼolturrur le satan oojo aten Yudayoi-- nemera-- kake elejisho; ng'orai-- aau ninje-- pepuonu nebatatakino nkejek inono neyolou-- aajo aatonyorra iye."
Revelation3:10 Tiaraki nitorripo ororei lʼolng'iria lai-- nayeu naarrip si iye te saa enkitasuroto nalotu shumata olmaa pookin-- peitasuri loomanya tʼenkop."
Revelation3:11 Ng'orai-- alotu asioki; mbung'a akurraki ina niata-- pemea o obo enkaja enkitook ino."
Revelation3:12 Ologilu-- naitaa ninye eng'apet engaji Engai ai-- nemeitoki ninye apuku tukul-- nasir shumata enye engarna Engai ai o engarna e Yerusalem ng'ejuk nara engang' Engai ai nadou aing'ua shumata o Engai ai-- o engarna ai ng'ejuk."
Revelation3:13 Oloata engiyok-- njening' enajoki Olmumua sirito."
Revelation3:14 Tisiraki olmalaika lʼesirit natii atua Laodikea: Kuna ejo ele oji Amen-- ele jakeni supat osipa-- laa ninye enkiterata enkitobirata Engai:"
Revelation3:15 Ayolo nkitobirat inono-- ajo mirobi nimirowua. Oi-- ten emut irobi arashu irowua!"
Revelation3:16 Kake tiaraki nimololong' ake-- mirowua nimirobi-- naanotaa iye aitung'ua enkutuk ai."
Revelation3:17 Amu ijo iye: ara oladupani-- ataraposhe tukul namalau toki; kake miyolo-- ajo iata enkurruna o leyat-- nira aisinani o modooni niminjopo."
Revelation3:18 Aaigwen iye-- wou enatii nanu-- nyang'u sahabu natiikaki tʼenkima-- pidupore-- o ilkilani ooibor Enjopo-- pemelioi enkurruna ino-- tiaraki niminjopo; nyang'u eilata oo ngonyek aelie ngonyek inono-- pitum atadolishoi."
Revelation3:19 Ore kulo lanyor-- naitame naar; onaa-- tonyua niala."
Revelation3:20 Ng'orai-- aitashe te kutukaji-- aoshiosh. Oloning' oltoilo lai nebol kutukaji-- nalotu atua ainos endaa te nebo o ninye-- o ninye te nebo o nanu."
Revelation3:21 Ologilu-- naisho ninye-- peton te nebo o nanu tʼolorika lai lʼenkigwena-- anaa patigilua nanu naton te nebo o Papa tʼolorika lʼenkigwena lenye."
Revelation3:22 Oloata engiyok-- njening' enajoki Olmumua sirito."
Revelation4:1 Ore peidipai kuna baak-- nadol kutukaji natabole te shumata. Ore oltoilo lʼenkiterata latoning'o-- netiu anaa oltoilo lʼemowuo laairorie nanu nejo: lepu ene-- naaitadol iye mbaak nemeata kata nemeaku akenya."
Revelation4:2 Ore nabo kata natii tʼolmumua. Naa ng'orai-- etipikaki te shumata olorika lʼenkitoria netii obo otonita ilo orika."
Revelation4:3 Ore olotonita-- neya tʼeng'or anaa osoit yaspis o sarder-- nemanita olakira Ai olorika lʼenkitoria otiu anaa smaragid."
Revelation4:4 Netii si kulekai orikan tikitam o ong'wan oomanita ilo orika-- natadua too lelo orikan ilpaiyani tikitam o ong'wan ootonita-- ooishopokoki ilkilani ooibor-- neata shumata oo lukuny enye ilkarandan lʼenkitoria le sahabu."
Revelation4:5 Nepuku tiatua olorika lʼenkitoria nkiwang'at o nkikurrukurrot o iltoiloi-- netii nkilang'eta naapishana naaiwuwu tʼengomom olorika-- naa ninje ilmumuan oopishana lʼEngai."
Revelation4:6 Netii engomom olorika enaiposha e bilauri nailiil anaa kristal; ore tʼempolos olorika lʼenkitoria o mbat-- nemanita ng'wesi ong'wan naabore ngonyek tʼengomom o tekurum."
Revelation4:7 Ore ena ng'wes elukunya-- netiu anaa olng'atuny-- ore engai ng'wes e are-- netiu anaa olashe-- ore eng'wes e uni-- neata engomom anaa oltung'ani-- ore eng'wes e ong'wan-- netiu anaa olkelerua oipirri te shumata."
Revelation4:8 Neata eng'wes pookin too kuna ong'wan naipuko ile-- nebore ninje oriong' o tiatua ngonyek-- nemeeng'ieng'a dama o kiarie ejo: Sinyati-- sinyati-- sinyati Engai Olaitoriani-- tʼengolon pookin-- otii opa-- netii taata-- naa ninye olotu!"
Revelation4:9 Ore peaki ng'wesin enkitadararoto o enkitook o ashe ilo otonita olorika lʼenkitoria neishiu nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin--"
Revelation4:10 nebatatakino kulo paiyani tikitam o ong'wan ilo oton tʼolorika neserem oloishiu nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin-- nenang' ilkarandan lʼenkitoria lenye tʼengomom olorika nejo:"
Revelation4:11 Eaku-- Olaitoriani o Engai ang'-- ping'amu enkitook o enganyit o engolon; amu iye oitobira ntokitin pookin-- ore tʼolbae lʼeyeunoto ino-- peitobiraki."
Revelation5:1 Nadol tʼengaina e tatene e ilo oton tʼolorika lʼenkitoria enkitabu nasira atua o oriong'-- nateenaki too lmishiren oopishana."
Revelation5:2 Nadol olmalaika ogol-- eipotisho tʼoltoilo kitok ajo: Kang'ai oaku-- pebolu enkitabu negil ilmishiren lenyena?"
Revelation5:3 Neaku metii te shumata ana tʼenkop ana tiabori enkop oloidim atabolu enkitabu arashu aing'orai.
Revelation5:4 Naishir naleng'-- tiaraki neitu etumi oloaku-- pebol enkitabu aisoma ana aing'oraa."
Revelation5:5 Naajoki obo too lelo paiyani: minjir! Ng'orai-- etigilua olng'atuny lora lʼenkishomi e Yuda-- entonata e David-- abolu enkitabu negil ilmishiren lenyena oopishana."
Revelation5:6 Naitoki adol tʼempolos olorika lʼenkitoria o ng'wesin ong'wan o ilpaiyani embalelo eitashe tʼempolos-- natiu anaa eteyeng'aki-- neata mowuarak naapishana o ngonyek naapishana-- naa ninje ilmumuan oopishana lʼEngai ooirriwakaki enkop pookin."
Revelation5:7 Nelotu nea enkitabu tʼengaina e tatene e ilo oton tʼolorika.
Revelation5:8 Ore peidip ninye aibung'a enkitabu-- nebatatakino ng'wesi ong'wan o ilpaiyani tikitam o ong'wan tʼengomom embalelo-- eata pookin engauo oo singolioitin o ngirran e sahabu naabore loirienito-- nera ninje sayat oo sinyat--"
Revelation5:9 nerany Osingolio ng'ejuk ejo: Kitumoki iye-- pimbung' enkitabu nigil ilmishiren lenyena; amu kiteyeng'aki-- ninyang'aki yook Engai t'osarge lino aitung'ua enkishomi pookin o enkutuk o olosho o olorere pookin--"
Revelation5:10 nintaaki yook Engai ilkarsisi o laidasak nikipuo aaku looitorisho tʼenkop.
Revelation5:11 Nadol nanu naning' oltoilo loo lmalaikan kumok oomanita olorika lʼenkitoria o ng'wesin o ilpaiyani-- naa ore esiana iip tomon kat iip tomon kumok naleng'--"
Revelation5:12 nejo tʼoltoilo kitok: Eaku peng'amu embalelo nateyeng'aki-- engolon o endupai o eng'eno o enkidimata o enganyit o enkitook o emayani."
Revelation5:13 Ore enkitobirata pookin natii shumata o enkop o abori enkop o enaiposha o pookin naatii atua-- naning' pookin ejo: Njeata ilo oton tʼolorika lʼenkitoria o embalelo-- emayani o enganyit o enkitook o engolon nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin."
Revelation5:14 Nejo ng'wesi ong'wan: Amen! Nebatata ilpaiyani tikitam o ong'wan neserem ilo oishiu metabaiki nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin.
Revelation6:1 Nadol embalelo ebolu obo loo lelo mishiren oopishana; naning' nabo oo nena ng'wesi ong'wan ejo anaa tʼoltoilo lʼendarata: Wou!
Revelation6:2 Nadol-- ng'orai-- embarta naibor. Ore ilo okedito-- neata engauo; neishori olkaranda lʼenkitoria-- nepuku egilunore-- o petum engilunoto."
Revelation6:3 Ore pegil olekai mishire-- naning' engai ng'wes ejo: Wou!"
Revelation6:4 Neitoki engai barta-- nanyokie apuku; ore olokedito-- neishooki ninye engolon naitainye eseriani tʼenkop-- metarakinoto ninje aten; neishooki ninye olalem kitok."
Revelation6:5 Ore pegil ilo mishire li okuni-- naning' ina ng'wes e uni ejo: Wou! Nadol nanu-- ng'orai-- embarta narok; ore olokedito-- neata ninye entemet tʼengaina enye."
Revelation6:6 Naning' oltoilo tiatua nena ng'wesi ong'wan ejo: Ore enkibaba engano naibor tʼengosholai nabo-- ore nkibabani uni oo lmoya too ngoshola are; nimishoroo ina ilata o enaisho."
Revelation6:7 Ore pegil olmishire li ong'wan-- naning' oltoilo lʼeng'wes e ong'wan ojo: Wou!"
Revelation6:8 Nadol-- ng'orai-- embarta pukoti; ore olokedito ninye-- neji enkea-- nesuj ninye ewueji oo lootuata. Neishori ninje engolon-- pear ematua e ong'wan enkop metua tʼolalem o tʼolamei o tʼenkea o too lowuarak lʼenkop."
Revelation6:9 Ore pegil olmishire le imiet-- nadol tiabori olperere tʼenkidasare iltauja loo lelo ootaraki tʼolbae lʼororei lʼEngai o lʼenjakenishu naata--"
Revelation6:10 neishir ninje tʼoltoilo kitok nejo: Metabaiki anu ianyu-- iye-- Laitoriani sinyati osipa-- nimingwenaki nintalaku osarge lang' too lelo oomanya tʼenkop?"
Revelation6:11 Neishori pooki obo too ninje olkila oibor-- nejokini ninje meeng'ieng'ata enkiti kata-- metabana neitabaiari lelo shorueta lenye o lalashera lenye-- lemeata kata nemeari si anaa ninje opa."
Revelation6:12 Ore pegil olmishire le ile-- ng'orai-- neaku enkikirikirata kitok enkop-- neroku engolong' anaa olgunia loo lpapit-- o olapa anaa osarge;"
Revelation6:13 nedoiki lakir le shumata enkop-- neijia-- anaa peraru olng'aboli ilng'abolo lenyena-- teni eipiripir ninye olkutati kitok."
Revelation6:14 Neiwang'ieki shumata anaa enkitabu nairinaki; neidurrieki ildonyo o looigeruno pookin tʼewueji enye.
Revelation6:15 Ore ilkarsisi lʼenkop o ilkituak o ladupak o singan o loolakuno pookin-- neisudori tiatua ngapunia o soito loo ldonyo"
Revelation6:16 nejoki ildonyo o soito: Entuurokinoto shumata ang' niopoopo yook tʼengomom e ilo oton tʼolorika lʼenkitoria o tʼengomom engoro embalelo.
Revelation6:17 Amu etabaua engolong' kitok engoro enye; naa ang'ai oidim aitasho?
Revelation7:1 Ore tekurum oo nena-- nadol ilmalaikan ong'wan ooitashe too nkutot pokira ong'wan enkop-- eibooio ilkutat ong'wan lʼenkop-- pemekutisho olkutati tʼenkop ana tʼenaiposha ana tʼoljani hoo obo."
Revelation7:2 Nadol olekai malaika eilepu tʼenkilepunoto engolong'-- oata olmishiret lʼEngai naishiu-- nebuaki tʼoltoilo kitok kulo malaikan ong'wan ooishooki-- peitame enkop o enaiposha--"
Revelation7:3 ajoki: Emintame enkop arashu enaiposha arashu ilkeek-- metabana nikipik singan lʼEngai ang' olmishire too nkirribon enye."
Revelation7:4 Naning' esiana oo kulo ootipikaki olmishire: naa elfun iip o artam o ong'wan ooing'ua njomito pookin oo nkera Israel.
Revelation7:5 Ore tʼenkishomi e Yuda-- naa elfun tomon o are ootimishiraki; ore tʼenkishomi e Ruben-- naa elfun tomon o are ootimishiraki; ore tʼenkishomi e Gad-- naa elfun tomon o are ootimishiraki;"
Revelation7:6 ore tʼenkishomi e Aser-- naa elfun tomon o are ootinaishiraki; ore lʼenkishomi e Naftali-- naa elfun tomon o are ootimishiraki; ore tʼenkishomi e Manase-- naa elfun tomon o are ootimishiraki;"
Revelation7:7 ore tʼenkishomi e Simeon-- naa elfun tomon o are ootimishiraki; ore tʼenkishomi e Levi-- naa elfun tomon o are ootimishiraki; ore tʼenkishomi e Isashar-- naa elfun tomon o are ootimishiraki;"
Revelation7:8 ore tʼenkishomi e Sebulon-- naa elfun tomon o are ootimishiraki; ore tʼenkishomi e Yosef-- naa elfun tomon o are ootimishiraki; ore tʼenkishomi e Benyamin-- na elfun tomon o are ootimishiraki."
Revelation7:9 Ore tekurum oo kuna nadol-- ng'orai-- esiamu kitok nemeidim o obo aikena-- ooing'ua loreren pookin o njomito o loshon o nkutukie pookin-- eitashe tʼengomom olorika lʼenkitoria o tʼengomom embalelo-- eishopokoki ilkilani ooibor-- neata ilng'osil loo ltuka too ngaik enye--"
Revelation7:10 nedar tʼoltoilo kitok ejo: En Engai ang' naton shumata olorika lʼenkito ria-- enkitopuata o nʼembalelo!"
Revelation7:11 Neitashe ilmalaikan pookin aaman olorika lʼenkitoria-- o ilpaiyani o ng'wesin ong'wan-- nebatata neijululokino engomom olorika lʼenkitoria neserem Engai"
Revelation7:12 ejo: Amen-- ore emayani o enkitook o eng'eno o elikinoto e ashe o enkitaaroto enkitook o enkidimata o engolon-- njeaku nʼEngai ang' metabaiki nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin! Amen!"
Revelation7:13 Nealu obo too lpaiyani naajoki: Kakua kulo ooishopokoki ilkilani ooibor? Kaji eing'ua?
Revelation7:14 Najoki nanu ninye: Laitoriani lai-- iyolo iye. Naajoki ninye nanu: Era kulo looing'ua atua osina kitok-- neisuj ilkilani lenye neiborrie ninje tʼosarge lʼembalelo."
Revelation7:15 Onaa-- etii ninje engomom olorika lʼenkitoria lʼEngai neisyayaki ninye dama o kiarie tiatua engaji enye; ore oloton te shumata olorika lʼenkitoria-- nemany shumata enye."
Revelation7:16 Nemeitoki aapuo aatum olamei arashu enkure-- nemeitoki aadoiki ninje engolong' arashu eikai pookin;"
Revelation7:17 amu elairrita ninje embalelo natii empolos olorika lʼenkitoria-- nerikoki ninje ngonyek oo ngariak naaishiu; nelajut Engai ilkiyo pookin too ngonyek enye."
Revelation8:1 Ore pegil olmishire le opishana-- negira shumata anaa enusu saa."
Revelation8:2 Nadol kulo malaikan oopishana ooitashe tʼengomom Engai-- neishori ninje mowuarak naapishana."
Revelation8:3 Nepuku olekai malaika aitashe tʼengomom olperere lʼenkidasare-- neata emoti nairishoreki e sahabu-- neishori loirienito kumok-- peponiki sayat oo sinyat shumata olperere lʼesahabu otii engomom olorika lʼenkitoria."
Revelation8:4 Neilep empuruo oo loirienito lʼesayata oo sinyat tʼengaina olmalaika abaiki Engai.
Revelation8:5 Nedumu olmalaika emoti nairishoreki neigany tʼenkima olperere nebukoki enkop. Neaku endarata o iltoiloi o nkiwang'at o nkikirikirat.
Revelation8:6 Ore lelo malaikan oopishana ooata mowuarak-- neitobir peosh."
Revelation8:7 Neosh olmalaika lʼelukunya emowuo-- nepuku soito lʼenjan o enkima etushulare osarge-- nedoiki enkop; nepejo ematua e uni enkop-- nepejo ematua e uni oo ljanito-- nepejo nkujit naanyori pookin."
Revelation8:8 Neitoki aosh olmalaika le are emowuo; nelotu anaa oldonyo kitok oiwuwu tʼenkima-- nenang'akini atua enaiposha; neaku ematua e uni enaiposha osarge--"
Revelation8:9 nee ematua e uni oo ng'wesi naaishiu naatii enaiposha-- neiminyeki ematua e uni oo meilini."
Revelation8:10 Neitoki aosh olmalaika li okuni emowuo; nedou olakira sapuk aing'ua shumata oiwuwu anaa enkilang'et nedoiki ematua e uni oo wuason o noo ljorroi.
Revelation8:11 Neji engarna e ilo akira olkurto lʼentim-- neaku ematua e uni oo ngariak olkurto lʼentim-- neeye iltung'anak kumok engare-- amu eitaduaraki naleng'."
Revelation8:12 Neitoki aosh olmalaika le ong'wan emowuo-- near ematua e uni engolong' o ematua e uni olapa o ematua e uni oo lakir-- pepiki ematua enye e uni enaimin-- nemeitoki ematua e uni endama awang'u-- naa neijia si etiu enkiarie."
Revelation8:13 Nadol-- naning' olmalaika obo oipirri te shumata ejo tʼoltoilo sapuk: Ee-- kake aiya-- aiya-- aiya-- ndai loomanya tʼenkop-- tʼolbae loo lkulekai toiloi leton eng'or loo lmalaikan okuni ooitoki aaosh emowuo."
Revelation9:1 Neosh olmalaika le imiet emowuo; nadol olakira oing'ua shumata-- nedoiki enkop-- neishooki ninye embolet engumoto easuroto--"
Revelation9:2 nebol ninye ena gumoto easuroto-- nepuku empuruo tʼengumoto ailep shumata-- netiu empuruo anaa en engaji empejoto sapuk-- neigany enaimin engolong' o shumata tʼempuruo naing'ua ena gumoto."
Revelation9:3 Nepuku ilmaat tiatua empuruo aapuo shumata enkop; neishooki ninje engolon anaa peata nkulupan engolon tʼenkop.
Revelation9:4 Nejokini ninje: emiony nkujit tʼenkop-- arashu entoki nanyori-- arashu oljani-- kake iltung'anak ake lemeata olmishire lʼEngai too nkirribon enye."
Revelation9:5 Neishooki ninje-- pemeony metuata-- kake peitame ninje lapaitin imiet; neaku emion enye anaa emion ten eony enkulupa oltung'ani."
Revelation9:6 Ore too nona olong'i nepuo aaing'oru iltung'anak enkea-- neilany enkea ninje."
Revelation9:7 Netiu kulo maat anaa mbartan naaitobiraki aapuo enjore; neata too lukuny enye ilkarandan anaa lʼesahabu-- netiu ngomomi enye anaa ngomomi oo ltung'anak--"
Revelation9:8 neata ilpapit anaa ng'oroyok-- netiu lala lenye anaa lala loo lng'atunyo--"
Revelation9:9 neata enkishopoto anaa olkila lʼesekengei-- ore oltoilo loo naipuko enye anaa en oo lgarrin ooyetita mbartan kumok naapuo enjore;"
Revelation9:10 neata ilkidong'o anaa loo nkulupan o onyeta too lkidong'o-- neishooki engolon-- peony iltung'anak lapaitin imiet;"
Revelation9:11 neata ninje olkarsis lenye-- laa olmalaika lʼengumoto easuroto-- neji engarna enye tʼenkutuk oo Lhebrayoi Abadon-- neji tʼen oo Lgrikini Apolion."
Revelation9:12 Eidipa osina lʼenkiterata atulusoi; ng'orai-- epon epuonu sinaitin aare tekurum."
Revelation9:13 Neosh olmalaika le ile emowuo; naning' oltoilo eing'ua nkutot ong'wan olperere lʼenkidasare lʼesahabu otii engomom Engai--"
Revelation9:14 nejoki olmalaika le ile oata emowuo: Talaku ilmalaikan ong'wan ooteenaki tʼolkeju kitok Farati.
Revelation9:15 Nelakuni kulo malaikan ong'wan-- ooitobirakinore esaa o engolong' o olapa o olari-- pear metuata ematua e uni oo ltung'anak."
Revelation9:16 Ore esiana enjore nakedito mbartan-- naa elfun kat elfun kumok; naning' esiana enye--"
Revelation9:17 nadol neijia mbartan tʼenduaroto-- o lelo ookedito-- eata ilkilani lʼesekengei laaijo lʼenkima o loo pusi soito o loo nkibiritini. Ore lukuny oo mbartan-- netiu anaa lukuny oo lng'atunyo-- nepuku too nkutukie enye enkima o emburuo o enkibiriti."
Revelation9:18 Nearieki ematua e uni oo ltung'anak too kuna tabo pokirauni-- tʼenkima o tʼempuruo o tʼenkibiriti-- naapuku too nkutukie enye."
Revelation9:19 Amu ore engolon oo mbartan-- naa en oo nkutukie o noo lkidong'o; netiu ilkidong'o lenye anaa lasuria ooata lukuny neonyisho too ninje."
Revelation9:20 Ore iltung'anak ootelekutua too nona tabo-- neitu eala aapal nkitobirat oo ngaik enye-- pemeitoki aasai ilmeneng'a o muain naaitobiraki te sahabu o tʼengosholai o tʼosuiai o too soito o too nkeek-- nemedolisho nemening'isho nemeidim aashom--"
Revelation9:21 neitu eala tʼolbae lʼearata metua enye-- arashu esakutore-- arashu entalare-- arashu empurrore enye."
Revelation10:1 Nadol olekai malaika ogol edou aing'ua shumata; neishopokoki eng'atamboi neata olakira Ai tʼelukunya enye-- netiu engomom enye anaa engolong' o nkejek enyena anaa ng'apeta enkima--"
Revelation10:2 neata tʼengaina enye enkiti kitabu nabolo-- neroro tʼenkeju enye e tatene enaiposha-- neroro tʼenkeju e kedyanye enkop."
Revelation10:3 Nebuak tʼoltoilo sapuk anaa peipurrito olng'atuny. Ore pebuak-- neiro ndarat naapishana too ltoiloi lenye--"
Revelation10:4 Ore peiro nena darat naapishana too ltoiloi lenye-- najo asir; naning' oltoilo aing'ua shumata naajoki: Teena enairoro nena darat naapishana-- tʼolmishire; misir ninje!"
Revelation10:5 Ore ilo malaika latadua eitashe tʼenaiposha o tʼenkop-- nedumu engaina enye e tatene aitorioki shumata--"
Revelation10:6 neituruj te ilo oishiu metabaiki nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin-- ninye oitobira shumata o ntokitin naatii atua-- o enkop te nebo o naatii atua-- o enaiposha o naatii atua-- ajo pemeitoki aatai engai kata--"
Revelation10:7 kake ore too ngolong'i oltoilo lʼolmalaika le opishana-- teni eosh emowuo-- neitabaiari emikio Engai-- neijia anaa peitayolo singan lenyena loora layolounok."
Revelation10:8 Naaitoki airorie oltoilo latoning'o aing'ua shumata naajoki: Nno-- tudumu enda kiti kitabu nabolo-- natii engaina e ilo malaika ororita tʼenaiposha o tʼenkop."
Revelation10:9 Nalo nanu enetii olmalaika najoki: Njooki ena kiti kitabu! Naajoki ninye: Nko-- toijoi-- kintaduar engoshoke ino-- kake ore tʼenkutuk-- emelok anaa enaisho."
Revelation10:10 Nadumu nanu ena kiti kitabu tʼengaina olmalaika naijoo-- nemelok ninye tʼenkutuk ai anaa enaisho; ore paidip ataama-- neduaru engoshoke ai."
Revelation10:11 Naajoki ninye: meata kata nimintoki iye aitayolo mbaak e akenya too loshon o loreren o nkutukie o ilkarsisi kumok.
Revelation11:1 Naaishori nanu entiani anaa eng'udi-- naajoki obo: Nyo-- tetema engaji sinyati Engai o olperere lʼenkidasare o kulo ooserem tiatua."
Revelation11:2 Ore ilo leng'oti ti aulo engaji sinyati-- nturraki oriong'-- nimitem! Amu eishooki loreren lemeata Engai-- nepuonu aaroro engang' sinyati lapaitin artam o are."
Revelation11:3 Nalaisho iljaken lainei aare-- peitayolou ninje mbaak e akenya ngolong'i iip tomon o iip are o ntomoni ile-- eishopo ilguniani."
Revelation11:4 Kulo lelo oirienito aare o lelo kilang'eta aare-- ooitashe tʼengomom Olaitoriani lʼenkop."
Revelation11:5 Naa ten eyeu oltung'ani near ninje-- nepuku enkima too nkutukie enye-- nenya ilmang'ati lenye-- ore oltung'ani pookin oyeu neitame ninje-- neari ninye metua."
Revelation11:6 Neata lelo engolon naigenye ninje shumata too ngolong'i enkitayolounoto enye-- pemesha-- neata engolon naibelekenyie engare metaa osarge-- near enkop tʼentaboi pookin nayeu naarie."
Revelation11:7 Ore peitabaia enjakenishu enye-- nearare ninje ina ng'wes naing'ua easuroto-- negilu ninje-- near metuata."
Revelation11:8 Neirrag mpopong'i enye tʼengoitoi e ina ang' sapuk-- naji tʼemumuaishu: Sodom o Misri-- enetooshokoki si Olaitoriani esalaba."
Revelation11:9 Ore kulekai loo loshon o nkishomitie o nkutukie o loreren-- nedol mpopong'i enye ngolong'i uni o nusu-- nemeisho mpopong'i enye metunukari too nkuraren."
Revelation11:10 Neng'idakino ninje kulo oomanya atua enkop-- nerany tʼenjipai-- neirriwakino ninje nkishoorot aten; amu eisilo kulo ayolounok aare lelo ootii enkop."
Revelation11:11 Ore peishunye ngolong'i uni o nusu-- nejing' Olmumua lʼenkishui oing'ua Engai-- atua ninje-- neitashe too nkejek enye-- neibung' enkuretishu kitok kulo ootadua ninje."
Revelation11:12 Nening' ninje oltoilo sapuk oing'ua shumata ajoki ninje: Eleputu ene wueji! Neilep ninje aapuo shumata tʼeng'atamboi-- nedolita ilmang'ati lenye ninje."
Revelation11:13 Ore te ina saa neaku enkikirikirata sapuk enkop-- neurori ematua e tomon engang': neari metuata tʼenkikirikirata enkop ngam elfun napishana-- ore lootelekutua-- nejing' enkuretishu-- neitaa kitok Engai natii shumata."
Revelation11:14 Eidipa osina le are atulusoi-- ng'orai-- elotu osina li okuni asioki."
Revelation11:15 Neosh olmalaika le opishana emowuo. Neaku iltoiloi kituak ooing'ua shumata-- nejo ninje: Eidipa enkarsishu olmaa ataa en Olaitoriani lang' o ne Kristos lenye-- neitorisho metabaiki nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin."
Revelation11:16 Ore ilpaiyani tikitam o ong'wan ootoni tʼengomom Engai too lorikan lʼenkitoria-- nebatata too ngomomi enye aaserem Engai--"
Revelation11:17 nejo: Kiliki yook iye ashe-- Olaitoriani o Engai magilani-- litii taata-- naa iye otii opa-- tiaraki nitang'amua engolon ino kitok nintorisho;"
Revelation11:18 negoro loreren-- nelotu engoro ino o enkata naigwenakinyeki lootuata-- neishori olkwaje singan linono loora layolounok o sinyat o kulo ooure engarna ino-- looti o ilkituak-- neiminyeki looiminye enkop."
Revelation11:19 Neboli engaji sinyati Engai te shumata-- nedoli osanduku lʼosotua lenye tiatua engaji enye-- neaku enkiwang'ata o iltoiloi o endarata o enkikirikirata enkop o enjan oo soito sapuk."
Revelation12:1 Nelioi olponoto kitok te shumata-- naa eng'oroyoni naishopokoki engolong' netii olapa abori oo nkejek enyena-- ore shumata elukunya enye-- netii olmarisian lʼenkitoria loata lakir tomon o aare."
Revelation12:2 Nemena ninye neishir ninye tʼemion eishoi.
Revelation12:3 Neitoki alioi olekai ponoto te shumata-- naa ng'orai-- entiamasi sapuk nanyokie-- naata lukuny naapishana o mowuarak tomon-- netii shumata oo lukuny enyena nkeenda enkitoria naapishana:"
Revelation12:4 ore ol-kidong'oi lenye-- neyetaa ematua e uni oo lakir anang'aki enkop-- neitashe ina tiamasi tʼengomom e ina ng'oroyoni naata emion eishoi-- peiye-- teni eisho-- eijoo enkerai enye."
Revelation12:5 Neiu ninye engaiyoni-- naa ninye olairrita loreren lemeata Engai pookin tʼeng'udi esekengei. Neilepieki enkerai enye enetii Engai o olorika lenye lʼenkitoria."
Revelation12:6 Neilanyisho ina ng'oroyoni alo ang'ata-- ewueji naitobiraka Engai ninye-- peitotii ninye ngolong'i iip tomon o iip are o ntomoni ile."
Revelation12:7 Nejing' olarrabal shumata. Ore Mikael o ilmalaikan lenyena nearare entiamasi; nearare si entiamasi te nebo o ilmalaikan lenyena--"
Revelation12:8 nemegilu nemeitokini aatum ewueji enye te shumata.
Revelation12:9 Nenang'uni abori entiamasi kitok-- naa ninye olasurai musana-- oji oloirirua o satan-- oitapong'oo olmaa pookin; etanang'uaki enkop o ilmalaikan lenyena te nebo o ninye."
Revelation12:10 Naning' oltoilo kitok te shumata ojo: Etaa taata enkitopuata o engolon o enkarsishu nʼEngai ang'-- o enkitoria en e Kristos lenye-- tiaraki naiturraiyoki olaitang'oroni loo lalashera lang'-- oitang'oro ninje tʼEngai dama o kiarie."
Revelation12:11 Etigilutua ninje tʼosarge lʼembalelo o tʼororei lʼenjakenishu enye-- neitu enyor empuan enye metabaiki enkea."
Revelation12:12 Onaa-- enting'idata-- ndai shumat o loomanya tiatua. Ee-- kake aiya kulo oomanya tʼenkop o tʼenaiposha. Amu elotu satan adoiki ndai-- neata engoro sapuk-- neyolo ajo enkiti kata ake eata."
Revelation12:13 Ore pedol ina tiamasi ajo etanang'aki aitadou enkop-- neipirrioki ina ng'oroyoni natoiwuo engaiyoni."
Revelation12:14 Neishori ina ng'oroyoni naipuko are naaijo nʼolmotony kitok-- peipirri ninye alo ang'ata ewueji enye-- eneitotiyeki enkata nabo o nkatan are o enusu kata-- tʼengomom entiamasi."
Revelation12:15 Neiponyaki entiamasi engare ina ng'oroyoni tʼenkutuk enye anaa olkeju lʼengare-- pewuapaa engare ninye."
Revelation12:16 Kake etaretoko enkop eng'oroyoni abol enkutuk aijoo ina are naiponya entiamasi tʼenkutuk enye.
Revelation12:17 Negoroki entiamasi eng'oroyoni-- nelo ninye aarare kulo lʼeishoi enye ootelekutua-- lepon eibung'ita nkitanapat Engai-- neata enjakenishu e Yesus."
Revelation13:1 Naitashe tʼosunyai lʼenaiposha-- nadol eng'wes naing'ua enaiposha-- naata mowuarak tomon o lukuny naapishana-- neata shumata oo mowuarak enyena ilkarandan lʼenkitoria tomon-- neata shumata oo lukuny enyena ngam oo morot."
Revelation13:2 Ore ina ng'wes-- padol-- netiu anaa olowuaru keri-- netiu nkejek enyena anaa nʼemuny-- netiu enkutuk enye anaa enkutuk olng'atuny-- neisho entiamasi ninye engolon enye o olorika lenye lʼenkitoria o enkidimata kitok."
Revelation13:3 Nadol elukunya enye nabo naijo etaremoki metua; ore ilo bae lenye lʼenkea-- neishiu-- neing'asia enkop pookin tekurum ina ng'wes--"
Revelation13:4 neserem ninje entiamasi-- amu eishoo eng'wes engolon-- neserem ninje eng'wes nejo: Kang'ai onyanyukie eng'wes-- naa ng'ai oidim ataarare ninye?"
Revelation13:5 Neishooki ninye enkutuk nairorie mbaak sapuki o ildeketa; neishooki ninye engolon metabaiki lapaitin artam o are.
Revelation13:6 Nebol ninye enkutuk enye amor Engai-- nemor engarna enye o engaji enye o kulo oomanyita shuniata."
Revelation13:7 Neishooki ninye metaarare sinyat negilu ninje; neishooki ninye engolon meitoria enkishomi o enkutuk o olorere pookin.
Revelation13:8 Neserem ninye kulo pookin oomanya atua engop-- leitu esira ngam enye tʼenkitabu empuan Embalelo nataraki-- opa tʼenkiterunoto olmaa."
Revelation13:9 Oloata enkiyok-- njening'!"
Revelation13:10 Teni epik oltung'ani atua engaji eenata-- nelo si ninye atua engaji eenata; teni ear obo tʼolalem metua-- meata kata nemeari si ninye tʼolalem metua. Ene etii olng'iria o enkirukoto oo sinyat."
Revelation13:11 Nadol engai ng'wes eilepu aing'ua enkop; neata ninye mowuarak are-- anaa embalelo-- neiro si ninye anaa entiamasi."
Revelation13:12 Neasishore ninye engolon e ina ng'wes enkiterata-- tʼengomom enye; neisho enkop o pookin oomanya atua meteserema ina ng'wes elukunya-- idya naishiuwo eremoto enye enkea;"
Revelation13:13 neitobir ilponot kituak-- oo meitadou enkima aitung'ua shumata tʼengomom oo ltung'anak--"
Revelation13:14 neitapong'oo kulo oomanya atua enkop tʼolbae loo lponot oishooki ninye-- peas tʼengomom e ina ng'wes; nejoki kulo oomanya atua enkop-- peitobir aten emua e ina ng'wes naata olbae t'olalem neishiu."
Revelation13:15 Neishooki ninye meishoo enkiyang'et ina mua-- peiro ina mua eng'wes-- neisho metaari metuata kulo leitu eserem emua eng'wes."
Revelation13:16 Nearaki ninje pookin-- looti o ilkituak-- ladupak o laisinak-- loolakuno o singan-- metipiki ninje olkigeroto tʼengaina enye e tatene arashu tʼenkirribo enye--"
Revelation13:17 pemeidim oltung'ani ainyang'u arashu atimira-- leme elde oata olkigeroto lʼengarna e ina ng'wes ana esiana engarna enye"
Revelation13:18 Ene etii eng'eno. Oloata endamunoto-- njemus esiana eng'wes; amu era esiana oltung'ani-- nera esiana enye iip ile o ntomoni ile o ile."
Revelation14:1 Nadol ina Balelo eitashe tʼoldonyo le Sion o te nebo o ninye iltung'anak elfun iip o artam o ong'wan-- ooata engarna enye o engarna e Menye etisiraki too nkirribon enye."
Revelation14:2 Naning' nanu oltoilo oing'ua shumata-- laijo oltoilo loo ngariak kumok; laijo si oloo ndarat kituak; ore ilo toilo latoning'o-- netiu anaa oloo laoshok lʼenkinanda eoshito enkinanda."
Revelation14:3 Nerany ninje Osingolio ng'ejuk tʼengomom olorika lʼenkitoria o tʼengomom oo nena ng'wesi ong'wan o tʼengomom oo lelo paiyani; nemetii oltung'ani oidim aiteng'enuoi ilo singolio neme lelo tung'anak elfun iip o artam o ong'wan-- ooinyang'uaki tʼenkop."
Revelation14:4 Naa ninje leitu epiki oloirerio te nebo o ng'oroyok-- — amu era ninje ntoiye — o kulo oosujita Embalelo ewueji pookin enelo. Nera ninje ooinyang'uaki tiatua iltung'anak metaa ilmomo lʼenkiterata lʼEngai o lʼEmbalelo."
Revelation14:5 Neitu etumi too nkutukie enye elejare-- amu meata entibili."
Revelation14:6 Nadol olmalaika eipirri agiroo te shumata-- oata lomon lʼeng'ida loo nkatan pookin-- peinosaki kulo oomanya atua enkop o loreren o njomito o nkutukie o loshon pookin--"
Revelation14:7 nejo ninye tʼoltoilo kitok: Entureita Engai ninjosho ninye enkitook; amu eewuo enkata enkigwena enye. Entasai ele oitobira shumata o enkop o enaiposha o ngonyek oo ngariak.
Revelation14:8 Nesuju olekai malaika ajo: etabatate-- etabatate Babilon-- ina ang' kitok-- naitooko loreren lemeata Engai pookin tʼenaisho torrono entalare enye."
Revelation14:9 Nesuju olekai malaika li okuni ninye otejo tʼoltoilo kitok: Teni eserem oltung'ani eng'wes o emua enye neng'amu olkigeroto tʼenkirribo enye ana tʼengaina enye--"
