Revelation14:10 nelaok ninye si enaisho engoro Engai-- natubukokoki atua enkikombe engoro enye-- eitu eitushuli-- neisili tʼenkima o tʼenkibiriti tʼengomom oo lmalaikan sinyat o nʼEmbalelo."
Revelation14:11 Neilep empuruo enkisiloto enye shumata metabaiki nkatan pookin-- nemeata ninje eng'ieng'ata dama o kiarie-- lelo ooteserema eng'wes o emua enye-- o olotang'amua olkigeroto lʼengarna enye."
Revelation14:12 Ene etii olng'iria loo sinyat-- netii kulo looibung' nkitanapat Engai o enkirukoto e atua Yesus."
Revelation14:13 Naning' oltoilo oing'ua shumata ejo: Tisira! Teshi lootuata looe tiatua Olaitoriani eba taata. Esipa-- ejo Olmumua-- ajo epuo aaeng'ieng'a ninje too nyamalareitin enye-- amu esuj nkitobirat enye ninje."
Revelation14:14 Nadol-- naa ng'orai-- eng'atamboi naibor. Ore tʼeng'atamboi neton obo-- laijo Oinoti lʼoltung'ani-- neata olkaranda lʼenkitoria lʼesahabu tʼelukunya enye-- neata tʼengaina enye emundo napi."
Revelation14:15 Nepuku olekai malaika aing'ua engaji sinyati-- nebuaki tʼoltoilo kitok ilo otonita te shumata eng'atamboi: Rriwai emundo ino-- tudung'o; amu eewuo enkata enkisambuare-- amu etoiyo enkisambuare enkop."
Revelation14:16 Ore ilo otonita eng'atamboi-- nenang'aki emundo enye enkop-- neisambuni enkop."
Revelation14:17 Nepuku olekai malaika aing'ua engaji sinyati natii shumata-- neata emundo napi."
Revelation14:18 Nepuku olekai malaika aing'ua olperere lʼenkidasare-- oata engolon aitore enkima-- neipot ninye ilo oata emundo napi tʼoltoilo kitok: Rriu emundo ino napi nidung' ilmomo lʼoljani lʼolmarua lʼenkop; amu eoto nkululu enyena."
Revelation14:19 Nenang'u olmalaika emundo enye enkop nedung' ilmomo lʼoljani lʼolmarua lʼenkop-- nenang'aki ninje atua enkironyet engoro kitok Engai."
Revelation14:20 Neironyi ina kironyet ti aulo engang'-- nepuku osarge tiatua enkironyet metabaiki sekenge oo nkutukie oo mbartan; neba engadoro anaa nang'arot osoit iip tomon o iip ile."
Revelation15:1 Nadol olekai ponoto kitok naing'asiai naleng' te shumata. Naa ilmalaikan oopishana-- ooata ntabo naapishana naabaiye-- amu ninje-- peishunye engoro Engai."
Revelation15:2 Nadol entoki anaa enaiposha e bilauri nashulare enkima. Ore kulo ootigilutua aaing'ua enetii eng'wes o emua enye o olkigeroto lenye o esiana engarna enye-- neitashe tʼembata e ina aiposha e bilauri neata ngauoi oo singolioitin lʼEngai--"
Revelation15:3 nerany Osingolio le Mose-- lʼosinga lʼEngai-- o Osingolio lʼEmbalelo-- nejo: Kituak nkitobirat inono neing'asiai-- Olaitoriani-- Engai magilani. Supati ngoitoi inono nesipa-- lekarsis loo loreren."
Revelation15:4 Kang'ai-- lemeata kata nimikiure-- Olaitoriani-- nemeitaa engarna ino kitok? Amu iye ake ora sinyati; amu epuonu loreren pookin nikiserem; amu eidipaki aatabolu nkigwenat inono."
Revelation15:5 Ore peishunye kuna-- nadol eboluni engaji sinyati olng'obor lʼenjakenishu te shumata--"
Revelation15:6 nepuku aaing'ua engaji sinyati lelo malaikan oopishana ooata ntabo naapishana-- eishopokoki olkila oibor lemeata entioto-- neteenikiaki nkimeitani esahabu ilgoon lenye."
Revelation15:7 Ore nabo too nena ng'wesi ong'wan-- neisho lelo malaikan oopishana ngirran esahabu naapishana naabore engoro Engai naishiu metabaiki nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin."
Revelation15:8 Neigany engaji sinyati empuruo naing'ua enkitook Engai o engolon enye; nemetii oltung'ani oidim atijing'a engaji sinyati-- metabana neishunye ntabo naapishana oo lmalaikan oopishana."
Revelation16:1 Naning' oltoilo kitok oing'ua engaji sinyati-- ojoki ilmalaikan oopishana: Enjom-- entubukoki nena girran naapishana naabore engoro Engai-- enkop."
Revelation16:2 Nelo ol elukunya abukoki engirra enye tʼenkop-- nejing' iltuduta torrok naleng' iltung'anak ooata olkigeroto lʼeng'wes neserem emua enye."
Revelation16:3 Nebukoki oli are engirra enye atua enaiposha; neaku enaiposha osarge anaa lʼoltung'ani otua-- nee iltauja ooishiu pookin ootii atua enaiposha."
Revelation16:4 Nebukoki oli okuni engirra enye atua ilkejek loo ngariak o atua ngonyek oo ngariak-- neaku ninje osarge."
Revelation16:5 Naning' olmalaika loo ngariak ejo: Olaitoriani-- iye ora supat-- litii taata-- naa iye otii opa-- lora sinyati-- tiaraki ningwenaka neijia--"
Revelation16:6 amu eibukoitie sargeta loo sinyat o loo layolounok-- ninjoo iye ninje osarge metooko-- amu eaku too ninje."
Revelation16:7 Naning' nanu olekai malaika lʼolperere ejo: Ee-- Laitoriani Engai-- tʼengolon pookin-- esipa nkigwenat inono naa supati."
Revelation16:8 Nebukoki oli ong'wan engirra enye atua engolong'-- neishori ninye metapejo iltung'anak tʼenkima."
Revelation16:9 Nepeji iltung'anak tʼenkirowuaj kitok-- nedek ninje engarna Engai-- naata engolon oo kuna tabo-- neitu eala aaitaa ninye kitok."
Revelation16:10 Nebukoki ole imiet engirra enye shumata olorika lʼenkitoria lʼeng'wes-- neaku enkarsishu enye enaimin; neony ninje ilng'ejepa lenye tʼemion--"
Revelation16:11 nedek Engai te shumata tʼolbae loo mioitin o tʼolbae loo ltuduta lenye-- neitu eala aaing'ua nkitarruot enye."
Revelation16:12 Nebukoki ole ile engirra enye shumata emoipo kitok Farati-- nemita engare enye-- peitobirakini ilkarsisi lʼenkilepunoto engolong' engoitoi naimu."
Revelation16:13 Nadol epuku ilmumuan duruk okuni tʼenkutuk entiamasi o tʼenkutuk eng'wes o tʼenkutuk olayolounoni lʼelejare-- ootiu anaa nduan;"
Revelation16:14 amu era ninje ilmumuan loo loiriruani ooas ilponot-- nepuo ngaloli pookin olmaa enetii ilkarsisi-- aaiturrurroki ninje enjore engolong' kitok Engai-- lʼengolon pookin."
Revelation16:15 Ng'orai-- alotu anaa olapurroni. Tesh oloishololo-- neiteng'el ilkilani lenyena-- pemelo meishopo nedoli enkurruna enye."
Revelation16:16 Neiturrurroki ninje eweji neji t'enkutuk oo Lhebrayoi: Harmagedon.
Revelation16:17 Nebukoki ole opishana engirra enye atua olng'inai. Nepuku oltoilo kitok oing'ua shumata tʼenetii olorika lʼenkitoria lʼEngai-- nejo: Eidipe."
Revelation16:18 Neaku enkiwang'ata o iltoiloi o ndarat-- neaku enkikirikirata enkop kitok-- neitu eaku enkikirikirata kitok naba nji-- eiter enkata natii iltung'anak tʼenkop."
Revelation16:19 Neoro ina ang' kitok aaku matuan uni-- neurori ngang'itie oo loreren lemeata Engai. Nedamuni Babilon-- ena ang' kitok-- tʼengomom Engai-- peisho ninye enkikombe enaisho engoro napi enye."
Revelation16:20 Neilanyisho looigeruno lʼenaiposha-- neitu eitokini aadol ildonyo."
Revelation16:21 Nedou enjan sapuk oo soito neshaiki iltung'anak-- neba anaa mosor. Nedek iltung'anak Engai tʼolbae lʼentaboi enjan oo soito-- amu entaboi sapuk naleng'."
Revelation17:1 Nelotu obo too lelo malaikan oopishana ooata nena girran naapishana-- naairorie nanu ajoki: Wou ene-- amu ayeu naaitadol iye ena ng'oroyoni entalare kitok-- naton too ngariak kumok--"
Revelation17:2 neas ilkarsisi lʼenkop mbaak torrok entalare te nebo o ninye-- nemerai loomanya atua enkop tʼenaisho entalare enye."
Revelation17:3 Naanap ninye tʼolmumua metabaiki ang'ata-- nadol eng'oroyoni natonita shumata eng'wes nanyokie naleng'-- nabore ngam oo morot-- neata lukuny naapishana o mowuarak tomon."
Revelation17:4 Neishopokino ina ng'oroyoni olkila odo o olonyokie-- neikodo tʼesahabu o too soito sidan o musetani enkinyang'a kitok naleng'-- neata enkikombe esahabu tʼengaina enye-- nabore ntorrok o loirerion lʼentalare enye--"
Revelation17:5 nesira tʼenkirribo enye engarna-- naa emikio aiko nji: Babilon kitok-- ng'otonye entalare o noo mbaak torrok enkop."
Revelation17:6 Nadol nanu ina ng'oroyoni etemere tʼosarge loo sinyat o tʼosarge loo ljaken le Yesus. Naing'asia naleng'-- padol ninye."
Revelation17:7 Naajoki olmalaika: Ainyo ping'asia? Aaliki iye emikio e ina ng'oroyoni o nʼeng'wes nanap ninye neata lukuny naapishana o mowuarak tomon.
Revelation17:8 Ore ina ng'wes nitadua-- opa etii-- nemetii taata-- neitoki elailepu aing'ua easuroto e satan-- nejing' erruoroto-- nepuo aaing'asia loomanya atua enkop-- leitu esiri ngam enye tiatua enkitabu empuan tʼenkiterunoto olmaa-- teni edol eng'wes-- ajo etii opa-- nemetii taata-- neitoki atii."
Revelation17:9 Ene etii endamunoto naata eng'eno: Ore lukuny naapishana-- naa ildonyo oopishana ootonita eng'oroyoni-- naa ilkarsisi oopishana."
Revelation17:10 Ore imiet etabatatate-- netii obo taata-- neton eitu elotu olekai; ore teni elotu-- nemeata kata nemebik enkiti kata."
Revelation17:11 Ore eng'wes-- natii opa-- nemetii taata-- naa ole isiet otii atua lelo oopishana-- nelo ninye atua erruoroto."
Revelation17:12 Ore nona mowuarak tomon nitadua-- naa ilkarsisi tomon-- leton eitu eng'amu enkarsishu; kake epuo aatum engolon anaa ilkarsisi esaa nabo te nebo o eng'wes."
Revelation17:13 Naa enkigwena nabo eata kulo-- neisho engolon o enkidimata enye eng'wes."
Revelation17:14 Naa ninje ooarare Embalelo-- negilu Embalelo ninje (amu ninye Olaitoriani loo laitoriak o Olkarsis loo lkarsisi)-- o te nebo o ninye looipotokoki o lootegeluaki o lairukok."
Revelation17:15 Naajoki nanu: Ore ngariak nitadua-- naatonita ina ng'oroyoni entalare-- naa loshon o siamin o loreren o nkutukie."
Revelation17:16 Ore nona mowuarak tomon nitadua-- o eng'wes-- naa kulo ooibai ina ng'oroyoni entalare-- neing'ua ninye openy meishopo-- nenya ninje nkiri osesen lenye-- nepejoo ninye katukul tʼenkima."
Revelation17:17 Amu etipika Engai atua iltauja lenye-- peitobir enayeu ninye-- neas enkigwena nabo-- neisho enkarsishu enye eng'wes-- metabana neitabaiari rorei lʼEngai."
Revelation17:18 Ore ina ng'oroyoni nitadua-- naa engang' kitok-- naata enkarsishu aitore ilkarsisi lʼenkop."
Revelation18:1 Ore peishunye kuna-- nadol olekai malaika otadouo aing'ua shumata-- oata engolon kitok-- newang'u enkop tʼenkitook enye."
Revelation18:2 Nedar ninye tʼoltoilo kitok ajo: Etabatate-- etabatate Babilon-- idya kitok-- neaku olmuate loo loiriruani o enkibooroto oo lmumuan duruk pookin o enkibooroto oo ntaritik duruk naaibai pookin."
Revelation18:3 Amu etooko loreren lemeata Engai pookin enaisho engoro entalare enye-- neas ilkarsisi lʼenkop mbaak torrok entalare te nebo o ninye-- nedupore lamirak lʼenkop tʼengolon olng'warra lenye."
Revelation18:4 Naning' olekai toilo oing'ua shumata ojo: Entung'ai atua ninye-- olorere lai-- piming'arierie nkitarruot enyena-- nimitumutumu si ntabo enyena."
Revelation18:5 Amu eilepu nkitarruot enyena aabaiki shumata-- nedamu Engai ng'ok enyena."
Revelation18:6 Entalaaki ninye anaa petalaaka si ninye-- ningilielie tʼerisioroto oo nkitobirat enyena. Ore enkikombe natubukoko-- nibukokiki ninye aigil are."
Revelation18:7 Anaa peitaa kion kitok neitumuru kion-- neijia enjoo ninye osina o enkilishoto naba nji. Amu ejo ninye tʼoltau lenye: Aton ara enkarsis-- mara engoliai-- namadol enkilishoto tukul."
Revelation18:8 Onaa-- epuonu ntabo enyena engolong' nabo: enkea-- enkilishoto-- enkure-- nepejori ninye tʼenkima katukul-- amu egol Engai Olaitoriani oigwenaki ninye."
Revelation18:9 Nepuo aaishiraki neilishoki ninye ilkarsisi lʼenkop ootaasa mbaak torrok entalare neiguran te nebo o ninye-- teni edol empuruo empejoto enye."
Revelation18:10 Nepuo aaitashe tʼenelakwa tʼenkuretishu emion enye nejo: Oi-- kake aiya-- ena ang' kitok Babilon-- engang' naikarra-- amu kitabaikia tʼesaa nabo enkigwena ino."
Revelation18:11 Nepuo lamirak lʼenkop aaishiraki ninye neilishoki-- tiaraki nemekure etii oltung'ani oinyang'u ntokitin enye--"
Revelation18:12 anaa nʼesahabu-- o noo ngoshola-- o noo soito oogol enkinyang'a-- o soito ooji lulu-- o ilkarashi oopuyapui neibor-- o ilkilani oodo-- o le hariri-- o nkilani naanyokio-- o pooki shani orropil-- o pooki toki oo lala loo ljang'ito sapukin-- o pooki toki naitobirieki lkeek sidan-- o noo suia-- o noo sekenge-- o nʼosoit owang'--"
Revelation18:13 o ngabobok oo mdalasini-- o ngoirienito naairishoreki-- o eilata narropil-- o ilbani-- o enaisho-- o eilata lʼoljani-- o entaba naibor-- o engano-- o nkishu-- o ntare-- o mbartan-- o ilgarrin-- o seseni o iltauja loo ltung'anak;"
Revelation18:14 o ilmomo ootonyorra oltau lino-- kitung'aitie-- o ntokitin pookin naapir o naaikishaan-- kitulusoitie-- nimintoki adol katukul."
Revelation18:15 Ore lamirak loo nona masaa-- ootudupore ninje-- nepuo aaitashe tʼenelakwa tʼenkuretishu emion enye-- eishir neilish"
Revelation18:16 aajo: Kake aiya-- aiya-- aiya ena ang' kitok-- naishopokoki nkilani naapuyapui neibor-- o nkilani naado-- o nkilani naanyokio-- neikodi tʼesahabu o too soito oogol enkinyang'a o too lulu!"
Revelation18:17 Amu tʼesaa nabo eitarruoiyoki masaa kumok naaba nji. O ilkituak loo meilini pookin-- o pookin ooasisho too meilini-- o pookin ooitobirisho tʼenaiposha-- neitashe tʼenelakwa--"
Revelation18:18 neishir pedol empuruo empejoto enye nejo: Kaa ang' narisiore ena ang' tʼenkitook?
Revelation18:19 Nepik ninje enterit shumata oo lukuny enye-- nebuak aaishir-- neilish-- nejo: Kake aiya-- aiya ena ang' kitok nainotie endupoto kulo pookin looata meilini tʼenaiposha-- too masaa enyena-- amu eitarruoiyoki tʼesaa nabo."
Revelation18:20 Enting'idakinoto ndai ninye-- iye shumata-- o ndai sinyat o lairriwak o layolounok; amu eigwenaka Engai ninye enkigwena inyi."
Revelation18:21 Nedumu olmalaika ogol osoit kitok laijo osoit oituutishoreki anang'aki atua enaiposha-- nejo: Neijia eurokini enkop tʼolkutati kitok nabo Babilon-- ena ang' kitok-- nemeitokini ninye aadol tukul;"
Revelation18:22 nemeitokini aaning' tiatua iye oltoilo loo loosh engauo oo singolioitin o loosh nkisuleta o ndulen o mowuarak; nemeitokini aatum tiatua iye oltung'ani arriya lʼenkyas engarriyano oo nabo; nemeitokini aaning' tiatua iye oltoilo loo soito ooituut engano tukul;
Revelation18:23 nemeitoki ailang'isho tiatua iye eong'an enkilang'et-- nemeitokini aaning' oltoilo lʼosanja o lʼesanja tiatua iye. Amu era opa lamirak linono ilkituak lʼenkop; amu esakutore ino naitapong'oiye loreren pookin lʼenkop;"
Revelation18:24 nenyorrikini tiatua ninye osarge loo layolounok o loo sinyat o loo kulo pookin ootaraki tʼenkop.
Revelation19:1 Ore peishunye kuna-- naning' oltoilo loo siamin kituak te shumata-- oojo: Haleluya! Ore enkitopuata o enkitook o engolon-- njeaku nʼEngai ang'--"
Revelation19:2 amu esipa naa supati nkigwenaitin enyena-- tiaraki naigwenaka ninye ina ng'oroyoni entalare-- naitarruoiye enkop pookin tʼentalare enye-- netalaakaki osarge loo singan lenyena ngaik enyena."
Revelation19:3 Nejo ninje kat are: Haleluya! neilep empuruo enye alo shumata metabaiki nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin.
Revelation19:4 Ore lelo paiyani tikitam o ong'wan o ng'wesi ong'wan-- nebatata aaserem Engai naton tʼolorika lʼenkitoria aajo: Amen. Haleluya!"
Revelation19:5 Nelotu oltoilo oing'ua olorika lʼenkitoria ojo: Entadarai Engai ang'-- ndai singan lenyena pookin o kulo ooure ninye pokira-- looti o ilkituak."
Revelation19:6 Naning' nanu anaa oltoilo loo siamin kituak-- o anaa oltoilo loo ngariak kituak-- o anaa oltoilo loo ndarat naagol-- ejo: Haleluya! Amu etang'amua Engai ang'-- Olaitoriani tʼengolon pookin-- enkarsishu."
Revelation19:7 Mating'idata nikining' enjipai-- maitaa ninye kitok-- amu etabaua enkiama Embalelo neitobirakino eng'oroyoni enye--"
Revelation19:8 neishooki ninye meishopo olkila sidai oibor naleng'; amu ore olkila oibor sidai-- naa supaton oo sinyat."
Revelation19:9 Naajoki: Tisira! Teshi kulo ooipotokoki endaata Embalelo. Naajoki: Ore kulo-- naa rorei oosipa lʼEngai."
Revelation19:10 Nabatatakino nkejek enyena aserem ninye. Naajoki ninye: Ng'orai-- minko neijia! Amu ara olang'arani lino o loo lalashera linono o loo kulo ooata enjakenishu e Yesus. Teserema Engai! Amu ore enjakenishu e Yesus-- naa Olmumua lʼenkitayolounoto."
Revelation19:11 Nadol shumata etabole-- naa ng'orai-- embarta naibor. Ore olokedito neji: Supat-- nesipa-- neigwenu neara tʼesupato."
Revelation19:12 Netiu ngonyek enyena anaa olng'ejep lʼenkima-- neata tʼelukunya enye nkeenda enkitoria kumok-- neata ninye engarna natisiraki-- nemetii olekai otayolo-- leme ninye ake."
Revelation19:13 Neishopito ninye olkila osuakino osarge-- neji engama enye Ororei lʼEngai."
Revelation19:14 Nesujita ninye iltimito le shumata ookedito mbartan naaibor-- neishopito nkilani naaibor sidan naleng'."
Revelation19:15 Nepuku olalem opi tʼenkutuk enye naarie loreren lemeiruk pookin; neirrita ninje tʼeng'udi esekengei-- neroro ninye enkironyet enaisho engoro kitok Engai magilani."
Revelation19:16 Neata tʼolkila lenye o tʼenkupes enye engarna nasira: Olkarsis loo lkarsisi o Olaitoriani loo laitoriak.
Revelation19:17 Nadol olmalaika oitashe tiatua engolong' nedar tʼoltoilo kitok nejoki ilmotonyi pookin ooipirri te shumata: Wotu-- enturrurrokinoto endaata kitok Engai--"
Revelation19:18 pinyanya nkiri oo lkarsisi o noo mbartan o noo kulo ookedito ninje o nkiri oo loolakuno o noo singan-- noo looti o lkituak."
Revelation19:19 Nadol eng'wes o ilkarsisi lʼenkop o iltimito lenyena lʼenjore eiturrurrote aarare ilo okedito embarta-- o iltimito lenyena."
Revelation19:20 Neibung'i ina ng'wes te nebo o ilo ayolounoni lʼelejare-- oitobira ilponot t'engomom enye neitapong'orie kulo ootang'amutua olkigeroto lʼeng'wes neserem emua eng'wes. Nenang'akini kulo pokira are eishiu atua olbalbal lʼenkima naiwuwu tʼenkibiriti."
Revelation19:21 Neari ilkulekai tʼolalem le ilo okedito embarta-- ilo alem opuku tʼenkutuk enye. Neraposho ilmotonyi pookin too nkiri enye."
Revelation20:1 Nadol olmalaika edou aing'ua shumata neata embolet ewueji easuroto o olpisiai kitok tʼengaina enye.
Revelation20:2 Neibung' ninye entiamasi-- ol opa asurai musana-- lora oloirirua o satan-- neen enkata oo larin iip tomon--"
Revelation20:3 nenang'aki atua ewueji easuroto-- neigenoo-- neen shumata tʼolmishire-- pemeitoki ninye aitapong'oo loreren-- metabana neishunye larin iip tomon; ore peishunye lelo-- meata kata nemelaki ninye enkiti kata."
Revelation20:4 Nadol lorikan-- ore lelo ootonie ninje-- neishooki enkigwena. Nadol iltauja loo kulo ootaraki tʼolbae lʼenjakenishu e Yesus o lʼororei lʼEngai-- leitu eserem eng'wes o emua enye-- neitu eng'amu olkigeroto tʼenkirribo o tʼengaina enye; neishiu neitore ninje te nebo o Kristos larin iip tomon."
Revelation20:5 Ore ilkulekai ootuata-- neitu epiu metabana neishunye larin iip tomon. Ena empiunoto enkiterata."
Revelation20:6 Teshi o sinyat loong'ar empiunoto enkiterata-- amu meata engai kea engolon nashororie ninje."
Revelation20:7 Ore peidipai larin iip tomon-- nepuoi aalak satan aing'ua enkibooroto enye--"
Revelation20:8 nepuku ninye aitapong'oo loreren ootii nkutot pokira ong'wan enkop-- Goog o Magoog-- neiturrur ninje aiko enjore-- neba esiana enye anaa osunyai lʼenaiposha."
Revelation20:9 Neilep ninje metabaiki endapasho enkop-- neman enkirragata oo sinyat o engang' nanyorri. Nedou enkima aing'ua shumata tʼEngai amut ninje."
Revelation20:10 Nenang'akini oloirirua oitapong'oiye-- olbalbal lʼenkima o enkibiriti-- enetii si eng'wes o olayolounoni lʼelejare; nepuoi aaitame dama o kiarie o nkatan pookin."
Revelation20:11 Nadol olorika lʼenkitoria kitok oibor-- ore ilo otonie olorika-- nedanya enkop o shumata engomom enye-- nelai ewueji enye."
Revelation20:12 Nadol lootuata-- ilkituak o looti-- eitashe tʼengomom olorika lʼenkitoria-- neboluni nkitabuni. Neboli engai kitabu-- naa enkitabu empuan; neigwenakini lootuata too mbaak naatisiraki tiatua nkitabuni-- tʼerisioroto oo nkitobirat enye."
Revelation20:13 Neitai enaiposha lootuata ootii atua ninye-- neitai enkea o gehena lootuata ootii atua ninje; neigwenakini oltung'ani pookin tʼerisioroto oo nkitobirat enyena."
Revelation20:14 Nenang'akini enkea o gehena olbalbal lʼenkima. Naa ninye enkea e are-- olbalbal lʼenkima."
Revelation20:15 Ore oltung'ani leitu etumi-- etisiraki engarna enye tʼenkitabu empuan-- nenang'akini olbalbal lʼenkima."
Revelation21:1 Nadol shumata ng'ejuk o enkop ng'ejuk-- amu etulu soiye shumata elukunya o enkop elukunya--"
Revelation21:2 nemekure etii enaiposha. Nadol engang' sinyati-- Yerusalem ng'ejuk-- edou te shumata aing'ua Engai-- eitobiraki anaa esanja natakajakaki olmoruo lenye."
Revelation21:3 Naning' oltoilo kitok oing'ua olorika lʼenkitoria ejo: Ng'orai-- emanyata Engai te nebo o iltung'anak-- nelamany te nebo o ninje-- nepuo aaku ninje loreren lenyena-- netii ninye openy-- Engai-- e nebo o ninje."
Revelation21:4 Nelajutu Engai ilkiyo pookin too ngonyek enye nemeitoki atii enkea arashu enkilishoto arashu enkishirata arashu meitoki atii emion; amu etulusoitie mbaak elukunya.
Revelation21:5 Nejo ilo oton tʼolorika lʼenkitoria: Ng'orai-- aitaa ntokitin pookin ng'ejuko. Naajoki: Tisira-- amu supati kulo rorei nesipa."
Revelation21:6 Naajoki ninye: Eidipe. Ara nanu A o O-- enkiterata o enkiting'oto. Ayeu naisho Oloata enkure tʼenjorro engare empuan pesho."
Revelation21:7 Ologilu-- nelajung'u kuna pookin-- naaku nanu Engai enye-- neaku ninye engerai ai."
Revelation21:8 Kake ore looing'ashaa-- o lemeiruk-- o looisho osina-- o larak-- o looas mbaak torrok oo nkiri-- o lasakutok-- o looserem muain neme Engai-- o lalejak pookin-- nepuo aajing' olbalbal lʼengumoto-- eneiwuwu enkima o enkibiriti; naa ninye enkea e are."
Revelation21:9 Nelotu obo too lelo malaikan oopishana ooata ngirran naapishana naaigany ntabo naapishana enkiting'oto-- naairorie nanu ejo: Wou ene-- maitadua ina ng'oroyoni-- esanja Embalelo."
Revelation21:10 Naarik tʼolmumua shumata oldonyo kitok oado-- naaitadol engang' kitok-- Yerusalem sinyati-- edou te shumata aing'ua Engai."
Revelation21:11 Neata ninye enkitook Engai-- netiu enkilang'et enye osoit oji yaspis owang' naleng'."
Revelation21:12 Neata esundai sapuk naado-- neata kishomini tomon o are-- o shumata oo kishomini ilmalaikan tomon o are-- netisiraki ngam too kishomini-- naa ngam oo ntipati tomon o are oo nkera Israel."
Revelation21:13 Netii engalo nailepunye engolong' kishomini uni-- netii empolos enkiarie kishomini uni-- netii moikwape kishomini uni-- o engalo nadoiyorie engolong' kishomini uni."
Revelation21:14 Neata esundai engang' ntonat tomon o are o tiatua ninje ngam oo lairriwak tomon o are lʼEmbalelo.
Revelation21:15 Ore ilo laairorie-- neata entiani esahabu-- peiye etem engang' o kishomini o esundai enyena."
Revelation21:16 Ore ina ang'-- neitorisi mbat pokira ong'wan-- nerisioro engadoro o endapasho. Netem ninye engang' tʼentiani-- neaku nang'arot osoit iip tomon kat tomon o are; nerisioro engadoro o endapasho o engadoro nailep engang'."
Revelation21:17 Netem esundai enye-- nera ntemeta oo ngaik iip o artam o ong'wan-- t'entemet oo ltung'anak naata olmalaika."
Revelation21:18 Ore enjetata esundai enye-- naa yaspis-- ore engang' naa esahabu sidai natiu anaa bilauri sidai."
Revelation21:19 Ore ntonat esundai engang'-- netakajaki too soito sidan oogol enkinyang'a. Ore entonata elukunya naa yaspis-- ore en e are naa yakuti sidai-- ore en e uni naa akiki naibor-- ore en e ong'wan naa smaragid--"
Revelation21:20 ore en e imiet naa akiki warikoi-- ore en e ile naa akiki nanyokie-- ore en e napishana naa sabariyadi-- ore en e isiet naa smaragid nanyori-- ore en e enturuj naa yakuti warikoi-- ore en e tomon naa akiki nanyori-- ore en e tomon o nabo-- naa akiki naijo eng'atamboi-- ore en e tomon o are naa ametistos."
Revelation21:21 Nera nena kishomini tomon o are soito sidan ooji lulu tomon o are-- ore kishomi pookin-- neitaunyeki lulu nabo. Ore ngoitoi engang'-- naa esahabu sidai-- nawang' naleng' anaa bilauri berlel."
Revelation21:22 Neitu adol engaji sinyati tiatua-- amu era Olaitoriani-- Engai magilani-- engaji sinyati enye-- o Embalelo."
Revelation21:23 Nemeyeu ina ang' engolong' ana olapa-- peilang'aki ninye-- amu eilang'aki enkitook Engai ninye-- ore enkilang'et enye-- naa Embalelo."
Revelation21:24 Nepuo loreren aalimana tʼenkilang'et enye; neau ilkarsisi lʼenkop enkitook enye atua ninye.
Revelation21:25 Nemeitokini aaigen kishomini enyena dama-- amu meitoki atii enkiarie ine."
Revelation21:26 Neau ninje enkitook o enganyit oo loreren aapik atua ninye.
Revelation21:27 Nemejing' atua ninye entoki duruki arashu enaitobir entorroni ana elejare-- neme lelo ake ootisiraki ngam enye tiatua enkitabu empuan Embalelo oojing'."
Revelation22:1 Naaitadol ninye olkeju lʼengare empuan-- nailiil anaa bilauri-- naing'ua ilo orika lʼenkitoria lʼEngai o Embalelo."
Revelation22:2 Ore tʼempolos engoitoi enye-- o too mbat pokira are olkeju-- netii nkeek empuan-- naata ilmomo mpukunot tomon o are-- neiu ilmomo lenye olapa pookin-- naa mbenek oo nena keek ninje naaishiunye loreren lemeata Engai."
Revelation22:3 Nemeitoki atii oldeket katukul. Naa ine etii olorika lʼenkitoria lʼEngai o Embalelo-- nepuo singan lenyena aaisyayaki ninye"
Revelation22:4 nedol ninje engomom enye-- nepiki engarna enye too nkirribon enye."
Revelation22:5 Nemeitoki atii enkiarie katukul-- nemeyeu enkilang'et-- arashu eong'an engolong'-- amu Olaitoriani Engai-- oisho ninje eong'an-- neitore ninje metabaiki nkatan pookin o nkatan pookin."
Revelation22:6 Naajoki nanu: Era kulo rorei supati nesipa; eirriua Olaitoriani-- Engai oo lmumuan loo layolounok-- olmalaika lenye-- meitadua singan lenyena ntokitin nemeata kata nemepuonu aasioki."
Revelation22:7 Ng'orai-- alotu asioki. Tesh oloibung' rorei lʼenkitayolounoto tʼena kitabu."
Revelation22:8 Naa nanu-- Yohanes-- otoning'o nadol kuna baak. Ore paning' nadol-- nabatatakino enkop-- asai too nkejek olmalaika laaitadua nanu kuna baak."
Revelation22:9 Naajoki ninye: Ng'orai-- minko neijia-- amu ara si nanu osinga anaa iye o lalashera linono o kulo looibung' rorei lʼena kitabu. Tasaiya Engai!"
Revelation22:10 Naajoki nanu: Mien rorei lʼenkitayolounoto lʼena kitabu tʼolmishire! Amu etinyikua enkata.
Revelation22:11 Olora torrono-- njeaku torrono oade; olora duruki-- njeaku duruki oade: kake olora supat-- njeaku supat oade-- o olora sinyati-- njeaku sinyati oade."
Revelation22:12 Ng'orai-- alotu asioki-- netii olkwaje lai te nebo o nanu-- paisho oltung'ani pookin anaa peikununo nkitobirat enyena."
Revelation22:13 Ara nanu A o O-- enkiterata o enkiting'oto-- ol elukunya o olobaiye."
Revelation22:14 Teshi kulo-- looibung' nkitanapat enyena-- petum engolon nang'arie nkeek empuan-- nejing' too kishomini atua engang'."
Revelation22:15 Amu ti aulo etii ildiain o lasakutok o looas mbaak torrok oo nkiri-- o larak-- o looserem muain neme Engai-- o pookin oonyor neitobir elejare."
Revelation22:16 Nanu-- Yesus-- oirriwaiye olmalaika lai-- peijakenoki ndai kuna baak-- naara noo sirito. Ara nanu entonai o enkishon e David-- nara ilo akira lʼentadekenya oibor."
Revelation22:17 Nejo Olmumua o esanja: Wou! Ore ilo oning'-- metejo: Wou! Oloata enkure-- njelotu; ore oloyeu-- njeea engare empuan pesho!"
Revelation22:18 Aijakenoki oltung'ani pookin oning' rorei lʼenkitayolounoto Eena kitabu: Teni eponiki ninje-- nelaponiki Engai ninye ntabo naatisiraki tiatua ena kitabu."
Revelation22:19 Teni eitai oltung'ani too rorei l'enkitabu ena kitayolounoto-- neitai si Engai ematua enye tiatua nkeek empuan o tiatua engang' sinyati-- naatisiraki tiatua ena kitabu."
Revelation22:20 Ore ilo oijakenu kuna-- nejo: Ee-- alotu asioki. Amen-- wou-- Laitoriani Yesus!"
